 I Kauśīdyavīryotsāhanāvadāna
  oṃ namaḥ śrīsarvabuddhabodhisatvebhyaḥ 
 yaḥ śrīmāñ chrīghano loke saddharmaṃ samupādiśat 
 śāsanāni trilokeṣu jayantu tasya sarvadā  Rm 
 athāśoko mahārājaḥ kṛtāñjaliḥ pramoditaḥ 
 upaguptaṃ yatiṃ natvā punar evam abhāṣata  Rm 
 bhadanta śrotum ichāmi punar anyat subhāṣitaṃ 
 tad yathā guruṇādiṣṭaṃ tathā deṣṭuṃ ca me 'rhati  Rm 
 iti saṃprārthitaṃ rājñā śrutvā so 'rhan yatiḥ sudhīḥ 
 upagupto narendraṃ taṃ samālokyaivam ādiśat  RmA 
 sādhu śṛṇu mahārāja yathā me guruṇoditaṃ 
 tathāhaṃ te pravakṣyāmi śrutvā cāpy anumodaya  Rm 
 purāsau bhagavān buddhaḥ śākyasiṃho dayānidhiḥ 
 dharmarājo jagacchāstā sarvajñaḥ sugato jinaḥ  Rm 
 Rm 
 sarvavidyākalābhijñaḥ ṣaḍabhijño munīśvaraḥ 
 mārajil lokavin nātho vināyakas tathāgataḥ  Rm 
 śravastyāṃ jetakāraṇye mahodyāne manorame 
 anāthapiṇḍadākhyasya gṛhasthasya mahātmanaḥ  Rm 
 nānāvṛkṣaiḥ samāpanne nānāpuṣpapraśobhitaiḥ 
 nānāphalabharānamraiḥ kalpapādapasannibhaiḥ  Rm 
 aṣṭāṅgaguṇasaṃpannajalaiḥ padmotpalādibhiḥ 
 puṣpaiś ca paripūrṇābhiḥ puṣkariṇībhir āśrite  Rm 
 nānājantugaṇaiś cāpi mithasnehanivandhitaiḥ 
 nānāpakṣigaṇaiś cāpi saṃrāvair upasevite  Rm 
 tasmin divyamanoramya ārāme pariśobhite 
 puṇyakṣetre jināvāse vihāre maṇimaṇḍite  Rm 
 śrāvakair bhikṣubhiḥ sārddhaṃ bodhisatvagaṇair api 
 sarvasatvahitārthena tasthau dharmaṃ prakāśituṃ  Rm 
 evaṃ tatra samāsīnaṃ saṃbuddhaṃ dharmadeśinaṃ 
 dṛṣṭvā dharmottamaṃ śrotuṃ sarve lokāḥ samāyayuḥ  Rm 
 devā daityāś ca siddhāś ca yakṣagaṃdharvakinnarāḥ 
 grahā vidyādharāś cāpi nāgāś ca garuḍā api  Rm 
 sarve 'pi lokapālāś ca munayaś ca maharṣayaḥ 
 brāhmaṇāḥ kṣatriyāś cāpi vaiśyāś ca maṃtriṇo janāḥ  Rm 
 amātyāḥ sādhavaḥ śūdrāḥ sārthavāhā mahājanāḥ 
 dhanino vaṇijaś cāpi gṛhasthāḥ paurikā api  Rm 
 tathā jānapadāś cāpi grāmyāḥ kārpaṭikā api 
 evam anye 'pi satvāś ca saddharmaśravaṇārthinaḥ  Rm 
 pūjāpaṃcopahārāṇi gṛhītvā bhaktisaṃyutāḥ 
 saddharmaṃ saugataṃ śrotum anumodya samāyayuḥ  Rm 
 sarve tatra praviṣṭās te dṛṣṭvā taṃ sugataṃ jinaṃ 
 vismitānaṃditāḥ pūjāṃ kṛtvā natvā yathākramaṃ  Rm 
 sarve tatra samāsīnāḥ parivṛtāḥ puraskṛtāḥ 
 taṃ dṛṣṭvā sadguruṃ dharmaṃ śrotuṃ tasthuḥ samāhitāḥ  Rm 
 athāsau bhagavān dṛṣṭvā lokān sarvān samāhitān 
 ādimadhyāntakalyāṇaṃ dideśa dharmam uttamaṃ  Rm 
 evaṃ nityam asau nāthaḥ sarvasatvahitārthikaḥ 
 dharmaṃ prakāśayan loke tasthau bhānur ivoditaḥ  Rm 
 Rm 
 tasmiṃś ca samaye tatra śrāvastyāṃ sanmahājanaḥ 
 āḍhyaḥ śreṣṭhī mahābhogo vistīrṇasuparigrahaḥ  Rm 
 śrāddho bhadrāśayo dhīmān sarvabandhusuhṛtpriyaḥ 
 tīrthikaśrāvako mānī babhūva dhanagarvitaḥ  Rm 
 tadāsau sundarīṃ bhāryyāṃ kuladharmasamānikāṃ 
 nītvā kāmaguṇāsakto reme nityaṃ tayā saha  Rm 
 tasyaivaṃ ramatas tasyāṃ bhāryāyāṃ sucirād api 
 putro na duhitā vāpi nodbabhūva kathaṃ cana  Rm 
 tad aputro gṛhastho 'sau putrābhidarśanotsukaḥ 
 kapolaṃ svakare dhṛtvā vyacintayad raho gataḥ  Rm 
 aho daivān na me putraḥ putrī vādyāpi nāsti yat 
 tan me syuḥ saṃpado vyarthāyāsāṃ bhoktā na vidyate  Rm 
 kiṃ mamaitair dhanai ratnaiḥ kevalaṃ duhkhasādhanaiḥ 
 yeṣāṃ bhoktā na vidyeta vyarthaṃ mayā hy upārjitaṃ  Rm 
 hy aputrasya jagac chūnyaṃ saṃsāre niḥsukhaṃ mama 
 yato na varddhate dharmas taj janmāpi ca nisphalaṃ  Rm 
 kim upāyaṃ kariṣyāmi yato bhāgyaṃ na vidyate 
 daivo hi valavāṃl loke kim upāyair guṇair valaiḥ  Rm 
 kutrātra śaraṇaṃ yāsye hy aputro 'haṃ kulāntakaḥ 
 tan me syāt ko 'tra sanmitraṃ saṃkaṭe yaḥ samuddharet  Rm 
 nūnaṃ me pitaraḥ sarve piṇḍavichedadarśinaḥ 
 matparaṃ durlabhaṃ matvā bhaviṣyanti nirāśitāḥ  Rm 
 sarvathāhaṃ vinaṣṭo 'smi kuladharmavināśakaḥ 
 kiṃ paratra prabhokṣyāmi ko me piṇḍaṃ pradāsyati  Rm 
 iti cintāviṣaṇṇaṃ taṃ dṛṣṭvā sarve ca bāndhavāḥ 
 Rm 
 samupetya samāmaṃtrya duhkhahetum apṛchan  Rm 
 kiṃ duḥsthito 'si sādho 'tra kiṃ cāpi duḥkhacintayā 
 vaktavyaṃ cet tad asmākaṃ sarvathā vaktum arhasi  Rm 
 iti pṛṣṭe gṛhastho 'sau dīrghaniśvāsam utsṛjan 
 sarvāṃs tān bāndhavān dṛṣṭvā duḥkhahetum udaharat  Rm 
 bhavantaḥ śrūyatāṃ sarvair mama duḥkhasya kāraṇaṃ 
 yad adyāpi na me putraḥ putrī vāpi na vidyate  Rm 
 saṃpado me gṛhe santi sarvaratnasamanvitāḥ 
 sarvadravyasamṛddhāś ca tāsāṃ bhoktā na vidyate  Rm 
 tat sarvaṃ nakṣyate vyarthaṃ mayā yātnair upārjitaṃ 
 aputrasya hi sarvasvaṃ nūnaṃ rājā grahīṣyti  Rm 
 aputro 'haṃ hy apuṇyātmā gantavyaṃ maraṇaṃ dhruvaṃ 
 pretībhūtasya me ko 'nyaḥ piṇḍadānaṃ pradāsyati  Rm 
 mayā na prakṛtaṃ puṇyaṃ saṃpadarthaprasaṃginā 
 tan me sarvaṃ nirarthaṃ syāt ko māṃ pāpāt samuddharet  Rm 
 iha bhogyaṃ prabhuktvāpi kiṃ me sāram avasthitaṃ 
 kevalaṃ dhanasaktasya paratra sadgatiḥ kathaṃ  Rm 
 iti cintā hṛdi sthitvā cittaṃ me tudate 'niśaṃ 
 evaṃ cittavyathākrāntaḥ śalyaviddha ivāsmy ahaṃ  Rm 
 tad vyathāharaṇopāyaṃ dātavyaṃ mama taddhitaṃ 
 anyathā ced ihāmutra vinaṣṭaḥ syāṃ nirāśitaḥ  Rm 
 iti tenoditaṃ śrutvā sarve te bāndhavā janāḥ 
 karuṇāviṣṭacittās taṃ bodhayantaḥ samabruvan  Rm 
 mā mā bhaiṣṭhā mahābhāga tyaja cintāṃ vacaḥ śṛṇu 
 tadupāyaṃ vayaṃ brūmas tat kuruṣva samāhitaḥ  Rm 
 devatārādhanāṃ kṛtvā kuruṣva vaṃśayācanāṃ 
 nūnaṃ vaṃśaṃ pradāsyanti devatās te prasāditāḥ  Rm 
 Rm 
 eṣa loke pravādo 'sti yad āyācanahetutaḥ 
 putrā duhitaro vāpi jātā devaprasādataḥ  Rm 
 tathā naiva pramāṇaṃ syāc chāstre karmapramāṇataḥ 
 tat tu devaprasādena karmaś śīghraṃ prasiddhyate  Rm 
 tad eva devavairuddhe karma vighnair nihanyate 
 tasmād daivaprasiddhyarthaṃ śraddhābhaktisamāhitaḥ  Rm 
 devatārādhanāṃ kṛtvā sarvakāryyaṃ prasādhayet 
 iti matvā bhavāṃś cāpi satputrapratipattaye  Rm 
 bhāryyayā saha bhaktyā ca devatāyācanāṃ kuru 
 tato raktaiḥ priyāṃ bhāryām ṛtusnātāṃ prakāmataḥ  Rm 
 gāḍham āliṃgya saṃrakto dharmavījaṃ praropaya 
 tato devaprabhāvena suniṣpannaḥ prasiddhitaḥ  Rm 
 tvatputraḥ saṃprajāyeta satyam evaṃ pramāṇaya 
 iti teṣāṃ vacaḥ śrutvā gṛhastho 'sau vinoditaḥ  Rm 
 tatheti ca pratiśrutya bhāryyayā saha moditaḥ 
 śivabrahmādideveśān iṃdrādidigadhīśvarān  Rm 
 jalāśrayavanārāmacatvaramaṇḍapālayān 
 sūryyādīṃś ca grahān sarvā bhairavādyāś ca mātṛkāḥ  Rm 
 svakulādhipatīṃ devān anyāṃś ca tribhavasthitān 
 sarvān evaṃ samārādhya pūjayitvā vidhānataḥ  Rm 
 saṃtānaṃ prārthayitvāsau patnyā saha tathāramat 
 tadā kaścin mahāsatvaḥ svargāc cyutvā bhuvaṃ gataḥ  Rm 
 tasya gṛhapateḥ patnyā garbhe sa samupāviśat 
 tataḥ sā śreṣṭhino bhāryyāpannasatvāśu gurviṇī  Rm 
 garbhe satvaṃ samutpannaṃ matvā bharttāram abravīt 
 svāmin prasīda mā bhūs tvaṃ viṣaṇno 'tra sukhī bhava  Rm 
 tava bhāgyād dhi me garbhe nūnaṃ satvaḥ pravarttate 
 Rm 
 yad garbhe dakṣiṇe bhāge sthitaḥ saṃparivarttate  Rm 
 tan nūnaṃ dārako 'yaṃ syāt satyam eva na saṃśayaḥ 
 iti bhāryāvacaḥ śrutvā gṛhastho 'sau pramoditaḥ  Rm 
 bhāryāyā garbham ālokya satyam ity anvamanyata  Rm 
 tato 'sau sahasā vandhusuhṛnmitrasahāyakān 
 prāhūya puratas teṣāṃ mudaivaṃ samudānayat  Rm 
 aho bhāgyān mamotpannaṃ yad abhivāṃchitaṃ mayā 
 dhanyo 'smi nāvagītaḥ syād devatānuprasādataḥ  Rm 
 cirābhilaṣitaṃ putramukhaṃ paśyeya sāṃprataṃ 
 kṛtyā me pratikurvīta bhṛtaś ca prativibhṛyāt  Rm 
 dāyādyaṃ pratipadyeta vaṃśo me sthitiko bhavet 
 suhṛdo me prasannāḥ syur dviṣantaś ca viṣāditāḥ  Rm 
 mayā yāvanti dānāni puṇyāni prakṛtāni ca 
 etatpuṇyaphalair nityaṃ maṃgalaṃ bhavatu dvayoḥ  Rm 
 etatpuṇyānubhāvena bhūyān mātā nirāturā 
 sukhaṃ sunotu satputraṃ mā pāpaṃ samudāgamat  Rm 
 iti tenoditaṃ śrutvā sarve bandhusuhṛtsakhāḥ 
 tathāstv ity anumodantaḥ svasvālayaṃ samāyayuḥ  Rm 
 tato 'sau garbhiṇī kāntā kramād garbhapravarddhitā 
 vaidyopadiṣṭam āhāraṃ bhuktvācarad yathā sukhaṃ  Rm 
 tataś ca samaye 'sūta putraṃ kāntaṃ manoharaṃ 
 sarvalakṣaṇasaṃpannaṃ bhadrāṃśaṃ maṃgalānvitaṃ  Rm 
 tac chrutvaiva gṛhastho 'sau suprasannaḥ pramoditaḥ 
 dṛṣṭvā taṃ dārakaṃ saumyaṃ naiva tṛptiṃ samāyayau  Rm 
 tato jñātīn samāhūya kṛtvā jātimahaṃ mudā 
 putranāmābhisaṃskartuṃ bhūya etān samabravīt  Rm 
 bhavanto dṛśyatāṃ siddhaṃ mamabhilaṣitaṃ cirāt 
 Rm 
 tan nāmāsya yathāyogyaṃ prasiddhaṃ kriyatāṃ śubhaṃ  Rm 
 iti tasya vacaḥ śrutvā sarve te jñātayo mudā 
 dārakaṃ taṃ samālokya naṃditāḥ samabhāṣata  Rm 
 yasmin dine hy ayaṃ jātas tadā sarve 'pi paurikāḥ 
 nanditās tad bhavatv ayaṃ nāmnā nanda iti śrutaḥ  Rm 
 athāsau dārako nandaḥ samyag dehopacāraṇe 
 pitrāṣṭāsu ca dhātrīṣu paritoṣya samarpitaḥ  Rm 
 tato 'sau kramaśas tāsāṃ dhātriṇām upacārataḥ 
 dine dine pravṛddho 'bhūd dhradasthaṃ paṃkajaṃ yathā  Rm 
 evaṃ pravarddhamāno 'sau ṣaḍvarṣiko yadābhavat 
 tadā kuśīdasaṃvṛtto babhūva viratotsavaḥ  Rm 
 sadā śayyāsanasthas tat samutthātuṃ na caichata 
 śayyāsanasthitaś caiva bhuktvā naivācarat kvacit  Rm 
 sadā svāntargṛhastho 'pi sutīkṣṇabuddhimān sudhīḥ 
 adhītya sarvaśāstrāṇi satyadharmarato 'bhavat  Rm 
 atha śreṣṭhī pitā dṛṣṭvā putram evaṃ kuśīditaṃ 
 sarvavidyāguṇādhāraṃ dṛṣṭvā caivaṃ vyacintayat  Rm 
 kathaṃ cid yo mayā prāpto devatāsaṃprasādataḥ 
 so 'pi putro mamābhāgyād bhavaty evaṃ kuśīditaḥ  Rm 
 sarvavidyāguṇādhāraṃ sarvaśāstravicakṣaṇaḥ 
 kiṃ mamānena putreṇa dusthiteneva roginā 
 yataḥ svasthaśarīro 'pi bhuktvaivaṃ paśuvat sthitaḥ  Rm 
 kim atrāhaṃ kariṣyāmi yat putro 'yaṃ ni rudyamaḥ 
 kim īdrigjantunā kāryyaṃ kuladharmopahāriṇā  Rm 
 dhig me daivaṃ prayatnaṃ ca sarvaṃ tat syān nirarthakaṃ 
 kim upāyaṃ kariṣyāmi sarvathāhaṃ vibhagnitaḥ  Rm 
 evaṃ cintāparīto 'sau gṛhasthaś ca vyacintayat 
 pūraṇo me 'sti śāstā yaḥ pṛcheyaṃ tad upāyakaṃ  Rm 
 iti matvā gṛhastho 'sau tad āśramaṃ samāgataḥ 
 pūraṇaṃ taṃ guruṃ natvā papraccha tadupāyatāṃ  Rm 
 Rm 
 bhagavan bho mahābhijña śāstāsi me prasīda tat 
 yan mayā pṛchyate kāryyaṃ tat samādeṣṭum arhasi  Rm 
 iti tenārthitaṃ śrutvā tīrthiko mānagarvitaḥ 
 āśu siddhaṃ kariṣyāmo yat kāryyaṃ te 'tra tad vada  Rm 
 iti proktvaivam āśvāsya pūraṇo 'tyabhimānikaḥ 
 pravadaṃs taṃ gṛhasthaṃ vai sarvathaivam abodhayat  Rm 
 iti tena samādiṣṭaṃ śrutvā gṛhapatir mudā 
 kṛtāñjalipuṭo natvā taṃ guruṃ samabhāṣata  Rm 
 bhagavan bho vijānīyā yo me putraḥ prajāyate 
 sa pravṛddho nirutsāhī kuśīdo varttate 'dhunā  Rm 
 sadā śayyāsthito bhuṅkte bhuktvā śete nirudyamaḥ 
 notsahati kvacid gaṃtuṃ paśuvat tiṣṭhate gṛhe  Rm 
 na śayanāt samutthāya śrotuṃ draṣṭuṃ samicchati 
 gṛhe śayyāsanārūḍho rogīva vasate sadā  Rm 
 tadupāyaṃ kathaṃ kuryyāṃ yenāyaṃ śayanotthitaḥ 
 śrotuṃ draṣṭuṃ ca gaṃtuṃ ca karttuṃ kāryyaṃ yathotsahet  Rm 
 tathā me bhagavan putraṃ kuladharme niyojaya 
 bhavān eva hi me śāstā tad dhitaṃ kartum arhasi  Rm 
 ity evaṃ prārthitaṃ tena śrutvāsau pūraṇo yatiḥ 
 tasya gṛhapateś cittaṃ praharṣayan samabravīt  Rm 
 are mā gā viṣādaṃ tvaṃ cintayā kiṃ pratapyase 
 asmāsu vidyamāneṣu ṣaṭsu vijñeṣu śāstṛṣu  Rm 
 tad ahaṃ te mahābhāga sārddhaṃ sarvaiś ca tīrthikaiḥ 
 ṛddhyā gatvā kariṣyāmi dārakaṃ vistayotthitaṃ  Rm 
 yadāsau dārako hy asmān sarvān dṛṣṭvā samutthitaḥ 
 kṛtvā praṇāmam asmākaṃ dharmmaṃ śrotuṃ samutsahet  Rm 
 śrutvā dharmasamutsāhāt kuśalāni samācaret 
 tatkuśalaiḥ samāpanno vīryavān sa bhavet sudhīḥ  Rm 
 Rm 
 tatas te sarvakāryāṇi sādhayet sa samudyataḥ 
 svakuladharmakarmāṇi kuśalī saṃcariṣyate  Rm 
 evaṃ me vacanaṃ satyaṃ dṛṣṭvā samyak pramāṇaya 
 tad viṣādaṃ parityajya karttavyaṃ hi tathā kuru  Rm 
 iti tena samādiṣṭaṃ śrutvā sa gṛhabhṛn mudā 
 sahasā svagṛhaṃ gatvā tad bhojyaṃ samasādhayat  Rm 
 athāsau pūraṇo 'nyaiś ca tīrthikaiḥ sārddham āgataḥ 
 gṛhe gatvā puras tasya paryyaṅke samupāśrayat  Rm 
 tathāsau tān samāgatvā kramaśa āsane sthitān 
 dṛṣṭvā saṃharṣitaḥ śreṣṭhī sahasā putram abravīt  Rm 
 putra paśya gṛhe 'smākaṃ śāstāraḥ samupasthitāḥ 
 tat samutthāya natvaitāñ chāstṝn bhojyaiḥ pravāraya  Rm 
 ity uktvā janakenāsau dārako na samutthitaḥ 
 draṣṭum api na cotsehe kiṃ namec ca pravārayet  Rm 
 bahuśaḥ preryyamāṇo 'pi pitrā sa bandhubhiḥ saha 
 dārakas tān samāsīnān draṣṭum api na caichata  Rm 
 kiṃ punar utthito natvā bhojaṇaiḥ saṃpravārayet 
 tathā śayyāsanārūḍha evaṃ tasthau nirutsavaḥ  Rm 
 tatas te tīrthikāḥ sarve dṛṣṭvaivaṃ nirutsavaṃ 
 nānāvidhiprayatnais tam utthāpayitum ārabhan  Rm 
 tathāpi naiva śayyāyā udatiṣṭhat sa dārakaḥ 
 svadharmadeśakāṃś cāpi tān draṣṭum api naihata  Rm 
 evaṃ cānutthitaṃ dṛṣṭvā taṃ te sarve ca tīrthikāḥ 
 haṭhāc cainaṃ samutthāpya vaśīkarttuṃ parākraman  Rm 
 tathaitāṃs tīrthikān sarvān eva garvābhivāditān 
 Rm 
 dṛṣṭvābhisaṃmukhāyātān bhīto 'rautsīt sa dārakaḥ  Rm 
 tathā taṃ ruditaṃ dṛṣṭvā sarve te lajjayā bhiyā 
 pratijagmur vibhinnāsyāḥ svasvālayāni bheditāḥ  Rm 
 tathā gṛhapatir dṛṣṭvā sarvān etān parāyitān 
 pratibhinnaviṣaṇnātmā tasthau cintāvimohitaḥ  Rm 
 atha śrībhagavān buddhaḥ sarvadarśī vināyakaḥ 
 paśyan satvān samuddhartuṃ dadarśa taṃ kuśīditaṃ  Rm 
 dṛṣṭvā tasya kuśīdasya karmavṛttiparaṃparāṃ 
 tat kuśīdaṃ samuddhartum aryānaṃdaṃ samabravīt  Rm 
 paśyānaṃda gṛhasthasya śrāvastīpuravāsinaḥ 
 putro naṃda iti khyātaḥ sāmprataṃ saṃkuśīdikaḥ  Rm 
 asau me darśanād eva nūnaṃ vīryyaṃ samārabhan 
 sahasotthāya sa natvā dharmaṃ praśṛṇuyān mudā  Rm 
 tato me śāsane dharmaṃ pracaret sa sudhīḥ sadā 
 kramād bodhicarīṃ pūryya saṃbodhiṃ cāpi lapsyati  Rm 
 tasmāt tasya gṛhe gatvā tīrthikadarppachittaye 
 saddharme saṃpratiṣṭhāpya sarvān bodhau niyojaye  Rm 
 ity ādiṣṭaṃ munīndreṇa śrutvānandaḥ sa harṣitaḥ 
 karttavyaṃ bhagavann evam ity anumodito 'bhavat  Rm 
 tato bhagavatā tena suvarṇābhā marīcayaḥ 
 utsṛṣṭās taiś ca tad geham avabhāsya vyaśodhayat  Rm 
 yadā tair dārakaḥ spṛṣṭo buddhamaitrīmarīcibhiḥ 
 tadā prahlāditaś cāsāv ity evaṃ samacintayat  Rm 
 aho kasya prabhāvo 'yaṃ yenaivam avabhāsitaṃ 
 prahlāditaś ca me kāyas tan na jāne kutaḥ kathaṃ  Rm 
 iti cintāṃ samālambya kautukākrāntamānasaḥ 
 samantato nirīkṣyaivaṃ tasthau gehe suvismitaḥ  Rm 
 Rm 
 tathā taṃ vismitaṃ dṛṣṭvā bhagavān bhikṣubhiḥ saha 
 sahasā tadgṛhaṃ gatvā prādur āsīt prabhāsayan  Rm 
 tatra sa dārako 'paśyad bhagavantaṃ tam āsthitaṃ 
 kāntaṃ divyātiriktābhaṃ samantabhadrarūpiṇaṃ  Rm 
 dṛṣṭvaiva sahasotthāya natvā pādau pramoditaḥ

 tat prajñaptāsane sthitvā dharmaṃ deṣṭuṃ samārabhat  Rm

 pitarau jñātivargāś ca sarve 'py āsan suvismitāḥ  Rm

 Rm

 Rm

 ratnākaraṃ samāgantuṃ prārebhe saha vāṇijaiḥ  Rm

 Rm

 Rm 
 raśmayas tāḥ samantāc ca trailokyaṃ śāmabhāsayan  Rm

 Rm 
 sarvapāpavinirmuktāḥ sarve 'pi sugatiṃ yayuḥ  Rm

 bṛhatphalāṃs tataś caivam avṛhān atapān gatāḥ 
 ḥsudṛśāṃś ca tato yātā tathā caivaṃ sudarśanān  Rm 
 akaniṣṭhaṃ tathā gatvā sarvān etān vyabhāsayan 
 teṣu ye saṃsthitā lokāḥ sarve tābhiś ca raśmibhiḥ  Rm

 yābhir vayaṃ parispṛṣṭā mahatsaukhyaṃ labhāmahe

 tathā tā raśmayaś caināṃ gāthābhiḥ samacodayan 
 anityaṃ khalu saṃsāraṃ duḥkhaṃ śūnyaṃ hy anātmakaṃ  Rm

 dhunīta mārasainyāṃś ca naḍāgāram iva dvipaḥ

 yo hy asmiṃ dharmavaineye 'tyapramattaś caret sudhīḥ  Rm

 yad ayaṃ sārthabhṛn nando mama dharmābhisaṃrataḥ 
 Rm 
 asya puṇyavipākena bodhicittaṃ samāpnuyāt  Rm

 ity ādiṣṭaṃ munīndreṇa śrutvānaṃdaḥ sasāṃghikaḥ 
 anumodya guruṃ natvā tatheti prābhyanaṃdata  Rm 
 evaṃ me guruṇādiṣṭaṃ dharmotsāhapravṛddhaye 
 tathā tava mayā khyātaṃ satyam etat pradhāryyatāṃ  Rm 
 evaṃ rājaṃs tvayāpy evaṃ kṛtvānumodanāṃ tathā 
 dharmaprotsāhanāṃ kṛtvā karttavyaṃ buddhadarśanaṃ  Rm 
 saddharmacaraṇotsāhe cāraṇīyāḥ prajāḥ sadā 
 ity etad guruṇādiṣṭaṃ śrutvāśokaḥ sa bhūmipaḥ  Rm 
 satyam evaṃ pratiśrutya prābhyanandat sapārṣadaḥ  Rm 
 tat kauśīdyāvadānaṃ munivarakathitaṃ śraddhayā yaḥ śṛṇoti 
 śrutvā yaḥ śrāvayed yaḥ pratidinam aniśaṃ buddhasevānuraktaḥ 
 hitvā kleśān praduṣṭān sakalakalivalān mārapakṣāṃś ca jitvā 
 pāraṃ gatvā guṇābdher vrajati sa subhagaṃ śrīghanasya caritraṃ 
  iti ratnamālāyāṃ kauśīdyavīryyotsāhanāvadānaṃ

 II Snātāvadāna
 athāśoko nṛpendro 'sau saddharmacaraṇotsavaḥ 
 upaguptaṃ guruṃ natvā kṛtāñjalipuṭo 'vadat  Rm 
 bhadanta śrotum ichāmi punar anyat subhāṣitaṃ 
 yathā te guruṇā khyātaṃ tathā me khyātum arhasi  Rm 
 iti tena nṛpeśena prārthyamāno jināṃśajaḥ 
 upaguptaḥ samāmaṃtrya taṃ kṣitīśaṃ samabravīt  Rm 
 sādhu suṣṭhu mahāraja śṛṇu dharmaṃ samāhitaḥ 
 yathā me guruṇādiṣṭaṃ tathātra te pracakṣyate  Rm 
 puraikasamaye yo 'bhūc chākyasiṃho dayākaraḥ 
 dharmarājo jagacchāstā sarvajñaḥ sugato jinaḥ  Rm 
 sarvavidyākalāvijñaḥ ṣaḍabhijño munīśvaraḥ 
 samantabhadrakṛn nātho vināyakas tathāgataḥ  Rm 
 sa śrāvastyāṃ mahodyāne jetārāme manohare 
 anāthapiṇḍadasyaiva vihāre maṇimaṇḍite  Rm 
 śrāvakair bhikṣubhiḥ sārddhaṃ bodhisatvair upāsakaiḥ 
 devāsuramahārājair manujendraṃ sapārṣadaiḥ  Rm 
 sarvalokādhipaiś cāpi traidhātukanivāsitaiḥ 
 caturvarṇaiś ca pauraiś ca tathānyaiś ca śubhārthibhiḥ  Rm

 gurukṛtaḥ puraskṛtya parivṛto 'valokitaḥ  Rm 
 ādimadhyāntakalyāṇaṃ dharmaṃ loke prakāśayan 
 sarvasatvahitārthena vijahāra samāhitaḥ  Rm 
 tasmiṃś ca samaye tatra śrāvastyāṃ ye vaṇigjanāḥ 
 te paṃcaśatamātrāṇi ratnākaraṃ samāgatāḥ  Rm

 bhānos tīkṣṇakarais taptā gharmatāpābhikheditāḥ 
 Rm

 Rm

 Rm

 yad adya jāyate 'vṛṣṭiṃ durbhikṣaṃ copavarttate  Rm 
 tad asmatpāpato nūnaṃ tat pāpaparihāṇaye 
 saṃbuddhaśaraṇaṃ kṛtvā saddharmasamavāptaye  Rm 
 sasaṃghaṃ sevituṃ nityam iche tad anumodyatāṃ 
 sa eva bhagavān nāthaḥ kṛtvātra śubhatāṃ sadā  Rm 
 suvṛṣṭiṃ cārayitvā ca subhikṣaṃ kārayed dhruvaṃ 
 tato 'smākaṃ tadāpy atra maṃgalaṃ syāt samaṃtataḥ  Rm 
 sadā saddharmam ādhāya saukhyaṃ bhuktvā bhajemahi 
 dharmeṇa śubhatā nityaṃ dharmeṇa jīyate vipat  Rm 
 dharmeṇa pālyate sarvaṃ dharmeṇa sadgatiṃ vrajet 
 dharmaṃ tu saugataṃ bhadraṃ sarve prāhur munīśvarāḥ  Rm 
 saddharmaṃ samavāptuṃ taṃ saṃbuddhaṃ bhajatādarāt 
 buddha eva jagadbaṃdhuḥ sarvasatvahitaṃkaraḥ  Rm 
 buddha eva jaganmitraṃ sarvasatvasukhapradaḥ 
 buddha eva jagattrātā sarvasatvānukaṃpakaḥ  Rm 
 buddha eva jagadbhartā dharmārthasukhasaṃpradaḥ 
 buddha eva jagacchāstā sarvasattvānubodhakaḥ 
 buddha eva jagannātho bodhisaṃbhārapūrakaḥ 
 buddha eva jagatsvāmī saṃbodhimārgadeśakaḥ 
 buddha eva mahāvīraḥ sarvamāraprabhaṃjakaḥ  Rm 
 buddha eva mahāsatvaḥ ṣaḍabhijño jagatprabhuḥ 
 buddha eva trilokeṣu dharmarūjā munīśvaraḥ 
 yenaiva trijagallokaṃ pālitaṃ putravat sadā  Rm 
 sa eva bhagavān buddhaḥ sevanīyaḥ śubhārthibhiḥ 
 yenaivaṃ triṣu lokeṣu sarvalokādhipeśvaraḥ  Rm 
 rājate jayate tena siddho 'yaṃ dharmmarāj jinaḥ 
 yathā ca triṣu lokeṣu bodhicaryāḥ prakāśayan 
 Rm 
 karoti bhadratāṃ nityaṃ tathātrāpi kariṣyati  Rm 
 saṃsthāpayati saddharme yathā traidhātuvāsinaḥ 
 satvān prabodhayann asmān niveśayet tathā khalu  Rm 
 tataḥ sarve vayaṃ dhṛtvā saddharmaṃ śubhadaṃ śivaṃ 
 yaśopuṇyasukhaṃ bhuktvā yāsyāmo 'nte sukhāvatīṃ  Rm 
 iti matvā tathāsmābhiś candano 'yaṃ jineśvaraḥ 
 mahatsatkārapūjābhiḥ sevitavyo mudā sadā  Rm 
 iti saṃbhāṣya taiḥ sarvais tathety abhyanumoditaiḥ 
 maṃtribhiḥ saha rājā sa prayayau taj jināśramaṃ  Rm 
 tatra prāptaḥ praviṣṭaś ca dṛṣṭvā taṃ caṃdanaṃ muniṃ 
 kṛtāṃjalipuṭo natvā cakāra prārthanām iti  Rm 
 namas te bhagavac chāstaḥ vayaṃ te śaraṇaṃ gatāḥ 
 tat prasanno bhavāsmākaṃ kṣantavyā cāparādhatā  Rm 
 yad avṛṣṭiḥ pravṛttātra tad asmatpāpataḥ khalu 
 tatpāpaparihāṇāya saddharmaṃ deṣṭum arhasi  Rm 
 tad bhavantaṃ vayaṃ sarve snāpayitvā sasāṃghikān 
 yathāśakty upacāraiś ca samichāmo 'rcituṃ pure  Rm 
 tat prasīda munīndro 'si yathāsmākaṃ hitaṃ bhavet 
 tathāsmatpuram āgatvā śubhaṃ kartuṃ samarhasi  Rm 
 iti tenārthitaṃ rājñā śrutvā sa caṃdano muniḥ 
 tūṣṇībhūtvā tathety evaṃ adhyuvāsa sa sāṃghikaḥ  Rm 
 tataḥ sa nṛpatir jñātvā tad adhivāsitaṃ muneḥ 
 pādau natvā punar dṛṣṭvā sahasā svaṃ puraṃ yayau  Rm 
 tataḥ pure ca mārgeṣu śodhayitvā samaṃtataḥ 
 sugaṃdhijalasaṃsiktam akārayan mahītalaṃ  Rm 
 tataḥ puṣpāvakīrṇṇaṃ ca kārayitvā samaṃtataḥ 
 dhvajacchatravitānaiś ca tatpuraṃ paryyabhūṣayat  Rm 
 tatas tan nagare madhye kārayitvā saro varaṃ 
 tad gaṃdhodakasaṃpūrṇam akārayat praśobhitaṃ  Rm 
 tatra puṣpābhiḥ saṃyuktaṃ kṛtvā tīre samaṃtataḥ 
 chatradhvajapatākāni vitatya paryyamaṇḍayat  Rm 
 Rm 
 āsanāni ca prajñapya sasaṃghasya kramān muneḥ 
 svarṇakuṃbhāṃś ca saṃsthāpya śucigaṃdhāmbupūritān  Rm 
 tato pūjopacārāṃ bhojyopakaraṇāni ca 
 sādhayitvopasaṃsthāpya saṃgītisahitāni ca  Rm 
 tato rājā sa sāmātyaiḥ paurikaiś ca samanvitaḥ 
 taṃ buddhaṃ puram ānetuṃ jināśramam agān mudā  Rm 
 tatra sa sahasā prāpto dṛṣṭvā taṃ candanaṃ muniṃ 
 kṛtāṃjalipuṭo natvā gamanaṃ prārthayad iti  Rm 
 sarvajña bhagavaṃ gantuṃ samayo varttate 'dhunā 
 sarvaṃ ca sādhitaṃ siddhaṃ tadāśv āgantum arhasi  Rm 
 evaṃ tenārthite rājñā sa saṃbuddhaḥ sasāṃghikaḥ 
 pātracīvaram ādāya prāgāt tatpurasaṃmukhaḥ  Rm 
 yadāsau bhagavān buddhāḥ prātihāryyaṃ pradarśayan 
 lokān bhāsāvasaṃbhāsya prācaran prāptagopuraṃ  Rm 
 tadākampad rasā sābdhir vavau vāyuḥ sumaṃgalaṃ 
 kṣutpipāsā hatā ye ca te sarve paritṛptitāḥ  Rm 
 ye ca hīnendriyāḥ satvās te ca pūrṇendriyā babhuḥ 
 nirdhanā dhanināś cāsan rogino nirujo 'bhavan  Rm 
 baṃdhanasthā vimuktāś ca duḥkhitāḥ sukhino 'bhavan 
 unmattāḥ susmṛtiṃ prāptā nagnā āsan suvastrikāḥ  Rm 
 gurviṇyā yāś ca tāḥ sarvāḥ pramadāḥ sukhasūtikāḥ 
 ciravairānusaṃbaddhā maitrībhūtāḥ samācaran  Rm 
 ye ca pāparatāḥ satvā daśākuśalacārikāḥ 
 te sarve parisaṃtṛptāḥ puṇyakāmāḥ pracerire  Rm 
 evam anye ca ye tatra pāpakā upasargikāḥ 
 te sarve vilayaṃ yātāḥ te sarve saṃśubhāṅkitāḥ  Rm 
 evaṃ sarvaprakāreṇa hatvā sarvam amaṅgalaṃ 
 kṛtvā bhadraṃ ca sarvatra sasaṃghaḥ sa pure 'viśat  Rm 
 kramāt pradakṣiṇenaivaṃ pracaritvā mahotsavaiḥ  Rm 
 Rm 
 vaṃdyamānas tu taiḥ sarvaiḥ sadevāsuramānavaiḥ  Rm 
 taṃ nṛpaṃ purataḥ kṛtvā rājamārgam upāsaran 
 tat sarovarasaṃprāpto dṛṣṭvā tīre samāśrayat  Rm 
 tataḥ sa bhagavān buddho yathā prajñapta āsane 
 ekacīvarakas tasthau snātuṃ tatra sarovare  Rm 
 tato nṛpādayaḥ sarve lokās taṃ caṃdanaṃ muniṃ 
 sasaṃghaṃ snāpayām āsuḥ svarṇakumbhāmbubhiḥ kramāt  Rm 
 kṛtvā snānaṃ tato 'nyatra yathāprajñapta āsane 
 sasaṃgho bhagavān tasthau svaprabhāvaṃ pradarśayan  Rm 
 atha rājā sa taṃ buddhaṃ samāsīnaṃ sasāṃghikaṃ 
 cīvaraprāvṛtaṃ kṛtvā pūjāṅgaiḥ samapūjayat  Rm 
 tataś ca bhojanaiḥ śuddhaiḥ praṇītair vyañjanair api 
 paṃcāmṛtaiś ca pānaiś ca sutṛptiṃ samatoṣayat  Rm 
 tataś ca bhojanāṃte saṃśodhayitvā mukhādikaṃ 
 nīcāsane samāsīnaḥ kṛtāṃjalipuṭo nṛpaḥ  Rm 
 suprasannamukhāmbhojaḥ sa maṃtrījanapaurikaiḥ 
 natvā kṣamāpayitvā taṃ sasaṃghaṃ prārthayat tathā  Rm 
 sarvajña bhagavan nātha kṣamasva no 'parādhatāṃ 
 prasīda sarvathā rakṣa dṛṣṭvāsmān pāpacāriṇaḥ  Rm 
 tad durbhikṣavināśāya suvṛṣṭiṃ cāraya drutaṃ 
 sarvasatvahitārthāya saddharmaṃ ca samādiśa  Rm 
 ity evaṃ prārthite tena rājñā lokahitārthinā 
 saṃbuddho bhagavāṃś caivaṃ svāśīrvacanam abravīt  Rm 
 ārogyam astu te rājan sarvatrāpi ca maṃgalaṃ 
 subhikṣaṃ sarvadāpy atra nirvighnaṃ bodhim āpnuhi  Rm 
 iti svāśīrvaco datvā saṃbuddhaḥ sa sasāṃghikaḥ 
 tataś ca svāśramaṃ prāgāt sa nṛpajanam anvitaḥ  Rm 
 evam asya munīndrasya traimāsyaṃ ca niraṃtaraṃ 
 tenākāri nṛpendreṇa sevā satkārapūjanaiḥ  Rm 
 tataḥ śakro mahendro 'sau dṛṣṭvā tat sugatārcitāṃ 
 tad durbhikṣapraśāṃtyarthaṃ suvṛṣṭiṃ samacārayat  Rm 
 Rm 
 tato jalāśrayāny ambupūritāni samaṃtataḥ 
 padmotpalādipuṣpaiś ca channāni rurucus tadā  Rm 
 tṛṇair navāṅkurodbhūtaṃ sādvalaiś ca prarūḍhitaiḥ 
 pratichannā haridvastraiḥ prāvṛtaiva rarāja bhūḥ  Rm 
 vṛkṣāś cāpi haritpatraiḥ samāchannāḥ praśobhitāḥ 
 puṣpaiḥ prasphullitair amyaiḥ phalaiś ca saṃcakāsire  Rm 
 kramāc caivaṃ prarūḍhāni śasyāni varddhitāni ca 
 pariniṣpannasiddhāni pravipecuḥ samaṃtataḥ 
 tataḥ sarve janāś caivaṃ saṃprayātāṃ subhikṣatāṃ 
 dṛṣṭvānaṃdaṃ samuccāryya pracerire praharṣitāḥ  Rm 
 atha rājā sa tān sarvān mahāharṣapramoditān 
 dṛṣṭvā bhūyaḥ samāmaṃtrya vabhāṣa saṃprabodhayan  Rm 
 bhavanto dṛśyatām asya saṃbuddhasyānubhāvatā 
 yasya puṇyānubhāvena prajātaiva subhikṣatā  Rm 
 tasmān nityaṃ tathaivāsya saṃbuddhasya jagatprabhoḥ 
 mahatsatkārapūjābhiḥ karttavyaṃ bhajanaṃ sadā  Rm 
 evaṃ yadi sadā cāsya saṃbuddhasya jagatprabhoḥ 
 pūjābhiḥ satkariṣyanti sadātra maṃgalaṃ bhavet  Rm 
 tasmād asya munīndrasya nakhakeśavidarbhitaḥ 
 gandhastūpaḥ pratisthāpya sevitavyaḥ sadārcanaiḥ  Rm 
 iti saṃbhāṣya rājāsau tais tathety anumoditaiḥ 
 saha bauddhāśramaṃ gatvā natvā taṃ prārthayan muniṃ  Rm 
 namas te bhagavaṃ chāstar vayaṃ te śaraṇasthitāḥ 
 sadā caivaṃ kariṣyāmo bhavatsevām upāsthitāḥ  Rm 
 tat prasīda sadā pātra vihṛtya dharmam ādiśan 
 vijayasva na cānyatra mā vraja no 'nukaṃpayā  Rm 
 tenaivaṃ prārthite rājñā bhagavāṃś ca sa caṃdanaḥ 
 Rm 
 taṃ nṛpaṃ sajanaṃ dṛṣṭvā prasannāsyo 'bravīt tathā  Rm 
 naiva rājan mayā bodhir ekasyārthe prasādhitā 
 api ca sarvasatvānāṃ hitārthe hy anukaṃpinā  Rm 
 tasmād atra sadā naiva sthāsyāmy ahaṃ sasāṃghikaḥ 
 sarvatrāpi careyāhaṃ saddharmaṃ saṃprakāśituṃ  Rm 
 yadi me śraddhayā nityaṃ sevāṃ kartuṃ samichatha 
 keśastūpaṃ pratisthāpya sevyata sarvadārcanaiḥ  Rm 
 tatas te 'tra sadā rājye subhikṣaṃ maṃgalaṃ bhavet 
 durbhikṣatā ca kutrāpi nākramiṣyati kadā cana  Rm 
 iti matvā tvayā gatvā triratnaśaraṇaṃ svayaṃ 
 sarvasatvāś ca saddharme preraṇīyāḥ prayatnataḥ  Rm 
 ity ādiśya munīṃdro 'sau chitvā svān nakharāṃs tathā 
 keśāṃś cāpy avatāryyaivaṃ tasmai rājñe svayaṃ dadau  Rm 
 tato rājā sa taṃ buddhaṃ natvā keśāṃ nakhāṃś ca tān 
 samādāya praharṣeṇa pratyāyayau svam ālayaṃ  Rm 
 tatra prāptaḥ pure madhye puṣkariṇyās taṭāntike 
 tat keśanakharān ropya gaṃdhastūpam akārayat  Rm 
 tasmiṃ siddhe pratisthāpya vidhinā ca mahotsavaiḥ 
 nityaṃ satkārapūjābhiḥ sevāṃ cakre prasannadhīḥ  Rm 
 etat puṇyānubhāvena loke 'ṃdhe 'pariṇāyake 
 jagalloke hitaṃ kartuṃ bhaveyaṃ sugatas tathā  Rm 
 iti dhṛtvā pracitte 'sau praṇidhānaṃ narādhipaḥ 
 gaṃdhajalaiś ca taṃ stūpaṃ snāpayitvā sadārcayat  Rm 
 pratisthāpya mahaṃ cāpi gatvā ca śaraṇe mudā 
 aṣṭāṃgaiś ca praṇatvaivaṃ mahotsāhair asevayat  Rm 
 tathā sarve janāś cāpi śraddhayā taṃ prabhejire 
 ye gatāḥ śaraṇaṃ tatra te sarve nirvṛtiṃ yayuḥ  Rm 
 aham evāvasiṣṭaḥ sa teṣāṃ yo 'bhūn narādhipaḥ 
 saṃbodhipraṇidhiṃ dhṛtvā naivaṃ nirvāṇam āyayau  Rm 
 Rm 
 etat puṇyānubhāvaiś ca suvṛṣṭiḥ saṃpracāritā 
 sarvadāpy abhavat tatra subhikṣaṃ nirupadravaṃ  Rm 
 etad dharmānubhāvaiś ca sarvatra sāṃprataṃ labhe 
 pūjāsatkāramānyāni yaśodharmasukhāni ca  Rm 
 yatra yatra pragachāmi tatra tatra samaṃtataḥ 
 itthaṃ satkārapūjābhir mānito 'haṃ sasāṃghikaḥ  Rm 
 tac chāstāraṃ samārādhya yaśodharmasukhepsubhiḥ 
 śubheṣu sarvadā nityaṃ caritavyaṃ prayatnataḥ  Rm 
 śubhena sukhatā nityaṃ bhavel loke samaṃtataḥ 
 pāpena duḥkhatā caivaṃ miśritenāpi miśritā  Rm 
 tasmāt pāpaṃ viramyaivaṃ miśritāni vihāya ca 
 śubheṣv eva prayatnena caritavyaṃ sukhārthibhiḥ  Rm 
 ity ādiṣṭaṃ munīndreṇa sarve te sāṃghikās tathā 
 śrutvā pramenire satyaṃ karmabhāvaṃ bhavālaye  Rm 
 pāpebhyo viratā nityaṃ miśritebhyo 'pi te sadā 
 sadā śubheṣu niratāḥ sarve saṃcerire samāhitāḥ  Rm 
 evaṃ rājaṃs tvayā nityaṃ pāpāc ca miśritād api 
 viramya sarvathā dharme caritavyaṃ sukhāptaye  Rm 
 prajāś cāpi vinirvāryya sarvathā pāpacāraṇāt 
 śrāvayitvā ca saddharmaṃ yojanīyāḥ śubhe sadā  Rm 
 tathā te sarvadā nityaṃ sarvatra viṣayeṣv api 
 suvṛṣṭiḥ pracarec caivaṃ maṃgalaṃ nirupadravaṃ  Rm 
 iti tena samādiṣṭaṃ upaguptena śāsinā 
 śrutvāśoko nṛpo 'stv evam ity anandat sapārṣadaḥ  Rm 
 snātāvadānaṃ tad idaṃ niśamya ye śrāvayanti pratibodhya lokān 
 te pāpanirmuktaviśuddhadehāḥ prayānti nūnaṃ sugatālayeṣu  Rm 
  iti ratnāvadānamālāyāṃ snātāvadānaṃ samāptam 
 Rm 
 III Cakrāvadāna
 athāśoko narendro 'sau bhūyo natvā kṛtāṃjaliḥ 
 upaguptaṃ guruṃ prāha śrotum anyat subhāṣitaṃ  Rm 
 bhadanta śrotum ichāmi bhūyo 'py anyat subhāṣitaṃ 
 yathā te guruṇā khyātaṃ tathā me vaktum arhasi  Rm 
 iti tenārthite rājñā bhūyo 'py asau jināṃśajaḥ 
 upagupto yatir bhikṣus taṃ nṛpam evaṃ abravīt  Rm 
 yathā me guruṇādiṣṭaṃ vakṣye 'haṃ te subhāṣitaṃ 
 sādhu cittaṃ samādhāya śṛṇu rājan samāhitaḥ  Rm 
 yaḥ purāsīn mahābuddhaḥ sarvajñaḥ śrīghano jinaḥ 
 sarvavidyākalābhijño dharmarājas tathāgataḥ  Rm 
 śāstārhan sugato nāthas traidhātukavināyakaḥ 
 sa śākyādhipatir loke hitāya ca samaṃtataḥ  Rm 
 saddharmadeśanāṃ kṛtvā bodhimārgaṃ prakāśayan 
 bhikṣuśrāvakasaṃghaiś ca bodhisatvaiś ca sāṃghikaiḥ  Rm 
 upāsikāgaṇaiś caivam upāsakagaṇaṃ saha 
 rājagṛham upāśritya veṇuvane jināśrame  Rm 
 kalaṃdake nivāpākhye mahodyāne samāśritaḥ 
 ādimadhyāṃtakatyāṇaṃ dideśa dharmam uttamaṃ  Rm 
 tad dharmadeśanāṃ śrotuṃ devāsuramanuṣyakāḥ 
 yakṣakinnaragaṃdharvāḥ siddhavidyādharādayaḥ  Rm 
 garuḍā nāgarājāś ca mahāharṣasamanvitāḥ 
 brāhmaṇā kṣatriyāś caiva rājāno rājaputrakāḥ  Rm 
 vaiśyāś ca śreṣṭhinaḥ śūdrā maṃtriṇo mātṛkājanāḥ 
 sārthavāhāś ca paurāś ca dhaninaś ca vaṇigjanāḥ  Rm 
 evam anye 'pi lokāś ca sarve te saṃpraharṣitāḥ 
 mahatsatkārapūjābhiḥ sarvopakaraṇais tathā  Rm 
 Rm 
 pūjayitvā pravaṃditvā saṃbuddhaṃ sugataṃ muniṃ 
 parivṛtya puraskṛtya tasthau sarvānya tasthire  Rm 
 saddharmavāṃchitāḥ sarve śrotuṃ tatra samāgatāḥ  Rm 
 tasmiṃś ca samaye pūryyāṃ śrāvastyāṃ subhago vaṇik 
 anyattamaḥ sārthavāha āsīn mahādhanaḥ sudhīḥ  Rm 
 tena bhāryyā subhadrāṃgī jātidharmasamānikā 
 pariṇītā kulasthityai kuladharmānusārataḥ  Rm 
 tatas tau daṃpatī raktau snehānubandhitau mudā 
 yathākāmaṃ prabhuṃjānau sanramāte yathechayā  Rm 
 tatas tasya gṛhasthasya bhogyeṣv evābhirāgiṇaḥ 
 svakulavṛttidharmeṣu pramādād anapekṣiṇaḥ  Rm 
 vyavahāre viraktasya prodyamarahitasya ca 
 arjanopāyamaṃdasya kevalaṃ vyayakurvataḥ  Rm 
 dine dine kraṃān nityaṃ ativyayān nirāgamat 
 saṃpadaḥ kṣīṇatāṃ yātā griṣmakāla iva hradāḥ  Rm 
 tatas tasya gṛhasthasya bhāryā yā kuladharmikā 
 saṃpadaḥ kṣīnatāṃ dṛṣṭvā gṛhe caivaṃ vyacintayat  Rm 
 ayaṃ me puruṣo bharttā sārthavāho vaṇik dhanī 
 bhāgyam eva gṛhe bhuktvā nivasati nirudyamaḥ  Rm 
 atyarthavyayatā yatra vidyate na tathāgamaḥ 
 sā ca saṃpat kiyat kālaṃ tiṣṭhet kṣīṇaṃ vrajet kramāt  Rm 
 tad ayaṃ puruṣaś cāpi kathaṃ sustho bhaviṣyati 
 kena saṃdhāryyate lokair vihīne bhogyasaṃcaye  Rm 
 vṛddho 'py ayaṃ bhaven nūnaṃ daridro 'pi bhavet tathā 
 tadā kiṃ paribhuktvaivaṃ gṛhe tisthet kathaṃ sukhī  Rm 
 yasya saṃpad gṛhe nāsti kathaṃ sa puruṣaḥ sukhī 
 Rm 
 svayaṃ bhoktuṃ na śaktaḥ syāt kiṃ punar dānam ācaret  Rm 
 dānaṃ vinā na saṃsāre kiṃ sārasukham āpsyate 
 dānenaiva hi labhyante yaśodharmasukhāni ca  Rm 
 dānena śuddhyate cittaṃ śuddhacitto bhavet sudhiḥ 
 sudhiyā sādhyate śīlaṃ śīlavān syāc chubhaṃkarī  Rm 
 śubhakarmā ca saddharmaṃ kṛtvā yāsyati sadgatiṃ 
 tasmād aham imaṃ nāthaṃ bharttāraṃ puruṣaṃ prabhuṃ  Rm 
 saddharmasukhasaṃprāptyai prerayeyaṃ dhanārjane 
 dhanavān puruṣo loke sarvārthasādhane kṛtī  Rm 
 dharmārthakāmamokṣāṇāṃ mūlaṃ prāhur dhanaṃ budhāḥ 
 bhartur hi puruṣasyāpi trivargakāryyasādhane  Rm 
 sahāyaḥ kathyate prājñaiḥ satī bhāryyānucāriṇī 
 asya bhartur hy ahaṃ bharyyā satī dharmārthasādhane  Rm 
 manaḥ protsāhitaṃ kṛtvā prerayeyaṃ dhanārjane  Rm 
 iti niścitya sā sādhvī dṛṣṭvā bharttāram ādarāt 
 dharmārthasādhane caivaṃ protsāhayitum abravīt  Rm 
 svāmi bharttāsi me nātho devatāpi tvam eva hi 
 tan mayā vakṣyate tathyaṃ paratreha sukhāya te  Rm 
 tathyaṃ ca tacchṛṇuṣvaivam anyathā cet tu mā kuru  Rm 
 yad bhavān purusaḥ prāḍhyaḥ sārthavāho vaṇik prabhuḥ 
 sadā bhogyāni bhuktvaiva sthitvā naivaṃ praśobhati  Rm 
 tat pramādaṃ parityaktvā yaśodharmasukhāptaye 
 satyadharmānusāreṇa kuruṣva dhanasādhanaṃ  Rm 
 dhanena sādhayed bhogyaṃ bhogyena pālayet tanuṃ 
 dehena sādhayed dharmaṃ dharmeṇa satsukhaṃ labhet  Rm 
 kiṃ ca yatra gṛhe svāmī vyavahāranirudyamaḥ 
 tatra sarve janāś cāpi niṣatsyaṃty avasādinaḥ  Rm 
 api yatra gṛhe svāmī vyavahārasamudyataḥ 
 tatra sarve janāś caiva pracareyuḥ samudyamāḥ  Rm 
 yac ca dānamahotsāhaṃ yatra gehe na vidyate 
 sa kiṃ geho na ramyaḥ syāc chūnyāraṇye śmaśānavat  Rm 
 Rm 
 yasmin gṛhe sadā nityaṃ dānapuṇyamahotsavaṃ 
 sa eva mandiro ramyasvargavat pratibhāsyate  Rm 
 yasmiṃś cāpi gṛhastho hi dānapuṇyanirutsahaḥ 
 svayam eva prabhuktvaivaṃ vasate paśuvat sa kiṃ  Rm 
 dhanyās te puruṣā vīrā yaśodharmasukhānvitāḥ 
 kṛtvā dānavṛṣotsāhaṃ sukhaṃ bhuktvā vasaṃti ye  Rm 
 teṣām eva hi saṃsāre susāraṃ jīvitaṃ khalu 
 ye kṛtvā dānapuṇyāni svayaṃ saukhyaṃ ca bhuṃjate  Rm 
 dānenaiva hi lobhyaṃte yaśodharmasukhāni ca 
 anyathā naiva lapsyante tataḥ saṃpan nirarthitā  Rm 
 kiyat kālaṃ ca jīveyur ye bhuktvaiva sukhaṃ sthitāḥ 
 avaśyaṃ sarvaśo hitvā mṛtā yāyur yamālayaṃ  Rm 
 tatra karmasahāyāṃs tān dṛṣṭvā dharmādhipo yamaḥ 
 nirṇayitvā ca tat karma prerayet karmabhuktaye  Rm 
 ye ca pāpakarā duṣṭā prerayet tān tu durgatau 
 ye tu puṇyakarā bhadrāḥ prerayet tāṃś ca sadgatau  Rm 
 tatra karmaphalāny evaṃ duḥkhāni ca 
 sukhāni ca sarvatheha paratrāpi bhuṃjate sarvajāṃtavaḥ  Rm 
 śubhena sadgatiṃ yayād yaśodharmasukhānvitāḥ 
 pāpena durgatiṃ yāyād dhikpravādāsukhānvitāḥ  Rm 
 evaṃ matvā prabho svāmin yaśodharmasukhāptaye 
 svakulavṛttim ādhāya prodyamasva dhanārjane  Rm 
 sadā dānamahotsāhaṃ kṛtvā sadgatilabdhaye 
 yathechayā sukhaṃ bhuktvā pālayasva sadā janān  Rm 
 tatas te maṃgalaṃ nityaṃ bhaved iha paratra ca 
 saphalaṃ mānuṣaṃ janma nūnaṃ sadgatim āpnuyāt  Rm 
 iti bhāryāvacaḥ śrutvā sa gṛhastho vaṇik sudhīḥ 
 bhāryāṃ tāṃ vallabhāṃ kāntāṃ dṛṣṭvā caivaṃ samabravīt  Rm 
 ayi priye subhadrāsi mama bhāryānucāriṇī 
 yat tvayā bhāṣitaṃ satyaṃ tat kariṣyāmi sarvathā  Rm 
 kiṃ tu tvaṃ me priyā bhāryā vallabhātimanoharā 
 tat kathaṃ tvāṃ priyāṃ tyaktvā kutra yāsye dhanārthataḥ  Rm 
 Rm 
 sārthavāho hy ahaṃ cāpi tat kathaṃ nīcavṛttibhiḥ 
 ratnārjanaṃ kariṣyāmi tato ratnākaraṃ vraje  Rm 
 tasmāt priye subhadrāṃgī sati dharmānucāriṇī 
 gṛhakāryyaṃ samādhāryya vasa bhuktvā yathāsukhaṃ  Rm 
 yāvan nāhaṃ gṛhe prāptas tāvad dhairyyaṃ samāśraya 
 śīghram evāgamiṣyāmi maṃ smṛtvā mānvatapyathāḥ  Rm 
 iti bharttoditaṃ śrutvā sā ca bhāryānutāpitā 
 galadaśrumukhī natvā svāminaṃ tam abhāṣata  Rm 
 he nātha supriya svāmin māṃ vihāya kathaṃ vrajeḥ 
 tvayā vinā kathaṃ gehe tiṣṭheyāhaṃ yathā vane  Rm 
 darśane śravaṇe vāpi gaṃdhatailānulepane 
 sparśane bhojane pāne suvastraparibhūṣaṇe  Rm 
 saurabhyā 'ṅgane cāpi bhāṣane gamane kvacit 
 nidrābhoge tathā naiva vidyeta me 'bhilāṣatā  Rm 
 tavaiva smaraṇaṃ kṛtvā niḥśvasantī muhur muhuḥ 
 virahānalasaṃtaptā vrajeyaṃ maraṇaṃ dhruvaṃ  Rm 
 mṛtāyāṃ mayi te gehe ko 'nurakṣen nu saṃpadaḥ 
 śrutvā me maraṇaṃ nūnaṃ dhakṣyase virahānalaiḥ  Rm 
 tadaitābhiś ca saṃpattiratnaiś ca kiṃ kariṣyasi 
 aputrasya hi sarvasvaṃ nūnaṃ rājā grahīṣyati  Rm 
 tadātmanā vikhidyaivaṃ dūraṃ mā gā vihāyatāṃ 
 gṛhe sthitvā mayā sārddhāṃ sukhaṃ bhuktvodyamaṃ kuru  Rm 
 atrāpi bahavaḥ santi vaṇiksaṃghā mahājanāḥ 
 paṇyaṃ prasāryya taṃ sārddhaṃ sādhayasva dhanaṃ sukhaṃ  Rm 
 kiyat kālaṃ ca jīveva santatiś ca na vidyate 
 tat kiṃ nau bahubhī ratnair mā gā ratnākaraṃ hy ataḥ  Rm 
 yāvajjīvaṃ sukhaṃ bhuktvā dānaṃ kṛtvā sadārthine 
 saṃvṛtyā prārjaya dravyaṃ svagehe saṃsthito rama  Rm 
 mā dhāva priya kutrāpi kiṃ vā ratnākare labhet 
 svagṛhe 'pi labhej jantuḥ svakarmanirmitaṃ dhanaṃ  Rm 
 svakṛtaṃ karma tad bhāvi nirmāṇasadṛśaṃ phalaṃ 
 Rm 
 sarvatrāpi labhanty eva mahāntaḥ kṣudrikā api  Rm 
 tathā ye sujanā loke sadhanā sadguṇāśrayāḥ 
 te 'pi kṣaṇād bhavanty eva nirdhanā bhikṣutāśritāḥ  Rm 
 ye cāpi durjanā loke nirdhanā nirguṇāś ca ye 
 te 'pi labhanti mānyārhaṃ sevyante cāpi sajjanaiḥ  Rm 
 tathā ye vaṇijo dhīrāḥ sārthavāhā maṇīchayā 
 ratnākaraṃ gatās teṣāṃ ke cit svastisamāgatāḥ  Rm 
 ke cit tatra samudre vā bhagnanaukā dhanaiḥ saha 
 patitāḥ sannimajjantā mṛtāś ca vilayaṃ gatāḥ  Rm 
 ke cid vīryabalenaivaiḥ samuttīrya prayatnataḥ 
 akiṃcanyāḥ paribhraṣṭā riktahastā gṛhāgatāḥ 
 evaṃ sarve 'pi satvāś ca svakṛtakarmanirmitaṃ 
 phalaṃ bhuktvā bhramanty evaṃ saṃsāre ṣaḍgatiṣv api  Rm 
 iti karmapramāṇatvaṃ jñātvā saṃpadvipattitā 
 mā khedaya svam ātmānaṃ dharmaṃ kṛtvā sukhaṃ vasa  Rm 
 tathā nau maṃgalaṃ nityaṃ sarvatrāpi bhavet khalu 
 yāvajjīvaṃ sukhaṃ bhuktvā sadgatiṃ ca vrajemahi  Rm 
 iti bhāryoditaṃ śrutvā sārthavāhātmajaḥ sa ca 
 taṃ priyāṃ ramaṇīṃ bhāryyāṃ dṛṣṭvaivaṃ samabhāṣata  Rm 
 bhadre satyaṃ tvaṃ yā proktaṃ yat svakarmapramānatā 
 iti matvāham ichāmi gantuṃ ratnākare 'pi hi  Rm 
 yad abhāvi na tad bhāvi bhāvi cen na tad anyathā 
 sarvatrāpi bhaven nūnaṃ tenābdhiṃ gantum īhyate  Rm 
 yadi bhāgyaṃ mamāsty evaṃ svasti syād gamane khalu 
 ratnāni bahuśo labdhā pratyāgacheya siddhitāḥ  Rm 
 atha me bhāgyatā naiva nūnaṃ tatra vipattitā 
 mahattīrthe nimagno 'haṃ mṛto yāsye surālayaṃ  Rm 
 yathā bhaṭṭā mahāvīrā yaśodharmasukhāptaye 
 śatruṃ jetuṃ mahotsāhair viśanti raṇamaṇḍale  Rm 
 tatra ke cid dhatā vīrā yaśodharmānvitā mṛtāḥ 
 sahasā te prayānty evaṃ svargasaukhyānubhoginaḥ  Rm 
 aham api vaṇikputraḥ sārthavāhātmajo hy ahaṃ 
 Rm 
 tat tathāhaṃ gaṃiṣyāmi ratnākaraṃ na cānyataḥ  Rm 
 yadi svasti gṛhaṃ prāpsye yaśoratnasukhānvitaḥ 
 mṛto 'tha nirmalībhūtvā svarge saukhyam avāpnuyāṃ  Rm 
 iti matvā priye bhadre mā viṣīda sukhāṃ vasa 
 yāvan nāhaṃ gṛhaṃ prāptas tāvad bhajeṣṭadevatāṃ  Rm 
 sarvathāhaṃ gamiṣyāmi svakulakīrtilabdhaye 
 anivarttī hy ahaṃ kāryye tan māṃ tvaṃ mā nivāraya  Rm 
 iti bharttur vacaḥ śrutvā nirbandhaṃ gamanaṃ prati 
 sā satī taṃ svabharttāraṃ natvā prāha kṛtāṃjaliḥ  Rm 
 svāmiṃs tvaṃ sarvathā gantuṃ yadīchasi mahāmbudhiṃ 
 dhairyyam ālamvya saṃpaśyan mārge vraja samāhitaḥ  Rm 
 svasti te vrajato mārge sarvatrāpi divāniśaṃ 
 svasti pratyāgate caivaṃ bhūyān nityaṃ śubhaṃ sadā  Rm 
 yātrāsiddhimahāsaṃpadyaśodharmasukhānvitaḥ 
 svasti śīghraṃ samāgacha vrajā te 'stu sadā śivaṃ  Rm 
 iti bhāryoditaṃ śrutvā sārthavāhas tatheti saḥ 
 pratijñāya vaṃksaṃghān sarvān āhūya cābravīt  Rm 
 bhavanto 'haṃ samichāmi yośodharmasukhāptaye 
 svakulavṛttim ādhāya gantuṃ ratnākarāṃbudhau  Rm 
 tatra gantuṃ mayā sārddhaṃ yadi yūyaṃ samichatha 
 tat paṇyaṃ sahasādāya samāyāta caremahi  Rm 
 iti tenoditaṃ śrutvā sarve te vaṇijo mudā 
 sahasā paṇyam ādāya tatra gantum upākraman  Rm 
 atha sārthapatiḥ śīghraṃ taiś ca paṃcaśataiḥ saha 
 svastyayanavidhiṃ kṛtvā pratasthe saṃpramoditaḥ  Rm 
 tataḥ kramād atikramya grāmajanapadāni te 
 vilaṃghyāraṇyadeśāṃś ca tīraṃ prāpur mahodadheḥ  Rm 
 tato nāvaṃ samāruhya tāni paṃcaśatāni ca 
 pravitatya dhvajaṃ śubhraṃ jagāhire 'mbudhau kramāt  Rm 
 tathā te vahanārūḍhā vātānukūlato dhruvaṃ 
 kramād dvīpāṃś ca laṃghitvā ratnākaraṃ samāyayuḥ  Rm 
 tatra ratnākaraṃ prāptā devatā supramodataḥ 
 te mithaḥ kalahaṃ kṛtvā pratyāgaṃtuṃ na śekire  Rm 
 Rm 
 ciram evaṃ virodhitvād ratnāni ca na lebhire 
 bāṃdhavāṃś ca muhuḥ smṛtvā tasthuḥ sarve vilaṃvitāḥ  Rm 
 atrāṃtare ca sā nārī sārthavāhapriyā satī 
 bharttrā vinā gṛhaṃ śūnyam amanyata nirutsavāt  Rm 
 yad dine prasthito bhartā sārthavāhaḥ purād vahiḥ 
 tad dinārabhya sā nārī gaṇayantī dinaṃ prati  Rm 
 bharttur eva muhuḥ smṛtvā virahavedanāturā 
 niḥśvasantī muhuś caivam adhairyyā paritāpinī  Rm 
 kṛśāṅgā pāṇḍuvarṇā ca virukṣākīrṇakeśinī 
 prasādhanānabhīchantī malinavasanāvṛtā  Rm 
 darśanaśravaṇe cāpi gaṃdhānvāharaṇe 'pi ca 
 bhojaneṣv api pāne ca sparśane gamaneṣv api  Rm 
 kutūhare tathānyatra manorame 'pi cādbhute 
 sarvatra viṣayeṣv evaṃ na protsahe yathāturā  Rm 
 bharttur viyogaduḥkhārttā roginīva viṣādinī 
 asahyamadanākrāntā dhairyyopāyavicetanā  Rm 
 bhartur āgatim ālambya kṣaṇaṃ dhairyyasamāśritā 
 bhartāram eva saṃsmṛtvā gṛha eva nyaṣīdata  Rm 
 na nidrāṃ śayane bheje nānyasmṛtau mano 'nudat 
 prabhum evaṃ samādhyātvā tasthau dhyāyīva yogavit  Rm 
 athaivaṃ vikalībhūtāṃ yauvanīṃ tāṃ pativratāṃ 
 kācid ekā sakhī bhadrā saṃnirīkṣyābravīd rahaḥ  Rm 
 bhadre kin te viṣāda tvaṃ vibhāsi tvaiḥ yathāturā 
 mā viṣīda yad arthan te tad vadasva mayi priye  Rm 
 kathaṃ notsahase bhadre svakuladharmacāriṇi 
 kautuke cādbhute cāpi sarvatra viṣayeṣv api  Rm 
 bhojane bhūṣaṇe cāpi draṣṭuṃ śrotuṃ na vāṃchasi 
 kiṃ viṣādena siddhaṃ te tat prabhukṣva yathāsukhaṃ  Rm 
 Rm 
 iti tayodite sakhyā sārthavāhapriyāpi sa 
 tāṃ sakhīṃ pramadāṃ kāntāṃ dṛṣṭvā caivam abhāṣata  Rm 
 nāhaṃ bhogārthinī bhadre nāpi kāmātirāgiṇī 
 kiṃ tu dharmānuraktāsmi tat kathaṃ svāminaṃ vinā  Rm 
 tenāhaṃ viṣayāṃ tyaktvā smṛtvā bharttāram eva taṃ 
 svāgāra eva tiṣṭhāmi bhogyeṣv api ca nispṛhā  Rm 
 kadā sa me priyo bharttā gṛhe pratyāsariṣyati 
 iti ciṃtāṃ samādhāya tiṣṭhāmi yoginī yathā  Rm 
 yāvac ca sa priyaḥ svāmī nāyāti svagṛhaṃ prati 
 tāvad evaṃ na bhokṣye 'haṃ bhogyāni surasāny api  Rm 
 viṣayeṣv api sarveṣu na me vāṃchā priyaṃ vinā 
 nānyacciṃtā ca me citte tasmād evaṃ sthitā sadā  Rm 
 yāvat svāmī na me dṛṣṭas tāvat sthāsyāmy ahaṃ tathā 
 api me jivitaṃ yātu na ca yāyāṃ gṛhād bahiḥ  Rm 
 strīṇāṃ hi devatā svāmī dharmo 'pi bhartṛsevayā 
 tasmāt smṛtvaiva bharttāraṃ bhājāmy ahaṃ pativratā  Rm 
 kutra dharmaṃ cariṣyāmi yasyā nāsti gṛhe pumān 
 tat manasaiva bharttāraṃ dhyātvā bhaje divāniśaṃ  Rm 
 dhig me janma nirarthaṃ syād yasyā na yauvane patiḥ 
 vṛddhatve kiṃ kariṣyāmi svāminā ca dhanair api  Rm 
 varam evādya me mṛtyur na mithyā cirajīvitaṃ 
 yasmāc ciram api sthitvā mṛtyuduḥkhaṃ tad eva hi  Rm 
 yam evālaṃvya jīvāmi sa yadi nāgamiṣyati 
 kim eva jīvitenāpi kevaladuḥkhabhāvinā  Rm 
 dhanyās tā hi striyo bhadrāḥ svasvāmisahacārikāḥ 
 kṛtvā dharmaṃ sadā gehe saukhyaṃ bhuktvā vasanti yāḥ  Rm 
 mā bhūt tu mādṛśi kācid abhadrā duḥkhabhāginī 
 samyagbhogyaiś ca kiṃ tasyā yasyā bharttā na yauvane  Rm 
 tathāpi kiṃ kariṣyāmi nāryy ahaṃ hi pativratā 
 tasmāt tam eva bharttāraṃ smṛtvā sthāsyāmi sarvadā  Rm 
 Rm 
 iti tayoditaṃ śrutvā sā sakhī hitakāriṇī 
 tadupāyahitaṃ kartuṃ tāṃ sakhīṃ ca samabravīt  Rm 
 bhadre satyaṃ tvayā proktaṃ strīṇāṃ hi devatā patiḥ 
 tathāpi vakṣyate bhadre tava prītyā ca tac chṛṇu  Rm 
 yāvan nivasate gehe bhartā kāmarasārataḥ 
 tāvat strī sevayen nityaṃ dharmaṃ bhartur anujñayā  Rm 
 yadā bharttā gṛhe na syād dūradeśaṃ gatas tathā 
 yāvad gṛhaṃ na cāyātas tāvad devaṃ bhajet patiḥ  Rm 
 pates te devatāsmākaṃ viṣṇur nārāyaṇo hariḥ 
 tasmād enaṃ prabhor nāmnā smṛtvā nityaṃ bhajārcaya  Rm 
 sa eva kāmado devaḥ kāmadhātvīśvarādhipaḥ 
 saṃsārasthitidharmastho ratibhogyasukhapradaḥ  Rm 
 tasyaiva hy anubhāvena preryyamāno mano bhuvāḥ 
 bharttā te sahasā prāyāt svasti ratnaiś ca saṃyutaḥ  Rm 
 tatas te saphalaṃ janma saṃsāre prabhunā saha 
 dānaṃ kṛtvā sukhaṃ bhuktvā yāvajjīvaṃ sukhaṃ vasa  Rm 
 evaṃ sakhyoditaṃ Śrutvā ramaṇī sā pativratā 
 tatheti pratisaṃśrutya punas tām avadat sakhīṃ  Rm 
 satyaṃ bhadre yathā proktaṃ tvayā me hitakāraṇaṃ 
 tathāhaṃ saṃbhajiṣyāmi smṛtvā nāmnā prabhor hariṃ  Rm 
 yathā svasti samāyātaḥ svāmī ratnasamṛddhibhṛt 
 tadā hy ekaṃ suvarṇasya cakraṃ dāsyāmi viṣṇave  Rm 
 ity evaṃ sā pratijñāya viṣṇum evaṃ samasmarat  Rm 
 namas te bhagavan viṣṇo hare nārāyaṇa prabho 
 prasīda paśya māṃ nārīṃ prabhuṃ ca prāpayāśu me  Rm 
 yadā me puruṣo bharttā svasti gehasamāgataḥ 
 tadopaḍhaukayiṣyāmi svarṇacakraṃ hare tava  Rm 
 iti sakhyāḥ puraḥ proktvā smṛtvā nityaṃ hariṃ mudā 
 svarṇacakraṃ ca saṃkalpya tasthau bhartuḥ smaranti sa  Rm 
 tadaiva sārthavāho 'sau sarvasārthagaṇaiḥ saha 
 bahuratnāni saṃgṛhya pratasthe sahasā tataḥ  Rm 
 tataḥ svasti samuttīryya mahodadhes tadāgataḥ 
 sarvasārthagaṇaiḥ sārddhaṃ sahasā gṛham āyayau  Rm 
 Rm 
 tatas taṃ gṛhasaṃprāptaṃ dṛṣṭvā sā naṃditā satī 
 pādau natvā puraḥ sthitvā svaṃ pravṛttam abhāṣata  Rm 
 svāmin yadā bhavān gehāt prasthito māṃ vihāya ca 
 tadārabhya sadā smṛtvā tvām evāsmi sthitā gṛhe  Rm 
 tadāham anayā sakhyā dṛṣṭvā tvadvirahāturā 
 tad duḥkhaṃ me vinodārthaṃ preritā smaraṇe hareḥ  Rm 
 tadārabhya sadā nityaṃ smṛtvā taveṣṭadevatāṃ 
 bhajāmi satataṃ bhaktyā tavāśu gamanārthinī  Rm 
 cakraṃ ekaṃ suvarṇasya saṃkalpya śraddhayā mayā 
 prārthanāpi kṛtā nityaṃ tava yātrāprasiddhaye  Rm 
 yathā me prārthitaṃ sarvaṃ tathā siddhaṃ hi sāṃprataṃ 
 tan me saṃkalpitaṃ deva pūrayeyaṃ tathā prabho  Rm 
 tat pūjāṃgaṃ samādāya śakraṃ samupaḍhokituṃ 
 devakulaṃ gamiṣyāmi tad anujñāṃ pradehi me  Rm 
 iti bhāryoditaṃ śrutvā sārthavāho 'numoditaḥ 
 pūraya tvaṃ priye satyaṃ gacchety evam abhāṣata  Rm 
 tataḥ sānujñayā bhartuḥ satī sārddhaṃ sakhījanaiḥ 
 pūjāṃgāni ca taṃ cakraṃ dhṛtvā devakulaṃ yayau  Rm 
 tasmiṃ kṣaṇe sa saṃbuddho bhagavān karuṇāmayaḥ 
 loke satvān samuddhartum apaśyad buddhacakṣuṣā  Rm 
 tām evaṃ prasthitāṃ dṛṣṭvā bhadrāṃ saddharmacāriṇīṃ 
 praikṣac ca bhagavān enāṃ pratyekabodhilābhinīṃ  Rm 
 tato 'sau bhagavān buddhaḥ saṃnirīkṣya ca tāṃ satīṃ 
 sarvān bhikṣugaṇāṃ chiṣyān samāmaṃtryābravīt tathā  Rm 
 paśyadhvaṃ bhikṣavo yūyaṃ dārikaṃ tāṃ subhadrikāṃ 
 nūnaṃ maddarśanād eṣā bodhicittam avāpnuyāt  Rm 
 samyakkuśalamūlāni samavaropayiṣyati 
 dhruvaṃ pratyekabodhau ca praṇidhānaṃ kariṣyati  Rm 
 tasmāt saṃdarśanaṃ datvā dārikāṃ tāṃ subhāvinīṃ 
 pratyekabodhicaryāyāṃ supratisthāpayāmy ahaṃ  Rm 
 tatra ca gantum ichanti ye mayā saha bhikṣavaḥ 
 Rm 
 pātracīvaram ādāya te prāyātaṃ caremahi  Rm 
 ity ādiṣṭaṃ jinendreṇa śrutvā sarve 'pi sāṃghikāḥ 
 pātracīvarasaṃyuktās tatra gaṃtum upācaran  Rm 
 tato 'sau bhagavān buddhaḥ svaprabhāvaṃ pradarśayan 
 sarvaiś ca sāṃghikaiḥ sārddhaṃ rājagṛham upāsarat  Rm 
 tatra mārge samāyātā dārikā sasakhīvṛtā 
 taṃ buddhaṃ śrīghanaṃ dūrād dadarśa saṃprabhāsvaraṃ  Rm 
 dvātriṃśallakṣaṇopetam aśītivyaṃjanānvitaṃ 
 divyātikrāntasaundaryyaṃ samantabhadrarūpakaṃ  Rm 
 sahasreṇātiriktābhaṃ saumyaṃ kāntaṃ manoharaṃ 
 puṇḍarīkam ivodbhāsaṃ ratnāṅgam iva jaṃgamaṃ  Rm 
 sākṣāt puṇyāvatāraṃ ca dṛṣṭvā cātyanumoditā 
 sahasopetya tac cakram upaḍhaukitum aichata  Rm 
 evaṃ tāṃ cakram ādāya saṃbuddham upaḍhaukituṃ 
 prayātaṃ tāṃ sakhī dṛṣṭvā nivārayitum abravīt  Rm 
 nāyaṃ nārāyaṇo bhadre sugato 'yaṃ jitendriyaḥ 
 tad asmai mā pradehīdaṃ cakraṃ saṃkalpitaṃ hareḥ  Rm 
 evaṃ nivāryyamānāpi sakhībhiḥ sā ca bhadrikā 
 saddharmaguṇavāṃchantī tāḥ sakhīḥ punar abravīt  Rm 
 sakhyo bhāgyān mayāpy evaṃ saṃbuddho dṛśyate 'dhunā 
 tad adya saphalaṃ janma saṃsāre jīvitaṃ ca me  Rm 
 yadābhāsparśitā cāpi satvāḥ kleśavimocitāḥ 
 saṃvṛttisukhasaṃprāptā nirvṛttim api cāpnuyuḥ  Rm 
 yannāmoccāraṇād vāpi saṃbhāvyasmaraṇād api 
 mārapāśavinirmuktāḥ saṃbodhipadam āpnuyuḥ  Rm 
 yaddharmaśravaṇād evaṃ nityānumodanād api 
 sarvapāpavinirmuktāḥ sadgatiṃ samavāpnuyuḥ  Rm 
 yatsaṃgheṣu supātreṣu kiṃcinmātrārppanād api 
 saṃsāre 'nantasaukhyāni bhuktvā yāyuḥ sukhāvatīṃ  Rm 
 yenaivaṃ pālitāḥ satvāḥ ṣaḍgaticaritā api 
 Rm 
 bodhayitvā ca saddharme sthāpitā nirvṛtāv api  Rm 
 yasya dharmānubhāvāc ca maṃgalaṃ bhuvanatraye 
 sarve satvā sukhāḍhyāś ca saṃbodhipadacāriṇaḥ  Rm 
 so 'py ayaṃ bhagavān nāthaḥ śāstā trailokyādhipaḥ 
 nūnaṃ me puṇyabhāgyena dṛśyate 'yatnato 'dhunā  Rm 
 tad ahaṃ kuśalinī syāṃ hi saṃbuddhena darśitā 
 mahābhāgyavatī cāsmi yad ayaṃ sadguruḥ sudhīḥ  Rm 
 amṛgyamāna evetthaṃ labhyate purato mayā 
 tad ahaṃ pūjayitvemaṃ cakraṃ ca samupaḍhaukituṃ  Rm 
 ichāmy asmai munīṃdrāya nirvṛtipadalabdhaye 
 api cātra sadā naiva saṃbuddho lapsyate tathā  Rm 
 kadā cid dhi jinotpattiḥ puṣpam audunvaraṃ yathā 
 mānuṣye 'pi sadā naiva janma bhavānucāriṇāṃ 
 puṇyair eva hi mānuṣyaṃ lapṣyate janma dullabhaṃ  Rm 
 mānuṣye 'labhyamāne tu kathaṃ buddhānusevanā 
 buddhasevāṃ vinā kena bodhicittam avāpnuyāt  Rm 
 bodhicittaṃ vinā kasya saddharmeṣu matiś caret 
 vinā dharmamatiṃ ko hi bodhicaryyāṃ samācaret  Rm 
 bodhicaryāṃ vinā loke hitaṃ kartuṃ kathaṃ caret 
 loke hitam akṛtvaiva kutaḥ puṇyam avāpnuyāt  Rm 
 apuṇyena kathaṃ kleśān hitvā nirvṛtim āpnuyāt 
 tasmāt kleśavimuktyarthaṃ nirvṛttipadalabdhaye  Rm 
 imaṃ buddhaṃ jagannātham ichāmy abhyarcituṃ mudā 
 buddha eva jagannāthaḥ sarvasatvahitārthadaḥ  Rm 
 saddharmadeśakaḥ śāstā saṃbodhijñānanāyakaḥ 
 tasmād enaṃ samutsṛjya nānyam ichāmi cārcituṃ  Rm 
 asyaiva śaraṇaṃ gatvā bhajiṣyāmi sadāpy ahaṃ  Rm 
 iti sā dārikā proktvā cakram ādāya moditā 
 saṃbuddhaṃ cārppituṃ tasmai pūjāṃ kartum upāyayau  Rm 
 atha sā taṃ muniṃ natvā pūjābhiś ca samarcayat 
 taṃ cakraṃ samupasthāpya natvaivaṃ praṇidhiṃ vyadhāt  Rm 
 Rm 
 yathāyaṃ sugato buddho niḥkleśo vijitendriyaḥ 
 tathāham api śuddhātmā nirvṛtipadam āpnuyāṃ  Rm 
 tathāsau bhagavān buddho dṛṣṭvā tatpraṇidhiṃ tataḥ 
 suprasannamukhāmbhojād vyasṛjat saṃsmitāmṛtaṃ  Rm 
 tatsmitasahoccāryamāṇā paṃcavidhāṃśavaḥ 
 ke cid ūrddhvaṃ gatāḥ ke cid adho yātāś ca te 'ṃśavaḥ  Rm 
 ye ca yātā adholoke te saṃjīvanarake gatāḥ 
 kālasūtre ca saṃghāte tathā ca raurave tataḥ  Rm 
 mahārauravake cāpi tapane ca pratāpane 
 avīcau cārbude cāpi nirarbude tathāṭaṭe  Rm 
 hahave huhuve caivam utpale padmake tathā 
 mahāpadme 'pi caiteṣu ṣoḍaśeṣu samaṃtataḥ  Rm 
 tathopanārakeṣv evaṃ sarveṣv api ca te 'ṃśavaḥ 
 prasṛtā bhāsayitvaivaṃ prākāśayan samaṃtataḥ  Rm 
 ye śītanarakās teṣu tūṣṇībhūtā nipātitāḥ 
 ye uṣṇanarakās teṣu śītībhūtā vyabhāsayan  Rm 
 teṣu ye pāpinaḥ satvā duḥkhātivedanāturāḥ 
 te sarve taddyutispṛṣṭās tadduḥkhavedanojjhitāḥ  Rm 
 śāṃtasaukhyānubhūtāś ca vismayoddhatamānasāḥ 
 dṛṣṭvaiva saha saṃmīlya mithaś caivam abhāṣata  Rm 
 aho citraṃ bhavanto 'dya kiṃ nu vayam itaś cyutāḥ 
 anyatra caritāḥ smaḥ kiṃ vatāhosvin na manyate  Rm 
 iti saṃdigdhacittānāṃ teṣāṃ cittaprabodhane 
 bhagavān nirmitaṃ tatra praiṣayac ca samaṃtataḥ  Rm 
 atha taṃ nirmitaṃ saumyaṃ dṛṣṭvā te saṃprasāditāḥ 
 bhūyo dṛṣṭvābhimodanto mithaś caivaṃ vabhāṣire  Rm 
 bhavanto nu vayaṃ sarve nānyatra caritā itaḥ 
 api tv ayam ihāyātaḥ satvo hy apūrvadarśanaḥ  Rm 
 Rm 
 nūnam asyānubhāvena nirduḥkhā susukhā vayaṃ 
 iti te nirmite tasmin bauddhe cittaṃ prasādya ca  Rm 
 namo buddhāya te tāyinn ity uktvā śaraṇaṃ yayuḥ 
 tataḥ sarve ca te satvās tadbuddhasmṛtidhāriṇaḥ  Rm 
 niḥpāpāḥ kuśalādhyāś ca sadgatiṃ sahasā yayuḥ 
 ye tathorddhaṃ gatās te ca buddhasmitotsṛtāḥ karāḥ  Rm 
 gatvā cāturmahārājabhuvaneṣu tato gatāḥ 
 trayastriṃśāś ca yāmāś ca tathā ca tuṣitāṃ gatāḥ  Rm 
 nirmāṇaratikāṃ cānyanirmitavaśavarttinaḥ 
 brahmakāyikalokaṃ ca tathā brahmaprohitaṃ  Rm 
 mahābrāhmaṇalokāṃś ca parīttābhaṃ tathā gatāḥ 
 apramāṇaṃ tato yātā ābhāsvarāṃ tathā gatāḥ  Rm 
 parīttaśubham evaṃ ca hy apramāṇaśubhaṃ tathā 
 śubhakṛtsnam anabhraṃ ca puṇyaprasavasaṃjñikaṃ  Rm 
 bṛhatphalaṃ tathā caivam abṛham atapaṃ tathā 
 sudṛśaṃ bhuvanaṃ caiva sudarśanaṃ tathā gatāḥ  Rm 
 akaniṣṭhaṃ tathā gatvā proccair evam aghoṣayan  Rm 
 anityaṃ khalu saṃsāraṃ duḥkhaṃ śūnyaṃ hy anātmakaṃ 
 iti matvā triratnāni saṃbhajadhvaṃ samāhitāḥ  Rm 
 niṣkrāmatārabhadhvaṃ ca yujyadhvaṃ buddhaśāsane 
 dhunīta mṛtyusainyāś ca naḍāgāraṃ yathā karī  Rm 
 yo 'py asmin dharmavaineye hy apramattaś cariṣyati 
 sa hitvā jātisaṃsāraṃ duḥkhasyāntaṃ kariṣyati  Rm 
 evaṃ tā arciṣaḥ sarvāṃl lokadhātūn samaṃtataḥ 
 avabhāsya śubhe satvān vinīya punar āgatāḥ  Rm 
 bhagavato 'grataḥ sthitvā kṛtvā pradakṣiṇatrayaṃ 
 ūrṇāyāṃ ca munīndrasya sarvā antardadhus tviṣaḥ  Rm 
 tadānandaḥ samutthāya kṛtāṃjalipuṭo nataḥ 
 Rm 
 jānubhyāṃ bhuvi saṃsthitvā bhagavantaṃ samabravīt  Rm 
 nānāraṅgakalāpas te vaktrān niṣkasito muneḥ 
 yenāvabhāsitāḥ sarvā sūryeṇodayatā yathā  Rm 
 vigatoddhavā dainyamadaprahīṇā buddhā jagaty uttamahetubhūtāḥ 
 nākāraṇaṃ śaṃkhamṛṇālagauraṃ smitam upadarśayanti jinā jitārayaḥ  Rm 
 tatkālaṃ svayam adhigamya dhīrabuddhyā śrotṝṇāṃ śramaṇajinendra kāṃkṣitānāṃ 
 dhīrābhir munivṛṣa vāgbhir uttamābhir utpannaṃ vyapanaya saṃśayaṃ śubhābhiḥ  Rm 
 nākasmāl lavaṇajalādrirājadhairyyāḥ saṃbuddhāḥ smitam upadarśayanti nāthāḥ 
 yasyārthe smitam upadarśayanti dhīrās taṃ śrotuṃ samabhilaṣanti janaughāḥ  Rm 
 ity ānaṃdavacaḥ śrutvā saṃbuddho bhagavān asau 
 tat smitahetum ādeṣṭuṃ tam ānandaṃ samabravīt  Rm 
 evam etat tathānanda nāhetvapratyayaṃ smitaṃ 
 prāviṣkurvanti saṃbuddhā arhantaḥ sugatā jināḥ  Rm 
 paśyānandānayā nāryyā cakraṃ me samupārppitaṃ 
 pūjayitvā praṇatvā ca bodhau ca praṇidhiḥ kṛtā  Rm 
 anena dānadharmeṇa kuśalaiś ca samanvitāḥ 
 dārikeyaṃ subhadrāṃśā divyabhogyaṃ samāpnuyāt  Rm 
 na paṃcadaśakalpāni vinipātaṃ gamiṣyati 
 tataś cakrāntaro nāma pratyekasugato sudhīḥ  Rm 
 arhaṃ kleśavimuktātmā paṃcābhijño jitendriyaḥ 
 sarvasatvānukaṃpī ca brahmacārī bhaviṣyati  Rm 
 yan mayi sugate buddhe cittam asyāḥ prasīdati 
 tena puṇyabaleneyaṃ pratyekabodhim āpsyati  Rm 
 sugateṣu kṛtaṃ puṇyaṃ na kṣiṇoti kadā cana 
 kramāt tena viśuddhātmā saṃbodhim api cāpnuyāt  Rm 
 iti matvā triratneṣu cittam evaṃ prasādya ca 
 śraddhayā saṃprakarttavyaṃ satkāraṃ bodhivāṃchibhiḥ  Rm 
 ity ādiṣṭaṃ munīndreṇa śrutvā sarve janāś ca te 
 Rm 
 tathety abhyanumodantas triratnasevino 'bhavan  Rm 
 tato buddhānubhāvena tac cakraṃ khe samudgataṃ 
 kṣaṇaṃ buddhopari sthitvā chatram ivojjvalan babhau  Rm 
 tataś ca viyato gatvā hariharmyopari sthitaṃ 
 sudarśanam ivoddīptaṃ babhau rasmisamutkiran  Rm 
 tato 'sau bhagavān buddho dṛṣṭvā tāṃ dārikāṃ svayaṃ 
 śirasi pāṇinā spṛṣṭvā svāśīrvacanam ādiśat  Rm 
 bhadre te maṃgalaṃ bhūyā vinipātaṃ na cāpnuhi 
 kramāt pāramitāḥ pūryya pratyekaṃ bodhiṃ āpnuhi  Rm 
 ity āśīrvacanaṃ datvā saṃbuddho 'sau munīśvaraḥ 
 tato rājagṛhaṃ gaṃtuṃ upācarat sasāṃghikaḥ  Rm 
 tato 'sau dārikā cāpi natvā taṃ sugataṃ punaḥ 
 dṛṣṭvaivaṃ muhuḥ smṛtvā svagehaṃ samupāyayau  Rm 
 tatra gehe praviṣṭvāsau dārikā saṃpramoditā 
 bharttur agre ca tadvṛttam ācakhye sarvam ādarāt  Rm 
 bharttāpy asau tathā śrutvā buddhadharmānumoditaḥ 
 tayaivaṃ bhāryayā sārddhaṃ bheje ratnatrayaṃ sadā  Rm 
 evaṃ me guruṇā khyātaṃ tathā te kathyate mayā 
 tvam apy evaṃ mahārāja triratnāni sadā bhaja  Rm 
 prajāś cāpi triratnānāṃ bhajane preraya prabho 
 tathā te maṃgalaṃ nityaṃ bodhiṃ cāpi samāpnuyāḥ  Rm 
 iti tenopaguptena bhāṣitaṃ tat subhāṣitaṃ 
 śrutvāśoko narendro 'sau mumoda saha pārṣadaiḥ  Rm 
 etac cakrāvadānaṃ munivaraguṇadaṃ yaḥ śṛṇoti prasādya 
 śrutvā yaś cānumodya pramuditamanasā śrāvayaty evam anyān 
 sa jitvā kleśasaṃghān vigatakalimalo buddhadharmānucārī 
 pūtātmā sadguṇāḍhyaḥ munivaranilayaiḥ saṃprayāti pramodāt  Rm 
  iti ratnāvadānamālāyaṃ cakrāvadāno nāma samāptam 
 Rm 
 IV Pretikāvadāna
 athāśoko mahīpālaḥ saddharmacaraṇotsavaḥ 
 upaguptaṃ guruṃ natvā kṛtāñjalipuṭo 'vadat  Rm 
 bhadanta śrotum ichāmi punaranyat subhāṣitaṃ 
 yathā me guruṇā proktaṃ tathā vaktuṃ samarhasi  Rm 
 iti tena narendreṇa prārthite 'sau jināṃśajaḥ 
 upagupto mahābhijñas taṃ nareśam abhāṣata  Rm 
 yathā me guruṇādiṣṭaṃ tathā vakṣyāmi te 'dhunā 
 tathāpi śrūyatāṃ rājan tava dharmapravṛddhaye  Rm 
 puraikasamaye cāsau saṃbuddho bhagavāñ jinaḥ 
 cailakaiś ca tathānyais tatsaddharmaguṇavāṃchibhiḥ  Rm 
 rājagṛham upāśritya veṇuvane jināśrame 
 karaṇḍakanivāpākhye tasthau dharmaṃ samādiśat  Rm 
 tad dharmmadeśanāṃ śrotuṃ sadevāsuramānuṣāḥ 
 siddhavidyādharāś cāpi yakṣagaṃdharvakinnarāḥ  Rm 
 garuḍā nāgarājāś ca rākṣasāś ca mahoragāḥ 
 sarve lokādhipāś cāpi sasainyaparivārakāḥ  Rm 
 rājāno rājamātrāś ca brāhmaṇāś ca mahājanāḥ 
 maṃtriṇo śreṣṭhinaś cāpi sārthavāhāś ca paurikāḥ  Rm 
 ṛṣayo yoginaś cāpi yatayo brahmacāriṇaḥ 
 evam anye 'pi lokāś ca parivṛtya samaṃtataḥ  Rm 
 satkṛtya svaryya pūjāṅgaiḥ sarvopakaraṇair api 
 mānayitvā ca taṃ nāthaṃ dṛṣṭvā tasthuḥ samāhitāḥ  Rm 
 tasmiṃś ca samaye tatra maudgalyāyana ātmavit 
 sa pretabhuvane gatvā caran pretīm apaśyata  Rm 
 svakeśaromasaṃchannāṃ dagdhasthūnāmahākṛtiṃ 
 sūcīmukhīṃ mahatkāyīṃ parvatasaṃnibhodarāṃ  Rm 
 piṅgalakeśinīṃ raudrīṃ pradīptāgniśikhām iva 
 Rm 
 tīvrātivedanākrāntāṃ tṛṣārttaṃ parimūrchitāṃ  Rm 
 tatrāyuṣmān sa maudgalyo dṛṣṭvā tāṃ pretikāṃ ciraṃ 
 kaiṣeti sahasopetya papracha samupāgatāṃ  Rm 
 kiṃ tvayā prakṛtaṃ pāpaṃ yenaivaṃ duḥkhabhāginī 
 tṛṣārttā jalamārgantī bhramitvā carase 'dhunā  Rm 
 iti tena yatīśena pṛṣṭvā sā pretikā tataḥ 
 taṃ yatiṃ saugataṃ natvā praruditvāvadat tathā  Rm 
 bhadanta tad vijānīyāḥ pāpakāriṇy ahaṃ yataḥ 
 evaṃ tṛṣṇāprataptāṅgā bhramāmi jalalālasā  Rm 
 yatrāham udakaṃ pātuṃ gachāmi tṛṣṇayānvitā 
 atra paśyāmi nadyādijalādhārān viśoṣitān  Rm 
 yadā varṣati deve ca dṛṣṭvā tadambupātitaṃ 
 pātum ichantl tṛṣṇārttā sahasāhaṃ pradhāvitā  Rm 
 tadā paśyāmi tadvinduvisphuliṅganibhojvalān 
 dṛṣṭvaivaṃ nirāśāndhā bhramāmi dikṣu sarvataḥ  Rm 
 kiṃ mayā prakṛtaṃ pāpaṃ yenāsmy evaṃ supāpinī 
 tan me pāpaṃ jagacchāstā pṛchyatāṃ bhavatādarāt  Rm 
 nūnaṃ so bhagavāñ chāstā yan me karmapurākṛtaṃ 
 vyākariṣyati tat sarvaṃ tathā lokaprabodhane  Rm 
 yac chrutvānye 'pi satvāś ca saṃvignamanaso drutaṃ 
 viramya pāpamārgebhyaś cariṣyanti śubhe sadā  Rm 
 tasmād bhadanta sarvajñas tava śāstā sa pṛchyatāṃ 
 vyākuryān mama sarvatra yat karma prakṛtaṃ purā  Rm 
 asmannāmnā sa saṃbuddho vaṃdyatāṃ bhavatā yathā 
 ity uktvā sā tam ātmajaṃ natvā pretā gṛhaṃ yayau  Rm 
 sa maudgalyas tathety uktvā tat saṃdeśam anusmaran 
 sahasaitat paripraṣṭuṃ veṇuvanam upāyayau  Rm 
 tadādau bhagavān dṛṣṭvā tan maudgalyam upāgataṃ 
 prahasan suprasannāsyaḥ samāmaṃtryaitad abravīt 
 kaṃcit te kuśalaṃ vatsa kuto 'trāsi samāgataḥ 
 lokeṣu kiṃ pravṛttāṃtaṃ tat pracakṣva mahāmate 
 Rm 
 iti pṛṣṭe jinendreṇa sa maudgalyaḥ purogataḥ  Rm 
 ādau tasya muner natvā tat pravṛttam udāharat 
 āgato 'smi bhadanto 'haṃ caritvā pretabhūmiṣu  Rm 
 tatra sthito 'ham īkṣan tāṃ pretīm ekāṃ bhayānakīṃ 
 dagdhasthūṇānibhāṃ nagnāṃ parvatasannibhodarāṃ  Rm 
 sūcīchidramukhacchidrāṃ kaṃkārayantrikām iva 
 svakeśaromasaṃchannāṃ jvalitāgniśikhām iva  Rm 
 tivrātivedanākrāntām ārttasvarānurodināṃ 
 durgandhām aśucivyāptāṃ svakeśaparitāpitāṃ  Rm 
 viṇmūtrānubhoktuṃ ca sākṣāt pāpāvatārikāṃ 
 bhagavan sā mayā dṛṣṭvā tṛṣṇārttā jalalālasā  Rm 
 bhramantī jalamārgantī jalāśrayeṣu sarvataḥ 
 nadīkūpataḍāgādin udapānajalāśrayān  Rm 
 svechāmbupūritān dṛṣṭvā prādhāvat sahasā yadā 
 tasyā darśaṇamātreṇa te sarve 'pi jalāśrayāḥ  Rm 
 nirjalāḥ paṃkaśeṣeṇa śuśuṣuś ca samaṃtataḥ 
 tathā viśoṣitāṃ dṛṣṭvā nadyādīṃs tāñ jalāśrayān  Rm 
 nirāśā paritaptāṅgā sā pretī paryamūrchata 
 tataś ca punar utthāya kṣuttṛṣṇonmādacāriṇī  Rm 
 jalaṃ cānnaṃ samanveṣṭuṃ babhrāma dikṣu sarvataḥ 
 tathāpi sā jalaṃ nāsādayat kuhāpi vā  Rm 
 tato 'titṛṣṇayā taptā viṇmūtrabhoktum aichata 
 tad api kṛcchrato 'nviṣya bhuktvā tṛptiṃ na sā yayau  Rm 
 tathāmedhyāni bhuktvāpi kadācin naiva tṛptitā 
 kṣuttṛṣṇāhatāklāntā patitā kheditāvasat  Rm 
 māṃ dṛṣṭvā sahasotthāya śanair mandasvarāvadat 
 svāgataṃ bho bhavān aitu rakṣa māṃ pāpinīṃ laghu  Rm 
 pānīyaṃ dehi me bhadra pānīyaṃ dātum arhasi 
 iti proktābhidhāvanti pānīyaṃ mām ayācata  Rm 
 tato 'ham avadaṃ caināṃ pānīyaṃ nātra vidyate 
 kātvam evaṃ nu duḥkhāni bhuktvātra vasase kathaṃ  Rm 
 kiṃ tvayā hi kṛtaṃ pāpaṃ yenaivaṃ duḥkhatādhunā 
 Rm 
 vaktavyaṃ cec ca tat pāpaṃ sarvaṃ me vaktum arhasi  Rm 
 iti me gaditaṃ śrutvā sa pretī punar abravīt 
 kiṃ mayā vakṣyate pāpaṃ yat purā kudhiyā kṛtaṃ  Rm 
 sarvajño hi bhavacchāstā sa evaṃ paripṛchyatāṃ 
 tat sarvāṇi ca me pāpaṃ sa vyākuryāt sa sarvavit  Rm 
 asmannāmnā ca saṃbuddho vaṃdyatāṃ bhavatādarāt 
 iti tayoditaṃ śrutvā pratijñāya tatheti ca  Rm 
 bhavantaṃ praṣṭum āyāmi tat samādeṣṭum arhasi 
 ārttasvarā rudantī sā pretī vindati vedanāṃ  Rm 
 yena viṇmūtradhānāni tena dhāvati duḥkhitā 
 tad api kṛcchrato labdhvā bhuṃkte kiṃ cit kadā cana  Rm 
 evaṃ sā pāpinī pretī dṛṣṭātiduḥkhitā mayā 
 kiṃ tayā prakṛtaṃ pāpaṃ martyaloke sudāruṇaṃ  Rm 
 yenaivaṃvidhaduḥkhaṃ sā hy anubhavati sāṃprataṃ 
 kadā sā pāpato muktā kathaṃ ca sugatiṃ vrajet  Rm 
 tat sarvaṃ vadatāṃ śāsta sarvasatvaprabodhane 
 iti tenārthite cāsau bhagavān punar abravīt  Rm 
 maudgalyāyana sā pretī pāpinī matsarī kudhīḥ 
 tayā yat prakṛtaṃ pāpaṃ yena sā duḥkhabhāginī  Rm 
 tat sarvaṃ te pravakṣyāmi śṛṇu śrotuṃ yadīchasi  Rm 
 purāsīd bhagavān buddhaḥ kāśyapo nāma sarvavit 
 sarvavidyādhipo nātho dharmarājas tathāgataḥ  Rm 
 samantabhadrakṛc chāstā traidhātukavināyakaḥ 
 jino 'rhan sugatas trāyī saṃbodhimārgadeśakaḥ  Rm 
 sa satvānāṃ hitārthena bodhicaryāḥ prakāśayan 
 vārāṇasīm upāśritya mṛgadāve jināśrame  Rm 
 śrāvakair bhikṣubhiḥ sārddhaṃ bodhisatvagaṇair api 
 tasminn eva parṣatmadhye tasthau dharmaṃ samādiśat  Rm 
 tasmiṃś ca samaye tasya bhikṣur anyatamo yatiḥ 
 anyatranagare gatvā pratyāgachat svam āśramaṃ  Rm 
 Rm 
 tatra mārge tṛṣārtto 'sau dūrāt kūpaṃ vilokayan 
 sahasā samupāgatya kūpāntikam upāyayau  Rm 
 tadaikā dārikā tatra pūrayitvā ghaṭaṃ jalaiḥ 
 sahasā śirasohitvā gṛhaṃ gantum upācarat  Rm 
 sa tṛṣārtto yatir dṛṣṭvā tām ambughaṭavāhikāṃ 
 samupetya jalaṃ pātuṃ prārthayan samupācarat  Rm 
 bhaginyo 'haṃ tṛṣārtto 'smi dūradeśād upāgataḥ 
 tvāṃ dṛṣṭvā sahasopetya jalaṃ pātum ihāgataḥ  Rm 
 tad bhaginī jalaṃ dehi jīvaya māṃ tṛṣāturaṃ 
 datvā me jīvanaṃ tvaṃ tac ciraṃ jīvyā niroginī  Rm 
 iti tenārthitaṃ dṛṣṭvā dārikāsau durāśayā 
 mātsaryyaprahatatvātā taṃ bhikṣuṃ paryyabhāṣata  Rm 
 are bhikṣo 'tra māyāhi mriyase yadi vā khalu 
 na te dadāmi pānīyaṃ ghaṭo pūrṇo bhaven mama  Rm 
 kūpe yatnāt samuddhṛtya pūrayitvāmbunā ghaṭe 
 prohitvāyaṃ mayānītas tvadarthe kiṃ na manyate  Rm 
 nirlajja kva nu te lajjā parakīyāmbum ichasi 
 rājā kiṃ tvaṃ dhanī vāsi gurur vā kiṃ na manyate  Rm 
 ity ākṣepaṃ pratikṣipya taṃ bhikṣuṃ saugataṃ yatiṃ 
 adatvaivāmṛtaṃ kiṃ cit satvarā sā gṛhaṃ yayau  Rm 
 tato bhikṣus tṛṣārtto 'pi lajjayāsau nyavarttate 
 anyatraivaṃ samāyācya pītvā yayau svam āśramaṃ  Rm 
 tatrāśrame taror mūle paryaṇkam upabhujya saḥ 
 anuśocaya tāṃ nārīṃ manasaivaṃ vyaciṃtayat  Rm 
 aho sā durmatī nārī mātsaryyaprahatāśayā 
 kathaṃ na manyate hy evaṃ mānuṣyajanma durllabhaṃ  Rm 
 mānuṣyaṃ puṇyato labdhvā nisphalaṃ kriyate tayā 
 dhik tāṃ durāśayāṃ mūḍhāṃ yasyā janma nirarthakaṃ  Rm 
 kadaiṣā pāpato muktvā sadgatiṃ samavāpsyati 
 mā gāt sā narake duḥkhaṃ bhūyād dharmānumodinī  Rm 
 śīghraṃ lokeśvarasmārttaṃ labdhvā vrajatu sanmatiṃ 
 Rm 
 ity evaṃmanasā bhāṣya sa bhikṣur vijitendriyaḥ  Rm 
 triratnasmaraṇaṃ kṛtvā tasthau dhyānasamāhitaḥ 
 tato 'sau dārikā gehe prāptā bhartuḥ purogatā  Rm 
 etat sarvaṃ pravṛttāṃtaṃ vistareṇābravīn mudā 
 svāmin nadyāmbusaṃpūrṇaṃ ghaṭaṃ dhṛtvāgatā pathi  Rm 
 tato bhikṣur upāgatya pānīyaṃ māṃ prayācati 
 adatvaivaṃ jalaṃ tasmai bhikṣave satvarāgatā  Rm 
 vahuśo yācyamānāpi kiṃ cin naiva dadāmy ahaṃ 
 iti tayoktamātre 'sau bharttā sādhur api krudhā 
 tāṃ bhāryāṃ rukṣaṇetreṇa dṛṣṭvā caivam abhāṣata  Rm 
 are pāpini durbuddhe kathaṃ na dīyate tvayā 
 kiyad vyeti jalaṃ datvā bhikṣave tṛṣitāya te  Rm 
 jalamātrapradāne 'pi yasyāḥ śraddhā na vidyate 
 sā kim annaṃ dhanaṃ ratnaṃ kathāṃ dātuṃ samutsahet  Rm 
 dhik tvāṃ pāpinīṃ duṣṭāṃ yasyā nāsti dayārthine 
 kiṃ tvayā mama satyāpi yaśodharmapraghātayā  Rm 
 yady evaṃ na pradadyās tvaṃ kasmai cid arthine jalaṃ 
 preyasīm api bhārye tvāṃ parityakṣyāmy ahaṃ khalu  Rm 
 yadi me priyatāṃ kartum ichasi snehacetasā 
 arthino mānayitvā tad dānaṃ kartuṃ samutsaheḥ  Rm 
 no ced evaṃ mayā tyaktā vraja mā tiṣṭha me gṛhe 
 avaśyaṃ nau viyogaḥ syād ekānte maraṇaṃ dhruvaṃ  Rm 
 kiṃ tvādṛśyā striyā puṃsaḥ kevalaṃ dharmahānaye 
 dharmaṃ vinā na me kāryyaṃ dākṣiṇyāpi ca bhāryayā  Rm 
 kiṃ tvayā kāṃtayāpy evaṃ mātsaryyakuladurdhiyā 
 dharma eva vinaśyeta tad vraja mā gṛhe vasa  Rm 
 dharmeṇa rakṣyate lokaḥ kāntayā kiṃ hi rakṣyate 
 tat kāntāpi parityājyā yadi pāpanuraginī  Rm 
 Rm 
 bhāryā hi pālanīyā sā yadi dharmārthinī satī 
 kiṃ tvaṃ pāpārthinī duṣṭā yaśodharmavināśinī  Rm 
 naivāhaṃ ca tvayā sārddhaṃ bhoktuṃ rantuṃ samutsahe 
 kriyate cet tvayā dharmas tathā vasa mayā saha  Rm 
 no ced evaṃ mayā tyaktā tvaṃ mā tiṣṭha gṛhe vraja 
 evaṃ bharttrocyamānāpi pramadā sā na bodhitā  Rm 
 mātsaryyālīḍhacittatvād roṣitā caivam abravīt 
 naiva sthāsyāmy ahaṃ yāsye kiṃ sthitvaivaṃ vininditā  Rm 
 kiyat tvayy aparādhaṃ me yat tathāhaṃ vimocitā 
 kiṃ sa bhikṣur gurur rājā mitraṃ vā te pitā suhṛt  Rm 
 jñātir vā sa sakhā vandhuḥ kiṃ ca bhrātā prabhur dhanī 
 pradattaṃ kiṃ adattaṃ ca kiyan naṣṭaṃ bhavet yataḥ  Rm 
 naiva kiṃcic ca dāsyāmi kasmai cid bhikṣave 'rthitaṃ 
 adatvā me bhavet kiṃ hi dāsyāmy ahaṃ yathechayā  Rm 
 dāsyāmi vā na dāsyāmi kā carcātra tathā tava 
 pāpaś cen mayi pacyeta dharmo vāpi tathā mama  Rm 
 tvam atra mā kṛthāś cintāṃ kiṃ tvayātra vicāryyate 
 śubhaṃ vāpy aśubhaṃ vā me tava kiṃ tad vicāratā  Rm 
 tathāpi mama doṣaṃ ced yāsyāmi na vasāmy ahaṃ 
 varaṃ prāṇaparityājyaṃ na tu dānaṃ dadāmy ahaṃ  Rm 
 ity asau pramadākruṣya bhartur ākṣipya garvitā 
 kvacit kiṃcic ca kasmaicid dadau naiva kadācana  Rm 
 gṛhe tithīn upāyātān dṛṣṭvaivātipraroṣitā 
 vahudhā kruṣya tān gehān nyakāsayad balādapi  Rm 
 tadāśīrvacanāny evaṃ śrutvāpi parikopitā 
 hasati nindayitvaināṃ paribhāṣya nyakāsayat  Rm 
 sadā badhvā gṛhadvāraṃ yācakāgatiśaṃkayā 
 koṣṭha eva samāsīnā kadācin na viniryayau  Rm 
 Rm 
 sarvadā svāminā sārddhaṃ kṛtvaivaṃ kalahaṃ muhuḥ 
 svayam eva prabhuktvāsau kālam evam ayāpayat  Rm 
 tataḥ kāla upāyāte pramadā sā rujānvitā 
 tadāpy evaṃ na cotsehe kiṃcid dātuṃ samarthine  Rm 
 tataḥ pravṛddharogārttā tṛṣṇārttā pariśoṣitā 
 mṛtā sā narake yātā pretī bhavati sāṃprataṃ  Rm 
 yā cābhūd dārikā duṣṭā mātsaryyaprahatāśayā 
 saivaiṣā hi tvayā dṛṣṭā pretī narakavāsinī  Rm 
 iti maudgalya dṛṣṭvaivaṃ pratyakṣaṃ pāpaduḥkhinīṃ 
 sarvādā śraddhayārthibhyo dātavyaṃ jalam ādarāt  Rm 
 sarvavastupradānānāṃ jaladānaṃ mahattaraṃ 
 sarveṣāṃ jīvanaṃ yasmād amṛtaṃ saṃvaraṃ jalaṃ  Rm 
 jalapānaṃ vinā sarve na jīvanti hi jantavaḥ 
 tad amṛtaṃ jalaṃ śuddhaṃ dātavyam arthine sadā  Rm 
 jalam eva hi pītvā te nirāhārās tapasvinaḥ 
 yogino 'nekavarṣāni jīvanti prāṇino yathā  Rm 
 sarvāhārābhisaṃtyaktā jivaṃti prāṇino jalaiḥ 
 sarvān na paribhuktvāpi na jīvanti jalair vinā  Rm 
 tad amṛtapradānaṃ taj jīvadānaṃ pracakṣyate 
 sarvavastupradānebhyo jaladānaṃ praśasyate  Rm 
 viśeṣād grīṣmakāle tu tṛṣārttāya ca rogine 
 bālavṛddhāturebhyaś ca dātavyaṃ jalam āditaḥ  Rm 
 jaladānaṃ mahādānaṃ jaladānasamaṃ na hi 
 yenābhidhāryyate prāṇaṃ tat phalaṃ saṃpraśasyate  Rm 
 sarvadhātupradānebhyaḥ sarvaratnapradānataḥ 
 sarvānnabhogyadānebhyo jaladānaṃ mahīyate  Rm 
 kanyākoṭipradānāc ca gajakoṭipradānataḥ 
 gavāṃ koṭipradānāc ca jaladānaṃ mahīyate  Rm 
 saptaratnamayībhūmipradānāc ca mahīyate 
 evaṃ sarvapradānebhyo jaladānaṃ mahattaraṃ  Rm 
 tṛpyante devatāḥ sarve pitṛlokās tathāpare 
 sarve bhūtāś ca satvāś ca jalenaiva sadāpi hi  Rm 
 tathā dravyāni sarvāṇi bhūtāni hy aśuciny api 
 jalābhiṣiktamātreṇa śuddhyante sarvadā khalu  Rm 
 jalaṃ vinā na tṛpyante bhuktvāpi divyabhojanaṃ 
 Rm 
 tasmāt sarvapradānānāṃ jaladānaṃ mahīyate  Rm 
 tathā ye ca sudhāṃ pītvā divyakāntā samarpitā 
 ramanti tridaśāḥ svarge te hi sarve jalapradāḥ  Rm 
 cakravarttī nṛpendro yo ramaṇībhiḥ sahāmṛtaṃ 
 bhuktvā ramati saṃmodī so 'pi cāmbupradānataḥ  Rm 
 evaṃ cānye 'pi ye lokā yathechā sukhabhoginaḥ 
 niḥkleśā nirujā bhadrās te hi sarve jalapradāḥ  Rm 
 ye tu nīcāśayādīnāḥ kṣutpipāsāturāḥ kṛśāḥ 
 yācakāḥ preṣyakāś cāpi sarve te 'mbho'pradānikāḥ  Rm 
 jaladānodbhavaṃ puṇyaṃ saṃkhyātuṃ naiva śakyate 
 sarvair api munīṃdraiś ca kim anyair vibuddhair janaiḥ  Rm 
 matveti śraddhayā nityaṃ divyāmṛtābhivāṃchibhiḥ 
 arthibhyaḥ sarvasatvebhyo dātavyaṃ jalam ādarāt  Rm 
 ity ādiṣṭaṃ munīndreṇa śrutvā sarve ca bhikṣavaḥ 
 sarvebhyaḥ sarvadā kartuṃ jaladānaṃ samaichan  Rm 
 athānandaḥ samutthāya natvā taṃ śrīghanaṃ guruṃ 
 kṛtāṃjalipuṭo pṛchan tatpāpaparimocanaṃ  Rm 
 kadā sā bhagavan pretī tatpāpāt parimokṣyate 
 sarvasatvābhibodhārthaṃ tat samādeṣṭum arhasi  Rm 
 ity ānandena pṛṣṭe 'sau sarvajño bhagavāṃs tadā 
 tam ānaṃdaṃ samārabhya prāha pāpavimocanaṃ  Rm 
 śṛṇv ānaṃda samādhāya yena sā parimokṣyate 
 sarvasatvaprabodhāya tad upāyaiḥ pracakṣyate  Rm 
 sā pretī narakeṣv evaṃ sarveṣu bhramitā sadā 
 duḥkhābhivedanākhinnā paritaptānutāpitā  Rm 
 tataḥ kālāntare saivaṃ smṛtvā ratnatrayaṃ yadi 
 Rm 
 namo buddhāya dharmāya saṃghāyeti vaded yadā  Rm 
 tadā lokeśvaro sarvalokanātho jinātmajaḥ 
 dṛṣṭvā tāṃ sahasopetya svaprabhābhiḥ parispṛśet  Rm 
 yadā lokeśvarābhābhiḥ sparśitā sā sudhī satī 
 tadātisaukhyatāṃ labdhvā vismitaivaṃ vyacintayet  Rm 
 aho saukhyaṃ mayā labdhaṃ kasyānubhāvato 'dhunā 
 kim āhosvid itaś cyutvāgato 'nyatra vasāmy ahaṃ  Rm 
 iti cintāri tiṣṭhantī vismayoddhatamānasīṃ 
 dṛṣṭvā lokeśvaraś caināṃ bodhayitum upācaret  Rm 
 upetya tarpayitvā ca svatanuniḥsṛtair jalaiḥ 
 vividhair bhojanaiś cāpi pratarppayet sa bodhirāṭ  Rm 
 tato 'sau pāpinī pretī pītvā tat tanujāmṛtaṃ 
 paritṛptā viśuddhāṅgā natvā taṃ prārthayet tathā  Rm 
 namas te bhagavan nātha kṛpayā māṃ samuddhara 
 darśaya dharmamārgaṃ me sadā te śaraṇaṃ vraje  Rm 
 tayaivaṃ prārthite cāsau lokanātho dayānidhiḥ 
 darśayitvāryamārgaṃ ca śrāvayed dharmadeśanāṃ  Rm 
 yāṃ śrutvaiva ca sā pretī sarvapāpavimocitā 
 tataś cyutvā viśuddhātmā janma bodhikule labhet  Rm 
 tatra bodhicarīḥ prāptuṃ cared vratam upoṣadhaṃ 
 tadvratapuṇyabhāvaiś ca bodhicaryyāḥ samācaret  Rm 
 kramād bodhicarīḥ pūryya bodhipraṇidhimānasaḥ 
 bodhisatvo mahāsatvo bhaviṣyati na saṃśayaḥ  Rm 
 tato lokahitaṃ kṛtvā saṃbodhipadam āśrayan 
 sarvadā ca sukhaṃ bhuktvā sukhāvatīṃ gamiṣyati 
 tatrāmitābhasaṃbuddhaṃ sevitvā samupāśrayan 
 saṃbodhijñānaṃ āsādya nirvṛtiṃ cāpy avāpsyati  Rm 
 yady asau smarate pretī triratnānāṃ samāhitā 
 tadā caivaṃ tataś cyutvā saukhāvatīṃ gamiṣyati  Rm 
 no ced evaṃ hi sā pretī sadāpi narake vaset 
 yāvan na smarate buddhaṃ tāvan na mokṣyate tataḥ  Rm 
 Rm 
 evaṃ sarve 'pi ye satvā yāvanto narakāsthitāḥ 
 tāvantas te 'pi sarve ca duṣṭāḥ pāpānucārikāḥ  Rm 
 yadaiṣāṃ ye triratnānāṃ smaranty anutāpitāḥ 
 namo buddhāya dharmāya saṃghāyeti vadaṃti ca  Rm 
 tadā tatpāpanirmuktā viśuddhāṅgāḥ śubhāśayāḥ 
 saddharmācaraṇaṃ kartum utsaheyuḥ samāhitāḥ  Rm 
 tato lokeśvaro dṛṣṭvā tān satvān dharmabhājanān 
 bodhayitvā prayatnena bodhimārge niyojayet  Rm 
 tataḥ sarve ca te satvā bodhipraṇidhimānasāḥ 
 sarvasatvahitārthena samicheyuḥ śivāṃ carīṃ  Rm 
 tatas te narakāc cyutvā saṃprayāyuḥ sukhāvatīṃ 
 tatrāmitābhanāthasya dharmaṃ śrutvānumoditāḥ  Rm 
 bodhicaryyāḥ samāśritya kuryur lokahitāni te 
 kramād bodhicarīḥ pūryya sarvakleśavimuktigāḥ  Rm 
 saṃbodhijñānam āsādya nirvṛtiṃ samavāpnuyuḥ 
 evam anye 'pi ye satvā lokeśasaraṇaṃ gatāḥ  Rm 
 te āśu pāpanirmuktāḥ sukhāvatīṃ vrajanti hi 
 ye ye lokeśvaraṃ smṛtvā bhajanti satataṃ mudā 
 te te sarve ca niḥpāpā bhavanti bodhibhāginaḥ  Rm 
 tasmāl lokeśvaraṃ smṛtvā gatvā ca śaraṇaṃ sadā 
 trimaṇḍalaviśuddhena caritavyaṃ vratottamaṃ  Rm 
 vratottamaṃ samākhyātam āryāṣṭāṃgikapoṣādhaṃ 
 sarveṣāṃ api puṇyānāṃ tadvratapuṇyam uttamaṃ  Rm 
 yenaivāśu viśuddhyaṃte ghorapātakināpi ca 
 tasmād etat mahatpuṇyaṃ vratarājaṃ vidur jināḥ  Rm 
 yasya puṇyānubhāvena pūryya pāramitāgaṇāḥ 
 sarvakleśān vinirjitya śīghraṃ bodhim avāpnuyuḥ  Rm 
 ye 'py atītāś ca saṃbuddhāḥ sarvajñāḥ sugatā jināḥ 
 te 'pi tadvratapuṇyais tu śīghraṃ bodhim avāpnuvan  Rm 
 ye 'py etarhi ca saṃbuddhāḥ saṃbodhidharmadeśakāḥ 
 Rm 
 te 'py etadvratapuṇyaiś ca bhavanti bodhipāragāḥ  Rm 
 ye cāpy anāgatā buddhā bhaviṣyanti tathāgatāḥ 
 te 'py etadvratapuṇyais tu lapsyante bodhisaṃpadaṃ  Rm 
 evam anye 'pi ye prājñāḥ saṃbodhipadavāṃchitāḥ 
 te 'py etadvratam ādhāya labhanti bodhisaṃpadaṃ  Rm 
 tasmād etadvrataṃ dhṛtvā dātavyaṃ dānam adarāt 
 etat phalaṃ sadākṣīṇaṃ sūte kalpatarur yathā  Rm 
 etadvratadharāḥ satvāḥ saddharmācaraṇodyatāḥ 
 sarvathā na vrajaṃty eva durgatiṣu kadācana  Rm 
 sadaiva sugatiṃ prāptāḥ sarvasatvānukaṃpinaḥ 
 saddharmācaraṇaṃ dhṛtvā bodhisatvā bhavanti te  Rm 
 ye ca lokeśvaraṃ smṛtvā caranty etadvrataṃ sadā 
 te paśyanti sadāpy enaṃ lokanāthaṃ jagatprabhuṃ  Rm 
 tena lokeśvareṇāpi dṛśyaṃte te 'pi sarvadā 
 ye ca lokeśasaṃdṛṣṭās te sarve bodhibhāginaḥ  Rm 
 bodhisatvā mahāsatvāḥ saṃbodhiṃ samavāpnuyuḥ 
 ye smaranti sadā nityaṃ lokeśaṃ karuṇāmayaṃ 
 sahasā durgatiṃ tyaktvā muktvā yāyuḥ sukhāvatīṃ  Rm 
 ye ca taccharaṇaṃ gatvā bhajaṃti taṃ jinātmajaṃ 
 sarvapāpavinirmuktās te 'pi yāyuḥ sukhāvatiṃ  Rm 
 ye sugandhair jalaiḥ śuddhaiḥ snāpayanti jagadguruṃ 
 mandākinyāṃ ca te snātvā śuddhā yāṃti sukhāvatiṃ  Rm 
 paṃcagaṃdhādisaurabhyair lokeśaṃ lepayaṃti ye 
 cakravarttipadaṃ bhuktvā te 'pi yāṃti sukhāvatīṃ  Rm 
 cīvaraṃ ye dadaṃty asmai te divyavastrasaṃyutāḥ 
 sarvadharmādhināthāś ca yāṃti cāṃte sukhāvatīṃ  Rm 
 satkṛtya śraddhayā ye 'pi puṣpais tam arcayanti ye 
 Rm 
 te surendrapadaṃ prāpya yānti cānte sukhāvatīṃ  Rm 
 saurabhyayojitair dhūpair ye bhajanti tam īśvaraṃ 
 te narendrapadaṃ bhuktvā yāṃti cānte sukhāvatiṃ  Rm 
 ye dadanti ca bhaiṣajyaṃ tasmai lokādhipāya ca 
 cakravarttipadaṃ prāpya yāṃti te ca sukhāvatīṃ  Rm 
 ye dadanti pradīpāni tasmai lokeśvarāya ca 
 te mahendrapadaṃ bhuktvā yānti cānte sukhāvatīṃ  Rm 
 naivedyaṃ ye dadanty asmai te bhavanti nareśvarāḥ 
 divyabhogyāni bhuktvā ca yānti cānte sukhāvatīṃ  Rm 
 ye ca pānaṃ dadanty asmai te pītvā satataṃ sudhāṃ 
 svarge ramanti devendrā yānti cānte sukhāvatīṃ  Rm 
 phalamūlādikaṃ dattaṃ yaiś ca tasmai sutāyine 
 yathepsitasukhaṃ bhuktvāṃte 'pi yāṃti sukhāvatīṃ  Rm 
 tāmbūlaṃ pūgasaṃyuktaṃ lokeśāya dadanti ye 
 surūpāḥ satsukhaṃ bhuktvāṃte 'pi yānti sukhāvatīṃ  Rm 
 śayyāsanaṃ pradattaṃ yais tasmai satvānukaṃpine 
 te kṣitīśaśriyaṃ bhuktvā yānty aṃte ca sukhāvatīṃ  Rm 
 siṃhāsanaṃ pradattaṃ yais tasmai dharmānuśāsine 
 te vaṃdyāḥ sarvalokaiś ca yānty ante ca sukhāvatīṃ  Rm 
 chatraṃ tasmai pradattaṃ yais te nṛpāś cakravarttinaḥ 
 yaśodharmasukhaṃ bhuktvā saṃprayānti sukhāvatīṃ  Rm 
 patākāṃ ye prayachanti tasmai lokādhipāya cā 
 te 'pi sarvāṃ mahīṃ bhuktvā yānti cānte sukhāvatīṃ  Rm 
 tasmai ye ca prayachanti dhāturatnagaṇāni ca 
 te narendrāś caturdvīpāṃ bhuktvā yānti sukhāvatīṃ  Rm 
 ye vitānaṃ vitanvaṃti gehe tasya kṛpānidheḥ 
 te narendrāḥ surendrāś ca bhūtvā yāṃti sukhāvatīṃ  Rm 
 trailokyādhipates tasya ye kurvanti pradakṣiṇāṃ 
 te narendraśriyaṃ bhuktvā yānti cānte sukhāvatīṃ  Rm 
 saṃgītair ye prakurvanti pūjāṃ tasya jagat prabhoḥ 
 sadā subhāṣitāny eva śṛṇvanti te guṇākarāḥ  Rm 
 cāmarair vyajanair vāpi taṃ nāthaṃ vījayanti ye 
 Rm 
 te nṛpāḥ suralakṣmīṃ ca bhuktvā yāṃti jinālaye  Rm 
 śodhayanti ca ye nityaṃ vihāre kāruṇānidheḥ 
 divyanetrāś ca te saukhyaṃ bhuktvā yāṃti surālayaṃ  Rm 
 kṛtvā ramyaṃ vihāraṃ ca lokeśāya dadanti ye 
 te mahendraśriyaṃ bhuktvā saṃprayānti sukhāvatīṃ  Rm 
 vihāre tatra saṃsiddhe yaṣṭim āropya ye narāḥ 
 suvarṇakalaśāṃś chatradhvajaghaṇṭāvalīyutān  Rm 
 paṃcavarṇapatākābhiḥ puṣpasragbhiś ca saṃyutān 
 saṃpratisthāṃ prakurvati mahotsāhair vidhānataḥ  Rm 
 te narendrāḥ surendrāś ca yaśodharmasukhānvitāḥ 
 māheśvaryyaśriyaṃ bhuktva yānti cānte sukhāvatīṃ  Rm 
 padyagadyamayaiḥ stotrair ye stuvaṃti taṃ īśvaraṃ 
 niḥpāpāḥ sukhinaḥ prājñās te prayānti sukhāvatīṃ  Rm 
 ye cāṣṭāṃgapraṇāmāni asmai śāstre prakurvaṃte 
 cakravartīpadaṃ bhuktvā te prayānti jinālayaṃ  Rm 
 ye smaranti sadā nityaṃ tam īśaṃ sugatātmajaṃ 
 te sadyaḥ pāpanirmuktā ante yānti sukhāvatīṃ  Rm 
 ye ye satvāś ca taṃ nāthaṃ smṛtvā bhajanti sarvadā 
 te te sarve na yānty eva durgatiṣu kadācana  Rm 
 sadāpi sadgatiṣv eva yātāḥ saukhyasamanvitāḥ 
 saddharmācaraṇaṃ kṛtvā saṃprayānti sukhāvatīṃ  Rm 
 evaṃ ye pāpinaś cāpi lokeśaṃ śaraṇaṃ gatāḥ 
 te 'pi pāpavinirmuktāḥ śuddhā yāṃti jinālayaṃ  Rm 
 evaṃ lokeśvaro nāthaḥ puṇyakṣetraṃ śubhapradaḥ 
 ciṃtāmaṇiḥ kalpavṛkṣo yathepsitaphalapradaḥ  Rm 
 Rm 
 na hi tena samaḥ kaścin mahatpuṇyaphalapradaḥ 
 kuto 'dhikas tu vidyeta traidhātubhuvaneṣv api  Rm 
 tenaiva sakalāḥ satvā bodhayitvā prayatnataḥ 
 āryyamārge pratiṣṭhāpya preritā nirvṛtāv api  Rm 
 pāpiṣṭho api satvāś ca tenopetya svayaṃ tathā 
 narakebhyaḥ samuddhṛtya saṃpreritāḥ sukhāvatīṃ  Rm 
 evaṃ sarve 'pi satvāś ca nānopāyavidhānataḥ 
 darśayitvāryyamārgāṇi tena bodhau niveśitāḥ  Rm 
 tasmāt sarvādhikeśaḥ sa lokeśvaro maheśvaraḥ 
 sarvadharmānubhartā sa lokanāthaḥ pratīyate 
 kenāpi gaṃtuṃ tasya puṇyaskaṃdhaṃ na śakyate 
 mayāpi śakyate naivaṃ sarvaiś cāpi munīśvaraiḥ 
 evaṃ matvā tvam ānaṃdaḥ lokanathaṃ dayodadhiṃ  Rm 
 sarvadevādhideveśaṃ smṛtvaiva satataṃ bhaja 
 tatas te maṃgalaṃ nityaṃ sarvadāpi samaṃtataḥ  Rm 
 kutaś cin naiva vidyeran bhayāni vividhāny api 
 yatra lokeśvarasmṛtis tatrotpātabhayaṃ na hi  Rm 
 agner api bhayaṃ naiva nāpy utpātamarudbhayaṃ 
 na codakabhayaṃ tatra na ca bhūmibhayaṃ khalu  Rm 
 vidyutpātabhayaṃ nāpi na cāśanibhayaṃ sadā 
 na ca śatrubhayaṃ kvāpi nāpi rājabhayaṃ tathā  Rm 
 na ca caurabhayāny evaṃ na ca rogabhayāni ca 
 sarvabhayaḥ praśāmyante lokeśasmṛtibhāvataḥ  Rm 
 sarve 'py upadravāś caivaṃ prayāṃti vilayaṃ tataḥ 
 evaṃ lokeśvaro nātho mahatpuṇyānubhāvavān  Rm 
 yenaivaṃ trijagallokaṃ pālitaṃ putravat sadā 
 tasmāl lokeśvaro nityaṃ sevitavyaḥ śubhārthibhiḥ  Rm 
 yasya dharmānubhāvena sarvatrāpi śivaṃ sadā 
 iti matvā tvayānaṃda tad dharmāñ chrāvayan sadā  Rm 
 prerayitvā ca tadbhaktau saṃbodhau saṃpraveśaya 
 Rm 
 etatpuṇyānubhāvais tvam apy evaṃ kuśalī bhavan  Rm 
 bodhisatvo mahāsatvo bhaven nūnaṃ jinātmajaḥ  Rm 
 ity ādiṣṭaṃ munīndreṇa śrutvānaṃdaḥ sasāṃghikaḥ 
 tatheti pratimoditvā sadā lokeśam asmarat  Rm 
 evaṃ rājaṃs tvayā cāpi smṛtvā lokeśvaraḥ sadā 
 sevitavyaḥ prayatnena bodhipraṇidhicetasā  Rm 
 tatas tvaṃ sahasā sarvapāpebhyaḥ parimocitaḥ 
 bodhisatvo viśuddhātmā prayāsyasi sukhāvatīṃ  Rm 
 ity evaṃ guruṇādiṣṭaṃ upaguptena dhīmatā 
 śrutvā rājānumoditvā so 'bhyanandat sapārṣadaḥ  Rm 
 idaṃ śrutvāvadānaṃ ye śrāvayitvā parān api 
 bhajaṃti lokanāthaṃ te saṃprayāyuḥ sukhāvatīṃ  Rm 
  iti ratnāvadānamālāyaṃ pretikāvadānaṃ samāptam 
 Rm 
 V Śālapuṣpāvadāna
 athāśoko mahīpālo bhūyaḥ śrotuṃ subhāsitaiḥ 
 upaguptaṃ guruṃ natvā kṛtāṃjalir avocat  Rm 
 bhadanta śrotum ichāmi punar anyat subhāṣitaṃ 
 tad arhasi samādeṣṭuṃ lokānāṃ puṇyavṛddhaye  Rm 
 iti vijñāpite tena nṛpendreṇa prasādinā 
 upagupto yatiś cāpi taṃ nṛpaṃ pratyabhāṣata  Rm 
 śṛṇu rājan mahābhāga sarvalokahitārthabhṛt 
 yathā me guruṇādiṣṭaṃ vakṣye 'haṃ te tathā khalu  Rm 
 puraikasamaye buddho bhagavāñ chrīghano jinaḥ 
 śrāvastyāṃ jetakāraṇye vihāre maṇimaṇḍite  Rm 
 śrāvakair bhikṣubhiḥ saṃghair bodhisatvagaṇaiḥ saha 
 saddharmadeśanāṃ kartuṃ vyaharal lokaśāsituṃ  Rm 
 taddharmadeśanāṃ śrotuṃ sarve satvāḥ samāgatāḥ 
 brāhmaṇāḥ kṣatriyāś cāpi rājāno rājamātrikāḥ  Rm 
 vaiśyāḥ śūdrā amātyāś ca maṃtriṇaḥ sādhavo janāḥ 
 śreṣṭhinaḥ sārthavāhāś ca dhaninaś ca vaṇiggaṇāḥ  Rm 
 paurājānapadāś cāpi nānādeśasamāgatāḥ 
 devā daityāś ca gandharvā yakṣakinnararākṣasāḥ  Rm 
 siddhāvidyādharāḥ sādhyā vasavaś ca grahādhipāḥ 
 nāgeṃdrā garuḍāś caivam ṛṣayo brahmacāriṇāḥ  Rm 
 yogino yatayaś cāpi lokapālāḥ sasainyakāḥ 
 sarve taṃ sugataṃ natvā dharmaṃ śrotum upāgatāḥ  Rm 
 satkṛtya pūjayitvā ca kṛtāṃjalipuṭo mudā 
 parivṛtya puraskṛtya dṛṣṭvā tasthuḥ samāhitāḥ  Rm 
 athāsau bhagavān dṛṣṭvā tān sarvān dharmavāṃchinaḥ 
 ādimadhyāntakalyāṇaṃ dideśa dharmam uttamaṃ  Rm 
 tatra devādayaḥ sarve tat saddharmāmṛtaṃ mudā 
 pītvā cābhyanumodantaḥ prāpur jñānaviśeṣatāṃ  Rm 
 Rm 
 śrāvasteyāt tadāneke dārikā dārakāś ca te 
 kusumān yācitaṃ śālabhaṃjikākhyaṃ giriṃ yayuḥ  Rm 
 tatra te sahasā gatvā dṛṣṭvā puṣpāṇy anekaśaḥ 
 prādāya samupāgatvā śrāvastyām acaran mudā  Rm 
 tatraikā dārikā vālā śreṣṭhiputrī pramoditā 
 śanaiḥ sā śālapuṣpāṇi prādāya pṛṣṭhato 'carat  Rm 
 tadā ca bhagāvān buddho bhikṣusaṃghasamanvitaḥ 
 śrāvastyāṃ bhojanaṃ bhuktvā tato bahir viniryayau  Rm 
 tatra sā dārikādrākṣīd bhagavantaṃ tam āgataṃ 
 dvātriṃśal lakṣaṇāśītivyaṃjanaṃ samalaṃkṛtaṃ  Rm 
 vyāmaprabhāvirājantaṃ sahasreṇādhikaprabhaṃ 
 jaṃgamam iva ratnāṅgaṃ samantabhadrarūpikaṃ  Rm 
 dṛṣṭvaivaṃ śrīghanaṃ nāthaṃ dārikā sā pramoditā 
 śraddhayārcayituṃ puṣpair manasaivaṃ vyaciṃtayat  Rm 
 aho puṇyaṃ mayā labdhaṃ yat saṃbuddho dṛśyate 'dhunā 
 evaṃ kadā kathaṃ kutra drakṣyate 'yaṃ munīśvaraḥ  Rm 
 bhāgyenaivaṃ mayā labdhaṃ saṃbuddhadarśanaṃ tathā 
 nūnaṃ bhāgyavatī cāsmi yat puṇyanidhir āpyate  Rm 
 tasmāt puṇyaṃ mahāratnaṃ prāptum upetya sādaraṃ 
 etaiś ca kusumaiḥ sarvair arhāmy etaṃ samarcituṃ  Rm 
 kadāyaṃ lapsyate bhūyaḥ paravaśyā striyā mayā 
 tad ahaṃ sahasopetya puṣpāṇy asmāy upākire  Rm 
 sadā notpadyate nātra saṃbuddho hi kadā cana 
 atisudurllabhaṃ hy asya darśanaṃ ca sadā na hi  Rm 
 mānuṣyaṃ durllabhaṃ janma vinā puṇyair na labhyate 
 mānuṣye 'labhyamāne 'pi saṃbuddhe sevyate kathaṃ  Rm 
 mānuṣye labhyamāne 'pi kṣaṇaṃ saṃpat sudurllabhā 
 narair apy akṣaṇaprāptaiḥ kathaṃ buddhe 'nusevyate  Rm 
 tad adya mānuṣī bhūtvā prāpyaivaṃ sukṛtau kṣaṇaṃ 
 yady atra kusumair ebhiḥ saṃbuddhaṃ nārcayāmy ahaṃ  Rm 
 Rm 
 tato me niṣphalaṃ janma mānuṣye vyartham eva hi 
 kiṃ mamānena dehena sarvathaikāntanāśinā  Rm 
 kim anenāpi jīvena mṛtyau nityaṃ puraḥsthite 
 kiyat kālaṃ ca jīveyaṃ gacheyaṃ maraṇaṃ dhruvaṃ  Rm 
 ciraṃ sthitvāpi kiṃ sāraṃ saṃbuddhabhajanaṃ vinā 
 varaṃ prāṇaparityāgaṃ kṛtvā saṃbuddhadarśanaṃ  Rm 
 anityaṃ khalu saṃsāraṃ sarvadehādikaṃ dhanaṃ 
 etad eva tu satsāraṃ yad buddhe bhajanaṃ sadā  Rm 
 tadaitaiḥ kusumaiḥ sarvaiḥ pūjayāmi munīśvaraṃ 
 kathaṃ na pūjayisyāmi saṃbuddhaṃ trijagadguruṃ  Rm 
 iti niścitya sā vālā dṛṣṭvā taṃ sugataṃ mudā 
 sahasopetya taiḥ sarvaiḥ sālapuṣpair avākiran  Rm 
 tataḥ pradakṣiṇīkṛtya praṇamya taṃ praharṣitā 
 kiṃ cid dūre parāvṛtya tasthau dṛṣṭvā muniṃ mudā  Rm 
 tato 'sau bhagavān buddhas tasyā āyurvihīnatāṃ 
 matvā tāṃ saṃnrīksyaivaṃ svaṃ vihāraṃ samāyayau  Rm 
 atha sā dārikā bhūyas tathānyatkusumāni ca 
 gṛhasyārthe samādātuṃ tataḥ śālavanaṃ yayau  Rm 
 tatra śālataruṃ dṛṣṭvā praphullakusumānvitaṃ 
 tatpuṣpāṇi samācetuṃ sahasā sā ruroha taṃ  Rm 
 tatrāvaruhya puṣpāṇi cinvantī sā pramodataḥ 
 agraśākhāsamārūḍhā papāta sahasā tataḥ  Rm 
 patitā sā virugnāṅgā tīvrātivedanāturā 
 hā hatāsmīti niścitya saṃbuddhasmaraṇaṃ vyadhāt  Rm 
 namo buddhāya dharmāya saṃghāya sugatāya ca 
 iti proktvaiva saṃbuddhaṃ smaranti maraṇaṃ yayau  Rm 
 tataḥ svargopapannā sā vismitaivaṃ vyacintayat 
 kutaś cyutvā kuhotpannā kena vā kuśalena ca  Rm 
 iti cintāparītā sā sahasaivaṃ vyabuddhyata 
 martyāc cyutvāgatā svarge buddhe puṣpapradānataḥ  Rm 
 iti buddhvā ca sā bhadrā suprasāditamānasī 
 tam eva sugataṃ nāthaṃ smṛtvā natvābhyanandata  Rm 
 Rm 
 tato devair upanītaṃ divyapuṣpasvalaṃkṛtaṃ
