 vimānaṃ sā samāruhya devasabhām upāyayau  Rm 
 tasmiṃś ca samaye śakraḥ sudharmāyāṃ suraiḥ saha 
 saṃbuddhavarṇanāṃ kṛtvā tasthau devān pramodayan  Rm 
 tathā tāṃ samupāyātāṃ śālapuṣpābhyalaṃkṛtāṃ 
 dṛṣṭvā divyātivarṇābhāṃ papracha vismito hariḥ  Rm 
 gātraṃ kena vimṛṣṭakāṃcananibhaṃ padmotpalābhaṃ tava 
 divyaśrīr atulākṛteyam iha te kena prabhā niḥsṛtā 
 vaktraṃ kena vibuddhapadmasadṛśaṃ cāmīkarābhaṃ tava 
 kasya tvaṃ varadevate phalam idaṃ yat karmajaṃ bhujyate  Rm 
 iti prokte surendreṇa sā bhadrā devakanyakā 
 taṃ devādhipatiṃ natvā kṛtāṃjalipuṭo 'bravīt  Rm 
 saśrāvakā narāditya ākīrṇaśālapuṣpakaiḥ 
 tatkarmakuśalaṃ kṛtvā rājate me 'dhikaṃ tanuḥ  Rm 
 jalajenduviśuddhābhaṃ vadanaṃ me 'bhirocate 
 etatkarmānubhāvena vijānīyāḥ sureśvara  Rm 
 tayeti proditaṃ śrutvā devendro 'sau suvismitaḥ 
 dṛṣṭvā caināṃ subhadrāṅgīṃ praharṣayann abhāṣata  Rm 
 aho guṇamayaṃ kṣetraṃ sarvadoṣavivarjitaṃ 
 yatra nyastaṃ tvayā vījam itthaṃ svargopapattaye  Rm 
 ko nārcayet pravarakāṃcanarāśigauraṃ buddhaṃ vibuddhakamalāyatapatranetraṃ 
 yatrādhikārajanitāni viśobhitāni kāṃtāmukhāni kamalāyatalocanāni  Rm 
 dhanyo 'si tvaṃ subhadrāṃgi saṃbuddhaguṇabhāvini 
 sarvathā hi sa saṃbuddhaḥ sevitavyaḥ sadāpi ca  Rm 
 yasya puṇyaprasādāt tvaṃ sadyaḥ svarge samāgatā 
 sa eva bhagavān nāthaḥ saṃsmṛtvā sevyatāṃ sadā  Rm 
 tatas te sarvadā nityaṃ maṃgalaṃ syāt samaṃtataḥ 
 ciraṃ divyasukhaṃ bhuktvā yāyāś cānte sukhāvatīṃ  Rm 
 ity ādiṣṭaṃ surendreṇa sā devakanyakā sudhīḥ 
 anumodya ca taṃ śakraṃ natvā svam ālayaṃ yayau  Rm 
 Rm 
 tataḥ sā saṃsthitā devīprāsāde divyamaṇḍite 
 divyabhogyasukhaprāptā moditvaivaṃ vyacintayet  Rm 
 yac cyutvāhaṃ manuṣyebhyo 'dhunā svargasamāgatā 
 tat saṃbuddhaprasādena jānāmi nānyathā khalu  Rm 
 yan mayā pūjito buddhaḥ śālapuṣpair vanodbhāvaiḥ 
 tatpuṇyaphalabhogyārthe āgatāhaṃ surālayaṃ  Rm 
 yad divyasukhasaṃprāptaṃ tat saṃbuddhaprasādataḥ 
 tena tam evaṃ saṃbuddhaṃ punar gacheya vaṃdituṃ  Rm 
 na yuktaṃ saugate gantuṃ paryyuṣitena vāsasā 
 yuktaṃ tu saugate gaṃtum aparyuṣitavāsasā  Rm 
 iti sā manasā matvā devakanyā subhadrikā 
 snātvā saurabhyaliptāṃgā divyaśuddhāmvarāvṛtā  Rm 
 divyālaṃkāramālādimaulīkuṇḍalamaṃḍitā 
 anekadevakanyābhir apsarobhiḥ samanvitā  Rm 
 divyapūjopacārāṇi gṛhītvā sahasā yayau 
 tasyām eva niśi svarddhyā bhāsayantī samaṃtataḥ  Rm 
 jetavanam upetyāsau praviveśa jinālayaṃ 
 tataḥ pradakṣiṇaṃ kṛtvā praṇamya caraṇau muneḥ  Rm 
 paṃcopahārapūjābhiḥ pūjayitvā kṛtāṃjaliḥ 
 natvā ca purataḥ tasthau saddharmaśravaṇotsukā  Rm 
 athāsau bhagavāṃs tasyā jñātvāśayaviśuddhatāṃ 
 ādimadhyāntakalyāṇaṃ dideśa dharmam uttamaṃ  Rm 
 catvāri cāryyasatyāni niḥkleśapuṇyalabdhaye 
 daśakuśalamūlāni samyaksatvaviśuddhaye  Rm 
 āryyāṣṭāṅgikamārgāṃś ca saṃbodhimārgalabdhaye 
 bodhipākṣikadharmāṃś ca saṃbuddhaguṇalabdhaye  Rm 
 athāsau devakanyā tāṃ saddharmadeśaṇaṃ muneḥ 
 śrutvānumoditā cāpi prāpya dharmaviśeṣatāṃ  Rm 
 jñānavajreṇa satkāyadṛṣṭiśailaṃ vibheda sā 
 śrotāpattiphalaṃ prāptā dṛṣṭasatyābhavat tadā  Rm 
 tato bhūyaḥ praṇamyaivaṃ bhagavantaṃ kṛtāṃjaliḥ 
 suprasannamukhāmbhojo trir udānam udāharat  Rm 
 Rm 
 bhagavann idam asmākaṃ mahāpuṇyasukhodayaṃ 
 jananyāpi kṛtaṃ nāpi na pitrā na ca vaṃdhubhiḥ  Rm 
 na jñātibhir na mitraiś ca na sahāyasuhṛjjanaiḥ 
 nāpi sālohitaiś cāpi pitṛlokair na cāparaiḥ  Rm 
 na rājñā na cāmātyair na maṃtribhir na ca paurikaiḥ 
 na gurubhir na vipraiś ca na yatibhir na tāpasaiḥ  Rm 
 na devair nāpi daityaiś ca nāpi lokādhipair api 
 tathānyaiś ca kṛtaṃ naiva yad idaṃ bhavatā kṛtaṃ  Rm 
 uchoṣito yad asmākaṃ rudhirāśrusaritpatiḥ 
 asthimayo mahāchailo yad asmābhiś ca laṃghitaḥ  Rm 
 tavānubhāvāt pihitaḥ sughoro hy apāyamārgo bahudoṣayuktaḥ 
 apāvṛtā svargagatiḥ supuṇyā nirvāṇamārgaś ca mayopalabdhaḥ  Rm 
 bhavatprasādān nirupetadoṣaṃ mayādya labdhaṃ suviśuddhacakṣuḥ 
 prāptaṃ ca śāntaṃ padam āryyakāntaṃ tīrṇaś ca duḥkhārṇavapāram asmi  Rm 
 naravarendrasurāsurapūjite vigatajanmajarāmaraṇādayaḥ 
 bhavasahasrasudullabhadarśane saphalam adya mune tava darśanaṃ  Rm 
 tataḥ praṇatvā caraṇāraviṃdau muneḥ prakṛtvā tṛpradakṣiṇāṃ ca 
 prajātaharṣā sugataṃ jineṃdraṃ smṛtvā ca bhūyo divam āyayau sā  Rm 
 tathā svargasamāyātā devakanyā mumoda sā 
 yathā vaṇig labdhalābho rogamukto yathāturaḥ  Rm 
 samyagniṣpannaśasyāpto yathā ca kṛṣikārmikaḥ 
 siddhayātrāpralabdhārthaḥ sārthavāho vaṇig yathā  Rm 
 atha te bhikṣavaḥ sarve dṛṣṭvaivam avabhāsitaṃ 
 saṃdigdhavismitāś caivaṃ paprachus taṃ munīśvarāṃ  Rm 
 bhagavann adya rātrau ko bhavato 'ntikam āgataḥ 
 brahmā vā surarājo vā lokapālagaṇā api  Rm 
 asmābhir jñāyate nāyaṃ yo 'dya rātrāv ihāgataḥ 
 Rm 
 tad asmān vismitān sarvān bodhayituṃ samarhasi  Rm 
 iti tair bhikṣubhiḥ pṛṣṭo bhagavān sa munīśvaraḥ 
 tāṃś ca bhikṣugaṇān sarvān samāmaṃtryābravīt tathā  Rm 
 na hi sa bhikṣavo brahmā nāpi vāsau surādhipaḥ 
 naiva lokādhipālāś ca yādya rātrāv ihāgatā  Rm 
 api tu dārikā dṛṣṭā yuṣmābhiḥ sagatā pathi 
 yayāhaṃ sālapuṣpaiś ca prāvakīryyābhitoṣitaḥ  Rm 
 sā māṃ puṣpair avākīryya gṛhasyārthe punar vanaṃ 
 gatā puṣpāṇy upāhartuṃ vṛkṣārūḍhāpatat taroḥ  Rm 
 tato 'sau patanodvignā vedanākrāṃtacetasā 
 triratnāni smaranty eva dehaṃ tyaktvā divaṃ yayau  Rm 
 tatra svarge samāsādya smṛtva māṃ sugataṃ punaḥ 
 draṣṭuṃ dharmaṃ ca me śrotum ihāsau samupāgatā  Rm 
 tan mayā deśitaṃ tasyai saṃbodhidharmam uttamaṃ 
 śrutvā sā cānumodyaivaṃ saṃharṣitā divaṃ yayau  Rm 
 ity evaṃ bhikṣavo matvā triratnāni śubhārthibhiḥ 
 sevitavyāni saṃsmṛtvā gatvā ca śaraṇaṃ sadā  Rm 
 ye bhajanti triratnāni saṃsmṛtvā śaraṇaṃ gatāḥ 
 durgatiṃ te na gachaṃti vrajanti sadgatiṃ sadā  Rm 
 ye nindanti triratnāni pratikṣipya pramādataḥ 
 sadgatiṃ te na gachanti vasanti narake sadā  Rm 
 tasmān nityāṃ triratnāni saṃsmṛtvā śaraṇaṃ gatāḥ 
 satkṛtya bhāvayitvā ca bhajadhvaṃ bodhivāṃchayā  Rm 
 tathā vo maṅgalaṃ nityaṃ sarvatra sarvadā bhavet 
 kramād bodhicarīṃ pūrya saṃbodhim api lapsyatha  Rm 
 ity ādiṣṭaṃ munīndreṇa śrutvā te bhikṣavo mudā 
 tathety abhyanumodantas triratnāni sadābhajan  Rm 
 ity evaṃ guruṇādiṣṭaṃ mayaivaṃ te pracakṣyate 
 śrutvaitac chrāvayitvā ca triratnāni sadā bhaja  Rm 
 tatas tvaṃ kramaśaś caiva bodhicaryāṃ samācaran 
 sarvapāpavinirmuktaḥ sukhāvatīṃ samāvrajeḥ  Rm 
 ity etad guruṇādiṣṭaṃ upaguptena bhikṣuṇā 
 Rm 
 śrutvā rājā tathety evam abhyanandat sapārṣadaḥ  Rm 
 tat saṃbuddhānubhāvaṃ munivarakathitaṃ śālapuṣpāvadānaṃ 
 ye śrutvā śrāvayanti pramuditamanasaḥ śraddhayā bodhikāmāḥ 
 te sarvakleśamuktāḥ sakalaguṇadharā bodhicaryyānuraktāḥ 
 kṛtvā loke hitārthaṃ jinavaravasatiṃ saṃprayaṃti praharṣaiḥ  Rm 
  iti śālapuṣpāvadānaṃ samāptaṃ 
 Rm 
 VI Sūkaryavadāna
 punar evaṃ yatīśo 'sāv upagupto jināṃśajaḥ 
 triratnasmṛtijaṃ puṇyaṃ khyātuṃ nṛpam abravīt  Rm 
 mahatpuṇyānubhāvatvaṃ triratnasmṛtisaṃbhavaṃ 
 tad ahaṃ te pravakṣyāmi śṛṇu rājan samāhitaḥ  Rm 
 dharmatā khalu devānāṃ svargacyavanadharmmiṇāṃ 
 paṃcapūrvanimittāni prādurbhaveyur ātmani  Rm 
 akliṣṭāni hi vāsāṃsi kliśyeyuś cyavanāntike 
 amlānāni ca mālyāni mlāyeran sahasā khalu  Rm 
 daurgandhaṃ niḥsared dehāt kakṣābhyāṃ sveda udbhavet 
 pracyutisamaye prāpte svāsane na dhṛtiṃ labhet  Rm 
 etatpaṃcanimittāni svargāc cyavanadharmiṇāṃ 
 sarveṣāṃ prodbhaveyuś ca pracyutisamayāgame  Rm 
 puraikadevaputrasya tathā cyavanadharmiṇaḥ 
 etatpaṃcanimittāni prādur āsaṃś cyuteḥ puraḥ  Rm 
 atha cyavanadharmāsau devaputro viṣāditaḥ 
 avaśyaṃ cyavanaṃ svargān matvā rautsīd adhīritaḥ  Rm 
 āvartya svavimānasthaḥ parivarttya vimūrchitaḥ 
 punaś caitanyam āsādya vilapaṃ paryyadevataḥ  Rm 
 hā mandākini hemāvjavyāpte puṇyāmbuvāhini 
 tvayi snātvapy ahaṃ cyutvā yāsyāmi durgatiṃ kathaṃ  Rm 
 hā caitraratham utsṛjya kva krīḍeyaṃ yathechayā 
 hā nandanavanaṃ ramyaṃ tyaktvāhaṃ kva rameya ca  Rm 
 hā miśrikāvanaṃ divyaṃ tyaktvā ramye kuhādhunā 
 hā pāruṣyavanaṃ tyaktvā kva ramyāmy apsarogaṇaiḥ  Rm 
 kva sukhaṃ lapsyate pāṇḍukaṃvalakaśilāṃ vinā 
 Rm 
 hā devasamitiṃ tyaktvā kva śroṣyāmi subhāṣitāṃ  Rm 
 hā hā sudarśanaṃ ramyaṃ puraṃ tyaktvā vraje cyutaḥ 
 prāsādaṃ vaijayaṃtañ ca kadā drakṣyāmy ahaṃ punaḥ  Rm 
 hā śakrapramukhair devaiḥ sārddhaṃ kṛdāpramoditaḥ 
 adhunā me kva tat saukhyaṃ śrotuṃ cāpi na lapsyate  Rm 
 hā devyam amṛtaṃ tyaktvā kiṃ prabhokṣyāmi sāṃprataṃ 
 divyakāmasukhaṃ bhuktvā punar durgatim āśrayan  Rm 
 kiyad duḥkhaṃ ca saṃbhoktuṃ yāsyāmi narakeṣv ahaṃ 
 etad divyamahotsāhād bhraṣṭo 'haṃ narake gataḥ  Rm 
 mahadduḥkhābhisaṃtaptaḥ sahiṣyāmi kathaṃ tadā 
 hā hato 'smi svapāpena kiṃ pāpaṃ prakṛtaṃ mayā  Rm 
 yenetaḥ svargataś cyutvā punar yāsyāmi nārakān kiṃ 
 upāyaṃ kariṣyāmi na yāyāṃ yena durgatiṃ  Rm 
 ko me śāstātra vidyeta yo māṃ dharme niyojayet 
 dharmeṇa rakṣyate prāṇī narake saṃsthito 'pi ca  Rm 
 dharmaṃ vinātra devo 'pi svargāt prabhransyate punaḥ 
 kiṃ karomi kva yāsyāmi nātropāyaṃ tu manyate  Rm 
 sarvathāham itaś cyutvā gacheyaṃ durgatiṃ khalu 
 itaś cyutasya me janma labdhavyaṃ bhuvane kuha  Rm 
 iti dhairyaṃ samādhāya manasaivaṃ vyalokayat 
 cyutvetaḥ saukaraṃ janma prāptavyaṃ saptame dine  Rm 
 evaṃ svāptagatiṃ dṛṣṭvā papāta savimūrchitaḥ 
 athādrākṣīn mahendras taṃ patitaṃ bhuvi mūrchitaṃ  Rm 
 dṛṣṭvā ca sahasopetya sudhāsekair asiṃcayat 
 tato 'sau cetanāṃ labdhvā śanair utthāya taṃ prabhuṃ  Rm 
 dṛṣṭvā pādau pariṣvajya natvaivaṃ prārthayad rudan 
 hā hā nātha mahendro 'si sarvalokādhipaḥ prabhuḥ  Rm 
 mām adhaḥ patitaṃ dṛṣṭvā nopekṣāṃ kartum arhasi 
 Rm 
 bhavān hi jagatāṃ rājā svāmī bharttā patiḥ prabhuḥ  Rm 
 nātho dharmānuśāstā ca tan māṃ rakṣatum arhasi 
 tvadṛte 'nyo na me kaścid rakṣako vidyate 'tra hi  Rm 
 tad anukaṃpayā dṛṣṭyā dhṛtvā mām uddhara prabho 
 yadi māṃ rakṣituṃ nātha na śaknoti bhavān api  Rm 
 ko māṃ samuddhared anyo hā hato narake vraje 
 maṃḍākinyāṃ tvayā sārddhaṃ snātvā pūtātmako 'py ahaṃ  Rm 
 kathaṃ ca narake gatvā vaseyam aśuciṃ caran 
 sahāpsarogaṇair nityaṃ caritvā naṃdane vane  Rm 
 divyasaṃgītivādyaiś ca ramāmi saṃpramoditaḥ 
 adyetaḥ patito pṛthvyāṃ rājagṛhopajāṃgale  Rm 
 saukaraṃ janma lapsyāmi saptame divase khalu 
 tatra mūtrapuriṣādīn amedhyān api kṛcchrataḥ  Rm 
 labdhvā bhuktvā cariṣyāmi vyādhasaṃghair upadrutaḥ 
 bahuvarṣasahasrāṇi bhūtvaivaṃ sūkarātmajaḥ  Rm 
 amedhyakardame nityaṃ vatsyāmy āvartya saṃcaran 
 evaṃ divyāmṛtaṃ bhuktvā ramitvā bhavatā saha  Rm 
 kathaṃ hi nārake gatvā bhokṣye 'medhyāni saṃcaraḥ 
 imaṃ kalpataruṃ tyaktvā yathepsitaphalapradaṃ  Rm 
 jāṃgalaṃ vṛkṣam āśritya sthito bhokṣyāmi kiṃ tadā 
 sarvathāhaṃ cyuto 'smītaḥ prerito hi svakarmaṇā  Rm 
 vividhāni ca duḥkhāni bhoktuṃ yāsyāmi nārake 
 tad upāyaṃ pradātavyaṃ bhavatā me 'nukaṃpinā  Rm 
 yenāśu durgater muktaḥ prāgacheyaṃ ca svargatiṃ 
 sarvathā rakṣa māṃ nātha yady asti te kṛpā mayi  Rm 
 bhavān māṃ patitaṃ dṛṣṭvā nopekṣāṃ kartum arhati 
 bhavān eva jagacchāstā sarvalokādhipaḥ prabhuḥ  Rm 
 tad āśu māṃ prayatnena samuddhartuṃ samarhati 
 idaṃ te darśanaṃ nātha paścimaṃ me bhavet khalu  Rm 
 Rm 
 janmaśatasahasraiś ca durlabhaṃ syād dhi saṃgamaṃ 
 ity evaṃ vilapaṃ devaputras sa taṃ surādhipaṃ  Rm 
 natvā pādau nirīkṣyaiva tasthāv aśrugalanmukhaḥ 
 atha śakraḥ surendro 'sau dṛṣṭvaivaṃ pravilāpitaṃ  Rm 
 kāruṇyā krāntacittas tam āśvāsayann abhāṣata 
 mā kṛthā rodanaṃ bhadra samāśvasi hi dhīraya  Rm 
 kriyante kiṃ prayatnāni sarvathā maraṇaṃ dhruvaṃ 
 mṛtyur mahāvaliṣṭho hi sarvasatvāntakārakaḥ  Rm 
 hrīyante mṛtyunā sarve mṛtyuḥ kena nihanyate 
 anirvāyo hi sarvatra sarvatraidhātukeṣv api  Rm 
 sarveṣām api jantūnām ekānte maraṇaṃ dhruvaṃ 
 tasmān mā bhes tathā mṛtyoḥ kiṃ viṣādena sidhyate  Rm 
 tad dhairyyataiḥ samālaṃvya triratnaṃ śaraṇaṃ vraja 
 gatvā ca śaraṇaṃ teṣāṃ smara nityaṃ samāhitaḥ  Rm 
 tatas tvaṃ durgatiṃ muktvā sadgatiṃ samavāpnuyāḥ 
 etad eva hi saṃsāre mahopāyaṃ śubhāptaye  Rm 
 nānyad dhi vidyate kiṃcin mṛtyau sādhāraṇe dhruve 
 tad anyaccetanāṃ hitvā triratnāny abhisaṃsmaran  Rm 
 namo buddhāya dharmāya saṃghāyeti vadan bhaja 
 ye triratnasmṛtiṃ dhṛtvā mṛtās te puṇyabhāginaḥ  Rm 
 kramād bodhicarīṃ prāpya yāyuś cānte sukhavatīṃ 
 tvaṃ cāpi triratnānaṃ smṛtvā mṛtaḥ supuṇyadhṛk  Rm 
 kramād bodhicarīṃ prāpya saṃprayāyāḥ sukhāvatīṃ 
 itīndreṇa samādiṣṭaṃ śrutvā devasuto 'tha saḥ  Rm 
 tathety anusaṃmodya punar natvaivam abravīt 
 adyārabhya mahendrāhaṃ triratnānaṃ sadā smaran  Rm 
 gatvā ca śaraṇaṃ teṣāṃ upāsako bhave khalu 
 ity uktvā sa mahendrasya puraḥ sthitvā kṛtāñjaliḥ  Rm 
 anusmṛtya triratnānāṃ namaskṛtim udāharat 
 namo buddhāya bhadrāya namo dharmāya tāyine  Rm 
 Rm 
 namaḥ saṃghāya nāthāya sarvadāpi name bhaje 
 adyārabhya triratnānāṃ sadāhaṃ śaraṇaṃ vraje  Rm 
 upāsako bhaven nityaṃ namāmi satataṃ smaret 
 ity uktvā devaputro 'sau kāladharmayutaś cyutaḥ  Rm 
 tuṣite devaloke 'bhūd upapannaḥ supuṇyataḥ 
 dharmatā khalu devānāṃ ye devāḥ svargataś cyutāḥ  Rm 
 te 'dholokeṣu gacheyur na tūrddhvabhuvaneṣu hi 
 atha śakro narendro 'sau dṛṣṭvā taṃ svargataś cyutaṃ  Rm 
 kutrāsau labhate janma ity adhastād vyalokayat 
 kim asau sūkarīgarbha utpanno vā na veti ca  Rm 
 apaśyat sarvataś cainaṃ na dadarśa kuhāpi sa 
 tato 'sau vismitaḥ śakro divyena cakṣuṣā punaḥ  Rm 
 kutrāsau labhate janma ity evaṃ samalokayat 
 vata tiryyakṣu jāto 'sau preteṣu ca prajāyate  Rm 
 atha narakeṣu vā jāta ity evaṃ samalokayat 
 teṣu triṣv apy apāyeṣu nādrākṣīt taṃ samaṃtataḥ  Rm 
 tato manuṣyalokeṣu jāto veti dadarśa ca 
 tatrāpi ca sa sarvatra nādrākṣīt taṃ sureśvaraḥ  Rm 
 tataś caturmahārājabhuvaneṣu prajāyate 
 iti teṣu ca sarvatra vilokayan dadarśa na  Rm 
 tataś ca vismitaḥ śakras trayastriṃśe vyalokayan 
 tatrāpi taṃ na cādrākṣīt kutrāpi ca samaṃtataḥ 
 evaṃ sarvatra lokeṣu vilokayaṃs tadudbhavaṃ 
 adṛṣṭvā vismitaḥ śakraḥ punar evaṃ vyaciṃtayat 
 aho vata mahāścaryyaṃ yan mayāpi na dṛśyate  Rm 
 kutrāsau jāyate nūnaṃ na manye tat pravṛttitāṃ 
 ko nu jñāsyati tadvṛttiṃ buddhād anyo na kaścana  Rm 
 buddha eva jagaddarśī ṣaḍabhijñas trikālavit 
 tasmād aham ito gatvā saṃbuddhe samupācaran  Rm 
 Rm 
 vijñapyaivaṃ ca tadvṛttiṃ praṣṭum arhāmi sāṃprātaṃ 
 ity evaṃ manasā dhyātvā devendro 'sau savismayaḥ  Rm 
 sahasā jetakāraṇye jināśramam avātarat 
 tatrāsau sugataṃ dṛṣṭvā saharṣavismayānvitaḥ  Rm 
 praṇamya purataḥ sthitvā kṛtāṃjalipuṭo 'vadat 
 bhagavaṃs tad vijānīyā yad ihāham upāgataḥ  Rm 
 tathāpi praṣṭum ichāmi tat samādeṣṭum arhasi 
 ekaḥ kālagato devaputraḥ svargāc cyuto gataḥ  Rm 
 ṣaṭsu lokeṣu sarvatra dṛśyate na mayā hy asau 
 kutrāsau jāyate śāstar mayā na dṛśyate kvacit  Rm 
 tasyotpattiḥ kuha sthāne tat samādeṣṭum arhasi 
 itīndravacanaiḥ śrutvā sa saṃbuddho munīśvaraḥ  Rm 
 tasya puṇyātmanaḥ sthānaṃ iṃdrāya samacakṣatac 
 kauśika tuṣito nāma lokadhātuḥ prasiddhitaḥ  Rm 
 tatrāsau modate devo gatvā triśaraṇaṃ cyutaḥ 
 ityādiṣṭaṃa munīndreṇa śrutvā sa tridaśādhipaḥ  Rm 
 vismitaḥ suprasannātmā praṇatvaivaṃm udānayat 
 aho buddham aho dharmam aho saṃghaṃ śubhaṃkaraṃ  Rm 
 yat saṃśaraṇamātre 'pi satvā yānti śubhālayaṃ 
 ye buddhaṃ śaraṇaṃ yānti na te gachaṃti durgatiṃ  Rm 
 prahāya pātakān sarvān divyalokam upāsate 
 ye dharmaṃ śaraṇaṃ yānti na te gachaṃti durgatiṃ 
 prahāya mānuṣān kāyān divyān kāyān upāsate  Rm 
 ye saṃghaṃ śaraṇaṃ yānti na te gachanti durgatiṃ 
 prahāya sarvaduḥkhāni divyasaukhyāny upāsate  Rm 
 dhanyās te puruṣā bhadrāḥ saṃbodhipadagāminaḥ 
 ye saṃsmṛtvā triratnāni vrajanti maraṇaṃ dhruvaṃ  Rm 
 athāsau bhagavāñ chrutvā śakreṇaivaṃ subhāṣitaṃ 
 tathānuvarṇayan prāha kauśikaṃ taṃ surādhipaṃ  Rm 
 evam etad dhi devendra yathaivaṃ tvaṃ prabhāṣase 
 Rm 
 dhanyās te puruṣā bhadrā triratnaṃ bhajaṃti ye  Rm 
 ye buddhaṃ śaraṇaṃ yānti na te gachanti durgatiṃ 
 kleśavairīṃ vinirjitya saṃbodhiṃ samavāpnuyuḥ  Rm 
 ye dharmaṃ śaraṇaṃ yānti na te gachanti durgatiṃ 
 māradharmavinirmuktā bodhidharmān avāpnuyuḥ 
 ye saṃghaṃ śaraṇaṃ yāṃti na te gachaṃti durgatiṃ 
 pātakebhyo vinirmuktāḥ saṃprayānti sukhāvatīṃ  Rm 
 na bhajanti munīndraṃ ye te bhramaṃti bhavārṇave 
 saṃbodhimārgato bhraṣṭā naṣṭā gachanti durgatiṃ  Rm 
 ye śṛṇvaṃti na saddharmaṃ te kleśaparidāhitāḥ 
 māradharmaratā duṣṭāḥ praṇaṣṭā yāṃti durgatiṃ 
 na mānayaṃti ye saṃghaṃ na te jānaṃti sadgatiṃ 
 sadā duḥkhābhisaṃtaptā bhraṣṭā gachaṃti durgatiṃ 
 nindanti ye triratnāni te duṣṭā mārapākṣikāḥ 
 naiva caraṃti sanmārge vinaṣṭā yaṃti durgatiṃ 
 tasmād ye mānavāḥ santo vāṃchanti sadgatiṃ sadā 
 taiḥ saṃsmṛtvā triratnānāṃ karttavyaṃ śaraṇaṃ mudā  Rm 
 ye smaranti triratnānāṃ na te gachaṃti durgatiṃ 
 prahāya pātakān sarvāñ śīghraṃ yānti sukhāvatīṃ  Rm 
 sukhāvatyāṃ jinendrasya dharmaṃ śrutvānumoditāḥ 
 bodhicittaṃ samāsādya caranti bodhicārikāṃ  Rm 
 tatas tāḥ kramataḥ pūryya saṃvṛttipāram āgatāḥ 
 paramārthacarīṃ prāpya nirvṛttiṃ samavāpnuyuḥ  Rm 
 idaṃ hi bodhimārgānāṃ vījaṃ vijñāya kauśika 
 triratnasmaraṇaṃ nityaṃ karttavyaṃ bodhivāṃchibhiḥ  Rm 
 kadāpi naiva moktavyaṃ triratnasmaraṇaṃ sadā 
 gatvā ca śaraṇaṃ teṣāṃ triratnānāṃ samācara  Rm 
 evaṃ tena munīndreṇa samādiṣṭaṃ sa kauśikaḥ 
 śrutvaivam ity anujñāya prābhyanandat prasāditaḥ  Rm 
 tato 'sau bhagavantaṃ taṃ natvā sa racitāṃjaliḥ 
 tridhā pradakṣiṇīkṛtya punar natvā divaṃ yayau  Rm 
 Rm 
 tato devapure gatvā sudharmamaṃdire sthitaḥ 
 devalokān samāmaṃtrya tat pravṛttaṃ samabravīt  Rm 
 bho bho devagaṇāḥ sarve śṛṇudhvaṃ tat samāhitaḥ 
 yad adbhutaṃ mahāpuṇyaṃ saṃbodhihetum ucyate  Rm 
 dharmatā khalu devānāṃ ye ye devā hi nākataḥ 
 cyutās te te prayānty adho na tūrddhvaṃ yānti ke cana  Rm 
 idānīṃ tu vrajeyus te ye devāḥ svargataś cyutāḥ 
 triratnaśaraṇaṃ kṛtvorddhvagatiṃ na tv adhogatiṃ  Rm 
 dṛśyatām amuko devaputras triśaraṇaṃ gataḥ 
 svargāc cyutvā samutpannas tuṣite 'sau pramodate  Rm 
 yūyam api ca tad dṛṣṭvā triratnānāṃ samāhitāḥ 
 gatvā ca śaraṇaṃ nityaṃ smṛtvā bhajadhvam ādarāt  Rm 
 tato yūyaṃ na yāyāta durgatiṣu kadā cana 
 sadā divyasukhaṃ bhuktvā prayāsyatha sukhāvatīṃ  Rm 
 ye buddhe śaraṇaṃ yāṃti na te gachanti durgatiṃ 
 kleśavairān vinirjitya saṃbodhipadam āpnuyuḥ  Rm 
 ye dharme śaraṇaṃ yānti na te gachanti durgatiṃ 
 māradharmavinirmuktā buddhadharmāṇy avāpnuiyuḥ  Rm 
 ye saṃghe śaraṇaṃ gatvā na te gachanti durgatiṃ 
 sarvapātakanirmuktā prayāsyaṃti sukhāvatīṃ  Rm 
 na bhajanti triratnaṃ ye te bhramanti bhavārṇave 
 saddharmanindakā bhraṣṭā naṣṭā gachanti durgatiṃ  Rm 
 durgatiṣu bhramaṃtas te duḥkhāni vividhāni ca 
 bhuktvā caranti duṣṭāṃśā naiva gachaṃti sadgatiṃ  Rm 
 tad duḥkhaṃ hātum ichaṃti sukhaṃ prāptuṃ ca ye sadā 
 te triratnaṃ sadā smṛtvā bhajaṃtāṃ śaraṇaṃ gatāḥ  Rm 
 tato vo maṃgalaṃ nityaṃ naiva yāyāta durgatiṃ 
 sadgatim eva yāyāta saṃbodhim api lapsyatha  Rm 
 iti tena surendreṇa samādiṣṭaṃ hitārthinā  śru
 tadā sarve 'pi devāś ca triratnaṃ śaraṇaṃ gatāḥ 
 Rm 
 sarvadānusmarantaś ca satkṛtyaivaṃ prabhejire  Rm 
 evaṃ devās tadā ye ye triratnaśaraṇaṃ gatāḥ 
 te te svargād api cyutvā naivāgachann adhogatiṃ  Rm 
 tata ūrddhvaṃ samudgamya prāgachaṃs tuṣitālaye 
 triratnaśaraṇaṃ yātā maitreyaṃ samupāśrayan  Rm 
 tathā śakraś ca tān sarvān maitreyasamupāśritān 
 dṛṣṭvānumodanāṃ kurvan prābhyanandat suraiḥ saha  Rm 
 iti me guruṇā khyātaṃ tathā te vakṣyate mayā 
 evaṃ matvā mahārāja triratnaśaraṇaṃ vraja  Rm 
 tatas te maṃgalaṃ nityaṃ sarvatrāpi bhaved dhruvaṃ 
 kramād bodhicarīḥ prāpya saṃbodhipadam āpnuyāḥ  Rm 
 prajāś cāpi mahārāja bodhayitvā prayatnataḥ 
 triratnaśaraṇe sthāpya tvayā dharmapravṛddhaye  Rm 
 ity evam upaguptena samādiṣṭaṃ subhāṣitaṃ 
 śrutvā rājā tathety evaṃ prānvamodat sapārṣadaḥ  Rm 
 ye puṇyaprāptukāmās tad idam avirataṃ sūkarīkāvadānaṃ 
 śṛṇvanti śravayanti pramuditamanasā durgatiṃ te na yānti 
 nirjitya kleśasaṃghāṃs triguṇahitakarā bodhicaryyānuraktā 
 maitreyaṃ bodhisatvaṃ tuṣitabhuvanāgāḥ saṃbhajanti prakāmaṃ  Rm 
  iti ratnāvadānamālāyāṃ sūkaryyavadānaṃ samāptaṃ 
 Rm 
 VII Vapuṣmatkumārāvadāna
 athaśoko mahīpālaḥ kṛtāṃjalipuṭo mudā 
 upaguptaṃ guruṃ natvā punar evam abhāṣata  Rm 
 bhadanta śrotum ichāmi punar anyat subhāṣitaṃ 
 sarvasatvahitārthāya tat samādeṣṭum arhasi  Rm 
 iti saṃprārthite tena rājñāśokena bhūbhujā 
 upagupto yatiś cāsau dṛṣṭvā taṃ nṛpam abravīt  Rm 
 sādhu rājan samādhāya śrūyatāṃ puṇyavṛddhaye 
 yathā me guruṇā khyātaṃ tathā te vakṣyate mayā  Rm 
 purāsīd bhagavān buddhaḥ śrīghanaḥ śakyakeśarī 
 sarvavidyāguṇācāryyas traidhātukavināyakaḥ  Rm 
 sugato 'rhan mahābhijño dharmarājas tathāgataḥ 
 jinaḥ samantabhadrāṃśaś caturbrahmavihārakaḥ  Rm 
 sa ekasamaye tatra kapilākhye purottame 
 nyagrodhāramake ramye vyaharac chrāvakaiḥ saha  Rm 
 tasmiṃś ca samaye tatra dharmmaṃ śrotuṃ samāgatāḥ 
 devāsuramahārājā yakṣagaṃdharvakinnarāḥ  Rm 
 garuḍā nāgarājāś ca siddhavidyādharā grahāḥ 
 yogino yatayaś cāpi munayo brahmacāriṇaḥ  Rm 
 rājānaḥ kṣatriyāś cāpi vaiśyāmātyāś ca maṃtriṇaḥ 
 śreṣṭhinaḥ sārthavāhāś ca paurā jānapadā api  Rm 
 evam anye 'pi satvāś ca ye saddharmaguṇavāṃchinaḥ 
 te sarve samupāgatya vaṃditvā taṃ munīśvaraṃ  Rm 
 pūjayitvā puraskṛtya parivṛtya samantataḥ 
 kṛtāṃjalipuṭo dharmaṃ śrotuṃ samupatasthire  Rm 
 athāsau bhagavān dṛṣṭvā tān sarvān dharmakāṃkṣiṇaḥ 
 ādimadhyāṃtakalyāṇaṃ dideśa dharmam uttamaṃ  Rm 
 taṃ ca dharmāmṛtaṃ pītvā sarve te saṃpramoditāḥ 
 Rm 
 satkṛtya śraddhayā nityaṃ bhajanta upatasthire  Rm 
 bhagavāṃś ca tathā nityaṃ sarvasatvahitārthataḥ 
 saddharmadeśanāṃ kṛtvā vyaharat sāṃghikaiḥ saha  Rm 
 tasmiṃś ca samaye tatra pure kapilavastuni 
 āsīc chākyo mahāsādhur mahābhogo mahādhanaḥ  Rm 
 tena kalatram ānītaṃ svakulasadṛśāt kulāt 
 tayā sa kāntayā sārddhaṃ rarāma paricārayan  Rm 
 tasyaivaṃ ramamāṇasya sā bhāryāsīt sugarbhiṇī 
 tato 'sau samaye 'sūta dārakaṃ divyasuṃdaraṃ  Rm 
 martyātikrāntavarṇābhaṃ divyakalpasuvarṇitaṃ 
 sūkṣmachaviṃ subhadrāṃgaṃ gauravarṇaṃ manoharaṃ  Rm 
 maheśākhyaṃ manāpaṃ ca darśanīyaṃ prasādikaṃ 
 abhirūpaṃ supuṣṭāṃgaṃ sarvalakṣaṇamaṇḍitaṃ  Rm 
 tatrāsau janako dṛṣṭvā dārakaṃ taṃ subhadrikaṃ 
 moditaḥ sahasā jñātiṃ samāhūyābravīt tathā  Rm 
 bhavantaḥ paśyatāṃ putro mamāyaṃ divyasuṃdaraḥ 
 asya jātimahaṃ kṛtvā nāmadheyaṃ pracakṣyatāṃ  Rm 
 iti tenoditaṃ śrutvā jñātayas te sasaṃmatāḥ 
 dṛṣṭvā taṃ vālakaṃ divyaṃ kalyavarṇaṃ susuṃdaraṃ  Rm 
 saṃmīlya saṃmataṃ kṛtvā dṛṣṭvā tasyāṅgalakṣaṇaṃ 
 kṛtvā jātimahaṃ nāma sthāpituṃ saṃvabhāṣire 
 yad ayaṃ dārako divyavapuḥ kalyātisuṃdaraḥ 
 tasmād bhavatu nāmnāyaṃ vapusmān iti viśrutaḥ 
 iti saṃbhāṣaṇāṃ kṛtvā sarve te jñātivargikāḥ  Rm 
 purastāt tasya śākyasya gatvā caivaṃ vabhāṣire 
 yad ayaṃ bhavataḥ putro divyavapur guṇānvitaḥ  Rm 
 tasmād bhavatu nāmnāyaṃ vapuṣmān iti viśrutaḥ 
 tatheti samabhikhyāya pitrā sa suta ātmajaḥ  Rm 
 aṣṭābhya upamātṛbhya upanyasto 'bhipālane 
 tato 'sau dārakas tābhir dhātrībhir upacāraṇaiḥ  Rm 
 Rm 
 pālito varddhitaḥ puṣṭa āsīt padmaṃ yathā hrade 
 kramāt pravarddhitaś cāsau kumāro 'bhūd yadā tataḥ  Rm 
 tadā suhṛtsahāyaiś ca sārddhaṃ krīḍitum ācarat 
 yatra yatra vapuṣmān sa cakrāma bhuvi saṃcaraṃ  Rm 
 tatra tatrābhavan medhyā bhūpradeśāḥ samaṃtataḥ 
 evaṃvidhamahāpuṇyamaheśākhyaḥ śivāśayaḥ  Rm 
 kāruṇiko mahāśrāddhaḥ svaparātmahitārthabhṛt 
 dharmakāmaḥ subhadrātmā pūjyo mānyo jitendriyaḥ  Rm 
 abhivādyaḥ kumāro 'pi vapuṣmān sa vyarājata 
 tataḥ karmavipākena preryyamānaḥ kumārakaḥ  Rm 
 sa vapuṣmān suhṛtsaṃghaiḥ sārddhaṃ puro viniryayau 
 tato 'sau jetakāraṇyaṃ dūrād dṛṣṭvā pramoditaḥ  Rm 
 ramituṃ tatra mahodyāne sahasā samupācarat 
 tataḥ samupaviṣṭo 'sau dṛṣṭvodyānaṃ pramoditaḥ  Rm 
 śāntarūpān yatīn paśyan vihāre harṣito 'viśat 
 tatrāsau bhagavantaṃ taṃ dadarśa samitisthitaṃ  Rm 
 dvātriṃśallakṣaṇāśītivyañjanaparimaṇḍitaṃ 
 vyāmābhālaṃkṛtaṃ kāmyaṃ śatasūryyādhikaprabhaṃ  Rm 
 samaṃtabhadrarūpaṃ ca ratnāṃgam iva jaṃgamaṃ 
 dṛṣṭvāsau suprasannātmā samupetya purogataḥ  Rm 
 pādau tasya muner natvā dharmaṃ śrotum upāviśat 
 athāsau bhagavān dṛṣṭvā tasya cittaṃ viśodhitaṃ  Rm 
 aryyasatyāni mārgaṃ ca dideśa bodhisādhanaṃ 
 tac chrutvā sugatoditaṃ vapuṣmān sa praharṣitaḥ  Rm 
 bhavābhisaraṇodvignaḥ saddharmaguṇam aichata 
 bhitvā sa jñānavajreṇa satkāyadṛṣṭiparvataṃ  Rm 
 śrotāpattiphalaṃ labdhvā dṛṣṭasatyo 'bhavat sudhīḥ 
 saṃsāraṃ cāsthiraṃ matvā bhavabhogyasunispṛhaḥ  Rm 
 pravrajyāṃ caritum aichat svākhyāte sugatāśrame 
 tato 'sau purato gatvā munīndrasya kṛtāṃjaliḥ  Rm 
 pādau natvā prasannāsyaḥ pravrajyāṃ samayācata  Rm 
 namas te bhagavañ chāstaḥ śaraṇaṃ bhavatāṃ vraje 
 Rm 
 tat pravrajyāvrataṃ dehi cariṣye brahmacārikāṃ  Rm 
 iti tenārthitaṃ dṛṣṭvā bhagavāṃs taṃ kumārakaṃ 
 pravrajyācaraṇāraktaṃ matvā caivaṃ samabravīt  Rm 
 kumāra yadi te vāṃchā pravrajyācaraṇe 'sti hi 
 pitror ādeśam āsādya prāgacha dāsyate tadā  Rm 
 iti śrutvā munīndrasya nirdeśaṃ tat tatheti saḥ 
 naṃditaś caraṇau natvā svagṛhaṃ sahasāgataḥ  Rm 
 tato gṛhe samāsādya pitroś ca purataḥ sthitaḥ 
 kṛtāṃjalipuṭo natvā vṛttāṃtaṃ samabhāṣata  Rm 
 adyāmba tāta saṃbuddho dṛśyate 'pūrvadarśanaḥ 
 sarvalakṣaṇasaṃpūrṇo divyātikāntasuṃdaraḥ  Rm 
 saṃsthitaḥ parṣadāṃ madhye bhāṣati dharmam uttamaṃ 
 apūrvaṃ śrūyate tasya subhāṣitavaco'mṛtaṃ  Rm 
 tatsubhāṣitasudhāṃ pītvā cittaṃ me tṛpyate na hi 
 bhūyas tad amṛtaṃ pātuṃ vratam ichāmi sāṃprataṃ  Rm 
 anye 'pi bahavo dṛṣṭvā bhikṣavo brahmacāriṇaḥ  Rm 
 śāntaśīlāḥ śubhātmāno dayākāruṇyamānasāḥ 
 tat sabhāgavrataṃ cartum ichāmi khalu sāṃprataṃ  Rm 
 tad anujñāṃ pradattaṃ me kṛpāsti yadi vāṃ mayi 
 evaṃ tasya svaputrasya vacanaṃ vajrasannibhaṃ  Rm 
 tau mātāpitarau śrutvā mūrchitau petatur bhuvi 
 tataḥ putraprayatnena cetanāṃ prāpya tau punaḥ  Rm 
 pariṣvajya svakaṃ putraṃ tam evaṃ paryyadevatāṃ 
 hā putra katham ajño 'si hātmaja vallabho 'si naḥ  Rm 
 hā suta vaṃcyase kena hā tāta kiṃ nu vāṃchasi 
 hā jīva katham ekānte tyaktvāsmān kva nu yāsyase  Rm 
 nandanaḥ supriyāś cāsi kena duḥkhena yāsyase 
 kiṃcid duḥkhaṃ na te dattaṃ asmābhir vā kadā cana  Rm 
 kutaḥ kiṃ jāyate duḥkhaṃ tad vadasva yadīhasi 
 ity evaṃ paridevitvā pitāsau cetasātmajaṃ  Rm 
 Rm 
 nivārayan pravaṃdhena bodhayituṃ samabravīt 
 tvaṃ kumāra vayastho 'si sukomalaḥ sukhaidhitaḥ  Rm 
 śītatāpāsahiṣṇuś ca yathechābhogyasaṃrataḥ 
 kiṃcid duḥkhānabhijñas tvaṃ tat kathaṃ pravrajeḥ suta  Rm 
 pravrajito gṛhaṃ tyaktvā bahirdeśe vases sadā 
 cīvaraprāvṛtaḥ piṇḍaṃ yācitvā svayam āhareḥ  Rm 
 anekajantusaṃcāre vane 'raṇye kathaṃ vaseḥ 
 jaṃgale durgame naikacaurākīrṇe kathaṃ careḥ  Rm 
 ekākī ca kathaṃ tiṣṭher vṛkṣamūle ca nirjane 
 śmaśāne saṃsthitaḥ paśyan mṛtakānto traseḥ kathaṃ  Rm 
 śayithāś ca kathaṃ śūnye gṛhe bhūtanivāsite 
 evaṃ suduṣkarīṃ caryyāṃ carituṃ katham ichasi  Rm 
 tat pravrajyāvrate cittaṃ mā kṛthās tvaṃ nivarttaya 
 iti madvacanaṃ śrutvā gṛhe sthitvā sukhaṃ rama  Rm 
 nityaṃ pravrajatāṃ duḥkhaṃ kiṃ siddhaṃ duḥkhacaryyayā 
 dharme vaṃchāsti cet putra gṛhe sthitvā cara vrataṃ  Rm 
 śṛṇvaṃś ca dharmaśāstrāṇi śrāvayaṃś ca bahūñ janān 
 dānaṃ kṛtvā viśuddhātmā triratnaṃ satataṃ bhaja  Rm 
 yasya kiṃcid gṛhe nāsti jñātir vaṃdhuś ca kaścana 
 nāpi mitragatiś cāpi pravrajyā tasya yujyate 
 kiṃ tava setsyate putra pravrajyāṃ pākuniṣṭhayā 
 sarvathā tyaja tadvāṃchā gṛhe dharmaṃ sukhaṃ cara 
 iti pitroditaṃ śrutvā vapuṣmān sa viśaṃkitaḥ  Rm 
 pitroḥ pādān punar natvā pratyuvāca prabodhayan 
 satyaṃ tāta gṛhe saukhyaṃ dharmāṇāṃ caram uttamaṃ  Rm 
 saṃpado 'pi samṛddhās te kāmabhogyaṃ mahatsukhaṃ 
 gṛhe parigrahāḥ poṣyās tad arthaṃ dhanam arjayet  Rm 
 Rm 
 arjane hi mahatkaṣṭaṃ rakṣaṇe 'pi prayatnatā 
 aneke saṃpado 'pāyā rājāgnyudakataskarāḥ  Rm 
 kṣaṇād dhareyur ākṛṣya tad duḥkhaṃ sahituṃ kathaṃ 
 saṃpado 'nte vipattiḥ syāt kasya saṃpadviniścalā  Rm 
 vipattau hīyate dhairyyam adhairyyāt kleśito bhavet 
 kleśito doṣam āpnoti tadā puṇye matiḥ kutaḥ  Rm 
 apuṇye kupitā lakṣmir naivāśraye gamiṣyati 
 lakṣmīvirahite gehe kuto dharmasya gocaraṃ  Rm 
 saṃpattau tu labhen mānaṃ mānād dhi jāyate madaḥ 
 madād pramādito dharme tadā dharmo gṛhe kutaḥ  Rm 
 adharmāt kāmabhogyaṃ tu kevalaṃ pāpasādhanaṃ 
 kāmārthe kleśitā lokāḥ kāmārthe duḥkhabhāginaḥ  Rm 
 kāmārthe pratihanyante tena kāme sukhaṃ kathaṃ 
 saṃty evaṃ tāta sarvatra bhayāni vividhāni hi  Rm 
 traidhātukabhavasthānāṃ kasya nāsti bhayaṃ kuha 
 daivāt sarvatra jāyante duḥkhāni ca sukhāni ca  Rm 
 kleśacittasamutthāni duḥkhāni ca bhayāni ca 
 yatra yatrāpi saṃyāti kleśitātmā sukhechayā  Rm 
 tatra tatrāpi karmotthair duḥkhair bhayaiś ca hanyate 
 yatra yatrāpi saṃyāti dharmacitto hitechayā 
 tatra tatrāpi sarvatra nirbhayaś carate sukhaṃ 
 yal lokānāṃ bhayasthānaṃ tatraiva ramate yatiḥ 
 vivikte nirjane 'raṇye vṛkṣamūle guhāsu ca  Rm 
 śūnyagehe śmaśāne 'pi sukhaṃ dhyātvā yatir vaset 
 svadharmai rakṣito yogī saṃyatātmā kuto bhayaḥ  Rm 
 kim eva vahuvādena nirvāṇārthimano mama 
 tan nirvātuṃ svadehe 'pi nirapekṣaḥ parivraje  Rm 
 tad anujñāṃ pradattaṃ me pravrajyāvratasādhane 
 yadi na dīyate 'nujñā mariṣye 'haṃ na saṃśayaḥ  Rm 
 iti tasyātmajasyaivaṃ nirvandhavacanaṃ pitā 
 Rm 
 śrutvā viyogaduḥkhārttaḥ punas taṃ sutam abravīt  Rm 
 mā putra sahasā kārṣī maraṇābhilāṣitaṃ manaḥ 
 sarvathāpy anivarttī tvam avaśyaṃ ced gamiṣyasi  Rm 
 yad ichasi vrataṃ kartuṃ saddharmārthimanas tava 
 pravraja śraddhayā putra svākhyāte buddhaśāsane  Rm 
 evaṃ bharttroditaṃ śrutvā tan mātā mūrchitāpatat 
 cirāt sā cetanāṃ prāptā rudantī cāvadat sutaṃ  Rm 
 hā putra katham ekānte māṃ vihāya kva yāsyasi 
 hā me jīvo 'si kiṃ paśyaṃ pravrajituṃ samīhasi  Rm 
 kiṃcid duḥkhaṃ na te dattaṃ mayāmvāyā kadā cana 
 kena duḥkhena te cittaṃ pravrajituṃ samichati  Rm 
 pravrajyā śobhate putra vṛddhatve vā daridrite 
 tvaṃ tu dahara ityaś ca tat pravrajyāṃ careḥ kathaṃ  Rm 
 yāvac ca jivitaṃ me 'sti tāvan mā gāḥ suta kvacit 
 yāvac cāsti gṛhe saṃpat tāvad bhuktvā sukhaṃ vasa  Rm 
 yadāhaṃ maraṇaṃ yātā yadā cāpattitā gṛhe 
 jñātimitraparityaktas tadā vrajasva vāṃchayā  Rm 
 ity ukte 'pi tayoḥ pitror udator vighnaśaṃkitaḥ 
 pādāṃ natvā vapuṣmān sa sahasā niryayau gṛhāt  Rm 
 tato veṇuvanaṃ gatvā praṇamya munim ādarāt 
 kṛtāṃjalipuṭo bhūtvā pravrajyāṃ samayācata  Rm 
 pitṛprāptābhyanujño 'haṃ nātha sāṃpratam āgataḥ 
 tat pravrajyāṃ vrataṃ dehi paṃcaśikṣāpadāni ca  Rm 
 upasampacchubhācāram anuśikṣāpadaṃ ca me 
 brahmacaryyaṃ cariṣyāmi saṃbodhau kṛtaniścayaḥ  Rm 
 adyāgreṇa mahābuddha bhavatāṃ śaraṇaṃ vraje 
 sadharmasāṃghikānāṃ cṃ kāyavākcittabhaktitaḥ  Rm 
 ity ukte bhagavān dṛṣṭvā pṛṣṭvā hastena tac chiraḥ 
 ehi bhikṣo kumāreti saṃvadaṃs taṃ samagrahīt  Rm 
 ehīti prokte sugatena muṇḍaḥ pātrī vapuṣmān sakaṣāyavāsāḥ 
 Rm 
 sadyapraśāntendriya eva tasthau svarṇṇaprabho buddhamanorathena  Rm 
 saccittalabdhaḥ sa muneḥ prasādāt prayujyamāno vyaharat samādhau 
 vyāyachamānaḥ khalu bodhimārge saṃbuddhadharme ghaṭamāna evaṃ  Rm 
 sarvaṃ ca saṃsāram anityatāhataṃ matvā ca traidhātugatiṃ vighātinīṃ 
 kleśāṃś ca sarvān pravihāya saṃyataḥ sākṣād varo 'rhaṃ sa babhūva sāṃghikaḥ  Rm 
 suvītarāgaḥ samaloṣṭahema ākāśacittaśubhagaṃdhivāsī 
 bhindann avidyāṃgam ivāṇḍakośaṃ prāptād abhijñāḥ pratisaṃvidaś ca  Rm 
 satkāralobheṣu parāṃmukhatvāt sa śakradevāsuramānuṣāṇāṃ 
 pūjyaś ca mānyo 'py abhivandanīyo babhūva sa brahmavihāracārī  Rm 
 atha te bhikṣavaḥ sarve taṃ dṛṣṭvā vismayānvitāḥ 
 bhagavantaṃ praṇamyaivaṃ paprachus tasya karmatāṃ  Rm 
 kenāyaṃ karmaṇā nātha vapuṣmān atisuṃdaraḥ 
 pravrajya sahasārhatvaṃ prāpto bhavati cātmavit  Rm 
 iti pṛṣṭe ca tair nātho bhagavāṃs tān samabravīt 
 bhikṣavaḥ śrūyatāṃ vakṣye tasya ca karma yat kṛtaṃ  Rm 
 etena yat kṛtaṃ karma tat kenānyena bhokṣyate 
 yenaiva yat kṛtaṃ karma tenaiva tad dhi bhujyate  Rm 
 puraikanavate kalpe vipaśvī nāma sarvavit 
 samudapādi loke 'rhan dharmarājas tathāgataḥ  Rm 
 vidyācaraṇasaṃpannaḥ sugato bhadrakṛj jinaḥ 
 sarvajño 'nuttaro nāthaḥ puruṣadamyasārathiḥ  Rm 
 śāstā traidhātukasthānāṃ vināyako guṇākaraḥ 
 saddharmaratnadāta sa bhagavān puṇyabhāskaraḥ  Rm 
 purīṃ vaṃdhumato rājño rājadhānīm upāśrayan 
 sārddhaṃ bhikṣugaṇaiḥ śiṣyai bodhisatvagaṇair api  Rm 
 hitāya sarvasatvānāṃ dideśa dharmam uttamaṃ 
 ādimadhyāṃtakalyāṇaṃ bodhicaryyānusārikaṃ  Rm 
 tataḥ sa buddhakāryyāṇi kṛtvā sarvāṇy aśeṣataḥ 
 nirvāṇam āyayau śānto vahnir ivendhanakṣayāt  Rm 
 tato vandhumatā rājñā tat tanuḥ saṃskṛto 'gninā 
 Rm 
 taddhātūś ca samāropya stūpa uccair mahān kṛtaḥ  Rm 
 tatra ratnamaye stūpe sadvidhāne pratiṣṭhite 
 nityasatkārapūjābhiḥ kāritaṃ ca mahotsavaṃ  Rm 
 saṃgītivādyanṛtyaiś ca mahānaṃdapracāribhiḥ 
 kārayitvā mahotsāhaṃ sthāpitaṃ sumahanmahaḥ  Rm 
 ekasmin divase tatra pumān eko daridritaḥ 
 tanmahāṃte dine 'nyasmiṃ stāpāṃgaṇam upāviśat  Rm 
 tatra stūpāṅgaṇe cāsau praviṣṭaḥ samalokayat 
 mlānībhūtāni puṣpāṇi prakīrṇṇāni samaṃtataḥ  Rm 
 tāni nirmālyapuṣpāṇi vikīrṇṇāni samaṃtataḥ 
 glānībhūtāny aśuddhāni dṛṣṭvā caivaṃ vyacintayat 
 ayaṃ caityo munīndrasya vipaścino guṇāṃbudheḥ  Rm 
 dhāturatnamayastūpaḥ sarvalokābhiḥ pūjitaḥ 
 etan nirmālyapuṣpais tu mlānitaiḥ pavaneritaiḥ  Rm 
 ākīrṇo malinībhūto hy aśuddheḥ syād aśobhitaḥ 
 tasmād etāni puṣpāṇi nirmālyāni samaṃtataḥ  Rm 
 apanīya viśuddhāya mārjayeyam iha drutaṃ  Rm 
 iti dhyātvā daridro 'sau nirmālyāny apanīya vai  Rm 
 saṃmārja nyāsamamārkṣī stūpāṃgaṇaṃ samaṃtataḥ 
 tataḥ stūpāṃgaṇaṃ sarvaṃ virajaṃ pariśodhitaṃ 
 dṛṣṭvā prasannacitto 'sau natvaivaṃ praṇidhiṃ dadhe 
 yan mayātra jinastūpe nirmālyāny apanīya vai 
 saṃmṛjya śobhanaṃ kṛtvā kuśalaṃ samupārjitaṃ 
 anena kuśalenāhaṃ sadā durgatimocitaḥ  Rm 
 evaṃvidhaguṇajñānalābhi bhūyāsam ātmavit 
 evaṃvidhaṃ ca śāstāraṃ saṃbuddhaṃ jñānabhāskaraṃ  Rm 
 ārāgayaṃ samāśritya labheyaṃ saugatiṃ gatiṃ 
 praṇidhānaṃ tathā dhṛtvā nityam evam upāśrayan  Rm 
 tatstūpe śaraṇaṃ gatvā bhaje ratnatrayaṃ sadā 
 bhikṣavaḥ kiṃ nu manyadhve yo puruṣaḥ daridrikaḥ  Rm 
 Rm 
 ayam eva vapuṣmān sa jñeyo hi nānyathā khalu 
 yat stūpāṃgaṇaṃ tena saṃbuddhaguṇabhāvinā  Rm 
 samantataḥ susaṃmṛjya pariśuddhīkṛtaṃ tadā 
 tena puṇyavipākena jāta āḍhyakule 'dhunā  Rm 
 divyābhisundaraḥ kāntaḥ sa vapuṣmān bhavaty ayaṃ 
 yat praṇidhiḥ kṛtaḥ stūpe natvā tena sucetasā  Rm 
 tena me śāsane 'py adya pravrajyārhan bhavaty ayaṃ 
 ārāgitas tathārhañ ca saṃbuddhaḥ sugato jinaḥ  Rm 
 anena bhikṣuṇā bodhiprāptena brahmacāriṇā 
 ity evaṃ karma jānīta sukṛtaṃ duṣkṛtaṃ bhave  Rm 
 yenaiva yat kṛtaṃ karma tenaiva tat phalaṃ gataṃ 
 na naśyanti hi karmāṇi kalpakoṭiśatair api  Rm 
 sāmagrīṃ prāpya kālaṃ ca phalaṃti khalu dehināṃ 
 abhuktaṃ kṣīyate naiva karma kvāpi kathaṃ cana  Rm 
 nāgnibhir dahyate karma vāyubhiś ca na śuṣyate 
 jalaiś ca klidyate nāpi kṣīyate nāpi bhūmiṣu  Rm 
 anyathāpi bhaven naiva karmaṇāṃ gatir ābhavaṃ 
 śuklānāṃ śubhataiva syāt kṛṣṇānāṃ durgatis sadā  Rm 
 miśritā miśritānaṃ tu bhujyaṃte sarvajantubhiḥ 
 tasmād apāsya kṛṣṇāni karmāṇi miśritāni ca  Rm 
 caraṇīyāṃ śubheṣv eva karmasu sukhavāṃchibhiḥ 
 tatheti bhikṣavaḥ sarve te ca lokāḥ sabhāśritāḥ  Rm 
 buddhavāco 'mṛtaṃ pītvā nananduḥ śubhakāminaḥ 
 evam etan mahārāja śrutaṃ me gurubhāṣitaṃ  Rm 
 evaṃ śrutvā tvayāpy evaṃ karttavyaṃ puṇyam eva hi 
 puṇyam eva bhavet trātā suhṛn mitraṃ hitaṃkaraḥ  Rm 
 nānyaḥ kaścid ihāmutra vidyate bhavacāriṇāṃ 
 tasmāt puṇyaṃ svayaṃ śrutvā karttavyam ādarāt sadā  Rm 
 prajāś ca śrāvayitvaivaṃ puṇye saṃsthāpaya sadā 
 ity evaṃ guruṇādiṣṭaṃ upaguptena bhikṣuṇā  Rm 
 śrutvā rājā janaiḥ sārddhaṃ tatheti prābhyanaṃdata 
 Rm 
 śṛṇvanti ye śrāvayantīha yaś ca vapuṣmato 'daḥ prathitāvadānaṃ 
 te kleśanirmuktaviśuddhacittāḥ prayānti nūnaṃ sugatālayeṣu  Rm 
  iti ratnāvadānamālāyāṃ vapuṣmatāvadānaṃ nāma samāptam 
 Rm 
 VIII Praśnottarāvadāna
 athāśoko mahīpālaḥ saṃbuddhaguṇalālasaḥ 
 upaguptaṃ guruṃ natvā prāṃjaliś caivam abravīt  Rm 
 bhadanta śrotum ichāmi punar anyat subhāṣitaṃ 
 yathā te guruṇādiṣṭaṃ tathā me khyātum arhasi  Rm 
 iti tena narendreṇa pṛṣṭe 'sau ca jināṃśajaḥ 
 upagupto yatir bhūyas taṃ nṛpeśam abhāṣata  Rm 
 śṛṇu rājaṃs tathā vakṣye yathā me guruṇoditaṃ 
 śrutvā ca bhavatāpy evaṃ karttavyaṃ dharmasādhanaṃ  Rm 
 puraikasamaye cāsau śākyasiṃhos dayākaraḥ 
 sarvajñaḥ sugato nāthaḥ śāstā traidhātukādhipaḥ  Rm 
 sarvavidyādhipo buddhaḥ ṣaḍabhijño munīśvaraḥ 
 mārajiṣṇur vinetārhaṃ dharmarājas tathāgataḥ  Rm 
 sarvasatvahitārthāya śrāvastyāṃ vahir āśrame 
 jetavane vihārasthe vyaharac chrāvakaiḥ saha  Rm 
 bodhisatvagaṇaiś cāpi sūpāsakaiś ca cailakaiḥ 
 devāsuragaṇaiś cāpi caturvarṇṇādimānavaiḥ  Rm 
 caturbhiś ca mahārājaiḥ sasainyaparivārakaiḥ 
 sarvasatvaiś ca pauraiś ca saddharmaguṇavāṃchibhiḥ  Rm 
 satkṛtya pūjayitvā ca parivṛtya puraskṛtaḥ 
 sa bhagavān sabhāmadhye siṃhāsane sthito vabhau  Rm 
 tadā sa bhagavān dṛṣṭvā tāṃ sabhāṃ samupasthitāṃ 
 ādimadhyāntakalyāṇaṃ dideśa dharmam uttamaṃ  Rm 
 te tad dharmāmṛtaṃ pītvā sarve lokāḥ pramoditāḥ 
 bhagavantaṃ punar natvā svasvasthānaṃ pratīyire  Rm 
 tato 'sau bhagavān rātrau dhyānāgāre samāviśan 
 paryyaṅkaṃ samupāśritya tasthau dhyānasamāhitaḥ  Rm 
 tadaikā devatā tasyāṃ rātrau svargāt samāgatā 
 svakāntyā bhāsayaṃty evaṃ jetavanam upāviśat  Rm 
 Rm 
 tatas tāṃ bhagavān dṛṣṭvā devatāṃ samupāgatāṃ 
 saṃnirīkṣya samāmaṃtrya tathaināṃ samabodhayat  Rm 
 devate svāgataṃ kacci kuśalaṃ te samehi bho 
 prāyātāsi yad arthena tad vadasva prapūraye  Rm 
 ity ādiṣṭe munīndreṇa tenāsau devatā mudā 
 saṃpṛchāvasaraṃ labdhvā harṣitā samupākramat  Rm 
 tatrāsau purato gatvā natvā pādau kṛtāṃjaliḥ 
 pradakṣiṇatrayaṃ kṛtvā tasthāv ekāntike muneḥ  Rm 
 sarvajetavanaṃ tasyā devatāyāḥ prabhāvataḥ 
 udāreṇāvabhāsena pravisphuṭaṃ vabhau tadā  Rm 
 tathāvabhāṣitaṃ dṛṣṭvā sarve te bhikṣusāṃghikāḥ 
 vismitāḥ sahasotthāya dṛṣṭvā tam upatasthire  Rm 
 atha sā devatotthāya kṛtāṃjalipuṭo 'gragā 
 bhagavantaṃ munīndraṃ taṃ praṇatvaivam apṛchata  Rm 
 sarvajña bhagavaṃ chāstaḥ yenāhaṃ samupāgatā 
 tadarthaṃ tvaṃ samādiśya cittaṃ me paribodhaya  Rm 
 ke narāḥ sugatiṃ yānti ke narāḥ svargagāminaḥ 
 keṣāṃ cāpi divārātrau sadā puṇyaṃ pravarddhate  Rm 
 ke cāpi durgatiṃ yāṃti ke cādhaḥ patitā narāḥ 
 keṣāṃ cāpi divārātrau sadā pāpaṃ pravarddhate  Rm 
 kiṃdado valavāṃ syāc ca kiṃdadaś ca praśobhitaḥ 
 kiṃdadaḥ sukhito lokaḥ cakṣuṣmān api kiṃpradaḥ  Rm 
 kiṃ nu vā niśitaṃ śastraṃ kiṃ vā hālāhalaṃ viṣaṃ 
 kiṃ ca prajvalito vahniḥ kiṃ mahad dāruṇaṃ tamaḥ  Rm 
 gṛhītaṃ kiṃ nu martyena kin teneha samujjhitaṃ 
 abhedyaṃ kavacaṃ kiṃ ca kiṃ vā tīkṣṇam ihāyudhaṃ  Rm 
 ko nv asau procyate cauro dhanaṃ kiṃ vā satāṃ mataṃ 
 ke vā traidhātuke loke procyante muṣitaiti  Rm 
 kaś ceha satsukhī loke ko vā ca parameśvaraḥ 
 ko vibhūṣito nityaṃ kaś cāpy atra vidaṃvitaḥ  Rm 
 vatsalo vāṃdhavo ko nu ko vā duṣṭāśayo ripuḥ 
 kiṃ mahad dāruṇaṃ duḥkhaṃ kiṃ mahat paramaṃ sukhaṃ  Rm 
 Rm 
 kiṃ ca loke priyo pathyaḥ kiṃ vāpathyaṃ na cāpriyaṃ 
 ko nu pīḍākaro vyādhiḥ ko nu vai ko bhiṣagvaraḥ  Rm 
 kenāyam āvṛto lokaḥ kena loko vaśīkṛtaḥ 
 kena tyajati mitrāṇi kena svargaṃ na gachati  Rm 
 kena mitrāṇi varddhyaṃte kena śāmyaṃti śatravaḥ 
 kena svargam avāpnoti kena mokṣaṃ ca gachati  Rm 
 kenāyaṃ badhyate lokaḥ kena loko vimucyate 
 kasyeha viprahāṇena nirvāṇam iti kathyate  Rm 
 kiṃ nu rājā ca caurāś ca syaṃdamānāḥ samudyatāḥ 
 no śaknuvanty apāhartuṃ striyo vā puruṣasya ca  Rm 
 kiṃ na dahati saptārciḥ kiṃ na bhinatti mārutaḥ 
 kiṃ vā na kledayaṃty āpaḥ kiṃ na kṣīṇaṃ ca bhūmiṣu  Rm 
 imaṃ saṃśayam adyāpi mama tac chetum arhasi 
 asmāl lokāt paraṃ lokaṃ ko gato 'tyaṃtavaṃcitaḥ  Rm 
 kiṃ nu hatvā sukhaṃ śete kiṃ ca hatvā na śocati 
 kasya caikasya dharmasya vadhaṃ saṃśasi gautama  Rm 
 mayaitad bhagavan pṛṣṭaḥ sarvajño 'si yato sudhīḥ 
 tan mama saṃśayaṃ chetuṃ samyag ādeṣṭum arhasi  Rm 
 tayaivaṃ pṛchyamāno 'sau bhagavān sarvavij jinaḥ 
 devatāṃ tāṃ samālokya tat praśnottaram abravīt  Rm 
 śṛṇu tvaṃ devate samyak kṛtvā cittaṃ samāhitaṃ 
 tavaitat paripṛchāyāḥ pratyuttaram udāhare  Rm 
 ārāmāropakā ye 'tra ye ca vā setukārakāḥ 
 prapātodakayānaṃ ca pradadanti pratiśrayaṃ  Rm 
 śraddhāśīlena satyena kṣamayā vītamatsarāḥ 
 te narāḥ sugatiṃ yānti te narāḥ svargagāminaḥ  Rm 
 teṣām eva hi martyānāṃ divārātrau niraṃtaraṃ 
 avichinnāḥ puṇyadhārāḥ pravarddhyante sadā khalu  Rm 
 daśākuśalakarttāro yena saddharmaniṃdakāḥ 
 te narā durgatiṃ yānti bhramanti pāpacāriṇaḥ  Rm 
 ye cātatāyino martyāḥ svakuladharmanaṣṭakāḥ 
 te narāḥ patitā yanti narake duḥkhabhāginaḥ  Rm 
 Rm 
 teṣāṃ pāpiṣṭhasatvānāṃ divārātrau niraṃtaraṃ 
 avichinnāḥ pāpadhārāḥ pravahante sadā khalu  Rm 
 annado valavān bhogī vastradaḥ śobhito bhavet 
 pānadaḥ sukhitaḥ tṛptaś cakṣuṣmān bhavati dīpadaḥ  Rm 
 duṣṭavāg niśitaṃ śastraṃ rāgo hālahalaṃ viṣaṃ 
 dveṣaḥ prajvalito vahnir avidyā dāruṇaṃ tamaḥ  Rm 
 gṛhītaṃ yat svayaṃ dattaṃ yad gṛhe tad ihojjhitaṃ 
 abhedyaṃ kavacaṃ kṣāntiḥ prajñā tīkṣṇaṃ mahāyudhaṃ  Rm 
 vitarko 'kuśalaś cauraḥ śilaṃ dhanaṃ satāṃ mataṃ 
 te eva muṣitā loke yaiḥ śīlaṃ vinipātitaṃ  Rm 
 alpechaḥ satsukhī loke saṃtuṣṭaḥ parameśvaraḥ 
 śīlavān bhūṣito nityaṃ naṣṭaśīlo vidaṃvitaḥ  Rm 
 vatsalo vāndhavaḥ puṇyaṃ pāpaṃ duṣṭāśayo ripuḥ 
 nārakaṃ dāruṇaṃ duḥkhaṃ skaṃdhābhāvaparaṃ sukhaṃ  Rm 
 kāmāḥ priyā apathyā hi mokṣaḥ pathyo priyaḥ satāṃ 
 dveṣaḥ pīḍākaro vyādhiḥ buddha eko bhiṣagvaraḥ  Rm 
 ajñānenāvṛto loko mohanaḥ pravaśīkṛtaḥ 
 lobhāt tyajati mitrāṇi saṃgāt svargaṃ na gachati  Rm 
 tyāgān mitrāṇi varddhante maitryā śāmyanti śatravaḥ 
 śīlāt svargam avāpnoti jñānān mokṣaṃ su gachati  Rm 
 ichayā badhyate loko nīchayā ca vimucyate 
 tṛṣṇāyā viprahāṇena nirvāṇam iti kathyate  Rm 
 puṇyaṃ rājā ca caurāś ca syaṃdamānāḥ samudyatāḥ 
 na śaknuvaṃty apāhartuṃ striyo vā puruṣasya ca  Rm 
 puṇyaṃ na dahate vahnir bhinatti ca na mārutaḥ 
 puṇyaṃ na kledayaṃty āpo naiva kṣīṇvaṃti bhūmayaḥ  Rm 
 vidyamāneṣu bhogyeṣu puṇyaṃ yena na saṃcitaṃ 
 asmāl lokāt paraṃ lokaṃ sa gato 'tyaṃtavaṃcitaḥ  Rm 
 krodhaṃ hatvā sukhaṃ śete krodhaṃ hatvā na śocati 
 Rm 
 krodhasyaikasya dharmasya vadhaṃ saṃśāmi sarvadā  Rm 
 etat praśnottaraṃ śrutvā devatāsau pramoditā 
 bhagavaṃtaṃ punar natvā prasaṃśyaivam avocata  Rm 
 dhanyo 'si bhagavan buddha sarvapraśnottarapradaḥ 
 sarvajño jagatāṃ śāstā ṣaḍabhijño munīśvaraḥ  Rm 
 vīrasya ca na paśyāmi brāhmaṇyaṃ parinirvṛtiṃ 
 sarvavīro bhayātītas trātuṃ loke 'bhiśaktibhāg  Rm 
 ity uktvā devatā bhūyaḥ kṛtvā pradakṣiṇatrayaṃ 
 natvā pādau munīndrasya tata eva divaṃ yayau  Rm 
 atha te bhikṣavaḥ sarve śrutvā śāstrānudeśitaṃ 
 satyam evaṃ parijñāya samyak karmasu cerire  Rm 
 evam etan mahārāja guruṇā me prabhāṣitaṃ 
 śrutvā caivaṃ parijñāya saddharme nirato bhava  Rm 
 dharmeṇa sugatiṃ yāyāt pāpena durgatiṃ vrajet 
 tasmād dharmaṃ puraskṛtya prajāḥ samyak prapālaya  Rm 
 daśākuśalakarmāṇi tyaktvā saṃvṛtim ācara 
 sarvopakaraṇaṃ dānaṃ dātavyaṃ svargavāṃchinā  Rm 
 duṣṭasaṃgaṃ parityajya hatvā rāgaviṣaṃ muhuḥ 
 dveṣāgniśamanaṃ kṛtvā hy avidyā saṃpraghātyatāṃ  Rm 
 kāmavitarkatāṃ tyaktvā bodhipraṇidhicetasā 
 trikāyaśodhanaṃ kṛtvā śīladhanam upārjyatāṃ  Rm 
 skaṃdhābhāvaṃ parijñāya matvā duṣṭāśayaṃ ripuṃ 
 kṣamāsv āvaraṇaṃ dhṛtvā duṣṭasaṃghān vijīyatāṃ  Rm 
 māradharmān vinirjitya saṃbodhidharmasādhane 
 dhairyavīryamahotsāhair udyamaṃ kriyatāṃ sadā  Rm 
 kleśamānamadāñ jitvā kṛtvā cittaṃ samāhitaṃ 
 sarvasatvahitārtheṣu dhyātāṃ bodhisādhanaṃ  Rm 
 lokaṃ māyāsamudbhūtam ajñānatamasāvṛtaṃ 
 dṛṣṭvā prajñāpradīpena preryatāṃ sugateḥ pathi  Rm 
 evaṃ rājan bhavān matvā duṣṭasaṃgān vivarjayet 
 Rm 
 satsaṃgaṃ nirato nityaṃ triratnasevako bhava  Rm 
 sarvā api prajāś caivaṃ paribodhya prayatnataḥ 
 preraṇīyā tvayā rājan saṃvṛtticaraṇe sadā  Rm 
 evaṃ matvā bhavāṃ rājā saṃsārasāram āpnuvan 
 kramād bodhicarī pūrya saṃbuddhapadam āpnuyāt  Rm 
 ity etad guruṇādiṣṭam upaguptena bhikṣuṇā 
 śrutvā tatheti rājāsāv abhyanaṃdat saparṣikāḥ  Rm 
 devatāparipṛchākhyasūtraṃ śṛṇvaṃti ye mudā 
 śrāvayaṃti ca te saukhyaṃ bhuktvā yāṃti sukhāvatīṃ  Rm 
  iti devatāparipṛchāsūtraṃ samāptaṃ 
 Rm 
 IX Śuklāvadāna
 athāśoko nareṃdraś ca kṛtāṃjalipuṭo mudā 
 upaguptaṃ guruṃ natvā punaḥ śrotuṃ samarthayat  Rm 
 bhadaṃta śrotum ichāmi punar anyat subhāṣitaṃ 
 yathā te guruṇādiṣṭaṃ tan mamākhyātum arhasi  Rm 
 iti pṛṣṭe nṛpeṇāsauv upagupto jināṃśajaḥ 
 tam aśokaṃ mahīnāthaṃ saṃnirīkṣya samabravīt  Rm 
 śṛṇu vakṣyāmi te rājaṃ yathā me guruṇoditaṃ 
 śrutvaitad bhavatāpy evaṃ karttavyaṃ dharmam ādarāt  Rm 
 puraikasamaye rājaṃ śākyasiṃho dayāṃbudhiḥ 
 sarvajño dharmarāṇ nāthaḥ śāstā traidhātukādhipaḥ  Rm 
 sarvavidyādhipo buddhaḥ ṣaḍabhijño munīśvaraḥ 
 jino 'rhan sugato buddhas tathāgato vināyakaḥ  Rm 
 bhagavān satvahitārthena pure kapilavastuni 
 nyagrodhamaṇḍitodyāne karaṇḍakanivāpake  Rm 
 śrāvakabhikṣusaṃghaiś ca bodhisatvagaṇaiḥ saha 
 saddharmadeśanāṃ kartuṃ vijahāra jināśrame  Rm 
 tad dharmaṃ śrotum āyātair upāsakaiś ca cailakaiḥ 
 devāsuragaṇaiś cāpi caturbhi lokapālakaiḥ  Rm 
 cāturvarṇṇyair manuṣyaiś ca paurajānapadādibhiḥ 
 saṃbodhicaraṇotsāhaiḥ saddharmaguṇalālasaiḥ  Rm 
 satkṛto pūjitaś caivaṃ parivṛtya puraskṛtaḥ 
 bhagavān sa sabhāmadhye siṃhāsanasthito vabhau  Rm 
 tatra sa bhagavān dṛṣṭvā sabhāṃ tāṃ samupasthitāṃ 
 ādimadhyāṃtakalyāṇaṃ dideśa dharmam uttamaṃ  Rm 
 tat saddharmāmṛtaṃ pītvā sarve satvāś ca moditāḥ 
 tathainaṃ śrīghanaṃ nityaṃ bhejire dharmalālasāḥ  Rm 
 tasmiṃś ca samaye tatra pure kapilavastuni 
 rohiṇākhyo mahāchākyo dhanāḍhyo dhanadopamaḥ  Rm 
 mahābhogo mahāśrāddhaḥ suviśālaparigrahaḥ 
 dātā sādhur mahā dhīraḥ pratyuvāsa sukhānvitaḥ  Rm 
 samaye tena śākyena svakulasadṛśāt kulāt 
 bhāryā nītā subhadrāṅgī svakuladharmacāriṇī  Rm 
 tato 'sau rohiṇaḥ śākyas tayaiva kāntayā saha 
 Rm 
 mahāragānurāgeṇa rarāma paricārayan  Rm 
 tasyaivaṃ ramamāṇasya kṛīḍato 'py anurāgataḥ 
 na putro na sutā vāpi sucireṇāpy ajāyata  Rm 
 tato 'sau rohiṇaḥ putrīputralābhe samutsukaḥ 
 putracintāparaḥ koṣṭhe sthitvaivaṃ ca vyacintayat  Rm 
 īyatsaṃpad gṛhe me 'sti na ca putrasutāpi na 
 etā me saṃpado rājā mamātyayād grahīṣyati  Rm 
 hā me saṃpad vinaṣṭā syāt paratrāpi gatir na hi 
 vyarthas majjanma saṃsāre yato me santatir na hi  Rm 
 ko me kuryāc ca saṃskāraṃ kaś ca piṇḍaṃ pradāsyati 
 kutrāhaṃ śaraṇaṃ yāyāṃ hā daivanihato 'smy ahaṃ  Rm 
 iti cintāviṣaṇṇo 'sau śokāgāre vyavasthitaḥ  Rm 
 kapolaṃ svakare dhṛtvā tasthau bhogyanirutsukaḥ 
 evaṃ cintāsamākrāntaṃ rohiṇaṃ taṃ nirutsukaṃ  Rm 
 dṛṣṭvā sarve suhṛnmitrā vāndhavāś ca vyabodhayan 
 kim evaṃ tiṣṭhase bhadra kiṃ ca duḥkhaṃ prajāyate  Rm 
 vaktavyaṃ cet tathāsmākaṃ vaktum arhasi sarvathā 
 iti pṛṣṭe ca taiḥ sarvair vandhumitrasuhṛjjanaiḥ  Rm 
 rohiṇo 'sau puras teṣāṃ sarvam evam abhāṣata 
 bhavantaḥ śṛṇuta sarve kathyate duḥkhatā mayā  Rm 
 mahatī me gṛhe saṃpad asyā bhoktā na vidyate 
 kathaṃ me vidyate vaṃśas tat prakāraṃ na manyate  Rm 
 yadi vo 'sti mayi snehas tad upāyaṃ pracakṣyatāṃ 
 evaṃ tenārthitaṃ śrutvā sarve te snehavaṃdhitāḥ  Rm 
 tasya vaṃśasamutpatter upāyaṃ samupādiśan 
 mā kārṣīḥ śokatāṃ bhadra tad upāyaṃ nu vidyate  Rm 
 devatārādhanāṃ kṛtvā yācasva putram ātmanā 
 avaśyaṃ devatānāṃ te prasannānāṃ prasādataḥ  Rm 
 putro vā duhitā vāpi bhaviṣyati na saṃśayaḥ 
 ity etat taiḥ samādiṣṭaṃ śrutvāsau rohiṇo mudā  Rm 
 devatārādhanāṃ kartuṃ prayatātmā samārabhat 
 pūjāṅgaiḥ pūjāyitvā ca brāhmaṇaṃ harim īśvaraṃ  Rm 
 Rm 
 iṃdrādilokapālāñ ca saṃtatiṃ samayācata 
 evaṃ putrābhinandī sa sadāraḥ vaṃśakāmyayā  Rm 
 devatārādhanaṃ kṛtvā tasthau nityaṃ samutsukaḥ 
 tathāpi tasya śākyasya svadaivaparimāṇataḥ  Rm 
 na putro na ca putrī vā suciram apy ajāyata 
 tato 'sau rohiṇaḥ śākyo devatāsu nirāśayā  Rm 
 putravāṃchāviraktātmā tasthau gehe nirutsavaḥ 
 asti caiṣa mahārāja pravādo laukikodbhavaḥ  Rm 
 yad devatāprasādena jāyate saṃtatiḥ khalu 
 evaṃ ced vā tathā rājann ekaikasya bhavet khalu  Rm 
 yathā putrasahasraṃ vā nṛpasya cakravarttinaḥ 
 api tu saṃmukhībhāvāt tristhānānāṃ nṛpeśvara  Rm 
 putrā vāpi sutāś cāpi jāyaṃte prāṇināṃ khalu 
 tadyathā pitarau raktau kalyā cartumatī prasūḥ 
 gaṃdharvaḥ prasthitaḥ kāle tadā garbhe samudbhavet  Rm 
 tataś ca samaye tasya rohiṇasyānurāgiṇaḥ 
 bhāryyā kalyāvatībhūtā snātvā ratiṃ samārabhat  Rm 
 tadaikā devatā svargāc cyutvā karmānubhoginī 
 tasya śākyasya bhāryyāyā garbhe sā samupāviśat  Rm 
 tataḥ svāpannasatvā sā matvā garbhasamudbhavaṃ 
 svāmino 'gre rahaḥ sthitvā harṣitaivaṃ nyavedayat  Rm 
 svāminn āpannasatvāsmi vaṃśa āvāṃ samudbhavet 
 tad bhavān sarvakṛyāni kārayatv anumoditaḥ  Rm 
 iti bhāryoditaṃ śrutvā rohiṇo 'sau pramoditaḥ 
 bhāryāṃ tāṃ garbhiṇīṃ dṛṣṭvā saṃsmitaḥ pratyabhāṣata  Rm 
 satyaṃ me bhāṣitaṃ bhadre matvā bhava samāhitā  Rm 
 pramādam atra mā kārṣī yadi snehāsti te mayi 
 evaṃ te kuśalaṃ bhadre yadi putraṃ janiṣyasi  Rm 
 tadā niṣkāśayāmi tvāṃ yadi putrīṃ janiṣyasi 
 iti bhartur vacaḥ śrutvā sā strī vivṛddhadohadā 
 Rm 
 bhartur viyogaśaṃkārttā babhūva parikheṭitā  Rm 
 yāvat sā samaye sūta dārikāṃ divyasuṃdarīṃ 
 śuklavastraparītāṅgāṃ garbhamalāviliptitāṃ  Rm 
 tatas tāṃ dārikāṃ jātāṃ śrutvāsau rohiṇo ruṣā 
 pratyākhyātuṃ svayaṃ bhāryāṃ viveśa sūtikāgṛhe  Rm 
 prajāpatyā tayā bhartur upanītā puraḥ sutā 
 śuklavastraparītāṅgā bhadrāṅgī divyasuṃdarī  Rm 
 tataḥ sa rohiṇo dṛṣṭvā tāṃ sutāṃ divyasuṃdarīṃ 
 śuklavastraparītāṅgāṃ paravismayam āyayau  Rm 
 aho bhāgyān mayā labdhā suteyaṃ bhadrarūpiṇī 
 yad eṣā sahajaiḥ śuklavastraiḥ prāvṛtya jāyate  Rm 
 tasmān nūnaṃ iyaṃ sākṣād devakanyāvatāritā 
 saddharmacāriṇī bhadrā bhaviṣyati na saṃśayaḥ  Rm 
 ity uktvāsau pitā śākyaḥ paśyaṃs tāṃ dārikāṃ cirāt 
 atṛpto niścalākṣaś ca tasthau saṃmūrchito yathā  Rm 
 tato jñātīn samāhūya kṛtvā jātimahaṃ mudā 
 tan nāmakaraṇaṃ tasyās tān punaḥ sa samabravīt  Rm 
 bhavanto 'syāḥ sutāyā me bhadrāṅgyā anurūpataḥ 
 nāmadheyaṃ prasiddhena karttavyaṃ kriyatāṃ śubhaṃ  Rm 
 iti tenārthite tasyāḥ sarve te jātayas tathā 
 sahajaśuklavastrāṅgaṃ dṛṣṭvaivaṃ saṃvabhāṣire  Rm 
 yad iyaṃ dārikā saumyā bhadrāṃgī divyasuṃdarī 
 śuklavastrāvṛtā jātā tac chukleti prasidhyatu  Rm 
 iti saṃbhāṣaṇāṃ kṛtvā sarve te jñātayas tathā 
 rohiṇaṃ taṃ samāmaṃtrya tathaivaṃ samudāharat  Rm 
 yad iyaṃ te sutā bhadra bhadrāṅgī divyasuṃdarī 
 śuklavastrāvṛtā jātā tac chukleti pracakṣyatāṃ  Rm 
 tathety anumataṃ kṛtvā tena pitrā prasāditā 
 śuklā sā duhitāṣṭāsu dhātrīṣu samupārpitā  Rm 
 tatas tāsāṃ ca dhātrīṇām upacārapracārataḥ 
 varddhitābhūt suramyāṅgī hradastham iva paṃkajaṃ  Rm 
 yathā yathā ca sā śuklā parivṛddhābhavat kramāt 
 Rm 
 tathā tathā ca tad vastraṃ vavṛddhe nirmalī 'bhavat  Rm 
 na ca kāyo 'py abhūt tasmāt malābhiliptadurbhagaḥ 
 vabhau tu nirmalaḥ śuddhaḥ sugaṃdhiparivāhakaḥ  Rm 
 yadā sā dārikā śuklā parivṛddhā kramād abhūt 
 kumārī sarvalokānāṃ manonetrābhihāriṇī  Rm 
 tataḥ sā śikṣituṃ vidyā guruṇāṃ samupāśritā 
 śikṣitvā kramaśo vidyāṃ pāram āśu yayau sudhīḥ  Rm 
 tadā ye ye ca tāṃ śuklām apaśyad divyasuṃdarīṃ 
 te te sarve 'pi paśyanto vismitā moham āyayuḥ  Rm 
 tatas te brāhmaṇādyāś ca tadguṇākṛṣṭamānasāḥ 
 svasvadūtena tāṃ śuklāṃ rohiṇaṃ prārthayan muhuḥ  Rm 
 jātiśreṣṭho hy ahaṃ vipras tac chuklāṃ me dātum arhasi 
 iti tāṃ brāhmaṇaputrā rohiṇaṃ pratyayācayan  Rm 
 rājaputro 'smy ahaṃ vīras tat sutā me pradīyatāṃ 
 iti rājakumārās taṃ rohiṇaṃ tāṃ samarthayan  Rm 
 ahaṃ vaiśyaḥ prajābhartā tac chuklāṃ me dātum arhasi 
 iti vaiśyakumārās tāṃ rohiṇaṃ prārthayari muhuḥ  Rm 
 ahaṃ maṃtrisuto vijñas tac chuklā me pradīyatāṃ 
 iti maṃtrisutāḥ sarve rohiṇaṃ pratyayācayan  Rm 
 mahāmātyasuto 'haṃ hi tac chuklāṃ me prayachatāṃ 
 ity āmātyakumārās tāṃ rohiṇaṃ pratyayācayan  Rm 
 evam anye 'pi lokāś ca rūpadravyābhimāninaḥ 
 svasvadūtena tāṃ śuklāṃ rohiṇaṃ pratyayācayan  Rm 
 evaṃ sarvaiś ca tair nityaiḥ prārthyamāno mahājanaiḥ 
 rohiṇaḥ sa viṣaṇṇātmā sthitvaivaṃ ca vyacintayat  Rm 
 hā me duḥkhāni jātāni katham atra pratikriyā 
 sarvathāhaṃ praṇaṣṭaḥ syāṃ sutayāḥ kāraṇe 'dhunā  Rm 
 yady ekasmai pradāsyāmi sutām etāṃ manoharāṃ 
 anye sarve 'pi me vairā bhaviṣyaṃti tadā khalu  Rm 
 avaśyaṃ me sutā hīyaṃ vairiṇī māṃ haniṣyati 
 evaṃ duḥkhānudāyinyā putryāpi kiṃ mamaitayā  Rm 
 iti cintāviṣaṇṇo 'sau tac cintākulamānasaḥ 
 Rm 
 kapolaṃ svakare sthāpya tasthau koṣṭhe nirutsavaḥ  Rm 
 evaṃ cintāvibhinnāsyaṃ pitaraṃ taṃ viṣādinaṃ 
 sā śuklā duhitā dṛṣṭvā praṇatvaivam abhāṣata  Rm 
 kim evaṃ tiṣṭhase tāta kiṃ te duḥkhaṃ nu jāyate 
 kathyatāṃ tad yadi sneho mayi te varttate pitaḥ  Rm 
 iti putryā vacaḥ śrutvā pitā sa ruṣitāśayaḥ 
 niḥsnehas tāṃ sutāṃ śuklāṃ dṛṣṭvaivaṃ paryyabhāṣata  Rm 
 tvan nimitte mahad duḥkhaṃ jāyate me kuputrike 
 kiṃ tavāgre kathitvaitaṃ yato naiva pratikriyā  Rm 
 avaśyaṃ tvaṃ sutā śatruḥ sarvathā māṃ haniṣyasi 
 evaṃ duḥkhābhidāyinyā putryāpi kiṃ mama tvayā  Rm 
 iti pitroditaṃ śrutvā sā śuklā prahatāśayā 
 sahasā pitaraṃ natvā rudaṃtyaivaṃ abhāṣata 
 tāta kiṃ me nimittena duḥkhaṃ te jāyate kathaṃ 
 sarvathaitat pravaktavyaṃ yadi te 'haṃ sutātmajā 
 tad upāyaṃ kariṣyāmi yena duḥkhaṃ nihanyate  Rm 
 tad etat sarvathā tāta mamāgre vaktum arhasi 
 iti putryodite bhūyaḥ pitāsau rohiṇo 'vadat  Rm 
 tat kin te kathyate putri yato nāsti pratikriyā 
 bahavaḥ prārthayitāras tava rājasutādayaḥ  Rm 
 kumārā brāhmaṇā vaiśyāḥ śūdrāś ca maṃtrinaṃdanāḥ 
 amātyanaṃdanāś cāpi sārthavāhasutādayaḥ  Rm 
 evam anye 'pi ye cānyā guṇadravyābhimānitāḥ 
 paurikā grāmikāś cāpi kularūpābhimānikāḥ  Rm 
 etaiḥ sarvair ahaṃ nityaṃ sumudritas tvadarthibhiḥ 
 katham atra kariṣyāmi cetanā me na vidyate  Rm 
 tvam evaikā hi me putrī bahavo yācakāś ca te 
 ekasmai yadi dāsyāmi sarve 'nye syur mamāhitāḥ  Rm 
 atas tvāṃ khaṇḍaśaḥ kṛtvā sarvebhyo 'py arpaye ca vai 
 evaṃ tu kriyamāṇe me kuśalatvaṃ bhaviṣyati  Rm 
 anyathā ced bhaven naiva kuśalaṃ me sadāpi hi 
 Rm 
 iti pitroditaṃ śrutvā śuklā sā mṛtyuśaṃkita  Rm 
 moditeva pituḥ pādau praṇatvaivam abhāṣata 
 prasīda mā kṛthāḥ khedaṃ mamaitat kāraṇe pitaḥ  Rm 
 tathāhaṃ te kariṣyāmi yathā doṣo na vidyate 
 nāhaṃ kāmārthinī tāta tad anujñāṃ pradehi me  Rm 
 pravrajitvā cariṣyāmi bhagavacchāsane vrataṃ 
 ity etad bhāṣitaṃ putryā śrutvāsau rohiṇaḥ pitā  Rm 
 putrīviyogam āśaṃkya punar evam abhāṣata 
 mā kṛthāḥ sarvathā putri pravrajyācaraṇe manaḥ  Rm 
 tvaṃ strī vālā na śaknuyāḥ pravrajyāṃ carituṃ sute 
 pravrajyāyāṃ vrataṃ kaṣṭaṃ puruṣair api duṣkaraṃ  Rm 
 tvaṃ tu vālā subhadrāṃgī komalā divyasuṃdarī 
 kathaṃ tad duṣkarasthāne vrataṃ kartuṃ saheḥ sute  Rm 
 tan mā kṛthās tathā vāle pravrajyāyāṃ manas tyaja 
 yadi kāmārthinī nāsi kasmai cid dāsyate na hi  Rm 
 tat putri svagṛhe sthitvā vrataṃ dhṛtvā sukhaṃ vasa 
 yadi kāmārthinī vāsi putri teṣāṃ tvadarthināṃ  Rm 
 svayaṃvaravidhiṃ kṛtvā svayaṃ vara yam ichasi 
 tadā me dūṣaṇaṃ nāsti tavāpi dūṣaṇaṃ na hi  Rm 
 sarvatrāpi hi lokeṣu vidhir eṣa pravarttate 
 tasmāt teṣāṃ kumārāṇāṃ patiṃ bhadraṃ svayaṃ vara  Rm 
 tenaiva patinā sārddhaṃ vrataṃ kṛtvā sukhaṃ cara 
 tadā santatim utpādya bhuktvā bhogyaṃ yathā sukhaṃ  Rm 
 saṃvṛtticaraṇaṃ kṛtvā tathānte svargam āpnuyāḥ 
 tenaivaṃ mā kṛthāḥ putri pravrajyācaraṇe manaḥ  Rm 
 kiṃ te pravrajyayā siddhyen mahadduṣkaracaryyayā 
 ity ukte janakenāsau śuklā kāmaparāṅmukhā  Rm 
 saddharmacaraṇaprepsuḥ pitaram evam abravīt 
 nāhaṃ kāmārthinī tāta saṃbodhipadavāṃchinī  Rm 
 tasmād bhogyāny api tyaktvā caritum ichāmi sadvrataṃ 
 sabhayāḥ saraṇāḥ kāmāḥ sakleśāś ca viṣopamāḥ  Rm 
 tasmāt kāme na me vāṃchā nirvāṇe eva me manaḥ 
 Rm 
 sadevāsuramānuṣyā ye satvāḥ kāmarāgiṇaḥ  Rm 
 sarve te kleśitāś cāndhāś caranti pātakeṣv api 
 kṛtvā te pātakāny evaṃ gachanti durgatiṣv api  Rm 
 vividhāni ca duḥkhāni bhuṃjate narakāsthitāḥ 
 brāhmaṇā api dhīrāś ca vaidikā brahmacāriṇaḥ  Rm 
 te 'pi kāmānurāgena bhraṣṭā gacchaṃti durgatiṃ 
 tapasvino mahābhijñāḥ śuddhātmānā jitendriyāḥ 
 te 'pi kāmānurāgena bhraṣṭā gacchaṃti durgatiṃ 
 yatayo yoginaś cāpi nirgraṃthāś ca digaṃvarāḥ  Rm 
 te 'pi kāmānurāgena bhraṣṭā gacchanti durgatiṃ 
 rājānaḥ kṣatriyāś cāpi kṛtvā yuddhaṃ parasparaṃ  Rm 
 āhave nidhanaṃ yānti tad api kāmakāraṇe 
 amātyā maṃtriṇaś cāpi mārayanti parārdhinaḥ  Rm 
 tatpāpair durgatiṃ yānti tad api kāmahetunā 
 yodhāraś ca mahāvīrā yuddhaṃ kṛtvā parasparaṃ  Rm 
 saṃgrāme nidhanaṃ yānti tad api kāmakāraṇe 
 vaṇijaḥ sārthavāhāś ca ratnadravyātilālasāḥ  Rm 
 samudre patitāḥ kecin mṛtāḥ kecic ca jaṃgale 
 kecin mṛtā mahāraṇye cauraiḥ kecid upadrutāḥ  Rm 
 kṣutpipāsāhatāḥ kecin mṛtā mārge rujānvitāḥ 
 śītavātātapākrāntā mṛtā kecic chramāturāḥ  Rm 
 kecid gṛhagatā eva mṛtāḥ kecic ca roginaḥ 
 kecid bhāraṃ vahantaś ca mṛtāḥ kecid bhayānvitāḥ  Rm 
 jantubhiḥ khāditāḥ kecit tat sarvaṃ kāmahetunā 
 kṛṣiṇaś ca dinaṃ yāvat kṣatrakarmasamudyatāḥ  Rm 
 dinānte gṛham agatya śerate te mṛtā iva 
 evam anye 'pi lokāś ca śilpipreṣyajanādayaḥ  Rm 
 dāsadāsījanāś cāpi svasvakarmasamudyatāḥ 
 evaṃ nityam aviśrāntaṃ kuṭuṃvadhanasādhane  Rm 
 vahaṃti kheditāḥ kleśaṃ tat sarvaṃ kāmahetunā 
 evaṃ caurādiduṣṭāś ca paradravyāpahāriṇaḥ  Rm 
 pātakāny api kurvanti tad api kāmakāraṇe 
 kecic ca paradravyāṇi haranti hārayanti ca  Rm 
 kecid dhatvāpi sarvaṃ haranti krūramānasāḥ 
 dhanārthe kiṃ na kurvanti duṣṭā lubdhāś ca nirdayāḥ  Rm 
 Rm 
 praghnanti pitarau kecit te 'pi ghnanti gurūn api 
 kecid vighnanti mitrāṇi jñātivandhujanān api  Rm 
 patnīputraduhitṝś ca bhrātrīṃś ca bhāginīr api 
 kecid ghnanti sahāyāṃś ca dāsadāsījanāny api  Rm 
 bālān vṛddhāṃś ca nārīṃś ca tat sarvaṃ kāmakāraṇe 
 kecic ca prāṇinaḥ pakṣimṛgamatsyādijantukān  Rm 
 hatvā khādanti pāpiṣṭhās tad api kāmakāraṇe 
 evaṃ tiryyaggaṇāś cāpi pakṣisiṃhādijantavaḥ  Rm 
 parasparaṃ nihatyaivaṃ khādanti kāmahetunā 
 evaṃ śathāvaṃcayantas trāsayanto 'pi vālakān  Rm 
 adattaṃ pratigṛhnanti tad api kāmakāraṇāt 
 mithyākāmaratāḥ kecit paradārāṃś ca kāminīḥ  Rm 
 haranti chadmanā cāpi tad api kāmakāraṇe 
 yac ca mṛṣāvadaṃto 'pi parakāryyābhighāṭakāḥ  Rm 
 sādhayanti svakāryāṇi tad api kāmahetunā 
 yac ca piśunavādena suhṛnmitrānucāriṇāṃ 
 virodhaṃ kārayanty evaṃ tad api kāmahetunā  Rm 
 yac ca pāruṣyavādena gurusādhujanān api 
 paribhāṣya vinindanti tad api kāmakāraṇe  Rm 
 yat saṃbhinnapralāpena suhṛnmitrānuyāyināṃ 
 cittāni bhedayanty evaṃ tad api kāmakāraṇe  Rm 
 yac ca māyānurāgeṇa sādhūnāṃ dharmacāriṇāṃ 
 prabhedayanti cittāni tad api kāmahetunā  Rm 
 yad īrṣyāmatsarālīḍhā dṛṣṭvā paraguṇarddhitāṃ 
 vyāpādaṃ cintayanty evaṃ tad api kāmakāraṇe  Rm 
 yan mithyādṛṣṭikā loke sarvadharmaprahāsikāḥ 
 bhogyāni bhuṃjate hṛtvā tad api kāmakāraṇe  Rm 
 kecij jātiparibhraṣṭā nīcajātiprasaṃgatāḥ 
 svakuladharmabhraṣṭāś ca tad api kāmakāraṇe  Rm 
 evaṃ sarve 'pi satvāś ca sadgatiparivartinaḥ 
 kāmarthe kleśitātmāno bhramanti durgatau sadā  Rm 
 Rm 
 evaṃ yāvanti duḥkhāni saṃsāre ṣaḍgatiṣv api 
 tāni sarvāṇi satvānāṃ jāyante kāmahetunā  Rm 
 evaṃ matvā tu ye vijñāḥ kāmaṃ tyaktvā virāgiṇaḥ 
 pravrajitvā suniḥkleśā brahmacaryyaṃ caranti te  Rm 
 tato me sabhaye kāme saraṇe ca viṣopame 
 vidvadbhir garhite tāta manovāṃchā na varttate  Rm 
 tatpravrajyāṃ samāśritya bhagavaccharaṇaṃ gatā 
 brahmacaryyaṃ caritvāhaṃ prāptum ichāmi nirvṛtiṃ  Rm 
 buddho hi jagatāṃ śāstā dharmarājo vināyakaḥ 
 tat tasya śaraṇe gatvā caritum ichāmi saccarīṃ  Rm 
 yady asti te mayi snehaḥ saddharme cānurāgatā 
 tad anumodanāṃ kṛtvānujñāṃ me dātum arhasi  Rm 
 yadi tu saugate dharme 'py anujñāṃ me dadāsi na 
 tīrthayātrāṃ bhramiṣyāmi sarvadāhaṃ virāginī  Rm 
 iti putrīvacaḥ śrutya śākyo 'sau rohiṇaḥ pitā 
 sutādharmaviyogatvaṃ vijñāyaivam acintayat  Rm 
 yad iyaṃ me sutā bhadrā nirāśravā virāginī 
 avaśyaṃ svagṛhaṃ tyaktvā pravrajet sarvathā khalu  Rm 
 avaśyaṃ me 'nayā putryā viyogaṃ sarvathā bhavet 
 sarvathā hy anivāryyeyaṃ vrajatu saugatāśrame  Rm 
 yadāyaṃ saugate dharme pravrajitvā nirāśravā 
 brahmacaryyaṃ caraty evaṃ tato nirvṛtim āpnuyāt  Rm 
 yad iyaṃ me sutā kāntā subhadrā divyasuṃdarī 
 yadi gehaṃ parityaktvā tīrthayātrāṃ kariṣyati  Rm 
 tadā nūnam iyaṃ bhrāṃtā tīrthikadharmasaṃratā 
 kuladharmaparibhraṣṭā vinaṣṭā syān na saṃśayaḥ  Rm 
 tato 'smākaṃ yaśodharmavinaṣṭo 'pi bhavet khalu 
 tasyāś ca dūragāminyā darśanaṃ syāt sudullabhaṃ  Rm 
 Rm 
 tasmād asyā na karttavyā vāraṇā dharmasādhane 
 caratu saugatīṃ caryyām iyaṃ hi nirvṛtaye  Rm 
 tathā cet saphalaṃ janma mānuṣye syān mamāpi ca 
 teneyaṃ jagatāṃ bhartuḥ śāsane caratu vrataṃ  Rm 
 ity evaṃ manasā dhyātvā śākyo 'sau rohiṇaḥ pitā 
 śuklāṃ tāṃ svātmajāṃ bhadrāṃ saṃnirīkṣyaivam abravīt  Rm 
 satyam evaṃ sute bhadre yathoddiṣṭaṃ tvayā khalu 
 kiṃ tu tvaṃ dārikā nārī pravrajyāṃ tat kathaṃ careḥ  Rm 
 pravrajyā duṣkarasthānaṃ nārīṇāṃ tu viśeṣataḥ 
 tat pravrajyāvrate sthitvā mā paścāt paritapyathāḥ  Rm 
 yadi tvaṃ niścayenaiva pravrajyāvratam ichasi 
 tac carasva munīndrasya śāsane vratam ādarāt  Rm 
 yathā ca guruṇādiṣṭaṃ śrutvā tathā samāhitaḥ 
 samyak chikṣāḥ samādhāya cara nityam atandritā  Rm 
 saṃbuddhaśāsanaṃ dhṛtvā śraddhābhaktisamanvitā 
 triratnaśaraṇaṃ gatvā bodhivrataṃ samācara  Rm 
 iti pitrā samādiṣṭe śuklā sā pratimoditā 
 natvā pādau pituś caivaṃ jananyāś caraṇe 'namat  Rm 
 tataḥ sā jananī dṛṣṭvā tāṃ śuklāṃ svātmajāṃ priyāṃ 
 pariṣvajya rudanty evaṃ pravrajyāyāṃ nyavārayat  Rm 
 hā putri katham ekānte māṃ tyaktvā kva vrajiṣyase 
 hā jīva kiṃ nu paśyantī pravrajituṃ tvam īhase  Rm 
 kiṃ cid duḥkhaṃ na te dattaṃ mayāmvayā kadā cana 
 kenaivaṃ hetunā putrī pravrajituṃ tvam ichasi  Rm 
 tvaṃ tu nārī subhādrāṅgī kumārī divyasuṃdarī 
 kiṃcid duḥkhānabhijñā ca tat pravrajyāṃ kathaṃ care  Rm 
 yāvaj jīvāmy ahaṃ caiva tāvat mā gāḥ kuhāpi hi 
 yāvac cāsti gṛhe saṃpat tāvad bhuktvā sukhaṃ vasa  Rm 
 yadāhaṃ maraṇaṃ yātā yadā cāpi gṛhe vipat 
 jñātimitrajanais tyaktvā tadā vrajasva vāṃchayā  Rm 
 iti mātrā niṣiddhe 'pi śuklā sā vighnaśaṃkitās 
 mātuḥ pādau praṇatvaiva sahasā niryayau gṛhāt  Rm 
 Rm 
 tataḥ sā satvarā gatvā nyagrodhārama āśrame 
 dadarśa bhikṣuṇībhikṣūn śantaśīlāñ jiteṃdriyān  Rm 
 tān sarvān kramato natvā vihāre samupāviśat 
 tatrasthaṃ sugataṃ nātham apaśyac chrighanaṃ jinaṃ  Rm 
 dvātriṃśallakṣaṇāśītivyaṃjanaiḥ parimaṃḍitaṃ 
 sahasreṇādhikābhāsaṃ vyāmābhaparirocitaṃ  Rm 
 śāntātmānam subhadrāṃśaṃ samantabhadrarūpiṇaṃ 
 ratnarāśim ivojjvālaṃ sumerum iva jaṃgamaṃ  Rm 
 dṛṣṭvaiva niścalā tasthau harṣotphullatanūruhā 
 dṛṣṭvaivaṃ sucirāt tasya śrīghanasyāntike yayau  Rm 
 tathaivaṃ samupāyātāṃ dṛṣṭvā tāṃ bhagavān muniḥ 
 svāgataṃ dārike bhadre ehīty uktvā samagrahīt  Rm 
 tato 'sau dārikā śuklā svāgatāsmi munīśvara 
 ity uktvā prāṃjaliṃ kṛtvā nanāma caraṇau muneḥ  Rm 
 tato bhagavatā tena preṣitā mātur antike 
 sā śuklā sahasā gatvā gautamyāc caraṇe 'namat  Rm 
 tathā tāṃ samupāyātāṃ śuklāṃ sadvratavāṃchinīṃ 
 dṛṣṭvā sā gautamī spṛṣṭvā hastenaiva samagrahīt  Rm 
 tataḥ pravrājayitvā sā gautamyā bhikṣuṇī kṛtā 
 khikkhirīpātrahastāṅkā saṃgatābhūj jitendriyā  Rm 
 yenaiva śuklavastreṇa prāvṛtā samajāyata 
 tataḥ paṃcasuraktaṃ jātāni cīvarāṇy api  Rm 
 tair eva civarai raktaiḥ prāvṛtā pariśobhitā 
 sā śuklā suprasannāsyā muṇḍitāpy abhyarocata  Rm 
 tato buddhānubhāvena supraśāntasubhāvinī 
 jitvā kleśārivargāṃś ca śikṣāpāraṃ samāyayau  Rm 
 matvānityaṃ ca saṃsāraṃ bhavagatiṃ vighātinīṃ 
 nihatya sarvasaṃskāragatīsatanadharmiṇī  Rm 
 māracaryyāvinirmuktā sākṣād arhatvam āyayau 
 avidyāṅgaṃ vinirbhidya prāptavidyā śubhāśayā  Rm 
 abhijñā guṇasaṃpannā pratisaṃvidvatī sudhīḥ 
 suvītarāgiṇī dhīrā loṣṭhahemasamānikā  Rm 
 Rm 
 ākāśasamacittā ca pāṇītalasamāśayā 
 niraṃjanāvikalpā ca śrīkhaṇḍatulyavāsinī  Rm 
 svātmasatkāralābheṣu parāṇmukhī sunispṛhā 
 sarvasatvahitādhāni saṃbuddhadharmacāriṇī  Rm 
 sadevāsuralokānāṃ pūjyā mānyā samantataḥ 
 vaṃdanīyā cābhitoṣyā ca vabhūva brahmacāriṇī  Rm 
 atha te bhikṣavaḥ sarve dṛṣṭvā tāṃ brahmacāriṇīṃ 
 vismitāḥ sugataṃ natvā paprachur iti sādaraṃ  Rm 
 bhagavan kim iyaṃ śuklā purā karmākaroc chubhaṃ 
 yena vastrāvṛtā jātā bhavaty evaṃ ca bhikṣuṇī  Rm 
 tat sarvaṃ naḥ samādeṣṭum arhasi sarvavid guro 
 yad anayā kṛtaṃ karma bhikṣuṇyā śuklayā purā  Rm 
 iti tair bhikṣubhiḥ pṛṣṭe bhagavān sa munīśvaraḥ 
 tān bhikṣusāṃghikān sarvān saṃnirīkṣyaivam abravīt  Rm 
 śṛṇudhvaṃ bhikṣavaḥ sarve yad anayā kṛtaṃ purā 
 tat sarvaṃ kathayiṣyāmi sarvalokābhibodhane  Rm 
 purāsminn eva bhadrākhye kalpe 'bhūt kāśyapo jinaḥ 
 saṃbuddhaḥ sugato nātho dharmarājas tathāgataḥ  Rm 
 sarvavidyādhipaḥ śāstā traidhātukavināyakaḥ 
 sarvajño bhagavān arhan brahmacārī hitaṃkaraḥ  Rm 
 sa munīndro jagannātho vārāṇasīm upāśrayan 
 mṛgadāve vane ramye vyaharac chrāvakaiḥ saha  Rm 
 bhikṣubhir bodhisatvaiś ca bhikṣuṇībhir upāsakaiḥ 
 sārddham upāsikābhiś ca yatibhiś ca maharṣibhiḥ  Rm 
 tatrastho bhagavān buddho sarvasatvahitāya saḥ 
 ādimadhyāntakalyāṇaṃ dideśa dharmam uttamaṃ  Rm 
 tadaikānyatarā kācic chreṣṭhibhāryā śubhāśayā 
 sukalyāṇārthinī śrāddhā saddharmamānasī sudhīḥ  Rm 
 kena cit karaṇiyena mṛgadāvam upācarat 
 tatra bhikṣūn kramād dṛṣṭvā saṃbuddhāntikam upāyayau  Rm 
 tatra sā samupāgatya dadarśa taṃ munīśvaraṃ 
 dvātriṃśallakṣaṇāśītivyaṃjanair upalakṣitaṃ  Rm 
 vyāmābhālaṃkṛtaṃ saumyaṃ śatasūryyādhikaprabhaṃ 
 supraśāntendriyāṃ kāmyaṃ samaṃtabhadrarūpakaṃ  Rm 
 Rm 
 ratnarāśim ivojjvālaṃ sumerum iva jaṃgamaṃ 
 tathā dṛṣṭvaiva prāmodāt sāṃjaliṃ samupāgatā  Rm 
 natvā pādau munes tasthāv ekāntike kṛtāṃjaliḥ 
 tataḥ sa bhagavān dṛṣṭvā tasyāś cittaṃ viśodhitaṃ  Rm 
 ādimadhyāntakalyāṇaṃ dideśa dharmam uttamaṃ 
 tat saddharmāmṛtaṃ pītvā sā śūdrī pariharṣitā  Rm 
 sasaṃghaṃ sugataṃ nāthaṃ bhojayituṃ samaichata 
 tataḥ sā svagṛhe gatvā sādhayitvā subhojanaṃ  Rm 
 saṃbuddhapramukhaṃ saṃghaṃ svāṃtargehe nyamaṃtrayat 
 tatra svasvāsanāsīnaṃ saṃbuddhaṃ taṃ sasāṃghikaṃ  Rm 
 pūjayitvā tadarhaiś ca bhojanaiḥ samatoṣayat 
 tataḥ sā śraddhayā tebhyaḥ sarvebhyo 'pi prasannitā  Rm 
 buddhapramukhasaṃghebhyaḥ pratyekaṃ cīvaraṃ dadau 
 tato nityaṃ ca sā bhaktyā cakre saṃbuddhasevanāṃ  Rm 
 tatpuṇyaiś cāpi saddharme pravrajituṃ samaichata 
 tato 'sau pitarau natvābhyanujñāpya prasādinī  Rm 
 bhagavacchāsane gatvā pravrajyāvratam ācarat 
 tasmāt kiṃ bhikṣavo yūyaṃ manyadhve yābhavat tadā  Rm 
 śreṣṭhibhāryā na cānyā sā śuklaivaiṣeti manyata 
 yad anayā prasādinyā buddhapramukhasāṃghike  Rm 
 pratyekaṃ cīvaraṃ dattaṃ pravrajyā cāpi sādhitā 
 etatpuṇyavipākena prāvṛtya śuklavāsasā  Rm 
 jātā pravrajitā caiṣā bhavati brahmacāriṇī 
 ity evaṃ karmajaṃ bhogyaṃ prāṇino bhuṃjate bhave  Rm 
 yenaiva yat kṛtaṃ karma tenaiva bhujyate phalaṃ 
 na naśyaṃti hi karmāṇi kalpakoṭiśatair api  Rm 
 sāmagrīṃ prāpya kālaṃ ca phalaṃti khalu dehināṃ 
 abhuktaṃ kṣīyate naiva karma kvāpi kathaṃ cana  Rm 
 nāgnibhir dahyate karma vāyubhiś ca na śuṣyate 
 jalaiś ca klidyate nāpi kṣīyate nāpi bhūmiṣu  Rm 
 anyathā ca bhaven naiva karmagatiḥ kathaṃ cana 
 śuklānāṃ śubhatā nityaṃ kṛṣṇānāṃ duḥkhatā sadā  Rm 
 miśritā miśritānāṃ ca jaṃtubhir bhujyate gatiḥ 
 tasmād apāsya kṛṣṇāni karmāṇi miśritāni ca  Rm 
 caritavyaṃ śubheṣv eva karmasu sukhavāṃchibhiḥ 
 Rm 
 tatheti bhikṣavaḥ sarve te ca lokaḥ sabhāsthitāḥ  Rm 
 śrutvā tat sugatādiṣṭam abhyanandan prasāditāḥ 
 evam etan mahārāja guruṇā me prabhāṣitaṃ  Rm 
 evaṃ rājaṃs tvayāpy evaṃ karttavyaṃ puṇyam ādarāt 
 puṇyam eva bhave vandhubhrātā mitraṃ suhṛtsakhā  Rm 
 nānyaḥ puṇyāt paraḥ kaścid vidyate bhavacāriṇāṃ 
 tasmāt puṇyaṃ svayaṃ kṛtvā lokeṣv api pracāraya  Rm 
 prajāś ca bodhayitvaivaṃ puṇyamārge pracāraya 
 ity evaṃ guruṇādiṣṭam upaguptena bhikṣuṇā  Rm 
 śrutvā tatheti rājāsau prābhyanandaj janaiḥ saha  Rm 
 ya idaṃ śuklāvadānaṃ jinavarakathitaṃ puṇyahetor narāṇāṃ
 śṛṇvanti śravayanti pramuditamanasaḥ sadguṇaprāptukāmāḥ 
 te sarve kleśamuktāḥ suvimalamanaso bodhicaryā carantaḥ
 satsaukhyāny eva bhuktvā munivaranilaye saṃprayātā vasanti  Rm 
  iti ratnamālāyāṃ śuklāvadānaṃ nāma samāptam

 X Hiraṇyapāṇyavadāna
 athāśoko mahīpāla upaguptaṃ jināṃśajaṃ 
 kṛtāṃjalipuṭo natvā punar evam abhāṣata  Rm 
 bhadanta śrotum ichāmi punar anyat subhāṣitaṃ 
 yathā te guruṇā khyātaṃ tathā vaktuṃ samarhasi  Rm 
 evaṃ tena nṛpendreṇa prārthite sa jinātmajaḥ 
 upagupto mahābhijñas taṃ nṛpaṃ caivam abravīt  Rm 
 śṛṇu rājaṃs tathā vakṣye yathā me guruṇoditaṃ 
 śrutvā caivaṃ sadā bodhicaryāṃ cara samāhitaḥ  Rm 
 puraikasamaye 'sau ca śākyamunis tathāgataḥ 
 sarvajñaḥ sugato nāthaḥ śāstā traidhātukādhipaḥ  Rm 
 sarvavidyādhipas tāyī ṣaḍabhijño munīśvaraḥ 
 jino 'rhaṃ bhagavān buddho dharmarājo vināyakaḥ  Rm 
 śrāvastyāṃ vahir udyāne jetavane jināśrame 
 anāthapiṇḍadārāme vihāre maṇimaṇḍite  Rm 
 bhikṣubhiḥ śrāvakaiḥ sārddhaṃ bhikṣuṇībhir upāsakaiḥ 
 triratnopāsikābhiś ca cailakaiś ca śubhāśayaiḥ  Rm 
 bodhisatvagaṇaiś cāpi sahānyaiś ca maharṣibhiḥ 
 osaddharmadeśanāṃ datvā tasthau lokahitārthataḥ  Rm 
 tat saddharmāmṛtaṃ pātuṃ prājagmuḥ sadguṇārthinaḥ 
 devā daityāś ca nāgāś ca yakṣagaṃdharvakinnarāḥ  Rm 
 siddhavidyādharādyāś ca lokapālagaṇādayaḥ 
 brāhmaṇāḥ kṣatriyāś cāpi vaiśyāḥ śūdrāś ca maṃtriṇaḥ  Rm 
 amātyāḥ śreṣṭhinaś cāpi dhaninaś ca mahājanāḥ 
 vaṇijaḥ sārthavāhāś ca tadanye 'pi ca sajjanāḥ  Rm 
 paurā jānapadāś cāpi sarve te samupāgatāḥ 
 taṃ buddhaṃ sugataṃ natvā pūjayitvā samaṃtataḥ  Rm 
 parivṛtya paraskṛtya tasthuḥ sāṃjalayo mudā 
 athāsau bhagavān dṛṣṭvā tān sarvān samupāsthitān 
 ādimadhyāntakalyāṇaṃ dideśa dharmam uttamaṃ  Rm 
 tat saddharmāmṛtaṃ pītvā sarve satvāḥ surādayaḥ 
 harṣitā anumodanto vabhūvur bodhicāriṇaḥ  Rm 
 Rm 
 evaṃ nityaṃ ca te satvāḥ pītvā dharmāmṛtaṃ muneḥ 
 triratnaśaraṇaṃ gatvā bhejire samupāśritāḥ  Rm 
 tadaiva samaye tasyāṃ śrāvastyāṃ puri saṃsthitaḥ 
 āsīd gṛhapatiḥ prāḍhyo mahābhogyasamṛddhimān  Rm 
 kuvelavan mahāśrīmān suvistīrṇaparigrahaḥ  Rm 
 śrāddho dātā mahābhogī sarvalokahitārthabhṛt 
 evaṃ maharddhikasyāpi tasya gṛhapateś ciraṃ 
 na putro na ca putrī vā samudapādi daivataḥ  Rm 
 tato 'putro gṛhastho 'sau vaṃśavichinnakheṭitaḥ 
 kapolaṃ svakare sthāpya viṣādyaivaṃ vyacintayat  Rm 
 anekadhanaratnādyāḥ saṃpado me maharddhikāḥ 
 viśālaparivārāś ca vidyante suparigrahāḥ  Rm 
 putro me duhitā vāpi vidyate na kathaṃ cana 
 saṃpado 'pi nirarthāḥ syur yato bhoktā na vidyate  Rm 
 hā hā sarvaṃ vinaṣṭaṃ syād yato me santatir na hi 
 kiṃ me 'nayā samṛddhyāpi yatra vaṃśo na vidyate  Rm 
 vyartham eva mayā dravyaṃ kaṣṭena samupārjitaṃ 
 kiṃ kariṣyāmi taddravyaṃ sarvathā maraṇe sati  Rm 
 ke hi grastā na saṃsāre mṛtyusarppeṇa jaṃtavaḥ 
 mayi mṛtyuprayāte 'tra saṃskāraṃ kaḥ kariṣyati  Rm 
 durgatiśodhanaṃ kaś ca piṇḍam ekaṃ pradāsyati 
 nūnaṃ madatyayād rājā sarvasvam āhariṣyati  Rm 
 tadā nāmāpi me loke na kaś cana grahīṣyati 
 yad artham eva saṃpattīḥ sādhayāmi prayatnataḥ  Rm 
 tad eva yadi nāsty evaṃ tat kiṃ me syāt sujīvite  Rm 
 varam evādya mṛtyur na mithyācirajīvanaṃ 
 yasmāc ciram api sthitvā mṛtyuduḥkhaṃ tadaiva hi  Rm 
 tan me bhogye 'pi vāṃchā na bhuktvāpi kiṃ sukhaṃ vinā 
 aputrasya sukhaṃ naiva paratreha niranvayāt  Rm 
 tan me janmāpi vyarthaṃ syād dhy aputro 'smi niranvayāt 
 hā hato 'haṃ svadaivena kiṃ mayātra kariṣyate  Rm 
 kasyāgre saṃvadiṣyāmi ko me buddhiṃ pradāsyati 
 Rm 
 kasyāhaṃ śaraṇaṃ yāsye ko māṃ samuddhariṣyati  Rm 
 iti cintāviṣaṇno 'sau tasthau koṣṭhe yathāturaḥ 
 nirutsāhī gṛhān naiva nirapāyāt kadācana  Rm 
 etac cintāviṣaṇṇābhaṃ taṃ gṛhasthaṃ suhṛjjanāḥ 
 dṛṣṭvaiva sahasopetya bodhayituṃ samabruvan  Rm 
 kiṃ te duḥkhaṃ samutpannaṃ kenaivaṃ tiṣṭhase sakhe 
 vaktavyaṃ cet tadā āśu sarvathā vaktum arhasi  Rm 
 iti pṛṣṭe suhṛdbhis tair gṛhasthaḥ sa viniśvasan 
 tān sarvān suhṛdo dṛṣṭvā tad duḥkhaṃ samudāharat  Rm 
 suhṛdo me bhavanto hi tan mayātra pracakṣyate 
 saṃpattir mahatī me 'sti putro naiva sutāpi naḥ  Rm 
 tena me saṃpadaḥ sarvā vinakṣyanti nirarthitāḥ 
 etac cintāviṣārttāhaṃ tiṣṭhāmi putravāṃchitaḥ  Rm 
 aputrasya sukhaṃ nāsti paratreha samaṃtataḥ 
 tan me janmāpi vyarthaṃ syād aputrasya niranvayāt  Rm 
 tathā hato 'haṃ svadaivena kiṃ mayātra cariṣyate 
 iti tenodite sarve jñātivaṃdhusuhṛjjanāḥ  Rm 
 tasya grīhapateś caivāṃ tad upāyaṃ samādiśat 
 kiṃ bhadrātra viṣādena yatra devādhikāratā  Rm 
 tathāpi kriyatāṃ yatnaṃ klaibyaṃ tyaktvā tvayādhunā 
 yad aśakyaṃ valair dravyais tad upāyena śakyate  Rm 
 tasmāt klaibyam iha tyaktvā kuru yatnaṃ samāhitaḥ 
 devatārādhanāṃ kṛtvā sarvakāryyaṃ hi sādhayet  Rm 
 tadādau devatāḥ pūjya yācasva putram ātmanā 
 tato devaprasādena tavadharmānubhāvataḥ 
 putro vā duhitā vāpi samupapatsyate dhruvaṃ  Rm 
 tatas te saṃtatiś caivaṃ varddhiṣyati kramāt tathā 
 tadāpi bhṛśato muktaḥ sadgatiṃ samavāpnuyāt  Rm 
 iti taiḥ samupādiṣṭaṃ śrutvāsāv anumoditāḥ 
 devatārādhanaṃ kartuṃ prayatātmā samārabhat  Rm 
 pūjāṃgaiḥ pūjayitvaivaṃ brahmāṇaṃ harim īśvaraṃ 
 iṃdrādilokapālānāṃ saṃtatiṃ samayācata  Rm 
 Rm 
 evaṃ putrābhilāsī sa sadā ca santatīchayā 
 devatārādhanaṃ kṛtvā tasthau nityaṃ samutsukaḥ  Rm 
 nityam evaṃ kṛtasyāpi tasya daivapraṇāmataḥ 
 na putro duhitā vāpi nodapādi cirād api  Rm 
 tathā cāpi gṛhastho 'sau devatāsu nirāśayā 
 santatyucchinnacintārttas tasthau bhūyo viṣāditaḥ  Rm 
 tataḥ kaścit suhṛt sādhuḥ saṃbuddhopāsakaḥ sudhīḥ 
 taṃ gṛhastham upāgatya tathaivaṃ paryyabodhayat  Rm 
 sādho kin te viṣādena tad dhīraṃ samupāśraya 
 yadi te santatau vāṃchā tan me śrutvā tataś cara  Rm 
 kim evaṃ devatāḥ pūjya yācase putram ādarāt 
 yatra daivādhikāratvaṃ tatra kiṃ devatā valaṃ  Rm 
 vaṃśārthe yadi te bhaktir asty evaṃ devatāsu tat 
 saṃbuddhaśaraṇaṃ gatvā saddharmaṃ samupāśraya  Rm 
 tato dharmānubhāvena buddhasyāpi prasādataḥ 
 nūnaṃ te satsutaḥ śīghram utpatsyati na saṃśayaḥ  Rm 
 yadi notpatsyate putras tava devavirodhataḥ 
 puṇyam utpatsyate nūnaṃ tena sadgatim āpnuyāt  Rm 
 ye buddhaśaraṇaṃ yānti te labhanti śubhāśayaṃ 
 ye viśuddhāśayā loke saddharmaṃ te śṛṇvanti hi  Rm 
 ye saddharmānuśṛṇvan to bodhicittaṃ labhanti te 
 pralabdhabodhicittā ye te caranti guṇārthinaḥ  Rm 
 guṇakāmāś ca ye loke te bhajanti jinātmajān 
 bodhisatvānubhāvena bodhicaryāṃ samāpnuyuḥ  Rm 
 bodhicaryāratā ye ca na te gachaṃti durgatiṃ 
 sarvakleśagaṇāñ jitvā saukhyāvatīm avāpnuyuḥ  Rm 
 evaṃ matvā jinaṃ smṛtvā saddharmaṃ samupāśrayeḥ 
 tatas te saṃbhaved bhadram ihāmutrāpi sarvataḥ  Rm 
 iti tenoditaṃ śrutvā gṛhastho 'sau 'numoditaḥ 
 tatheti pratisaṃśrutya saṃbuddhaṃ smartum aichata  Rm 
 tato gṛhapatir nityaṃ sadāraḥ śraddhayānvitaḥ 
 saṃbuddhaṃ sugataṃ smṛtvā vaṃśam evam ayācata  Rm 
 namas te bhagavan nātha bhavatāṃ śaraṇaṃ vraje 
 Rm 
 tan māṃ karuṇāya dṛṣṭyā draṣṭum arhasi sarvathā  Rm 
 bhavān eva hi jagannāthaḥ sarvasatvahitārthadaḥ 
 tvayā mahyaṃ hitārthāya satputraṃ dātum arhasi  Rm 
 ity evaṃ sa gṛhī sādhuḥ putrābhilaṣitaḥ sadā 
 sabhāryyaḥ sugataṃ smṛtvā tathā nityaṃ samutsukaḥ  Rm 
 tadaiva samaye kaścid devaputro divaś cyutaḥ 
 sa saṃbuddhānubhāvena tadbhāryāgarbham āviśat  Rm 
 tataḥ svāpannasatvābhūt sā bhāryā gṛhiṇaḥ satī 
 dohadalakṣaṇopetā kṛśāṅgī bhāvinī kramāt  Rm 
 pravṛddhagarbhā sā dṛṣṭvā svayaṃ ca garbham ādarāt 
 dakṣapārśvagataṃ satvaṃ matvā caivaṃ vyaciṃtayat  Rm 
 nūnaṃ me jāyate garbhe satvo buddhānubhāvataḥ 
 yad ayaṃ dakṣiṇe vartti tena putro bhavet khalu  Rm 
 iti niścitya sā nārī putrotpatyāśayā mudā 
 svasvāmino pure sthitvā rahasyaivaṃ nyavedayat  Rm 
 dṛṣṭyāryyaputra varddhasva yad ahaṃ garbhiṇī bhave 
 nūnam ayaṃ bhavet putro yat sthito dakṣiṇodare  Rm 
 iti bhāryoditaṃ śrutvā sa gṛhasthaḥ pramoditaḥ 
 daksiṇaṃ vāhum unnamya nandann evam udānayat  Rm 
 cirābhilaṣitaṃ putramukhaṃ paśyeyaṃ sāṃprataṃ 
 jātaḥ syān nāmajātā me kulavaṃśasthitir bhavet  Rm 
 kṛtyāni ca prakurvīta bibhṛyād bharaṇaṃ prati 
 nūnaṃ buddhānubhāvena satputro 'pi bhaviṣyati  Rm 
 yad asmākaṃ kṛtaṃ pūrvaṃ karma dānādikaṃ śubhaṃ 
 etat puṇyānubhāvena bhavet kuśalam etayoḥ  Rm 
 tatas tena sadā bharttā saha saṃmodacāriṇī 
 pathyāhāropacāraiś ca varddhito sukhacāriṇī  Rm 
 tataḥ sā samaye sūta putraṃ divyātisuṃdaraṃ 
 darśanīyaṃ susaumyāṅgaṃ prāsādikaṃ manoharaṃ  Rm 
 sarvāṅgalakṣaṇopetaṃ sadīnārakaradvayaṃ 
 sarvasatvamanāpīśam abhirūpaṃ subhadrikaṃ  Rm 
 tataḥ sā jananī tasya vālakasya karadvayaṃ 
 Rm 
 dīnārāṃkitam ālokya saharṣaṃ vismitābhavat  Rm 
 tato 'sau janakaś cāpi jātaṃ putramahādbhutaṃ 
 sakhībhir veditaṃ śrutvā vismito draṣṭum āyayau  Rm 
 tataḥ prajāpatiḥ sāpi vismito svāmino 'grataḥ 
 darśayitvā sutaṃ putraṃ śaṃkitaivaṃ nyavedayat  Rm 
 svāmiṃ paśya mahāścaryyam asya hemānvitau karau 
 tac chubhaṃ vāpy aśubhaṃ vā darśayitvā vicāraya  Rm 
 iti bhāryyoditaṃ śrutvā dṛṣṭvā taṃ vālakaṃ ciraṃ 
 dīnāraṃ bhujayoḥ paśyaṃ tasthau savismayānvitaḥ  Rm 
 tatas tasya gṛhastho 'sau nimittaṃ jñātum ādarāt 
 naimittikaṃ samāhūya dārakaṃ tam adarśayat  Rm 
 bhavanto dṛśyatām asya dārakasya karadvayaṃ 
 tan nimittaṃ parijñāya tat phalaṃ vaktum arhatha  Rm 
 ity ukte tena te sarve dṛṣṭvā taṃ dārakaṃ śubhaṃ 
 dīnāre bhujayoś cāpi parijñāyaivam abravīt  Rm 
 sādho gṛhapate hy asya dārakasya karadvayaṃ 
 suvarṇalakṣaṇopetaṃ tat te bhadraṃ bhavet khalu  Rm 
 tavāyaṃ dārako dātā maheśākhyo bhavet kila 
 svahastaṃ saṃprasāryyaiva hemavṛṣṭiṃ kariṣyati  Rm 
 apanīya svayaṃ hastād idaṃ dīnāram arpayet 
 apanīte punar anyat prādur bhavet tato 'dhikaṃ  Rm 
 ity evaṃ taiḥ samādiṣṭaṃ śrutvā saṃharṣito gṛhī 
 tato jātimahaṃ kṛtvā jñātīn evam abhāṣata  Rm 
 bhavanto dārakasyāsya śubhākṣarasamanvitaṃ 
 nāmadheyaṃ yathāyogyaṃ kriyatāṃ saṃprasiddhitaṃ  Rm 
 iti tenārthitaṃ śrutvā sarve te jñātayas tathā 
 dṛṣṭvā tasya nimittāni saṃmatenaivam abruvan  Rm 
 yasmād dhastadvayo 'py asya hiraṇyenopalakṣitaṃ 
 tan nāmnā prasiddho 'stu hiraṇyapāṇir ity ayaṃ  Rm 
 evaṃ jñātisamudiṣṭaṃ śrutvāsau sa gṛhādhipaḥ 
 tatheti tasya putrasya cakre nāmavyavasthitaṃ  Rm 
 tato hiraṇyapāṇiḥ sa dārakaḥ pratipālane 
 aṣṭāsu yo 'pi dhātrīṣu tena pitrā samarpitaḥ  Rm 
 tābhiḥ prapālyamāno 'sau pathyapuṣṭopacāraṇaiḥ 
 varddhito 'bhūt kramād āśu hradastham iva paṃkajaṃ  Rm 
 Rm 
 tathā kramāt pravṛddho 'sau hiraṇyapāṇir ātmavit 
 śrāddho bhadrāśayo dhīmān svaparārthahitārthikaḥ  Rm 
 tataḥ sa śikṣituṃ vidyāḥ sadguruṃ samupāśrayat 
 kramāt teṣāṃ prasādāc ca vidyāpāraṃ yayau laghuḥ  Rm 
 tato 'sau dārako vidvān dātā śraddhāsamanvitaḥ 
 svahastaṃ saṃprasāryyaiva dadau dānaṃ yathepsitaṃ  Rm 
 gurubhyo brāhmaṇebhyaś ca yācakebhyaḥ sa dārakaḥ 
 svahastaṃ saṃprasāryyaiva dadau hemaṃ yathepsitaṃ  Rm 
 tathā tad dānam ākarṇya śravaṇabrāhmaṇādayaḥ 
 arthino dhanalubdhāś ca saṃpratīyuḥ samaṃtataḥ  Rm 
 tathā taṃ samupetyaivaṃ sarvadigbhyaḥ samāgatāḥ 
 vālāvṛddhādayo dīnā yayācire yathepsitaṃ  Rm 
 tadā hiraṇyapāṇiḥ sa dṛṣṭvaitān arthino mudā 
 sarvopakaraṇaiś cāpi sarvāṃs tān samatoṣayat  Rm 
 tatas te yācakāḥ sarve tenaiva paritarpitāḥ 
 yathechayā sukhaṃ bhuktvā pracerur dharmamānasā  Rm 
 tathā vīthigataś caivaṃ hastadvayaṃ prasārya saḥ 
 hemarāśiṃ samutthāpya sarvebhyaḥ pradadau mudā  Rm 
 tathā sarve 'pi te lokā dhanāḍhyāḥ sukhino 'bhavan 
 naiko 'bhūt kṛpano duḥkhī no 'pi kaścid daridritaḥ  Rm 
 sarve 'pi dhaninaḥ prāḍhyā dātāro bhogino 'bhavan 
 satyadharmānuraktāś ca saddharmaśravaṇārthinaḥ  Rm 
 tadā tasyaiva tat kīrttiḥ sarvatra bhuvaneṣv api 
 lokair udgīryamāno 'sau prasasāra samaṃtataḥ  Rm 
 tad dṛṣṭvā brāhmaṇo lobhī mātsaryyaprahatāśayaḥ 
 tad yaśaḥ pratilabdhaṃ sa manasaivaṃ vyacintayat  Rm 
 yad asya bhujayor hema cintāmaṇisamaṃ khalu 
 tenāyaṃ bhavate śrīmān prārthitārthādhikapradaḥ  Rm 
 yac cāyaṃ dārakaḥ śrāddhaḥ prārthanāsaṃpradāyakaḥ 
 tad ahaṃ prārthanāṃ kṛtvā pratigṛhṇīya tat maṇiṃ  Rm 
 ity asau manasā dhyatvā lobhākṛṣṭo tvarānvitaḥ 
 Rm 
 taṃ hiraṇyabhujaṃ pretya tad dīnāraṃ samayācata  Rm 
 jayo 'stu te sadā sādho dīrghāyuś ca sumaṃgalaṃ 
 tathaiva tvaṃ sadā bhūyā arthināṃ kalpapādapaḥ  Rm 
 tvatkīrttyā samāhūtaḥ prāgato 'smi yad āśayā 
 tadarthaṃ pūrayitvā me cittaṃ harṣaya sarvataḥ  Rm 
 ity evaṃ prārthite tena vipreṇābhipragalbhinā 
 dṛṣṭvā hiraṇyapāṇiḥ sa taṃ vipraṃ pratyabhāṣata  Rm 
 sādhu vipra prasīda tvaṃ yadarthaṃ samupāgataḥ 
 tadarthaṃ saṃpradatvādya harṣayiṣyāmi te manaḥ  Rm 
 tac chaṃkā mā kṛthā hy atra yad yat te hṛdi rocate 
 tat tan nūnaṃ pradāsye te tad vadasva yad īhitaṃ  Rm 
 iti tenoditaṃ śrutvā vipro 'sau saṃpraharṣitaḥ 
 svastīty āśīrvaco datvā tad dīnāram ayācata  Rm 
 sādho hiraṇyapāṇe yat tava hastasamudbhavaṃ 
 tad dīnāraṃ pradatvā me cittaṃ saṃharṣayārthadaḥ  Rm 
 iti tenoditaṃ śrutvā tat pitāsau suvismitaḥ 
 savandhujñātimitras taṃ putram evam abhāṣata  Rm 
 śṛṇu putra mayā proktaṃ tavaiva hitakāraṇaṃ 
 yadi te svāminī prītis tat karttavyaṃ hi sarvathā  Rm 
 tvaṃ hi putra mayā labdhaḥ saṃbuddhasyānubhāvataḥ 
 tat saṃbuddhaśāsane kāryyam eva dātu samarhasi  Rm 
 yac cedan bhujayor jātaṃ dīnāraṃ maṇisaṃnibhaṃ 
 tad api sugatasyaiva prabhāvān manyatāṃ khalu  Rm 
 yac cedaṃ te karodbhūtaṃ jīvitaṃ sahajendriyaṃ 
 tat svakarāt samuddhṛtya kathaṃ dadyā dvijātaye  Rm 
 yadīdaṃ dāsyate hastāt samuddhṛtya valād api 
 tadā te jīvitaṃ vāpi sahānena vrajaṃ khalu  Rm 
 tasmād evaṃ parijñāya yadi te jīvita priyaṃ 
 tad evaṃ sahajaṃ hema mā pradāhi dvijātaye  Rm 
 tad anyad dīyatāṃ tasmai yad yad vastu samīchitaṃ 
 idaṃ tu sarvathānyasmai dātavyaṃ naiva yatnataḥ  Rm 
 yenaiva tvaṃ maheśākhyo sarvārthiprārthitārthadaḥ 
 tena yadā paribhraṣṭas tadā kiṃ tena manyase  Rm 
 yenāpi ca tvayā sarve yācakāḥ saṃpratarpitāḥ 
 Rm 
 tac cintāmaṇisāmānyaṃ kathaṃ dātuṃ samichasi  Rm 
 yat tvayā sukṛtaṃ karma prakṛtvā puṇyam ācitaṃ 
 nūnaṃ tasya vipākatvaṃ bhuṃjayos te pratiṣṭhitaṃ  Rm 
 tasmād idaṃ mahāratnaṃ kasmiñcin mā pradīyatāṃ 
 datvā tv idaṃ mahāratnaṃ kim anyal labdham ichasi  Rm 
 yadi tv idaṃ mahāratnaṃ dātum evaṃ pratiṣṭhitaṃ 
 saṃpradehi jinendrāya tat puṇyam akṣayaṃ vahuṃ  Rm 
 puṇyena labhyate janma śuddhavamṣe mahatkule 
 puṇyena dīyate kīrttiṃ nirvṛtiṃ ca samāpnuyāt  Rm 
 yadi puṇye 'sti te vāṃchā tad buddhaśaraṇaṃ gataḥ 
 dehi buddhānuśāsinyā tad dānaṃ hi mahatphalaṃ  Rm 
 tato nityaṃ sukhaṃ bhuktvā kṛtvā saṃbodhisādhanaṃ 
 kramād bodhicariṃ prāpte nirvṛtiṃ vā samāpnuyāḥ  Rm 
 iti pitrā samādiṣṭaṃ śrutvāsau hemabhṛt sudhīḥ 
 tatheti niścayaṃ kṛtvā punar evam abhāṣata  Rm 
 satyaṃ tāta tvayādiṣṭaṃ tat sarvaṃ hitam eva me 
 tasmāt tathā cariṣyāmi tvadājñāṃ śirasā vahan  Rm
