 kiṃ tu satyaṃ mayā proktām idaṃ dātuṃ dvijātaye 
 tat katham anyathā kṛtvā puṇyam eva samāpnuyāt  Rm 
 tat satyaṃ pūraṇe tāta pradadyāmi mamātmanaḥ 
 atha na dāsyate hy atra kiyat kālaṃ hi jīvitaṃ  Rm 
 yad idaṃ bhujayor hemaṃ mamātmasahasaṃbhavaṃ 
 tathaivaṃ sahajīvena vinakṣyati na saṃśayaḥ  Rm 
 yathedaṃ tu mahāratnaṃ mama devasamudbhavaṃ 
 tathaivaṃ saṃpradatvāsmai punaḥ prāpsyāmi te 'dhikaṃ  Rm 
 yathā buddhānubhāyena saṃjātaṃ karayor idaṃ 
 tathā satyānubhāvena punar anyaj janiṣyate  Rm 
 dharmeṇa tuṣyate buddho mūlaṃ dharmasya satyavāk 
 tat satyapāraṇārthena dāsyāmy aham idaṃ maṇiṃ  Rm 
 satyaṃ vinā na phullante puṇyāni prakṛtāny api 
 mlānibhūtāni naśyante śasyānīvāmṛtaṃ vinā  Rm 
 satyena varddhate dharmaṃ dharmeṇa pālyate naraḥ 
 dharmiṣṭhaḥ sadgatiṃ yāti tasmāt satyaṃ mahadvalī  Rm 
 tasmāt satyavalenātra yaśodharmārthalabdhaye 
 sarvathāsmai pradāsyāmi mā kṛthās taṃ nivāraṇaṃ  Rm 
 Rm 
 iti putravacaḥ śrutvā pitā sa vismayānvitaḥ 
 tathety abhyanumoditvā tasthau tūṣṇī vilokayan  Rm 
 tato hiraṇyapāṇiḥ sa matvā pitrādhivāsitaṃ 
 tad dīnāraṃ sahasotkṛtya viprāya pradadau mudā  Rm 
 tat pradattam asau vipraḥ pratigṛhya pramoditaḥ 
 datvāśīrvacanaṃ tasmai svagṛhaṃ sahasā yayau  Rm 
 tataś cānantaraṃ tasya bhuje 'nyat tadguṇādhikaṃ 
 dīnāraṃ divyaratnābhaiḥ prādurāsīn mahādbhutaṃ  Rm 
 tad dattānaṃtarodbhūtaṃ dīnāraṃ tadguṇādhikaṃ 
 dṛṣṭvā śrutvā ca sarve te lokā āśu suvismitāḥ  Rm 
 tato hiraṇyapāṇiḥ sa evaṃ lokān praharṣayan 
 saṃbuddhaśāsane dātuṃ jetavanam upācarat  Rm 
 tatra bhikṣūn yatīn dṛṣṭvā saddharmacaraṇotsukaḥ 
 saṃbuddhaṃ sugataṃ draṣṭuṃ vihāraṃ samupāviśat  Rm 
 tatrāsau bhagavantaṃ tam adrākṣīt samitisthitaṃ 
 dvātriṃśallakṣaṇāśītivyaṃjanaiḥ parimaṃḍitaṃ  Rm 
 vyāmaprabhāsam ujvālaṃ sahasreṇādhikaprabhaṃ 
 śānteṃdriyaṃ subhadrāṃgaṃ saumyarūpaṃ manoharaṃ  Rm 
 dṛṣṭvāsau suprasannātmā sahasā samupāgataḥ 
 natvā pādau munes tasya purastāt samupāśrayan  Rm 
 tatrāsau bhagavān tasya dṛṣṭvāśayaviśuddhatāṃ 
 ādimadhyāntakalyāṇaṃ dideśa dharmam uttamaṃ  Rm 
 taṃ dharmaṃ sugatādiṣṭaṃ śrutvāsau saṃpramoditaḥ 
 ānaṃdaṃ samupāśritya praṇamyaivaṃ vyajijñapat  Rm 
 bhadanta dātum ichāmi saṃghebhyo bhojanaṃ khalu 
 tad ājñāṃ dehi me śāsta yadi te 'sti kṛpā mayi  Rm 
 iti vijñāpite tena hiraṇyapāṇinā mudā 
 sa ānaṃdaḥ samālokya dārakaṃ taṃ samādiśat  Rm 
 sādhu vatsa mahābhāgyād bhadram ālocitaṃ tvayā 
 yady atra dāsyate bhojyaṃ kārṣāpaṇaṃ pradīyatāṃ  Rm 
 evaṃkṛte tu te vatsa maṃgalaṃ sarvadā bhavet 
 ataś ca durgatiṃ hitvā sadgatiṃ samavāpnuyāḥ  Rm 
 ity ānaṃdasamādiṣṭe dārako 'sau pramoditaḥ 
 svayaṃ hastau prasāryyaiva hemarāśiṃ vyadhāt punaḥ  Rm 
 tāṃ dṛṣṭvā bhikṣavaḥ sarve vismitāḥ saṃpraharṣitāḥ 
 Rm 
 taddravyaiḥ sādhayāmāsa bhojyāni surasāni ca  Rm 
 tataḥ sa dārako bhojyais taiḥ praṇītasusādhitaiḥ 
 saṃbuddhapramukhaṃ sarvasāṃghikaṃ samatoṣayat  Rm 
 tato 'sau bhojanānte ca saṃbuddhapramukhaṃ kramāt 
 sarvasaṃghaṃ praṇamyaivaṃ punas tasthau kṛtāṃjaliḥ  Rm 
 tataḥ śrībhagavān dṛṣṭvā tasyāśayaviśuddhatāṃ 
 āryyasatyaṃ samāyuktaṃ dideśa dharmam uttamaṃ  Rm 
 tac chrutvā hemapāṇiḥ sa satkāyadṛṣṭiparvataṃ 
 prabhitvā jñānavajreṇa viṃśatiśikharodgataṃ  Rm 
 śrotāpattiphalaṃ prāpto dṛṣṭasatyo 'bhavat tataḥ 
 saṃbuddhasagaṇaṃ natvā svagehaṃ harṣito yayau  Rm 
 tatra sarvaṃ sa tadvṛttaṃ pitror ākhyāya harṣitaḥ 
 pravrajyācaraṇānujñāṃ pitarau pratyayācata  Rm 
 cittaṃ me rocate tāta pravrajyāvratasādhane 
 tad anujñāṃ pradattaṃ me hitaṃ mayi yadīcchatha  Rm 
 iti putroditaṃ śrutvā svātmajaṃ sa pitāvadat 
 mā kṛthā sahasā putra pravrajyācaraṇe manaḥ  Rm 
 pravrajyācaraṇe bhaikṣyaṃ duḥkhinām eva tadvrataṃ 
 tvaṃ vṛddhimān mahādātā tat pravrajyāṃ kutaś careḥ  Rm 
 kiṃ vāpyate vivāhas tvaṃ daharaś ca kumārikaḥ 
 pravrajyā duṣkaraṃ sthānaṃ tat kathaṃ pracaret sutaḥ  Rm 
 tat tāvat tvaṃ yuvā putra vivāhitvā kulastriyaṃ 
 bhuktvā saukhyaṃ yathākāmaṃ gṛhe dharmaṃ samācara  Rm 
 tato vaṃśaṃ samutpādya kulasthitiprasiddhaye 
 kuladharmaṃ pratisthāpya tataḥ pravraja vārddhikaḥ  Rm 
 yadā vṛddho daridraś ca pravrajyāṃ hi tadā caret 
 yāvad yuvā samṛddhaś ca tāvat tvaṃ pravraja kathaṃ  Rm 
 saṃpattiḥ kṣaṇayauvanyam etan māravaladhruvaṃ 
 tadetadā kathaṃ putra pravrajyāvratam ācareḥ  Rm 
 ity etad duṣkaraṃ matvā pravrajyācaraṇe manaḥ 
 sarvathā tvaṃ vinirvārya kuladharmaṃ samācara  Rm 
 tatas te maṃgalaṃ nityaṃ imu putra bhaved dhruvaṃ 
 Rm 
 yaśodharmasukhānvetya sadgatiṃ cāpy avāpnuyāḥ  Rm 
 iti pitroditaṃ śrutvā dārako 'sau viśaṃkitaḥ 
 bodhayan pitaraṃ dharme punar evam abhāṣata  Rm 
 satyam eva tathā tāta yad etad bhāṣyate tvayā 
 tathāpi śrūyatāṃ tāta yad abhiprāyakaṃ mama  Rm 
 anityaṃ khalu saṃsāraṃ jīvitaṃ cāpi bhaṃguraṃ 
 kṣaṇadhvaṃsi śarīraṃ ca kṣaṇasaṃpad ghanopamaṃ  Rm 
 evaṃ paśyan ahaṃ tāta saṃsārabhoganispṛhaḥ 
 pravrajyāvratam āśritya prāptum ichāmi nirvṛtiṃ  Rm 
 api ca dullabhaṃ janma mānuṣaṃ bhavacāriṇāṃ 
 sarveṣām api jantūnāṃ maraṇaṃ sarvathā dhruvaṃ  Rm 
 mānuṣye labhyamāne tu kuto dharmānubhāvanā 
 vinā dharmānubhāvena kathaṃ sadgatim āpnuyāt  Rm 
 saṃbuddho 'pi sasaṃgho 'yaṃ sthāsyati na sadeha ca 
 anyatrāpi vrajen nūnaṃ nirvṛtiṃ vā gamiṣyati  Rm 
 saṃbuddhe nirvṛtiṃ yāte saddharmo 'pi vinakṣyate 
 saddharmāntargate loke mlechadharmavalī bhavet  Rm 
 mlechadharmavalīkrānte sarvatra bhūmimaṃḍale 
 sarvalokāś ca kāmāṃdhā bhaveyuḥ kleśamāninaḥ  Rm 
 tada dharmānusaṃvṛttau matiḥ kasyāpi no caret 
 pravrajyāsaṃvaraṃ dhartuṃ kaḥ samartho bhaviṣyati  Rm 
 naiva saṃyujyate cittaṃ pravrajyāsaṃvaraṃ vinā 
 aviśodhitacittātmā na yāyāt paramāṃ gatiṃ  Rm 
 tac cittaye viśuddhyarthaṃ nirvāṇapadalabdhaye 
 pravrajyāsaṃvaraṃ dharttuṃ ichāmi tāta sāṃprataṃ  Rm 
 tad yadi me hitaṃ draṣṭum ichasi tāta sarvadā 
 tad anujñāṃ samādātum arhasi mātra cāraye  Rm 
 iti puroditaṃ śrutvā pitā sa paribodhitaḥ 
 tathety anumataṃ kṛtvābhavat tūṣṇīvyavasthitaḥ  Rm 
 tadā tajjananī cāsau dṛṣṭvā taṃ sutam ātmajaṃ 
 snehād aśru vimocantī nivārayitum abravīt  Rm 
 hā putra katham ekānte māṃ vihāya kva yāsyase 
 mā putra sahasā gacha kiṃcit kālaṃ vinodaya  Rm 
 yāvaj jīvāmy ahaṃ tāta tāvan mā gāḥ kuhāpi ca 
 Rm 
 mṛtāyāṃ mayi bho putra tadā vrajasva vāṃchite  Rm 
 acireṇaiva māṃ mṛtyur grahīṣyati na saṃśayaḥ 
 tāvad eva gṛhe sthitvā dānaṃ kurvan sukhaṃ vasa  Rm 
 iti mātroditaṃ śrutvā putro 'sau parimoditaḥ 
 natvā tāṃ jananīm evaṃ bodhayitum abhāṣata  Rm 
 yat tvayāmve rudanty evaṃ mṛtyunāma prakīrtitaṃ 
 tena me coditaṃ cittaṃ pravrajyāvratasādhane  Rm 
 dhruvaṃ janmavatāṃ mṛtyur mṛtānāṃ janma ca dhruvaṃ 
 parivarttini saṃsāre mṛtaḥ ko hi na jāyate  Rm 
 dharmiṣṭho vīryāvāṃś cāpi maraṇaṃ yāti sarvataḥ 
 pāpiṣṭho nighnitaś cāpi maraṇaṃ yāti sarvataḥ  Rm 
 dharmiṣṭhaḥ satsukhaṃ bhuktvā mṛto yāty eva sadgatiṃ 
 pāpiṣṭho duḥkhatāṃ bhuktvā mṛto gachati durgatiṃ  Rm 
 yadā saṃtyajate jantuḥ saṃsāraprāṇavāyunā 
 tadā saṃtyajyate sarvair vaṃdhumitrajanair api  Rm 
 tadā na vidyate ko 'pi hitakārī sahānugaḥ 
 dharma ekaḥ sahāyaḥ syāt sarvatrāpi hitārthakṛt  Rm 
 tasmāt mātaḥ prayatnena karttavyaṃ dharmam ādarāt 
 dharmeṇa rakṣyate sarva ihāmutra sahāpi hi  Rm 
 dharmeṇaivābhipālyante vālavṛddhāturādayaḥ 
 dharmeṇa sudhṛtāḥ satvā nimagnā duḥkhasāgare  Rm 
 dharmeṇa jīyate duṣṭo dharmeṇa jīyate kaliḥ 
 dharmeṇa jīyate rāgo mṛtyur dharmeṇa jīyate  Rm 
 dharmeṇa sukule janma lakṣmī dharmeṇa sthīyate 
 vidyāyaśo 'rthamoksāś ca prāpyante dharmataḥ khalu  Rm 
 dharmaṃ tu saugataṃ kāryaṃ sarvalokahitaṃkaraṃ 
 sugatasyāpi dharmeṣu pravrajyādharmam uttamaṃ  Rm 
 yam āśritya mahāsatvā jitvā kleśagaṇān laghuḥ 
 sākṣād arhatpadaṃ prāpya vrajanti nirvṛtiṃ parāṃ  Rm 
 iti matvā hi te sarve bhikṣavo bhavanispṛhāḥ 
 pravrajyāvratam āśritya bhavanti brahmacāriṇaḥ  Rm 
 tathātrāhaṃ samichāmi pravrajyāvratam uttamaṃ 
 tad anujñāṃ pradatvā me nātra kāryo viṣāditaḥ  Rm 
 Rm 
 yadi na dīyate 'nujñā tad api no viyogataḥ 
 akasmān mṛtyunā ghrāya grasiṣyati puro hi naḥ  Rm 
 tadā kiṃ te kariṣyāmi mamāpi kiṃ kariṣyasi 
 kṛtvānuśocanāṃ caiva yāsyāmo maraṇaṃ dhruvaṃ  Rm 
 iti mātaḥ parijñāya tad anujñāṃ pradehi me 
 viṣādaṃ mā kṛthā atra prasādīnī bhavet prabhu  Rm 
 tathā te maṃgalaṃ nityam ihāmutrāpi saṃbhavet 
 ahaṃ ca saugataṃ dharmaṃ dhṛtvā nirvṛtim āpnuyāṃ  Rm 
 iti putroditaṃ śrutvā mātāsau paribodhitā 
 tathānumodanāṃ kṛtvā tasthau tūṣṇīvyavasthitān  Rm 
 atha hiraṇyapāṇiḥ saḥ pitror matvābhisaṃmataṃ 
 tayoś ca caraṇe natvā sahasā niryayau gṛhāt  Rm 
 tatra jñātigaṇāṃś cāsau vandhumitrasuhṛjjanān 
 kṛpaṇātithisaṃghādiṃ vāṃchitārthair atoṣayat  Rm 
 tato 'sau vāṃdhavān sarvān saṃtarpya paribodhayan 
 āśu jetavanaṃ gatvā vihāraṃ samupāviśat  Rm 
 tatrāsau sugataṃ dṛṣṭvā kṛtāṃjalipuṭo mudā 
 bhagavaṃtaṃ tam ānamya pravrajyāṃ samayācata  Rm 
 namas te bhagavac chāsta bhavatāṃ caraṇaṃ vraje 
 tat pravrajyāvrataṃ datvā brahmacaryaṃ pradehi me  Rm 
 iti tenārthite 'sau śrībhagavān tam abhāṣata 
 ehi bhikṣo kumāra tvaṃ brahmacaryaṃ carehi sa  Rm 
 iti prokto munīndro 'sau pāṇinā tac chiraḥ spṛśan 
 samyakpravājayitvāśu svasaṃghe taṃ samagrahīt  Rm 
 ehīti proktamātre 'pi jinendreṇa sa muṇḍitaḥ 
 khikkhirīpātrahastābhūc lcīvaraprāvṛtaḥ sudhīḥ  Rm 
 tataḥ śikṣāsu śikṣitvā prāpyopasaṃpado 'pi ca 
 vyāyacchad ghaṭamānaś ca samādhiṣu samāhitaḥ  Rm 
 tad idaṃ paṃcagaṃdaṃ ca bhavacakraṃ calācalaṃ 
 viditvā sarvasaṃskāragatiś cāpi vighāṭinī  Rm 
 bhiṃdan sarvam avidyāṅgaṃ prāpya vidyāḥ śubhaṃkarāḥ 
 pratisaṃvidguṇaprāpto jitakleśagaṇo yatiḥ  Rm 
 sākṣād arhatpadaṃ prāpya vītarāgo jitendriyaḥ 
 samaloṣṭasuvarṇaś ca vāsīcaṃdanasaṃnibhaḥ  Rm 
 Rm 
 ākāśasamacittaś ca nirvikalpo niraṃjanaḥ 
 saṃsārabhogyasatkāralābhalobhasunispṛhaḥ  Rm 
 paṃcābhijñapadaprāpto caturbrahmavihārikaṃ 
 sadevāsuramartyānāṃ traidhātukanivāsināṃ  Rm 
 pūjyo mānyo 'bhivaṃdyaś ca babhūva sa hiraṇyabhṛt 
 tatas te bhikṣavaḥ sarve dṛṣṭvā taṃ dārakaṃ yatiṃ  Rm 
 vismitāḥ śrīghanaṃ natvā paprachus tasya karmatāṃ 
 bhagavan kena dharmeṇa hiraṇyapāṇir ayaṃ sudhīḥ  Rm 
 sarvārthino hi saṃtarpya sākṣād arhan bhavaty api 
 iti tair bhikṣubhiḥ pṛṣṭe bhagavān tān tathābravīt  Rm 
 śrūyatāṃ bhikṣavaḥ sarvair yuṣmābhir vismitāśayaiḥ 
 anena yat kṛtaṃ karma tan mayā kathyate 'dhunā  Rm 
 purāsīd bhagavān buddhaḥ kāśyapo 'rhan munīśvaraḥ 
 sarvavidyādhipaḥ śāstā tathāgato vināyakaḥ  Rm 
 sasāṃghiko jinendro 'sau vārāṇasīm upāśritaḥ 
 bodhicaryāṃ samādiśya kṛtvā dharmamayaṃ jagat  Rm 
 sarvāṇi buddhakāryāṇi samāpya nirvṛtiṃ yayau 
 tadā rājā kṛkī nāma matvā taṃ nirvṛtiṃ gataṃ  Rm 
 vidhivad agnisaṃskāraṃ kārayitvā mahārcanaiḥ 
 tatas taddhāturatnāni garbha āropya sādarāt  Rm 
 hemaratnamayaṃ stūpaṃ kārayām āsa sa prabhuḥ 
 tat susiddhaṃ pratiṣṭhāpya sadvidhānair mahotsavaiḥ  Rm 
 mahaś cāpi tadā tatra sthāpayitvā bhajan nṛpaḥ 
 tasminn āropyamānāyāṃ yaṣṭyāṃ pūjāparigrahī  Rm 
 kintavo kaṃdaro nāma nidadhe rūpakadvayaṃ 
 tataḥ sa pādayor natvā praṇidhānaṃ vyadhāt tathā  Rm 
 yan mayā śraddhayā bhaktyāropitaṃ rūpakadvayaṃ 
 yat puṇyaṃ ca vipākena jāyeyaṃ sukule sadā  Rm 
 karodbhavasuvarṇaiḥ saṃtarpayitvārthino janān 
 evaṃvidhaṃ ca śāstāram ārogya samupāśritaḥ  Rm 
 etad dharmaṃ samāsādya prāpnuyāṃ paramāṃ gatiṃ 
 tena puṇyavipākena praṇidhānena bhūyasā  Rm 
 hiraṇyapāṇir ayaṃ dātā bhavaty arhaṃ sa sāṃprataṃ 
 evaṃ sarve 'pi saṃsāre bhuṃjate karmajaṃ phalaṃ  Rm 
 Rm 
 yenaivaṃ yat kṛtaṃ karma tenaiva bhuṃjyate phalaṃ 
 abhuktaṃ kṣīyate naiva karma kvāpi kadā cana  Rm 
 śubhaṃ vāpy aśubhaṃ vāpi bhuktaṃ tu kṣīyate khalu 
 nāgnibhir dahyate karma klidyate nodakair api  Rm 
 vāyubhiḥ śuṣyate nāpi bhūmiṣu kṣīyate na hi 
 anyathāpi bhaven naiva saṃsāre karmaṇo gatiḥ  Rm 
 śubhasya śubhataiva syāt kṛṣṇasya kṛṣṇataiva hi 
 miśrasya miśritaiva syād anyathā na sadā bhavet  Rm 
 evaṃ matvātha saṃsāre caritavyaṃ sadā śubhaṃ 
 na praṇasyaṃti karmāṇi kalpakoṭiśatair api  Rm 
 sāmagrīṃ prāpya kālaṃ ca phalanti prāṇināṃ khalu 
 ity asau bhagavān buddhaḥ satkarmadeśanāmataiḥ  Rm 
 tarpayan sa kalāṃl lokān tato viśrāntam ādadhau 
 iti śāstroditaṃ śrutvā sarve te bhikṣusāṃghikāḥ  Rm 
 śubheṣv eva sadā nityaṃ saṃpraceruḥ samāhitaḥ 
 mahārāja tvayāpy evaṃ caritavyaṃ śubhe sadā  Rm 
 bodhayitvā prajāñ caivaṃ sthāpanīyāḥ śubhe sadā 
 tatas te maṃgalaṃ nityaṃ sarvatrāpi bhavet khalu 
 kramād bodhicarīṃ prāpya saṃbodhipadam āpuṇyāḥ  Rm 
 iti tena samādiṣṭaṃ śrutvā sa nṛpatīśvaraḥ 
 tathety abhyanumoditvā prābhyanaṃdat sapārṣadaḥ  Rm 
 śṛṇvanti ye śrāvayantīha yaś ca hiraṇyapāṇer avadānam etat 
 te kleśamuktāḥ sugatānubhaktāḥ prayānti nūnaṃ sugatālayeṣu  Rm 
  iti śrīratnamālayāṃ hiraṇyapāṇyavadānaṃ nāma samāptaṃ 
 Rm 
 XI Hastakāvadāna
 athāśoko mahīpālaḥ kṛtāṃjalipuṭo mudā 
 upaguptaṃ guruṃ natvā bhūyo 'py evam abhāṣata  Rm 
 bhadanta śrotum ichāmi punar anyat subhāṣitaṃ 
 yathā te guruṇākhyātaṃ tathā me vaktum arhasi  Rm 
 iti tena narendreṇa pṛṣṭo 'sau sugatāṃśajaḥ 
 upagupto mahābhijñas taṃ nṛpaṃ pratyabhāṣata  Rm 
 śṛṇu rājan mahābhāga yathā me guruṇoditaṃ 
 tathāhaṃ te pravakṣyāmi tad anumodanāṃ kuru  Rm 
 puraikasamaye caivaṃ śrīghano 'sau tathāgataḥ 
 saṃbuddhaḥ sugataḥ śāstā sarvadharmānudeśakaḥ  Rm 
 śrāvastyāṃ vahir udyāne jetavane manorame 
 anāthapiṇḍadodyāne vihāre sugatāśrame  Rm 
 bhikṣubhiḥ śrāvakaiḥ sārddhaṃ upāsakaiś ca cailakaiḥ 
 bodhisatvair mahāsatvais tadanyaiś ca maharṣibhiḥ  Rm 
 vyaharat sarvahitārthāya dharmāmṛtaṃ pravarṣayan 
 tat saddharmāmṛtaṃ pātuṃ prayayur bodhikāminaḥ  Rm 
 lokapālā mahārājā svasvasainyajanaiḥ saha 
 brāhmaṇāḥ kṣatriyā vaiśyāḥ śūdrāś ca maṃtriṇo janāḥ  Rm 
 amātyāḥ sādhavaḥ paurā dhaninaś ca mahājanāḥ 
 vaṇijaḥ sārthavāhāś ca tathānye sarvajātikāḥ  Rm 
 sarvadigbhyaḥ samāgatya sarve te samupāgatāḥ 
 taṃ buddhaṃ sugataṃ nāthaṃ pūjayitvā samaṃtataḥ  Rm 
 parivṛtya purodhāya śakhyāviguṇakāmitāḥ 
 kṛtāṃjalipuṭo tasthuḥ saddharmacaraṇotsukāḥ  Rm 
 athāsau bhagavān dṛṣṭvā tān sarvān samupasthitān 
 ādimadhyāntakalyāṇaṃ dideśa dharmam uttamaṃ  Rm 
 tat saddharmāmṛtaṃ pītvā sarve lokādhipādayaḥ 
 harṣitās te 'numodanto vabhūvuḥ paribodhitāḥ  Rm 
 tadaiva samaye tasyāṃ śrāvastyāṃ purisaṃbhavaḥ 
 āsīd gṛhapatiḥ prāḍhyaḥ kuveravat samṛddhimān  Rm 
 śrāddho dātā mahābhogī sarvahitārthabhṛt 
 Rm 
 triratnasevako dhīmān suviśālaparigrahaḥ  Rm 
 saṃgṛhī vidhivad bhāryāṃ svakuladharmacāriṇī 
 pariṇītā yathākāmaṃ saṃrame paricārayan  Rm 
 tasyāsau ramaṇī bhāryā saṃvṛttā garbhiṇī satī 
 asūta samaye putraṃ prāsādikaṃ manoharaṃ  Rm 
 sa ca jātismaro vālo jātamātraḥ svakau bhujau 
 saṃdṛṣṭvāliṃgya cuṃvitvā pariṣvajyaivam abravīt  Rm 
 aho vatādya me hastau sucireṇa samudbhavau 
 aho labdhāv imau hastau sucireṇa mayādhunā  Rm 
 tenaivaṃ jātamātreṇa dṛṣṭaṃ kṛtaṃ prabhāṣitaṃ 
 dṛṣṭvā śrutvā ca sā mātā trāsitā vismitābhavat  Rm 
 kim etad iti saṃtrastā dṛṣṭvā taṃ dārakaṃ mudā 
 bharttāraṃ sahasāhūya agram enam adarśayat  Rm 
 tadāsau dārakaś cāpi dṛṣṭvā taṃ janakaṃ mudā 
 hastau dṛṣṭvā tathāliṃgya cuṃvayitvā caivam abravīt  Rm 
 aho vatādya me hastau sucireṇa samudbhavau 
 aho labdhāv imau hastau sucireṇa mayādhunā  Rm 
 iti saṃdarśayaṃ hastāv evaṃ cāpy avadac chiśuḥ 
 dārako 'sau punaḥ supto nidrāṃ bheje yad ichayā  Rm 
 tato 'sau janako 'py etad dṛṣṭvā śrutvā pravismitaḥ 
 kiṃ etad iti sāśaṃkā jñātin āhūya cābravīt 
 bhavanto 'dya prajātaṃ me putraratnaṃ manoharaṃ 
 tan nimittaṃ nirīkṣyaitat satyaṃ me vaktum arhatha 
 iti tenoditaṃ śrutvā sarve te jñātayo mudā 
 tat putraṃ dārakaṃ draṣṭuṃ tat koṣṭhaṃ samupādiśat 
 tathāsau dārakaś caivaṃ tān dṛṣṭvā samupasthitān 
 bhujau paśyan pariṣvajya cuṃvitvaivam abhāṣata 
 aho vatādya me hastau sucireṇa mayādhunā 
 bhavanto 'rhatsu mā cittaṃ dūṣayata kadā cana 
 kharāṃ vācaṃ ca mārhatsu niścārayata sarvadā 
 evaṃ saṃdarśayaṃ hastau vacanaṃ saṃvadaṃ śiśuḥ 
 dārako 'sau punaḥ supto nidrāṃ bheje yad ichayā 
 etat te jñātayo dṛṣṭvā śrutvā sarve 'pi vismitāḥ 
 kim etad iti bhāṣanto vabhūvuḥ parisaṃkitāḥ  Rm 
 tatas te jñātayaḥ sarve vijñāya tasya lakṣaṇaṃ 
 saṃmīlya tam upāmaṃtrya gṛhasthaḥ pratiharṣitaḥ  Rm 
 tasya jātimahaṃ kṛtvā punar evam avocata 
 bhadanto dārakasyāsya nāmadheyaṃ pramāṇataḥ  Rm 
 Rm 
 yathāyogyaprasiddhena karttum arhatha sāṃprataṃ 
 iti tenoditaṃ śrutvā sarve te jñātayas tataḥ  Rm 
 saṃmīlya saṃmataṃ kṛtvā taṃ gṛhasthaṃ samabruvan 
 yad ayaṃ te suto vālo jātamātraḥ svakau bhujau  Rm 
 paśyan āliṃgyā cuṃvitva mudā caivaṃ prabhāṣate 
 tad ayaṃ dārako nāmnā hastaka iti viśrutaḥ  Rm 
 bhavatu sarvalokeṣu suciraṃ cāpi jīvatu 
 tatheti pratinaṃditvā gṛhastho 'sau pramoditaḥ  Rm 
 tena nāmnā prasiddhena prathayām āsa taṃ sutaṃ 
 tato 'sau dārakas tena pitrā putrābhinaṃditaḥ 
 upanyastopadhātrīṣu dhāraṇapratipālane  Rm 
 tatas tāsāṃ prayatnaiḥ sa pathyopacāraṇaiḥ kramāt 
 dine dine pravṛddho 'bhūd hradastham iva paṃkajaṃ  Rm 
 evaṃ sa hastakas tābhiḥ pālyamānaḥ pravarddhitaḥ 
 kumāraḥ sakhibhiḥ sārddhaṃ krīḍāsthānaṃ gato 'ramat  Rm 
 tatra teṣāṃ sakhīnāṃ ca hastako 'sau puraḥsthitaḥ 
 hastāv āliṃgya saṃrakṣya cuṃvitvaivam abhāṣata  Rm 
 aho vatādya me hastau sucireṇa samudbhavau 
 aho labdhāv imau hastau sucireṇa mayādhunā  Rm 
 bhavanto 'rhatsu mā cittaṃ dūṣayata kadācana 
 kharāṃ vācaṃ ca mārhatsu niścārayata keṣu cit  Rm 
 iti saṃrakṣitau hastau tenaivaṃ ca prabhāṣitaṃ 
 dṛṣṭvā śrutvābhavan sarve sakhāyātīvavismitāḥ  Rm 
 tataś ca janakenāsau lipiśālāniveśitaḥ 
 guruṃ samyag upāśritya vidyāpāraṃ yayau laghu  Rm 
 tatra teṣāṃ guruṇāṃ ca hastako 'sau puraḥsthitaḥ 
 hastau dṛṣṭvā samāliṃgya cuṃvitvā caivam abravīt  Rm 
 aho vatādya me hastau sucireṇa samudbhavau 
 aho labdhav imau hastau sucireṇa mayādhunā  Rm 
 bhavanto 'rhatsu mā cittaṃ dūṣayata kadā cana 
 kharāṃ vācaṃ ca mārhatsu niścārayata keṣu cit  Rm 
 iti dṛṣṭvā ca saṃśrutya sarve te guravo 'pi ca 
 sarve śiṣya gaṇāś cāpi vabhūvur vismayānvitāḥ 
 yasmiṃś ca samaye tatra deśe bhayaupakrame 
 Rm 
 janakāyaḥ samudbhrānto 'gopāyat svasvabhāṇḍakaṃ 
 tadāsau hastako 'py evaṃ samudbhrāntaḥ svakau bhujau 
 saṃbhujya gopayitvaivaṃ janakāyam abhāṣata 
 aho vatādya me hastau sucireṇa samudbhavau 
 aho labdhāv imau hastau sucireṇa mayādhunā 
 bhavanto 'rhatsu mā cittaṃ dūṣayata kadā cana 
 kharāṃ vācaiva mārhatsu niścārayata keṣu cit 
 evaṃ hastau susaṃrakṣya tenaivaṃ ca prabhāṣitaṃ 
 dṛṣṭvā śrutvā ca te sarve lokā āsan suvismitāḥ  Rm 
 tato 'sau hastako 'nyasmiṃ divase sakhibhiḥ saha 
 jetavanaṃ mahodyānaṃ jināśrame upāyayau  Rm 
 tatrādrākṣīt mahābuddhaṃ bhagavantaṃ sabhāsthitaṃ 
 dvātriṃśallakṣaṇāśītivyaṃjanaiḥ parimaṃḍitaṃ  Rm 
 vyāmaprabhāsamuddīptaṃ śatasūryādhikaprabhaṃ 
 śāntendriyaṃ subhadrāṃgaṃ saumyakāntaṃ manoharaṃ  Rm 
 dṛṣṭvāsau suprasannātmā sahasā samupāgataḥ 
 pādau tasya muner natvā dharmaṃ śrotuṃ puro 'viśat  Rm 
 tato 'sau bhagavān tasya dṛṣṭvāśayaṃ viśodhitaṃ 
 ādimadhyāntakalyāṇaṃ dideśa dharmam uttamaṃ  Rm 
 taṃ sugatoditaṃ dharmaṃ āryyasatyasamanvitaṃ 
 śrutvāsau hastako vijñaḥ satkāyadṛṣṭiparvataṃ  Rm 
 saṃbhidya jñānavajreṇa viṃśatiśikharodgataṃ 
 śrotāpattiphalaṃ prāpto dṛṣṭasatyo 'bhavat tataḥ  Rm 
 saṃbuddhasugataṃ natvā svagehaṃ sahasā yayau  Rm 
 tatraitat sarvavṛttāṃtaṃ pitror ājñāya harṣitaḥ 
 pravrajyāsādhane 'nujñāṃ pitarau pratyayācata  Rm 
 cittaṃ me rocate tāta pravrajyāvratasādhane 
 tad anujñāṃ pradattaṃ me hitaṃ mayi yadīchatha  Rm 
 iti putroditaṃ śrutvātmajaṃ taṃ pitāvadat 
 mā kṛthāḥ sahasā putra pravrajyāsādhane manaḥ  Rm 
 pravrajyā duṣkaraṃ sthānaṃ tad anyadvratam ācara 
 pravrajyāgrahaṇaṃ vṛddhe daridrite suśobhite  Rm 
 tvaṃ ca putra kumāro 'si daharo 'tisukomalaḥ 
 kiṃcid duḥkhe 'nabhijñāya tat pravrajyāṃ careḥ kathaṃ  Rm 
 tad yāvad yauvanaṃ dehaṃ yāvat saṃpac ca te gṛhe 
 tāvad gehe sukhaṃ bhuktvā gṛhī dharmaṃ samācara  Rm 
 yadā vṛddho daridro ca pravrajyāyāṃ tadā cara 
 Rm 
 yāvad yuvā samṛddhaś ca tāvat tvaṃ pravrajeḥ kathaṃ  Rm 
 saṃpattikṣaṇayauvanyaṃ etan mārasya gocaraṃ 
 tad etasmiṃ kathaṃ putra pravrajyāvratam ācareḥ  Rm 
 ity etad duṣkaraṃ matvā pravrajyācaraṇe manaḥ 
 yatnenāpi vinivārya kuladharme samāśraya  Rm 
 tatas te maṃgalaṃ nityam ihāmutrāpi sarvataḥ 
 yaśodharmasukhāny evaṃ sadgatiṃ samavāpnuyāḥ  Rm 
 iti vākyaṃ pituḥ śrutvā hastako 'sau viśaṃkitaḥ 
 pitarau bodhayan dharme punar evam abhāṣata  Rm 
 satyam etat tathā tāta tvayaivaṃ satyam ucyate 
 atrāpi śrūyatāṃ tāta mamābhiprāyam ucyatāṃ  Rm 
 anityaṃ khalu saṃsāraṃ jīvitaṃ cāpi caṃcaraṃ 
 kṣaṇadhvaṃsi śarīraṃ ca saṃpac cāpi ghanopamā  Rm 
 evaṃ dṛṣṭvā ha tātāhaṃ saṃsārasukhaniḥspṛhaḥ 
 pravrajyāvratam ādhāya prāptum ichāmi sadgatiṃ  Rm 
 api ca janma mānuṣyaṃ dullabhaṃ bhavacāriṇāṃ 
 tatrāpi maraṇaṃ nityaṃ purataḥ sarvasaṃmukhaṃ  Rm 
 mānuṣyaṃ labhyamāne hi kuto dharmānucāritaṃ 
 vinā dharmānucāreṇa sadgatiṃ katham āpnuyāṃ  Rm 
 saṃbuddho 'pi sadā nātra saṃsthāpyati sasāṃghikaḥ 
 ato 'nyatrāpi yāyād vā nirvṛtiṃ cāvrajet khalu  Rm 
 saṃbuddhe nirvṛtiṃ yāte saddharma lapsyate kutaḥ 
 saddharmāntargate loke māracaryyā samācaret  Rm 
 māracaryyāsamākrānte sarvatra bhuvaneṣv api 
 sarve satvāś ca kāmārttā bhaveyuḥ kleśabhāginaḥ  Rm 
 tadā dharmānucāreṣu buddhiḥ kasya kathaṃ caret 
 pravrajyāsaṃvaraṃ sthātuṃ kaḥ samartho bhavet tadā  Rm 
 na ca saṃśuddhyate cittaṃ pravrajyāsaṃvaraṃ vinā 
 aviśodhitacitte hi naiva yāyāc chivāṃ gatiṃ  Rm 
 tac cittapariśuddhyarthaṃ nirvṛte ca yad āptaye 
 pravrajyāvratam ādātum ichāmi tāta sāṃprataṃ  Rm 
 yad atra yadi me tāta hitaṃ kartuṃ samichasi 
 pravrajyāsādhane 'nujñāṃ dātuṃ me prārhasi drutaṃ  Rm 
 iti putravacaḥ śrutva sa gṛhastho 'nubodhitaḥ 
 Rm 
 tathety abhyanumoditvā tad anujñāṃ vyasṛjata  Rm 
 tac chrutvā jananī cāsau dṛṣṭvā taṃ putram ātmajaṃ 
 viyogaduḥkhasaṃkārtā rundanty evaṃ nyavārayat  Rm 
 hā putra katham ekānte māṃ vihāya kva yāsyasi 
 sahasā putra mā kārṣī pravrajyācaritaṃ manaḥ  Rm 
 yāvaj jīvāmy ahaṃ jīva tāvan mā pravrajātmaje 
 mṛtāyāṃ mayi putra tvaṃ pravrajasva yathechayā  Rm 
 acireṇa hi me mṛtyur bhaviṣyati na saṃśayaḥ 
 tāvad eva gṛhe dharmaṃ kurvan bhuktvā sukhaṃ vasa  Rm 
 iti mātur vacaḥ śrutvā putro 'sau paricoditaḥ 
 mātaraṃ tāṃ praṇatvaivaṃ bodhayitum abhāṣata  Rm 
 yat tvayāmve rudanty evaṃ mṛtyunāmātra kīrttyate 
 tena me preritaṃ cittaṃ pravrajyāvratadhāraṇe  Rm 
 dhruvaṃ janmavatāṃ mṛtyuḥ saṃsāre parivarttinaḥ 
 jāto na mriyate ko hi mṛtaḥ kaś ca na jāyate  Rm 
 gṛhastho dharmakṛc cāpi yāty evaṃ maraṇaṃ dhruvaṃ 
 brahmacārī vanastho 'pi yāty evaṃ maraṇaṃ khalu  Rm 
 gṛhastho bahubhir yatnaiḥ prakṛtvā dravyasādhanaṃ 
 kṛcchreṇa sādhayan dharmaṃ mṛto yāti surālayaṃ  Rm 
 yāvad dharmaphalaṃ svarge tāvad bhuktvā sukhaṃ vaset 
 tato dharmaphale hīne svargāc cyuto yated adhaḥ  Rm 
 adholokeṣv avīcyādau narakeṣu bhramec ciraṃ 
 vividhāni ca duḥkhāni bhuktvā jīvaṃ ciraṃ vaset  Rm 
 yāvan na jāyate tasya puṇyānumodanā matau 
 tāvat karmajaduḥkhāni prabhuktvā narake caret  Rm 
 yadā tu jāyate tasya triratnasmaraṇe matiḥ 
 tadā tatsmṛtipuṇyena dharme 'numodyate matiḥ  Rm 
 yadā puṇyānurāgeṇa saṃbuddhaśaraṇaṃ vrajet 
 tadā taṃ sugataṃ dṛṣṭvā dharmākaraiḥ parispṛśet  Rm 
 sugate dṛkprabhāspṛṣṭe pāpaduḥkhair vimocitaḥ 
 narakebhyaḥ samuttīrya prayāyāt sugatālayaṃ  Rm 
 tatrāpi yadi dharmeṣu caran nityam ataṃdritaḥ 
 kramād bodhicarīṃ prāpya prayāyāt paramāṃ gatiṃ  Rm 
 evaṃ māta gṛhastho hi kṛtvāpi dharmam ādarāt 
 Rm 
 sukhaduḥkhāni saṃbhuktvā saṃsāre carate bhraman  Rm 
 kathaṃ cit sucireṇaivaṃ sugatasya prasādataḥ 
 bhavacārakanirmuktaṃ prayāyāt paramāṃ gatiṃ  Rm 
 pravrajyārhatpadaṃ prāpya prāptum ichāmi nirvṛtiṃ 
 tan mamātra tvayā māta naiva kāryā nivāraṇā  Rm 
 yadi puṇye 'sti te vāṃchā tad anujñāśu dīyatāṃ 
 yadi na dīyate 'nujñā tad api nau viyogatā  Rm 
 akasmāt mṛtyur āgatya bhaviṣyati purāpi nau 
 tadā te kiṃ kariṣyāmi kiṃ mamāpi kariṣyasi  Rm 
 sadānuśocanām eva kṛtvā jīvaṃ tyajevahi 
 iti mātar viditvā tvaṃ tadanujñāṃ pradehi me  Rm 
 vighnatāṃ mā kṛthā hy atra dharme bhavānumodinī 
 tathā cec chubhatā nityam ihāmutrāpi te bhavet  Rm 
 ahaṃ ca saugatiṃ caryāṃ kṛtvā yāsyāmi nirvṛtīṃ 
 iti putroditaṃ śrutvā matāsau paribodhitā  Rm 
 tathānumodanāṃ kṛtvābhavat tūṣṇīvyavasthitā  Rm 
 athāsau hastako vijñaḥ pitror matvābhisaṃmataṃ 
 tayoḥ pādān praṇatvaivaṃ sahasā niryayau gṛhāt  Rm 
 tato jñātigaṇān sarvān vandhumitrasuhṛjjanān 
 sarvān atithivargāṃś ca vāṃchitārthaiḥ pratoṣayan  Rm 
 santarpya bodhayitvā ca sahasā saṃpraharṣitaḥ 
 jetavanaṃ pragatvā sa vihāraṃ samupāviśat  Rm 
 tatrasthaṃ sugataṃ dṛṣṭvā sahasā samupāyataḥ 
 kṛtāṃjalipuṭo natvā pravrajyāṃ samayācata  Rm 
 namas te bhagavan nātha bhavatāṃ śaraṇaṃ vraje 
 tat pravrajyāṃ vrataṃ dehi cariṣye brahmasaṃvaraṃ  Rm 
 iti tenārthite buddho bhagavān tam abhāṣata 
 ehi bhikṣo kumārātra cara brahmavrataṃ varaṃ  Rm 
 ity ādiśya munīndro 'sau pāṇinā tac chiraḥ spṛśan 
 samyak pravrājayitvāśu svasaṃghe taṃ samagrahīt  Rm 
 ehīty ādiṣṭamātre 'pi munīndreṇa sa hastakaḥ 
 muṇḍitaḥ khiṣkhirīpātrahasto 'bhūc cīvarāvṛtaḥ  Rm 
 kramāc chikṣā samāsādya prāpyopasaṃpado 'pi ca 
 vyāyaccha ghaṭamānaś ca samādhiṣu samāhitaḥ  Rm 
 tad idaṃ paṃcagaṃḍaṃ ca bhavacakraṃ calācalaṃ 
 viditvā sarvasaṃskāragatiś cāpi vighātinī  Rm 
 bhindan sarvam avidyāṅgaṃ prāpya vidyāgaṇāḥ śivāḥ 
 Rm 
 pratisaṃvidguṇāḥ prāpya jitvā kleśagaṇāṃ yatiḥ  Rm 
 sākṣād arhatpadaṃ prāptaḥ vītarāgo jiteṃdriyaḥ 
 samaloṣṭahiraṇyaś ca vāsīcaṃdanasaṃnibhaḥ  Rm 
 ākāśasamacittāṃgo nirvikalpo niraṃjanaḥ 
 saṃsārabhogyasatkāralābhalobhaparāṅmukhaḥ  Rm 
 paṃcābhijñāpadaprāptaś caturbrahmavihārakaḥ 
 sadevāsuramartyānāṃ traidhātukanivāsināṃ  Rm 
 pūjyo mānyo 'bhivaṃdyo 'bhūd dhastako 'rhaṃ yatiḥ sudhīḥ 
 sahasā kleśagaṇāñ jitvā sākṣād arhan bhavaty api  Rm 
 tatas te bhikṣavaḥ sarve dṛṣṭvā taṃ dārakaṃ yatiṃ 
 vismitāḥ śrīghanaṃ natvā paprachus tasya karmatāṃ  Rm 
 tad adya bhagavac chāstaḥ sarvasatvānubodhaye 
 yad anena kṛtaṃ karma tat samādeṣṭum arhati  Rm 
 iti te bhikṣubhiḥ pṛṣṭe bhagavān sa munīśvaraḥ 
 tān svaśiṣyān yatīn bhikṣūn samāmaṃtryābravīt tathā  Rm 
 śṛṇudhvaṃ bhikṣavaḥ sarve yūyaṃ hi vismayānvitāḥ 
 yad anena kṛtaṃ karma tan mayā vaḥ pracakṣyatāṃ  Rm 
 purāsīd bhagavān buddhaḥ kāśyapo nāma sarvavit 
 ssarvatraidhātukādhīśaḥ sarvavidyādhipo jinaḥ  Rm 
 dharmarājo jagacchāstā tathāgato vināyakaḥ 
 sarvadharmānusaṃbharttā saṃbodhisaṃprakāśitaḥ  Rm 
 sasāṃghiko munīndro 'sau vārāṇasīm upāśritaḥ 
 sarvasatvahitārthena tasthau dharmaṃ samādiśat  Rm 
 tasya saddharmarājasya kāśyapasya jagadguroḥ 
 śāsane dvau yatī bhikṣū saṃśītikau vabhūvatuḥ  Rm 
 tayor eko mahādhīro vinīto 'rhaṃ vahuśrutaḥ 
 dvitīyo 'lpaśrutaḥ bhikṣuḥ pṛthagjanasamānikaḥ  Rm 
 yo 'sāv arhan mahāvijño vahuśruto vicakṣaṇaḥ 
 sa jñāto 'rhan mahāpuṇyaḥ sarvalokaiḥ prapūjitaḥ  Rm 
 yo 'bhūc cālpaśruto bhikṣuḥ saṃśītikaḥ pṛthagjanaḥ 
 sa kena cit pūjito naivaṃ yathā so 'rhaṃ yatiḥ sudhīḥ  Rm 
 yadā so 'rhan mahābhijño yatra yatra nimaṃtritaḥ 
 Rm 
 tenaiva sarvataḥ paścācchramanena sahācarat  Rm 
 tathānyasmin dine so 'rhaṃ dātrānyena nimaṃtritaḥ 
 gantukāmas tadā tatra paścācchramaṇam aicchata  Rm 
 tad āgamanam anviṣya naiva pratyalabhat kvacit 
 tatas taddarśanābhāvād anyam āhūya bhikṣukaṃ  Rm 
 taṃ paścācchramaṇaṃ kṛtvā dātur gṛham upācarat 
 tadanantaram evāsau tatrāśrame upāgataḥ  Rm 
 tam arhantam apaśyan sa tasthau tūṣṇī nirāśitaḥ 
 tathaivaṃ taṃ niṣīdantaṃ dṛṣṭvā te bhikṣavo narāḥ  Rm 
 tasyauddhatyamanaḥ kartum evam ūcuḥ parasparaṃ 
 bhadanta paśyatādyāyaṃ tenāhato na nīyate  Rm 
 anyo 'dya nīyate paścācchramaṇaḥ kena hetunā 
 iti tair bhikṣubhiḥ proktaṃ śrutvāsau pratibheditaḥ 
 tasyārhato 'ntike cittaṃ praduṣyābhyaśapat tathā  Rm 
 yad adya māṃ parityajya samāhūyānyato harāt 
 gachata bhojanaṃ bhoktuṃ tad ahasto bhavatv asau  Rm 
 tadāsau bhojanaṃ bhuktvā tenaivaṃ bhikṣuṇā saha 
 svāśramaṃ samupāyātas tam adrākṣīd ruṣākulaṃ  Rm 
 ity evaṃ śapitaṃ vāpi matvā so 'rhaṃ mahāmatiḥ 
 dṛṣṭvā taṃ kṛpayā dṛṣṭyā tūṣṇībhūtvā vyaciṃtayat  Rm 
 aho ayaṃ mahāmūḍha īdṛg mayi prabhāṣate 
 etat karmaphalaṃ ghoraṃ kathaṃ bhokṣyati nārake  Rm 
 yad ayaṃ mama doṣeṇa krodhenaivaṃ khalīkṛtaḥ 
 tad etat karmavaipākyaṃ mayaiva paripācyatāṃ  Rm 
 ity evaṃ manasā dhyātvā sa mahārhaṃ kṛpānidhiḥ 
 tatpāpapariśuddhyarthaṃ samādhiṃ vidadhe ciraṃ  Rm 
 tataḥ so 'py ayatir bhikṣur dṛṣṭvā taṃ dhyānasaṃsthitaṃ 
 paścāttāpāgnisaṃtaptes tatpādapraṇato 'vadat  Rm 
 bhadanta yan mayā rauṣyāt krodhābhibhūtacetasā 
 procitaṃ pātakaṃ ghoraṃ tad bhavān kṣantum arhati  Rm 
 yan mayā duṣṭacittena bhavato 'py upabhāṣyate 
 Rm 
 tadatyayaṃ bhavāñ chāstaḥ pratihartuṃ samarhati  Rm 
 adyāgreṇa sadā cāpi bhavatāṃ śaraṇaṃ vraje 
 tan me yad aparādhatvaṃ tat sarvaṃ kṣantum arhati  Rm 
 punar naitat kariṣye 'haṃ akarttavyaṃ yady atra hi 
 avaktavyaṃ ca yat kiṃ cin na tad vakṣyāmi sarvathā  Rm 
 abhāvyaṃ cāpi yat kiṃcid bhāvayiṣye na tat punaḥ 
 yad eva taṃ prakarttavyaṃ tad eva hi karomy ahaṃ  Rm 
 vaktavyam eva vakṣye 'haṃ bhāvyam eva prabhāvaye 
 etat sarvaṃ samāsena samādeṣṭuṃ samarhati  Rm 
 bhavadājñāṃ śirodhṛtvā satyam evaṃ caret sadā  Rm 
 iti tenārthitaṃ śrutvā sa samādheḥ samutthitaḥ 
 taṃ bhikṣuṃ kṛpayā dṛṣṭvā paśyann evaṃ samabravīt  Rm 
 śṛṇu vatsa samādhāya tvām atrāhaṃ prabodhaye 
 yathā me gaditaṃ śrutvā tathā kuru samāhitaḥ  Rm 
 prāṇihiṃsā na karttavyā tathādattapratigrahaṃ 
 strīṇāṃ saṃgānurāgaṃ ca akarttavyaṃ kadā cana  Rm 
 mṛṣāvādaṃ na vaktavyaṃ paiśūnyavacanaṃ tathā 
 saṃbhinnapralāpaṃ ca pāruṣyaṃ ca kadā cana  Rm 
 mithyādṛṣṭir abhidhyā ca vyāpādaṃ ca tathā sadā 
 bhikṣubhir manasā naiva ciṃtanīyā kadā cana  Rm 
 etāni daśapāpānāṃ mūlāni duḥkhadāni hi 
 tasmād evaṃ parijñāya tyaktavyāni sukhārthibhiḥ  Rm 
 punar anyac chṛṇuṣvātra vakṣye dāruṇapātakaṃ 
 saddharmāṇāṃ pratikṣepaṃ kartavyaṃ na kadā cana  Rm 
 tathā vāryāpavādatvaṃ vaktavyaṃ na kadā cana 
 paṃcānaṃtaryapāpāni naiva kāryāṇi kena cit  Rm 
 yāni śrutvāpi dṛṣṭvāpi bhāvayitvānumodya ca 
 patanto narakeṣv eva kleśāndhāni ca santi hi  Rm 
 tasmād etāni karmāṇi mānasāpi ca mā kṛthā 
 varjanīyāni yatnena saddharmasukhavāṃchibhiḥ  Rm 
 karttavyaṃ tu sadā nityam āryasatyānubhāvitaṃ 
 āryāṣṭāṃgikamārge ca caritvā vratam ādarāt  Rm 
 vratānām api sarveṣām āryāṣṭāṃgam upoṣadhaṃ 
 Rm 
 pravaraṃ vratam ākhyātaṃ sarvair api munīśvaraiḥ  Rm 
 yasya puṇyānubhāvena pariśuddhatrimaṃḍalāḥ 
 niḥśeṣapāpanirmuktāḥ prayānty arhatpadaṃ drutaṃ  Rm 
 evam etat parijñāya vrataṃ kṛtvā samācaran 
 tatas te kramataḥ pāpaṃ niḥśeṣaṃ kṣiṇuyād drutaṃ  Rm 
 tataś ca kramaśaḥ śikṣāḥ śikṣitvātra samāhitaḥ 
 triratnaśaraṇaṃ kṛtvā brahmacaryyaṃ samācara  Rm 
 tatas tvaṃ kramaśaś caivaṃ śodhayitvā trimaṃḍalaṃ 
 sarvakleśavinirmuktaḥ sākṣād arhan bhaviṣyasi  Rm 
 iti tenārhatādiṣṭaṃ śrutvāsau paribodhitaḥ 
 tatheti ca parijñāya tadvrataṃ kartum aichata  Rm 
 tathā tasyārhataḥ śāstuḥ sadaivaṃ śaraṇaṃ gataḥ 
 kramāc chikṣāś ca śikṣitvā tad upoṣadham ācarat  Rm 
 adhītya sakalā vidyā triratnasamupāśrayan 
 sarvakleśān vinirjitya brahmacaryaṃ samācarat  Rm 
 bhikṣavo jñāyatām eṣa yo 'sau bhikṣuḥ pṛthagjanaḥ 
 yad anenārhate śāstre śapitaṃ ruṣṭacetasā  Rm 
 tenāhasto vabhūvāyaṃ paṃcajanmaśatāny api 
 yac cānenārhataḥ śastur gatvā ca śaraṇaṃ sadā  Rm 
 adhītya sakalā vidyā brahmacaryaṃ samāśritaṃ 
 tenāyaṃ śāsanenātra pravrajyārhaṃ bhavaty api  Rm 
 iti hi bhikṣavo matvā caritavyaṃ śubhe sadā 
 śubhena sadgatiṃ yāṃti kṛṣṇena durgatiṃ sadā  Rm 
 miśritenāpi miśratvaṃ bhuṃjate sarvajaṃtavaḥ 
 yenaiva yat kṛtaṃ karma tasyaiva karmaṇaḥ phalaṃ  Rm 
 tenaiva bhujyate loke nānyena spṛśyate kvacit 
 abhuktaṃ kṣīyate naiva karma kvāpi kadā cana  Rm 
 bhuktaṃ tu kṣīyate karma śubhaṃ vāpy aśubhaṃ tathā 
 nāgnibhir dahyate kena vāyubhiś ca na śuṣyate  Rm 
 klidyate nodakaiś cāpi kṣīyate naiva bhūmiṣu 
 na praṇaśyanti karmāṇi kalpakoṭiśatair api  Rm 
 sāmagrīṃ prāpya kālaṃ ca phalanti prāṇināṃ khalu 
 evam etat prabhaṣitvā jinendro 'sau mahāmuniḥ  Rm 
 bodhayan sakalāṃl lokān samādhiṃ vidadhe tataḥ 
 iti śāstrā samādiṣṭaṃ śrutvā sarve ca sāṃghikāḥ  Rm 
 śubheṣv eva sadā raktāḥ pracerire samāhitāḥ  Rm 
 ity evaṃ me samākhyātaṃ guruṇā śāṇavāsinā 
 Rm 
 tathaivaṃ te mayā khyātaṃ śrutvā caivaṃ śubhe cara  Rm 
 prajāś ca śrāvayitvaivaṃ bodhayitvā prayatnataḥ 
 saddharmācaraṇeṣv evaṃ preraṇīyā narādhipa  Rm 
 tatas te maṃgalaṃ nityaṃ sarvatrāpi bhaved dhruvaṃ 
 kramād bodhipathaḥ prāpya saṃbodhim āpnuyāḥ khalu  Rm 
 iti tenopaguptena bhāṣitaṃ sa nareśvaraḥ 
 śrutvā tatheti vaṃditvā prābhyanandat sapārṣadaḥ  Rm 
 ye śṛṇvantīdam evaṃ pramuditamanaso hastakākhyāvadānaṃ
 ye cāpi śrāvayanti pratidinam aniśaṃ bodhicaryābhiraktāḥ 
 te sarve kleśamuktāḥ suvimalamanaso bodhisatvā guṇāḍhyā
 bhuktvā saukhyaṃ prakāmaṃ munivaranilayaṃ saṃprayāṃti pramodāḥ  Rm 
  iti śriratnamālāyāṃ hastakāvadānaṃ nāma samāptam 
 Rm 
 XII Sārthavāhāvadāna
 athāśoko mahīpālaḥ kṛtāṃjalipuṭo mudā 
 upaguptaṃ guruṃ natvā punar evam abhāṣata  Rm 
 bhadanta śrotum ichāmi punar anyat subhāṣitaṃ 
 yathā te guruṇādiṣṭaṃ tathā me khyātum arhasi  Rm 
 iti tena narendreṇa pṛṣṭe 'sau sugatātmajaḥ 
 upagupto yatiś caivaṃ taṃ nṛpaṃ pratyabhāṣata  Rm 
 śṛṇu rājan samādhāya yathā me guruṇoditaṃ 
 tathāhaṃ te pravakṣyāmi tac chrutvā mudito bhava  Rm 
 puraikasamaye caivaṃ śākyasiṃho jagadguruḥ 
 sarvajñaḥ sugataḥ śāstā sarvadharmānudeśakaḥ  Rm 
 sarvavidyādhipo nāthas traidhātukavināyakaḥ 
 dharmarājo munīndro 'sau sarvasatvahitaṃkaraḥ  Rm 
 śrāvastyāṃ vahir udyāne jetāhvaye mahāvane 
 anāthapiṇḍadārāme vihāre saugatāśrame  Rm 
 śrāvakair bhikṣubhiḥ sārddham upāsakaiś ca cailakaiḥ 
 bodhisatvagaṇaiś cāpi tathānyaiś ca maharṣibhiḥ  Rm 
 vyaharat satvahitārthena dharmāmṛtaiḥ pravarṣayan 
 tat saddharmāmṛtaṃ pātuṃ prāyayur bodhivāṃchinaḥ  Rm 
 lokapālagaṇāḥ sarve svasvasainyagaṇaiḥ saha 
 brāhmaṇāḥ kṣatriyāś cāpi vaiśyāḥ śūdrāś ca maṃtriṇaḥ  Rm 
 amātyā dhaninaḥ paurāḥ sādhavaś ca mahājanāḥ 
 vaṇijaḥ sārthavāhāś ca tathānye sarvajātikāḥ  Rm 
 sarvadigbhyaḥ samāgatya sarve te samupāgatāḥ 
 saṃbuddhaṃ śrīghanaṃ natvā pūjayitvā samaṃtataḥ  Rm 
 parivṛtya puraskṛtya saddharmaśravaṇārthinaḥ 
 kṛtāṃjalipuṭo dṛṣṭvā saṃtasthuḥ saṃmukhānatāḥ  Rm 
 athāsau bhagavān dṛṣṭvā tān sarvān samupāśritān 
 ādimadhyāṃtakalyāṇaṃ dideśa dharmam uttamaṃ  Rm 
 tat saddharmāmṛtaṃ pītvā sarve lokādhipādayaḥ 
 harṣitās te 'numodanto nananduḥ paribodhitāḥ  Rm 
 tadaiva samaye tasyāṃ śrāvastyāṃ puri saṃsthitaḥ 
 Rm 
 āsīt sāṃyātrikotsāhī sārthavāho mahodyamī  Rm 
 svakuladharmabhṛd vīraḥ svakulavṛttimānitaḥ 
 yaśodharmārthakāmāptyai samudraṃ gantum aichata  Rm 
 tato 'sau svāṃ priyāṃ bhāryāṃ bodhayitvā prayatnataḥ 
 svasahāyāś ca tāṃ sarvāṃ samāhūya samabravīt  Rm 
 bhavaṃto śrūyatāṃ sarve yad abhilaṣitaṃ mama 
 atrāsti yadi vo vāṃchā tan me svāgantum arhatha  Rm 
 ahaṃ ratnākaraṃ gantum iche ratnasamṛddhaye 
 tat prāyāta mayā sārddhaṃ yadi saṃpattim ichatha  Rm 
 iti tenoditaṃ śrutvā sarve te ratnalobhitāḥ 
 sahasā gaṃtum ichante ratnākare mahodadhau  Rm 
 tato 'sau sārthabhṛc chīghraṃ sarve sārthagaṇaiḥ saha 
 svastyayanavidhiṃ kṛtvā pratasthe saṃpramoditaḥ  Rm 
 tataḥ kramād vyatikramya grāmāraṇyavanāni ca 
 sarve te pracaranto vai tīraṃ prāpur mahodadheḥ  Rm 
 tato bhāṃḍāni naukāyām āropyāruhya ca svayaṃ 
 karṇadhāraprayatnais te jagāhire 'mbudhiṃ kramāt  Rm 
 tataḥ kramāt samullaṃghya bahudvīpāntarāṇi te 
 ratnākaraṃ samāsādya ratnāni samasādhayan  Rm 
 tatas te bahuratnāni samāsādya pramoditāḥ 
 tataḥ pratyāgatā abdhes tīrāntikaṃ samāyayuḥ  Rm 
 tatra tat karmadoṣeṇa kālavātair vighaṭṭitaṃ 
 bhidyate vahanaṃ teṣāṃ hṛdayaiḥ sā sahāśu tat  Rm 
 tadā te vaṇijaḥ sarve niḥprayatnapratikriyā 
 sarvabhāṇḍaiḥ sahāgāḍhe nipetur duṣkare 'mbudhau  Rm 
 kecit phalakam ālamvya samuttīrṇāḥ svavīryataḥ 
 kecid vāhuvalādhānaṃ samuttīrya sthalaṃ yayuḥ  Rm 
 kecic ca vilayaṃ prāptā nirālamvyanirāśrayāḥ 
 utpravanto nimajjantaḥ kheditā nidhanaṃ yayuḥ  Rm 
 tatas te vaṇijaḥ sarve ye viśiṣṭā viṣāditāḥ 
 te yaśodhanavibhraṣṭāḥ śūnyahastā gṛhaṃ yayuḥ  Rm 
 tathāsau sārthavāho 'pi gṛhaṃ prāpto viṣāditaḥ 
 etad vṛttaṃ svabhāryāyāḥ kathitvaivaṃ vyacintayat  Rm 
 hā hā me mandabhāgyatvāj jāyate mīdṛśī vipat 
 Rm 
 atrāhaṃ kiṃ kariṣyāmi yato bhāgyaṃ na vidyate  Rm 
 bhāgyavān puruṣo dhīro bhāgyavān kuśalī sudhīḥ 
 bhāgyena labhyate saṃpad yaśaḥ saukhyaguṇānvitaḥ  Rm 
 dhīḥ śrīlakṣmīyaśoratnaṃ valaṃ saṃpat kṣaṇādayaḥ 
 etadādyā guṇāḥ sarve śobhanti bhāgyam āśritāḥ  Rm 
 nihīnabhāgyavṛttes tu puruṣasyāpi saṃmate 
 etadādyādiguṇāḥ sarve na prasiddhyaṃti sarvataḥ  Rm 
 tad atra kiṃ kariṣye 'haṃ kva yāsyāmi dhanāptaye 
 dhanahīnā na śobhante gṛhasthāḥ sādhavo 'pi hi  Rm 
 varaṃ prāṇaparityāgaṃ na tu dravyair vinā gṛhe 
 paśuvan nirasaṃ bhuktvā sthāsyāmy evaṃ nirutsavaṃ  Rm 
 bhāgyena labhyate dravyaṃ bhāgyaṃ dharmeṇa labhyate 
 dharme hi jāyate sveṣṭadevatāyāḥ prasādataḥ  Rm 
 tad dharmabhāgyalabdhārthaṃ svakuladevatāṃ prati 
 samyag ārādhayitvaivaṃ yāyāṃ ratnākaraṃ punaḥ  Rm 
 manasīti viniścitya sa sārthavāhakaḥ punaḥ 
 svakuladevatāṃ samyag ārādhya samayācata  Rm 
 namas te devate nityaṃ bhaje 'haṃ śaraṇaṃ gataḥ 
 kṣaṃtavyaṃ me 'parādhatvaṃ prasīda parameśvara  Rm 
 itthaṃ sā devatā samyag ārādhya saṃpramoditā 
 sarvasārthān samāhūya punar evam abhāṣata  Rm 
 bho bhavanto vijānīdhvaṃ vayaṃ sarve vaṇigjanāḥ 
 tad atra bhavatām agre kathyate me samīhitaṃ  Rm 
 yad bhavanto vayaṃ sarve sārthavāhakulodbhavāḥ 
 tat tathaiva gṛhe sthitvā naiva śobhāṃ vrajemahi  Rm 
 tasmāt svakulavṛttisthaiḥ sarvair asmābhir udyataiḥ 
 yaśodharmasukhāptyarthaṃ karttavyaṃ dhanasādhanaṃ  Rm 
 dhanahīnā na śobhante gṛhasthā hi kuṭuṃvinaḥ 
 sārthavāho 'stu śobhante vahuratnārjanodyatāḥ  Rm 
 tad viṣādaṃ parityaktvā yaśoratnasukhāptaye 
 dhairyyam ālamvya sarvaiś ca karttavyaṃ dhanasādhanaṃ  Rm 
 dhanavān puruṣo lokaiḥ sarvatrāpi pramānyate 
 dhanena sādhayed dharmaṃ dharmeṇa sadgatiṃ vrajet  Rm 
 tasmān nityaṃ mahotsāhais ñltyaktvālasyakuśīdatā 
 arjanīyaṃ prayatnena dhanaṃ dānāya bhuktaye  Rm 
 dānaṃ vibhūṣaṇaṃ loke dānaṃ durgatinivāraṇaṃ 
 Rm 
 dānaṃ svargasya sopānaṃ dānaṃ śāntikaraṃ sadā  Rm 
 asmād dānaṃ sadā kartuṃ bhoktuṃ saukhyaṃ yathechayā 
 bhūyo ratnākaraṃ gaṃtum arhāmahe dhanārjane  Rm 
 tatra ratnāni saṃgṛhya svastipratyāgatā vayaṃ 
 yāvaj jīvaṃ sukhaṃ bhuktvā dānaṃ kṛtvā vasemahi  Rm 
 yadi daivo vipattiḥ syāt samudre patitā vayaṃ 
 tīrtharāje mṛtāḥ sarve yāsyāmaḥ svargatiṃ dhruvaṃ  Rm 
 yadi bhāgyād athāsmākaṃ devānāṃ ca prasādataḥ 
 yātrāsiddhir bhaven nūnaṃ yāvaj jīvaṃ sukhaṃ tadā  Rm 
 asmād ratnākare gantuṃ iche ratnapralabdhaye 
 tat prāyāta mayā sārddhaṃ yadi saṃpattim ichatha  Rm 
 iti tasyoditaṃ śrutvā te sarve vaṇijo mudā 
 tathā tena sahaichānta gantuṃ ratnākaraiḥ punaḥ  Rm 
 tato 'sau sārthabhṛc chīghraṃ dhṛtvā svastyayanaṃ mudā 
 sarve sārthagaṇaiḥ sārddhaṃ pratasthe svapurād vahi  Rm 
 tataḥ kramād vyatikramya grāmāraṇyavanāni ca 
 pracarantaś ca te sarve tīraṃ prāpur mahodadheḥ  Rm 
 tatra sarve 'pi te sārthā bhāṇḍāni vahane kramāt 
 āropya sahasārūḍhā jagāhire mahāmbudhau  Rm 
 tataḥ kramāt samullaṃghya vahudvīpāntarāṇi te 
 ratnākaraṃ samāsādya ratnāni samasādhayan  Rm 
 tatra te vahuratnāni samāgṛhya praharṣitāḥ 
 tataḥ pratyāgatāś cābdhes tīrāntikam upāyayuḥ  Rm 
 tatas taddaivayogena kālikāvātaghaṭṭitā 
 sā naukā bhidyate caivaṃ teṣāṃ vai hṛdayaiḥ saha  Rm 
 tadā te vaṇijaḥ sarve niḥprayatnapratikriyā 
 sarvabhāṇḍaiḥ sahāgāḍhe nyapatan duṣṭare 'mbudhau  Rm 
 tatra te vilayaṃ prāptā nirālaṃvā nirāśrayāḥ 
 unmajjanto nimajjantaḥ preritās tīram ūrmibhiḥ  Rm 
 kecit phalakam āśritya samuttīryya svavīryyataḥ 
 kecid vāhuvalādhānaiḥ samuttīryya sthalaṃ yayuḥ  Rm 
 kecin nihīnavīryyāṅgā hanyamānā mahormibhiḥ 
 utplavantā nimajjantaḥ kheditā nidhanaṃ yayuḥ  Rm 
 tatas teṣāṃ ca sārthānāṃ ye 'vaśiṣṭā sujīvinaḥ 
 Rm 
 yaśoratnaviyuktās te śūnyahastā gṛhaṃ yayuḥ  Rm 
 tathāsau sārthavāho 'pi gṛhaṃ gatvā viṣāditaḥ 
 etad vṛttaṃ svavaṃdhūnāṃ kathitvaivam abhāṣata  Rm 
 hā mayā kiṃ kṛtaṃ pāpaṃ yenedrig jāyate vipat 
 dvidhāpi siddhyate naiva yato bhāgyaṃ na vidyate  Rm 
 pāpair na siddhyate karma atra yatnasya kiṃ valaiḥ 
 dharmeṇa siddhyate karma tasmād dharmo valottamaḥ  Rm 
 tasmād dharmaṃ puraskṛtya karttavyaṃ dravyasādhanaṃ 
 dravyena sādhayet karma sadgatiṃ samavāpnuyāḥ  Rm 
 karma tu siddhyate samyak kulavṛttiṃ ca cāriṇāṃ 
 kulavṛttiṃ parityajya yo 'nyavṛttau caret kudhīḥ  Rm 
 sa ihāpi paribhraṣṭaḥ paratra durgatiṃ vrajet 
 yenaivaṃ sadgatiprāptis tadaiva karmma sādhayet  Rm 
 yato 'pi durgatiṃ prāptis tat karma tarhitaṃ budhaiḥ 
 tad atra kiṃ kariṣye 'haṃ kva yāsyāmy artham arjituṃ 
 arthaṃ vinā kathaṃ dharmaṃ karttavyaṃ hi kuṭuṃvibhiḥ  Rm 
 vinā dharmaṃ hi saṃsāre janma jīvaṃ ca nisphalaṃ 
 kiṃ te na pauruṣeṇāpi yena dharmaṃ na sādhyate  Rm 
 dhig dhig me janma saṃsāre jīvituṃ na tathotsahe 
 varaṃ prāṇaparityāgaṃ na tv evaṃ cirajīvitaṃ  Rm 
 avaśyaṃ jantubhir mṛtyur gantavyaṃ ekadhā dhruvaṃ 
 tato 'tra martum ichāmi na tv evam uṣituṃ gṛhe  Rm 
 evaṃjīvo na śobhe 'haṃ dhig pravādāgnidagdhitaḥ 
 kathaṃ me śāmyate duḥkhaṃ yenāhaṃ parikheditaḥ  Rm 
 kiṃ karttavyaṃ kva gantavyaṃ yatnaṃ cātra na vidyate 
 sarvathāhaṃ vinaṣṭo 'smi ko me 'sti rakṣako janaḥ  Rm 
 yaśodharmaparibhraṣṭo vrajeyaṃ durgatiṃ khalu 
 tadāhaṃ kiṃ kariṣyāmi dharmayaśaḥsukhānvitaḥ  Rm 
 mānuṣye labhyamāne hi kuto dharmānusādhanaṃ 
 vinā dharmmaṃ yaśodravyaḥ kiṃ saukhyaṃ gṛhavāsināṃ  Rm 
 vinā dharmayaśodravyair yo gṛhasthaḥ paśuḥ khalu 
 dharmeṇa sādhayed dravyaṃ yaśobhāgyasukhāptaye  Rm 
 dharmād dhi jāyate puṇyaṃ dānaśīlakṣamādibhiḥ 
 puṇyenaiva pralabhyante caturvargā api dhruvaṃ  Rm 
 Rm 
 tad eteṣāṃ mamaiko 'pi na vidyate kathaṃ cana 
 hā hato 'smi svadaivena kiṃ karomi vikheditaḥ  Rm 
 sarvathāhaṃ vinaṣṭo 'smi namo daivāya karmaṇe 
 evaṃ teṣāṃ svavaṃdhūnāṃ vilapītvā sa sārthapaḥ  Rm 
 tasthau cintākulībhūto dhanārjananirāśrayā 
 evaṃ vyavasthitaṃ dṛṣṭvā taṃ te sarve 'pi vāṃdhavāḥ  Rm 
 datvāśvāsaṃ vinodāya bodhayante dhruvaṃ tathā 
 sādho sārthapate satyaṃ tat sarvaṃ yat tvayocyate  Rm 
 tad evaṃ dhairyyam ālaṃvya prodyamasva gṛhe vasan 
 sādho kutrāpi mā dhāva nirmāṇasadṛśaṃ phalaṃ  Rm 
 yāvad evāmbhasā kumbhaḥ siṃdhāv andhau 'vapūryate 
 yad abhāvi na tad bhāvi bhāvi naiva tad anyathā  Rm 
 avaśyaṃ bhāvino bhāvā bhavaṃti sarvadehināṃ 
 avaśyaṃ bhāvino bhāvā na bhaveyus tathā yadi  Rm 
 pitrā tyaktaḥ kathaṃ rāmo rājyabhraṣṭo vanaṃ yayau 
 tatrāpi vasatas tasya bhāryā śītā pativratā  Rm 
 āhṛtya rakṣasā nītā kathaṃ laṃkāpure 'vasat 
 tato rāmeṇa vīryeṇa hatvāsau rāvaṇas tataḥ  Rm 
 pratyānīya punaḥ śītā tyaktā bharttrā svayaṃ kathaṃ 
 punar ṛṣeḥ samānīya sabhāmadhye parikṣitā  Rm 
 tataḥ pṛthyā svayaṃ gṛhya sītānītā rasātalaṃ 
 tatas tadvirahārttāsau rāmaḥ saṃsāranispṛhaḥ  Rm 
 nadyāṃ prāṇasvayaṃ tyaktvā janaṃ sārddhaṃ divaṃ yayau 
 evam anye 'pi rājāno yudhiṣṭhirā nṛpādayaḥ 
 rājyabhraṣṭā vane gatvā vibhramus te 'pi daivataḥ  Rm 
 evam anye 'pi lokāś ca sarvatraidhātukabhavāḥ 
 uttamā adhamā madhyā saṃti te 'pi svadaivataḥ  Rm 
 kecid gṛhe mṛtāḥ kecij jāyamānā mṛtā api 
 kecid vālye mṛtāḥ kecit kaumāratve mṛtās tathā  Rm 
 yauvane 'pi mṛtāḥ kecin mṛtā vṛddhe vadanti me 
 sarve 'py evaṃ mṛtā lokāḥ svasvadaivapramāṇataḥ  Rm 
 evaṃ devādayo lokāḥ sukhaduḥkhānuyoginaḥ 
 svasvadaivānubhāvena ṣaḍgatiṣu caranti te  Rm 
 kecid vālye sukhaṃ bhuktvā yauvane duḥkhabhāginaḥ 
 kecic ca yauvane saukhyaṃ bhuktvā vṛddhe suduḥkhitāḥ  Rm 
 Rm 
 kecic ca duḥkhitā vālye yauvane saukhyabhāginaḥ 
 vṛddhatvasya sukhībhūtā bhavaṃti te 'pi hi daivataḥ  Rm 
 sarve 'pi sukham ichanti duḥkhaṃ nechati kaś cana 
 tathā sukhāni saṃprāptuṃ yatnaṃ kurvanty anekaśaḥ  Rm 
 keṣāṃ cit siddhyate yatnaṃ keṣāṃ cid vā na siddhyati 
 keṣāṃ cid vighnatāṃ yāti tat sarvaṃ daivayogataḥ  Rm 
 tathā ca rogiṇāṃ rogā vaidyopacāraṇair api 
 varddhyante naiva śāmyante tad api daivayogataḥ  Rm 
 keṣāṃ cid rogiṇāṃ rogā vinā vaidyopacāraṇe 
 śāmyaṃte yatnato cāpi tad api daivayogataḥ  Rm 
 tathā cald maṃtriṇāṃ maṃtrāḥ siddhyante yatnato laghuḥ 
 keṣāṃ cid vighnatāṃ yānti tad api daivakāraṇāt  Rm 
 tathaivaṃ vaṇijāṃ lābhoḥ siddhyante yatnato 'pi ca 
 keṣāṃ cin naiva yatnena tad api daivayogataḥ  Rm 
 tathā vīrā raṇe śatruṃ vinā yatnaṃ jayaṃty api 
 kecit tu ripunā yuddhe hanyamānā mṛtāḥ pare  Rm 
 kecit kṛtvā mahāyuddhaṃ hanyamānāḥ parasparaṃ 
 tyaktvā dehaṃ gatāḥ svargaṃ tad api daivayogataḥ  Rm 
 evaṃ sāṃyātrikā ratnaṃ prāptuṃ ratnākaraṃ gatāḥ 
 kecid ratnāni saṃgṛhya svasti pratyāgatā gṛhaṃ  Rm 
 kecid ratnam alabdhaṃ vai śūnyahastā gṛhāgatāḥ 
 kecic ca nidhanaṃ yātās tatraiva makarālaye  Rm 
 kecid yatnāt samuttīrya jīvanto gṛham āgatāḥ 
 kecic ca jāṃgale caurair nihatā maraṇaṃ gatāḥ  Rm 
 kecic ca jaṃtubhir mārge hiṃsyamāne mṛtā vane 
 keṣāṃ cit siddhyate yātrā mahallābhasamanvitāḥ  Rm 
 keṣāṃ cid vighnatāṃ yānti tathāpi daivayogataḥ 
 kaiś cid gṛhe nidhiḥ prāptaḥ kaiś cid deśāntare vane  Rm 
 kaiś cid dūre bhramadbhiś ca naiva kiṃ cit kva cid dhanaṃ 
 keṣāṃ cid varddhate saṃpad yatnāyāsaṃ vinā laghu  Rm 
 keṣāṃ cid dhīyate saṃpad rakṣitāpi prayatnataḥ 
 keṣāṃ cit susthirā saṃpat keṣāṃ cid vala asthirā  Rm 
 keṣāṃ cij jāyate naiva nānopāyārjanair api 
 evaṃ nānāprakāraiś ca satvās traidhātukodbhavāḥ  Rm 
 Rm 
 bhuṃjate sukhaduḥkhāni svasvadaivānusāriṇāḥ 
 sukhasyānte hi duḥkhāni duḥkhasyānte sukhāni ca  Rm 
 bhuṃjante jaṃtavaḥ sarve bhramante ṣaḍgatiṣv api 
 tathā bhavanti mitrāṇi dviṣo 'pi hitakāriṇaḥ  Rm 
 mitrāṇy api dviṣo duṣṭā bhavaṃti daivayogataḥ 
 tathāmṛtaṃ viṣībhūtaṃ viṣaṃ cāpy amṛtī bhavet  Rm 
 tad api daivayogena tasmād daivaṃ mahad varaṃ  Rm 
 tathā ca brahmaṇaḥ śīrṣaṃ nikṛttaṃ śūlapāṇinā 
 tad api daivayogena tasmād daivaṃ mahāvalī  Rm 
 tathā cakrī suvīro 'pi vyādheṣu nihato mṛtaḥ 
 tad api daivayogena tasmād daivaṃ mahad valaṃ  Rm 
 yaś ca bhūtādhipaś ceśaḥ so 'py umatto digaṃvaraḥ 
 tad api daivayogena tasmād daivaṃ maheśvaraḥ  Rm 
 caṃdro 'pi ca kalaṃkāṅko māse māse 'pi hīyate 
 tad api daivayogena tasmād daivaṃ mahadvalaṃ  Rm 
 evaṃ candradineśau ca graheṇāpi nipīḍitau 
 tad api daivayogena tasmād daivaṃ mahāvalī  Rm 
 rāmo rakṣovijetāpi putreṇa nihato raṇe 
 tad api daivayogena tasmād daivaṃ mahāvalī  Rm 
 tathārjjunaḥ sudhīro 'pi putreṇāpi hato raṇe 
 tad api daivayogena tasmād daivaṃ mahāvalaṃ  Rm 
 tathā ca parśurāmeṇa mātāpi nihatā krudhā 
 tad api daivayogena tasmād daivaṃ mahāvalaḥ  Rm 
 biṃbisāro nṛpendro 'pi putreṇājātaśatruṇā 
 vaṃdhane māritaṃ caivaṃ tad api daivayogataḥ  Rm 
 tasmāc ca brahmadattena dharmapālo sa nandanaḥ 
 māritaḥ pramadātuṣṭyai tad api daivayogataḥ  Rm 
 rājñī ca durpatī mātā svātmajasyāpi rohitaṃ 
 pītvaiva nirdayā tuṣṭā tad api daivayogataḥ  Rm 
 kṣāntivādī muniś cāpi rājñā nirdayacetasā 
 asinā ghātito 'raṇye tad api daivayogataḥ  Rm 
 prasenajin nṛpeśo 'pi putreṇāpi svarājyataḥ 
 nirvāsito vane bhrāntas tad api daivayogataḥ  Rm 
 evam anye 'pi rājāno hatvā jñātī svavāṃdhavān 
 bhuṃjate prāpya rājyāni tad api daivayogataḥ  Rm 
 evaṃ pitrā sutās tyaktvā mātrā ca svātmajā api 
 vaṃdhumitrādibhis tyaktvā kecid daivānuyogataḥ  Rm 
 bhāryāpi svāminā tyaktvā bharttāpi bhāryyayā tathā 
 Rm 
 tad api daivayogena tasmād daivaṃ mahattaraṃ  Rm 
 putreṇāpi pitā tyaktaṃ mātāpi jananī tathā 
 dhātrī cāpi parityaktās tathā pautrapitāmahaḥ  Rm 
 tathā pitāmahas tyaktaḥ putraiś cāpy atinirdayaiḥ 
 tad api daivayogena tasmād daivaṃ mahattaraṃ  Rm 
 tathā rājñā svabhṛtyāś ca sevakā api sajjanāḥ 
 aparādhaṃ vinā tyaktās tad api daivayogataḥ  Rm 
 tathā sakhisahāyāṃ ca vaṃdhumitrasuhṛjjanān 
 parityaktvā nihaṃty ante tad api daivayogataḥ  Rm 
 tathā śiṣyān gurur hanti śiṣyo hanti gurum api 
 tad api daivayogena tasmād daivaṃ mahattaraṃ  Rm 
 tathāpi ghnanti bharttāraṃ svāminaṃ sevakānn api 
 tad api daivayogena tasmād daivaṃ mahattaraṃ  Rm 
 tathā ca svayam ātmānaṃ ghnanti kecid ruṣānvitāḥ 
 tad api daivayogena tasmād daivaṃ mahattamaḥ  Rm 
 kecic chastraiḥ svayaṃ hatvā kecid bhuktvā viṣādikaṃ 
 kecid agnau jale svabhre prapātāt patitā mṛtāḥ  Rm 
 kecit pāśaiḥ svayaṃ badhya mṛtāḥ kecic ca vaṃdhane 
 kecit pānāśanādīṃś ca tyaktvā yāṃti yamālayaṃ  Rm 
 evaṃ kṛtvāpi yānty eva kecid vāpi surālayaṃ 
 kecic ca narake yānti tat sarvaṃ daivayogataḥ  Rm 
 tathā mṛddārupāṣāṇe nānādhātupratiṣṭhitāḥ 
 devatāś ca dadanty evaṃ phalaṃ daivaniyogataḥ  Rm 
 pare 'pi svajanā iṣṭāḥ sahajā api ca dviṣaḥ 
 bhavanti tat kṣaṇād eva tad api daivayogataḥ  Rm 
 evaṃ traidhātukotpannāḥ sarve satvāś ca jaṃtavaḥ 
 ṣaḍgatiṣu bhramantas te caranti daivayogataḥ  Rm 
 kecid vīrā guṇāḍhyāś ca suṃdarā bhāgyamāninaḥ 
 sarvasaṃpatsamṛddhāś ca cakravarttinṛpādayaḥ  Rm 
 kecic ca nirguṇāḥ prāḍhyāḥ kecin nirguṇinaḥ śaṭhāḥ 
 kecic ca vikalāṃgāś ca guṇasaṃpattibhāginaḥ  Rm 
 kecic ca suṃdarā mūrkhā nirdhanā nirguṇāḥ śaṭhāḥ 
 kecic ca guṇinaḥ prāḍhyā nīcakarmānucāriṇaḥ  Rm 
 kecin nīcakulotpannāḥ guṇāḍhyāḥ sādhuvṛttayaḥ 
 Rm 
 dātāro dhanino vīrāḥ sarvasatvānupālakāḥ  Rm 
 kecid uccakulotpannā nirguṇā duṣṭavṛttayaḥ 
 kṛpaṇā vikalāṃgāś ca nirdayāś ca durāśayāḥ  Rm 
 kecid vīrā hy alābhijñāḥ kulīnāḥ sādhavo 'pi ye 
 te 'pi jātinihīne 'pi bhajaṃti śaraṇaṃ gatāḥ  Rm 
 kecic ca guṇavanto 'pi kucelāḥ kṛśagātrikāḥ 
 pretavad bhujyamānāś ca caraṃti bhikṣukā bhuvi  Rm 
 kecic ca nirguṇā vāpi vaṃcakā duṣṭamānasāḥ 
 mānyante sādhuval loke tad api daivayogataḥ  Rm 
 evaṃ nānāvidhā lokāḥ ṣaḍgatiṣu samudbhavāḥ 
 sukhaduḥkhāni bhuṃjante bhramaṃti daivayogataḥ  Rm 
 tasmād daivaṃ mahāvīraṃ sarvatraidhātukeṣv api 
 kenāpi śakyate naiva vaśe netuṃ kathaṃ cana  Rm 
 tena daivaṃ mahānāthaḥ sarvakarmādhipaḥ prabhuḥ 
 sraṣṭā bharttā ca harttā ca traidhātuvāsinām api  Rm 
 tasyāpy adhipatibrahmā sarvalokeśvaro vidhiḥ 
 tat tasya śaraṇaṃ gatvā bhaktyā nityaṃ samarcaya  Rm 
 tasmiṃ tuṣṭe vidhau devaiḥ parituṣṭaṃ bhaved dhruvaṃ 
 tato daivaprasādena sarvatra maṃgalaṃ bhavet  Rm 
 daive tuṣṭe susiddhyante sarvakarmāṇi yatnataḥ 
 viruddhe tu na siddhyante yatnaiḥ saṃsādhitāny api  Rm 
 tasmād daivādhipaṃ devaṃ brahmāṇaṃ caturānanaṃ 
 bhaja daivaprasannāya sarvakāryaprasiddhaye  Rm 
 daivaṃ brahmaprasādena śubhadaṃ saṃmukhī bhavet 
 tatas te maṃgalaṃ nityaṃ sarvakāryyeṣu saṃbhavet  Rm 
 evaṃ sārthapate natvā vidhānaṃ kāryyasādhanaṃ 
 vidhinārādhya sadbhaktyā kuruṣva karmasādhanaṃ  Rm 
 tathā cet sarvathā nityaṃ yātrāyaṃ maṃgalaṃ bhavet 
 anyad vā cintitaṃ kāryaṃ sarvāpy evaṃ prasatsyate  Rm 
 yadi vāṃchāsti te bhūyo gantuṃ ratnākaraṃ prati 
 tathābhyarcya vidhātāraṃ gachet svasti bhavet khalu  Rm 
 iti tenoditaṃ śrutvā sārthavāhas tatheti saḥ 
 pratijñāya samabhyarcya brahmāṇaṃ prārthayat tadā  Rm 
 namas te bhagavan brahmaṃ yātrāsiddhiṃ kuruṣva me 
 evaṃ vidhiṃ samārādhya sa sārthādhipatis tataḥ  Rm 
 ratnaṃ prāptyai punaḥ sārthān samāhūyābravīt tathā 
 Rm 
 bhavantaḥ śrūyatāṃ vākyaṃ yan mayā samudīritaṃ  Rm 
 atrāsti yadi vo vāṃchā tathā kartuṃ samudyatāṃ 
 ahaṃ ratnākaraṃ bhūyo gantuṃ ichāmi sāṃprataṃ  Rm 
 tad yadīchatha ratnāni tathā yāta mayā saha 
 kiṃ cāpy atra vayaṃ sarve sārthavāhakulodbhavāḥ  Rm 
 tad gṛhe paśuvad bhuktvā kathaṃ śobhī vrajemahi 
 saṃsāre sarvajaṃtūnāṃ ekadhā maraṇaṃ dhruvaṃ  Rm 
 tat kiṃ no maraṇe bhītyā mṛtyuṃ kena nivāryyate 
 yadi daivād vipattiḥ syād asmākaṃ karmmadoṣataḥ  Rm 
 sarvatīrthajalādhāre mṛtāḥ svargaṃ vrajemahi 
 yadi bhāgyāc ca no yātrā siddhā svastimatī bhavet 
 tadā jīvaṃ sukhaṃ dānaṃ kṛtvā svargaṃ vrajemahi 
 tad viṣādaṃ parityajya yaśodharmmasukhāptaye  Rm 
 vīryotsāhaṃ samādhāya samāyāta mayā saha 
 iti tasya vacaḥ śrutvā sarve te vaṇijo mudā  Rm 
 tatheti ca samutsāhaṃ kṛtvā gaṃtuṃ samudyatāḥ 
 tataḥ sarve 'pi te sārthā dhṛtvā svastyayanaṃ vidhiṃ  Rm 
 paṇyam ādāya tenaiva saha sārthabhṛtā yayuḥ 
 tatas te prasthitāḥ sarve grāmāraṇyavanasthalīḥ  Rm 
 samuttīryya kramād yātās tīraṃ prāpur mahodadheḥ 
 tatra nāvi samārūḍhā karṇadhāraprayatnataḥ  Rm 
 marutāṃte 'nukūlena jagāhire mahodadhiṃ 
 tatas teṣāṃ ca sarveṣāṃ daivayogānuyogataḥ  Rm 
 sā naukā kālikāvātasaṃkṣubdhābhūd vibheditā 
 tadā sarve 'pi te sārthā dṛṣṭvā naukāṃ vibheditāṃ  Rm 
 trasitāḥ sahasā tasmāt pratyāyayuḥ prayatnataḥ 
 tatas te vaṇijaḥ sarve vipaṃnāśā viṣāditāḥ  Rm 
 rātrau svasvagṛhe gatvā vibhagnāsā viṣedire 
 tathāsau sārthavāho 'pi lajjitaḥ khaṇḍitāśayaḥ  Rm 
 kheditātmā gṛhe tasthau mūkavad dhi natotsavaḥ 
 tato bhāryyā satī bhadrā patikhedavibheditaṃ 
 dṛṣṭvā taṃ vikalībhūtaṃ samupetyābravīt punaḥ  Rm 
 mā viṣādaṃ kṛthāḥ svāminn atra dhairyyaṃ samāśrayaḥ 
 dharmiṣṭhe śaraṇaṃ gatvā kuruṣva dharmasādhanaṃ  Rm 
 Rm 
 dharmmeṇa jīyate pāpaṃ niṣpāpo nirmalāśayaḥ 
 śuddhacitto viśuddhātmā puṇyātmā bhāgyam āpnuyāt  Rm 
 tato bhāgyavataḥ puṃso yad yat karmaṇi sādhitaṃ 
 tat tat sarvaṃ prasiddhyeta tasmād dharmaṃ carottamaṃ  Rm 
 dharmam eva suhṛd mitram ihāmutra sahānugaḥ 
 dharmmeṇa pālyate sarvaṃ tasmād dharmo jagatsuhṛt  Rm 
 dharmā nānāvidhā loke kulacaryyānusarataḥ 
 sarveṣām api dharmāṇāṃ dayā dharme viśiṣyate  Rm 
 dayāluḥ sugato buddho dharmarājas tathāgataḥ 
 samantabhadra ātmajñaḥ sarvasatvahitaṃkaraḥ  Rm 
 sarvajño mārajic chāstā jagannāthaḥ śubhārthadaḥ 
 ṣaḍabhijño jagadbharttā sarvalokādhipeśvaraḥ  Rm 
 tasmāt tasya munīndrasya sadbhaktyā śaraṇaṃ vrajan 
 saddharmaśaraṇaṃ kṛtvā bhaja nityam upāsakaḥ  Rm 
 tatas te naśyate pāpaṃ maṃgalaṃ ca bhaved dhruvaṃ 
 tadaiva sarvakāryāṇi sametsyaṃte na saṃśayaḥ  Rm 
 iti bhāryoditaṃ śrutvā sa sārthādhipatir mudā 
 tatheti saṃpratijñāya saṃbuddhaśaraṇaṃ yayau  Rm 
 namas te bhagavan nātha pāpistho 'haṃ sudurbhagaḥ 
 bhavatāṃ śaraṇaṃ gache tan māṃ dṛṣṭvāśu rakṣatāṃ  Rm 
 yan mayā prakṛtaṃ pāpaṃ kāritaṃ vānumoditaḥ 
 tat sarvaṃ deśayiṣyāmi tan me dehi śubhāṃ gatiṃ  Rm 
 bhavatāṃ sarvadā nātha śaraṇaṃ yāmy upāsakaḥ 
 anyo me śaraṇaṃ nāsti tan māṃ rakṣa sadā bhaje  Rm 
 tridhāpi me jagannātha yātrā bhagnā svadaivataḥ 
 gṛhasthaḥ sārthavāho 'haṃ tan me dehi susaṃpadaḥ  Rm 
 yanv ahaṃ sāṃprataṃ nātha bhavataṃ śaraṇaṃ vrajan 
 bhūyo ratnākaraṃ gantuṃ ichāmi ratnalabdhaye  Rm 
 yadi yātrā bhavet siddhi yāval lābhaṃ ca lapsyate 
 tadupāyena saṃbuddhaṃ pūjayeyaṃ sasāṃghikaṃ  Rm 
 ity evaṃ niścayaṃ kṛtvā saṃbuddhaṃ saṃsmaran muhuḥ 
 tāṃ bhāryyāṃ bhadrikāṃ dṛṣṭvā punar evam abhāṣata  Rm 
 bhadre tvayā yad ādiṣṭaṃ tathā kartuṃ samutsahe 
 adyāgreṇa jagannāthaṃ śaraṇaṃ yāsyāmy upāsakaḥ  Rm 
 Rm 
 bhadre nāmnā jinendrasya yāsye ratnākare punaḥ 
 yadi yātrā bhavet siddhi yāval lābhaṃ ca lapsyate  Rm 
 tadupārddhena ratnena sasaṃghaṃ sugataṃ tadā 
 yathārhaṃ pūjayiṣye 'ham iti saṃkalpitaṃ mayā  Rm 
 yadi daivād vipattiḥ syāt saṃbuddhanāma saṃsmaran 
 sarvatīrthajalādhāne mṛto yāyāṃ sukhāvatīṃ  Rm 
 tad atra yadi me kāryyaṃ śubhaṃ kartuṃ samichasi 
 tad viṣādaṃ parityajya dhairyyaṃ kṛtvā sukhaṃ vasa  Rm 
 iti bharttroditaṃ śrutvā sā bhāryyā bhadrikā satī 
 tatheti pratisaṃmodya svāminaṃ taṃ samabravīt  Rm 
 yady evaṃ te samīhāsti kṛtv etaṃ niścayaṃ prabho 
 saṃbuddhasmaraṇaṃ dhṛtvā gacha svastiṃ samācara  Rm 
 yadi buddhakṛpādṛṣṭiḥ satveṣu vidyate kila 
 tathāvaśyaṃ sa saṃbuddhaḥ paśyan tvāṃ cāpy acet khalu  Rm 
 tadā te maṅgalaṃ nityaṃ yātrā svastimatī bhavet 
 tatas te janma saṃsāre sāphalyaṃ ca bhavet khalu  Rm 
 tena svāmiṃ jineṃdrasya nāmasvastyayanaṃ dadhat 
 gacha yātrā susiddhāstu svasti pratyāgatāśu ca  Rm 
 iti bhāryoditaṃ śrutvā sa sārthādhipatir mudā 
 bhūyaḥ sārthagaṇān sarvān samāhūyābravīt tathā  Rm 
 bhavanta śrūyatāṃ vākyaṃ yan mayātra samīhitaṃ 
 ahaṃ ratnākaraṃ bhūyo gantum ichāmi sāṃprataṃ  Rm 
 tad asti yadi vo vāṃchā yaśaḥsaṃpatsukhāptaye 
 samāyāta mayā sārddhaṃ ratnākaraṃ vrajemahi  Rm 
 yadi bhāgyād dhi no yātrā siddhā svastimatir bhavet 
 yāvajīvaṃ sukhaṃ dharmaṃ kṛtvā svargaṃ vrajemahi 
 atha vā syād vipattir naḥ sarvatīrthajalāśraye 
 mṛtāḥ svargaṃ gamiṣyāmo hy avaśyaṃ maraṇe sati  Rm 
 paśuvat kiṃ gṛhe sthitvā sukhaṃ vā kiṃ yaśo vinā 
 yaśonvitā mṛtā ye hi tatpumāṃso narottamāḥ  Rm 
 yad artham eva jīvāmas tad arthaṃ yan na vidyate 
 kiṃ tena jīvitenāpi kevalaṃ duḥkhabhāginaḥ  Rm 
 varam evādya me mṛtyur na vyarthaṃ cirajīvitaṃ 
 Rm 
 yasmāc ciram api sthitvā mṛtyur kena nivāryyate  Rm 
 iti mṛtyubhayaṃ dṛṣṭvā sarvatrāpy anivāraṇaṃ 
 tyaktvā viṣādakauśīdyaṃ prodyamahyaṃ yaśorjane  Rm 
 evaṃ nānāprakāreṇa tena sārthabhṛtāpi te 
 bodhyamānā vaṇiksaṃghāḥ kiṃ cin naiva samūcire  Rm 
 abhadro 'yaṃ pumāṃ cāpi yato yātrā na siddhyati 
 iti tena mahāṃbhodhau naiko 'pi gantum aichata  Rm 
 atha sārthapatir dṛṣṭvā tān sarvān viratotsavān 
 eko 'pi vā svayaṃ gantum aichad ratnākaraṃ prati  Rm 
 tato bhāryāṃ samāmaṃtrya paribodhya prasannadhīḥ 
 svastyayanavidhiṃ kṛtvā pratasthe bhārakaiḥ saha  Rm 
 tataḥ paṇyaṃ samādāya bhāravāhajanaiḥ saha 
 purād vahi vinirgatya kramād deśāṃtaraṃ yayau  Rm 
 kramāc caṃcūryyamāno 'sau grāmāraṇyavanasthalīḥ 
 parikraman samullaṃghya prāpus tīraṃ mahodadheḥ  Rm 
 tatrāsau sārthabhṛd dṛṣṭvā taṃ samudraṃ mahāmbudhiṃ 
 kṛtāṃjalipuṭo natvā prārthayac charaṇaṃ gataḥ  Rm 
 namas te jīvam ādhāra sarvasatvārthasaṃpade 
 tvadāsayā samāyāmi tad āśāṃ me prapūraya  Rm 
 tato 'sau karṇadhāraṃ ca toṣayitvā prabodhayan 
 kṛtāṃjalipuṭo natvā saṃdhṛtvā samayācata  Rm 
 karṇadhāra mahāvāho tavāhaṃ śaraṇaṃ vraje 
 tat svasti cārayan naukāṃ yātrāsiddhiṃ prasādhaya  Rm 
 tathāsau vahanaṃ kṛtvā dṛḍhītaṃ gāḍhavaṃdhitaṃ 
 kṛtāṃjalipuṭo natvā saṃdhṛtvā samayācata  Rm 
 yathā mātā ca garbhasthaṃ vālakaṃ saṃprarakṣate 
 tathā mām eva garbhasthe nauke mātaḥ prarakṣatāṃ  Rm 
 tataś ca sugataṃ smṛtvā triratnaśaraṇaṃ gataḥ 
 kṛtāṃjalipuṭo bhūtvā praṇamyaivam ayācata  Rm 
 namas te bhagavan nātha yathā trāsi jagattrayaṃ 
 tathā māṃ kṛpayā dṛṣṭvā pāhi vraje ratnākare  Rm 
 ity evaṃ sārthavāho 'sau praṇatvā sugataṃ smaran 
 Rm 
 bhāṇḍāny āropya naukāyaṃ samārohaj janaṃ saha  Rm 
 tato 'sau naukrameṇaiva karṇadhāraprayatnataḥ 
 marutāṃ cānukūlena saṃjagāha mahāmbudhau  Rm 
 yat tatra sārthavāho 'sau saṃsmaran sugataṃ muhuḥ 
 tena puṇyabalenaiva sā naukā svastim ācaran  Rm 
 tathā kramāc caranty evaṃ dvīpalokāntarāṇi ca 
 vyatikramya suśighreṇa ratnākaraṃ samāyayau  Rm 
 tatra ratnākare prāpya ratnāni samasādhayan 
 tato ratnāni saṃgṛhya pratasthe vahanāsthitaḥ  Rm 
 tataḥ kramād vyatikramya dvīpalokāntarāṇi ca 
 tīraṃ prāpuḥ suśīghreṇa buddhadṛṣṭiprasādataḥ  Rm 
 tataḥ sthalaṃ samāsādya śailāraṇyavanasthalīḥ 
 grāmāṃ deśāṃ parikramya śrāvastyāṃ puram āyayau  Rm 
 tato gṛhe praviṣṭo 'sau bharyyayā saha moditaḥ 
 suhṛnmitrajanaiś cāpi kṛtvālāpaṃ nyaṣīdata  Rm 
 tataḥ sadyar gṛhastho 'sau bhāryyayā saha naṃditaḥ 
 bhāṇḍam udghāṭya ratnāni pratyavekṣitum ārabhat  Rm 
 tatra divyavicitrāṇi ratnāni vividhāni ca 
 dṛṣṭvā harṣaṃ samāsādya punar evaṃ vabhāṣate  Rm 
 mamaitāni suratnāni divyāny etādṛśāni hi 
 tatra divyavicitrāṇi nānāratnakulāni ca  Rm 
 labdhāni taj jinendrasya kṛpādṛṣṭiprasādataḥ 
 tasmād yathāpratijñātaṃ śraddhayā sāṃprataṃ mayā  Rm 
 yad upārddhaṃ pradātavyaiḥ śravaṇāyārhate 'pi naḥ 
 tad upārddhaṃ kathaṃ cānudātavyaṃ munaye 'rhate  Rm 
 yadi rājā vijānīyād etad arddhaṃ hare mama 
 ratnalubdho nareśo yaṃ daṇḍaṃ vā praṇayaṃ mayi  Rm 
 tadā me syād vipattiś ca tat kathaṃ kriyate mayā 
 aho daivād vipattir mām adyāpi ca na muṃcati 
 tat kathaṃ vā pratijñātaṃ pūrayituṃ na manyate 
 namas te bhagavan nātha sarvajño 'si munīśvaraḥ  Rm 
 rakṣa māṃ pāpinaṃ mūḍhanimagnaṃ duḥkhasāgare 
 ity asau sugataṃ smṛtvā taccintāvyathitāśayaḥ  Rm 
 kapolaṃ svakare dhṛtvā tasthau koṣṭhe nirutsavaḥ 
 Rm 
 tathaivaṃ sthitam ālokya svāmi naṃ taṃ viṣāditaṃ  Rm 
 sā bhāryā bhadrikopetya puraḥ sthitvābravīt tathā 
 svāmiṃ bharttaḥ kim eva tvaṃ sthito 'si duḥkhito yathā  Rm 
 kiṃ vā te jāyate duḥkhaṃ tad vaca cet priyāsmi te  Rm 
 iti bhāryoditaṃ śrutvā sa sārthādhipatiḥ punaḥ 
 tāṃ bhāryyāṃ samupāmaṃtrya punaś caivam abhāṣata  Rm 
 bhadre yaj jāyate duḥkhaṃ tat pravakṣye śṛṇu priye 
 yathā mayā pratijñātaṃ pūrayituṃ kathaṃ tathā  Rm 
 yady upārddhaṃ pradāsyāmi śravaṇāyārhate 'pi nu 
 etad arddhaṃ hared rājā lobhān me daṇḍayed api  Rm 
 ity evaṃ tadviṣādena vyathito 'haṃ nirutsavaḥ 
 tan me nātra pratīkāro kathaṃ kartuṃ na manyate  Rm 
 iti bharttroditaṃ śrutvā sā bhāryā punar abravīt 
 viṣādaṃ mā kṛthāḥ svāmiṃ śṛṇu yan me samīhitaiḥ  Rm 
 tāvad imāni saṃkalpaḥ paścāt tat samayāgate 
 pūjayā saha bhojaiś ca sasaṃghāyārhate 'rcayet  Rm 
 evaṃ kṛte tathā svāmin pratijñā tena setsyate 
 bhītiś cāpi na vidyeta tasmād evaṃ kuru prabho  Rm 
 iti bhāryāvacaḥ śrutvā sa sārthādhipatir mudā 
 tatheti pratisaṃśrutya punar evam abhāṣata  Rm 
 tāvad imāni sarvāṇi ratnāni te samarppaye 
 paścāt kāle sasaṃghaṃ taṃ pūjayiṣye munīśvaraṃ  Rm 
 idānīṃ sugaṃdhadhūpena pūjayeyaṃ munīśvaraṃ 
 ity uktvā sarvaratnāni bhāryāyāṃ sa nyadhāpayet  Rm 
 tato 'sau cāguruṃ krītvā kārṣāpaṇadvayena vā 
 gatvā jetavane vihāre tatra dvāre sthito gurum adhūpayet  Rm 
 tatrāpatramāno 'sau saṃbuddhaśaraṇaṃ gataḥ 
 kṛtāṃjalipuṭo natvā saṃsmaran prārthayat tathā  Rm 
 bhagavac chāstāsi sarvajño vijānīyā mamāśayaṃ 
 tadyathā me pratijñātaiḥ pūrayituṃ samarhasi  Rm 
 athāsau bhagavān tasya matvāśayaviśuddhatāṃ 
 Rm 
 mahad ṛdhyabhisaṃskāraṃ cakāra tatprasādataḥ  Rm 
 yena sa dhūpa ākāśe prābhyudgamya purīṃ ca tāṃ 
 sphuritvā khe punar abhrakūṭībhūtvābhyaśobhayat  Rm 
 tatrāsau sārthabhṛd dṛṣṭvā prātihāryaṃ tad adbhutaṃ 
 mahānaṃdaprasaṃnātmā punar evaṃ vyaciṃtayat  Rm 
 naitan me pratirūpaṃ syād yad ayaṃ sugato jinaḥ 
 mayā nābhyarcito ratnair dhig me cittabhayād drutaṃ  Rm 
 yanv ahaṃ sāṃprataṃ nāthaṃ prārthayitvā sasāṃghikaṃ 
 saratnaiḥ pūjayiṣyāmi bhojanaiś ca svake gṛhe  Rm 
 ity asau niścayaṃ kṛtvā kṛtāṃjalipuṭo mudā 
 saṃbuddhasaṃmukhaṃ gatvā praṇatvaivaṃ vyajijñapat  Rm 
 bhagavan nātha sarvajña kṣamasva me 'parādhatāṃ 
 bhavatāṃ pūjanāṃ kartum ichāmi me prasīdatu  Rm 
 ity evaṃ prārthite tena sa saṃbuddho munīśvaraḥ 
 tatheti pratisaṃmodya tūṣṇībhūtvā vyavasthitaḥ  Rm 
 tato 'sau sārthabhṛn matvā sugatenādhivāsitaṃ 
 praṇatvā ca muneḥ pādau sahasā svagṛhaṃ yayau  Rm 
 tatra sa bhāryyayā sārddhaṃ vaṃdhumitra janair api 
 praṇītaṃ bhojyapūjāṃgaṃ sādhayām āsa satvaraṃ  Rm 
 tato bhojyārcanāṃgāni sajjīkṛtya pramoditaḥ 
 vihāre sahasā gatvā natvā taṃ prārthayan muniṃ  Rm 
 bhagavan nātha saṃbuddha samayo 'yaṃ pravarttate 
 tad bhavān sāṃghikaiḥ sārddhaṃ samāgantuṃ samarhati  Rm 
 ity evaṃ prārthite tena sa saṃbuddhaḥ sasāṃghikaḥ 
 pratasthe sūryyavan mārge prātihāryaṃ pradarśayan  Rm 
 tataḥ kramāt purīṃ prāpya tad gṛhaṃ samupāviśat 
 tad datte pādyaṃ ādāya śuddhāsane nyaṣīdata  Rm 
 tatas tān sāṃghikān sarvān saṃbuddhapramukhān kramāt 
 svasvāsanasamāsīnān dṛṣṭvā samyak samarcayat  Rm 
 yathārhaṃ bhojanair vāpi varṇagandharasānvitaiḥ 
 saṃbuddhapramukhān saṃghān saṃtarpya paryatoṣayat  Rm 
 tataś ca bhojanānte sa śodhayitvā bhujādikaṃ 
 Rm 
 apanīya ca pātrāṇi tāmbūlādīn aḍhaukayat  Rm 
 tato yāni suratnāni pūrvasaṃkalpatāni hi 
 etaiḥ sarvaṃ suratnais taṃ saṃbuddhaiḥ samavākiran  Rm 
 tāni ratnāni sarvāṇi saṃbuddhasyānubhāvataḥ 
 muner upari khe gatvā chatrībhūtvā sthitā vabhau  Rm 
 tatas taṃ sa gṛhī dṛṣṭvā dviguṇasaṃpramoditaḥ 
 pādau tasya muner natvā praṇidhānaṃ vyadhāt tathā  Rm 
 anena dānadharmeṇa puṇyena kuśalena ca 
 bhaveyaṃ sugato buddho loke 'ndhe 'pariṇāyake  Rm 
 amukto mocayiṣyāmi tārayiṣyāmy atāritān 
 bhītān āśvāsya saṃbodhau sthāpayiṣyāmi nirvṛtau  Rm 
 tathāsau bhagavān buddhas tathāśayaviśodhitaṃ 
 saṃbodhau nihitaṃ cittaṃ jñātvā smitaṃ vyadhāt tathā  Rm 
 tadā tasya munīndrasya mukhapadmād vinirgatāḥ 
 paṃcavarṇā vibhāsanto viniśceruḥ subhānavaḥ  Rm 
 tatas te bhāsvarāḥ sarve pravisṛtāḥ samaṃtataḥ 
 kecid ūrddhaṃ gatāḥ kecin madhyaṃ kecid rasātale  Rm 
 kecid adho gatā yās te sarve te narakeṣu ca 
 nipataṃto vibhāsanto pravisasruḥ samaṃtataḥ  Rm 
 ye uṣṇanarakās teṣu śitībhūtā vicerire 
 ye śītanarakās teṣu nyapatad uṣṇikāś ca te  Rm 
 ye ye taiḥ kiraṇaiḥ spṛṣṭās te te sarve sukhānvitāḥ 
 yadā te sukhasaṃprāptās tadā te vismayānvitāḥ  Rm 
 aho naḥ sukham adyaivaṃ katham etad vyacintayan 
 kiṃ nu vayam itaś cyutvā kutra yātāsma sāṃprataṃ  Rm 
 āhosvid upapannāḥ syur anyatra bhuvaneṣv api 
 iti saṃdehināṃ teṣāṃ satvānāṃ paribodhane  Rm 
 bhagavān nirmite buddhaṃ preṣayan narakān prati 
 dṛṣṭvā taṃ nirmitaṃ muniṃ vismitā harṣitāś ca vai  Rm 
 te sarve narakā lokāḥ saṃmīlya saṃvabhāṣire 
 na bhavanta itaś cyutvā gatāsmānyatra bhūmiṣu  Rm 
 kiṃs tv ayaṃ nu mahāsatvaḥ hy apūrvadarśanaḥ pumān 
 Rm 
 nūnam asyānubhāvena duḥkhāni samitāni ca  Rm 
 tad vayam enam ānamya vaṃde mayā pramuktaye 
 iti saṃbhāṣya te sarve natvā tac charaṇaṃ gatāḥ  Rm 
 namo buddhāya dharmāya saṃghāyeti vavandire 
 iti te nirmite tasmin prasādya cittam āratāḥ  Rm 
 sarvapāpavinirmuktā martyadevālayaṃ yayuḥ 
 evaṃ te bhānavaḥ sarve sarvatra narakeṣv api  Rm 
 prodyante nārakān sarvān pratyāyayur muneḥ puraḥ 
 tathā tad bhānavaś caivam upariṣṭāṃ gatā api  Rm 
 te 'pi sarve caturlokapālānāṃ bhuvanāni ca 
 avabhāsya kramāt sarvān devalokān abhāsayan  Rm 
 tathākaniṣṭhaparyantaṃ traidhātukān abhāsayan 
 evaṃ sarvāś ca tān sarvān avabhāsya samaṃtataḥ  Rm 
 gāthāḥ prodghoṣayantaś ca pralayaṃ saugate vṛṣe 
 anityaṃ khalu saṃsāraṃ duḥkhaśūnyaṃ hy anātmakaṃ  Rm 
 tasmāt māraṃ parityajya gachadhvaṃ śaraṇaṃ muneḥ 
 niṣkrāmatārabhadhvaṃ kaṃ yujyadhvaṃ buddhaśāsane  Rm 
 mṛtyusainyaṃ dhunītāśu naḍāgāraṃ karī yathā 
 yo 'py asmin dharmavinaye hy apramattaś cariṣyati  Rm 
 tyaktvā jātisasaṃsāre duḥkhasyāntaṃ kariṣyati  Rm 
 atha te bhānavaḥ sarve traidhātubhuvaneṣv api 
 sarvān satvān samuddhṛtya punaḥ pratyāyayur muneḥ  Rm 
 atha te bhānavaḥ sarve bhagavantaṃ munīśvaraṃ 
 pradakṣiṇatrayaṃ kṛtvā mūrddhni cāntardadhur muneḥ  Rm 
 athaitat sabhāsīnā lokāḥ sarve sasāṃghikāḥ 
 tat tadadbhutam ālokya vabhūvur vismayoddhatāḥ  Rm 
 athānaṃdaḥ samutthāya kṛtāṃjalipuṭo mudā 
 bhagavantaṃ guruṃ natvā papracha smitakāraṇaṃ  Rm 
 bhagavan bhavato vaktrāt paṃcavarṇāḥ subhāṃsavaḥ 
 vinirgatā diśaḥ sarvān avabhāsya śatā punaḥ  Rm 
 bhavān hi sugato śāstā saṃbuddho bhagavañ jinaḥ 
 Rm 
 nirmado nirahaṃkāraḥ mānamātsaryyavarjitaḥ  Rm 
 tad bhava bhagavaṃ kasmāt smitaiḥ karoti sāṃprataṃ 
 dṛṣṭvaivaṃ taṃ smitaṃ sarve ime lokāḥ pravismitāḥ  Rm 
 nāhetuḥ sugatā buddhā arhanto vigatoddhavāḥ 
 darśayanti smitaṃ kecit tat kena bhavataḥ smṛtaṃ  Rm 
 tad etad dhetum ichanti śrotuṃ sarve ime janāḥ 
 tad etat kāraṇaṃ śāstaḥ samādeṣṭuṃ samarhati  Rm 
 ity evaṃ prārthite tena śiṣyeṇānaṃdayoginā 
 tatheti pratisaṃmodya tam ānaṃdaṃ vabhāṣata  Rm 
 evam etat tathānaṃda yathaiva bhāṣasi tvayā 
 tat smitaṃ yadarthaṃ me tad vakṣye śṛṇutādarāt  Rm 
 paśyānaṃda mamānena sārthavāhena sādhunā 
 ebhī ratnaiś ca satkṛtya kṛtā pūjā svabhaktitaḥ  Rm 
 anena kuśalenaiva sārthavāho mahāsudhīḥ 
 kramād bodhicarīṃ prāpya pūryya pāramitā daśa  Rm 
 saṃbodhipākṣikān dharmān prāpya brahmavihārikaḥ 
 saṃbodhiṃ samavāpyaivaṃ jitvā māragaṇān api  Rm 
 buddho ratnottamo nāma sarvajño 'rhaṃ tathāgataḥ 
 dharmarājo jagaṃnātho loke śāstā bhaviṣyati  Rm 
 tad anumodanāṃ kṛtvā saddharmaṃ bhajatādarāt 
 dharmeṇaiva jagaj jitvā māracaryāvinirgataḥ  Rm 
 bhadracarī samāsādya saṃbodhipadam āpnuyāt 
 dharnio hi jagatāṃ mitram ihāmutra samantataḥ  Rm 
 hitakārī suhṛd iṣṭaḥ sarvadāpi sahānugaḥ 
 tasmād dharmaṃ samādhāya saṃcaradhvaṃ samāhitaḥ  Rm 
 tena vā maṃgalaṃ nityaṃ sarvabhāvī bhaved dhruvaṃ  Rm 
 iti śāstrā samādiṣṭaṃ śrutvānaṃdaḥ sapārṣadaḥ 
 tatheti moditas taṃ ca guruṃ natvā sa naṃdataḥ  Rm 
 so 'pi sārthapatiś caiva svakaṃ vyākaraṇaṃ kila 
 munīndreṇa samādiṣṭaṃ śrutvātīvābhyanaṃdatat  Rm 
 tataś cābhiprasannātmā samutthāya kṛtāṃjaliḥ 
 bhagavaṃtaṃ sasaṃghaṃ taṃ praṇatvaivaṃ vyatijñapat  Rm 
 namas te bhagavan nātha sarvadharmādhipeśvaraḥ 
 Rm 
 bhavatāṃ śaraṇaṃ kṛtvā bhavāmy aham upāsakaḥ  Rm 
 yan mayā prakṛtaṃ pāpaṃ kāritaṃ cānumoditaṃ 
 tat sarvaṃ deśayiṣyāmi tan me dehi śubhāṃ cariṃ  Rm 
 bodhau cittaṃ samādhāya triratnaṃ samupāśraye 
 kṣamasva me 'parādhatvaṃ tan māṃ rakṣa mudā tathā  Rm 
 evaṃ tenārthitaṃ śrutvā sa saṃbuddho 'bhyadhāt punaḥ 
 yathā te 'bhihitaṃ sādho tathā saṃsetsyate dhruvaṃ  Rm 
 tasmāc cittaṃ samādhāya triratnaśaraṇaṃ gataḥ 
 sarvasatvahitaṃ kṛtvā bodhicaryāṃ samācara  Rm 
 tatas tvaṃ kramato hy evaṃ pūrya pāramitā drutaṃ 
 bodhisatvo mahāsatvo bhaved bodhim avāpnuyāt  Rm 
 etat satyaṃ parijñāya saddharmaṃ saṃprasādhaya 
 tena te maṃgalaṃ nityaṃ sarvatrāpi bhaved dhruvaṃ  Rm 
 jayo 'stu te sadā bodhau siddhyatu praṇihitaṃ drutaṃ 
 ciraṃ jīvaṃ hitaṃ loke dharmaṃ dhṛtvā sukhaṃ vasa  Rm 
 ity asau bhagavān buddhas tasmai datvāśiṣaṃ śubhāṃ 
 saṃghaiḥ saha samutthāya svaṃ vihāraṃ yayau tataḥ  Rm 
 atha sārthapatiś cāsau sadāraḥ saṃpramoditaḥ 
 triratnaśaraṇaṃ kṛtvā saddharmeṣu sadācarat  Rm 
 tathā sarve 'pi satvāś ca śrutvā tasya pravṛttitāṃ 
 bodhicittaṃ samādhāya triratnaśaraṇaṃ yayuḥ  Rm 
 etat me guruṇākhyātaṃ saṃśrutaṃ yathā mayā 
 tathātraivaṃ tava prītyā kathyate saṃprabudhyatāṃ  Rm 
 tathā rājan tvayāpy evaṃ svayaṃ dhṛtvā vṛṣaṃ śubhe 
 bodhayitvā prajāś cāpi sthāpanīyāḥ sadā śubhe  Rm 
 evaṃ cet te sadāpy evaṃ sarvatrāpi sumaṃgalaṃ 
 bhaven nūnaṃ mahārājan satyam etan na saṃśayaḥ 
 dharmeṇa nirjitaṃ pāpaṃ dharmeṇa jīyate kudhīḥ 
 dharmeṇa nirjitā mārā dharmeṇa bodhim āpnuyāt 
 tasmād bodhipadaṃ prāptuṃ yadīcchatha narādhipaḥ 
 bodhicittaṃ samādhāya sadā ratnatrayaṃ bhaja 
 tathā taṃ kramaṇo rāja bodhicaryyāhitāya ca 
 sarvamāragaṇām jitvā saṃbodhim āpnuyā dhruvaṃ 
 etat tenopaguptena guruṇādiṣṭaṃ samādarāt 
 Rm 
 śrutvā rājo tathety evaṃ pratyanandan sapārṣadaḥ 
 ye śṛṇvantīdam evaṃ praṇihitamanasaḥ sārthavāhāvadānaṃ 
 ye cāpi śrāvayanti pramuditamanasaḥ sarvalokahitārthaṃ 
 te sarve bodhisatvā vijitakalimalo buddhadharmānuraktāḥ 
 saṃbhuktvā satsukhāni prathitaguṇayutā buddhakṣetre prayānti 
  iti śrīratnamālāvadānakathāyāṃ sārthavāho'vadānaṃ nāma dvādaśa 
 Rm 
 XIII Vaḍikāvadāna
 oṃ namaḥ śrīsarvabuddhabodhisatvebhyaḥ 
 yaḥ śrīmāñ chrīghano loke saddharmaiḥ samupādiśat 
 śāsanāni trilokeṣu jayantu tasya sarvadā  Rm 
 avadānatatvaṃ vakṣyāmi natvā taṃ śrīghanaṃ guruṃ 
 purābhūt pāṭalīputre nagare svargasannibhe  Rm 
 aśoko nṛparājendras triratnasevakaḥ kṛtī 
 ekasmin samaye tatra sa rājā svajanaiḥ saha  Rm 
 paurikaiś ca sabhāṃ kṛtvā saddharmaṃ śrotum aicchata 
 tadā sa saugato bhikṣur upagupto jināṃśajaḥ  Rm 
 lokān dharmotsukān dṛṣṭvā samādheḥ sahasotthitaḥ 
 tatsabhāyāṃ samākramya siṃhāsane śubhāsane  Rm 
 bhāsayaṃs tatsabhālokāṃs tasthau pūrṇasudhāṃśuvat 
 athāśoko mahīpālaḥ sa maṃtripaurikaiḥ saha  Rm 
 pūjāṅgaiḥ pūjayitvā tam upaguptam avandata 
 sthitvā bhūmau svajānubhyām uttarāsaṅgam udvahan  Rm 
 kṛtāñjaliḥ puṭo natvā punar evam abhāṣata 
 bhadanta śrotum icchāmi saddharmaṃ sukhasaṃpradaṃ  Rm 
 yathoktaṃ śrīmunīndreṇa tathā deṣṭuṃ ca me 'rhati 
 evaṃ tena mahīndreṇa prārthite sa yatīśvaraḥ  Rm 
 upagupto narendraṃ taṃ samāmantryaivam abravīt 
 sādhu suṣṭhu mahārāja śṛṇu saddharmam ādarāt  Rm 
 yathā me guruṇā khyātaṃ tathā vakṣyāmi te hite 
 purā sa bhagavān buddhaḥ śakyasiṃho śubhākaraḥ  Rm 
 dharmarājo jagacchāstā sarvajñaḥ sugato jinaḥ 
 sarvavidyākalāvijñaḥ ṣaḍabhijño munīśvaraḥ  Rm 
 mārajil lokavin nātho vināyakas tathāgataḥ 
 śrāvastyāṃ jetakāraṇye mahodyāne manorame  Rm 
 anāthapiṇḍadākhyasya gṛhasthasya mahātmanaḥ 
 nānāvṛkṣasamākīrṇe nānāpuṣpapraśobhitaiḥ  Rm 
 nānāphalabharānamraiḥ kalpavṛkṣasamānikaiḥ 
 aṣṭāṅgaguṇasaṃpannajalaiḥ padmotpālādibhiḥ  Rm 
 supuṣpaiḥ paripūrṇābhiḥ puṣkariṇībhir āśrite 
 nānājantuguṇaiś cāpi mithaḥ snehānuvandhitaiḥ  Rm 
 nānāpakṣigaṇaiś cāpi saṃharṣair upasevite 
 tasmiṃ divyamanoramye munisaṃghaniṣevite  Rm 
 puṇyakṣetre jināvāse vihāre maṇimaṇḍite 
 śrāvakair bhikṣubhiḥ sārddhaṃ bodhisatvair upāsakaiḥ  Rm 
 sarvasatvahitārthena tasthau dharmmaṃ prakāśituṃ 
 Rm 
 evaṃ tatra sabhāsīnaṃ saṃbuddhaṃ dharmabhāṣiṇaṃ  Rm 
 dṛṣṭvā dharmāmṛtaṃ pātuṃ sarvalokāḥ samāyayuḥ  Rm 
 daivā daityāś ca siddhāś ca yakṣagaṃdharvakinnarāḥ 
 grahā vidyādharāḥ sādhyā nāgeṃdrā garuḍā api  Rm 
 sarve 'pi lokapālāś ca munayaś ca maharṣayaḥ 
 yatayo yoginaś cāpi tīrthikāś ca tapaśvinaḥ  Rm 
 brāhmaṇāḥ kṣatriyāś cāpi vaiśyāḥ śūdrāś ca maṃtriṇaḥ 
 amātyāḥ koṭṭavārāś ca sārthavāhā mahājanāḥ  Rm 
 śilpino vaṇijaś cāpi gṛhasthāḥ paurikā janāḥ 
 tathā jānapadāś cāpi grāmyāḥ kārpaṭikā api  Rm 
 evam anye 'pi satvāś ca sarvajātisamudbhavāḥ 
 pūjāpaṃcopahārāṇi gṛhītvā bhaktimānasā  Rm 
 saddharmaṃ śraddhayā śrotum anumodya samāyayuḥ 
 tatra sarve praviṣṭās te dṛṣṭvā taṃ sugataṃ jinaṃ  Rm 
 vanditvānanditāḥ sarve pūjāṃ cakrur yathākramaṃ  Rm 
 tato natvā samāsīnāḥ parivṛtya pramoditāḥ 
 dharmmaṃ śrotuṃ puraskṛtya tasthuḥ sāñjalayo mudā  Rm 
 atha sa bhagavān dṛṣṭvā tāṃl lokān dharmavāñchinaḥ 
 ādimadhyāntakalyāṇaṃ dideśa dharmam uttamaṃ  Rm 
 evaṃ sa bhagavān nityaṃ sarvasatvahitārthikaḥ 
 dharmaṃ prakāśayaṃ loke tasthau dīptāṃśumān iva  Rm 
 tasminn avasare tatra śrāvastyāṃ purisaṃbhavaḥ 
 āḍhyaḥ śreṣṭhī mahābhogaḥ suvistīrṇaparigrahaḥ  Rm 
 śrāddho bhadrāśayo dhīraḥ sarvalokasuhṛtpriyaḥ 
 tīrthikasevako mānī vabhūva śrīmadānvitaḥ  Rm 
 tadā sa sundarībhāryāṃ kuladharmasamānikāṃ 
 ādāya ratisaṃrakto reme nityaṃ yathāsukhaṃ  Rm 
 tasyaivaṃ ramamāṇasya bhāryā sābhūt sugarbhiṇī 
 tataḥ pravṛddhagarbhā sā pāṇḍuvarṇā vyarājata  Rm 
 tataḥ sā garbhasaṃjātaṃ putraṃ tasyām upāśritaṃ 
 putraṃ matvābhinaṃdaṃtī bharttāram evam abravīt  Rm 
 svāmin garbhe prajāto me yat kukṣau dakṣiṇāśritaḥ 
 dārako 'yaṃ bhavet putraḥ nūnaṃ tasmāt pramodaya  Rm 
 iti bhāryoditaṃ śrutvā sa gṛhasthaḥ praharṣitaḥ 
 garbhe sa vyāśritaṃ dṛṣṭvā mudaivaṃ samudānayat  Rm 
 vata me jāyate putras tad ahaṃ bhāgyavān bhave 
 putramukhaṃ hi paśyeyaṃ vaṃśasthitir bhaved api  Rm 
 yan mama vidyate puṇyaṃ dānaśīlādisaṃcitaṃ 
 tenānayor dvayor astu jananīputrayoḥ śivaṃ  Rm 
 evaṃ proktvā gṛhasthaḥ sa śraddhayā saṃpramoditaḥ 
 bhikṣvarthibrāhmaṇebhyaś ca dadau dānaṃ yathepsitaṃ  Rm 
 Rm 
 kuleṣṭadevatāś cāpi samabhyarcya yathāvidhi 
 tac chubhaṃ prārthayan nityaṃ tasthau putrasamutsukaḥ  Rm 
 tataḥ sā bhadrikā nārī pathyopacārabhoginī 
 asūta samaye putraṃ suṃdaraṃ lakṣaṇānvitaṃ  Rm 
 tataḥ sa janakaḥ śrutvā saṃprajātaṃ sutaṃ mudā 
 sahasā samupāsritya dadarśa taṃ sasuṃdaraṃ  Rm 
 darśanīyaṃ subhadrāṅgaṃ prāsādikaṃ manoharaṃ 
 dṛṣṭvāpi suciraṃ paśyann eva tasthāv atṛptitaḥ  Rm 
 tato jātimahaṃ kṛtvā tasya pitrā prasādinā 
 vaḍika iti nāmnā prakhyāpito 'bhūt sa dārakaḥ  Rm 
 tataḥ sa vālako 'ṣṭābhyo dhātrībhyaḥ pratipālane 
 mānayitvānusaṃbhāṣya pitrā samarpito 'bhavat  Rm 
 tathā sa vaḍiko vālo 'ṣṭābhir dhātrībhir ādarāt 
 pālyamānaḥ pravṛddho 'bhūt hradastham iva paṃkajaṃ  Rm 
 yadā sa dārakaḥ paṃcavarṣito 'bhūn madānvitaḥ 
 tadā vidyopalabdhārthī lipiśālām upāviśat  Rm 
 tatra sa sadguruṃ natvā kramāl lipīn mudāgrahīt 
 gurubhaktiprasādena lipipāraṃ yayau laghu  Rm 
 tataḥ sa gurubhiḥ samyac chiṣyamāṇaḥ subuddhimān 
 adhītya sarvaśāstrāṇi vidyāpāraṃ yayau laghu  Rm 
 tadā tad vaḍikasyāpi pūrvakarmavipākataḥ 
 dehe kasmāt samutpanno mahāvyādhiḥ parākramat  Rm 
 tadā sa vyādhinā tena pīḍyamāno 'bhimūrchitaḥ 
 asahyavedanākrānto virurāva divāniśaṃ  Rm 
 tathā taṃ vyādhināghrātam asahyavedanāturaṃ 
 krandantaṃ sa pitā dṛṣṭvā kṛpayaivaṃ vyaciṃtayat  Rm 
 hā me daivaviruddhena putro 'yaṃ vyādhimūrchitaḥ 
 asahyavedanākrānto bhoktum api na vāñchati  Rm 
 avaśyaṃ maraṇaṃ yāyāt kathaṃ jīved abhuktavān 
 mṛte putre mariṣye 'haṃ snehaduḥkhaṃ kathaṃ sahe  Rm 
 iti cintāvyathākrānto bhogye 'pi viratotsavaḥ 
 tam eva svātmajaṃ paśyaṃs tasthau snehābhivandhitaḥ  Rm 
 mātāpi taṃ sutaṃ dṛṣṭvā snehaduḥkhāgnitāpitā 
 Rm 
 mṛtyuśaṃkā paritrastā rudantī samupācarat  Rm 
 tadā tasya suhṛnmitravāṃdhavāḥ samupāgatāḥ 
 sarve te rogiṇaṃ dṛṣṭvā snehārttā evam abruvan  Rm 
 kiṃ bho svasthaṃ na te dehe bhoktuṃ kiṃ vā na vāñchasi 
 bhuṃkṣva yathepsitaṃ pathyaṃ tiṣṭha dhairyaṃ samāśrayan  Rm 
 iti prokte 'pi taiḥ sarvaiḥ sa vaḍiko jvarānvitaḥ 
 dṛṣṭvaiva tān muhuḥ paśyan naiva kiñcid abhāṣata  Rm 
 tataḥ sarve 'pi te dṛṣṭvā taṃ vaḍikaṃ rujāturaṃ 
 mṛtyuśaṃkāviṣādigdhaṃ pitaraṃ taṃ tathāvadan  Rm 
 sādho 'sya varddhate rogas tad rogavyupāśāntaye 
 sahasā vaidyam āhūya darśayasva samāhitaḥ  Rm 
 upadiṣṭaṃ yathā tena vaidyena sudhiyā tathā 
 paricaryyāṃ samādhāya kurūpacāram ādarāt  Rm 
 tathā pathyopacāreṇa siddhauṣadhyasahair api 
 kramād asya śarīrastho rogaḥ śāntiṃ vrajed dhruvaṃ  Rm 
 tatas te 'yaṃ suto bhadraḥ paripuṣṭatanuḥkṛtī 
 svakuladharmam ādhāya sukhaṃ jīvec chubhe caran  Rm 
 iti matvā mahābhāga mā kṛthās tad viṣādanaṃ 
 dhairyam ālamvya devāṃś ca smṛtvā bhuktvā sukhaṃ vasa  Rm 
 ity evaṃ samupādiśya tad gṛhasthāt samutthitāḥ 
 sarve te snehaduḥkhārttāḥ svasvageham upācarat  Rm 
 tataḥ sa gṛhabhṛt tasya putrasya rogaśāṃtaye 
 sadvaidyaṃ samupāhūya sādaraṃ samadarśayat  Rm 
 tasya roganimittaṃ sa vaidyo dṛṣṭvā samīkṣya ca 
 pathyauṣadhyupacāreṇa samāhita upācarat  Rm 
 tathāpi tasya tadrogaḥ parivṛddho dine dine 
 kenāpi hy upacāreṇa naiva śāntim upāyayau  Rm 
 tadrogaṃ varddhitaṃ dṛṣṭvā janakaḥ sa viṣāditaḥ 
 bhūtikaṃ sahasāhūya rogahetum apṛcchata  Rm 
 tataḥ sa bhūtiko dṛṣṭvā tasya rogapraśāntaye 
 sa bhūtadevatābhyaś ca valiṃ prādād yathāvidhi  Rm 
 tathāpi vṛṃhito rogas tasya karmavipākataḥ 
 kiñcid api viśeṣeṇa naiva śāntim upāyayau  Rm 
 tataḥ sa janako dṛṣṭvā tad rogaṃ parivarddhitaṃ 
 āyurvidam upāmaṃtrya rogahetum apṛcchata  Rm 
 Rm 
 sa ayurvidako dṛṣṭvā tasya grahadaśāphalaṃ 
 kudaśāvyupaśāntyarthaṃ grahapūjām upādiśat  Rm 
 tathā sa janakas tasya rogiṇo grahaśāntaye 
 brāhmaṇaṃ samupāmantrya grahapūjām akārayat  Rm 
 tathāpi tasya tadrogo varddhito na śamaṃ yayau 
 daivena samupāghrāte tadupāye na siddhyate  Rm 
 tathā sa janakas tasya putrasya rogavṛddhitaṃ 
 dṛṣṭvā nirāśayā bhinnacitto mūrcchām upāyayau  Rm 
 tadā sā supriyā bhāryā bharttāraṃ taṃ vimohitaṃ 
 dṛṣṭvaiva samupāgṛhya samāśvāsyaivam abravīt  Rm 
 svāmin dhairyyaṃ samālambya tyaja citte vimohatāṃ 
 kim asmākaṃ prayatnena daivasyātra pramāṇike  Rm 
 sarvathā bhāvino bhāvāḥ phalaṃti sarvajīvināṃ 
 yad abhāvi na tad bhāvi bhāvi cen na tad anyathā  Rm 
 tasmād daivaprasādāya svakuleśeṣṭadevatāḥ 
 anusmṛtya samārādhya yācasva putrajīvitaṃ  Rm 
 iti bhāryoditaṃ śrutvā sa gṛhastho 'numoditaḥ 
 kuladevaṃ samabhyarcya prārthayad evam ādarāt  Rm 
 prasīda me kuleśa tvaṃ kṣamasva hy aparādhatāṃ 
 tavaiva śaraṇastho 'haṃ tan me putraṃ prarakṣatāṃ  Rm 
 evaṃ tena gṛhasthena prārthite 'pi divāniśaṃ 
 tasya rogo vivṛddho 'bhūn naiva śāmyam upākramat  Rm 
 tathā brahmādidevāṃś ca sarvān lokādhipān api 
 vihāramaṇḍapārāmakṣetrāraṇyasamāśritān  Rm 
 nadīkūpataḍāgādijalāśrayapratisthitān 
 balibhoktṝn kalaṃkasthān mārgaśṛṅgāṭakāśritān  Rm 
 evam anyatra sarvatra pratisthitān samarcayan 
 putrasyārogyakauśalyaṃ jīvitaṃ sa samarthayan  Rm 
 tathāpi tasya rogo na śamito 'bhūt pravarddhitaḥ 
 tatas taṃ janako dṛṣṭvā nirāśā mūrchito 'patat  Rm 
 tadā sa vaḍiko rogī pitaraṃ taṃ vimūrchitaṃ 
 pṛthivyāṃ patitaṃ dṛṣṭvā śanair nīcasvaro 'vadat  Rm 
 hā hā me jāvate pāpaṃ yenāyaṃ patitaḥ pitā 
 Rm 
 snehaduḥkhāgnisaṃtaptaḥ putrato maraṇaṃ vrajet  Rm 
 hā tātottiṣṭha māṃ paśya mā tyajātmajaṃ āturaṃ 
 dhairyyam ālamvya saṃdhāya rakṣa māṃ samupasthitaḥ  Rm 
 ity asau vilapan putraḥ pitaraṃ taṃ vimūrchitaṃ 
 dṛṣṭvā bhojanakety aśru muñcaṃs tasthau nirāśritaḥ  Rm 
 tadā sā supriyā bhāryyā bharttāraṃ taṃ vimūrchitaṃ 
 dṛṣṭvaiva sahasāliṃgya samutthāpyaivam abravīt  Rm 
 svāmin dhairyaṃ samālaṃbya paśya māṃ te priyaṃ satīṃ 
 tyaktvā dainyaṃ samādhāya paśyan rakṣātmakaṃ priyaṃ  Rm 
 iti bhāryoditaṃ śrutvā sa gṛhastho samutthitaḥ 
 dṛṣṭvā tāṃ supriyāṃ bhāryāṃ putraṃ caivam abhāṣata  Rm 
 hā daiva kiṃ mayā pāpaṃ prakṛtaṃ dāruṇaṃ purā 
 yenāyaṃ sukṛtī putraḥ tyaktvā māṃ kva prayāsyati  Rm 
 hā hā me saṃpadaś caitāḥ samṛddhāḥ samupārjitāḥ 
 ko nu bhoktā bhaved āsāṃ vyarthaṃ nakṣyanti sarvaśaḥ  Rm 
 kim atrāhaṃ kariṣyāmi yāsyāmi śaraṇaṃ ca kaṃ 
 ko nu māṃ sahasā rakṣed datvā putrasya jīvitaṃ  Rm 
 kim atrāsya rujaḥ śāntyai kariṣyāmi pratikriyāṃ 
 na jāne parimūḍho 'smi cetanā me na vidyate  Rm 
 iti cintāparītātmā putrasnehavimohitaḥ 
 kāruṇākulacitto 'pi punar evaṃ vyacintayat  Rm 
 yad ime tīrthikā vijñā bhagavanto vicakṣaṇāḥ 
 sarvajñāḥ sadguṇādhārāḥ śāstāro me hitaṃkarāḥ  Rm 
 tat tān sarvān samāmaṃtrya gṛhe bhokṣyaiḥ samarcayan 
 imaṃ putraṃ puraḥ sthāpya darśayeyaṃ śubhāptaye  Rm 
 tat sudṛṣṭiprasādena nūnam asya bhavec chuvaṃ 
 tato hi kramaśo rogāḥ śāmyeyuḥ sarvathā laghu  Rm 
 tadāyam ātmajaḥ puṣṭo na rogī sutanuḥ sukhī 
 kṛtī śubharato bhogī kuladharme samācaret  Rm 
 iti niścitya sa śreṣṭhī tatra tīrthyāśrame gataḥ 
 tān sarvāṃs tīrthikān natvā prārthayed evam ādarāt  Rm 
 namo vo brahmavijñebhyo bhavatāṃ śaraṇaṃ vraje 
 vijñapyate yad arthaṃ tad anugrahītum arhata  Rm 
 Rm 
 iti tenoditaṃ śrutvā tīrthikās te 'bhimānikāḥ 
 sarve taṃ samupāmaṃtrya pramodayitum abruvan  Rm 
 sādhu vada mahāsādho yat te kāryaṃ samīhitaṃ 
 tat sarvaṃ sarvathāsmābhiḥ kṛtam evaṃ kariṣyate  Rm 
 iti tais tīrthikaiḥ prokte sa śreṣṭhī saṃprasāditaḥ 
 kṛtāñjalipuṭo natvā punar evam abhāṣata  Rm 
 bhagavanto mahāvijñā bhavanto guravo mama 
 tat sarvaṃ pratijānīta yad arthaṃ samupācare  Rm 
 tathāpi cārthayiṣye 'tra yan me kaṣṭaṃ pravarttate 
 tad vo vijñāpanaṃ kartuṃ bhavataḥ śaraṇaṃ vraje  Rm 
 yan mayā prakṛtaṃ pāpaṃ tena me svātmajādhunā 
 rogaiḥ saṃpīḍyate 'tīvaniḥsvastho maraṇaṃ vrajet  Rm 
 nānāsvastividhānair hi tasya rogo na śāmyati 
 bhiṣajāṃ kṛtayatnāni na siddhyanti kathaṃ cana  Rm 
 anekā devatāś cāpi prābhyarcya prārthito mayā 
 tathāpi śāmyate naiva tasya rogo vivarddhitaḥ  Rm 
 yathā yathā rujāśāntisvastyupāyakṛtāni hi 
 tathā tathā na tadrogaḥ praśāmyati pravarddhyate  Rm 
 kim upāyaṃ kariṣyāmi kena śāmyeta tadgadaḥ 
 tad upāyaṃ pradātavyaṃ yenāśu śāmyate kramāt  Rm 
 iti vijñāpanāṃ kartuṃ bhavatāṃ śaraṇaṃ vraje 
 tan me 'nukampayāsu no rogaśāntir vidhīyatāṃ  Rm
