 bhavanto me 'nuśāstāraḥ sarvajñā brahmacāriṇaḥ 
 tan me sukṛpayā dṛṣṭyā paritrātuṃ samarhata  Rm 
 iti tenārthitaṃ śrutvā sarve te tīrthikā api 
 śreṣṭhinaṃ taṃ samāmaṃtrya punar evaṃ samabruvan  Rm 
 śṛṇu sādho yad asmābhir hitārthaṃ te pracakṣyatāṃ 
 tat satyaṃ naḥ parijñāya pramāṇīkriyatāṃ kila  Rm 
 vayaṃ hi sarvalokānāṃ śāstāro hitasādhakāḥ 
 tasmād atra viṣādatvaṃ mā kṛthā dhairyam āśraya  Rm 
 adyaiva sahasā gatvā vayaṃ dṛṣṭvā tavātmajaṃ 
 niḥpāpaṃ nīrujaṃ svāsthyaṃ kariṣyāmaḥ sujīvitaṃ  Rm 
 apy etad vacanaṃ satyaṃ śrutvā dṛṣṭvā pramāṇaya 
 Rm 
 anyathā na bhavet kvāpi hy asmākaṃ brahmacāriṇāṃ  Rm 
 iti tais tīrthikaiḥ proktaṃ śrutvā sa gṛhasattamaḥ 
 tatheti pratiharṣitvā natvā tān svagṛhaṃ yayau  Rm 
 tatra sa gṛha āsādya dāsidāsajanaiḥ saha 
 tadarhabhojyapūjāṅgasāmagrīṃ samasādhayat  Rm 
 tasminn eva kṣaṇe tatra sarve te tīrthikā mudā 
 sahasā samupāgatya svasvāsane upāviśat  Rm 
 tathā tān samupāsīnān dṛṣṭvā śreṣṭhī sa moditaḥ 
 pūjāṅgaiḥ kramato 'bhyarcya bhojanaiḥ samatoṣayat  Rm 
 tataś ca bhojanānte sa vaḍikaṃ taṃ priyātmajaṃ 
 rogiṇaṃ samupāhṛtya teṣāṃ puro 'bhyadarśayat  Rm 
 te sarve tīrthikā dṛṣṭvā vaḍikaṃ taṃ rujānvitaṃ 
 tadāmayanimittaṃ ca nirīkṣyaivam upādiśat  Rm 
 aho hy asya mahārogaṃ mahāpātakasaṃbhavaṃ 
 tatpātakavimuktyai tu dātavyaṃ dānam ādarāt  Rm 
 tadyathā navaratnāni hemalakṣapalāni ca 
 śraddhayā brahmacāribhyaḥ saṃpradadyāt samarcayan  Rm 
 yady etad dīyate dānaṃ tvayā gṛhapate tathā 
 bhagnakuṣmāṇḍadarinamahiṣīśatadakṣiṇā  Rm 
 purā dattā naṃdarājñā asmākaṃ brahmacāriṇāṃ 
 pādasphoṭāmayas tasya śāṃto 'bhūt tatprabhāvataḥ  Rm 
 tathāsya sarvapāpāni vinakṣyanti na saṃśayaḥ 
 tataḥ sarve 'pi rogāś ca vinakṣyanti kramād drutaṃ  Rm 
 tato rogair vimukto 'yaṃ kuśalī svāsthyam āpnuyāt 
 tataḥ puṣṭo viśuddhāṅgaḥ suśīlaḥ sukṛtī sudhīḥ 
 svakulācāradharmiṣṭho vaṃśāṃś cāpi samuddharet  Rm 
 iti matvā tvayā sādho dātavyaṃ dānam ādarāt 
 anyathā na bhavet svasti tavāsya naṃdanasya ca  Rm 
 iti tair gaditaṃ śrutvā sa śreṣṭhī paribodhitaḥ 
 tasyātmajasya trāṇārthaṃ tathā dātum udācarat  Rm 
 tataḥ sa punar abhyarcya tān sarvāns tīrthikān patīn 
 pradadau navaratnāni svarṇalakṣapalāni ca  Rm 
 tatas te tīrthikāḥ sarve dṛṣṭvā tāni pramoditāḥ 
 sarvāny api pratigṛhya tathāśīrvacanaṃ daduḥ  Rm 
 svasty astu te sadā sādho kalyāṇam astu sarvathā 
 Rm 
 nīrogī suciraṃ jīvyā jayo 'stu te samantataḥ  Rm 
 etad eva samādiśya sarve te tīrthikās tataḥ 
 tāni sarvāṇi vastūni pratigṛhyāśramaṃ yayuḥ  Rm 
 tathāpi tasya rogā na śamitā varddhitāḥ kramāt 
 svadaivaphalabhogyāni bhoktavyāni hi sarvathā  Rm 
 tatas taj janako dṛṣṭvā svātmajaṃ taṃ rujāturaṃ 
 nirāśāmūrchito bhūmau nipataṃ vyalapat tathā  Rm 
 hā daiva kiṃ mayā pāpaṃ dāruṇaṃ prakṛtaṃ purā 
 yato 'yaṃ svātmajaḥ putraḥ puro me maraṇaṃ vrajet  Rm 
 kṛtāny upāyayatnāni dānāni vividhāni ca 
 sarvāṇy etāni matpāpair nisphalāni bhavanti hi  Rm 
 kiṃ mayātrāpi karttavyaṃ ko 'tra me hitam ādiśet 
 sarvathāhaṃ vinaṣṭo 'smi ko 'pi trātā na vidyate  Rm 
 kasyātra śaraṇaṃ yāsye ko no rakṣed dayādṛśā 
 sarve vayaṃ vinaṣṭāsma hā daiva śaraṇaṃ vraje  Rm 
 ity evaṃ vilapaṃtaṃ taṃ janakaṃ vaḍiko 'pi saḥ 
 dṛṣṭvā śanaiḥ samāhūya pura evam abhāṣata  Rm 
 bho tāta kiṃ tvayātrāpi karttavyaṃ hi mayāpi ca 
 sarveṣām api jantūnāṃ daivagatiḥ pramāṇikā  Rm 
 iti matvā viṣādatvaṃ hṛdaye mā kṛthās tyaja 
 saṃbuddhaśaraṇaṃ kṛtvā bhaja nityam anusmaran  Rm 
 buddha eva jagacchāstā trātā lokahitaṃkaraḥ 
 durgatitārako nātho bharttā sadgatināyakaḥ  Rm 
 tad evaṃ sugataṃ smṛtvā saddharmaṃ samupāśrayan 
 saṃghānāṃ bhajanaṃ kṛtvā cinu puṇyaṃ samāhitaḥ  Rm 
 triratne sādhitaṃ puṇyaṃ na kṣiṇuyāt kadā cana 
 yadi daivād vipattiḥ syāt puṇyaṃ tu labhate varaṃ  Rm 
 puṇyena rakṣyate lokaḥ puṇyena sadgatiṃ vrajet 
 tasmāt puṇyaṃ mahāratnaṃ cinu dhairyaṃ samāśrayan  Rm 
 avaśyamaraṇe loke kiṃ viṣādena siddhyate 
 iti matvāpi taṃ buddhaṃ smṛtvā bhaja samāhitaḥ  Rm 
 tathāhaṃ vā tam evātra saṃbuddhaṃ śaraṇaṃ vrajan 
 saṃsmṛtvā bhajanaṃ kurvan vrajeya maraṇaṃ dhruvaṃ  Rm 
 yadi tasya jinendrasya kṛpāsti mayi pāpini 
 Rm 
 tatkṛpādṛkprasādena jīveya nīrujaḥ punaḥ  Rm 
 yadi daivabalenāhaṃ mṛte tatsmṛtipuṇyataḥ 
 sarvathā durgatiṃ tyaktvā sadgatiṃ punar āpnuyāṃ  Rm 
 evaṃ jñātvā tvayā tāta mā kriyatāṃ viṣādatā 
 saṃsāre 'vaśyaṃ marttavyaṃ sarveṣām api janmināṃ  Rm 
 ity uktvā sa rujārtto 'pi vaḍiko dhairyyam āśrayan 
 saṃbuddhaṃ śaraṇaṃ kṛtvā smṛtvā tasthau samāhitaḥ  Rm 
 tathā sa gṛhabhṛc chreṣṭhī śrutvaitad ātmajoditaṃ 
 satyam etat parijñāya buddhaṃ smṛtvā tathāvadat  Rm 
 namo buddhāya dharmāya saṃghāya ca sadā smare 
 adyārabhya sadā nityaṃ bhavatāṃ śaraṇaṃ vraje  Rm 
 yadi vo 'sti kṛpā loke rakṣantu naḥ suduḥkhinaḥ 
 sarvathā kṛpayā dṛṣṭyā dṛṣṭvāśu trātum arhati  Rm 
 yathānye tribhave lokā bhavadbhiḥ pratipālitāḥ 
 tathāsmān kṛpayā dṛṣṭvā trātum arhati sarvathā  Rm 
 rakṣatu bhagavan nātha jīvayeyaṃ mamātmajaṃ 
 kṛpayānugrahaṃ kṛtvā putraratnaṃ prayaccha me  Rm 
 yadi jīved ayaṃ putro bhavaddṛṣṭiprasādataḥ 
 bhavatāṃ śaraṇe sthitvā caratu vratam ādarāt  Rm 
 ity evaṃ smaraṇaṃ kṛtvā saṃbuddhaśaraṇaṃ vrajan 
 sa śreṣṭhī taṃ sutaṃ dṛṣṭvā tasthau mohavinoditaḥ  Rm 
 tasminn eva kṣaṇe lokāṃ trātuṃ sa bhagavān muniḥ 
 saṃpaśyan kṛpayā dṛṣṭyā prādrākṣīt tān saduḥkhinaḥ  Rm 
 tathā tān duḥkhino dṛṣṭvā bhagavān sa jineśvaraḥ 
 sahasā tān paritrātuṃ buddharasmiṃ vyamuñcata  Rm 
 tābhiḥ kanakavarṇābhiḥ saṃbuddharaśmibhis tadā 
 samantāt samatikramya tad gṛham avabhāsitaṃ  Rm 
 tato maitryaṃśavaś cāpi tena bhagavatā punaḥ 
 samutṣṛṣṭās tanau tasya paryaspṛśan prasāditāḥ  Rm 
 tatas tasya tanus taiḥ saṃspṛṣṭamātre samaṃtataḥ 
 prahlāditā sukhaprāptā svāsthyatāṃ samupāyayau  Rm 
 tataḥ sa vaḍikaḥ svāsthyaṃ prāpya nirmalamānasaḥ 
 vismitaḥ pitaraṃ paśyan samāmaṃtryaivam abravīt  Rm 
 aho buddhasya māhātmyam aho dharmānubhāvatā 
 aho saṃghaprabhāvatvaṃ paśya tāta muneḥ prabhāṃ  Rm 
 Rm 
 yasyānusmṛtimātreṇa kṛpā loke prasāryate 
 dhanyo 'yaṃ bhagavān buddho jayatv evaṃ sadā sthitaḥ  Rm 
 yasya dayānubhāvena jīvema nīrujaḥ sukhī 
 pāpaiś cāpi vimukto 'ham iti satyaṃ pramanyate  Rm 
 tasmāt tam eva śāstāraṃ saṃbuddhaṃ śaraṇaṃ vraje 
 yāvadbhavam anusmṛtvā bhajeya samupāśritaḥ  Rm 
 evaṃ buddhaguṇān smṛtvā vaḍikaḥ sa pramoditaḥ 
 kṛtāñjaliḥ smaran bhūyaḥ praṇatvaivam ayācata  Rm 
 namas te bhagavan nātha bhavatāṃ śaraṇaṃ vraje 
 yāvadbhavaṃ triratnānāṃ bhaveyaṃ sevakaḥ sadā  Rm 
 ity evaṃ sugataṃ smṛtvā vaḍikaḥ so 'bhibodhitaḥ 
 bhūyo bhūyaḥ smaran natvā tasthau svāsthyatvam āgataḥ  Rm 
 tadā sa bhagavān buddho dṛṣṭvā taṃ śuddhamānasaṃ 
 saddharmaṃ samupādeṣṭuṃ tad dvāre samupāsarat  Rm 
 taddvārasamupāsīnaṃ taṃ munīndraṃ raviprabhaṃ 
 dṛṣṭvaiva vismito dvāsthaḥ sahasā gṛham āviśat  Rm 
 tatra gṛhapatiṃ dṛṣṭvā vaḍikaṃ taṃ ca sādaraṃ 
 purataḥ samupetyaiva vyajñāpayat sasatvaraḥ  Rm 
 gṛhapate munīndro 'tra gṛhadvāra upasthitaḥ 
 tad atra sahasopetya samāmaṃtrya praveśaya  Rm 
 iti tenoditaṃ śrutvā vaḍikaḥ sa prasāditaḥ 
 utthitaḥ sahasopetya taṃ munīndraṃ mudānamat  Rm 
 natvā taṃ sugataṃ gehe prajñapya svāsanaṃ mudā 
 vijñapya samupāmaṃtrya praveśayaṃs tathārthayan  Rm 
 svāgataṃ bhagavan vāṃche bhavatāṃ śaraṇaṃ mune 
 praviśatu jagannātha vijayasvāsane śubhe  Rm 
 iti tenodite buddho bhagavān sa samāviśan 
 svāsane samupāsīno vaḍikaṃ taṃ tathāvadat  Rm 
 kiṃ te vaḍika duḥkhatvaṃ vādhakaś ca kathaṃ vada 
 iti bhagavatā pṛṣṭo vaḍikaḥ sa tathāvadat  Rm 
 kāyikaṃ jāyate duḥkhaṃ cetasikaṃ ca me mune 
 tad bhavān kṛpayā dṛṣṭyā śamayet tat prabādhanaṃ  Rm 
 iti tad vijñāpitaṃ śrutvā bhagavān sa munīśvaraḥ 
 Rm 
 taccittaduḥkhaśāntyarthaṃ maitrīdharmam upādiśat  Rm 
 vaḍikātra sadā loke maitracittaṃ samācara 
 anena te manodāhaṃ praśāmyeta sadāpi hi  Rm 
 ity ādiśya munīndraḥ sa punar evaṃ vyaciṃtayat 
 vatendrakṣīrikāṃ nāma mahauṣadhāṃ samānayet  Rm 
 iti cittamataṃ śāstuḥ parijñāya surādhipaḥ 
 ādāya kṣīrikāṃ nāma mahauṣadhīm upānayat  Rm 
 tatra so surarājas taṃ bhagavantaṃ praṇamya tāṃ 
 mahauṣadhīm upasthāpya pura evaṃ samabravīt  Rm 
 bhagavan pratigṛhṇātu divyauṣadhīm imāṃ bhavān 
 anayātra yathākāryaṃ sādhayatu sukhāptaye  Rm 
 ity ukte tena śakreṇa dṛṣṭvā tāṃ bhagavān muniḥ 
 gṛhītvā vaḍikāyaivaṃ pradatvā caivam ādiśat  Rm 
 gṛhāṇa vaḍikemāṃ te kāyikaduḥkhaśāminīṃ 
 anayā te śarīre saṃskriyatām upacāraṇaiḥ  Rm 
 ity ādiṣṭe munīndreṇa vaḍikaḥ so 'numoditaḥ 
 tatheti tāṃ samādāya yathādiṣṭam upācarat  Rm 
 tatas tasya tanū rogair vimuktā paripuṣṭitā 
 krameṇa śāmyasaundaryaṃ prāpyābhiparyaśobhata  Rm 
 tataḥ śāstrā yathādiṣṭaṃ vaḍikena tathā hṛdi 
 maitrī prabhāvitā loke svātmaje supriye yathā  Rm 
 tadā tasya mahadduḥkhaṃ cetasikaṃ śaśāma tat 
 mahāmaitryā pariṣikte hṛdaye 'gnir ivāmbubhiḥ  Rm 
 tataḥ sa vaḍikaḥ svasthaḥ pariśuddhendriyaḥ sudhīḥ 
 bhagavantaṃ tam ānamya prārthayad evam ādarāt  Rm 
 vande 'haṃ bhavatāṃ pādau sarvadā śaraṇaṃ vraje 
 tathā ca sarvadā nātha kṛpayā trātum arhati  Rm 
 yady evaṃ bhavatāṃ śāstaḥ kṛpādṛṣṭir na vidyate 
 mṛto 'haṃ narake 'dyāpi gato duḥkhāny avāpnuyāṃ  Rm 
 yad evaṃ svasthito jīve tat te kṛpāmbubhāvataḥ 
 tathā me 'nugrahaṃ kartuṃ nityam arhati sarvadā  Rm 
 ity evaṃ prārthanāṃ kṛtvā bhūyaḥ sa vaḍiko mudā 
 sāñjaliḥ praṇatiṃ kṛtvā paśyaṃs tasthau munīśvaraṃ  Rm 
 tathā tajjanakaḥ śreṣṭhī sadāraḥ saṃpramoditaḥ 
 triratne śaraṇaṃ kṛtvā saṃbuddhaṃ taṃ samarcayat  Rm 
 Rm 
 tataḥ sa gṛhabhṛc chreṣṭhī dṛṣṭvā taṃ sugataṃ mudā 
 kṛtāñjalipuṭo natvā prārthayad evam ādarāt  Rm 
 vande te caraṇau śāstaḥ sarvadā śaraṇaṃ vraje 
 evaṃ no 'nugrahaṃ kartuṃm arhati kṛpayā sadā  Rm 
 tataḥ sa bhagavān buddhas tathāstv iti samādiśat 
 ṛddhyākāśaṃ samutplutya svam āśramam upāyayau  Rm 
 tatra sa bhagavān prāptaḥ sabhāmadhye samāśritaḥ 
 etad vṛṣṭi samākhyāya tasthau dharmaṃ samādiśat  Rm 
 tadā sa vaḍiko bhūyo buddhaguṇān anusmaran 
 sa saṃghaṃ sugataṃ bhojyaiḥ pūjayituṃ samaichata  Rm 
 tadā sa nṛpate rājñaḥ prasenajita ānataḥ 
 etat sarvaṃ pravṛttāṃtaṃ nivedyaivam abhāṣata  Rm 
 rājann ahaṃ mahārogī triratnaśaraṇaṃ vraje 
 tat triratnakṛpādṛṣṭer jīve rogair vimocitaḥ  Rm 
 tan mayā sa munīndro 'pi sarvasaṃghaiḥ sahādhunā 
 samāmaṃtrya gṛhe bhojyaiḥ pūjayituṃ samicchyate  Rm 
 tan me 'nugrahaṇaṃ kṛtvā lokānāṃ puṇyavṛddhaye 
 tadadhivāsanāṃ kṛtvā samanujñāpaya prabho  Rm 
 iti tenārthitaṃ śrutvā sa rājābhyanumoditaḥ 
 vaḍikaṃ taiḥ samālokya praśaṃsyaiva samādiśat  Rm 
 vaḍika tvaṃ mahāsādhus tad buddhaśaraṇaṃ gataḥ 
 tathānuśraddhayā nityaṃ bhaja ratnatrayaṃ sadā  Rm 
 iti rājñābhyanujñātaṃ śrutvā sa vaḍiko mudā 
 nṛpatiṃ taṃ praṇatvaivaṃ svagṛhaṃ samupāyayau  Rm 
 tatra gṛhe samāsādya kṛtvānumataṃ pituḥ 
 śāstu nimaṃtraṇāṃ kartuṃ vihāre samudācaran  Rm 
 tatra sa samupāviṣṭo dṛṣṭvā taṃ śrīghanaṃ mudā 
 kṛtāñjalipuṭo natvā prārthayad evam ādarāt  Rm 
 bhagavaṃs tad vijānīyād yadarthaṃ samupāvraje 
 tathāpy atra bhavadagre prārthaye 'nugrahaṃ kuru  Rm 
 yad ahaṃ roganirmuktaḥ puna janma ivāptavān 
 tad bhavatāṃ kṛpādṛṣṭeḥ prasādād itin manyate  Rm 
 tad ahaṃ bhavatāṃ sarvasaṃghānāṃ bhojanair gṛhe 
 pūjayituṃ samiche tad anugrahītum arhati  Rm 
 Rm 
 iti saṃprārthitaṃ tena śrutvā sa bhagavān muniḥ 
 tathety abhyanumoditvā tūṣṇībhūtvādhyuvāsa tat  Rm 
 tataḥ sa vaḍiko matvā bhagavatādhivāsitaṃ 
 mudā tasya muneḥ pādau natvāśu svagṛhaṃ yayau  Rm 
 tatra sa sahasā gehe vandhumitrajanaiḥ saha 
 saṃghārhabhojyapūjāṅgaṃ sāmagrīṃ samasādhayat  Rm 
 tataḥ sa sarvasāmagrīṃ sādhayitvāsanāni ca 
 prajñapya śuddhite bhūmau maṃdayitvā samantataḥ  Rm 
 tatas taṃ śrīghanaṃ buddhaṃ sasaṃghaṃ svajanaiḥ saha 
 āmaṃtrituṃ vihāre sa sahasā samupācarat  Rm 
 tatra sa samupāviṣṭo dṛṣṭvā taṃ śrīghanaṃ mudā 
 sasaṃghaṃ sāṃjalir natvā prārthayad evam ādarāt  Rm 
 bhagavan sādhyate sādhyaṃ samayo varttate 'dhunā 
 tad bhavāṃ sāṃghikaiḥ sārddhaṃ vijayituṃ samarhati  Rm 
 iti tenārthitaṃ śrutvā tatheti sa munīśvaraḥ 
 pātracīvaram ādhāya sarvasaṃghaiḥ sahācarat  Rm 
 tatra mārgeṣu sarvatra nagare ca samantataḥ 
 prakāśayan prātihāryaṃ tad gṛhaṃ samupāviśat  Rm 
 tatra gṛhe samāsādya pādārghaṃ pratigṛhya saḥ 
 svāsane samupāviśya kramāt tasthau sasāṃghikaḥ  Rm 
 tadā sa vaḍiko dṛṣṭvā taṃ buddhaṃ svāsane sthitaṃ 
 sasaṃghaṃ sarvapūjāṅgaiḥ sarvapuṣpaiḥ samarcayat  Rm 
 tataś ca surasair bhojyaiḥ supraṇītaiḥ suhādhitaiḥ 
 varṇagandharasopetaiḥ sarvais tāṃ samatoṣayat  Rm 
 tataś ca bhojanānte sa pātrādīny apanīya ca 
 mukhādīṃ śodhayitvā ca pūgauṣadhīn praḍhaukayat  Rm 
 tataḥ sa prāñjalir natvā sasaṃghaṃ sugataṃ mudā 
 purastho manasā hy evaṃ praṇidhānaṃ vyadhāt smaran  Rm 
 anena kuśalenāhaṃ loke 'ndhe 'pariṇāyake 
 yathāyaṃ bhagavān buddhas tathā bhūyāsam ātmavit  Rm 
 yathānena munīndreṇa jagal loko 'bhipālitaḥ 
 tathāhaṃ sarvalokānāṃ pālayeyaṃ samantataḥ  Rm 
 atīrṇāṃs tārayiṣyāmi mocayiṣyāmy amocitān 
 anāsvastān samāśvāsya sthāpayiṣyāmi nirvṛtau  Rm 
 Rm 
 ity evaṃ manasā tena praṇidhānaṃ kṛtaṃ mudā 
 matvā sa bhagavān buddho smitaṃ prāvirvyadhān mudā  Rm 
 tadā tasya munīndrasya mukhāt paṃca surasmayaḥ 
 nisṛtya triṣu lokeṣu bhāsayantaḥ samāsaran  Rm 
 yāpi kāś cid adholoke prasṛtā narakeṣu tāḥ 
 uṣṇeṣu śītalībhūtā śītaleṣu tathoṣṇikāḥ  Rm 
 tadā tābhiḥ parispṛṣṭāḥ sarve nairayikā janāḥ 
 mahatsaukhyaṃ samāsādya vismitāś caivam ālapat  Rm 
 aho saukhyaṃ kathaṃ hy evam anyatra kiṃ gatā vayaṃ 
 kasya puṇyānubhāvena kvāsmākaṃ jāyate sukhaṃ  Rm 
 iti cintābhidagdhānāṃ teṣāṃ cittaprabodhane 
 bhagavān nirmitaṃ buddhaṃ saṃpreṣya samadarśayat  Rm 
 tatra taṃ nirmitaṃ buddhaṃ dṛṣṭvā sarve 'pi te mudā 
 vismitāḥ sahasaṃmīlya punar evaṃ vabhāṣire  Rm 
 aho samantabhadro 'yaṃ puruṣo dṛśyate 'dhunā 
 nūnam asyānubhāvena saukhyaṃ no jāyate khalu  Rm 
 iti saṃbhāṣya te sarve tasmin buddhe prasāditāḥ 
 namo buddhāya dharmāya saṃghāya ceti prāvadan  Rm 
 tataḥ sarve 'pi te satvās triratnasmṛtipuṇyataḥ 
 te durgativinirmuktāḥ sadgatiṃ samupāyayuḥ  Rm 
 evaṃ tā raśmayaḥ sarvā avabhāsya samaṃtataḥ 
 sarvasatvān samuddhṛtya muneḥ pratyāyayuḥ punaḥ  Rm 
 tathā yā raśmayaḥ kāścid upariṣṭāt prasāritāḥ 
 tāḥ sarvān devalokānāṃ avabhāsya samantataḥ  Rm 
 yāvad bhavāgraparyaṃtaṃ bhāsayantaḥ prasāritāḥ 
 evaṃ cāpi mahāśabdam udghuṣya samudācaran  Rm 
 anityaṃ khalu saṃsāraṃ duḥkhaṃ śūnyam anātmakaṃ 
 tad bhave sadgatiṃ hitvā saddharmaṃ bhajatādarāt  Rm 
 niṣkrāmatārabhadhvaṃ ca yujyadhvaṃ buddhaśāsane 
 dhunīta mṛtyusainyaṃ ca naḍāgāram iva dvipaḥ  Rm 
 yo 'py asmin dharmavaineye hy apramattaś caret sadā 
 Rm 
 sa hitvā jātisaṃsāraṃ duḥkhasyāntaṃ kariṣyati  Rm 
 ity evaṃ tan mahāśabdaṃ śrutvā sarve 'pi te surāḥ 
 tathety abhyanumodantas triratnaśaraṇaṃ yayuḥ  Rm 
 tathā tā arciṣaḥ sarvā avabhāsya samaṃtataḥ 
 punaḥ pratyāgatās tasya muner antikam āyayuḥ  Rm 
 tatas tā arciṣaḥ sarvāḥ saṃmīlya samupāsthitāḥ 
 kṛtvā pradakṣiṇāṃ traidham uṣṇīṣe 'ntardadhau muneḥ  Rm 
 athānaṃdas tam ālokya vismitaḥ sahasotthitaḥ 
 kṛtāñjalipuṭo natvā paprachaivaṃ munīśvaraṃ  Rm 
 bhagavan bhavato vaktrāt paṃcavarṇāḥ suraśmayaḥ 
 vinisṛtā diśaḥ sarvā bhāṣayanti samantataḥ  Rm 
 nākāraṇaṃ jinā buddhā darśayanti smitaṃ kvacit 
 bhavatsmitaṃ samālokya sarve bhavanti vismitāḥ  Rm 
 taddhetu śrotum ichaṃti sarve 'pīme sabhāśritāḥ 
 tad eṣāṃ saṃśayaṃ chetuṃ taddhetu samupādiśa  Rm 
 iti tenārthitaṃ śrutvā bhagavān sa munīśvaraḥ 
 tāṃ ca sarvāṃ sabhāṃ dṛṣṭvā tathānandam abhāṣata  Rm 
 paśyānaṃda mamānena vaḍikenānumodinā 
 saṃgheṣu śraddhayā bhaktyā satkṛtya bhajanaṃ kṛtaṃ  Rm 
 etatpuṇyavipākena vaḍiko 'yaṃ sudhīḥ kṛtī 
 kramād bodhicarīḥ pūrya daśabhūmīśvaro bhavan  Rm 
 sarvamāragaṇāṃ jitvā saṃbodhiṃ samavāptavān 
 ślakṣṇavāṇyabhidho buddhas tathāgato bhaviṣyati  Rm 
 yad anena triratneṣu śaraṇaṃ saṃprasādinā 
 praṇidhānaṃ kṛtaṃ tena saṃbuddho 'yaṃ bhaved dhruvaṃ  Rm 
 evaṃ matvā tathānaṃda triratnaśaraṇaṃ gataḥ 
 satkṛtya samupāśritya bhaja nityaṃ samāhitaḥ  Rm 
 ye satvāḥ śraddhayā smṛtvā triratnaśaraṇaṃ gatāḥ 
 durgatiṃ te na gachanti bhavanti bodhibhāginaḥ  Rm 
 evaṃ matvā triratnānāṃ satkṛtya śraddhayā mudā 
 saṃsmṛtya śaraṇaṃ gatvā bhaktavyaṃ bodhivāṃchibhiḥ  Rm 
 ity ādiṣṭaṃ munīndreṇa śrutvānaṃdaḥ sa moditaḥ 
 sāṃghikaṃ saha lokaiś ca tatheti prābhyanaṃdata  Rm 
 tataḥ sa bhagavāṃs tasmai vaḍikāya subhāgine 
 datvāśīrvacanaṃ bhūyaḥ samāmaṃtrya tam abravīt  Rm 
 Rm 
 vaḍika tvaṃ mahābhāga triratnaṃ śaraṇaṃ gataḥ 
 bodhicaryyāṃ caran nityaṃ saṃbodhiṃ samavāpnuyāḥ  Rm 
 iti satyaṃ parijñāya sarvasatvahitārthabhṛt 
 tathā ratnatrayaṃ smṛtvā bhaja nityaṃ samāhitaḥ  Rm 
 ity ādiśya munīndraḥ sa saṃghaiḥ sārddhaṃ samutthitaḥ 
 vaḍikaṃ taṃ samāmaṃtrya svavihāraṃ yayau tathā  Rm 
 tathā sa vaḍiko nityaṃ triratnaśaraṇaṃ gataḥ 
 sadā lokahitaṃ kṛtvā bodhicaryāṃ samācarat  Rm 
 etan me guruṇādiṣṭaṃ śrutaṃ mayā narādhipa 
 tathā te kathyate rājaṃ śrutvā caivaṃ prakāśaya  Rm 
 tathā tvayāpi rājendra satvānāṃ hitasādhane 
 triratnaśaraṇaiḥ kṛtvā karttavyā bodhicārikāḥ  Rm 
 tathā te sarvadā nityaṃ sarvatra maṃgalaṃ bhavet 
 kramād bodhicarīṃ pūrya saṃbodhim api cāpnuyāḥ  Rm 
 iti matvā mahārāja prajāś cāpi prabodhayan 
 saddharme saṃpratisthāpya sarvathā trātum arhasi  Rm 
 iti tenopaguptena samādiṣṭaṃ niśamya saḥ 
 rājā tatheti vijñapya prābhyanandat sapārṣadaḥ  Rm 
 śrutvāvadānaṃ vaḍikasya sādhor idaṃ narā ye 'bhyanumodayanti 
 sarve 'pi te lokahitānuraktā bhavanti bodhiguṇalābhikā hi  Rm 
  iti ratnāvadānatatve vaḍikāvadānaṃ samāptam 
 Rm 
 XIV Gāndharvikāvadāna
 athāśoko mahīpālaḥ śrotum anyat subhāṣitaṃ 
 upaguptaṃ yatiṃ natvā prārthayad evam ādarāt  Rm 
 bhadanta śrotum icchāmi punar anyat subhāṣitaṃ 
 tad yathā guruṇākhyātaṃ tathādeṣṭuṃ ca me 'rhati  Rm 
 iti tena narendreṇa prārthitaṃ sa jinātmajaḥ 
 śrutvā taṃ nṛpatiṃ dṛṣṭvā punar evaṃ samādiśat  Rm 
 śṛṇu rājan mayākhyātaṃ yathā me guruṇoditaṃ 
 tathā śrūtvānumoditvā śubhe caritum arhasi  Rm 
 purā sa bhagavān buddhaḥ śrāvastyāṃ bahir āśrame 
 jetāraṇye mahodyāne vihāre maṇimaṇḍite  Rm 
 bhikṣubhiḥ śrāvakaiḥ sārddhaṃ cailakair vratibhis tathā 
 bhikṣuṇībhis tathānyaiś cā mahāsātvair upāsakaiḥ  Rm 
 vihṛtya sarvasatvānāṃ samitisthitaḥ 
 saṃbodhisādhānaṃ dharmam upādeṣṭuṃ samārabhat  Rm 
 tadā tasya munīndrasya vaktrapadmād vinisṛtaṃ 
 tat saddharmāmṛtaṃ pātuṃ sarve satvā upagatāḥ  Rm 
 brahmaśakrādi devendrāḥ sarve lokādhipā api 
 daityendrāḥ sagaṇā yakṣāḥ siddhagaṃdharvarākṣasāḥ  Rm 
 vidyādharagaṇāś capi nāgeṃdrāś ca mahoragāḥ 
 garuḍāḥ kinnarendrāś ca tathānye 'pi samāgatāḥ  Rm 
 brāhmaṇā ṛṣayaś cāpi tāpasā brahmacāriṇaḥ 
 yatayo yogino vijñās tathānye tīrthikā api  Rm 
 rajānaḥ kṣatriyāś cāpi vīrā rājakumārakāḥ 
 amātyā maṃtriṇaś cāpi vaiśyāś cāpi prajādhipāḥ  Rm 
 śreṣṭhino vaṇijaś cāpi sārthavāhā mahājanāḥ 
 paurā jānapadā grāmyās tathā kārpaṭikā api  Rm 
 evaṃ anye 'pi satvāś ca sarve lokāḥ samāgatāḥ 
 tat saddharmāmṛtaṃ pātuṃ tad vihāre upāviśat  Rm 
 tatra taṃ śrīghanaṃ dṛṣṭvā samabhyarcya praṇamya ca 
 satkṛtya samupāśritya parivṛtya sāmāntataḥ  Rm 
 taṃ muṇīndraṃ samālokya śrotuṃ tad dharmadeśanāṃ 
 sāñjalayaḥ prasannāsyā upatasthuḥ samāhitāḥ  Rm 
 tathā tān samupāsīnān dṛṣṭvā sa bhagavāñ jinaḥ 
 āryasatyaṃ samārabhya saddharmaṃ samupādiśat  Rm 
 tat saddharmāmṛtaṃ pītvā sarve satvāḥ pramoditāḥ 
 Rm 
 triratnabhajanaṃ kṛtvā vabhūvur bodhicāriṇaḥ  Rm 
 tadāpi paṃcamātrāṇi gāṃdharvikaśatāni ca 
 śrāvastyāṃ puri jātāni samadāni pracerire  Rm 
 tadā tāṃ samadān dṛṣṭvā gaṃdharvādhipateḥ sutaḥ 
 supriyo nāma tan mādam īrṣyayā hantum udyayau  Rm 
 tataḥ sa supriyaḥ sarvagāndharvikasukauśalaḥ 
 divyavīṇāṃ samādāya tatraiva samupācarat  Rm 
 saptasvarān ekataṃtryām ekaviṃśatimūrchanāḥ 
 samudghoṣayamānaḥ ca svamatiṃ darśayan yayau  Rm 
 ṣaṇmahānagareṣv evaṃ paṭṭaneṣu samantataḥ 
 samudghoṣayamānaś ca śrāvastīṃ sa upāviśat  Rm 
 tatra taṃ samupāviṣṭaṃ dṛṣṭvā sarve 'pi paurikāḥ 
 śrutvā tad adbhutaṃ nādaṃ vismitāḥ samupācaran  Rm 
 tāni ca paṃcamātrāṇi gāṃdharvikaśatāny api 
 śrutvā dṛṣṭvā ca sarvāṇi vismayaṃ samupāyayuḥ  Rm 
 tada tāni ca sarvāṇi dṛṣṭvā paṃcaśatāny api 
 svasvamadābhimānatvāṃ pravihāya viṣedire  Rm 
 tataḥ sarve 'pi te tena sahavāde bhayānvitāḥ 
 nṛpater antikaṃ gatvā tat pravṛttiṃ nyavedayan  Rm 
 jaya prabho vijānīyād yad vayaṃ samupāgatāḥ 
 tad atra no bhayatrastāṃ trātum arhati sarvathā  Rm 
 atrāsau supriyo nāma gandharvādhipateḥ sutaḥ 
 nūnaṃ no madaghātāya vijetuṃ samupāgataḥ  Rm 
 tat tasyāpy abhimānatvāṃ nihaṃtuṃ satpratikriyāṃ 
 kriyatāṃ sahasāsmākam iti vijñāpanāṃ śṛṇu  Rm 
 iti vijñāpitaṃ sarvais taiḥ śrutvā sa narādhipaḥ 
 sarvāns tān samupāmaṃtrya pura evaṃ samādiśat  Rm 
 alpotsukā bhavanto 'tra bhavate mā viṣīdata 
 bhaviṣyāmo 'tra kālajñāś caratu sa yathechayā  Rm 
 iti rājñā samādiṣṭaṃ śrutvā te 'bhyanumoditāḥ 
 tad vivādabhayātaṃkaṃ tyaktvā sarve prasedire  Rm 
 tadā sa supriyas tatra dṛṣṭvā tān abhimānikān 
 teṣāṃ mānavighātārthaṃ manasaivaṃ vyacintayat  Rm 
 ayaṃ rājapi gāṃdharvavidyābhimāniko bhavet 
 tad anena sahātrāhaṃ vādaṃ kuryāṃ sabhāśraye  Rm 
 ity evaṃ niścayaṃ kṛtvā supriyaḥ so 'bhimānikaḥ 
 nṛpatiṃ tam upālabdhuṃ tat sabhāṃ samupācarat  Rm 
 tatra sa nṛpatir dṛṣṭvā supriyaṃ tam upāgataṃ 
 prajñapyāsanam āmaṃtrya praṇatvaivam abhāṣata  Rm 
 svāgataṃ te bhavann atra tiṣṭhāsane prasīda me 
 kim arthe 'tra samāyāsi tad ādeṣṭuṃ hi me 'rhasi  Rm 
 Rm 
 iti tenoditaṃ śrutvā supriyaḥ sa sabhāsthitaḥ 
 nṛpatiṃ taṃ samālokya pura evam abhāṣata  Rm 
 śṛṇu rājan mayākhyātaṃ śrutaṃ yat te yaśo mahat 
 tad guṇān bhavato draṣṭum ihāhaṃ samupācare  Rm 
 tan me darśaya rājendra gāndharvaguṇām ātmanaḥ 
 kas te sāstā gurur vāsti taṃ cāpi me pradarśaya  Rm 
 iti tenoditaṃ śrutvā sa rājā pratibhāṇavān 
 supriyaṃ taṃ samālokya tathety evam abhāṣata  Rm 
 sādhu paśya mahābhāga darśayisyāmi taṃ guruṃ 
 yo me śāstā mahābhijñaḥ sarvavidyāguṇādhipaḥ  Rm 
 sa me śāstādhunehaiva sarvasatvahitārthataḥ 
 jetāraṇye mahodyāne nivaśati vṛṣaṃ diśan  Rm 
 sādhu paśya mahābhāga taṃ guruṃ me hitārthadaṃ 
 tad ehi saha yāsyāma śāstāraṃ darśayāmi taṃ  Rm 
 iti tena narendreṇa samākhyātaṃ sa supriyaḥ 
 śrutvā tatheti pramodya gantum abhāṣata  Rm 
 sādhu rājan samichāmi śāstāraṃ tat pradarśaya 
 tena saha vivādāni kuryāṃ tatra nayāśu māṃ  Rm 
 iti tenoditaṃ śrutvā nṛpatiḥ sa tatheti hi 
 supriyaṃ taṃ samādāya vihāre gantum aichata  Rm 
 tataḥ sa nṛpatis tena supriyeṇābhimāninā 
 taiś ca paṃcaśatair anyair gāndharvikaiḥ sahācarat  Rm 
 tasminn avasare buddho bhagavān sa munīśvaraḥ 
 loke satvān samuddhartuṃ kṛpayā samapaśyata  Rm 
 tadā tena nareśena sārddham evam upāgataṃ 
 supriyaṃ taṃ sa ālokya manasaiva vyacintayat  Rm 
 aho vata sudhīr yā sā gandharvādhipanandanaḥ 
 pañcaśikho 'bhidho vīṇām ādāyehopasaṃkramet  Rm 
 iti tena munīndreṇa manasā paricintitaṃ 
 matvā pañcaśikhaḥ so 'pi tathāgantuṃ samaichata  Rm 
 tataḥ sa saptagaṃdharvasahasreṇa sahānvitaḥ 
 vaiḍūryadaṇḍavīṇāṃ saṃprādāya sahasācaran  Rm 
 tathā sa saṃkramaṃs tatra vihāre samupāviśan 
 dṛṣṭvā taṃ śrīghanaṃ natvā tāṃ vīṇāṃ samupānayat  Rm 
 tataḥ sa sugataṃ bhaktyā samabhyarcya prasannadhīḥ 
 tat saddharmāmṛtaṃ pātuṃ tat sabhāyām upāśrayat  Rm 
 tadā sa supriyo 'py enaṃ dṛṣṭvā mānābhigarvitaḥ 
 tāṃ vīṇāṃ kvanayann agre 'nuśrāvituṃ samārabhat  Rm 
 tatprakvāṇāt svarā sapta ekai viṃśati mūrchanāḥ 
 samutthitāḥ sarvalokacetānsi paryamohayan  Rm 
 tadā sarve 'pi te lokāḥ śrutvā tat prakvaṇān mudā 
 nṛpatipramukhāś cāpi paraṃ vismayam āyajuḥ  Rm 
 Rm 
 tataḥ sa bhagavāṃś cāpi tasya mānābhighātane 
 vaiḍūryadaṇḍavīṇāṃ tām anuśrāvitum ārabhat  Rm 
 ekaikasyāṃ hi tat taṃtryā naikasvaraviśeṣitāḥ 
 mūrchanāś ca tathā nānāvidhā niścāritās tathā  Rm 
 tataḥ śabdāt samuccerur gāthā evaṃ pracodināḥ 
 tadyatheha bhave sarvaṃ duḥkhaṃ śūnyaṃ hy anātmakaṃ  Rm 
 idaṃ kāyaṃ ca vīṇāvad indriyāṇi svarānī ca 
 mūrchanā iva cittāni jñātvā bodhau samācara  Rm 
 etadgāthām anuśrutvā sarve lokā nṛpādayaḥ 
 satyam etad iti jñātvā bodhicittaṃ pralehire  Rm 
 tadā sa supriyo 'py evaṃ śrutvā matvānumoditaḥ 
 paritatyāja gāṃdharvavidyāmadābhimānatāṃ  Rm 
 tato niryātya vīṇāṃ sa gandhakuṭyāṃ virāgitaḥ 
 bhagavacchāsane tatra pravrajituṃ samaichata  Rm 
 tadā taṃ śrīghanaṃ natvā supriyaḥ so 'numoditaḥ 
 kṛtāñjaliḥ puraḥ sthitvā pravrajyāṃ samayācata  Rm 
 vaṃde te caraṇau śāsta bhavatāṃ śaraṇaṃ vraje 
 tan me 'trānugrahaṃ kṛtvā pravrajyāṃ dātum arhati  Rm 
 iti tenārthitaṃ śrutvā bhagavān sa munīśvaraḥ 
 dṛṣṭvā tad āśayaṃ śuddhaṃ gaṃdharvaṃ taṃ tathāvadat  Rm 
 gaṃdharva saugate dharme pravrajituṃ yadīchasi 
 pitror ājñāṃ samāsādya prehi dāsyāmi te vrataṃ  Rm 
 ity ādiṣṭaṃ munīndreṇa śrutvā sa supriyo mudā 
 tatheti taṃ muniṃ natvā sahasarddhyā gṛhaṃ yayau  Rm 
 tatra sa sahasā prāpto natvā tau pitarau mudā 
 sāñjaliḥ purataḥ sthitvā prārthayad evam ādarāt  Rm 
 śṛṇu me vāñchitaṃ tāta yadi te kṛpayā mayi 
 tan mamānugrahaṃ kṛtvā saddharme māṃ niyojaya  Rm 
 ahaṃ hi saugataṃ dharmaṃ dṛṣṭvā vāñchāmi tad vrataṃ 
 tat pravrajyāṃ samāsādya prāptum ichāmi nirvṛtiṃ  Rm 
 anityaṃ khalu saṃsāraṃ tad atrāpi na me ratiḥ 
 avaśyaṃ hi bhaven mṛtyuḥ sarveṣāṃ prāṇinām api  Rm 
 evaṃ dṛṣṭvātra saṃsāre bhogyaṃ nechāmi niḥspṛhaḥ 
 tat pravrajyāvrataṃ dhṛtvā prāptum iche sunirvṛtiṃ  Rm 
 api cāsau munīndro hi sadātraiva na tiṣṭhati 
 buddhakāryaṃ samāpyaiva nirvṛtiṃ sarvathā vrajet  Rm 
 kiṃ cātra sarvadā naivam utpatsyate munīśvaraḥ 
 kadā cid evam utpanno loke bodhiṃ samādiśet  Rm 
 tathā ca durlabhaṃ janma sadgatau ca kṣaṇaṃ tathā 
 tatkṣaṇe 'labhyamāne 'tra kathaṃ dharmānulapsyate  Rm 
 dharmaṃ vinātra saṃsāre kiṃ sāraṃ sukhino 'pi hi 
 kṣaṇadhvansi śarīraṃ hi jīvitaṃ ca tṛṇāmbuvat  Rm 
 Rm 
 dharmeṇa sadgatiṃ yāyāt saṃbodhim api prāpnuyāt 
 tat pravrajyācariṃ dhṛtvā prāptum iche 'tra nirvṛtiṃ  Rm 
 tad ātra yadi vāṃ tāta kṛpāsti svātmaje mayi 
 sarvathānugrahaṃ kṛtvā tad anujñāṃ pradehi me  Rm 
 iti tenārthitaṃ śrutvā sa gandharvādhipaḥ sudhīḥ 
 suciraṃ taṃ sutaṃ dṛṣṭvā snehād evam abhaṣata  Rm 
 satyam evaṃ sutākhyātaṃ tathāpi me vacaḥ śṛṇu 
 pravrajyā duṣkarīcaryyā tat kathaṃ tvaṃ samācareḥ  Rm 
 tvaṃ hi yuvā pramatto 'si madanākrāṃtamānasaḥ 
 kāmabhogyasukhāraktas tat kathaṃ tad vrataṃ careḥ  Rm 
 pravrajito viraktātmā saṃsārabhogyanispṛhaḥ 
 sarvān parigrahāns tyaktvā sadaikāntī vane vase  Rm 
 sukule duḥkule cāpi yācitvā viraśāsanaṃ 
 bhuṃjīthās tat kathaṃ bhuktvā samādhiṃ saṃpradhāsyasi  Rm 
 ity evaṃ duṣkaraṃ jñatvā pravrajyāvratasādhane 
 sahasā mā kṛthāś cittaṃ nivāraya samāhitaḥ  Rm 
 yady ativāṃchase putra pravrajyāgrahaṇe tathā 
 vṛddhatve samupāśritya triratnaṃ tad vrataṃ cara  Rm 
 tat tvaṃ yāvad yuvā gehe saukhyaṃ bhuktvā yathepsitaṃ 
 vṛddhatve tad vrataṃ dhṛtvā triratnāni sadā bhaja  Rm 
 tathā cet te bhavej janma sāphalyaṃ bhavacāraṇe 
 sukhaṃ bhuktvā vrataṃ dhṛtvā nirvṛtiṃ vā samāpnuyāḥ  Rm 
 iti me vacanaṃ śrutvā matvaivaṃ tat prabodhitaḥ 
 tāvad gṛhe sukhaṃ bhuktvā smṛtvā ratnatrayaṃ vasa  Rm 
 iti pitroditaṃ śrutvā supriyaḥ so 'bhiśaṃkitaḥ 
 punas taṃ pitaraṃ dṛṣṭvā bodhayann evam abravīt  Rm 
 satyam evaṃ bhave tāta tathāpi vakṣyate mayā 
 tac chrutvāpi tvayā parijñāya vibudhyatāṃ  Rm 
 satkule durlabhaṃ janma tatrāpi durlabhaṃ kṣaṇaṃ 
 durlabhaṃ sugatotpādaṃ durlabhaṃ tadvrataṃ bhave  Rm 
 iti matvātra saṃsāre kleśamānamadākule 
 avaśyaṃ maraṇaṃ dṛṣṭvā prāptum iche 'tra nirvṛtiṃ  Rm 
 tad atra kṛpayā mahyam anujñāṃ dātum arhasi 
 yūyaṃ cāpi hi tad dharmabhāṇaiḥ sadgatim āpsyatha  Rm 
 iti hetoḥ pita tatra vilambaṃma kṛthā ciraṃ 
 sahasānugrahaṃ kṛtvā tad anujñāṃ pradehi me  Rm 
 iti tenārthitaṃ śrutvā sa gaṃdharvādhipaś cirāt 
 snehaduḥkhāgnisaṃtapto galadaśrumukho 'vadat  Rm 
 ayi supriya putra tvaṃ snehān mayā nivāryasa 
 yady ativāṃchase prāptuṃ nirvṛtiṃ tan samācara  Rm 
 saṃbuddhaśaraṇaṃ kṛtvā pravrajya saṃvaraṃ dadhat 
 Rm 
 triratnabhajanaṃ kṛtvā cara nityaṃ samāhitaḥ  Rm 
 iti pitroditaṃ śrutvā supriyaḥ so 'bhimoditaḥ 
 pitroḥ pādān praṇatvaiva sahasā niryayau gṛhāt  Rm 
 tataḥ sa sahasā gatvā vihāraṃ samupācarat 
 tatra prāpto munīndraṃ taṃ dṛṣṭvaiva samupāviśat  Rm 
 tatra taṃ śrīghanaṃ nātvā prāñjaliḥ pura āśrayan 
 suprasannamukhāṃbhojaḥ prārthayad evam ādarāt  Rm 
 sarvajña bhagavāñ chāstar ādiṣṭaṃ bhavatāyathā 
 tathānujñāṃ pituḥ prāpya prāgatāham ihādhunā  Rm 
 tad atra bhavatāṃ śāstaḥ śaraṇaṃ samupāgataḥ 
 brahmacaryaṃ cariṣyāmi tat pravrajyāṃ pradehi me  Rm 
 iti tenārthitaṃ śrutvā bhagavān sa jagadguruḥ 
 dṛṣṭvā tasyāśayaṃ śuddhaṃ punar eva samādiśat  Rm 
 ehi supriya bhikṣo 'tra cara brahmacariṃ śivāṃ 
 triratnaṃ śaraṇaṃ kṛtvā samādhiṃ samupāśrayat  Rm 
 tato dṛṣṭvā ca saṃsāraṃ kleśasaṃghasamākulaṃ 
 paṃcagaṃḍamayaṃ dehaṃ jīvitaṃ ca trināmvuvat  Rm 
 samādhisaṃvaraṃ dhṛtvā saṃbodhisādhanodyataḥ 
 sarvakleśaripuñ jitvā sākṣād arhatpadaṃ yayau  Rm 
 tataḥ supriyo bhikṣuḥ prāptābhijñaḥ kṛtī sudhīḥ 
 bhindan sarvam avidyāṅgaṃ nirvikalpo 'bhavad yatiḥ  Rm 
 samaloṣṭasuvarṇaś ca pariśuddhatrimaṃḍalaḥ 
 vāsīcaṃdanakalpo 'bhūd ākāśasamamānasaḥ  Rm 
 saṃsārabhogyasatkāramānyalābhaparāṅmukhaḥ 
 niḥkleśaḥ pariṣuddhātmā brahmacārī niraṃjanaḥ  Rm 
 sadevāsuralokānāṃ sarvabhuvanavāsināṃ 
 vaṃdyaḥ pūjyo 'bhinaṃdyaś ca mānanīyo bhavan babhau  Rm 
 tadaivaṃbhūtam arhantaṃ supriyaṃ tam śubhendriyaṃ 
 prālokya vismitāḥ sarve tatsabhāsthāḥ prasedire  Rm 
 tadā sarve 'pi te lokā devā daityāś ca kinnarāḥ 
 yakṣāḥ siddhāś ca gaṃdharvā nāgāś ca rākṣasā api  Rm 
 garuḍāś ca tathānye 'pi vidyādharāś ca sāpsarāḥ 
 sarve lokādhipāś cāpi triratnaśaraṇaṃ gatāḥ  Rm 
 saṃbuddhaśāsane tatra sāṃghikānāṃ samantataḥ 
 rakṣāvaraṇasaṃguptiṃ kṛtvābhajan samudyatāḥ  Rm 
 tad dṛṣṭvā tāni pañcāpi gāṃdharvikaśatāni ca 
 anumodya prasannāni saṃmīlyaivaṃ vabhāṣire  Rm 
 ete sarve vayaṃ nīce karmaṇi parivarttikāḥ 
 sukhānabhijñaduḥkhārttāḥ kleśinaḥ kṛchravṛttayaḥ  Rm 
 yad asmābhiḥ purā puṇyaṃ kiṃ cid vāpi na sādhitaṃ 
 tenāsyātra vayaṃ sarve duḥkhino nīcavṛttayaḥ  Rm 
 tad asmābhir ayam śāstā munīśvaraḥ sasāṃghikaḥ 
 satkṛtya bhojanair vāpi pūjanīyo yathāvidhiḥ  Rm 
 nūnam etadvipākena bhavemahi subhāginaḥ 
 Rm 
 tataḥ puṇyānusāreṇa bodhimārge caremahi  Rm 
 tataḥ krameṇa saṃprāpya bodhicaryyāṃ śubhāṃ carīṃ 
 carantas tadvipākaiś ca nirvṛtiṃ saṃlabhemahi  Rm 
 iti matvā vayaṃ sarve vijñapya nṛpatiṃ tathā 
 sasaṃghaṃ sugataṃ bhojyair arhāmahe samarcituṃ  Rm 
 tatheti saṃmataṃ kṛtvā sarve te 'bhyanumoditāḥ 
 nṛpater vijñāpanāṃ kartuṃ sahasā samupācaran  Rm 
 tatra te samupāsṛtya dṛṣṭvā taṃ nṛpatiṃ mudā 
 kṛtāñjalipuṭo natvā prārthayann evam ādarāt  Rm 
 jaya deva mahārāja lokān dharmeṇa pālaya 
 kiñcid vijñāpanāṃ karttuṃ vayam upāgatāḥ  Rm 
 vijānīyād bhavān hy etat tathāpi prārthayāmahe 
 śrutvā no 'nugrahaṃ kṛtvā kṛpayā tat prasīdatu  Rm 
 yad vayaṃ deva sarve 'tra nīcakarmānucāriṇaḥ 
 tat sasaṃghaṃ muniṃ bhojyaiḥ samichāmaḥ samarcituṃ  Rm 
 tad anujñāṃ pradatvā naḥ kṛpayoddhartum arhasi 
 etad vijñāpanāṃ kurmas tat prasīda nṛpādhipa  Rm 
 iti taiḥ prārthitaṃ śrutvā nṛpatiḥ so 'numoditaḥ 
 tān sarvān samupāmaṃtrya punar evaṃ samādiśat  Rm 
 sādhu bhavatu sarveṣāṃ yuṣmākaṃ satsamīhitaṃ 
 tat tathā kriyatāṃ buddhe satkāraṃ śraddhayādarāt  Rm 
 saṃbuddhe yat kṛtaṃ karma tat phalaṃ kṣiṇuyān na hi 
 kramād bodhicariṃ pūrya nirvṛtiṃ samavāpnuyāt  Rm 
 tad atra sarvathā yūyaṃ sasaṃghaṃ śrīghanaṃ muniṃ 
 yathārhabhojanaṃ bhaktyā pūjayadhvaṃ samādarāt  Rm 
 ity ādiṣṭam ḥ  ndreṇa śrutvā sarve 'pi te mudā 
 tatheti pratinaṃditvā nṛpaṃ natvā tato 'caran  Rm 
 tatas te saṃmataṃ kṛtvā vihāre sahasā gatāḥ 
 dṛṣṭvā taṃ śrīghanaṃ natvā prārthayann evam ādarāt  Rm 
 bhagavaṃs tad vijānīyād yad arthaṃ samupāgatāḥ 
 tathāpi prārthayeyaivam anugrahītum arhati  Rm 
 yad vayaṃ bhavatāṃ sarvasāṃghikānāṃ yathāvidhiṃ 
 pūjayituṃ samichāmo satkartuṃ bhojanair api  Rm 
 tad bhavāṃ kṛpayā dṛṣṭvā kṛtvāsmākaṃ anugrahaṃ 
 pure śvaḥ sāṃghikaiḥ sārddhaṃ vijayituṃ samarhasi  Rm 
 iti taiḥ prārthite sarvair bhagavān sa munīśvaraḥ 
 teṣāṃ dharmapravṛddhyarthaṃ tūṣṇībhūtvādhyuvāsa tat  Rm 
 tatas sarve 'pi te matvā bhagavatādhivāsitaṃ 
 bhūyas taṃ śrīghanaṃ natvā svaṃ puraṃ sahasā yayuḥ  Rm 
 tatra sarve 'pi te bhūmiṃ śodhayitvā samantataḥ 
 prajñapya svāsanāny evaṃ sāmagriṃ samasādhayan  Rm 
 Rm 
 tataḥ pūjopahārāṇi bhojyāṅgāni rasāni ca 
 peyāni supraṇītāni sādhayitvā pramoditāḥ  Rm 
 tatra taṃ sugataṃ sarvaṃ saṃghaṃ cāmaṃtrituṃ yayuḥ 
 vihāre samupasṛtya śrīghanaṃ saṃpraṇemire  Rm 
 kṛtāñjalipuṭo natvā sarve te samupasthitāḥ 
 saṃbuddhapramukhaṃ saṃghaṃ prārthayann evam ādarāt  Rm 
 sarvajña bhagavaṃ chāstaḥ samayo varttate 'dhunā 
 tad bhavān saṃghikaiḥ sārddhaṃ vijayituṃ samarhati  Rm 
 iti taiḥ prārthite dṛṣṭvā bhagavān sa sasāṃghikaḥ 
 pātracīvaram ādaya pratasthe saṃprabhāsayan  Rm 
 tatra mārgeṣu sarvatra prātihāryaṃ pradarśayan 
 sarveṣāṃ śubhatāṃ kṛtvā tat pure samupāviśat  Rm 
 pradakṣiṇakrameṇaivaṃ caraṃs tatra samaṃtataḥ 
 bhāsayaṃ bhadratāṃ kurvan tatpradeśe samācaran  Rm 
 tatra pādyārgham ādāya krameṇa saha sāṃghikaṃ 
 svāsane samupāviśya tasthau bhānur ivojvalan  Rm 
 tadā taṃ śrīghanaṃ sarvasaṃghaṃ ca svāsane sthitaṃ 
 dṛṣṭvā sarve 'pi te harṣāt pūjayituṃ samārabhan  Rm 
 tathā krameṇa saṃpūjya taṃ buddhapramukhaṃ gaṇaṃ 
 yathārhabhojanaiḥ sarvaṃ saṃtṛptaṃ samatoṣayan  Rm 
 tatas te bhojanāṃte tatpātrāṇi vyapanīya ca 
 karādīñ chodhayitvā tad bhūmiṃ ca paryaśodhayan  Rm 
 tataḥ pūgādikaṃ datvā punaḥ sarve 'pi te mudā 
 kṛtāñjalipuṭā natvā samupatasthire punaḥ  Rm 
 te ca gāṃdharvikāḥ sarve triratnaśaraṇaṃ gatāḥ 
 bodhipraṇidhim ādhāya prabhejire samāhitāḥ  Rm 
 veṇuvīṇāmṛdaṃgādi tūryasaṃgītivādanaiḥ 
 upasthitya sasaṃghaṃ taṃ śrīghanaṃ samatoṣayat  Rm 
 tada sa bhagavāṃ dṛṣṭvā teṣāṃ bhaktiprasādinīṃ 
 sarveṣāṃ śuddhacittāni vyamuñcat smitam uddhavāt  Rm 
 tat saṃsmitasahotpannāḥ paṃcavarṇāḥ śubhāṃśavaḥ 
 sarvatra bhuvane gatvā pracerur amṛtāṃśuvat  Rm 
 teṣāṃ ke cid adhogatvā narakeṣu samantataḥ 
 avabhāsya parispṛṣṭvā sarvatrāpi sukhaṃ daduḥ  Rm 
 tadā te nārakīyās tat prabhāspṛṣṭāḥ sukhānvitāḥ 
 kim etad iti saṃdigdhāḥ saṃmīlyaivaṃ vabhāṣire  Rm 
 aho nu jāyate saukhyam asmākaṃ sāṃprataṃ kathaṃ 
 vatānyatra gatāḥ smo 'dya kasya puṇyānubhāvataḥ  Rm 
 iti saṃdigdhacittānāṃ teṣāṃ manaḥ prabodhane 
 bhagavān nirmitaṃ buddhaṃ saṃpreṣayan samaṃtataḥ  Rm 
 tatrā taṃ saugataṃ dṛṣṭvā sarve te narakasthitāḥ 
 vismitāḥ samupāsṛtya vavandire prasāditāḥ  Rm 
 Rm 
 namo buddhāya dharmāya saṃghāya ca namas sadā 
 iti proktvā praṇatvā taccharaṇaṃ samupāyayuḥ  Rm 
 etatpuṇyānubhāvena sarve te narakotthitāḥ 
 sahasā svargatiṃ yātāḥ saddharme samudācaran  Rm 
 evaṃ tān sarvasatvāṃś ca samuddhṛtya samantataḥ 
 sarve te 'py aṃśavo bhūyas saṃbuddhāntikam upācaran  Rm 
 ke cid ūrddhvagatā yāvad akaniṣṭhaṃ samantataḥ 
 avabhāsya samudghuṣya tatraivaṃ samacodayan  Rm 
 anityaṃ khalu saṃsāraṃ śūnyaṃ hy anātmakaṃ 
 iti satyaṃ parijñāya triratnaṃ bhajatādarāt  Rm 
 niṣkrāmatārabhadhvaṃ ca yūjyadhvaṃ buddhaśāsane 
 dhunīta mārasainyāś ca naḍāgāraṃ yathā karī  Rm 
 yo 'py asmin saugate dharme hy apramattaś caret sadā 
 sa tyaktvā janma saṃsāre duḥkhasyāntaṃ kariṣyati  Rm 
 iti saṃcodayantas tāṃ sārvān devāṃś ca sarvataḥ 
 te sarve 'py aṃśavo bhāyaḥ sugatāntikam āyayuḥ  Rm 
 tatas te 'py aṃśavaḥ sarve saṃmīlya saṃgatā muneḥ 
 pradakṣiṇatrayaṃ kṛtvā tasyorṇāyāṃ samāviśan  Rm 
 tad dṛṣṭvā te sabhālokā vismayoddhatamānasāḥ 
 kim etad iti saṃcintya sarve tasthuḥ śakautukāḥ  Rm 
 athānaṃdaḥ samālokya tān sarvān vismayoddhavān 
 utthāya sāñjalir natvā śāstāraṃ taṃ samabravīt  Rm 
 bhagavans te mukhād bhāsiḥ paṃcavarṇā vinirgatā 
 avabhāsya diśaḥ sarvā ūrṇāyāṃ ca viśanti tāḥ  Rm 
 etad dṛṣṭvā sabhālokāḥ sarve 'pīme savismayāḥ 
 taddhetuṃ śrotum ichanti tad upādeṣṭum arhati  Rm 
 nāhetu hi smitaṃ buddhā darśayanti kadā cana 
 yad dhetau bhavatā śāstur hasitaṃ tat samādiśa  Rm 
 iti saṃprārthitaṃ śiṣyena sa munīśvaraḥ 
 tam ānaṃdaiḥ sabhāṃ cāpi samālokyaivam ādiśat  Rm 
 paśyānaṃda yad etair hi sarvai gāndharvikair api 
 mama sasāṃghikasyaivaṃ satkāraṃ prakṛtaṃ mudā  Rm 
 etatpuṇyavipākena sarve 'pīme bhavāntare 
 kramād bodhicarīṃ prāptā niḥkleśā vimalāśayāḥ  Rm 
 māracaryāvinirmuktāḥ pariśuddhās trimaṇḍalāḥ 
 varṇasvarābhidhāḥ sarve pratyekasugatā jināḥ  Rm 
 prāntāśayyāsānāsīnā hīnadīnānukampakāḥ 
 dakṣiṇīyā mahāsatvā bhaviṣyanti śubhaṃkarāḥ  Rm 
 evam etāt samālokya yūyaṃ yadi samichatha 
 tathātra śraddhayā nityaṃ triratnaṃ bhajatādarāt  Rm 
 ye triratnaṃ sadā bhaktyā satkṛtyaivaṃ bhajanti te 
 vihāya durgatiṃ nityaṃ sadgatiṃ samavāpnuyuḥ  Rm 
 Rm 
 iti matvātra saṃsāre yeṣāṃ vāṃchā sukhe śive 
 te satkṛtya triratneṣu śraddhayā bhajatāniśaṃ  Rm 
 ity ādiṣṭaṃ munīndreṇa śrutvā sarve ca te janāḥ 
 satyam evaṃ pratijñāya triratnaṃ sarvadābhajan  Rm 
 tad dṛṣṭvā bhikṣavaḥ sarve vismayoddhatamānasāḥ 
 kṛtāñjalipuṭā natvā paprachus taṃ munīśvaraṃ  Rm 
 yad evaṃ bhagavann ebhiḥ satkāraṃ prakṛtaṃ mahat 
 tat te kena supuṇyena samyag ādeṣṭum arhati  Rm 
 evaṃ tair bhikṣubhiḥ sarvaiḥ prārthite sa jineśvaraḥ 
 sarvāns tāñ chrāvakān bhikṣūn samālokyaivam ādiśat  Rm 
 śṛṇudhvaṃ bhikṣavaḥ puṇyaṃ yan mayā prakṛtaṃ purā 
 tad atra kathitaṃ śrutvā śraddhayābhyanumodata  Rm 
 purāsīd bhagavān buddhaḥ prabodhanābhidho jinaḥ 
 sarvajñaḥ sugataḥ śāstā dharmarājo munīśvaraḥ  Rm 
 sarvavidyādhipo nāthas tathāgato vināyakaḥ 
 mārajil lokavid bharttā subhadro 'rhan hitaṃkaraḥ  Rm 
 tadā sa bhagavān buddho janapadeṣu cārikāṃ 
 carann anyāṃ rājadhānīm anuprāptaḥ sasāṃghikaḥ  Rm 
 tatra tasya narendrasya krīḍodyāne taror adhaḥ 
 praviśya svāsanāsīnas tasthau vahnir ivojvalan  Rm 
 tadaikasmin dine tatra rājā kāntāpravādinaiḥ 
 saṃgītaiḥ saha saṃrakto ramituṃ samupāviśat  Rm 
 tatrasthaṃ taṃ samāsīnaṃ sugataṃ suprabhojvalaṃ 
 dṛṣṭvaiva sahasopetya natvā kṛtvā pradakṣiṇāṃ  Rm 
 samādhisthaṃ tam ālokya taṣṭhau ciram upāśrayan 
 tatas tanmukhapadmotthasaddharmāmṛtalipsayā  Rm 
 vādyamānaiḥ satair vādyair muniṃ prābodhayan nṛpaḥ 
 tataḥ sa sugato buddho samādheḥ śīghram utthitaḥ  Rm 
 sāntaḥpuraṃ nareṃdraṃ taṃ prādrākṣīt samupasthitaṃ 
 tadā taṃ nṛpatiṃ dṛṣṭvā sa saṃbuddhaḥ prabodhanaḥ  Rm 
 saddharmmaṃ samupādeṣṭuṃ samāmaṃtryaivam abravīt 
 ehi rājan mahāvāho svāgataṃ te mahīpate  Rm 
 saddharmaṃ samupāśritya bodhicaryāṃ samācara 
 sadā dānaṃ pradatvātra śīlaṃ dhṛtvā samāhitaḥ  Rm 
 kṣāntyā prasādayal lokān dharmavīryaṃ prasādhaya 
 bodhau cittaṃ samādhāya prajñāratnam upārjaya  Rm 
 tadratnānubhāvena saṃbodhimārgam āpnuyāḥ 
 tatas te maṅgalaṃ nityam ihāmutre sadā bhavet  Rm 
 sarvasatvahitaṃ kurvan sadgatim eva prāpnuyāḥ 
 iti matvā mahārāja saddharmaṃ samupāśrayan  Rm 
 triratnaṃ śaraṇaṃ kṛtvā satkṛtya bhaja sarvadā 
 triratneṣu kṛtaṃ puṇyaṃ na kṣiṇoti kadā cana  Rm 
 Rm 
 sarvadā satphalāny eva sūte bodhiṃ samarpayet 
 iti matvā mahārāja triratnaśaraṇaṃ gataḥ  Rm 
 bodhicaryāvrataṃ dhṛtvā cara nityaṃ samāhitaḥ 
 tathā te maṃgalaṃ nityaṃ sarvatrāpi bhaved dhruvaṃ  Rm 
 kramād bodhiṃ samāsādya saṃbuddhapadam āpnuyāḥ 
 iti tenārhatādiṣṭaṃ munīndreṇa sa bhūpatiḥ  Rm 
 śrutvā tatheti vijñapya prābhyanandat prabodhitaḥ 
 tataḥ sa mudito rājā taṃ munīndraṃ sasāṃghikaṃ  Rm 
 yathāvidhi samabhyarcya bhojanaiḥ samatoṣayat 
 tataś ca bhojanānte sa nṛpatiḥ sāñjalir mudā 
 taṃ munīndraṃ praṇatvaivaṃ praṇidhānaṃ hṛdo vyadhāt  Rm 
 anena kuśalenāhaṃ loke 'ndhe 'pariṇāyake 
 samyag bodhiṃ samāgamya bhaveyaṃ sugato jinaḥ  Rm 
 etat tena narendreṇa praṇidhānaṃ kṛtaṃ mudā 
 matvā sa sugatas tasya tathāśīrvacanaṃ dadau  Rm 
 jayo 'stu te sadā rājaṃ dharmeṇa pālaya prajāḥ 
 praṇidhānaṃ yathā bodhau tathā te siddhyatu dhruvaṃ  Rm 
 ity ādiṣṭaṃ munīndreṇa tena śrutvā sa bhūpatiḥ 
 muditaḥ sāñjalir natvā taṃ munīndraṃ samabravīt  Rm 
 adyārabhya sadā śāstas triratnaśaraṇaṃ gataḥ 
 saṃbodhisaṃvaraṃ dhṛtvā cariṣyāmi samāhitaḥ  Rm 
 tad bhavān kṛpayā dṛṣṭyā sadā māṃ draṣṭum arhati 
 sarvadā bhavatām eva śaraṇe 'smi samāsthitaḥ  Rm 
 iti saṃprārthanāṃ kṛtvā rājā sa sajano mudā 
 bhagavaṃtaṃ tam ānamya sānaṃdaḥ svapuraṃ yayau  Rm 
 tataḥ sa bhagavāñ chāstā samutthāya sasāṃghikaḥ 
 sarvatra bhadratāṃ kṛtvā svāśrame samupāyayau  Rm 
 manyatāṃ bhikṣavo yo 'sau rājā saṃbuddhasevakaḥ 
 aham eva tadābhūvan nānyo draṣṭavya eva saḥ  Rm 
 yan mayā śraddhayā tasya prabodhanasya tāyinaḥ 
 pūjākāri mahotsāhais tūryasaṃgītivādanaiḥ  Rm 
 tena puṇyavipākena mamātraiva mahotsavaiḥ 
 etair gāndharvikair evaṃ satkāraḥ prakṛtādhunā  Rm 
 evaṃ matvā mahatpuṇyaṃ saṃbuddhabhajanodbhavaṃ 
 triratnaṃ śaraṇaṃ kṛtvā bhajanīyaṃ śubhārthibhiḥ  Rm 
 yūyaṃ cāpi sadā nityaṃ śāstāraṃ sadguruṃ jinaṃ 
 saṃbuddhaṃ samupāśritya viharadhvaṃ samāhitāḥ  Rm 
 ity ādiṣṭaṃ munīndreṇa śrutvā te bhikṣavo mudā 
 sarve tatheti vijñapya triratnāni sadābhajan  Rm 
 iti me guruṇādiṣṭaṃ śrutaṃ mayā narādhipa 
 tathādhunā samākhyātaṃ tava puṇyapravṛddhaye  Rm 
 evaṃ rājaṃs tvayāpy evaṃ triratnaṃ śaraṇaṃ gataḥ 
 saṃbuddhaśāsanaṃ dhṛtvā cara dharmaṃ samāhitaḥ  Rm 
 Rm 
 prajāś cāpi tathā rājaṃ bodhayitvā prayatnataḥ 
 saṃbodhisādhane dharme yojanīyās tvayādarāt  Rm 
 tathā cet te sadā bhadraṃ bhaven nūnaṃ samantataḥ 
 kramād bodhiṃ samāsādya saṃbuddhapadam āpnuyāḥ  Rm 
 iti śāstrā samādeṣṭaṃ śrutvāśokaḥ sa bhūpatiḥ 
 tatheti pratimoditvā prābhyanandat sapārṣadaḥ  Rm 
 gāṃdharvikānām avadānam etac chrutvānumodanti narā mudā ye 
 te sarva enaḥparimuktacittā bhuktvā sukhāny eva labhanti bodhiṃ 
  iti ratnāvadānatatve gāṃdharvikāvādanaṃ samāptam 
 Rm 
 XV Sūkṣmatvacovadāna
 athāśoko mahīpālaḥ kṛtāṃjalipuṭo mudā 
 upaguptaṃ guruṃ natvā punar evam abhāṣata  Rm 
 bhadanta śrotum ichāmi punar anyat subhāṣitaṃ 
 tadyathā guruṇākhyātaṃ tathādeṣṭuṃ ca me 'rhasi  Rm 
 iti saṃprārthite rājñā sa yatiḥ sugatātmajaḥ 
 aśokaṃ taṃ nṛpaṃ dṛṣṭvā punar evam upādiśat  Rm 
 śṛṇu rājan mahābhāga yathā me guruṇoditaṃ 
 tathāhaṃ te pravakṣyāmi śrutvāpy evaṃ pramodaya  Rm 
 purā sa bhagavān buddhaḥ śākyasiṃho jagadguruḥ 
 vihāre jetakāraṇye vijahāra sasāṃghikaḥ  Rm 
 tasmiṃś ca samaye tatra sarve bhikṣugaṇā api 
 śrāvakāś cailakāś caiva sarva upāsakā api  Rm 
 sarve 'pi bhikṣuṇīsaṃghā upāsikāgaṇā api 
 bodhisatvagaṇāś cāpi saddharmasādhanodyatāḥ  Rm 
 sabhāmadhyāsanāsīnaṃ śrīghanaṃ taṃ jagadguruṃ 
 upatasthuḥ puraskṛtya parivṛtya samaṃtataḥ  Rm 
 tadā tasya munīndrasya mukhāmbhojavinirgataṃ 
 bhadradharmāmṛtaṃ pātuṃ sarve lokāḥ samāgatāḥ  Rm 
 śakrādayaḥ surendrāś ca brahmādayo maharddhikāḥ 
 lokapālā mahāvīrāḥ sasainyaparivārakāḥ  Rm 
 yogino yatayaś cāpi maharṣayas tapaśvinaḥ 
 brāhmaṇāś ca mahāvijñāḥ saddharmaguṇavāṃchinaḥ  Rm 
 rājāno rājaputrāś ca vaiśyā maṃtrijanā api 
 amātyāḥ śreṣṭhino bhaṭṭāḥ paurikāś ca gṛhādhipāḥ  Rm 
 sainyādhipāś ca yodhāraḥ sārthavahā mahājanāḥ 
 vaṇijaḥ śilpinaś cāpi grāmyāḥ kārpaṭikā api  Rm 
 evam anye 'pi lokāś ca saddharmaguṇavāñchinaḥ 
 sarve dharmāmṛtaṃ pātuṃ vihāre samupāgatāḥ  Rm 
 tatra prāptāḥ sabhāmadhye samāsīnaṃ munīśvaraṃ 
 śrīghanaṃ taṃ samālokya praṇatvā samupācaran  Rm 
 tatra te samupāsṛtya sarve taṃ śrīghanaṃ muniṃ 
 tridhā pradakṣiṇīkṛtvā samabhyarcya praṇemire  Rm 
 tataḥ sarve 'pi te lokāḥ parivṛtya samantataḥ 
 sāñjalayaḥ prasannāsyā upatasthuḥ samāhitāḥ  Rm 
 tadā sa bhagavān dṛṣṭvā sarvāṃs tān samupasthitān 
 ādimadhyāntakalyāṇam āryadharmam upādiśat  Rm 
 tat saddharmāmṛtaṃ pītvā sarve te tridaśādayaḥ 
 Rm 
 lokā dharmaviśeṣatvaṃ vijñāya prāṇanandire  Rm 
 tasminn avasare tatra śrāvastyāṃ pauriko gṛhī 
 śreṣṭhī mahājanaḥ śrimāñ chrāddho bhadrāśayābhavat  Rm 
 sa ekasmiṃ dine svasmin bhāṇḍālakoṣṭhake viśan 
 svasaṃpannicayaṃ dṛṣṭvā manasaivaṃ vyacintayat  Rm 
 aho me jāyate saṃpad dīyatī saṃpravarddhitā 
 tathāpi varddhyate tṛṣṇā yataḥ saukhyaṃ na kiṃ cana  Rm 
 yad ime caṃcalā bhogā jalacaṃdranibhā mama 
 anityā asthirāḥ padmapatrasthitajalopamā  Rm 
 tad atra kiṃ mano 'dyāpi tṛṣṇayākṛṣyate mama 
 yena carāmy ahaṃ loke duḥkhī bhavikalāśayaḥ  Rm 
 tat kiṃ me saṃpadā sāraṃ yataḥ saukhyaṃ na vidyate 
 dharmārthe gocaraṃ naiva kevalaṃ madavṛddhaye  Rm 
 madena varddhate mānaṃ mānāl loke pramādatā 
 pramādād dīpyate cerṣyā kopāgnir dīpyate tataḥ  Rm 
 kopāt krūrāśayaś caṇḍo nirdayo duritāśayaḥ 
 pāpātmā hiṃsako duṣṭo daśākuśalasādhakaḥ  Rm 
 svayaṃ naṣṭaḥ parāṃś cāpi nāśayati durāśayaḥ 
 tato 'tipāpasaṃrakto durācaro 'tidurmanāḥ  Rm 
 tato 'tidurmatir drohī saṃvṛttidharmaniṃdakaḥ 
 triratnāni pratikṣipya mahāpātakam ācaret  Rm 
 tato 'tipāpasaṃkliṣṭāḥ pramūḍho narakaṃ vrajet 
 narakeṣu bhraman nityaṃ duḥkhāny eva sadāśnuyāt  Rm 
 yad vātrāpi ca saṃsāre jīvitam adhruvaṃ khalu 
 kṣaṇadhvaṃsi śarīraṃ ca sārveṣāṃ maraṇaṃ dhruvaṃ  Rm 
 tad atrāham asārebhyo bhogebhyaḥ sāram uttamaṃ 
 saddharmaṃ samupādātuṃ yatnaṃ kuryāṃ samādarāt  Rm 
 saddharmaṃ saugataṃ dharmam ity ākhyātaṃ purāvidaiḥ 
 tad atra saugate kṣetre dānaṃ kurvīya sāṃprataṃ  Rm 
 bauddhakṣetre kṛtaṃ dānaṃ bodhivījaṃ bhaved dhruvaṃ 
 etad evātra saṃsāre sādhanīyaṃ śubhāptaye  Rm 
 dānena śuddhyate cittaṃ sucittaḥ sumatiṃ labhet 
 subuddhiḥ sadguṇāraktaḥ saṃvṛttiśīlabhṛt kṛtī  Rm 
 suśīlaḥ kṣāntimān dhīraḥ parātmasamabhāvikaḥ 
 sudhīro vīryavān sarvasatvārthasādhanodyataḥ  Rm 
 apradhṛṣyo mahāsatvaḥ kleśāridamako bhavet 
 tataḥ supariśuddhātmā samādhisusthito bhavet  Rm 
 tat samādhivalādhānaiḥ prajñābdhipāram āgataḥ 
 bodhiratnaṃ samāsādya bodhisatvo 'dhipo bhavet  Rm 
 etad ratnānubhāvena bhadraṃkalā samantataḥ 
 Rm 
 sarvamārān vinirjitya saṃbuddhapadam āpnuyāt  Rm 
 ity arhadbhir mahābhijñaiḥ samākhyātaṃ mayā śrutaṃ 
 tat saṃbuddhapadāṃ praptuṃ buddhaṃ bhajeya sāṃprataṃ  Rm 
 nūnaṃ buddhānubhāvena bhāvitaṃ setsyate dhruvaṃ 
 tad buddhapramukhaṃ sarvasaṃghaṃ pūjeya sādaraṃ  Rm 
 iti niścitya sa śrīmān gṛhasthaḥ saṃpramoditaḥ 
 bhagavaṃtaṃ sasaṃghan taṃ pūjayituṃ samaichata  Rm 
 tataḥ sa sajanaḥ śreṣṭhī triratnabhajanotsukaḥ 
 vihāre jetakāraṇye prayayau saṃpraharṣitaḥ  Rm 
 tatra taṃ śrīghanaṃ dṛṣṭvā sa gṛhasthaḥ pramoditaḥ 
 natvā pradakṣiṇīkṛtya samarcayad yathāvidhiḥ  Rm 
 tataḥ sa sajano natvā sāñjaliḥ saṃpramoditaḥ 
 munīndraṃ taṃ samālokya puraḥ sthitvaivam abravīt  Rm 
 sarvajña bhagavaṃ chāstar bhavatāṃ śaraṇaṃ vraje 
 tato 'bhilaṣite kārye prasīdatu jagadguro  Rm 
 bhagavaṃ bhavataḥ śāstuḥ sasaṃghasya jagadguroḥ 
 pūjayituṃ samichāmi tad anujñāṃ dadātu me  Rm 
 iti saṃprārthite tena bhagavān sa munīśvaraḥ 
 tathāstv iti pratijñāya tūṣṇībhūtvādhyuvāsa tat  Rm 
 tataḥ sa gṛhabhṛn matvā bhagavatādhyuvāsa taṃ 
 sāñjalis taṃ muniṃ natvā muditaḥ svagṛhaṃ yayau  Rm 
 tatra sa svajanaiḥ svasmiṃ gṛhe margeṣu sarvataḥ 
 pariśodhya sugaṃdhaiś ca pariṣiṃcyābhyaśobhayat  Rm 
 tatrāsanāni prajñapya vitānāni vitatya ca 
 muktapuṣpaiḥ samākīrya surabhiṃ samadhūpayat  Rm 
 tataḥ sa bhojyasāmagrīṃ sādhayitvā svavaṃdhubhiḥ 
 tathopahārasāmagrīṃ pariśuddhām asādhayat  Rm 
 tato 'nye dyur gṛhasthaḥ sa snātvā śuddhāṃvarāvṛtaḥ 
 saṃbuddhāmaṃtraṇaṃ kartuṃ vihāre sajano yayau  Rm 
 tatra taṃ śrīghanaṃ dṛṣṭvā sasaṃghaṃ sa purogataḥ 
 kṛtāñjalipuṭo natvā prārthayad evam ādarāt  Rm 
 bhagavan nātha sarvajña samayo vartate 'dhunā 
 tat sasaṃgho mamāvāse bhāvān āgantum arhati  Rm 
 iti saṃprārthite tena bhagavān sa sasāṃghikaḥ 
 pātracīvaram ādāya saṃpratasthe prabhāsayan  Rm 
 tatra sa bhagavān mārge kṛtvā bhadraṃ prabhāsayan 
 bhikṣusaṃghagaṇaiḥ sārddhaṃ śrāvastīṃ samupāviśan  Rm 
 tadābhūn nagare tatra sarvatrāpi sumaṅgalaṃ 
 upadravāṇi sarvāṇi sahasā vilayaṃ yayuḥ  Rm 
 andhā rūpāṇi paśyantaḥ śṛṇvanto vadhirā ravān 
 hīnendriyāś ca ye te 'pi pratilabdhendriyā vavuḥ  Rm 
 ksutpipāsāhatā ye ca te 'bhavan parituṣṭitāḥ 
 rogiṇo nīrujā āsan kuvelā rucirāmvarāḥ  Rm 
 Rm 
 mūkā āsan pravaktāro jaḍāś cāpi suvāgminaḥ 
 ciravairābhisaṃnaddhās te 'py āsan maitrabhāvitāḥ  Rm 
 ye ca caṇḍāśāyāḥ krūrās te 'py abhūvan dayālavaḥ 
 ye ca duṣṭā durācārās te santas samyamodyatāḥ  Rm 
 daridrā dhaninaḥ proḍhyā dūrvalā valino 'bhavan 
 ye śaṭhā vaṃcakāś cauras te āryāḥ satyavādinaḥ  Rm 
 evaṃ ye duḥkhinaḥ satvās te sarve sukhino 'bhavan 
 evaṃ sa bhagavāṃs tatra kṛtvā bhadraṃ samantataḥ  Rm 
 pradakṣiṇakrameṇaivaṃ sasaṃghaṃ tadgṛhe viśan 
 tatra tasya munīndrasya sa gṛhastho yathākramaṃ 
 pādyaṃ dadau sasaṃghasya sadārāḥ śucināmbunā  Rm 
 tataḥ sa suprāsannātmā sasaṃghaṃ taṃ munīśvaraṃ 
 prajñapte svāsane tatra yathākramaṃ nyaveśayat  Rm 
 tatra te sāṃghikāḥ sarve saṃbuddhapramukhāḥ kramāt 
 svasvāsane samāviśya samātasthuḥ samāhitāḥ  Rm 
 tataḥ svasvāsanāsīnān saṃbuddhapramukhān yatīn 
 tān sarvān sa gṛhī dṛṣṭvā yathāvidhi samarcayat  Rm 
 tataḥ sa sajanaḥ śreṣṭhī svahastena sasāṃghikaṃ 
 taṃ munīndraṃ sudhākalpair bhojanaiḥ samatarpayet  Rm 
 tataḥ saṃtṛptitaṃ dṛṣṭvā sasaṃghaṃ taṃ munīśvaraṃ 
 apanīya sa pātrāṇi tad dhastādīn vyaśodhayat  Rm 
 tataḥ sa sāñjalir natvā tān buddhapramukhān yatīn 
 puro nīcāsanāsīno dharmaṃ śrotum upāśrayat  Rm 
 tataḥ sa bhagavān dṛṣṭvā taṃ gṛhaṣṭhaṃ subhāvinaṃ 
 ādimadhyāntakalyāṇaṃ dharmām ādeṣṭum abravīt  Rm 
 ārogyam astu te nityaṃ gṛhapate sadā śivaṃ 
 bodhau cittaṃ samādhāya cara dharmaṃ samāhitaḥ  Rm 
 dharmeṇa jīyate pāpaṃ niṣpāpaḥ sadgatiṃ vrajet 
 sadgatau satsukhāny eva bhuktvā saṃcarate sadā  Rm 
 dharmeṇa puruṣo vidvān sarvavidyākalādhipaḥ 
 sudhiro guṇavān vijño bhavec chrīmān maharddhikaḥ  Rm 
 dharmeṇa suciraṃ jīved ārogyaṃ ca sadā tanau 
 sarvatrāpi bhaven nityaṃ maṃgalaṃ nirupadravaṃ  Rm 
 dharmo na naśyate kvapi hriyate nāpi kena cit 
 kenāpi naśyate naiva cālayituṃ kadā cana  Rm 
 nāgnibhir dahyate dharmaḥ klidyate nāpi codakaiḥ 
 vāyubhiḥ śuṣyate naiva kṣīyate nāpi bhūmiṣu  Rm 
 dharmeṇa bhūḥ sthirībhūtā dharmeṇa dīpyate 'nalaḥ 
 dharmeṇa calate vāyur dharmeṇa vahate jalaḥ  Rm 
 dharmeṇa dīpyate bhānur dharmeṇaivaṃ sudhākaraḥ 
 Rm 
 meghā dharmeṇa varṣāṇā bhūmiḥ śaṣyauṣadhībharāḥ  Rm 
 dharmeṇaivaṃ tathā sarve lokapālā maharddhikāḥ 
 sarvaduṣṭān vinirjitya pālayanti jagattraye  Rm 
 dharmo na śīyate kvāpi dharmo na paribhūyate 
 sarvatra jayate dharmo dharmo hi śobhate sadā  Rm 
 dharmahīnā na śobhante śrimanto guṇino 'pi ca 
 dharmmiṣṭhā eva śobhante daridrā nirguṇā api  Rm 
 dharmeṇa rakṣitā vīrāḥ saṃgrāme vijitārayaḥ 
 yaśomānyamahatsaṃpatsukhāni te labhanti ca  Rm 
 tathā vīrā vaṇiksārthā dharmeṇaivābhirakṣitāḥ 
 mahāmbudhiṃ samuttīrya ratnāny api labhanti ca  Rm 
 dharmavanto narā dhīrā buddhimanto vicakṣaṇāḥ 
 sarvavidyākalāvijñā jayante paravādinaḥ  Rm 
 tathā dharmānubhāvena śilpavidyākalāvidaḥ 
 yaśomānyaprasādaśrīsatsukhāni labhanti ca  Rm 
 tathā ca maṃtriṇo 'mātyā dharmavanto vicakṣaṇāḥ 
 rājyakāryāṇi sarvāṇi sādhayanto jayanty arīn  Rm 
 rājānaḥ kṣatriyāś caivaṃ dharmanītivicakṣaṇāḥ 
 sarvaduṣṭān vinirjitya virājante nārādhipāḥ  Rm 
 tathā dharmeṇa rājendraś cakravarttī mahīśvaraḥ 
 saptaratnasamāyuktaḥ sarvaśāstā virājate  Rm 
 tathā dharmadharā eva yatayo yogino 'pi ca 
 sarvakleśagaṇāñ jitvā labhanti paramaṃ padaṃ  Rm 
 tatharṣayo mahābhijñā dharmabhṛto maharddhikāḥ 
 yathābhilaṣitāṃ siddhiṃ prāpya mokṣaṃ vrajanti ca  Rm 
 tathā dharmānusāreṇa maṃtravidyārthasādhakāḥ 
 siddhisamṛddhisaṃprāptāḥ sādhayanti yathehitaṃ  Rm 
 tathā ca mānavāḥ sarve lokā dharmānusārataḥ 
 nihīnamadhyamotkṛṣṭāḥ prabhavanti mahītale  Rm 
 tathā dharmānusāreṇa lokā daityādayo 'pi ca 
 nihīnamadhyamotkṛṣṭā pracaranti rasātale  Rm 
 tathā svargeṣu devāś ca svasvadharmānubhāvataḥ 
 sukhāni suciraṃ bhuktvā pravasanti pramoditāḥ  Rm 
 evaṃ sarvatra lokeṣu svasvadharmānubhāvataḥ 
 sarve satvāḥ sukhaprāptāḥ pracaranti yathechayā  Rm 
 evaṃ traidhātukotpannāḥ satvāḥ sarve surādayaḥ 
 svasvadharmānusāreṇa bhramanti ṣaḍgatiṣv api  Rm 
 kim atra vahunoktena dharma eva jagatprabhuḥ 
 dharmeṇaiva sadā nityaṃ rakṣitaḥ pracarec chubhe  Rm 
 ṣubhena siddhyate cittaṃ śuddhacittaḥ sudhīr bhavet 
 subuddhiḥ sadguṇādhāraṃ sadguruṃ samupāśrayet  Rm 
 tadguror upadeśena caran nityaṃ samāhitaḥ 
 bodhicittaṃ samādhāya triratnāni sadā bhajet  Rm 
 etatpuṇyānubhāvena saddharmasādhanodyataḥ 
 Rm 
 bodhisatvo mahāsatvo bodhicaryāṃ vrataṃ caret  Rm 
 tato māragaṇāñ jitvā pūrya pāramitāḥ kramāt 
 trividhāṃ bodhim āsādya saṃbuddhapadam āpnuyāt  Rm 
 evaṃ dharmavaraṃ matvā triratnaśaraṇaṃ gataḥ 
 saddharmaṃ samupaśritya cara bodhipadāptaye  Rm 
 mṛtyukāle vipattau ca dharmma evānugas suhṛt 
 tadā sarve tyajanty āśu ko 'pi naiva sahānugaḥ  Rm 
 dharma eva tadā trātā sarvatrāpy anugaḥ suhṛt 
 tasmād dharmo mahāratnaṃ sādhanīyaṃ prayatnataḥ  Rm 
 evaṃ sa bhagavāñ chāstā dharmasyābhyanubhāvatāṃ 
 samādiśya kṣaṇaṃ tasthau tūṣṇībhūtvā samāhitaḥ  Rm 
 tatas tasya munīndrasya pādau sa mudito gṛhī 
 praṇatvā manasā caivaṃ praṇidhānaṃ sāmadadhe  Rm 
 anena kuśalenāhaṃ sarvakleśavivarjitaḥ 
 pratyekāṃ bodhim āsādya nirvṛtiṃ samavāpnuyāt  Rm 
 tataḥ sa suprasannāsyo gṛhasthaḥ sajano mudā 
 bhagavataṃ tam ālokya puras tasthau samāhitaḥ  Rm 
 tadā sa bhagavāṃs tasya śrīmato hṛdaye sthitaṃ 
 praṇidhānaṃ parijñāya susaṃsmitaṃ vyamuñcata  Rm 
 tatas tasya munīndrasya mukhapadmāt surasmayaḥ 
 paṃcavarṇā vinirgatya sarvatra samudācaran  Rm 
 tāsāṃ yā raśmayo yātā adholoke samantataḥ 
 tāḥ sarvanarakeṣv evam avabhyāsya samāsarat  Rm 
 tadā tābhiḥ parispṛṣṭāḥ sarve te narakasthitāḥ 
 mahatsaukhyaṃ samāsādya vismayaṃ samupāyayuḥ  Rm 
 tatra sarve 'pi te satvāḥ parasparasamāgatāḥ 
 sarvaduḥkhavinirmuktāḥ saṃmīlyaivaṃ samabruvan  Rm 
 aho citraṃ kim adyaivaṃ mahat saukhyaṃ prajāyate 
 kiṃ nu vayaṃ bhavanto 'smāc cyutā anyatra cāgatāḥ  Rm 
 yad asmākaṃ mahad duḥkhaṃ tat sarvaṃ śāmyate 'dhunā 
 saṃjāyate mahāsaukhyaṃ tad adbhutaṃ na manyate  Rm 
 nūnam atrādhunā ko 'pi bodhisatvaḥ samāgataḥ 
 yasmād iyaṃ mahāraśmir avabhāsya prasaryati  Rm 
 iti ciṃtābhidagdhānaṃ teṣāṃ cittaprabodhane 
 bhagavān nirmitaṃ buddhaṃ sarvatra tatra preṣayet  Rm 
 tadā taṃ saugatiṃ mūrttiṃ dṛṣṭvā sarve 'pi te mudā 
 aho citram iti proktvā vismitāś caivam abruvan  Rm 
 nehaivetaś cyutāḥ sarve nāpy anyatra gatā vayaṃ 
 ihaiva saṃsthitāḥ sarve narake pravasāmahe  Rm 
 api tv ayaṃ mahān satvo 'pūrvadarśana āgataḥ 
 nūnam asyānubhāvena saṃjāyante sukhāni naḥ  Rm 
 tad asmiṃ sugatākare vayaṃ sarve prasāditāḥ 
 upetya praṇatiṃ kṛtvā sarvathā saṃbhajemahi  Rm 
 iti saṃbhāṣya sarve te nārakīyāḥ pramoditāḥ 
 Rm 
 upetya taṃ mahāsatvaṃ sāñjalayo 'bhinemire  Rm 
 namo buddhāya dharmāya saṃghāye ca namaḥ sadā 
 ity uktvā ca triratnānāṃ saṃsmṛtvā śaraṇaṃ yayuḥ  Rm 
 iti te nirmite tasmiṃ cittaṃ prasādya nirmalāḥ 
 sarvanirmuktakarmāṇaḥ sahasā sadgatiṃ yayuḥ  Rm 
 tathā corddhagatā yās tāḥ kramāc cāturmahādhipān 
 samārabhya trayastriṃśān sarvāṃś cāpi surālayāt  Rm 
 yāvad bhavāgraparyantam avabhāsya prasāritāḥ  Rm 
 tathā cāpi samodghuṣya sarvān devān anodayan 
 anityaṃ khalu saṃsāraṃ duḥkham śūnyam anātmakaṃ 
 iti matvā śubhe nityaṃ caritavyaṃ sadāpi ca  Rm 
 niṣkrāmatārabhadhvaṃ tad yujyadhvaṃ buddhaśāsane 
 dhunīta mṛtyusainyāni naḍāgāraṃ karī yathā  Rm 
 yo hy asmiṃ dharmavinaye hy apramattaś cariṣyati 
 tyaktvā janmātra saṃsāre duḥkhasyāntaṃ kariṣyati  Rm 
 iti matvātra saṃbodhipadaṃ yadi samichatha 
 tac chraddhayā triratnāni bhajadhvaṃ sarvadādarāt  Rm 
 etac chabdaṃ samākarṇya sarve devāḥ prabodhitāḥ 
 triratnaṃ śaraṇaṃ kṛtvā prabhejire sadādṛtāḥ  Rm 
 evaṃ tā raśmayaḥ sarvāḥ sarvāṃl lokāṃc chubhe vṛṣe 
 bodhayitvā pratisthāpya pratyāyayur muneḥ puraḥ  Rm 
 tatra tā raśmayaḥ sarvāḥ piṇḍitās tasya tāyinaḥ 
 tridhā pradakṣiṇīkṛtvā sūrṇāyāṃ nyaviśat punaḥ  Rm 
 tad dṛṣṭvā vismitāḥ sarve lokās te samitisthitāḥ 
 kiṃ dharmam ādiśed buddha iti saṃciṃtya tasthire  Rm 
 athānando mahābhijñaḥ samutthāya kṛtāñjaliḥ 
 puraḥ sthito munīndraṃ taṃ praṇatvā prārthayat tathā  Rm 
 bhagavān nānāvidhā raśmir bhavanmukhābjanirgatāḥ 
 avabhāsya jagallokaṃ bhavadūrṇāṃ niveśitā  Rm 
 mārajin nirmalasvānto nirvikalpo niraṃjanaḥ 
 nāhetvapratyayaṃ buddhā nirdainyā nirmadoddhavāḥ 
 smitaṃ caṃdrakarāhāsaṃ darśayanti kadācana  Rm 
 tad yad arthaṃ bhavān smitaṃ darśayati munīśvara 
 tad arthaṃ śrotum icchaṃti sarve lokā ime 'dhunā  Rm 
 tad bhavāṃ yat samādeṣṭum ichati sāṃprataṃ mune 
 tad dharmaṃ samupādiśya prasādayatv imāṃ sabhāṃ  Rm 
 iti tena vaśiṣyeṇa prārthite sa munīśvaraḥ 
 tam āyuṣmantam ānandaṃ samāmaṃtryaivam abravīt  Rm 
 evam etat sadānaṃda nāhetvapratyayaṃ smitaṃ 
 saṃbuddhā api te sarve darśayanti kadā cana  Rm 
 yad arthe smitam ānaṃda darśitaṃ sāṃprataṃ mayā 
 Rm 
 tad arthaṃ saṃpravakṣyāmi tac chṛṇudhvaṃ samāhitāḥ  Rm 
 paśyasi tvaṃ tadānaṃda śreṣṭhinānena yan mama 
 evaṃvidhaṃ sasaṃghasya satkāraṃ śraddhayā kṛtaṃ  Rm 
 etatpuṇyavipākena mayi cittaprasādataḥ 
 ayaṃ śrīmān mahāsatvo bodhisatvo bhavet sudhīḥ  Rm 
 tataḥ kleśavimuktātmā pariśuddhatrimaṃḍalaḥ 
 sūkṣmatvag iti vikhyātaḥ pratyekabuddha ātmavit  Rm 
 bhaviṣyati mahābhijñaḥ saṃvṛtiparamārthavit  Rm 
 evam etat mahatpuṇyavījam ārādhitaṃ mama 
 sāsane śrīmatānena śraddhayā bodhicetasā  Rm 
 buddhakṣetre kṛtaṃ puṇyaṃ na kṣiṇoti kadā cana 
 saṃbodhisatphalaṃ dadyān nānyad dharmaphalaṃ khalu  Rm 
 evaṃ mahattaraṃ puṇyaṃ buddhakṣetreṣu satkṛtaṃ 
 matvā taccharaṇaṃ kṛtvā triratnaṃ bhajatādarāt  Rm 
 ye buddaśaraṇaṃ gatvā bhajanti sarvadādarāt 
 te sadā sadgatiṃ yātāś caraṃti bodhisaṃvaraṃ  Rm 
 ye dharmaṃ śaraṇaṃ kṛtvā śrutvā bhajanti sādaraṃ 
 sarve te 'kleśino bhadrāḥ saṃprayānti jinālayaṃ  Rm 
 ye saṃghe śaraṇaṃ gatvā bhajanti śraddhayā sadā 
 na te gacchanti duḥkhatvaṃ sadā yānti sukhāvatīṃ  Rm 
 iti matvā tathā yūyaṃ sadā nityaṃ samāhitāḥ 
 triratnaśaraṇaṃ kṛtvā bhajadhvaṃ śraddhayādarāt  Rm 
 tena puṇyavipākena yūyaṃ sarve 'pi sarvathā 
 trividhāṃ bodhim āsādya saṃbuddhapadam āpsyatha  Rm 
 iti śāstrā munīndreṇa samādiṣṭaṃ niśamyate 
 sarve 'pi sāṃghikāḥ sarve lokāś ca saṃpramoditāḥ  Rm 
 tatheti pratisaṃśrutya triratnaṃ śaraṇaṃ gatāḥ 
 satkṛtya śraddhayā nityaṃ prabhejire samāhitāḥ  Rm 
 so 'pi śreṣṭhī tathā śāstrā samādiṣṭaṃ tadātmanaṃ 
 vyākaraṇaṃ samākarṇya prābhyanandat prabodhitaḥ  Rm 
 tataḥ prabhṛti sa śrīmāṃs triratnaṃ śaraṇaṃ gataḥ 
 satkṛtya śraddhayā nityaṃ sadā bheje pramoditaḥ  Rm 
 tataḥ sa bhagavāñ chāstā sasāṃghikaḥ samutthitaḥ 
 tathā sarvatra bhadrāṇi prakurvan svāśramaṃ yayau  Rm 
 ity evaṃ guruṇākhyātaṃ tathā mayātra kathyate 
 tvam apy evaṃ mahārāja śrutvā dharmaṃ śubhe cara  Rm 
 prajāś cāpi tathā dharmaṃ śrāvayitvā prabodhayan 
 bodhimārge pratiṣṭhāpya śubhe 'bhyava sadādarāt  Rm 
 tathā te sarvadā nityaṃ maṃgalaṃ nirupadravaṃ 
 bhaven nūnaṃ mahārāja satyam etat prabudhyatāṃ  Rm 
 etatpuṇyavipākena daśapāramitā api 
 paripūryya krameṇaivaṃ saṃbodhim api cāpsyai  Rm 
 evaṃ satyaṃ parijñāya triratnaṃ śaraṇaṃ gataḥ 
 satkṛtya śraddhayā nityaṃ bhaja bodhiṃ yadīchasi  Rm 
 Rm 
 iti tenārhatā śāstrā samādiṣṭaṃ niśamya saḥ 
 nṛpas tatheti saṃśrutya prābhyanandat sapārṣadaḥ  Rm 
 sūkṣmatvaco 'vadānaṃ yat tad idaṃ ye narā mudā 
 satkṛtya śraddhayā bhaktyā śṛṇvanti śrāvayanti ca  Rm 
 te sarve sadgatiṃ yātā bhuktvā saukhyāni sarvadā 
 saddharmaṃ samupāśritya saṃprayānti jinālayaṃ  Rm 
  iti ratnāvadānatatve sūkṣmatvaco'vadānaṃ samāptaḥ 
 Rm 
 XVI Pretikāvadāna
 athāśoko mahārājaḥ kṛtāñjalipuṭo mudā 
 upaguptaṃ yatiṃ natvā punar eva samabravīt  Rm 
 bhadanta śrotum ichāmi punar anyat subhāṣitaṃ 
 tadyathā guruṇādiṣṭaṃ tathādeṣṭuṃ ca me 'rhasi  Rm 
 iti saṃprārthitaṃ tena rājñā sa yatir ātmavit 
 tam aśokaṃ mahīpālaṃ samālokyaivam ādiśat  Rm 
 śṛṇu rājan mahābhāga yathā me guruṇoditaṃ 
 tathāhaṃ te pravakṣyāmi śrutvānumodanāṃ kuru  Rm 
 purā sa bhagavān buddhaḥ śākyasiṃho jagadguruḥ 
 sarvajñaḥ sugataḥ śāstā dharmarājas tathāgataḥ  Rm 
 bhikṣubiḥ śrāvakaiḥ sārddhaṃ cailakair bhikṣuṇīgaṇaiḥ 
 upāsakair mahāśrāddhais tathā copāsikāgaṇaiḥ  Rm 
 bodhisatvagaṇaiś cāpi saddharmasādhanodyataiḥ 
 kṛtakṛtyair mahābhijñaiś caturbrahmavihārakaiḥ  Rm 
 rājagṛhe puropānte veṇuvane śubhāṅkite 
 karaṇḍakanivāpākhye mahodyāne jināśrame  Rm 
 vihṛtya sarvasatvānāṃ hitārthena sabhāśritaḥ 
 ādimadhyāntākalyāṇaṃ dharmam ādeṣṭum ārabhat  Rm 
 tadā sarve 'pi devendrāḥ sadevāḥ kamalāsanaḥ 
 sarve lokādhipāś cāpi yakṣagaṃdharvakinnarāḥ  Rm 
 siddhā vidyādharāḥ sādhyā rākṣasā dānavādhipāḥ 
 nāgeṃdrā garuḍāś cāpi sajanaparivārakāḥ  Rm 
 ṛṣayo brahmaṇāś cāpi yatayo yogino 'pi ca 
 rājāno rājaputrāś ca maṃtriṇo 'pi ca  Rm 
 amātyāḥ sainyalokāś ca sārthavāhā mahājanāḥ 
 vaṇijaḥ śilpinaś cāpi gṛhasthāḥ paurikā janāḥ  Rm 
 grāmyā jānapadāś cāpi kārpaṭikāś ca nairgamāḥ 
 tathānye 'pi samāyātāḥ saddharmaguṇavāṃchinaḥ  Rm 
 tatra sarve 'pi te lokā vihāre samupāgatāḥ 
 taṃ munīndraṃ samāsīnaṃ dṛṣṭvā natvā pramoditāḥ  Rm 
 tridhā pradakṣiṇīkṛtvā samabhyarcya yathākramaṃ 
 natvā sāñjalayaḥ sarve parivṛtya samaṃtataḥ  Rm 
 tat saddharmāmṛtaṃ pātuṃ suprasannamukhāmbujaṃ 
 śrīghanaṃ taṃ samālokya samātasthuḥ samāhitāḥ  Rm 
 tadā sa bhagavān dṛṣṭvā tān sarvān samupasthitān 
 āryasatyaṃ samārabhya saddharmaṃ samupādiśat  Rm 
 tat saddharmāmṛtaṃ pītvā lokāḥ sarve 'pi te mudā 
 Rm 
 saṃbodhisādhanotsāhāḥ pracerire pramoditāḥ  Rm 
 tasminn avasare tatra rājagṛhāntike vane 
 veṇuvanāntike paṃcapretaśatāni cerire  Rm 
 nagnāny atikṛtāṅgāni dagdhasthūṇākṛtīni vai 
 romavastrāṇi rukṣāṇi śailopamodarāṇi ca  Rm 
 sūcīchidramukhāny asthiyaṃtravad ucchṛtāny api 
 kṣutpipāsābhidagdhāni hīnadīnasvarāṇy api  Rm 
 tīvraduḥkhāni taptāni pralapanti vihāyasi 
 vibhramanti sadā kvāpi kiñci sthitiṃ na lebhire  Rm 
 tadaikasmin dine tatra maudgalyāyana ātmavit 
 āyuṣmān saugato bhikṣur mahābhijño dayānvitaḥ  Rm 
 pūrvāhne pātram ādāya kāṣāyacīvarāvṛtaḥ 
 rājagṛhe pure piṇḍaṃ yācituṃ samupācaran  Rm 
 tatra yatiḥ sa tāṃ pretāṃ sarvān vibhramato 'mvare 
 dṛṣṭvene ka iti dhyātvā paśyañ janair upācaran  Rm 
 te sarve pretakāś cāpi dṛṣṭvā taṃ bhikṣum āgataṃ 
 sahasopetya natvāgre rudanta etad abruvan  Rm 
 bhadanta bhavatāṃ pādau vandāmahe samānatāḥ 
 tad asmākaṃ hitaṃ kṛtvā kṛpayā trātum arhati  Rm 
 vayaṃ rājagṛhe jātāḥ paurāḥ paṃcaśatāny api 
 svakarmaparibhuṃjānaḥ pretībhūtāś carāmahe  Rm 
 tadā vayam ime sarve gṛhasthāḥ śreṣṭhino narāḥ 
 mahādhanā mahābhogās tīrthikā dharmasevakāḥ  Rm 
 yad vayaṃ matsārākrāntamānasāḥ kuṭukuñcakāḥ 
 āgṛhītapariṣkārāḥ kevalārjanasādhakāḥ  Rm 
 naiva kiñ cit tadā dānam adadmahi kadā cana 
 arthinam āgataṃ dṛṣṭvā prākuṣyāmahi roṣitāḥ  Rm 
 paradattāny api śrutvā dṛṣṭvā cāpi praroṣitāḥ 
 dīyamāneṣu vighnāni prākurmahi prayatnataḥ  Rm 
 saugatā api cārhantaḥ pretā iveyam āgatāḥ 
 ity asmābhiḥ pramohāndhaiḥ paribhāṣyābhininditāḥ  Rm 
 tata ete vayaṃ sarve kālaṃ kṛtvā ca sāṃprataṃ 
 evaṃ pretālayotpannā duḥkhārditāś carāmahe  Rm 
 iti bhadanta vijñāya gatvā rājagṛhe bhavān 
 kṛpayāsmatpravṛttāṃtaṃ jñātīnāṃ purato vadan  Rm 
 chandakabhikṣaṇaṃ kṛtvā buddhādiṃ sarvasāṃghikaṃ 
 asmannāmnā samabhyarcya bhojayituṃ samarhati  Rm 
 saṃbuddhapramukhebhyaś ca saṃghebhyo bhavatādarāt 
 asmannāmnā prakarttavyaṃ praṇāmam api sadguro  Rm 
 dakṣiṇādeśanāpy asmannāmnā buddhādisāṃghikaiḥ 
 Rm 
 bhavatā kārayitavyā ity asmāsu kṛpāṃ kuru  Rm 
 yathāsmākam itaḥ pretalokā muktir bhaved dhruvaṃ 
 tathāsmāsu bhavāmc chāstā kṛpayā kartum arhāti  Rm 
 iti taiḥ prārthitaṃ sarvaiḥ sa maudgalyāyanaḥ sudhīḥ 
 śrutvā tatheti saṃśrutya tūṣṇībhūtvādhyuvāsa tat  Rm 
 tatas tān pretikān sarvān sa maudgalyāyano yatiḥ 
 samālokya samāśvāsya punar etat samabravīt  Rm 
 tatra yūyaṃ ca sarva śvaḥ pravṛtte saṃghabhojane 
 sasaṃghaṃ śrīghanaṃ draṣṭuṃ samāyāta samādarāt  Rm 
 iti tenārhātādiṣṭaṃ śrutvā te pretakā api 
 tatheti hi pratijñāya praṇatvā taṃ vane yayuḥ  Rm 
 tataḥ sa saugato bhikṣur maudgalyo yatir ātmavit 
 gatvā rājagṛhe teṣāṃ jñātīnāṃ samupācaran  Rm 
 tatra sarvatra teṣāṃ tat jñātīnāṃ bhavaneṣu sa 
 gatvā teṣāṃ pravṛttāṃtaṃ sarvam evaṃ nyavedayat  Rm 
 tataḥ sa tatra sarvāṃs tāṃ jñātīn āhūya sādaraṃ 
 teṣāṃ pretagater muktihetor evaṃ samabravīt  Rm' 
 śṛṇuta bho mahābhāgya yūyaṃ sarve samāhitāḥ 
 yuṣmākaṃ jñātivargāṇāṃ muktihetuṃ pravakṣyate  Rm 
 yato yuṣmatsagotrās te matsariṇo durāśayāḥ 
 āgṛhītapariṣkārā daśākuśalasaṃcarāḥ  Rm 
 nāpi dānaṃ pradattaṃ taiḥ kasmai ci kvāpi kiṃ cana 
 paradattāny api śrutvā dṛṣṭvā vā paryabhāṣyata  Rm 
 arhanto bhikṣavo vā tair yācakāś ca gṛhāgatāḥ 
 paribhāṣyābhisaṃtarjya niṣkāsitā gṛhād valāt  Rm 
 pretā iva sadā bhikṣāṃ yācitveme 'bhibhuṃjate 
 ity arhato yatī cāpi dṛṣṭvaiva te 'bhyanindayan  Rm 
 etatkarmavipākais te pretībhūtā vane 'dhunā 
 kṣutpipāsāhatā nityaṃ vibhramyante 'bhiduḥkhitāḥ  Rm 
 tat tesāṃ tan mahatpāpamuktihetor ihādhunā 
 saṃbuddhaśāsane dānaṃ kartum ichāmy ahaṃ khalu  Rm 
 mayaitad dakṣiṇādeśās tan nāmnā kārayiṣyate 
 tadā tat pāpamuktās te sarve yāyur divaṃ dhruvaṃ  Rm 
 tad atra śraddhayā yūyaṃ yathāśakti mayārthitāḥ 
 saṃghabhojanasāmagriṃ sarve pradātum arhaya  Rm 
 saṃghabhojye pravṛtte 'tra sarve te pretikā api 
 draṣṭuṃ samāgamiṣyanti yūyaṃ cāgaṃtum arhatha  Rm 
 ity uktvā prārthite tena maudgalyena dayālunā 
 śrutvā taj jātayaḥ sarve vismayāṃ samupāyayuḥ  Rm 
 tatas te vismitāḥ sarve tat pretagatimuktaye 
 Rm 
 tat bhojyasāmagrīṃ śraddhayā dātum icchire  Rm 
 ke cit tasmai suvarṇāni ke cid ratnāni saṃdaduḥ 
 ke cid ropyādi dhātūṃś ca dravyāni vividhāni cā  Rm 
 taṇḍulāni daduḥ ke cid dadur dhānyāni ke cana 
 ke cid daduḥ kalāyāṃś ca godhūmāṃś ca yavān api  Rm 
 kulmāṣān masurāṃś cāpi māṣacanakasarṣapān 
 mudgāṃś cāpi tathānyāṃś ca sarvān vrīhin daduḥ pare  Rm 
 tilapriyaṃgusiddhārthān bhaṃgāś ca rājikā api 
 mūlaśākakadamvāṃś ca patrapuṣpāṃkurāṇi ca  Rm 
 śṛṅgaverātipakvāni phalāni vividhāni ca 
 surasāni supathyāni pradaduś cāpare mudā  Rm 
 tiktāmlalavaṇādīni rasāni vividhāni ca 
 śunṭhīś ca pippirīś cāpi maricāni dadur mudā  Rm 
 hiṅguṃ ca jīrakāṃś cānye viḍarkasaiṃdhavādi ca 
 anye ghṛtāni tailāni pradaduḥ śraddhayā mudā  Rm 
 śaktūṃś ca piṣṭakāṃś cānyamodakāṃś ca dadur mudā 
 tathā dadhīni dugdhāni madhuni ca guḍāni ca  Rm 
 tathānye sarkarāś cāpi pradaduḥ śraddhayā mudā 
 tathauṣadhāni pathyāni pācakāni daduḥ pare  Rm 
 lāṅgalīpūgatāmbūlaravaṃgādīni saṃdaduḥ 
 sarvapeyāni bhojyāni vividhāny api 
 sarve te jñātayas teṣāṃ saṃghabhokṣyāya saṃdaduḥ  Rm 
 evaṃ te sarvavastūni datvā sarve pramoditāḥ 
 sāṃjalayaḥ praṇatvā taṃ maudgalyaṃ yatim ūcire  Rm 
 bhadanto 'nugrahaṃ kṛtvā saṃbuddhapramukhaṃ bhavān 
 sarvasaṃghaṃ samabhyarcya bhojayatu pratoṣayan  Rm 
 vayam apy āgamiṣyāmaḥ pravṛtte saṃghabhojane 
 tān pretān samupāyātān sarvān draṣṭuṃ sabāndhavāḥ  Rm 
 iti taiḥ prārthitaṃ śrutvā tatheti sa prabodhayan 
 tāni dravyāni sarvāṇi gṛhītvā svāśrame yayau  Rm 
 tataḥ sa bhikṣur āyuṣmān vihāre samupācaran 
 dṛṣṭvā taṃ śrīghanaṃ natvā sāñjaliḥ samupāśrayan  Rm 
 tatra sa bhagavān dṛṣṭvā taṃ maudgalyam upasthitaṃ 
 prahasan suprasannāsyaḥ samāmaṃtryaitad abravīt  Rm 
 kaṃ cit te kuśalaṃ vatsa kuto 'trāsi samāgataḥ 
 lokeṣu kiṃ pravṛttāṃtaṃ tan pracakṣva mahāmate  Rm 
 ity ādiṣṭe munīndreṇa sa maudgalyāyanaḥ sudhīḥ 
 bhagavantaṃ tam ānatvā sāñjalir etad abravīt  Rm 
 bhagavan kṛpayā śāstaḥ sarvatra kauśalaṃ mama 
 rājagṛhe pure piṃḍaṃ yācituṃ samupācaran  Rm 
 tatra mārge vanopānte paṃca pretaśatāny api 
 dṛṣṭvā māṃ samupasṛtya praṇatvaitad vadanti vai  Rm 
 bhadanta tad vijānīyā yad vayaṃ pretikā ime 
 sarve rājagṛhe jātā gṛhasthāḥ paurikāḥ khalu  Rm 
 Rm 
 tadā vayaṃ svayaṃ naṣṭā daśākuśalacāriṇaḥ 
 ete svadaivayogena pretībhūtāś carāmahe  Rm 
 tad bhavān kṛpayāsmākaṃ pretagativimuktaye 
 jñātīnām api sarveṣāṃ karmaplotiṃ nivedya hi  Rm 
 chandakabhikṣaṇaṃ kṛtvāpy asmannāmnā sasāṃghikaṃ 
 bhagavantaṃ samabhyarcya bhojayituṃ samarhati  Rm 
 asmannāmnāya saṃbuddhaṃ sasaṃghaṃ namatāṃ bhavān 
 dakṣiṇādeśanāś cāsmannāmnā deśayatum arhasi  Rm 
 tato nūnaṃ vayaṃ sarve pretagativimocitāḥ 
 nirmuktapāpakāḥ śuddhāḥ prāpnuyāma surālayaṃ  Rm 
 ity asmatprārthanāṃ kṛtvā kṛpayāsmān samuddharan 
 bodhimārge pratisthāpya pātum arhati sarvadā  Rm 
 iti teṣāṃ vacaḥ śrutvā tathā rājagṛhe gataḥ 
 tad jñātīnāṃ puras teṣāṃ pravṛttāṃtaṃ nivedya ca  Rm 
 chandakabhikṣaṇaṃ tebhyo yācitvāham ihācare 
 tathārcayitum ichāmi bhagavantaṃ sasāṃghikaṃ  Rm 
 iti me prārthanāṃ kṛtvā bhavāṃ chāstā jagadguruḥ 
 tad adhivāsanāṃ kṛtvā kṛpayā tān samuddhara  Rm 
 iti saṃprārthitaṃ tena bhagavān sa munīśvaraḥ 
 tatheti saṃpratiśrutya tūṣṇībhūtvādhyuvāsa tat  Rm 
 tato matvā sa maudgalyo bhagavato 'dhivāsitaṃ 
 sahasā bhojyasāmagrīṃ sapauraiḥ samasādhayat  Rm 
 tato 'nye dyuḥ prabhātāyāṃ sarvasādhitasiddhite 
 sāñjalis taṃ munīndraṃ ca praṇatvaitat samabravīt  Rm 
 bhagavan sarvasāmagrīṃ saṃsādhitaṃ susiddhyate 
 tat sarvasāṃghikaiḥ sārddhaṃ sahasāgaṃtum arhati  Rm 
 iti saṃprārthite tena bhagavāṃ sa munīśvaraḥ 
 bhikṣuṃ prāha samāhūya gaṇḍīm ākoṭyatām iti  Rm 
 tadādiṣṭaṃ munīndreṇa śrutvā bhikṣus tatheti saḥ 
 āśrutya sahasādāya gaṇḍīm ākoṭayat tadā  Rm 
 tad gaṇḍīśabdam ākarṇya sarve te sāṃghikā api 
 vihāre sahasāgatya bhagavantaṃ praṇemire  Rm 
 tataḥ sa bhagavāṃs tatra svāsane samupāviśat 
 sarve te sāṃghikāś cāpi kramāt svasvāsane 'viśan  Rm 
 tatas tad jñātayaḥ sarve tatrānye paurikā api 
 tān pretān draṣṭum āyātā upatasthuḥ sakautukāḥ  Rm 
 tadā te pretikāḥ sarve prakṣiptāḥ karmavāyubhiḥ 
 bahulokāntare dure yātās tasthur vimohitāḥ  Rm 
 tadā sa yatir ālokya sarvasaṃghān samāsthitān 
 tadjñātibandhuvargāṃś ca pretān draṣṭuṃ samācarat  Rm 
 tatra pretān adṛṣṭvā sa maudgalyo vismitāśayaḥ 
 kiṃ te 'tra nāgatā veti samantato vyalokayat  Rm 
 Rm 
 vilokayan sa sarvatra nādrakṣīt tāṃ samaṃtataḥ 
 sa saṃdigdhaḥ punas tatra samyagdṛṣṭyā vyalokayat  Rm 
 sarvatrāpi sa tāṃ pretān adṛṣṭvā vismayānvitaḥ 
 sarvatra magadhe 'paśyat samyagdṛśā samāhitaḥ  Rm 
 tatrāpi ca sa sarvatra naiva kaṃ cid apaśyate 
 tato 'tivismito 'nyatra divyadṛśābhyalokayat  Rm 
 aṃgavaṃgakaliṃgeṣu saurāṣṭramagadheṣu ca 
 tatrāpi tān adṛṣṭvā sa narakeṣu samantataḥ 
 divyena cakṣuṣā paśyan na ca tatrāpy apaśyata  Rm 
 tataś caturmahārājabhuvaneṣu samantataḥ 
 sa divyacakṣuṣā paśyaṃs tatrāpi nābhyapaśyata  Rm 
 tatrāpi tān adṛṣṭvā sa maudgalyo vismayānvitaḥ 
 devālayeṣu sarvatra krameṇa samalokayat  Rm 
 tatrāpi tāṃ samanteṣu sa maudgalyo 'tivismitaḥ 
 tān adṛṣṭvātisaṃdigdho bhagavatāntike 'carat  Rm 
 tatra sa purato gatvā śāstāraṃ taṃ munīśvaraṃ 
 kṛtāñjalipuṭo natvā paprachaitat pravṛttitāṃ  Rm 
 bhagavan sarvalokeṣu paśyatā divyacakṣusā 
 mayā na dṛśyate kaś cit te pretāḥ kvādhunā gatāḥ  Rm 
 teṣāṃ nāmnā bhavatpūjāṃ karttum etat prasādhitaṃ 
 yad atra nāgatāḥ kecit tat te pretā gatāḥ kuha  Rm 
 dṛśyante na mayā kvāpi sarvatrāpi samīkṣyate 
 eko 'pi nāgato hy atra kva gatās te 'dhunā khalu  Rm 
 tan me cittaṃ prasaṃdigdhaṃ dṛṣṭvā śāstā bhavān sudṛk 
 teṣāṃ gatiṃ samākhyāya saṃbodhayitum arhati  Rm 
 iti saṃprārthite tena maudgalyena sa sarvavit 
 bhagavāṃs taṃ samālokya maudgalyam etad abravīt  Rm 
 maudgalya mā kṛthā yatnaṃ khedam evābhipatsyase 
 gatās te pretikāḥ sarve sudūrabhuvane 'dhunā  Rm 
 sarve te yatidevarṣipratyekasugatair api 
 adṛśye viṣaye yātāḥ preritāḥ karmavāyubhiḥ  Rm 
 yadi sarvāṃ ca tāṃ draṣṭuṃ vāṃchasi tvam ihāśritaḥ 
 sarvāṃs tāṃ darśayiṣyāmi paśya buddhānubhāvatāṃ  Rm 
 tad atra tvaṃ samādāya gaṇḍīm ākoṭaya drutaṃ 
 oṃ namo bhagavate aparimitāyurjñānasuviniścitatejorājāya tathāgatāyārhate samyakambuddhāya  tadyathā 
 oṃ puṇye puṇye mahāpuṇye aparimitapuṇye aparimitapuṇyajñānasaṃbhāropacite 
 oṃ sarvasaṃskārapariśuddhe dharmate gagaṇasamudgate svabhāvaviśuddhe mahānayaparivāre svāhā 
 aṣṭottaraśatākṣaryyānayāsaṃlabdhacetanāḥ  Rm 
 sarve te 'trāgamiṣyanti gaṇḍīśabdābhināditāḥ 
 iti śāstrā samādiṣṭaṃ śrutvā sa pratibodhitaḥ  Rm 
 sahasā tat sabhāmadhye gaṇḍīm ākoṭayat tathā 
 tad gaṇḍīśabdam ākarṇya sarve te pretikā api 
 Rm 
 pariśuddhāśayā draṣṭuṃ vihāre samupācaran  Rm 
 tatra sarve 'pi te pretā dṛṣṭvā taṃ śrīghanaṃ mudā 
 tridhā pradakṣiṇīkṛtya sāñjalayaḥ praṇemire  Rm 
 kramāt tāṃ sarvasaṃghāṃś ca praṇatvā te pramoditāḥ 
 sarve 'py ekāntam āśritya paśyanta upatasthire  Rm 
 tatra tad jñātayaḥ sarve paurikāś cāpare 'pi ca 
 tān pretān samupāsīnān dṛṣṭvā tasthuḥ sakautukāḥ  Rm 
 evaṃ sarve 'pi te pretāḥ svasvajñātīn upasthitān 
 bhātrādīn bandhuvargāṃś ca dṛṣṭvaivam upatasthire  Rm 
 tataḥ so 'rhan mahābhijño maudgalyas tān upasthitān 
 pretān sarvān samālokya natvāhaivaṃ munīśvaraṃ  Rm 
 bhagavan nātha sarvajña te pretāḥ sarva āgatāḥ 
 tad eṣāṃ bhagavāṃ cchāstānugrahaṃ karttum arhati  Rm 
 nivedyeti sa maudgalyaḥ saṃbuddhapramukhaṃ kramāt 
 sarvaṃ saṃghaṃ samabhyarcya bhojayan samatoṣayat  Rm 
 tataḥ sa sarvasaṃghaṃ taṃ dṛṣṭvā saṃtṛptikaṃ mudā 
 apanīyāśu pātrāṇi hastādīn samaśodhayat  Rm 
 tataḥ khapurasūkṣmailātāmbūlādi rasāyanaṃ 
 datvā kṣamārthanāṃ kṛtvā prārthayat sa munīśvaraṃ  Rm 
 bhagavan nātha sarvajña bhavāṃ chāstā sasāṃghikaḥ 
 dakṣiṇādeśanām ebhyaḥ pretebhyaḥ kartum arhati  Rm 
 iti saṃprārthitaṃ śrutvā sarve te pretikā mudā 
 sasaṃghaṃ taṃ muniṃ natvā sādaram upatasthire  Rm 
 tataḥ sa bhagavān dṛṣṭvā sasaṃghas tān upasthitān 
 dakṣiṇādeśanāṃ tebhyaḥ sarvebhyo vidadhe śubhāṃ  Rm 
 ito dānād dhi yat puṇyaṃ tat pretān anugachatu 
 uttiṣṭhantaḥ prayānty ete sarve pretāḥ surālayaṃ  Rm 
 ity ādiśya punas tatra bhagavāṃ sa munīśvaraḥ 
 āryyasatyaṃ samārabhyāparimitāyuṣas tadā  Rm 
 dhāraṇyā guṇamāhātmyaṃ saddharmaṃ samupādiśat  Rm 
 saṃsāre mānuṣe janma durlabhaṃ bhavacāriṇāṃ 
 mānuṣye labhyamāne 'pi kṣaṇasaṃpat sudurlabhā  Rm 
 mānuṣye 'labhyamāne hi jantūnāṃ sukhatā kutaḥ 
 duḥkhāny eva bhave nityaṃ puṇye matiḥ kathaṃ caret  Rm 
 vinā puṇyamatiṃ jantuḥ saddharme katham ācaret 
 vinā saddharmabhāvena sadgatiṃ katham āpnuyāt  Rm 
 preteṣu sarvadā nityaṃ kṣutpipāsāvidāhitaḥ 
 tiryakṣu narakeṣv eva bhraman duḥkhāny avāpnuyāt  Rm 
 tad atra mānuṣe janmaprāptair yatnena mānavaiḥ 
 satkṛtya śraddhayā nityaṃ śrotavyaṃ sadvṛṣaṃ mudā  Rm 
 saddharmaśrutamātreṇa mahatpuṇyam avāpnuyāt 
 etat puṇyavipākena sadgurau sarvadā bhajet  Rm 
 Rm 
 sadguror upadeśena saddharmeṣv eva sadācaret 
 etatpuṇyavipākena sadgatiṃ sarvadā vrajet  Rm 
 tatra sukhāni saṃbhuktvā saṃcareta śubhe sadā  Rm 
 etad dharmānubhāvena mahatsamṛddhim āpnuyāt 
 mahatsamṛddhisaṃpatsu karttavyaṃ dānam arthiṣu  Rm 
 dānena varddhyate lakṣmīr lakṣmīmāṃ cchobhate pumān 
 sadbuddhiḥ sadguṇādhāro yaśobhāgyasukhānvitaḥ  Rm 
 tataḥ saugatadharmāṇi śrutvā nityaṃ prabodhitaḥ 
 triratnaśaraṇaṃ kṛtvā bhajed bhaktyā sadādarāt  Rm 
 etatpuṇyānubhāvena bodhicittaṃ samāpnuyāt 
 bodhicitte hi labdhe hi bodhisatvo bhavet kṛtī  Rm 
 tataḥ sa bodhicittena daśapāramitāḥ kramāt 
 paripūrya mahāsatvas trividhāṃ bodhim āpnuyāt  Rm 
 tato māragaṇāṃ jitvā pariśuddhas trimaṇḍalaḥ 
 qsākṣād arhatpadaṃ prāpya nirvṛtipadam āpnuyāt  Rm 
 evaṃ vijñāya martyena karttavyaṃ dānam arthine 
 dānena sadgatiṃ yāyād adātā durgatiṃ vrajet  Rm 
 durgatiṣu sadā bhuktvā duḥkhāni vividhāṃ sa 
 sarvadā duḥkhasaṃkliṣṭaḥ pāpeṣv evārataś caret  Rm 
 etatpāpavipākena daśasv akuśaleṣv api 
 nirato hy aviśaṃkena saṃcareta pramādataḥ  Rm 
 tataḥ so hy atipāpiṣṭhaḥ saddharmanindakaḥ kudhīḥ 
 svayaṃ naṣṭaḥ parāṃś cāpi nāśayen nāstikaḥ śaṭhaḥ  Rm 
 tato 'tipāpasaṃkliṣṭaḥ pratikṣipya jinān api 
 ghoreṣu narakeṣv eva gatvā bhraman sadā vaset  Rm 
 sadāpi narakeṣv evaṃ bhramatas tasya duḥkhinaḥ 
 kaścin naiva samuddhartuṃ śaknuyāt saugatād ṛte  Rm 
 yāvan na smarate buddhaṃ tāvat sa narake vaset 
 yad eva smarate buddhaṃ tadā syāc chuddhitāśayaḥ  Rm 
 tadā taṃ kṛpayā buddho dṛṣṭvā bauddhena cakṣuṣā 
 puṇyakareṇa saṃspṛṣṭvā samuddhared araṃ tataḥ  Rm 
 tatas taṃ pāpinaṃ bauddhā dharmāmbubhir viśodhya ca 
 krameṇa bodhimārgeṣu niyojayet prabodhayan  Rm 
 tataḥ sa pariśuddhātmā saṃbuddhaśāsane rataḥ 
 triratnaśaraṇaṃ kṛtvā saddharma eva prācaret  Rm 
 tataḥ satvahitārthe sa bodhicaryāsamudyataḥ 
 kramāt pāramitāḥ sarvā pūrayituṃ samudyamet  Rm 
 tataḥ pāramitāḥ sarvāḥ pūrayitvā samāhitaḥ 
 bodhisatvo mahāsatvo buddhātmajo bhaved api  Rm 
 tataḥ kleśagaṇāñ jitvā pariśuddhatrimaṃḍalaḥ 
 trividhāṃ bodhim āsādya nirvṛtipadam āpnuyāt  Rm 
 evaṃ matvā sadā nityaṃ triratnaśaraṇaṃ gatāḥ 
 saddharmaṃ samupāśritya caradhvaṃ mānavā mudā  Rm 
 ity ādiṣṭaṃ munīndreṇa śrutvā te brāhmaṇādayaḥ 
 Rm 
 sarve lokā parijñāya dṛṣṭasatyās tathācaran  Rm 
 tathā sarve 'pi te pretāḥ śrutvā tad dharmadeśanāṃ 
 mudā taṃ śrīghanaṃ natvā śuddhātmānas tato 'caran  Rm 
 tatas tad jñātayaḥ sarve dṛṣṭvā śrutvā sakautukāḥ 
 sasaṃghaṃ taṃ muniṃ natvā svasvālayaṃ yayur mudā  Rm 
 tataḥ sa bhagavān buddhaḥ samutthāya saṣāṃghikaḥ 
 dhyānālayaṃ samāśritya tasthau dhyānasamāhitaḥ  Rm 
 sa maudgalyāyanaś cāpi kṛtakṛtyaḥ pramoditaḥ 
 śāstāraṃ taṃ praṇatvaivaṃ svam āśramaṃ samāśrayat  Rm 
 tadā sarve 'pi te pretāḥ saṃbuddhe 'bhiprasāditāḥ 
 triratnasmaraṇaṃ kṛtvā tataś cyutā divaṃ yayuḥ  Rm 
 tatrotpannā hi te sarve mahatsaukhyasamanvitāḥ 
 pariśuddhasubhadrāṅgā vismitā etad abruvan  Rm 
 aho 'smākaṃ mahatsaukhyaṃ kim evaṃ jāyate 'dhunā 
 kutaś cyutāḥ kuhāyāmaḥ karmaṇā kena vā vayaṃ  Rm 
 atha buddhānubhāvena sarve te pretapūrvakāḥ 
 devaputrā anusmṛtvā prabodhitāḥ samabruvan  Rm 
 bhavanto yad vayaṃ sarve pretā buddhānubhāvataḥ 
 maudgalyasyārhato bhikṣoḥ kṛpādṛṣṭiprayatnataḥ  Rm 
 saṃbuddhadarśanaprāptās triratnaśaraṇaṃ gatāḥ 
 etat puṇyaparispṛṣṭāḥ pariśuddhatrikāyikāḥ  Rm 
 tataḥ pretagateś cyutvā svargaloke samāgatāḥ 
 mahaddivyasukhāny evam atra labhāmahe 'dhunā  Rm 
 etat satyaṃ parijñāya tasya śāstur jagadguroḥ 
 punaḥ sarve vayaṃ gatvā satkṛtya prabhajemahi  Rm 
 iti saṃbhāṣaṇaṃ kṛtvā sarve te pretapūrvakāḥ 
 devaputrāḥ śubhāmbhobhiḥ snātvā divyāmvarāvṛtāḥ  Rm 
 divyasugaṃdhaliptāṅgā divyālaṃkārabhūṣitāḥ 
 divyapūjopacārāṇi gṛhītvā mahadutsavaiḥ 
 sarvaṃ veṇuvanaṃ bhābhir avabhāsya samantataḥ  Rm 
 vihāre samupāsṛtya dṛṣṭvā taṃ śrīghanaṃ mudā 
 natvā pradakṣiṇīkṛtvā praharṣitā upācaran  Rm 
 tatra divyopacārais taiḥ pūjāṃgais taṃ munīśvaraṃ 
 sarve 'pi te samabhyarcya satkṛtya śraddhayābhajan  Rm 
 tatra caikāntam āśritya saddharmmaśravaṇotsukāḥ 
 kṛtāñjalipuṭāḥ sarve upatasthuḥ samāhitāḥ  Rm 
 atha sa bhagavān dṛṣṭvā tān sarvān samupasthitān 
 āryasatyaṃ samārabhaḥ saddharmaṃ samupādiśat  Rm 
 tat saddharmāmṛtaṃ pītvā sarve te pretapūrvakāḥ 
 devaputrāś ca dharmāṇāṃ viśeṣatvaṃ pralebhire  Rm 
 tatas te muditāḥ sarve saṃbodhipadavāṃchinaḥ 
 śāstāraṃ taṃ punar natvā samālokyaitad abruvan  Rm 
 bhagavan yad vayaṃ sarve vimuktakarmabaṃdhanāḥ 
 Rm 
 pretalokāt paricyutvā svarge yātāḥ sma sāṃprataṃ  Rm 
 divyasukhāni sāmbhuktvā devaiḥ saha pramoditāḥ 
 saddharmaguṇam ākarṇya carāmahe sadādhunā  Rm 
 tat kṛpālo yatas tasya maudgalyasya mahāmateḥ 
 kṛpadṛṣṭiprasādena nūnaṃ manyāmahe vayaṃ  Rm 
 tad bhavaddarśanaṃ prāpya pītvā dharmāmṛtāny api 
 muditāḥ śraddhayā bhaktyā triratnaṃ saṃbhajāmahe  Rm 
 etatpuṇyaiḥ parītāṅgāḥ pariśuddhāśayā mudā 
 bhavatāṃ darśanaṃ kartuṃ bhūyaḥ prāyāmahe vayaṃ  Rm 
 tathā ca bhavatāṃ śāstaḥ kṛpādṛṣṭiprasādataḥ 
 āryadharmāmṛtaṃ pītvā saṃtuṣṭiṃ na labhāmahe  Rm 
 tad vayaṃ bhavatām evaṃ sarvadā śaraṇaṃ gatāḥ 
 satkṛtya samupāsṛtya bhaktum ichāmahe punaḥ  Rm 
 tad bhavān kṛpayāsmā kaṃ kṛtvānugraham ābhavaṃ 
 saddharmaṃ samupādiśya sarvadā trātum arhati  Rm 
 bhavatāṃ kṛpayāsmābhi duḥkhābdhiḥ parilaṃghitaḥ 
 satkāyadṛṣṭiśailaṃ ca jñānavajreṇa bhidyate  Rm 
 jñānacakṣuś ca saṃprāptaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ māyāmayaṃ bhavaṃ 
 āryamārgaś ca saṃprāptaḥ prāptā ca nirvṛtiśrutiḥ  Rm 
 dhanyā ime vayaṃ sarve yad bhavaccharaṇaṃ gatāḥ 
 āryadharmāmṛtaṃ pītvā mahānandaṃ labhāmahe  Rm 
 dhanyās te puruṣāḥ sarve ye buddhaśaraṇaṃ gatāḥ 
 sadā dharmāmṛtaṃ pītvā kārāṃ kurvanti śāsane  Rm 
 evaṃ bhavāṃ jagacchāstā sarvasatvānukampayā 
 saddharmaṃ samupādiśya tiṣṭhatu sarvadā sukhaṃ  Rm 
 iti prabhākhya sarve te devaputrāḥ pramoditāḥ 
 taṃ munīndraṃ praṇatvā ca suprasannā divaṃ yayuḥ  Rm 
 tatra sarve 'pi te devās triratnaśaraṇaṃ gatāḥ 
 prabhejire sadā smṛtvā saṃbodhipadavāṃchinaḥ  Rm 
 tataḥ prātaḥ samutthāya bhagavān so 'numoditaḥ 
 taṃ maudgalyāyanaṃ śiṣyaṃ samāmaṃtryaivam abravīt  Rm 
 sādhu maudgalya saṃvṛttaṃ saphalaṃ te kṛpāmate 
 yat tvayā prakṛtaṃ kāyaṃ vaiyāvṛttaṃ suśobhitaṃ  Rm 
 yannāmnā bhikṣaṇaṃ kṛtvā buddhapūjā kṛtā tvayā 
 te sarve devalokeṣu samutpannāḥ pratisthitāḥ  Rm 
 te sarve 'dya niśāyāṃ matsakāśaṃ samupagatāḥ 
 teṣāṃ bhadrāśayaṃ dṛṣṭvā saddharmo deśito mayā  Rm 
 tat saddharmāmṛtaṃ pītvā te sarve 'pi pramoditāḥ 
 dṛṣṭasatyāḥ prakrāntāś ca gachanti tridaśālaye  Rm 
 tatra svarge 'pi te sarve triratnaśaraṇaṃ gatāḥ 
 prabhajanti sadā nityaṃ saṃbodhiguṇavāṃchinaḥ  Rm 
 yannāmnā yat kṛtaṃ karma tat phalaṃ te prabhuṃjate 
 Rm 
 evaṃ lokahitaṃ kartuṃ karttavyaṃ puṇyasādhanaṃ  Rm 
 evaṃ lokahitaṃ kṛtvā prakurvanti śubhāni ye 
 te pumāṃso mahāsatvā bodhisatvā jinātmajāḥ  Rm 
 evaṃ vijñāya lokānāṃ hitaṃ kartuṃ samudyataḥ 
 saddharmasādhaneṣv eva caritavyaṃ samāhitaḥ  Rm 
 iti śāstrā samādiṣṭaṃ śrutvā so 'rhaṃ mahāmatiḥ 
 satyam iti pratijñāya prābhyanandat prabodhitaḥ  Rm 
 tataḥ so 'rhan mahābhijñas tac chāstrādiṣṭam ādarāt 
 tad jñātīnāṃ purogatvā sarvam evaṃ nyavedayat  Rm 
 te 'pi ca jñātayaḥ sarve tenārhatā niveditaṃ 
 śrutvā satyam iti jñātvā prāmodyaṃ pratilebhire  Rm 
 tatas te jñātayaḥ sarve triratnaśaraṇaṃ gatāḥ 
 satkṛtya śraddhayā nityaṃ prabhejire samādarāt  Rm 
 iti me guruṇādiṣṭaṃ śrutaṃ mayā narādhipa 
 lokaprabodhanārthena tava prītyā prakathyate  Rm 
 evaṃ vijñāya rājendra pretānāṃ śubhasādhanaṃ 
 triratnabhajanaṃ lokaiḥ kārayituṃ tvam arhasi  Rm 
 tathā te maṃgalaṃ nityaṃ bhaven nūnaṃ samaṃtataḥ 
 sarvasatvahitodbhutaṃ mahatpuṇyaṃ hi satphalaṃ  Rm 
 iti matvā mahārāja lokān sarvān prabodhayan 
 pratiṣṭhāpya śubhe dharme pālayasva samāhitaḥ  Rm 
 iti śāstrā samādiṣṭaṃ śrutvāśokaḥ sa bhūpatiḥ 
 tatheti pratimoditvā prābhyanandat sapārṣadaḥ  Rm 
 pretāvadānaṃ manujā idaṃ ye śṛṇvanti ye cāpi niśāmayanti 
 te sarva evaṃ pratilabdhapuṇyā bhuktvā sukhāni pracaranti loke  Rm 
  iti ratnāva dānatatve pretikāvadānaṃ samāptam 
 Rm 
 XVII Kacaṃgalāvadāna
 athāśoko mahārājaḥ pramoditaḥ 
 upaguptaṃ yatiṃ natvā punar evaṃ abhāṣata  Rm 
 bhadanta śrotum icchāmi punar anyat subhāṣitaṃ 
 tadyathā guruṇādiṣṭaṃ tathādeṣṭuṃ ca me 'rhati  Rm
