 iti saṃprārthitaṃ rājñā śrutvā so 'rhan yatiḥ sudhīḥ 
 upagupto nareṃdrāṃ taṃ samalokyaivam ādiśat  Rm 
 sādhu śṛṇu mahārāja yathā me guruṇoditaṃ 
 tathāhaṃ te pravakṣyāmi śrutvā cāpy anumodaya  Rm 
 puraikasamaye buddhaḥ sākyasiṃho munīśvaraḥ 
 sarvajñaḥ sugataḥ sāstā dharmarājo vināyakaḥ  Rm 
 śrāvastyā nikaṭe 'raṇye jetāśrame śubhālaye 
 vihāre śrāvakaiḥ sārddhaṃ bhikṣubhiś cailakair api  Rm 
 bhikṣuṇībhiḥ suśilābhir upāsikāgaṇair api 
 upāsakais tathānyaiś ca triratnaśaraṇāgataiḥ  Rm 
 bodhisatvagaṇaiś cāpi satvoddharaṇatatparaiḥ 
 vijahāra jagallokaṃ dharmāṃśubhiḥ prabhāsayan  Rm 
 tat saddharmāmṛtaṃ pātuṃ sarve lokāḥ samāgatāḥ 
 śakrādayaḥ suparvāṇabrahmādi lokapālakāḥ  Rm 
 daityā nāgāś ca gaṃdharvā yakṣakinnararākṣasāḥ 
 garuḍā vidyādharāś cāpi sarve te saṃpracerire  Rm 
 tataḥ sarve 'pi te tatra puraskṛtya samantataḥ 
 parivṛtya sasaṃghaṃ tam upatasthuḥ samāhitāḥ  Rm 
 tadā sa bhagavān dṛṣṭvā tān sarvān samupasthitān 
 ādimadhyāntakalyāṇaṃ dideśa dharmam uttamaṃ  Rm 
 tat saddharmāmṛtaṃ pītvā sarve te saṃpramoditāḥ 
 dharmaviśeṣam ājñāya prābhyanandañ chūbhāśayāḥ  Rm 
 tasminn avasare tatra vṛddhārāmodakārthinī 
 kacaṅgalābhidhā kumbhaṃ dhṛtvā kūpāntike 'carat  Rm 
 tatra tāṃ bhagavān dṛṣṭvā matvā janmāntaraprasūṃ 
 ānaṃdaṃ samupāmaṃtrya pura evam abhāṣata  Rm 
 gachānaṃda tvam etasyāṃ vṛddhāyāṃ prārthayāmṛtaṃ 
 bhagavāṃs tṛṣito mātas tad ambu dīyatām iti  Rm 
 etad bhagavatādiṣṭaṃ śrutvānaṃdas tatheti saḥ 
 sahasā samupāśritya tāṃ vṛddhām evam abravīt  Rm 
 mātar me bhagavāñ chāstā tṛṣito 'yam ihādhunā 
 tat pānīyaṃ pradatvā me mahaddharmam avāpnuhi  Rm 
 Rm 
 iti saṃprārthitaṃ tena śrutvā sā sthavirā satī 
 tam ānandaṃ samālokya muditaivam abhāṣata  Rm 
 bhadanta sādhu tatrāham amṛtapūritaṃ ghaṭaṃ 
 svayam eva samānīya dāsyāmi vrajatāṃ bhavān  Rm 
 iti tayoditaṃ śrutvā sa ānaṃdaḥ prabodhitaḥ 
 upetyaivaṃ samākhyāya śāstuḥ pura upāśrayat  Rm 
 tadā sā sahasā kṛtvā ghaṭaṃ śuddhāmbupūritaṃ 
 svayam eva samādāya tatrābhisaṃmukhācarat  Rm 
 tatra sā samupāśritya prādrākṣīt taṃ munīśvaraṃ 
 dvātriṃśallakṣaṇāśītivyaṃjanapratimaṇḍitaṃ  Rm 
 vyāmaprabhābhibhāsvaṃtaṃ śatasūryādhikaprabhaṃ 
 jaṃgamam iva ratnābhaṃ saumyaṃ samantabhadrakaṃ  Rm 
 saha taddarśaṇāt tatra putrasnehasamudbhavāḥ 
 stanābhyāṃ praśrutās tasyāḥ kṣīradhārā niraṃtaraṃ  Rm 
 tato dharmānubhāvena smṛtvā pūrvabhavātmajaṃ 
 putra putreti soktvā taṃ pariṣvektum upācarat  Rm 
 tadā te bhikṣavaḥ sarve evaṃ tāṃ samupadrutāṃ 
 dṛṣṭvaiva sahasotthāya pradhārayitum ārabhan  Rm 
 tad dṛṣṭvā bhagavāṃ chastā sarvāṃs tāṃ sāṃghikān api 
 sahasā samupāmaṃtrya punar evaṃ samādiśat  Rm 
 mā bhikṣava imāṃ vṛddhāṃ dhārāyatātra muñcata 
 paṃcajanmaśatāny eṣā mātā me bhūyataḥ purā  Rm 
 tatpūrvajanmamāteyaṃ putrasnehānubhāvinī 
 samāliṃgatum īchantī mama gātre pradhāvati  Rm 
 yady atraiṣā nivāryyete gātra me śleṣmaṇād api 
 idānīṃ rudhiraṃ hy uṣṇaṃ kamṭhād asyāḥ kṣaret kṣaṇāt  Rm 
 kṛtajñatām anusmṛtvā dṛṣṭvemāṃ putralālasāṃ 
 kāruṇyād gātrasaṃśleṣaṃ dadāmy atrānukaṃpayā  Rm 
 iti śāstrā samādiṣṭaṃ śrutvā te sarvasāṃghikāḥ 
 tāṃ śāstuḥ pūrvaprasūṃ matvā vyavatasthuḥ savismayāḥ  Rm 
 tatkṣaṇād urddhavāhuḥ sā samīkṣya taṃ munīśvaraṃ 
 sahasā saṃpradhāvitvā samāliṃgya namac ciraṃ  Rm 
 tataś cirāt samutthāya sā vṛddhā sāñjalir mudā 
 śrīghanaṃ taṃ samālokya puras tasthau samāhitā  Rm 
 tadā sa bhagavān dṛṣṭvā tāṃ puraḥ samupāsthitāṃ 
 āryyasatyaṃ samārabhya saddharmaṃ samupādiśat  Rm 
 tat saddharmāmṛtaṃ pītvā sa vṛddhāpi kacaṃgalā 
 pariśuddhāśayā bhadrā bodhicaryā prabodhitā  Rm 
 satkāyadṛṣṭibhūmīdhraṃ viṃśatiśikharodgataṃ 
 nirbhidya jñānavajreṇa dṛṣṭasatyaprabodhitā  Rm 
 saṃprāpya śrotaāpattiphalaṃ sākṣat kṛtodyamā 
 sāṃjalis taṃ muniṃ natvā gāthā imā abhāṣata  Rm 
 Rm 
 yat karttavyaṃ svaputreṇa mātur duṣkarakāriṇā 
 tat kṛtaṃ bhavatā me 'tra cittaṃ mokṣaparāyaṇaṃ  Rm 
 durgatibhyaḥ samuddhṛtya svarge mokṣaṃ ca sāṃprataṃ 
 sthāpito 'haṃ prayatnena viśeṣasaṃprabodhane  Rm 
 tathā me 'nugrahaṃ kṛtvā saṃbodhipadasādhanaṃ 
 pravrajyāsaṃvaraṃ dātum arhati sāṃprataṃ bhavān  Rm 
 bhavatāṃ śaraṇaṃ kṛtvā triratnabhajanodyatā 
 pravrajyāsaṃvaraṃ dhṛtvā cariṣye brahmacārikāṃ  Rm 
 ity arthitaṃ tayā śrutvā bhagavān sa munīśvaraḥ 
 tasyāś cittaviśuddhatvaṃ matvaivaṃ samupādiśat  Rm 
 yadi śraddhāsti te mātaḥ pravrajyāsadhane khalu 
 bharttur anujñāṃ samāsādya prāgacha cara saṃvaraṃ  Rm 
 ity ādiṣṭaṃ munīndreṇa śrutvā sā saṃpramoditā 
 tathā hīti pratijñāya muniṃ natvā tato 'carat  Rm 
 tatra sā sahasā gehe gatvā taṃ svāminaṃ mudā 
 kṛtāṃjalipuṭo natvā puraḥ sthitvaivam abravīt  Rm 
 svāmi cchṛṇv adbhutaṃ vakṣye yad adyāhaṃ jalārthinī 
 ghaṭaṃ dhṛtvā vahir deśe kūpāntikam upācare  Rm 
 tatra māṃ samupāyātāṃ dṛṣṭvānando mahāyatiḥ 
 sahasā samupāśritya bhagavate 'mbu yācate  Rm 
 tato 'haṃ sahasā śuddhaiḥ pūrayitvā jalair ghaṭaṃ 
 dhṛtvā svayaṃ pradātuṃ tat sabhāyām upasaṃcare  Rm 
 tatra tam śrīghanaṃ dṛṣṭvā cittaṃ me snehamohitaṃ 
 kṣāradhārā stanābhyāṃ ca saṃpraśrutā niraṃtaraṃ  Rm 
 tatrāhaṃ sneharāgāṃdhā svātmajam iva taṃ muniṃ 
 ūrddhavāhuḥ pariṣvaktuṃ pradhāvāmi bhavāntare  Rm 
 evaṃ mām abhidhāvantīṃ dṛṣṭvā te sāṃghikā api 
 sarve pradhātum ichantaḥ pradhāvanti samutthitāḥ  Rm 
 tadā sa bhagavān dṛṣṭvā tān sarvān evam utthitān 
 sahasā samupāmaṃtrya pura evaṃ samādiśat  Rm 
 mā imāṃ sarvathā yūyaṃ nivārayitum arhatha 
 yan mameyaṃ puṇyaṃ ca śatajanmaprasū kila  Rm 
 tad atra māṃ samālokya svātmajasneharāgiṇī 
 pariṣvaktuṃ samīchantī pradhāvatīyam unmukhī  Rm 
 yady atreṣātra dhāryyeta purato me vimūrchitā 
 uṣṇaṃ rudhiram utsṛjya mṛtyuṃ yāyān na saṃśayaḥ  Rm 
 etac chāstrā samādiṣṭaṃ śrutvā te sāṃghikās tathā 
 prabodhitāḥ praṇatvā māṃ svasvāsane samāśritāḥ  Rm 
 evaṃ tena munīndreṇa samākhyātaṃ niśamya tat 
 sarvaṃ prabudhyamānāhaṃ purāvṛttaṃ smarāmi hi  Rm 
 tato 'haṃ vismayākrāṃtahṛdayātyabhinaṃditā 
 Rm 
 tat saddharmāmṛtaṃ pātum upatiṣṭhāmi sādaraṃ  Rm 
 tatra sa bhagavān dṛṣṭvā mām evaṃ samupasthitāṃ 
 āryasatyaṃ samārabhya samādiśati sadvṛṣaṃ  Rm 
 tat saddharmāmṛtaṃ pītvā mano me 'tipramodite 
 bhūyo 'pi tad rasāsvādatṛṣitaṃ pātum ichate  Rm 
 sarve te sāṃghikās tatra saddharmāmṛtatṛptitāḥ 
 śuddhātmānaḥ subhadrāṃgāḥ pariśuddhās trimaṃḍalāḥ  Rm 
 śuddhaśīlāḥ śubhācārā dayākāruṇyabhāvinaḥ 
 sarvasattvahitādhānāḥ saṃsāralābhanispṛhāḥ  Rm 
 samādhidhāraṇīvidyā ghaṭamānāḥ samāhitāḥ 
 sākṣād arhatpadaprāptā nirvikalpā niraṃjanāḥ  Rm 
 saṃbuddhaśaraṇaṃ kṛtvā saṃbodhisādhanodyatāḥ 
 vihāre samupāsīnāḥ pradṛśyante mayā prabho  Rm 
 tat sabhāgaṃ cariṃ prāptuṃ pravrajyāvratam ichyate 
 tad atra kṛpayā bharttas tad anujñāṃ pradehi me  Rm 
 iti bhāryāsamākhyātaṃ śrutvā so 'tidaridritaḥ 
 sāścaryastambhitas tasthau paśyaṃs tām eva niścalaḥ  Rm 
 tataḥ sa suciraṃ bhāryāṃ tām evam abhilokayan 
 viyogaśaṃkayā trastaḥ śanair evam abhāṣata  Rm 
 are nāri pramūdhāsi kim evaṃ tvaṃ prabhāṣase 
 katham evaṃ tvayākhyātaṃ ko 'tra satyaṃ pratīṣyati  Rm 
 yad asau bhagavān buddhaś cakravarttinṛpātmajaḥ 
 sarvatraidhātukādhīśo dharmarājo vināyakaḥ  Rm 
 jagacchāstā jagannāthaḥ sarvajñaḥ sugato jinaḥ 
 munīndro mārajid arhan ṣaḍabhijñas tathāgataḥ  Rm 
 bodhisatvo mahāsatvaḥ samaṃtabhadrarūpakaḥ 
 daśabalo maheśākhyo brahmacārī jitendriyaḥ  Rm 
 subrahmāmaradaityādilokānāṃ sarvadehināṃ 
 śaraṇyo mānanīyo hi vandyaḥ pūjyo bhavaty api  Rm 
 tvam evaṃ durbhagā nārī daridratātiduḥkhinī 
 dāsī paravatī preṣyā kṛpaṇā duḥkṛtākṛtiḥ  Rm 
 katham evaṃvidhāyās te garbhe jāto 'py asau mahān 
 bodhicittaṃ samāsādya prācarad bodhicārikāṃ  Rm 
 yataḥ puṇyavipākena pūrya pāramitāḥ kramāt 
 adhunā bodhim āsādya saṃbuddho 'yaṃ bhavaty api  Rm 
 etatpuṇyavibhāgena kathaṃ te īdṛśī gatiḥ 
 adyāpīdṛgavasthā hi kiṃ cit saukhyaṃ na vidyate  Rm 
 tad atra mā vadaivaṃ ca tathoktvā naiva śobhase 
 kas tavaitad vacaḥ śrutvā supratītaḥ pramāṇayet  Rm 
 dhik pravādāgnidagdhāṅgā mahatkaṣṭābhikhedītā 
 vamitvā rudhiraṃ hy uṣṇaṃ tvaṃ nūnaṃ maraṇaṃ vrajeḥ  Rm 
 mithyāvādābhisaṃkalpād api hi narake vrajet 
 tvam api ca tathā nūnaṃ narake na vrajeḥ kathaṃ  Rm 
 Rm 
 narakeṣu sadā nityaṃ duḥkhāni vividhāni vai 
 bhuktvātivedanākrāntā suciraṃ sthāsyase dhruvaṃ  Rm 
 iti bharttroditaṃ śrutvā sā vṛddhā strī kacaṃgalā 
 vibhinnahṛdayā tasthau tan nirāśābhimohitā  Rm 
 tadā sā sucireṇaiva saṃprāpya cetanāṃ tataḥ 
 bharttāraṃ taṃ punar dṛṣṭvā bodhayitum abhāṣata  Rm 
 svāminn atra prasīda tvaṃ mām evaṃ vada sarvathā 
 satyam etan mayā proktaṃ na mithyeti prakalpaya  Rm 
 yadi mithyāvacaḥ syān me tenāhaṃ narake vraje 
 atha me vacanaṃ satyam atrāhaṃ sadgatiṃ vraje  Rm 
 tenātrobhayathāpy eva viyogaṃ nau bhavet khalu 
 sarveṣām api jaṃtūnām avaśyaṃ maraṇaṃ bhave  Rm 
 kim evaṃ jīvitenāpi kevalaṃ duḥkhabhāginā 
 yatra na vidyate dharmmaṃ tatra kiṃ sukhatāpi ca  Rm 
 dharmārtham eva saṃsāre janmadehārthasādhanaṃ 
 dharmaṃ vinā kim etair naḥ kevalaṃ duḥkhatāptaye  Rm 
 iti matvā mahānto 'pi śrīmanto 'pi vicakṣaṇāḥ 
 sarvān parigrahān tyaktvā pravrajanti jināśrame  Rm 
 tathātrāhaṃ parijñāya saṃbuddhaśaraṇaṃ gatā 
 saddharmasādhanaṃ karttum ichāmi sāṃprataṃ prabho  Rm 
 tat pravrajyāvratānujñāṃ pradātuṃ me samarhasi 
 etatpuṇyavibhāgena tvaṃ cāpi sadgatiṃ vrajeḥ  Rm 
 yadi na dīyate 'nujñā pravrajyāvratasādhane 
 akasmāt mṛtyunāghrāte tadā kathaṃ nivāraye  Rm 
 kiyat kālaṃ ca jīveyaṃ vṛddhāhaṃ jirṇitendriyā 
 iti matvātra māṃ naivaṃ nivārayitum arhasi  Rm 
 kiṃ cāhaṃ jaratī vṛddhā tat te kiṃ snehatā mayi 
 vṛddhayā durbalāṅgātra kārye kiṃ nu prayojanaṃ  Rm 
 tvaṃ cāpi jarayākrānto vṛddho 'si durbalendriyaḥ 
 tat kiṃ te sneharāgeṇa vṛddhāyā mayi sāṃprataṃ  Rm 
 adyāpi kiṃ sukhāśā nau jarākrāntaśarīrayoḥ 
 avaśyaṃ mṛtyur atrāvāṃ samākramya grasiṣyati  Rm 
 tadāhaṃ kiṃ kariṣyāmi tvaṃ cāpi kiṃ kariṣyasi 
 śocitveva niṣatsyāmi tvam apy evaṃ niṣatsyasi  Rm 
 avaśyam atra saṃsāre bhāvi bhāvā phalanty api 
 kasyāpi bhūyate nātra bhāvi bhāvānyathā kvacit  Rm 
 svakṛtakarma evātra gṛhītvā sarvajaṃtavaḥ 
 yātā yānti ca yāsyaṃti dehaṃ tyaktvā yamālayaṃ  Rm 
 tatra yamājñayā sarve svakṛtakarmabhāginaḥ 
 dharmiṇaḥ sadgatiṃ yātāḥ pāpino durgatiṃ gatāḥ  Rm 
 evaṃ sarve ime satvāḥ svadaivaphalabhoginaḥ 
 sasukhāni ca duḥkhāni bhuktvā bhramanti sarvadā  Rm 
 Rm 
 evaṃ svāmin parijñāya sarvadā sukhavāṃchibhiḥ 
 dharmam evātra saṃsāre karttavyaṃ yatnataḥ sadā  Rm 
 dharman tu pravaraṃ śreṣṭhaṃ saugatasaṃvarodbhavaṃ 
 iti buddhaiḥ samākhyātaṃ tvayāpy etac chrutaṃ na kiṃ  Rm 
 tasmād ahaṃ munīndrasya śāsane śaraṇaṃ gataḥ 
 pravrajyāsaṃvaraṃ dharttum ichāmi sāṃprataṃ prabho  Rm 
 etatpuṇyavipākena pariśuddhās trimaṇḍalāḥ 
 sākṣād arhatpadaṃ prāpya nirvṛtipadam āpnuyāṃ  Rm 
 etad dharmavibhāgena tvaṃ cāpi sadgatiṃ vrajeḥ 
 iti matvā tathā svāmiṃs tad anujñāṃ dadātu me  Rm 
 tvam atra svagṛhe sthitvā triratnaśaraṇaṃ gataḥ 
 yāvaj jīvaṃ sukhaṃ bhuktvā śubhe cara sadādarāt  Rm 
 etatpuṇyavipākena tvaṃ cāpy evaṃ sudhīr bhaveḥ 
 tatas te saugate dharme vāṃchā jāyeta cetasi  Rm 
 tatas tvaṃ śraddhayā gatvā saṃbuddhaśāsane svayaṃ 
 pravrajyāsaṃvaraṃ prāpya sākṣād arhatvam āpnuyāḥ  Rm 
 iti matvā bhavān svāmin saddharmaṃ yadi vāñchati 
 tat pravrajyāvratānujñāṃ mahyaṃ pradātum arhati  Rm 
 iti tayoditaṃ śrutvā sa daridraḥ prabodhitaḥ 
 tāṃ bhāryāṃ suciraṃ dṛṣṭvā śanair evam abhāṣata  Rm 
 hā priye katham eva tvaṃ māṃ vihātuṃ samichasi 
 kim atrāhaṃ vadiṣyāmi tvayaivaṃ pratibhāṣate  Rm 
 yadi te 'sti mano dhairyyaṃ kṛtvā śraddhānvitāśrayā 
 pravraja saṃvaraṃ dhṛtvā cara satyasamāhitā  Rm 
 iti bhartroditaṃ śrutvā sā vṛddhāpi kacaṃgalā 
 bharttāraṃ taṃ praṇatvaivaṃ tato 'carat pramoditā  Rm 
 tataḥ sā sahasā gatvā tatrāśrame upāgatā 
 śrīghanaṃ taṃ samālokya purataḥ samupācarat  Rm 
 tatra tat purato gatvā sāñjaliḥ sā pramoditā 
 munīndraṃ taṃ praṇatvaivaṃ pravrajyāṃ samayācata  Rm 
 bhagavan nātha sarvajña bhavatāṃ śaraṇaṃ vraje 
 tad bhavāṃ kṛtvā kṛpayā mahyaṃ pravrajyāṃ dātum arhati  Rm 
 tayeti prārthitaṃ śrutvā bhagavān sa munīśvaraḥ 
 savyena pāṇinā tasyā vṛddhāyāḥ śirasi spṛśan  Rm 
 ehi mataś cara brahmacārikāṃ tvaṃ samāhitā 
 ity uktvā tāṃ samāgṛhya sāṃghike punar abravīt  Rm 
 gacha māta prajāpatyā gautamyāḥ śaraṇaṃ vraja 
 sārhantī bhikṣuṇīmātā pravrajyāṃ te pradāsyati  Rm 
 ity ādiṣṭaṃ munīndreṇa śrutvā sā pratinaṃditā 
 tathety āśrutya śāstāraṃ taṃ praṇatvā tato 'carat  Rm 
 tatra sā samupāsṛtya dṛṣṭvā tāṃ gautamīṃ mudā 
 Rm 
 upetya sāṃjalir natvā pravrajyāṃ samayācata  Rm 
 mātar atra samāyāmi bhavatyāḥ śaraṇaṃ mudā 
 tad bhavantī jaganmātā pravrajyāṃ pradadātu me  Rm 
 tayeti prārthitaṃ śrutvā gautamī sānumoditā 
 hastena śirasi spṛṣṭvā sāṃghikatāṃ samagrahīt  Rm 
 tatra sāśu prajāpatyāṃ pravrajitā yathāvidhiḥ 
 muṇḍitā khikkhirīpātrahastā kākhāyacīvarā  Rm 
 saumyendriyā subhadraṃgā vṛddhāpi sā kacaṃgalā 
 bhikṣuṇīgaṇamadhyasthā śāntarūpātyaśobhata  Rm 
 tataḥ sā bhikṣuṇī śāstu gautamyāś ca prasādataḥ 
 samādhidhāraṇīvidyādhyayanābhisamudyatā  Rm 
 hitvāvidyāgaṇaṃ prāptavidyābhijñāviśāradā 
 pratisaṃvidguṇādyāgu pariśuddhākṛtir vabhau  Rm 
 atha sā parivijñāya bhavacakraṃ calācalaṃ 
 viditvā saṃskāragatīś cābhivighātinīs tataḥ  Rm 
 sarvakleśagaṇāṃ jitvā pariśuddhas trimaṇḍalā 
 sākṣād arhatpadaṃ prāpya vabhūva brahmacāriṇī  Rm 
 tadā sā nirjitakleśā nirvikalpā niraṃjanā 
 caṃdanakalpasaurabhyā samaloṣṭhasuvarṇikā  Rm 
 saṃsārabhogasatkāraniṣpṛhākāśasannibhā 
 sarvasatvahitādhānā sarvasūtrāṃtapāragā  Rm 
 sadevāsuralokānāṃ tridhātukanivāsināṃ 
 vaṃdyā pūjyābhimānyā ca vabhūva sā subhāṣiṇī  Rm 
 yadā sa bhagavañ chāstā bhikṣuṇīnāṃ subhāṣitaṃ 
 saṃkṣepeṇa samuddiśya dhyānāgāre samāśrayat  Rm 
 tadā sā bhikṣuṇī tatra kacaṃgalā subhāṣiṇī 
 bhikṣuṇīnāṃ sabhāmadhye sutrāntaṃ samupādiśat  Rm 
 tac chrutvā bhagavāṃs tatra tayā sūtrāṃtadeśite 
 sarvāns tān sāṃghikān bhikṣūn samāmaṃtryaivam ādiśat  Rm 
 eṣo 'grā bhikṣavo mātā bhikṣuṇīnāṃ mamāśrame 
 sūtrāntabhāgakartṝṇāṃ yad uteyaṃ kacaṃgalā  Rm 
 ity ādiṣṭaṃ munīndreṇa śrutvā sarve 'pi sāṃghikāḥ 
 savismayā munīndraṃ taṃ paprachus tat purākṛtaṃ  Rm 
 bhagavann anayā karmaṃ kiṃ prakṛtaṃ purākṛtaṃ 
 imān sarvān sabhāsīnān prabodhayitum arhati  Rm 
 yeneyam śāsane bauddhe vṛddhā pravrajitādhunā 
 sākṣād arhatvam āsādya bhavati brahmacāriṇī  Rm 
 kiṃ vānayā purākarma kṛtaṃ kutra kadā kathaṃ 
 sūtrāntabhāgakartṝṇāṃ yenāgreyaṃ bhavaty api  Rm 
 kiṃcāpi prakṛtaṃ karmaṃ purānayā kadā kathaṃ 
 yenātra paścime garbhāvāse na dhārito bhavān  Rm 
 etat sarvaiḥ parijñāya bhagavānn asyāḥ purākṛtaṃ 
 imān sarvān sabhāsīnān prabodhayitum arhati  Rm 
 Rm 
 iti tair bhikṣubhiḥ sarvaiḥ prārthite sa munīśvaraḥ 
 sarvāṃs tān sāṃghikān dṛṣṭvā samāmaṃtryaivam ādiśat  Rm 
 śṛṇuta bhikṣavaḥ sarve yad yat kṛtaṃ purānayā 
 tat tat sarvaṃ pravakṣyāmi yuṣmākaṃ cittabodhane  Rm 
 purā me bodhisatvasya bodhicaryānucāriṇaḥ 
 paṃcajanmaśatāny eṣā janany āsīn niraṃtaraṃ  Rm 
 tadā me dadato dānam antarāyaḥ kṛto 'nayā 
 tenādyāpi daridreyaṃ durbhagā ca bhavaty api  Rm 
 pravrajyāyai tadai caiṣā vahudhā prārthitā mayā 
 naivānujñāṃ dadau mahyaṃ vighnam eva vyadhād dhaṭhāt  Rm 
 etatkarmavipākena vṛddhaiṣā duḥkhinī satī 
 pravrajyāsaṃvaraṃ prāptā carati mama śāsane  Rm 
 yadi naiṣā tadā dānaṃ vighnā mamākariṣyati 
 naiṣādhunā daridrātra bhavati hi kadā cana  Rm 
 pravrajyāyāṃ ca me vighnaṃ yadi naiṣākariṣyata 
 acariṣyad vrataṃ vālye na tu vṛddhātra sāṃprataṃ  Rm 
 yan mamaivaṃ kṛtaṃ vighnaṃ dāne vrate tadānayā 
 tenādhunā daridraiṣā vṛddhā vrataṃ caraty api  Rm 
 yat tadā sukṛtaṃ kiṃ cit prakṛtaṃ nānayā purā 
 tenāhaṃ paścime garbhāvāse 'dhunā na dhāritaḥ  Rm 
 yat sā māyā mahādevī mahāpuṇyārthasādhinī 
 tenāhaṃ paścime garbhāvāse tayātra dhāritaḥ  Rm 
 bhūyo 'py eṣā purā tatra vāraṇasyāṃ dvijātmajāḥ 
 kleśāgniparidagdhāṃgā daridrā kṛpaṇābhavat  Rm 
 tadā tatra munīndrasya kāśyapasya jagadguroḥ 
 śāsane śaraṇaṃ gatvā pravrajitācarad vrataṃ  Rm 
 tatra sa sarvaśāstrārthakovidātivicakṣaṇā 
 sarvasūtrāntasaddharmaṃ bhikṣuṇīnām upādiśat  Rm 
 tadā sā bhikṣuṇī tatra kiñcit kāryārtharoṣitāḥ 
 sarvās tā bhikṣuṇīr dāsīvādena paryabhāṣata  Rm 
 etatkarmavipākena saiṣādhunātiduḥkhitā 
 parasevākarā dāsī bhavati durbhagākṛtiḥ  Rm 
 yac cānayā tadā tatra vidyābhyāsīkṛtaṃ mudā 
 tenaiṣā sahasārhantī bhavati brahmacāriṇī  Rm 
 yac cāpy esā tadā tatra sūtrāntaṃ samupādiśat 
 tena sūtrāntavaktānām agrā bhavati sāṃprataṃ  Rm 
 evaṃ hi bhikṣavaḥ sarve manyadhvaṃ karmasaṃbhavaṃ 
 sukhaṃ duḥkhaṃ ca saṃsāre bhramatāṃ sarvadehināṃ  Rm 
 yenaiva yat kṛtaṃ karmaṃ tenaivaṃ bhujyate phalaṃ 
 abhuktaṃ kṣīyate naiva karmaṃ kvāpi kadā cana  Rm 
 nāgnibhir dahyate karmaṃ klidyate nodakair api 
 vāyubhiḥ śuṣyate naiva kṣīyate na ca bhūmiṣu  Rm 
 Rm 
 ahyathāpi bhaven naiva vipāke karmaṇaḥ phalaṃ 
 yad uptaṃ bhūtale bījaṃ tad eva sūyate phalaṃ  Rm 
 anyathā na bhavet kvāpi kṛtaṃ karmaṃ phalaṃ bhave 
 śubhasya karmaṇaḥ pāke śubhataiva sadā bhave  Rm 
 kṛṣṇasya kṛṣṇataiva syā miśritasyāpi miśritaṃ 
 evaṃ vijñāya kṛṣṇāni vihāya miśritāni ca  Rm 
 śubha eva sadāpy atra caritavyaṃ śubhārthibhiḥ 
 śubhena sadgatiṃ yāyāt kṛṣṇena durgatiṃ sadā  Rm 
 miśritena tathohe ca gatīr yāyād bhaved dhruvaṃ 
 iti matvātra saṃsāre sarvadā śubhavāñchibhiḥ 
 triratnabhajanaṃ kṛtvā caritavyaṃ śubhe sadā  Rm 
 ye bhajanti sadā buddhaṃ na te gacchanti durgatiṃ 
 sarvadā sadgatau bhadraṃ kṛtvā yānti jinālayaṃ  Rm 
 ye śṛṇvanti sadā dharmmaṃ na yānti te 'pi durgatiṃ 
 sarvadā bhadrasaukhyāni bhuktvā yānti sukhāvatīṃ  Rm 
 dānaṃ dadanti ye saṃghe te 'pi na yānti durgatiṃ 
 sarvadā śubhasaukhyāni bhuktvā yānti jināśrayaṃ  Rm 
 evaṃ matvātra saṃsāre triratnaṃ śaraṇaṃ gatāḥ 
 satkṛtya śraddhayā nityaṃ bhajadhvaṃ samupāsthitāḥ  Rm 
 triratneṣu kṛtaṃ karmaṃ tadvipāke mahatphalaṃ 
 aprameyam asaṃkhyeyaṃ saṃbodhipadasādhanaṃ  Rm 
 etatpuṇyānubhāvena bodhisatvāḥ sadā bhave 
 sarvasatvahitaṃ kṛtvā pracaranti yathechayā  Rm 
 nānārūpadharāḥ sarve satvārthasādhanodyatāḥ 
 saddharmaṃ samupādiśya pālayanti jagattrayaṃ  Rm 
 kramāt pāramitāḥ sarvāḥ paripūrya śubhānvitāḥ 
 sarvakleśagaṇāñ jitvā pariśuddhās trimaṇḍalāḥ  Rm 
 jitvā māragaṇāñ cāpi prāpya saṃbodhim uttamāṃ 
 sarvatra dharmasotkṛtvā tato nirvṛtim āyayuḥ  Rm 
 ye 'tītā jinās te 'pi triratnabhajanodyamāt 
 kramād bodhiṃ samāsādya nirvṛtipadam āgatāḥ  Rm 
 varttamānā jinās te 'pi triratnabhajanodbhavaiḥ 
 puṇyair bodhiṃ samāsādya gacheyur nirvṛtiṃ tathā  Rm 
 anāgatā jinās te 'pi triratnabhajanodbhavaiḥ 
 puṇyair evaṃ kramād bodhiṃ prāpya yāsyanti nirvṛtiṃ  Rm 
 ahaṃ cāpi tathā nūnaṃ triratnabhajanodyamī 
 etatpuṇyānubhāvena bodhiṃ prāpnomi sāṃprataṃ  Rm 
 tathāham api sarvatra kṛtvā dharmamayaṃ jagat 
 sarvān bodhau niyojyaivaṃ yāsyāmi nirvṛtiṃ dhruvaṃ  Rm 
 evaṃ ye ye bhajanty atra triratnaśaraṇaṃ gatāḥ 
 te te sarve 'pi saṃbodhiṃ prāpya nirvṛtim āyayuḥ  Rm 
 Rm 
 iti matvātra saṃsāre nirvṛtipadavāṃchinaḥ 
 triratnabhajanaṃ kṛtvā pracaradhvaṃ śubhe sadā  Rm 
 tathā kṛtvātra saddharmaṃbhuktvaiva satsukhāny api 
 kramād bodhiṃ samāsādya nirvṛtiṃ samavāpsyatha  Rm 
 ity ādiṣṭaṃ munīndreṇa śrutvā sarve 'pi te janāḥ 
 sāṃghikāś ca tathety uktvā prābhyanaṃdat prabodhitāḥ  Rm 
 tadā tatra janāḥ sarve triratnaśaraṇaṃ gatāḥ 
 satkṛtya śraddhayā nityaṃ prabhejire 'numoditāḥ  Rm 
 etatpuṇyānubhāvais tu tadā samaṃtataḥ 
 sarvadā maṃgalotsāhaṃ babhuva nirupadravaṃ  Rm 
 iti me guruṇākhyātaṃ śrutaṃ mayā tathocyate 
 śrutvā rājans tvam apy evaṃ triratnaṃ bhaja sarvadā  Rm 
 prajāś cāpi tathā dharmaṃ śrāvayitvā prabodhayan 
 triratnabhajanaṃ nityaṃ kārayituṃ sadārhasi  Rm 
 tathā te maṃgalaṃ nityaṃ sarvatrāpi bhaved dhruvaṃ 
 kramāt pāramitā pūrya bodhiṃ cāpi samāpsyasi  Rm 
 iti tenārhatādiṣṭaṃ śrutvāśokaḥ sa bhūpatiḥ 
 tathā hīti pratijñāya prābhyanandan sapārṣadaḥ  Rm 
 kacaṃgalāyā avadānam etac chṛṇvanti ye śrāvayatīha yaś ca 
 vihāya pāpaṃ khalu te 'pi sarve bhuktvā sukhāny eva sugatiṃ vrajanti  Rm 
  iti ratnamālāyām avadānatatve kacaṃgalāvadānaṃ samāptam 
 Rm 
 XVIII Dhanikāvadāna
 athāśoko mahīpālaḥ kṛtāṃjalipuṭo mudā 
 upaguptaṃ guruṃ natvā punar evaṃ samabravīt  Rm 
 bhadanta śrotum icchāmi punar anyat subhāṣitaṃ 
 tadyathā guruṇādiṣṭaṃ tathādeṣṭuṃ ca me 'rhati  Rm 
 iti saṃprārthitaṃ rājñā śrutvā so 'rhan sudhīr yatiḥ 
 upagupto narendraṃ taṃ samālokyaivam abravīt  Rm 
 śṛṇu rājan samādhāya yathā me guruṇoditaṃ 
 tathāhaṃ saṃpravakṣyāmi tava puṇyapravṛddhaye  Rm 
 puraikasamaye sa śrīśākyasiṃho munīśvaraḥ 
 sarvajñaḥ sugataḥ śāstā dharmarājo vināyakaḥ  Rm 
 bhikṣubhiḥ śrāvakaiḥ sārddhaṃ bhikṣuṇībhiś ca cailakaiḥ 
 upāsakai mahāśrāddhair upāsikāgaṇair api  Rm 
 bodhisatvagaṇaiś cāpi mahāsatvaiḥ śubhārthibhiḥ 
 sarvasatvahitārthāya bodhicaryāṃ prakāśibhiḥ  Rm 
 vṛjiṣu puri vaiśālyāṃ markaṭākhyahradāntike 
 kūṭāgāraguhāvāse vijahāra prabhāsayan  Rm 
 tat saddharmāmṛtaṃ pātuṃ tatra sarve samāgatāḥ 
 brahmaśakrādidevendrā lokapālā digāsthitāḥ  Rm 
 grahāḥ siddhagaṇāḥ sādhyā yakṣagaṃdharvakinnarāḥ 
 garuḍā nāgarājāś ca vidyādharāś ca dānavāḥ  Rm 
 rākṣasāḥ sagaṇāś caiva ṛṣayo brahmacāriṇaḥ 
 brahmaṇāḥ kṣatriyā bhūpā rājāno 'pi narādhipāḥ  Rm 
 tathā rājakumārāś ca vaiśyā maṃtrijanā api 
 gṛhasthāḥ śreṣṭhinaḥ paurāḥ sārthavāhā mahājanāḥ  Rm 
 vaṇijaḥ śilpinaś cāpi tathānye 'pi śubhārthinaḥ 
 grāmyā jānapadāś cāpi tathā kārpaṭikā api  Rm 
 evam anye 'pi lokāś ca saddharmāmṛtavāṃchinaḥ 
 sarve te samupāyātās tatrādrākṣus tam īśvaraṃ  Rm 
 sabhāmadhyāsanāsīnaṃ sarvasaṃghapuraskṛtaṃ 
 śrīghanaṃ taṃ samālokya sarve te samupāśritāḥ  Rm 
 natvā pradakṣiṇīkṛtya samabhyarcya yathākramaṃ 
 punaḥ sāñjalayo natvā parivṛtya samaṃtataḥ 
 tat saddharmāmṛtaṃ pātum upatasthuḥ samāhitāḥ  Rm 
 tadā sa bhagavān dṛṣṭvā tān sarvān samupasthitān 
 ādimadhyāntakalyāṇīṃ bodhicaryāṃ samādiśat  Rm 
 Rm 
 tadāryadharmam ākarṇya sarve lokāḥ pramoditāḥ 
 tadā te dharmavaiśeṣyaṃ matvā pratinanaṃdire  Rm 
 tadā tatra mahāpūryyāṃ vaiśālyāṃ pauriko mahān 
 gṛhastho dhaniko nāma śrīmān sarvaguṇī sudhīḥ  Rm 
 śrāddho bhadrāśayo dātā śuddhaśīlo vicakṣaṇaḥ 
 sarvasatvahitādhānād āsīt satpuruṣottamaḥ  Rm 
 patnī dharmasakhī tasya śīlavatyabhidhābhavat 
 tanayaś ca vaṃdānyākhyaḥ satyavatyabhidhā snuṣā  Rm 
 tadā tatra dvijā sarve bhaktimanto jagadguroḥ 
 pūjānimaṃtraṇe cakruḥ samayaṃ saṃmatās tathā  Rm 
 bhavanto yan munīndro 'yam atrāsmākaṃ hitechayā 
 saddharmaṃ samupādeṣṭuṃ sasaṃghaḥ samupāgataḥ  Rm 
 tad asmābhir munīndro 'yaṃ pūjanīyaṃ samādarāt 
 ato nimaṃtraṇīyo 'tra sarvaiḥ saṃbhūya nānyathā  Rm 
 ekaś cet kurute dravyamadād asya nimaṃtraṇaṃ 
 sarvair nirvāsanīyo 'sau yato 'nyadharmavighnakṛt  Rm 
 tadā sa dhaniko 'jñātvā samayaṃ tais tathā kṛtaṃ 
 svayam eva munīndraṃ taṃ pūjayituṃ samichata  Rm 
 tataḥ sa dhanikaḥ śrīmān divyasaṃpatsamṛddhimān 
 svayaṃ nimaṃtraṇaṃ karttuṃ sasaṃghasya muner yayau  Rm 
 tatra sa samupāsṛtya natvā taṃ śrīghanaṃ mudā 
 sasaṃghaṃ tat puraḥ sthitvā prārthayad eva sāṃjaliḥ  Rm 
 bhagavan nātha sarvajña bhagavaṃtaṃ sasāṃghikaṃ 
 pūjayituṃ samichāmi paśyan me 'nugrahaṃ kuru  Rm 
 iti saṃprārthitaṃ tena bhagavān sa munīśvaraḥ 
 tathā hīti pratiśrutvā tūṣṇībhūtvādhyuvāsa tat  Rm 
 tadā te brāhmaṇāḥ sarve saṃbhūya samupāgatāḥ 
 bhagavataś caraṇau natvā cakrur bhojyanimaṃtraṇaṃ  Rm 
 tac chrutvā bhagavān prāha tān dṛṣṭvā bhaktimānasān 
 pūrvam eva sasaṃghāham anenodya nimaṃtritaḥ  Rm 
 etad ākarṇya sarve te brāhmaṇā bheditāśayāḥ 
 paraṃ pratīkṣyamānāś ca śanaiḥ svasvagṛhaṃ yayuḥ  Rm 
 tataḥ sa dhaniko matvā munīndreṇādhyuvāsitaṃ 
 muditas taṃ muniṃ natvā sahasā svagṛhaṃ yayau  Rm 
 tatra sa svagṛhe gatvā vāṃdhaveṣṭajanais saha 
 tadarhabhojyasāmagrīṃ sahasā samasādhyayat  Rm 
 tato bhojyasthalaṃ tatra śodhayitvā samantataḥ 
 ratnadhvajair vitānaiś ca sa patākair amaṇḍayat  Rm 
 tato yathākramaṃ tatra divyaratnamayāni ca 
 svāsanāni samāstīryya sugaṃdhīḥ samadhūpayat  Rm 
 Rm 
 tataḥ sa prātar utthāya snātvā śuddhāmvarāvṛtaḥ 
 pūjāpādyārghasāmagrīṃ pratiṣṭhāpya pramoditaḥ  Rm 
 savāṃdhaveṣṭajanas tatra kūṭāgāre samācarat 
 sāñjalis taṃ muniṃ natvā prārthayad evam ādarāt  Rm 
 bhagavan nātha sarvajña samayo varttate 'dhunā 
 tat sasaṃgho mamāvāse vijayituṃ samarhasi  Rm 
 iti saṃprārthite tena bhagavān sa sasāṃghikaḥ 
 khikkhirīpātram ādāya pratasthe cīvarāvṛtaḥ  Rm 
 tatra sa bhagavān mārge kṛtvā bhadraṃ samantataḥ 
 prabhāsayan krameṇaivaṃ vaiśālyāṃ samupaviśat  Rm 
 tathāyātaṃ munīndraṃ taṃ śrīghanaṃ sāṃghikānvitaṃ 
 dṛṣṭvā vaiśālikāḥ lokāḥ sarve 'pi samapūjayan  Rm 
 evam abhyarcyamāno 'bhivaṃdyamāno 'bhinaṃditaḥ 
 bhāsayan bhadratāṃ kṛtvā saṃghaiḥ saha samācarat  Rm 
 tatra tasya gṛhe gatvā sasaṃghaḥ sa munīśvaraḥ 
 tad dattaṃ pādyam ādāya svāsane samupāśrayat  Rm 
 tatas te sāṃghikāś cāpi sarve tatra yathākramaṃ 
 tad dattaṃ pādyam ādāya svasvāsane samāśrayan  Rm 
 tataḥ sa dhaniko dṛṣṭvā sasaṃghaṃ taṃ munīśvaraṃ 
 svasvāsane samāsīnaṃ pūjāṅgaiḥ samapūjayat  Rm 
 tato divyopacārais taṃ bhagavantaṃ sasāṃghikaṃ 
 supraṇītai rasopetair bhojanaiḥ samatoṣayat  Rm 
 tadbhojyaṃ surasaṃ bhuktvā bhagavān sa sasāṃghikaḥ 
 amṛtair iva saṃtuṣṭas tṛptiṃ yayau pramoditaḥ  Rm 
 asaṃghaiḥ taṃ muniṃ tṛptaṃ dṛṣṭvā sa dhaniko mudā 
 tato 'panīya pātrāṇi taddhastādīny aśodhayat  Rm 
 tataḥ śuddhauṣadhīpūgatāmvūlādi rasāyanaṃ 
 buddhapramukhasaṃghebhyo muditaḥ sa svayaṃ dadau  Rm 
 tataḥ sa harṣito natvā taṃ munīndraṃ sasāṃghikaṃ 
 purataḥ sāñjaliḥ sthitvā prārthayad evam ādarāt  Rm 
 bhagavan nātha sarvajña bhavatāṃ śaraṇaṃ gataḥ 
 bhaktyaiva bhajanaṃ kurve tat kṣamasvāparādhatāṃ  Rm 
 sadaivaṃ kṛpayā dṛṣṭya paśyan bhavān sasāṃghikaḥ 
 mamānugraham ādhāya trātum arhati sarvathā  Rm 
 tataḥ sa bhagavāñ chāstā sasāṃghiko 'numoditaḥ 
 dhanikaṃ taṃ samālokya naṃdayann evam ādiśat  Rm 
 gṛhapate sadā nityam ārogyam astu vo dhruvaṃ 
 bodhipraṇidhisiddhiś ca bhūyād bhadraṃ ca sarvadā  Rm 
 tatas tasya priyā bhāryā śīlavaty anumoditā 
 sāñjaliḥ praṇatiṃ kṛtvā prārthayat taṃ munīśvaraṃ  Rm 
 bhagavan nātha sarvajña śvaś cātra bhavatām ahaṃ 
 Rm 
 pūjāṃ kartuṃ samicche tad anugrahītum arhati  Rm 
 tayeti prārthite dṛṣṭvā bhagavān sa tad āśayaṃ 
 śraddhānvitaṃ pratijñāya tuṣṇībhūtvādhyuvāsa tat  Rm 
 tataḥ sa bhagavāñ chāstā samutthāya sasāṃghikaḥ 
 bhāsayaṃ bhadratāṃ kṛtvā svāśrame ca samāśrayat  Rm 
 tataḥ paradine prātaḥ snātvā śuddhāṃvarāvṛtā 
 sādhitvā sarvasāmagrīṃ sā dūtaṃ preṣayan munau  Rm 
 sa dūtaḥ sahasā gatvā vihare taṃ munīśvaraṃ 
 sasaṃghaṃ sāṃjalir natvā punar evaṃ nyavedayat  Rm 
 bhagavan nātha sarvajña samayo varttate 'dhunā 
 tat sasaṃgho bhavāṃs tatra sahasāgantum arhati  Rm 
 tataḥ sa bhagavānn evaṃ bhadraṃ kṛtvā sasāṃghikaḥ 
 dhanikasya gṛhe gatvā pādyaṃ gṛhyāsane 'viśat  Rm 
 tatrāsane samāsīnaṃ sasaṃghaṃ taṃ munīśvaraṃ 
 dṛṣṭvā śīlavatī sātha yathāvidhi samarcayat  Rm 
 tataś ca sā muditā sarvaṃ saṃghaṃ buddhādikaṃ tathā 
 divyopacārasaṃyuktair bhojanaiḥ samatoṣayat  Rm 
 tataḥ saṃtarppitaṃ dṛṣṭvā śodhayitvā karādikaṃ 
 datvā tāmvurapūgādiṃ natvā sā samupāśrayat  Rm 
 tataḥ sa bhagavān tasmai datvāśiṣaṃ sasāṃghikaḥ 
 samutthāya tataś caivaṃ svavihāre samāśrayat  Rm 
 tathā sarve tadānyo 'pi dhanikasyātmajaḥ sudhīḥ 
 tat paredyu vihāraṃ taṃ gatvā natvā nyamaṃtrayat  Rm 
 bhagavānn api tasyaivaṃ dṛṣṭvā śraddhānvitaṃ manaḥ 
 tatheti pratimoditvā tūṣṇībhūtvādhyuvāsa ca  Rm 
 tataḥ sas taṃ muniṃ natvā svagṛhaṃ sahasāgataḥ 
 bāṃdhavaiḥ sarvasāmagrīṃ muditaḥ samasādhayat  Rm 
 tataḥ prātaḥ samutthāya snātvā śuddhāmvārāvṛtaḥ 
 vihāre samupāsṛtya natvaivaṃ munim abravīt  Rm 
 bhagavan nātha sarvajña samayo varttate 'dhunā 
 tat saṃgho bhavān gehe mamāgantuṃ samarhati  Rm 
 tataḥ sasaṃgha utthāya bhagavān sa tathācarat 
 tadgṛhe pādyam ādāya tatrāsane samāśrayat  Rm 
 tataḥ sa mudito buddhapramukbaṃ sarvasāṃghikaṃ 
 samabhyarcya tathā divyabhojanaiḥ samatoṣayat  Rm 
 tato 'panīya pātrāṇi śodhayitvā karādikaṃ 
 datvā pūgādikaṃ natvā purataḥ samupāśrayat  Rm 
 punaḥ sa sāṃjalir natvā prakṛtvā ca kṣamārthanāṃ 
 sasaṃghaṃ taṃ munīndraṃ tam saṃdṛṣṭvaivaṃ samupāśrayat  Rm 
 tadā tasya snuṣā cāpi satyavatī pramoditā 
 bhagavaṃtaṃ sasaṃghaṃ taṃ praṇatvaivaṃ nyamaṃtrayat  Rm 
 Rm 
 bhagavānn api tasyāś ca dṛṣṭva śraddhānvitaṃ manaḥ 
 tatheti pratimoditvā tuṣṇībhūtvā radhāṃ vyadhāt  Rm 
 tataḥ sa bhagavāṃs tasmai datvāśiṣaṃ sasāṃghikaḥ 
 tathā kṛtvā śubhaṃ loke gatvāśrame samāśrayat  Rm 
 tataḥ sāpi tathā prātaḥ snātvā śuddhāmvarāvṛtā 
 dūtenāpi munīndraṃ taṃ sasaṃghaṃ samacodayat  Rm 
 tathā sa bhagavāṃś cāpi sasāṃghikaḥ samutthitaḥ 
 pracaran bhadratāṃ kṛtvā tasyā gehe samāviśat  Rm 
 tatra pādyārgham ādāya bhagavān sa sasāṃghikaḥ 
 śubhāsane samāsīnas tasthau tatra prabhāsayan  Rm 
 tathāsthitaṃ munīndraṃ taṃ dṛṣṭvā saṃpramoditā 
 yathāvidhi samabhyarcya tathā bhojyair atoṣayat  Rm 
 tātas taṃ sugataṃ tṛptaṃ sasāṃghikaṃ samīkṣya sā 
 tatrāpanīya pātrāṇi hastādīṃ paryaśodhayat  Rm 
 tataḥ pūgādikaṃ datvā prārthayitvā kṣamāṃ tathā 
 sasaṃghaṃ taṃ muniṃ natvā sā sāñjalir upāśrayat  Rm 
 tathā sa bhagavāṃs tasyai datvāśīṣaṃ sasāṃghikaḥ 
 tato vihāyasā gatvā svāśrame ca samāśrayat  Rm 
 tathā sa dhaniko bhaktyā bhagavantaṃ sasāṃghikaṃ 
 divyādbhutarddhisaṃbhāraiḥ punar evaṃ nyamaṃtrayat  Rm 
 tatputreṇa tṛtīye 'hni caturthe snuṣayā tathā 
 sasaṃgho bhagavānn evaṃ divyabhogair nimaṃtritaḥ  Rm 
 tac chrutvā tad dvijāḥ sarve vaiśālikāḥ prajā api 
 alabdhāvasarāḥ śāstuḥ pūjāyāṃ praticukruśuḥ  Rm 
 tatas te saṃmataṃ kṛtvā sarve viprāḥ sapaurikāḥ 
 dhanikāya puraṃ kruddhāś cakrur nikāsanodyamaṃ  Rm 
 evaṃ tat samataṃ jñātvā bhagavān sa munīśvaraḥ 
 dhanikaṃ taṃ samāhūya pura evam upādiśat  Rm 
 sādho gṛhapate sarve ime vaiśālikā dvijāḥ 
 kruddhās te saṃghabhojye 'tra hy alabdhāvasarā mama  Rm 
 tad atra tvaṃ kṣamāṃ kṛtvā dvijān sarvān prabodhaya 
 kṛtvātra vinayaṃ dharme prasādayitum arhasi  Rm 
 ity ādiṣṭaṃ munīndreṇa śrutvā sa dhanikas tathā 
 ity āśrutya dvijān sarvān samupetyaivam abravīt  Rm 
 bhavanto na mayā jñātaṃ bhavatāṃ kopakāraṇaṃ 
 tad atra me samākhyāta yad arthe kupyate 'dhunā  Rm 
 iti tenoditaṃ śrutvā sarve te brāhmaṇā 
 kopāgniparidagdhāsyā dhanikaṃ taṃ ninindire  Rm 
 tatraiko brāhmaṇaḥ sādhur dayāluḥ sukṛtārthavit 
 dhanikaṃ taṃ samāmaṃtrya bodhayituṃ samabravīt  Rm 
 sādho gṛhapate 'smābhir yathātra samataṃ kṛtaṃ 
 Rm 
 tathā tat te pravakṣyāmi śrutvā tat pratibudhyatāṃ  Rm 
 bhavanto yan munīndro 'yam atrāsmākaṃ hitechayā 
 saddharmaṃ samupādeṣṭuṃ sasāṃghikaḥ samāgataḥ  Rm 
 tad asmābhir munīndro 'yaṃ pūjanīyaḥ samādaraiḥ 
 ato nimaṃtraṇīyo 'tra sarvaiḥ saṃbhūya nānyathā  Rm 
 ekaś cet kurute vittamadād asya nimaṃtraṇaṃ 
 sarvair nirvāsanīyo 'sau yato 'nyadharmavighnakṛt  Rm 
 ity asmābhiḥ kṛtaṃ sādho samayaṃ sarvasaṃmataṃ 
 tad vilaṃghya tvayaikena śāstuḥ pūjā kṛtā sadā  Rm 
 etad dheto ime sārve brāhmaṇā ruṣitās tathā 
 niṣkāsayitum ichanti tvām anyadharmavādhakaṃ  Rm 
 kiṃ cāpi bhagavān atra sarvadā sthāsyate na hi 
 tat sarve bhagavatpūjāṃ kartuṃ vāṃchanti sāṃprataṃ  Rm 
 yac cāyaṃ bhagavāñ chāstā dharmarājo munīśvaraḥ 
 sarvasatvahitārthāya samutpanna ihā 'dhunā  Rm 
 tathātra sarvasatvānaṃ hitaṃ kartum upācaran 
 saddharmaṃ samupādiśya caraty ayaṃ samaṃtataḥ  Rm 
 tathātrāpi hitaṃ kartum asmākaṃ samupāgataḥ 
 saddharmaṃ samupādiśya vijayate sasāṃghikaḥ  Rm 
 tad atra sarvalokānāṃ triratnabhajanotsavaṃ 
 dātum arhasi sarveṣām api puṇyapravṛddhaye  Rm 
 eka eva tvaṃ evaṃ tu mā kṛthā bhajanaṃ sadā 
 sarvaiḥ saṃbhūya te sāstuḥ karttavyaṃ bhajanaṃ sadā  Rm 
 iti tenoditam śrutvā dhanikaḥ sa vivodhitaḥ 
 brāhmaṇaṃ taṃ samālokya praṇatvaivam abhāṣata  Rm 
 mayā na jñāyate hy evaṃ bhavadbhiḥ samayaṃ kṛtaṃ 
 tad atra me 'parādhatvaṃ kṣantum arhanti sarvathā  Rm 
 yadi vo vidyate śraddhā triratnabhajane sadā 
 kurudhvaṃ sarvadāpy atra saṃbuddhabhajanaṃ khalu  Rm 
 yadā na vidyate pūjā saṃbuddhe 'smin sasāṃghike 
 tadaivāhaṃ kariṣyāmi saṃbuddhabhajanaṃ khalu  Rm 
 iti tena samākhyātaṃ śrutvā sarve 'pi te dvijāḥ 
 satyam iti parijñāya vabhūvus tat prasāditāḥ  Rm 
 tatas te brāhmaṇāḥ sarve saṃbhūya saha paurikaiḥ 
 bhagavataḥ sasaṃghasya nimaṃtritum upāsaran  Rm 
 tatra te brāhmaṇāḥ sarve sametya saha paurikaiḥ 
 sāñjalayo munīndraṃ taṃ natvaivaṃ prārthayan mudā  Rm 
 bhagavan nātha sarvajña trimāsyaṃ bhavatāṃ sadā 
 satkāraṃ kartum ichāma tvadanujñāṃ dadātu naḥ  Rm 
 iti taiḥ prārthite sarvair dṛṣṭvā sa bhagavān muniḥ 
 teṣām āśayaśuddhatvaṃ tūṣṇībhūtvādhyuvāsa tat  Rm 
 Rm 
 tatas te brāhmaṇāḥ sarve bhagavatādhivāsitaṃ 
 matvā sapaurikā natvā taṃ muṇiṃ svapure 'caran  Rm 
 tatra te paurikā viprāḥ śodhayitvā samamṭataḥ 
 bhojyakṣatre dhvajair uccair vitānaiḥ paryaśobhayan  Rm 
 tatrāsanāni prajñapya sarvasāmagrasādhanaṃ 
 kṛtvā sarve 'pi te lokā mahotsāhaṃ pracakrire  Rm 
 tatas te brāhmaṇāḥ prātaḥ snātvā śuddhāmvarāvṛtāḥ 
 tatrāśrame sametyaivaṃ natvā taṃ prārthayan muniṃ  Rm 
 bhagavan nātha sarvajña samayo varttate 'dhunā 
 tat sasaṃgho bhavāṃs tatra pure āgantum arhati  Rm 
 tataḥ sa bhagavān buddhaḥ sasaṃghaś cīvarāvṛtaḥ 
 khikkhiripātram ādāya saṃpratasthe prabhāsayan  Rm 
 tatra mārgeṣu sarvatra bhagavān sa sasāṃghikaḥ 
 bhāsayaṃ bhadratāṃ kṛtvā pracaraṃs tatpure 'viśat  Rm 
 tatra sa bhagavān kṣetre suśodhite sasāṃghikaḥ 
 tad dattaṃ pādyam ādāya svāsane samupāśrayat  Rm 
 saṃbuddhapramukhaṃ sarvaṃ saṃghaṃ te samatoṣayat 
 tatas taṃ sugataṃ tṛptaṃ saṃghaṃ cāpi vilokyate  Rm 
 tat pātrāṇy upanītvā tad dhastādīkaṃ vyaśodhayat 
 tataḥ sa pūgatāmbūramahauṣadhyarasāya naṃ  Rm 
 datvā kṣamārthanaṃ kṛtvā taṃ sasaṃghaṃ praṇemire 
 tatas te brāhmaṇāḥ sarve paurāś cāpi pramoditāḥ 
 tat saddharmāmṛtaṃ pātim upātasthuḥ samāhitāḥ  Rm 
 tatra sa bhagavān dṛṣṭvā sarvāṃs tān samupasthitān 
 āryyasatyaṃ samārabhya saddharmaṃ samupādiśat  Rm 
 tato bhadrāśiṣaṃ datvā bhagavān saha saṃghikaiḥ 
 bhāsayaṃ bhadratāṃ kurvan gatvā svāśramam āśrayat  Rm 
 evaṃ vaiśālikā lokās te traimāsyaṃ niraṃtaraṃ 
 yathārhabhojanaiḥ śāstuḥ sasaṃghasya prabhejire  Rm 
 tato 'nte dhanikaś cāpi patnī putraḥ snuṣāpi ca 
 saṃbuddhapramukhaṃ saṃghaṃ divyabhogyaiḥ samārcayat  Rm 
 bhagavānn api tathā tebhyo datvā śubhāśiṣaṃ tataḥ 
 samutthāya sasaṃghaś ca gatvāśrame samāśrayat  Rm 
 tataḥ sa dhanikaḥ patnīputrasnuṣāsamanvitaḥ 
 dṛṣṭasatyaḥ sadā ratnatrayasevārato 'bhavat  Rm 
 etatpuṇyānubhāvena bhūyo 'tiśrīsamṛddhimān 
 sarvalokahitaṃ kṛtvā pracacāra śubhe sadā  Rm 
 tad dṛṣṭvā vismitāḥ sarve bhikṣavaḥ samupāśritāḥ 
 bhagavantaṃ praṇatvaivaṃ paprachus tat purākṛtaṃ  Rm 
 bhagavan kiṃ purānena dhanikena vṛṣaṃ kṛtaṃ 
 kutra kathaṃ kadaitan naḥ sarvam ākhyātum arhati  Rm 
 Rm 
 iti tair bhikṣubhiḥ pṛṣṭe bhagavān sa munīśvaraḥ 
 sarvāns tāṃ saṃghikān dṛṣṭvā tadaivaṃ samupādiśat  Rm 
 śṛṇuta bhikṣavaḥ sarve yad anena vṛṣaṃ kṛtaṃ 
 tat patnyā ca putreṇa snuṣayā ca tad ucyate  Rm 
 varāṇasyām abhūt pūrvaṃ mālikaḥ kamalābhidhaḥ 
 durbhikṣakṣapite kāle parāṃ durgatim āgataḥ  Rm 
 patnī patnavikā nāma putraḥ kuvaliyābhidhaḥ 
 pāṭalokhyā snuṣā ceti vabhūvus tasya saṃmatāḥ  Rm 
 tadaikasmin dine tasya gṛhāntike prapuṣpite 
 udyāne sāyam āgatya pratyekabuddha āśrayet  Rm 
 te sarve ekavastrā hi paryyāyena nṛpālaye 
 datvā puṣpāṇi prāyātāḥ svabhavane niṣīdire  Rm 
 tadā sa ca gṛhasthās te tatrodāne jvalat prabhāṃ 
 dṛṣṭvā kiṃ mahojvālam udyāne iti vismitāḥ  Rm 
 sahasā te samutthāya tatrodyāne nirīkṣituṃ 
 sarvagatāḥ samīkṣantaḥ dadṛśus taṃ prabhāsayaṃ  Rm 
 tatra te samupāśritya dṛṣṭvā taṃ dhyānasaṃsthitaṃ 
 sāñjalayaḥ praṇatvaiva muditā svagṛhaṃ yayuḥ  Rm 
 tatra te svagṛhāsīnāḥ prātas tatpūjanotsukāḥ 
 nirddhanās tad vyathāṃ prāpu lūnapakṣāḥ khagā iva  Rm 
 tadā sa mālikas tasmai pūjāṃ kartuṃ samutsukaḥ 
 tad dravyaṃ svagṛhe samyag anviṣya samalokayat  Rm 
 tatra gṛhe sa sarvatra samanviṣya samaṃtataḥ 
 kañci mātram api dravyam alabdhaivaṃ vyaciṃtayat  Rm 
 aho mayā purā pāpaṃ prakṛtaṃ kiṃ yato 'dhunā 
 akiṃcanyo daridro 'smi kim atra jīvitena me  Rm 
 yato na vidyate dravyaṃ kiṃ cid api gṛhe mama 
 tat kena kariṣyāmi pūjām asya mahātmanaḥ  Rm 
 atrāyaṃ svayam āgatya mamodyāne samāśritaḥ 
 pratyekabuddha ātmajo dhyātvā tiṣṭhati bhāsayan  Rm 
 tad asya sugatasyātra karttavyā satkṛtir mayā 
 kadāyaṃ puri ramyatra samāgachet svayaṃ punaḥ  Rm 
 tat prātaḥ śūnyapātreṇa gached ito mamātmavit 
 tan mamātra bhave śūnyam iva janmāpi nisphalaṃ  Rm 
 yato mānyo 'bhipūjyo yaṃ pūjyate na kathaṃ cana 
 tatra kiṃ jāyate bhadraṃ puṇyaṃ vāsya kathaṃ kutaḥ  Rm 
 puṇyaṃ vinātra saṃsāre kiṃ sāraṃ janma nisphalaṃ 
 bhuktvāpi kiṃ sukhāny atra suciraṃ jīvite nanu  Rm 
 puṇyārthe jīvitaṃ janma tad atra yadi naśyati 
 kim eva jīvitenāpi janmanā pāpasādhinā  Rm 
 tan mṛtyur me varaṃ hy atra na mithyācirajīvitaṃ 
 avaśyam eva saṃsāre sarvatra maraṇaṃ dhruvaṃ  Rm 
 kim evaṃ dehapuṣṭena bhuktvā duḥkhāṃ sarvadā 
 tat kenāpi pradānena pūjayeyam imaṃ jinaṃ  Rm 
 Rm 
 puṇyena sadgatiṃ yāyāṃ pāpena durgatiṃ sadā 
 tat pāpaṃ parityaktuṃ puṇyaṃ prāptu yateya hi  Rm 
 yady atra pūjyate nāyaṃ drakṣyate ca kadā kuha 
 buddhapūjāṃ vinā bhadre puṇyaṃ ca lapsyate kutaḥ  Rm 
 yāvan na prāpyate puṇyaṃ tāvad durgaticāraṇaṃ 
 tasmāt puṇyaṃ prayatnena karttavyaṃ sukhatāptaye  Rm 
 tad atra śraddhayā kiṃcin mātreṇāpi svavastunā 
 satkṛtyainaṃ mahābhijñaṃ bhajeyaṃ samupasthitaḥ  Rm 
 iti dhyātvā viniścitya mālikaḥ saṃpramoditaḥ 
 bhāryāṃ putraṃ snuṣāṃ cāpi samāmaṃtryaivam abravīt  Rm 
 aye priye snuṣe putra yūyaṃ śṛṇuta madvacaḥ 
 yad atra kartum ichāmi tatra yūyaṃ prasādataḥ  Rm 
 yad atrāyaṃ mahābhijñaḥ svayam eva samāgataḥ 
 asmākaṃ gṛhe dravyaṃ kiñcit mātraṃ na vidyate  Rm 
 tat kenātra kariṣyāmaḥ pūjām asya mahātmanaḥ  Rm 
 yadi na pūjyate 'smābhiḥ sugato 'yaṃ munir yatiḥ 
 tadā puṇyaṃ vayaṃ kutra lapsyāmahe kadā kathaṃ  Rm 
 puṇyaṃ vinātra saṃsāre nisphalaṃ janma jīvitaṃ 
 tad vayaṃ puṇyato prāptuṃ yatema sarvathā vayaṃ  Rm 
 puṇyena sadgatiṃ prāpya pāpena durgatiṃ sadā 
 tat sadgatisukhaprāptyai puṇyaṃ kurvīmahi dhruvaṃ  Rm 
 caturṇāṃ vidyate 'smākam ekaṃ sarvasvam amvaraṃ 
 anenāpy enam āchādya prabhajamahi sāṃprataṃ  Rm 
 nādyarājakule nagnā gachāmaḥ kiṃ bhaviṣyati 
 etat me vacanaṃ śrutvābhyanumoditum arhatha  Rm 
 iti tenoditaṃ śrutvā patnī putraḥ snuṣāpi te 
 sarve 'py abhyanumoditvā tathā kurv iti procire  Rm 
 ity etat samayaṃ kṛtvā sarve te śraddhayānvitāḥ 
 gatvā tenaikavastreṇa taṃ prāchādya samārcayan  Rm 
 tatas te muditāḥ sarve kṛtāñjalipuṭā muneḥ 
 tasya pādau praṇatvaivaṃ praṇidhānaṃ pracakrire  Rm 
 anena vastradānena vayaṃ sarve śubhāśayāḥ 
 bhaveyaṃ sadgatiṃ yātā divyasaṃpattihāninaḥ  Rm 
 śāstāraṃ sugataṃ buddhaṃ samārādhya sadā bhave 
 triratnabhajanaṃ kṛtvā bhavema bodhicāriṇaḥ  Rm 
 iti tair muditaiḥ sarvaiḥ praṇidhānaṃ kṛtaṃ tathā 
 viditvā sa mahāvijñas tathāstv iti samādiśat  Rm 
 tatas tesāṃ manoharṣaṃ kṛtvā sa sugato muniḥ 
 tata uḍḍīya pakṣīva bhāsayan svāśrame yayau  Rm 
 tad dṛṣṭvā te nanditāḥ sarve buddhadharmānuśaṃsinaḥ 
 triratnasmaraṇaṃ kṛtvā pracerire sukhaṃ sadā  Rm 
 tatpuṇyapraṇidhānena dhaniko 'yaṃ sa mālikaḥ 
 Rm 
 jāto divyaprabhāvarddhiḥ patnīputrasnuṣānvitaḥ  Rm 
 manaḥśuddhividhānena dānenātiglaghīyasā 
 bhavanty alaghvyāḥ saṃkalpaiḥ saṃpadaḥ satvaśālināṃ  Rm 
 buddhakṣetreṣu yat karma sukṛtaṃ duḥkṛtaṃ tathā 
 mahattaratvam āsādya phalaty eva sadā bhave  Rm 
 iti matvātra saṃsāre karttavyaṃ sukṛtaṃ sadā 
 bauddhe satkṛtapuṇyena labhanti bodhisaṃpadaḥ  Rm 
 iti śāstrā samādiṣṭaṃ śrutvā sarve 'pi sāṃghikāḥ 
 menire cittavaimalyamūlaṃ dānaphalaśriyaṃ  Rm 
 tac chrutvā brāhmaṇās te 'pi tatpuṇyavismitā mudā 
 bhagavaṃtaṃ sadā smṛtvā prabhejire 'numoditāḥ  Rm 
 tathā te brāhmaṇāś cāpi sarve 'pi paurikās tathā 
 tatpuṇyapariśuddhāṃśā vabhuvuḥ kuśalodyatāḥ  Rm 
 helārpitaṃ ratnadhanaṃ tṛṇāgraṃ śraddhāvatīrṇaṃ tṛṇam apy anarghaṃ 
 anekaśobhānubhavaṃ hi cittaṃ cittaṃ nimittaṃ śubhasaṃbhavānāṃ  Rm 
 iti me guruṇādiṣṭaṃ śrutaṃ mayā tathocyate 
 śrutvāpy evaṃ mahārāja karttavyaṃ sukṛtaṃ sadā  Rm 
 prajāś cāpi mahārāja bodhayitvā prayatnataḥ 
 kramād bodhiṃ samāsādya saṃbuddhapadam āpnuyāḥ  Rm 
 iti tenārhatākhyātaṃ śrutvāśokaḥ sa bhūpatiḥ 
 tathā hīti pratijñāya prābhyanandat sapārṣadaḥ  Rm 
 idaṃ narā ye dhanikāvadānaṃ śṛṇvanti ye cāpi niśāmayanti 
 sukhāni bhuktvā sa śubhe sadā te sarve 'pi śamyānti jinālayan te 
  iti ratnāvadānatatve dhanikāvadānaṃ samāptam 
 Rm 
 XIX Raivatāvadāna
 athāśoko narendraḥ sa kṛtāṃjalipuṭo mudā 
 upaguptaṃ guruṃ natvā punar evam abhāṣata  Rm 
 bhadanta śrotum ichāmi punar anyat subhāṣitaṃ 
 tadyathā guruṇākhyātaṃ tathādeṣṭum ca me 'rhati  Rm 
 iti sāṃprārthitaṃ rājñā śrutvā so 'rhaṃ mahāmatiḥ 
 upagupto narendraṃ taṃ samālokyaivam ādiśat  Rm 
 sādhu śṛṇu mahārāja yathā me guruṇoditaṃ 
 tathāhaṃ te pravakṣyāmi śrutvaivaṃ paribudhyatāṃ  Rm 
 krauryeṇa dvirasanāḥ śuciveṣṭitānāṃ mithyāpavādaviṣamaṃ viṣam utsṛjanti 
 te pāpaśāpaparitāpaparaṃparārttās tīvravyalīkatimiravivaraṃ viśanti  Rm 
 tadyathābhūt purā bhikṣuḥ kāsmīre patitāśrame 
 raivatakābhidho bauddhaḥ sarvabhūtadayāśrayaḥ  Rm 
 sa kadācid dhanoddeśe vivikte sughaṭāntare 
 tarutvacaḥ kaṣāyena cakre cīvararaṃjanaṃ  Rm 
 tasminn avasare tatra piśunākhyadvijanmanaḥ 
 dhenuvatsā vane naṣṭā vabhūvur yūthanirgatāḥ  Rm 
 tadā sa brāhmaṇo dṛṣṭvā taṃ duṣṭāśitaśaṃkitaḥ 
 sarvatrāpi samanviṣṭā tatrāpy anveṣituṃ yayau  Rm 
 tatra taccīvarakvāthavāke vahnisamudgataṃ 
 dhūmaṃ sa dvija ālokya vatsapākam amanyata  Rm 
 tataḥ sa brāhmaṇaḥ sārddhaṃ svajanaiḥ śastrapāṇibhiḥ 
 tad draṣṭuṃ śailam āruhya sahasāgāt tadantike  Rm 
 tatra taṃ raivataṃ bhikṣuṃ dṛṣṭvā sa dvija ādarāt 
 upetya cūḍikaiḍyāhataṃ kumbham apaśyat  Rm 
 tad dṛṣṭvā śaṃkitaś cāsau vinayān samupāsaran 
 kim etat kriyate bhikṣor iti taṃ paryapṛchata  Rm 
 iti pṛṣṭe dvijenāsau raivato bhikṣur ādarāt 
 tatra cīvararāgo 'yam iti taṃ dvijam abravīt  Rm 
 asminn avasare tasyā pūrvakarmavipākataḥ 
 gomāṃsaraktapāṇīyaḥ sapākaḥ samapadyata  Rm 
 sukhaṃ duḥkhatvam ānāti śuklam apy eti kālatāṃ 
 vidhau vidhuratāṃ yāte dharmo 'py āyāty adharmatāṃ  Rm 
 mithyāpāpaprakaṭatā janakopaḥ padacyutiḥ 
 Rm 
 apuṇyaparipākānām etat pratyakṣalakṣaṇaṃ  Rm 
 doṣaḥ samunmiṣati yāty aguṇaḥ prakāśaṃ kāryaṃ viparyayam upeti viśīryate dhīḥ  Rm 
 puṃsāṃ purāvihitaḥ duḥkṛtapākakāle ke ke na nāma nipatanti mahābhighātāḥ  Rm 
 tataḥ sa brāhmaṇo 'py atra kumbhe kim iti śaṃkitaḥ 
 paśyāmīti viniścitya nirīkṣitum upācarat  Rm 
 viruddhāmiṣagaṃdhena rudhireṇa ca śaṃkitaḥ 
 apaśyan sa dvijaḥ kumbhe māṃsapiṇḍaṃ supakvitaiḥ  Rm 
 pratyakṣadoṣam ālokya dvijaḥ krodhito ruṣā 
 tam abhāṣata nirbhatsya tīvravaiśaśakaṃpitaḥ  Rm 
 aho vata sadācāraḥ sthito 'yaṃ vijane vane 
 yasyedṛśāni karmāṇi na kasyacid iha paśyati  Rm 
 pravrajyāraṃjitaḥ kāyaḥ kriyā mlechajanocitā 
 jānāti channapāpānāṃ kaḥ kūṭavrataśāntitāṃ  Rm 
 ity ukte tena sākṣepaṃ sa raivato 'py aciṃtayat 
 doṣe pratyakṣalakṣyasmin kiṃ bravīmi niruttaraḥ  Rm 
 mama daivāya ghāto 'yam ity ukte ko 'numanyate 
 hāsyāyatanatām eti pratyakṣyāpahnavī janaḥ  Rm 
 upasthitaṃ sahe sarvaṃ maunam ālambya kevalaṃ 
 ayaṃ me niḥpratīkāraḥ salilād agnidutthitaḥ  Rm 
 doṣe guṇātiśayam āśu guṇe 'pi doṣaṃ paiyūṣadhāmni viṣam apy amṛtaṃ viṣe ca 
 saṃdarśayaty aniśam adbhutarūpam eva kālendrajālikāvadhūr bhavitavyeyaṃ  Rm 
 ity evaṃ manasā dhyātvā raivataḥ sa mahāmatiḥ 
 svadaivasmaraṇaṃ kṛtvā tasthau yogasamāhitaḥ  Rm 
 iti dhyānaṃ samālambya sthitaṃ taṃ raivataṃ muniṃ 
 dṛṣṭvātiruṣitaś cāsau saṃtaryya paryabhāṣata  Rm 
 are re durmate bhikṣo kiṃ atra durjane vane 
 sthitvevaṃ dāruṇaṃ pāpaṃ sādhayitvā niṣīdasi  Rm 
 are pāpiṣṭha bhāṣasva yad arthe vālakāṃ vṛṣaṃ 
 hatvātra pacyate māṃsa tvayātmano pareṇa vā  Rm 
 pareṇāpi hataṃ dṛṣṭvā tat pāpaiḥ parilipyase 
 tat tvayā vṛṣabhī hatvā kathaṃ pāpair na dahyase  Rm 
 dhig dhik tvām atra rebhikṣo saṃbuddhaśāsane yataḥ 
 pravrajyāsaṃvaraṃ dhṛtvā nirjane vana āśrayan  Rm 
 mahadduḥkarakarmāṇi kṛtvaivaṃ tapase 'dhunā 
 are re śrūyate kiṃ na tvayā saṃbuddhabhāṣitaṃ  Rm 
 atha śrutvāpi te tatra śraddhā na vidyate khalu 
 kim evaṃ pātakaṃ kṛtvā pravrajyāsaṃvaraṃ caran  Rm 
 kevalaṃ pāpakāny eva sādhayitvātra tiṣṭhase 
 pravrajito viraktātmā pariśuddhatrimaṃḍalaḥ  Rm 
 sarvasatvadayādṛṣṭiś caren nityaṃ samāhitaḥ  Rm 
 adattaṃ kasya cid dravyaṃ gṛhīyān na kathaṃ cana 
 Rm 
 dayākaruṇyayuktātmā na kuryāt prāṇipīḍinaṃ  Rm 
 kāmabhogam adharmeṇa naiva bhuṃjyāt kadā cana 
 mṛṣāvādaṃ kadāpy atra naiva brūyāt kathaṃ cana  Rm 
 pāruṣyavacanaṃ cāpi naiva brūyāt kathaṃ cana 
 paiśunyavacanaṃ vāpi vaden na kasya cit puraḥ  Rm 
 saṃbhinnapralāpaṃ ca na pravadet kasya cid api 
 vyāpādaṃ kasya cic cāpi bhāvayen na kathaṃ cana  Rm 
 abhidhyāṃ ca tathā naiva ciṃtayet kasya cid api  Rm 
 mithyādṛṣṭiṃ sadā kvāpi bhāvayen na kadā cana 
 etāni daśapāpānāṃ mūlāni sarvathā tyajet  Rm 
 etāni ye samālabhya pracaranti pramādataḥ 
 te sarve kleśasaṃtaptā bhramanti duḥkhino bhave  Rm 
 tataḥ kleśāgnisaṃtaptāḥ pāpeṣv eva samāhitāḥ 
 duḥkhāny eva sadā bhuktvā narakeṣu bhramanti te  Rm 
 iti matvātra saṃsāre tyaktvaitāni daśāpi hi 
 santo nityam śubheṣv eva pracaranti samāhitāḥ  Rm 
 śubhena sadgatiṃ yānti papina durgatiṃ sadā 
 ity ākhyātaṃ jinaiḥ sarvaiḥ kiṃ naitac chrūyate tvayā  Rm 
 katham etad avajñāya pravrajitas tvam ācareḥ 
 dhik te cittaṃ yad evaṃ me govatsaṃ bhoktum ichati  Rm 
 pravrajito hi śuddhātmā pariśuddhas trimaṇḍalaḥ 
 sarvasatvadayācittaś caren nityaṃ samāhitaḥ  Rm 
 sarvasatvahitaṃ kṛtvā brahmacaryaṃ samāhitaḥ 
 bhikṣānnamātrasaṃkṛṣṭaḥ suniḥspṛhaś carec chubhe  Rm 
 samādhinirato yogī dhāraṇīparamārthabhṛt 
 sarvakleśān vinirjitvā sarvamāragāṇān api  Rm 
 sarvān parigrahān tyaktvā nirvikalpo niraṃjanaḥ 
 sākṣād arhatvam āsādya brahmacaryaṃ samācaret  Rm 
 evaṃ pravrajito bhikṣuś caran nityaṃ suśīlabhṛt 
 śivāṃ bodhiṃ samāsādya nirvṛtipadam āpnuyāt  Rm 
 tvaṃ tu pravrajito 'py evaṃ mahaddāruṇapātakaṃ 
 kṛtvātra nirjane bhuktvā carase mlechacārikāṃ  Rm 
 hā vatātra vinaṣṭo 'si yad etat pātakānvitaḥ 
 sahasā narake gatvā ciraṃ duḥkhāni bhokṣyasi  Rm 
 kiṃ tvayā prakṛtaṃ pāpaṃ purā janmāntare kathaṃ 
 yad atra saugate dharmaṃ prāpto 'py evaṃ durāśayaḥ  Rm 
 tac carasva samādhāya prāyaścittavrataṃ punaḥ 
 etatpāpābhisaṃśuddhyai punar vratasamāptaye  Rm 
 tathā te śuddhite kāye maṃgalaṃ ca bhavet kramāt 
 pariśuddhas trikāyaś ca pravrajyāsaṃvaraṃ cara  Rm 
 tadā tvaṃ sarvathā jitvā kleśān māragaṇānn api 
 sākṣād arhatvam āsādya brahmacārī bhaviṣyati  Rm 
 Rm 
 tadā tvaṃ pariśuddhātmā nirvikalpo niraṃjanaḥ 
 śivāṃ bodhiṃ samāsādya nirvṛtipadam āpnuyāḥ  Rm 
 iti tenoditaṃ śrutvā raivataḥ sa prabodhitaḥ 
 tathāpi maunam ādhāya tathau daivābhyanusmaran  Rm 
 evaṃ sthitaṃ tam ālokya brāhmaṇaḥ sa ruṣānvitaḥ 
 evaṃ dvidhā tridhāpy enaṃ paribhāṣyābhyanindayat  Rm 
 evaṃ dvidhā tridhāpy ukte brāhmaṇena sa raivataḥ 
 svadaivam abhyanusmṛtvā maunenaiva nyaṣīdata  Rm 
 svadaivacintayas tasya maunāt sa brāhmaṇo ruṣā 
 raivataṃ tāṃ katākṣeṇa dṛṣṭvainaṃ paryabhāṣata  Rm 
 are re durmate bhikṣo kim evaṃ tiṣṭhase 'dhunā 
 uttiṣṭhātra pravaṃdhitva nayāmi tvāṃ nṛpāntike  Rm 
 evaṃ tenodite 'py eva sthitaḥ sa raivato yatiḥ 
 kiṃ cin naivāvaden maunam evālambya nyaṣīdata  Rm 
 tataḥ sa brāhmaṇas tasya maunād atiprakopitaḥ 
 murddhni pāpam iva sthūlaṃ laguḍaṃ marpayātayat  Rm 
 tathābhighātyamāno 'pi raivataḥ sa samāhitaḥ 
 daivam evābhyanusmṛtvā tasthau niḥkaṃpitāśayaḥ  Rm 
 tathāsthitaṃ taṃ munim ātmavidyaṃ daivaṃ smaraṃtaṃ hy akṛtāparādhaṃ 
 nināya paścātkṛtavāhudaṃḍaṃ sadas tadā naṃdanabhūmibhartuḥ  Rm 
 tathāsthitaṃ tam ālokya sa dvijaḥ pratiroṣitaḥ 
 raktākṣaṃ raivataṃ vaddhvā sahasānayan nṛpāntike  Rm 
 tatra sa brāhmaṇo nītvā taṃ rājñaḥ sthitaḥ 
 tadvatsapiśitaṃ pakvam upasthāpya 'bhyadarśayat  Rm 
 tataḥ sa brāhmaṇaḥ krūras tasya bhikṣo savistaraṃ 
 sarvavṛttāṃtam ākhyāya taṃ nṛpaṃ paryakopayat  Rm 
 tad vatsamāṃsam ālokya nṛpatiḥ sa prakopitaḥ 
 raivataṃ taṃ yatiṃ vaddhvā cakre kārāgṛhātithiṃ  Rm 
 nirdoṣaḥ kleśam āśnāti tambhate guptapātakaḥ 
 jānāti kasya kaḥ śuddhiṃ citrākāreṣv asākṣiṣu  Rm 
 tatra sa vaṃdhanāgāre vaṃdhito 'pi sa sanmatiḥ 
 triratnasmaraṇaṃ kṛtvā tasthau daivānucintayan  Rm 
 tatraivaṃ vaṃdhanāgāre tasmin bhikṣau nivandhite 
 kāle na visnito rājā tad vicāre 'pi nāsmarat  Rm 
 tadānyasmin dine tatra te vatsāḥ sarva āgatāḥ 
 mātṛbhiḥ saha saṃsaktās tṛṇaṃ bhuktvā niṣedire  Rm 
 tān vatsān mātṛsaṃsaktān sarvān ālokya sa dvijaḥ 
 vismitaḥ punar ālokya paśyann evaṃ vyaciṃtayat  Rm 
 aho vatsā ime sarve kutra gatvādhunāgatāḥ 
 Rm 
 sarvatrānviṣyamānā hi kutrāpi nābhyadṛśyate  Rm 
 hā mamātra mahatpāpo jāyate sāṃprataṃ kathaṃ 
 yan mayā sahasā bhikṣor asamīkṣyāparādhyate  Rm 
 yathā bhikṣor ghaṭe mānsaṃ dṛṣṭvaiṣām iti cintayat 
 caurāyam iti taṃ bhikṣuṃ paryabhāṣaṃ ruṣābhṛtaṃ  Rm 
 aparādhaṃ vinārhaṃtam api bhikṣuṃ pratāḍayat 
 vaddhvā taṃ sahasā rājñaḥ puro 'tra samupānayaṃ  Rm 
 rājāpi mama vākyena sahasaiva nimaṃtrayan 
 vaddhvāśu vaṃdhanāgāre prasthāpayati sāṃprataṃ  Rm 
 tad atra kiṃ kariṣyāmi vatsāḥ sarve ihāgatāḥ 
 aparādhā yater neti vadeya sāṃprataṃ kathaṃ  Rm 
 yady avakṣyaṃ tathā rājā tadā me kupito nṛpaḥ 
 sarvasvam apahṛtvāpi prāhariṣyate mām iha  Rm 
 atha yadi bhayād rājño nāvadiṣyaṃs tathā kvacit 
 nūnaṃ taṃ yatim arhantam api rājā haniṣyate  Rm 
 tadāhaṃ kiṃ kariṣyāmi tadghorapātakānalaiḥ 
 pacyamānas sadāvīcau tiṣṭheyam atiduḥkhitaḥ  Rm 
 tad atra kiṃ kariṣyāmi yatropāyaṃ na vidyate 
 sarvathāhaṃ vinaṣṭo 'smi vrajeya śaraṇaṃ kuha  Rm 
 yad imaṃ saugataṃ bhikṣum arhantaṃ brahmacāriṇaṃ 
 anaparādhinaṃ hatvā kathaṃ pāpair na lepsyate  Rm 
 etair hi pātakair ghorair ahaṃ rājā janā ime 
 sarve vatsyāmahe 'vīcau bhuktvā duḥkhāni sarvadā  Rm 
 hā me daivād yateś cāpi nirjane vasato 'pi yat 
 ghaṭe 'bhidṛśyate vatsamānsībhūtaṃ hi cīvaraṃ  Rm 
 avaśyaṃ bhāvino bhāvā bhavanty eva na cānyathā 
 tad atra kiṃ kariṣyāmi bhikṣur vā kiṃ kariṣyati  Rm 
 tasyaiva karmadoṣeṇa māṃsībhūtaṃ hi cīvaraṃ 
 atha mamaiva daivena tad iti manyate na hi  Rm 
 tad atra kiṃ vadeyāhaṃ daivaṃ hi sarvakarmakṛti 
 iti mamārho 'py asya dūṣaṇaṃ nātra vidyate  Rm 
 tathapy etat pravṛttir na vaktavyaṃ kasya cid api 
 na gaṃtavyaṃ vahiḥ kvāpi sthātavyaṃ svagṛhe sadā  Rm 
 kadā cit skhalitā buddhir vāṇī ca vismṛtasya me 
 etad dhi pātakaṃ ghoraṃ samācakṣata kutra cit  Rm 
 tadāhaṃ niṃdyamāno 'tra sarvalokair itas tataḥ 
 bhratsyamānaḥ kathaṃ loke cariṣye duṣṭajaṃtuvat  Rm 
 iti dhyātvā viniścitya brāhmaṇaḥ sa viṣāditaḥ 
 kasyāpy etat pravṛttāṃtaṃ noce daurjanyalajjayā  Rm 
 tat pātakāgnisaṃtaptaḥ smṛtvārhantaṃ tam eva saḥ 
 prāyaścittavrataṃ kurvann iva tasthau gṛhāśritaḥ  Rm 
 evaṃ dvādaśavarṣāṇi nṛpeṇāpi sa vismṛtaḥ 
 Rm 
 raivato vaṃdhanāgāre tasthau dhyānasamāhitaḥ  Rm 
 atha dvādaśavarṣānte tac chiṣyāḥ sarva āgatāḥ 
 tat pravṛttiṃ samākarṇya vismitās te 'bhavaṃs tadā  Rm 
 tataḥ sarve 'pi te śiṣyāḥ saṃmīlya nṛpateḥ puraḥ 
 upetyaitat pravṛttāṃtaṃ samākhyāya nyavedayan  Rm 
 ārogyam astu te rājan lokān dharmeṇa pālaya 
 yadarthe vayam āyāmas tatra bhavān prasīdatu  Rm 
 yad asmākaṃ gurur bhikṣur aparādhaṃ vinā kathaṃ 
 bhavatā vaṃdhanāgāre sthāpitas tad vicāraya  Rm 
 iti tair bhikṣubhiḥ sarvais tac chiṣyaiḥ prārthite tadā 
 vyomavāṇī tathākhyāya narendraṃ taṃ vyabodhayat  Rm 
 tat khavāṇiṃ samākarṇya nṛpaḥ sa paribodhitaḥ 
 tac chiṣyaiḥ sārito bhikṣuṃ taṃ mumocāśu vaṃdhanāt  Rm 
 aho grāvāgralikhitā niścalā karmasaṃtatiḥ 
 prāptabhijño 'pi yat prāpa krūrakleśadaśāṃ tathā  Rm 
 taṃ yatiṃ nirgataṃ dṛṣṭvā sa rājābhyānutāpitaḥ 
 ninindā mandapuṇyatvaṃ pramādād dhatam ātmanaḥ  Rm 
 tadā sa nṛpati rājā sahasā tasya pādayoḥ 
 sāṃjaliḥ praṇatiṃ kṛtvā samutthāyaivam abravīt  Rm 
 bhadanto vicāryaiva pramadā yad bhavān mayā 
 sthāpito vaṃdhane tan me 'parādhaṃ kṣaṃtum arhati  Rm 
 vismṛtā me sahāyāṃ ca parijñātā na kena cit 
 daṇḍaḥ patati śuddheṣu prāptaḥ pāpe mahīpatau  Rm 
 ity uktaḥ kṣitipālena kṣāntiprakṣālitāśayaḥ 
 raivataḥ sa nareṃdraṃ taṃ samālokyaivam abravīt  Rm 
 rājan na te 'parādhatvaṃ mamaitat karmajaṃ phalaṃ 
 tad atra mā kṛthāḥ kheṭaṃ saugata ātmavidyutaṃ  Rm 
 tatas taṃ yatim arhantaṃ sa rājā sahasādarāt 
 cīvareṇa samāchādya piṃḍakena samārcayat  Rm 
 tadaitad vṛttim ākarṇya brāhmaṇaḥ sa tvarānvitaḥ 
 āgatya tat sabhāmadhye dattāśīḥ samupācarat  Rm 
 tatra sa samupāsṛtya rājñe datvā jayāśiṣāṃ 
 taṃ yatiṃ sāñjalir natvā prārthayan vinayāt kṣamāṃ  Rm 
 bhadanta bhavatām evam aparādham akārayan 
 tan me 'parādhatāṃ kṣaṃtum arhati sarvathā bhavān  Rm 
 ity ukte tena vipreṇa raivataḥ sa viśuddhadhīḥ 
 brāhmaṇaṃ taṃ viṣaṇṇāsyaṃ samālokyaivam abravīt  Rm 
 na manyur vidyate vipra na tvayāpakṛtaṃ mayi 
 mamaiva daivayā kena māṃsībhūtaṃ hi cīvaraṃ  Rm 
 tatrāhaṃ maunam ālambya sthito daivābhyanusmaran 
 tenātra kiṃ vadiṣyāmi daivā hi valavān bhave  Rm 
 na tvayāpākṛtaṃ kiñcid vipulakleśapātitaḥ 
 Rm 
 tan mamopanataṃ pāke svakarmasadṛśaṃ phalaṃ  Rm 
 yat sautkaṇṭhatayaiva sarvavipadaḥ kurvanti kaṇṭhagrahaṃ sarvāṅgaprasabhopabhogasubhagāḥ kliśyanti yat saṃpadaḥ 
 yat svāchaṃdyasukhāspadaṃ viharaṇaṃ dīrghaṃ ca yad vaṃdhanaṃ tat puṃsāṃ nijakarmapākaśavalaṃ saṃsāravallīphalaṃ  Rm 
 iti tenārhatākhyātaṃ śrutvā naṃdaḥ sa bhūpatiḥ 
 vismitaḥ kautukāc caivaṃ dṛṣṭvā taṃ yatim abravīt  Rm 
 tavāpi sumate kasya phalam etat kukarmaṇaḥ 
 kiṃ purā prakṛtaṃ karman tat samākhyātum arhati  Rm 
 iti pṛṣṭe narendreṇa raivataḥ sa sudhir yatiḥ 
 taṃ nareṃdraṃ samālokya bodhayituṃ tathāvadat  Rm 
 sādhu śṛṇu mahārāja yan mayā prakṛtaṃ purā 
 tad atrāhaṃ pravakṣyāmi sarvalokaprabodhane  Rm 
 vārāṇasyāṃ purā krūracarito 'bhūt kuthābhidhaḥ 
 gocauraḥ kutsikācāro gomāṃsavihitāśanaḥ  Rm 
 kadā cit sa vane gatvā hatvā govatsam ātmanā 
 tad vatsamāṃsam ādāya sahasā tato viniryayau  Rm 
 tatra gorakṣiṇo vatsanaṣṭam anviṣya sarvataḥ 
 dṛṣṭvā taṃ māṃsabhārārttaṃ kopāt samabhidudruvuḥ  Rm 
 tatra sa kutha ālokya tān sarvān samupadrutān 
 sahasopadruto 'raṇye pradudrāva vanāṃtare  Rm 
 tatra pratyekabuddhasya dhyānalīnasya so 'grataḥ 
 upanikṣipya tan māṃsaṃ tatraikānte nyalīyata  Rm 
 te 'pi gorakṣiṇaḥ sarve sānucarām abhidrutāḥ 
 tatra pratyekabuddhaṃ tam ālokya samupācaran  Rm 
 tatra sa kutha āgatya teṣāṃ gorakṣiṇāṃ puraḥ 
 gomāṃsaṃ darśayitvā taṃ caurāyam ity adarśayat  Rm 
 tatra te gobhṛtaḥ sarve gomāṃsaṃ tan muneḥ puraḥ 
 dṛṣṭvaiva sahasā kopāt taṃ munim abhyaghātayat  Rm 
 vadhyo 'yam iti taṃ vadhvā gopālās te prakopitāḥ 
 ākruśya sahasānītvā kārāgāre nyavaṃdhayat  Rm 
 tataḥ sa kutha ākarṇya taṃ yatiṃ vaṃdhane dhṛtaṃ 
 paścāttāpāgnisaṃtaptas tahīty evaṃ vyaciṃtayat  Rm 
 hā mayā pāpināpy evaṃ sādhyate pātakāni ca 
 avaśyaṃ vahnināvīcau kuṃhbhyāṃ pakṣye rataṃś ciraṃ  Rm 
 yad ayaṃ nirjane dhyāto pratyekabuddha ātmavit 
 caurāyam iti saṃdarśya vaṃdhane sthāpitomayā  Rm 
 etatpāpavipāke hi sarvadā narake sthitaḥ 
 tīvraduḥkhāgnisaṃtapta ante māṃ svakṛte phalaṃ  Rm 
 hā mayaivaṃ mahāghoraṃ pātakaṃ durdhiyā kṛtaṃ 
 kadā tat pātakān mukto vrajeyaṃ sadgatiṃ kathaṃ  Rm 
 Rm 
 hā sarvajña namas tubhyaṃ paśya mām atipāpinaṃ 
 bhavānn eva jagattrātā tan me 'pi trātum arhati  Rm 
 mayā mūḍhena duṣṭena mahāpātakam ācitaṃ 
 tad vimuktyām upāyaṃ me kṛpayā dātum arhati  Rm 
 iti kuthaḥ sa cāṇḍālaḥ smṛtvā saṃbuddham ādarāt 
 paścāttāpābhisaṃtaptas tasthau gehe pramohitaḥ  Rm 
 tataḥ sa cetanaṃ prāpya saṃbuddhasyānubhāvataḥ 
 sahasā tata utthāya tadantike upācarat  Rm 
 tatra sa samupāsṛtya tesāṃ gorakṣiṇaṃ puraḥ 
 kṛtāṃjalipuṭo natvā yācitvābhayam abravīt  Rm 
 bhavanto 'tra mayā pāpaṃ kṛtaṃ tat pratidekṣyate 
 tad bhavaṃtaḥ samākarṇya kṣaṃtum arhaṃti sarvathā  Rm 
 asya pratyekabuddhasya hy aparādho na vidyate 
 tatra mayātiduṣṭena cauro 'yam iti darśitaḥ  Rm 
 tad atra mucyatām eṣa pratyekasugato muniḥ 
 satkṛtyābhyarcya piṃḍena mānanīyo hi sarvadā  Rm 
 atraitat pātakaṃ nāsya mamaiva mastake pacet 
 tad aham eva vadhyo 'tra tad ayaṃ mucyatāṃ yatiḥ  Rm 
 iti tenoditaṃ śrutvā sarve gorakṣiṇo 'pi te 
 ruṣṭās taṃ sahasā vaddhvā paryyākhyāyātyatāḍayat  Rm 
 tat tāḍanaravaṃ śrutvā sa pratyekajinaḥ sudhīḥ 
 gopālāṃs tān samāmaṃtrya punar evaṃ samādiśat  Rm 
 bhavanto mucyatām eṣa māparādhe 'pi hanyatāṃ 
 kṣamā hi paramaṃ dharmaṃ tat kurvantu kṣamām iha  Rm 
 tantāsādyāgano yogaṃ kartum arhanti sarvathā 
 kiṃ daivaṃ nihataṃ hatvā yuṣmākaṃ setsyate phalaṃ  Rm 
 mayaitad vaṃdhanaṃ prāptaṃ mamaiva daivayogataḥ 
 tad asyāpy aparādho 'tra nāstīty eṣa vimucyatāṃ  Rm 
 iti pratyekabuddhena tenādiṣṭaṃ niśamyate 
 tatheti pratibuddhitvā tat kopaṃ mumucus tadā  Rm 
 atha te gobhṛtaḥ sarve śrutvā tasya muner vacaḥ 
 sahasā vinatiṃ kṛtvā vaṃdhanāt taṃ vyamuṃcayat  Rm 
 tatas te gobhṛtaḥ sarve taṃ pratyekamuniṃ mudā 
 cīvareṇa samāchādya samabhyarcyātyatoṣayan  Rm 
 tatra taṃ samupāśritya kṛtāṃjalipuṭo natāḥ 
 tad aparādhasaṃtaptāḥ prārthayann evam ādarāt  Rm 
 bhagavañ jñāyate 'smābhir bhavato nāparādhatā 
 tenāsmākaṃ kṣamāṃ kartum arhaty atra bhavān api  Rm 
 iti taiḥ prārthitaṃ śrutvā sa pratyekajinaḥ 
 tān sarvān gobhṛto dṛṣṭvā samāśvāsyaivam abravīt  Rm 
 bhavanto mā viṣīdantu dūṣaṇaṃ vā na vidyate 
 etad vṛttiṃ vijānāmi saugatā hi bhavārthavit  Rm 
 Rm 
 ity ādiśya sa sarvajñaḥ pratyekabuddha utthitaḥ 
 tata ākāśa utplutya svāśramaṃ gate āśrayan  Rm 
 tad dṛṣṭvā te janāḥ sarve gopālāḥ prativismitāḥ 
 tam eva sugataṃ smṛtvā saddharme sarvadācaran  Rm 
 yo 'sau kuthābhidho goghnaḥ praduṣṭo 'haṃ tadābhavat 
 tatpāpair narakeṣv evaṃ ciraṃ duḥkhāni bhuktavān  Rm 
 asmiñ janmany api prāptakleśadvādaśavārṣikaṃ 
 tad asyātrāparādhaṃ na mamaitad daivayogataḥ  Rm 
 iti mahārāja śubhāśubhaṃ svadaivataḥ 
 saṃsāre 'tra sadā puṇyaṃ karttavyaṃ satsukhārthibhiḥ  Rm 
 puṇyam evātra saṃsāre sārasarvārthasiddhidaṃ 
 puṇyaṃ vinā na siddhyante kṛtakarmāṇi sarvathā  Rm 
 puṇyena jāyate svarge puṇyena yānti sadgatiṃ 
 puṇyena sarvadā bhadraṃ kṛtvā yāṃti jinālayaṃ  Rm 
 daṃḍena mucyate vadhyaḥ puṇyasyaivānubhāvataḥ 
 daṃḍārho 'pi prahāreṇa prahārārho 'pi roṣataḥ  Rm 
 roṣārhā romaharṣanena mucyate puṇyato nṛpa 
 yāvantaḥ sūkhinaḥ sarvasaṃpatsamanvitāḥ  Rm 
 sarve te puṇyakarttāra iti jñeyā narādhipa 
 puṇyena śuddhyate cittaṃ śuddhāśayo bhavet sudhīḥ  Rm 
 subuddhiḥ sarvadā nityaṃ śubheṣv eva samācaret 
 śubhācāro viśuddhāṃgaḥ satyavādī jitendriyaḥ  Rm 
 pariśuddhāśayo dhīro bhavet satvahitārthabhṛt 
 tathaitat puṇyayuktātmā sarvavidyākalārthavit  Rm 
 bhaved dharmārthavijñaś ca suguṇaśrīsamanvitaḥ 
 tato māheśvarīsaṃpatprāpto lokahitodyataḥ  Rm 
 dānaṃ kṛtvā sadā saukhyaṃ bhuktyā nityaṃ śubhe caret 
 etatpuṇyavipākena pariśuddhas trimaṇḍalaḥ  Rm 
 śubhraśīlo viśuddhātmā sadāryavratam ācaret 
 etatpuṇyānubhāvena kṣantidharmārthasādhakaḥ  Rm 
 svaparātmasamābhāvī caret maitrīsukhānvitaḥ 
 etatpuṇyavipākena dharmotsāhaguṇānvitaḥ  Rm 
 sarvaduṣṭagaṇāñ jitvā caret satvahite kṛtī 
 etatpuṇyaprabhāvaiś ca sarvakleśān vinirjayan 
 samādhidhāraṇīvijñaś cared dhyānaṃ samāhitaḥ  Rm 
 etatpuṇyavipākaiś ca sarvaśāstrābdhipāragaḥ 
 prajñāratnaṃ samāsādya mahābhijñapadaṃ labhet  Rm 
 etatpuṇyānubhāvaiś cia sarvopāyavidhānavit 
 sarvasatvahitaṃ kṛtvā śubhe nityaṃ samācaret  Rm 
 etatpuṇyānubhāvaiś ca bodhipraṇidhimānasaḥ 
 sarveṣāṃ maṃgalaṃ kṛtvā bhadracaryāṃ samācaret  Rm 
 etatpuṇyaprabhāvaiś ca daśabalasamanvitaḥ 
 sarvamārān vinirjitya cared bodhivrataṃ sadā  Rm 
 etat puṇyabalenaiva saṃbodhijñānam uttamaṃ 
 Rm 
 mahāratnaṃ samāsādya bhavet sarvavināyakaḥ  Rm 
 tataḥ sarvatra lokeṣu kṛtvā bhadrāṇi sarvadā 
 bodhisatvo mahāsatvaḥ saṃbuddhapadam āpnuyāt  Rm 
 etatpuṇyānubhāvaiś ca sarvāṃs traidhātukāsthitān 
 satvān bodhau pratisthāpya kṛtvā dharmamayaṃ jagat  Rm 
 etatpuṇyavipākena dharmarājas tathāgataḥ 
 nirvṛta ālayalīno mahābuddho bhaved dhruvaṃ  Rm 
 evaṃ matvā mahārāja nirvṛtipadalabdhaye 
 yadīchasi tathā puṇyam eva karttavyam ābhavaiḥ  Rm 
 puṇyam eva mahāratnaṃ sarvatrāpi mahānugaṃ 
 sarvārthasiddhidaṃ bhadraṃ saṃbuddhapadasādhanaṃ  Rm 
 iti vijñāya rājendra hitvā pāpānurāgatāṃ 
 puṇyāny evātra saṃsāre karttavyāni hi sarvadā  Rm 
 pāpena sarvadāpy evaṃ durgatīṣv eva saṃgatāḥ 
 mūḍhā kleśāgnisaṃtaptā bhramanti bhavacārake  Rm 
 yāvaṃto duḥkhito duṣṭā saṃsāre kleśatāpitāḥ 
 sarve te pāpakarttāra iti buddhaiḥ prakathyate  Rm 
 iti matvā mahārāja sadā bhadraṃ yadīchasi 
 hitvā pāpānurāgatvaṃ saddharmaṃ cinu sādaraṃ  Rm 
 saddharmaṃ saugataṃ dharmaṃ yal lokaṃ hitasādhanaṃ 
 tenātra sarvadharmāṇāṃ pravaram agram ucyate  Rm 
 tad etaddharmasaṃprāptyai triratnaśaraṇaṃ gataḥ 
 satkṛtya śraddhayā nityaṃ bhajasva samupasthitaḥ  Rm 
 triratne yat kṛtaṃ karmaṃ śubhaṃ vāpy aśubhaṃ tathā 
 tat phalam aprameyam asaṃkhyeya mahattaraṃ  Rm 
 etatpuṇyānubhāvena sarve buddhā munīśvarāḥ 
 jagad dharmamayaṃ kṛtvā niḥkleśā parinirvṛtāḥ  Rm 
 evaṃ vijñāya bhūmīndra hitvā pāparatiṃ sadā 
 triratnabhajanaṃ kṛtvā cara nityaṃ sadā śubhe  Rm 
 abhuktaṃ kṣīyate naiva kvāpi karma śubhāśubhaṃ 
 yenaiva yat kṛtaṃ karmaṃ tenaiva bhujyate phalaṃ  Rm 
 nāgnibhir dahyate karmaṃ dahyate deha eva hi 
 nodakaiḥ klidyate karmaṃ klidyate tanur eva ca  Rm 
 nānilaiḥ śuṣyate karmaṃ kāya evābhiśuṣyate 
 na kṣītau kṣīyate karmaṃ kṣīyate tanur eva hi  Rm 
 anyathāpi bhaven naiva vipāke karmaṇaḥ phalaṃ 
 yathaiva yat kṛtaṃ yena tenaiva bhujyate tathā  Rm 
 kṛṣṇasya karmaṇaḥ pāke duḥkhataiva sadā bhave 
 śubhasya sukhatā nityaṃ miśritasyobhayaṃ tathā  Rm 
 evaṃ karmavipākotthaṃ śubhāśubhaphalaṃ sadā 
 bhuktvā sarvatra saṃsāre bhramanti sarvajaṃtavaḥ  Rm 
 evaṃ matvā mahārāja kṛṣṇāni miśritāni ca 
 vihāyātra śobheṣv eva caritavyaṃ sadā bhave  Rm 
 iti tenārhatādiṣṭaṃ śrutvānaṃdaḥ sa bhūpatiḥ 
 Rm 
 tatheti prativijñapya sajanaḥ prābhya naṃdataḥ  Rm 
 tataḥ sa nṛpatir bhūyo raivataṃ taṃ mahāmatiṃ 
 sucīvaraiḥ samāchādya sāṃjaliḥ praṇatiṃ vyadhāt  Rm 
 punar utthāya bhūpālas tam arhantaṃ kṛtāṃjaliḥ 
 praṇatvā vinayaṃ kurvan kramāc ca prārthayat tathā  Rm 
 bhadantātra prasīdasva kṣamasva me 'parādhatāṃ 
 sarvadā darśanaṃ datvānugrahaṃ kartum arhasi  Rm 
 ity ukte 'nena bhūpena raivataḥ sa prasāditaḥ 
 haṃsarāja ivāplutya bhāsayan khe samāyayau  Rm 
 tatrākāśe samāsīnaḥ prātihāryaṃ pradarśayan 
 lokaiḥ saṃdṛśyamāno 'sau dhyātvā tasthau samujvalan  Rm 
 tatas tair bhikṣubhiḥ śiṣyaiḥ samanvitaḥ prabhāsayan 
 tathākāśāś caraṃ gatvā svāśrame samupāśrayan  Rm 
 tad dṛṣṭvā sa nṛpo lokaiḥ sahātivismayānvitaḥ 
 triratnabhajanaṃ kurvan pracacāra sadā mudā  Rm 
 evaṃ hy adoṣena viśeṣayuktyā pratyakṣaṇakṣyīkṛtalakṣaṇena 
 alaṃkṛtaḥ sādhujanaḥ khalena nighnīkṛto 'pi na vikāram eti  Rm 
 evaṃ svadaivayogena jāyate hy aparādhatā 
 tan nānyasyāparādhatvaṃ vaktavyaṃ kena cit kva cit  Rm 
 iti me guruṇākhyātaṃ tathātra kathyate mayā 
 iti matvā mahārāja sadā dharme samācara  Rm 
 prajāś cāpi tathā rājan bodhayitvā prayatnataḥ 
 bodhimārge pratiṣṭhāpya pālayasva sadādarāt  Rm 
 tathā te maṃgalaṃ nityaṃ sarvaṃ cāpi bhavet sadā 
 kramād bodhiṃ samāsādya saṃbuddhapadam āpnuyāḥ  Rm 
 iti satyaṃ parijñāya triratnaśaraṇaṃ gataḥ 
 satkṛtya śraddhayā nityaṃ bhajasvātra samāhitaḥ  Rm 
 iti tenārhatādiṣṭaṃ śrutvāśokaḥ sa bhūpatiḥ 
 tathā hīti pratijñapya prābhyanandat sapārṣadaḥ  Rm 
 satkṛtyedaṃ narā ye kalimatidaraṇaṃ raivatasyāvadanaṃ śṛṇvanti śrāvayanti pramuditamanaso bhaktiśraddhāprasannāḥ 
 te sarve 'py evam atra vimalasumanasaḥ sarvadā satsukhāni bhuktvā kṛtvā subhadraṃ jinavaranilaye saṃprayānti pramodāṃ  Rm 
  iti ratnāvadānatatve raivatāvadānaṃ samāptam 
 Rm 
 XX Mahiṣāvadāna
 atha sa pārthivo 'sokaḥ kṛtāñjalipuṭo mudā 
 upaguptaṃ guruṃ natvā punar evam abhāṣata  Rm 
 bhadanta śrotum ichāmi punar anyat subhāṣitaṃ 
 tadyathā guruṇākhyātaṃ tathādeṣṭuṃ ca me 'rhati  Rm 
 iti saṃprārthitaṃ rājñā śrutvā so 'rhan mahāmatiḥ 
 upagupto nareṃdraṃ taṃ samālokyaivam ādiśat  Rm 
 sādhu śṛṇu mahārāja yathā me guruṇoditaṃ 
 tathāhaṃ te pravakṣyāmi sarve lokaprabodhane  Rm 
 tadyathā bhagavān buddhaḥ śākyasiṃho munīśvaraḥ 
 sarvajñaḥ sugataḥ śāstā dharmarājo vināyakaḥ  Rm 
 ṣaḍabhijño jagannātho mārajit tu tathāgataḥ 
 puraikasamaye sārddhaṃ bhikṣubhiḥ śrāvakaiḥ saha  Rm 
 cailakair bhikṣuṇībhiś caivam upāsikāgaṇair api 
 upāsākais tathānyaiś ca saddharmaguṇavāṃchibhiḥ  Rm 
 bodhisatvair mahāsatvair brahmendrādisurādhipaiḥ 
 sarve lokādhipaiś cāpi dānavendraiḥ śubhārthibhiḥ  Rm 
 nāgendrair garuḍendraiś ca yakṣagaṃdharvakinnaraiḥ 
 grahai vidyādharaiś cāpi tathānyaiś ca vṛṣārthibhiḥ  Rm 
 stūya mānārcyamānaś ca vaṃdyamāno 'bhinaṃditaḥ 
 sarvasatvahitārthena janapadeṣu sarvataḥ  Rm 
 saddharmaṃ samupādiśya pracacāra sasāṃghikaḥ 
 tathā ca kośale rāṣṭre varaṃ dharmam upādiśat  Rm 
 tato 'nyatrāpi saddharmam upadeṣṭuṃ tato 'carat 
 tatrānyasmin vane prāpto bhagavān sa sasāṃghikaḥ  Rm 
 sarvatra maṃgalaṃ kṛtvā pracacāra śanaiḥ kramāt 
 tatrārāṇye mahān yūtho mahiṣīṇāṃ samācarat  Rm 
 tatraiko mahiṣaś caṇḍo valavīryasamanvitaḥ 
 mahāśṛṃgo mahākāyaḥ pratyavasan madotkaṭaḥ  Rm 
 tatrāsan paṃcamātrāṇi mahiṣapālaśatāni ca 
 sarve tan mahiṣīyūtham anurakṣyādhyuvāsata  Rm 
 tadaikasmin dine tatra bhagavān sa sasaṃghikaḥ 
 pracaraṃs tatpradeśe taṃ mahiṣīyutham aikṣata  Rm 
 tadā te mahiṣīpālā taṃ munīṃdraṃ sasaṃghikaṃ 
 samupāyātam ālokya dūrād evam aghoṣayan  Rm 
 bhagavān mātra samāyāhi pathānyena vrajādhunā 
 asty atra mahiṣo duṣṭas tat sahasā carānyata  Rm 
 Rm 
 iti taiḥ śabditaṃ śrutvā bhagavān sa munīśvaraḥ 
 sasaṃghaḥ samupāśritya tāṃ dṛṣṭvaivam ahhāṣata  Rm 
 alpotsukābhavatv atra bhagavantaḥ kiṃ kuto bhayaṃ 
 kālajño 'haṃ jinendro 'smi tadarthe 'tra samācare  Rm 
 tadā sa mahiṣo duṣṭas taṃ munīndraṃ sasāṃghikaṃ 
 dūrād dṛṣṭvā samutthāya pradudrāva tadantike  Rm 
 tatra tadgaṃdham āghrāya dṛṣṭvā taṃ raktacīvaraṃ 
 ruṣā lāṃgūlam unnāmya saṃmukhaḥ prābhyadhāvata  Rm 
 tatra tena jinendreṇa pañcasiṃhā mahoddhatāḥ 
 abhinirmāya tatpṛṣṭhe sthāpitā bhīmarūpiṇaḥ  Rm 
 tathā nirmāya tatrāgniskaṃdhau dvāv atiprojvalau 
 ubhayoḥ pārśvayos tasya sthāpito bhīmanisvanau  Rm 
 tathātra kūṭasaṃkāśo nirmāya mahatī śilā 
 upariṣṭāt pratiṣṭhāpya darśitā tasya bhītaye  Rm 
 tatra sa mahiṣo 'drākṣīt tān siṃhān pṛṣṭhasaṃsthitān 
 pārśvayor ubhayor agniskaṃdhaur uparitāṃ śilāṃ  Rm 
 evaṃ sa mahiṣo duṣṭo mahābhayam upasthitaṃ 
 samantataḥ samālokya pravikheṭābhimohitaḥ  Rm 
 tatra sa trasito dṛṣṭvā parāyituṃ caturdiśaḥ 
 samantato bhayād vignas tasthau trāṇanirāśrayaḥ  Rm 
 tataḥ sa cakitas tasya munīndrasyābhisaṃmukhaṃ 
 upetya caraṇau natvā śaraṇaṃ samupāyayau  Rm 
 tatra tadbhayabhinnāsyaḥ parikhinnāśayo rudan 
 bhagavaṃtaṃ tam ālokya tasthau 'trāṇāśrayo puraḥ  Rm 
 tadā sa bhagavān dṛṣṭvā mahiṣyaṃ tam upasthitaṃ 
 śaraṇāgatam ālokya dharmam evam upādiśat  Rm 
 bhadramukheti saṃskārāḥ sarve 'nityā bhave dhruvāḥ 
 sarvadharmā anātmanaḥ śāntaṃ nirvāṇam eva hi  Rm 
 iti dharmaravam śrutvā sa tat puṇyānubhāvataḥ 
 pūrvajanmapravṛttāṃtaṃ smṛtvā prarurodānutāpitaḥ  Rm 
 evaṃ taṃ ruditaṃ dṛṣṭvā bhagavān sa munīśvara 
 bodhayituṃ samāśvāsya punar gāthe 'bhyabhāṣata  Rm 
 idānīṃ kiṃ kariṣyāmi tiryagyonigatasya te 
 akṣaṇapratipannasya kiṃ rodiṣi nirarthakaṃ  Rm 
 sādhu prasādyatāṃ cittaṃ mayi kāruṇike jine 
 tiryagyoniṃ virāgyeha tataḥ svargaṃ gamiṣyasi  Rm 
 ity ādiṣṭaṃ munīndreṇa śrutvā sa mahiṣas tadā 
 sarvaṃ smṛtvā purāvṛttaṃ manasaivaṃ vyaciṃtayat  Rm 
 hā mayā durdhiyājñena tyaktvā saddharmasaṃyamaṃ 
 krodhāgninā svayaṃ dagdhā saṃtāpare 'pi tāpitā  Rm 
 yenāhaṃ hā paribhraṣṭaḥ saddharmamaṇinā 'dhunā 
 viṣarāgāgnisaṃtaptaḥ kṛṣṇāhir iva durmatiḥ  Rm 
 Rm 
 tad atra kiṃ kariṣyāmi tiryakjātir ihādhunā 
 kiṃ mamānena kāyena duḥkhe pāpānusādhinā  Rm 
 yatra puṇyaṃ sukhaṃ nāsti tatra kiṃ jīvitena me 
 varam evādya me mṛtyur na tv evaṃ cirajīvitaṃ  Rm 
 avaśyaṃ mṛtyum āpnuyāṃ sarveṣāṃ maraṇaṃ dhruvaṃ 
 tad atra me śarīre kā snehatā jīvite 'pi vā  Rm 
 dhik kāyaṃ jīvitaṃ cāpi yena puṇyaṃ na sādhyate 
 puṇyam eva bhave sāraṃ sarvatra satsukhapradaṃ  Rm 
 puṇyaṃ vinātrā saṃsare kiṃ śrīsaṃpatsukhānvite 
 sarvaṃ vihāya gaṃtavyaṃ puṇyām ekaṃ tadānugaḥ  Rm 
 puṇyam eva jaganmitraṃ puṇyam eva sadānugaḥ 
 puṇyam eva mahatsāraṃ puṇyam eva hitārthadaṃ  Rm 
 tasmāt puṇyaṃ prayatnena sādhanīyaṃ bhave sadā 
 sarvatra sukhatāhetu puṇyam eveti kathyate  Rm 
 tat puṇyaratnasaṃprāptyai buddhasya śaraṇaṃ gataḥ 
 sarvathā smaraṇaṃ kṛtvā bhajeyeha samāhitaḥ  Rm 
 ity evaṃ manasā dhyātvā mahiṣaḥ sa prabodhitaḥ 
 taṃ buddhaṃ śrīghanaṃ natvānusmṛtvābhajān mudā  Rm 
 tataḥ sa bhagavāns tasya dṛṣṭvāśayaviśuddhatāṃ 
 saddharmaṃ samupādiśya sasaṃghaḥ svāśrame yayau  Rm 
 tatrāśrame samāsīno bhagavān sasasāṃghikaḥ 
 sarvasatvahitārthena saṃbodhidharmam ādiśat  Rm 
 taddharmadeśanāṃ śrotuṃ sarve lokāḥ samāgatāḥ 
 brahmaśakrādayo devā lokapālāś ca dānavāḥ  Rm 
 grahā vidyādharāḥ siddhā yakṣagaṃdharvakinnarāḥ 
 garuḍā nāgarājāś ca rākṣasāś ca śubhārthinaḥ  Rm 
 ṛṣayo brāhmaṇāś cāpi nṛpā rājakumārakāḥ 
 vaiśyāc ca maṃtriṇo 'mātyā gṛhasthāś ca mahājanāḥ  Rm 
 vaṇijaḥ sārthavāhāś ca śilpinaḥ paurikā api 
 grāmyā jānapadāś cāpi tīrthyāḥ kārpaṭikā api  Rm 
 evam anye 'pi lokāś ca saddharmaguṇavāṃ chinaḥ 
 sarve te samupāgatya tatrāśrame samāviśat  Rm 
 tatra taṃ śrīghanaṃ dṛṣṭvā bhikṣusaṃghapuraskṛtaṃ 
 natvā pradakṣiṇīkṛtvā samānarcur yathākramaṃ  Rm 
 tatas te praṇatiṃ kṛtvā parivṛtya samaṃtataḥ 
 tat saddharmāmṛtaṃ pātum upatasthuḥ samāhitāḥ  Rm 
 tadā sa bhagavān dṛṣṭvā tān sarvān samupasthitāṃ 
 ādimadhyāṃtakalyāṇaṃ saddharmaṃ samupādiśat  Rm 
 tat saddharmāmṛtaṃ pītvā sarve te saṃprabodhitāḥ 
 dharmaviśeṣam ājñāya triratnaṃ sarvadābhajan  Rm 
 tatra sa mahiṣaḥ pūrvajanmavṛttim anusmaran 
 tadā taddeham utsraṣṭuṃ manasaivaṃ vyaciṃtayat  Rm 
 hā duṣṭena mayā pūrvam ācitaṃ ghorapātakaṃ 
 Rm 
 tenāhaṃ mahiṣo duṣṭo bhavāmy atra yathoditaṃ  Rm 
 tad atra kiṃ prakurvīya paśus tat pāpaśodhaṇaṃ 
 tat triratnam anusmṛtvā careyāham upoṣadhaṃ  Rm 
 datvātrāham imaṃ kāyaṃ satvebhyaḥ śraddhayā 'dhunā 
 manasā sugataṃ dhyātvā martuṃ tiṣṭheya sāṃprataṃ  Rm 
 tad imaṃ deham utkṛtya tvagmānsarudhirādikaṃ 
 asthimajjādi sarvaṃ ca bhujantu prāṇino mudā  Rm 
 ye ye satvā imaṃ dehaṃ bhujanti surasaṃ mudā 
 te te sarve sadā dharmaṃ kṛtvā yāntu surālāyaṃ  Rm 
 tathaitat puṇyapākena muktvāsmān pāpakāśrayāt 
 āsādya sadgatau janma bhajeyaṃ sugataṃ sadā  Rm 
 iti dhyātvā viniścitya mahiṣaḥ sa prasannadhīḥ 
 tyaktvāhāraṃ tapaśvīva buddhaṃ smṛtvācarat tapaḥ  Rm 
 tathā sa mahiṣo dhyātvā triratnaṃ cābhyanusmaran 
 dehaṃ tyaktvā viśuddhātmā surālayaṃ samāyayau  Rm 
 tatra svarge sa utpanno mahāsukhasamanvitaḥ 
 vismitābhiprasannātmā tadaivaṃ samaciṃtayat  Rm 
 aho hi jāyate saukhyaṃ kutaś cyutvā kuhācare 
 kasya puṇyavipākena mamaivaṃ jāyate śubhaṃ  Rm 
 iti ciṃtayatas tasya mahiṣapūrviṇas tathā 
 vismayākrāṃtacittasya samutpannābhavan matiḥ  Rm 
 aho tiryaggateś cyutvā devaloka ihāsare 
 saṃbuddhasmṛtipuṇyena devo bhavāmi sāṃprataṃ  Rm 
 tad ahaṃ tasya munīndrasya draṣṭuṃ gacheya sāṃprataṃ 
 śraddhayā samupāśritya saddharmaṃ śṛṇuyāṃ punaḥ  Rm 
 iti mahiṣapūrvī sa devaputraḥ pramoditaḥ 
 tatra tasya munīndrasya darśane gaṃtum aichata  Rm 
 tataḥ sa muditaḥ snātvā śuddhadivyāṃvarāvṛtaḥ 
 divyagaṃdhānuliptāṃgo divyālaṃkārabhūṣitaḥ  Rm 
 divyapūjopahārāṇi gṛhītvā devagaṇaiḥ saha 
 tasyāṃ rātrau munīndrasya bhāsayann āśrame yayau  Rm 
 tatra taṃ śrīghanaṃ dṛṣṭvā muditaḥ samupāsaran 
 natvā pradakṣiṇīkṛtya samānarcca yathāvidhiḥ  Rm 
 tatas tasya munīndrasya sāṃjaliḥ sa praṇamya ca 
 saddharmadeśanāṃ śrotuṃ purataḥ samupāśrayat  Rm 
 tathā te tat sahāyāś ca devaputrāḥ prasāditāḥ 
 bhagavaṃtaṃ sāṃjalayaḥ upāśrayan  Rm 
 tataḥ sa bhagavān dṛṣṭvā sarvāns tān samupasthitān 
 āryyasatyasamārabhya saddharmaṃ samupādiśat  Rm 
 tatsaddharmāmṛtaṃ pītvā saha devaiḥ pramoditaḥ 
 devo mahiṣapūrvi sa dharmaviśeṣam āptavān  Rm 
 satkāyaduṣṭibhūmīndhraṃ viṃśatiśikharodgataṃ 
 nirbhidya jñānavajreṇa śrotaāpattim āyayau  Rm 
 Rm 
 tātaḥ sa dṛṣṭasatyas taṃ bhagavantaṃ munīśvaraṃ 
 kṛtāṃjaliḥ puṭo natvā trir udānam udānayat  Rm 
 bhagavann idam asmākaṃ kṛtaṃ na janakena hi 
 na mātrā na ca rājñāpi nānyena kena cit khalu  Rm 
 bhavataiva yad asmākaṃ kṛtapāpaviśodhanaṃ 
 tenābhiśoṣitāśeṣarudhirāśrusāritpariḥ  Rm 
 laṃghitā asthiśailāś ca pihitā pāpapaddhatiḥ 
 vivṛtāḥ svargamārgāś ca mokṣamārgaś ca darśitaḥ  Rm 
 mayāptaṃ vimalaṃ cakṣuḥ śāntam āryapadaṃ tathā 
 duḥkhārṇavaḥ samuttīrṇo bodhimārgo 'pi dṛśyate  Rm 
 tad bhavatāṃ kṛpādṛṣṭeḥ prasādān mama sāṃprataṃ 
 saṃsārajanma sāphalyaṃ buddhaputrāsmy ahaṃ yataḥ  Rm 
 adyārabhya sadā nityaṃ bhavatāṃ śaraṇaṃ gataḥ 
 bodhau cittaṃ samādhāya cariṣyāmi śubhāṃ cariṃ  Rm 
 tad atrānugrahaṃ kṛtvā bhavāñ chāstā jagaguruḥ 
 kṛpayā sarvadā paśyann evaṃ māṃ trātum arhati  Rm 
 iti saṃprārthitaṃ tena suparvaṇā niśamya saḥ 
 śāstā tasyāśayaṃ śuddhaṃ samalokyaivam ādiśat  Rm 
 sadho śṛṇu hitaṃ vakṣye sadā bhadraṃ yadīchasi 
 triratnaṃ śaraṇaṃ gatvā bhaja nityaṃ samādarāt  Rm 
 ye buddhaśaraṇaṃ kṛtvā bhajaṃti śraddhayā sadā 
 māracaryābhimuktās te saṃprayāṃti jinālayaṃ  Rm 
 ye dharmaṃ saugataṃ nityaṃ śṛṇvanti śraddhayā mudā 
 sarvapāpābhimuktās te saṃprayānti sukhāvatīṃ  Rm 
 ye ca saṃghe prakurvanti satkāraṃ śraddhayādarāt 
 te sarve durgater muktvā saṃprayānti surālayaṃ  Rm 
 triratnaśaraṇaṃ kṛtvā ye bhajanti sadādarāt 
 durgatiṃ te na gachaṃti sadā gachaṃti sadgatiṃ  Rm 
 sadgatau te sadā sthitvā triratnaṃ śaraṇaṃ gatāḥ 
 kṛtvā lokahitaṃ saukhyaṃ bhuktvā ramanti sarvadā  Rm 
 tataḥ pāramitāḥ sarvāḥ paripūrya yathākramaṃ 
 trividhāṃ bodhim āsadya nirvṛtiṃ samavāpnuyuḥ  Rm 
 iti nirvāṇasatsaukhyaḥ prāptuṃ yadi samichasi 
 triratnaṃ śaraṇaṃ kṛtvā bhaja nityaṃ samāhitaḥ  Rm 
 etatpuṇyānubhāvena pariśuddhas trimaṃḍalaḥ 
 kramād bodhiṃ samāsādya saṃbuddhapadam āpnuyāḥ  Rm 
 ity ādiṣṭaṃ munīndreṇa śrutvā sa paribodhitāḥ 
 tathety abhyanumoditvā punar evam abhāṣata  Rm 
 adya me saphalaṃ saṃpūritaṃ manorathaṃ 
 bodhiratnābhisaṃpanno buddhaputro 'smi sāṃprataṃ  Rm 
 sarvadā bhavatām eva śaraṇe 'haṃ samāsthitaḥ 
 triratnabhajanaṃ kurvañ cariṣye bodhisaṃvaraṃ  Rm 
 iti saṃprārthanāṃ kṛtvā devaputraḥ sa moditaḥ 
 Rm 
 śrīghanaṃ taiḥ punar natvā sasahāyo divaṃ yayau  Rm 
 tatra svarge sa saṃprāpto devaiḥ saha samāśritaḥ 
 triratnasmaraṇaṃ kurvan saukhyaṃ bhuktvā samācarat  Rm 
 tasyāṃ rātrau mahatkāntiṃ prabhāṃ dṛṣṭvā savismayāḥ 
 sarve te mahiṣīpālā vabhūvuḥ śaṃkitāśayāḥ  Rm 
 tataḥ prātaḥ samutthāya sarve te kautukānvitāḥ 
 saṃmīlya sahasā tatra buddhāśrame upācaran  Rm 
 tatra taṃ śrīghanaṃ dṛṣṭvā sarve te pratimoditāḥ 
 kṛtāṃjalipuṭo natvā samupatasthur ādarāt  Rm 
 tadā sa bhagāvān dṛṣṭvā tān sarvān samupasthitān 
 ādimadhyāṃtakalyāṇaṃ dideśa dharmam uttamaṃ  Rm 
 tat saddharmāmṛtaṃ pītvā sarve te pratibodhitāḥ 
 bhagavaṃtaṃ punar natvā paprachur evam ādarāt  Rm 
 bhagavann adya rātrau ka ihāśrame prabhāsayan 
 bhavatāṃ samupāyātas tat samādeṣṭum arhati  Rm 
 iti tair mahiṣīpālaiḥ paripṛṣṭe sa sarvavit 
 bhagavāṃs tān samālokya purāvṛttim upādiśat  Rm 
 yo 'trāsau mahiṣo duṣṭo dṛṣṭvāsmān samupadrutaḥ 
 samantato bhayaṃ dṛṣṭvā trasto me śaraṇaṃ gataḥ  Rm 
 tadā maddharmam ākarṇya pūrvajātim anusmaran 
 mayi cittaṃ prasādyaiva tyaktvāhārā tyajan tanuṃ  Rm 
 tato 'smatsmṛtipuṇyena pāpamukto viśuddhadhīḥ 
 svargaloke samutpanno devo bhavati sāṃprataṃ  Rm 
 sa eṣa devaputro 'dya niśāyām atra bhāsayan 
 devalokaiḥ sahāyāto darśanāya mamālāye  Rm 
 matsaddharmaṃ samākarṇya dṛṣṭasatyaḥ sa harṣitaḥ 
 devasaṃghaiḥ saha svarge svālaye pragatas tathā  Rm 
 ity ādiṣṭaṃ munīndreṇa śrutvātivismayoddhatāḥ 
 sarve te mahiṣīpālā mitha evaṃ samabruvan  Rm 
 aho citra hi yan nāma tiryyagyonigato 'pi saḥ 
 buddhaṃ sadgurum āsādya dharmaṃ śrutvābhavat sudhīḥ  Rm 
 sadgurau sugate cittaṃ prasādya viratāśanaḥ 
 trirātnasmaraṇaṃ kṛtvā prāṇaṃ tyaktvā divaṃ yayau  Rm 
 tato 'pīha samāgatya saṃbuddhaṃ śaraṇaṃ gataḥ 
 abhyarcya dharmam ākarṇya dṛṣṭasatyo divaṃ yayau  Rm 
 svarge 'pi tat tathā nityaṃ sadguroḥ śaraṇaṃ gataḥ 
 śraddhayā bhajanaṃ kurvaṃ chubhe 'carat samāhitaḥ  Rm 
 dhanyo 'yaṃ sugataḥ śāstā sarvasatvaśubhaṃkaraḥ 
 yatra cittaṃ prasādyaiva paśur api divaṃ gataḥ  Rm 
 vayaṃ tu mānavāḥ sarve katham enaṃ munīśvaraṃ 
 sadguruṃ samupāsādya śraddhayā na bhajemahi  Rm 
 Rm 
 tathā saddharmam ākarṇya prasādād asya sadguroḥ 
 atkṛtya sarvadā bhadraṃ na lābhema kathaṃ vayaṃ  Rm 
 viśeṣadharmam ājñāya dṛṣṭasatyāḥ samāhitāḥ 
 triratnabhajanaṃ kṛtvā nūnaṃ gachema sadgatiṃ  Rm 
 tad atra sadguror asya munīndrasyādhunā vayaṃ 
 sarve 'pi śraddhayābhyarcya bhajemahi samādarāt  Rm 
 tat sāddharmaṃ samākarṇya śraddhayā samupasthitāḥ 
 triratnabhajanaṃ kṛtvā caremahi śubhe sadā  Rm 
 tadādau sugatasyāsya sasaṃghasyā 'dhunā vayaṃ 
 yathārhabhojanenātra pūjayema prapuṣṭaye  Rm 
 iti saṃbhāṣaṇāṃ kṛtvā sarve te pratimoditāḥ 
 tatheti saṃmataṃ kṛtvā tatra buddhāśrame yayuḥ  Rm 
 tatra taṃ śrīghanaṃ dṛṣṭvā sasaṃghaṃ taṃ pramoditāḥ 
 sarvasāṃjalayo natvā prārthayann evam ādarāt  Rm 
 bhagavan nātha sarvajña bhagavaṃtaṃ sasaṃghikaṃ 
 pūjayituṃ samichāmas tann atrānugrahaṃ kuru  Rm 
 iti taiḥ prārthitaṃ śrutvā bhagavān sa munīśvaraḥ 
 teṣāṃ puṇyābhisaṃvṛddhyai tūṣṇībhūtvādhyuvāsa tat  Rm 
 tathādhyuvāsitaṃ matvā sarve te pariharṣitāḥ 
 pādau tasya munīndrasya natvā nijālayaṃ yayuḥ  Rm 
 tatra te muditāḥ sarve dadhikṣīrodanādikaṃ 
 yathārhabhojyasāmagriṃ sahasā samasādhayan  Rm 
 tatas te samaye gatvā tatra buddhāśrame mudā 
 sasāṃghikaṃ munīndraṃ taṃ praṇatvaivaṃ nyavedayan  Rm 
 bhagavan nātha sarvajña samayo varttate 'dhunā 
 tat saṃgha bhagavān pūjāṃ pratigrahitum arhati  Rm 
 iti taiḥ prārthite sarve bhagavān sasasāṃghikaḥ 
 utthāya bhojanakṣetre upācarān prabhāsayan  Rm 
 tatra pādyaṃ samādāya saṃbuddhapramukhāḥ kramāt 
 sarve te sāṃghikās tatra svasvāsane samāśrayan  Rm 
 tāṃ buddhapramukhān sarvān sāṃghikān svāsanāśritān 
 dṛṣṭvā te muditā sarve sāmānarcur yathākramaṃ  Rm 
 tatas te surasair bhojyaiḥ kṣīrodanaiḥ savyaṃjanaiḥ 
 praṇītair bhagavaṃtaṃ taṃ sasaṃghaṃ samatoṣayan  Rm 
 tatas taṃ sugataṃ tṛptaṃ sasāṃghikaṃ samīkṣya te 
 tat pātrāṇy apanīyāśu tad dhastādi samaśodhayan  Rm 
 tataḥ sapūgatāmburāmahauṣadharasāyanaṃ 
 saṃbuddhapramukhebhyas te saṃghebhyaḥ pradadur mudā  Rm 
 tatas te mahiṣīpālāḥ kṛtāṃjalipūṭā mudā 
 śrīghanaṃ taṃ sasaṃghaṃ ca natvā samupatasthire  Rm 
 tathā tan samupāsīnān sarvān dṛṣṭvā sa sarvavit 
 Rm 
 āryadharmaṃ samādiśya bodhimārge 'bhyayojayat  Rm 
 tat saddharmāmṛtaṃ pītvā sarve te 'bhyanumoditāḥ 
 saṃbuddhaśāsane tatra pravrajituṃ samīkṣire  Rm 
 tatās te mahiṣīpālāḥ sarve kṛtvābhisaṃmataṃ 
 kṛtāṃjalipuṭā natvā prārthayan taṃ munīśvaraṃ  Rm 
 bhāgavaṃ nātha sarvajña bhavatāṃ śāsane vayaṃ 
 pravrajituṃ samichāmas tan no 'nvāhartum arhati  Rm 
 iti taiḥ prārthitaṃ śrutvā bhagavān sa munīśvaraḥ 
 tān viśuddhāśayān sarvān samālokyaivam ādiśat  Rm 
 mātāpitror vinānujñāṃ pravrajyāṃ na dadāmy ahaṃ 
 tad anujñāṃ samādāya preta dāsyāmi vas tadā  Rm 
 ity ādiṣṭe munīndreṇa sarve te pratinaṃditāḥ 
 taṃ munīndraṃ praṇatvāśu svasvagehaṃ yayur mudā  Rm 
 tatra te sahasā gatvā samātāpitṛvāṃdhavān 
 paribodhya prayatnena prāpyānujñāṃ samācaraṃ  Rm 
 tatra te sahasā gatvā bhagavata upāsṛtāḥ 
 pādau sāṃjalayor natvā prārthayann evam ādarāt  Rm 
 bhagavan sarvavit pitṛprāptānujñāḥ samāgatāḥ 
 tatrānugraham ādhāya pravrajyāṃ dātum arhati  Rm 
 iti taiḥ prārthite śāstā bhagavān savyapāṇinā 
 teṣāṃ śiras susaṃspṛṣṭvā samālokyaivam ādiśat  Rm 
 sameta bhikṣavaḥ sarve yūyaṃ śraddhāsamaṃgitāḥ 
 pravrajyāvratam ādhāya carata brahmacārikāṃ  Rm 
 ity ādiṣṭe munīndreṇa sarve te muṇḍitā vabhuḥ 
 khikkhirīpātradharttāraḥ kākhāyacīvarāvṛtāḥ  Rm 
 tataḥ śastuḥ prasādena sarve te vimalāśayāḥ 
 pralabdhabodhisaccittāḥ śuddhaśīlā jiteṃdriyāḥ  Rm 
 bhitvāvidyāguṇāḥ samyak prāptavidyāviśāradāḥ 
 pratisaṃvitsusaṃprāptāḥ satyamārgasamanvitāḥ  Rm 
 samādhidhāraṇīvidyā ghaṭamānāḥ samāhitāḥ 
 kṣamānvitāḥ śubhātmāno yogino bhikṣavo 'bhavan  Rm 
 tatas te sarvasaṃsāraṃ matvānityaṃ cālācalaṃ 
 dṛṣṭvā ca sarvasaṃskāragatīr ahivighātinīḥ  Rm 
 sarvakleśagaṇān hitvā jitvā māragaṇān api 
 sākṣād arhatvam āsādya pracerur brahmacārikāḥ  Rm 
 tatas te bhikṣavaḥ sarve pariśuddhatrimaṃḍalāḥ 
 vītasaṃgā mahābhijñā nirvikalpā niraṃjanāḥ  Rm 
 samaloṣṭakasauvarṇāḥ satkāralābhanispṛhāḥ 
 akāśasamacittāṅgā bhave lābhaparāṅmukhāḥ  Rm 
 devāsurādi lokānāṃ traidhātukanivāsināṃ 
 pūjyā mānyāś ca vaṃdyāś ca babhūvur bodhicāriṇaḥ  Rm 
 Rm 
 tad dṛṣṭvā bhikṣavaḥ sarve vismayoddhatamānasāḥ 
 bhagavaṃtaṃ muniṃ natvā papracbus tat purākṛtaṃ  Rm 
 bhagavan kāni karmāṇi tena mahiṣapūrviṇā 
 kṛtāni devaputreṇa yair asau mahiṣo 'bhavat  Rm 
 ebhiś ca mahiṣīpālaiḥ kiṃ karma prakṛtaiḥ purā 
 yenārhatvaṃ samāsādya bhavaṃti brahmacāriṇaḥ  Rm 
 etat sarvaṃ samādiśya bhavāñ chāstātra sāṃprataṃ 
 asmākaṃ api cetāṃsi prabodhayitum arhati  Rm 
 iti tair bhikṣubhiḥ pṛṣṭe bhagavān sa munīśvaraḥ 
 tān sarvān sāṃghikān bhikṣūn samālokyaivam ādiśat  Rm 
 śṛṇuta bhikṣavaḥ sarve tena mahiṣapūrviṇā 
 purā kṛtāni karmāṇi tāni vakṣyāmi sāṃprataṃ  Rm 
 ebhiś ca mahiṣipālaiḥ purā yāni kṛtāny api 
 tāni sarvāṇi karmāṇi vakṣyāmi ca tathā 'dhunā  Rm 
 tadyathābhūt purā buddhaḥ kāśyapo 'rhans tathāgataḥ 
 sarvajñaḥ sugataḥ śāstā dharmarājo vināyākaḥ  Rm 
 bhagavān sa tadā pūryyāṃ varāṇasyā upāśrame 
 mṛgadāve samāśritya vijahāra sasāṃghikaḥ  Rm 
 tadā tasya munīndrasya śāsane tripiṭo yatiḥ 
 bhikṣur eko mahāvijño niścayārthaviśāradaḥ  Rm 
 tadaikasamaye bhikṣupaṃcaśataiḥ puraskṛtaḥ 
 sa sabhāyāṃ samāsīnaḥ saddharmaṃ samupādiśat  Rm 
 tasya te bhikṣavaḥ śikṣāḥ śaikṣāś ca saṃścayānvitāḥ 
 tripiṭārthaṃ parijñātuṃ paprachus taṃ guruṃ muhuḥ  Rm 
 evaṃ tair bhikṣubhiḥ pṛṣṭe sa guruḥ pratiroṣitaḥ 
 tān sarvāñ chrāvakāñ chiṣyāñ chaikṣāṃś ca paryabhāṣata  Rm 
 tatas te śrāvakāḥ sarve dṛṣṭvā taṃ ruṣitaṃ guruṃ 
 praṇatvā vinayaṃ kṛtvā punar evam abhāsire  Rm 
 bhavanta mā kṛthā roṣaṃ prasīdasva kṛpānidhe 
 vyākhyātaṃ bhavatā samyak tad asmābhi na budhyate  Rm 
 tad bhūyo 'pi bhavān etadarthaṃ samyak suvistaraṃ 
 asmac cetaṃ prabodhārthaṃ samupādeṣṭum arhati  Rm
