 yadīchasi sadā bhadre caritavyaṃ tvayādarāt  Rm 
 bhadraṃ tu jāyate śīghraṃ triratnabhajanodyamāt 
 tat triratnam upāśritya bhaja nityaṃ samāhitaḥ  Rm 
 triratne yat kṛtaṃ karmaṃ tan naiva kṣiṇuyā kvacit 
 yāvad bodhipadaṃ dadyā evaṃ mahattaraṃ vṛṣaṃ  Rm 
 ye triratnaṃ bhajanty atra na te gachanti durgatiṃ 
 sadaiva sadgatiṃ yānti bodhiṃ ca samavāpnuyuḥ  Rm 
 tisro hīmāḥ samākhyātā agrāḥ prajñaptayo nṛpa 
 yatra kiṃ cit kṛtaṃ karma tadvipāko mahān smṛtāḥ  Rm 
 tadyathā katamās tisro agrāḥ prajñaptayaḥ smṛtāḥ 
 triratne prakṛtā yās tā agrāḥ prajñaptayaḥ smṛtāḥ  Rm 
 tadyathā sarvasatvānāṃ traidhātukanivāsināṃ 
 buddha eva mahān agro jyeṣṭhaḥ śreṣṭho varottamaḥ  Rm 
 ye buddhaśraddhayā bhaktyā prabhajaṃti prasāditāḥ 
 sarve 'tyagraprasannās te jyeṣṭhāḥ śreṣṭhā varottamāḥ  Rm 
 tadagrābhiprasannānāṃ vipāko 'py agra uttamaḥ 
 tathā dharmāś ca ye sarve saṃskṛtā vāpy asaṃkṛtāḥ  Rm 
 teṣām api ca sarveṣāṃ buddhadharmāgra ucyate 
 tatra dharme prasannā ye te 'gre hi saṃprasannitāḥ 
 tad agrābhiprasannānāṃ vipāko 'py agra ucyate  Rm 
 ye ca saṃghā gaṇās teṣāṃ buddhasaṃgho 'gra ucyate 
 tatra saṃghe prasannā ye te 'gre 'bhisaṃprasādinaḥ  Rm 
 teṣām agraprasannānāṃ vipāko 'py agra ucyate 
 etāḥ prajñaptayas tisro hy agrāḥ khyāto munīśvaraiḥ  Rm 
 tad atra śraddhayā rāja triratne saṃprasannadhīḥ 
 satkāraiḥ samupāśritya bhaja nityaṃ samādarāt  Rm 
 etatpuṇyam asaṃkhyeyam aprameyaṃ mahattaraṃ 
 sarvasatvamahāsaukhyaguṇasaṃpattidāyakaṃ  Rm 
 evaṃ matvā mahatpuṇyaṃ sarvān satvān prabodhayat 
 triratnabhajanotsāhaiś cārayasva śubhe nṛpa  Rm 
 evaṃ te sarvadā bhadraṃ sarvatrāpi bhaved dhruvaṃ 
 kramād bodhiṃ samāsādya saṃbuddhapadam āpnuyāḥ  Rm 
 ity ādiṣṭaṃ munīndreṇa śrutvā sa nṛpatir mudā 
 tatheti hi pratijñāya prābhyanaṃdat prasāditaḥ  Rm 
 tataḥ sa nṛpa utthāya natvā taṃ jagadīśvaraṃ 
 mahānaṃdamahotsāhaiḥ svapuraṃ sajano yayau  Rm 
 tatra sa nṛpatī rājā prāsādatalam āśritaḥ 
 sa maṃtripaurikān sarvān samāmaṃtryaivam ādiśat  Rm 
 maṃtriṇaḥ paurikāḥ sarve śṛṇudhvaṃ vacanaṃ mama 
 Rm 
 yadi vāṃchāsti vo bhadre triratnaṃ bhajatādarat  Rm 
 yavad ayaṃ jagacchāstā viharaty atra sāṃghikaḥ 
 tāvad asya munīndrasya bhajata sarvadotsavaiḥ  Rm 
 vihāre sarvadā gatvā śraddhayā samupāśritāḥ 
 tat saddharmāmṛtaṃ pītvā mudā carata sadvṛtau  Rm 
 sarvāṃś ca saugatān bhikṣūn sarvopakaraṇair api 
 satkṛtya śraddhayāmaṃtrya mānayadhvaṃ sadādarāt  Rm 
 etan me vacanaṃ śrutvā triratnaśaraṇaṃ gatāḥ 
 saṃbodhipraṇidhānena carata bodhicārikāṃ  Rm 
 tathā te maṃgalaṃ nityaṃ sarvatrāpi bhaved dhruvaṃ 
 kramād bodhiṃ samāsādya labhata saugatiṃ gatiṃ  Rm 
 ity ādiṣṭaṃ munīndreṇa śrutvā te maṃtriṇo janāḥ 
 sarve vīrādayo lokās tatheti pratiśuśruvuḥ  Rm 
 tadā sarve 'pi te lokāḥ saddharmasādhanodyatāḥ 
 triratnabhajanaṃ kṛtvā pracerire samoditāḥ  Rm 
 tadārabhya sadā tatra maṃgalaṃ nirupadravaṃ 
 sarvatra sarvadāpy āsīt triratnasyānubhāvataḥ  Rm 
 iti me guruṇādiṣṭaṃ tathā te kathyate mayā 
 tvam apy evaṃ sadā rājan triratnaṃ śaraṇaṃ gataḥ  Rm 
 saddharmaṃ samupāśritya cara nityaṃ sadā śubhe 
 lokāś cāpi mahārāja bodhayitvā prayatnataḥ 
 triratnaśaraṇe sthāpya pālanīyāḥ sadā tvayā  Rm 
 evaṃ te maṃgalaṃ nityaṃ sarvatrāpi bhaved dhruvaṃ 
 kramād bodhiṃ samāsādya saṃbuddhapadam āpnuyāḥ  Rm 
 iti tenārhatādiṣṭaṃ śrutvāśokaḥ sa bhūmipaḥ 
 tathety abhyanumoditvā prābhyanaṃdat sapārṣadaḥ  Rm 
 dūtāvadānaṃ yad idaṃ mudā ye śṛṇvaṃti ye cāpi niśāmayanti 
 te sarva evaṃ tridive vrajanti saṃbuddhaloke 'pi saranti cānte  Rm 
  iti śriratnāvadānatatve dūtāvadānaṃ samāptam 
 Rm 
 XXVI Tairthikāvadāna
 athāśoko mahīpālaḥ kṛtāṃjalipuṭo mudā 
 upaguptaṃ tam arhantaṃ praṇatvaivam abravīt  Rm 
 bhadanta śrotum ichāmi punar anyat subhāṣitaṃ 
 tadyathā guruṇādiṣṭaṃ tathādeṣṭuṃ ca me 'rhati  Rm 
 iti saṃprārthitaṃ rājñā śrutvā sa sugatātmajaḥ 
 upagupto nareṃdraṃ taṃ samāmaṃtryaivam ādiśat  Rm 
 sādhu śṛṇu mahārāja yathā me guruṇoditaṃ 
 tathātrāhaṃ pravakṣyāmi śrutvānumodanāṃ kuru  Rm 
 tadyathā bhagavāṃc chāstā śrīghano 'rhan munīśvaraḥ 
 sarvajñaḥ sugato nātho dharmarājo vināyakaḥ  Rm 
 bhikṣubhiḥ śrāvakaiḥ sārddhaṃ tathā sarvaiś ca sāṃghikaiḥ 
 tatraiva jetakodyāne vihāre vyaharat purā  Rm 
 tad dharmadeśanāṃ śrotuṃ sarve lokaiḥ samāgataiḥ 
 devadānavagaṃdharvair yakṣakinnararākṣasaiḥ  Rm 
 siddhair vidyādharaiś cāpi nāgendrair garuḍair api 
 lokapālaiḥ sasainyaiś ca brāhmaṇaiś ca maharṣibhiḥ  Rm 
 yogibhir yatibhiś cāpi nirgranthibhiś ca tāpasaiḥ 
 rājabhiḥ kṣatriyaiś cāpi tathā rājakumārakaiḥ  Rm 
 vaiśyaiś ca maṃtribhiḥ śreṣṭhair gṛhasthaiś ca mahājanaiḥ 
 vaṇigbhiḥ sārthavāhaiś ca śilpibhiḥ paurikair api  Rm 
 grāmyair jānapadaiś cāpi kārpaṭikais tathāparaiḥ 
 triratnadarśanotsāhaiḥ saddharmaguṇavāṃchibhiḥ  Rm 
 satkṛto mānito nityaṃ pūjyamāno 'bhivaṃditaḥ 
 sarvasatvahitārthena varṣaṃ dharmāmṛtaṃ sadā  Rm 
 tadā tatra pure rājā prasenajin nṛpādhipaḥ 
 saṃbuddhaśāsanaṃ dhṛtvā triratnam abhajan mudā  Rm 
 tad dṛṣṭvā tīrthikāḥ sarve īrṣyāroṣāhatāśayāḥ 
 saṃmīlya saugataṃ dharmaṃ pratikṣipyaivam abruvan  Rm 
 bhavanto yad ayaṃ buddhaḥ sarvajña ṛddhimān kṛtī 
 tatsarvān imāṃ lokān svaṃ dharme saṃniyojayet  Rm 
 tadāsmadvacanaṃ śrotum apīchen nātra kaścana 
 sarve naḥ śrāvakāś cāpi bhajeyuḥ sugataṃ jinaṃ  Rm 
 tadā sarve vayaṃ lokai niṃdyamānaḥ samaṃtataḥ 
 katham atra cariṣyāmas tad anyatra caremahi  Rm 
 iti sarvair api prokte tīrthikopāsako dvijaḥ 
 sarvāns tāns tīrthikaṃ dṛṣṭvā punar evam abhāṣata  Rm 
 Rm 
 bhavaṃto ma viṣīdatvaṃ kartuṃ arhati sarvathā 
 tad upāyaṃ kariṣyāmi yenānyatra carej jinaḥ  Rm 
 iti tāns tīrthikān sarvān bodhayitvā sa durmatiḥ 
 nṛpater antike gatvā sādaram evam abravīt  Rm 
 śṛṇu rājan mahābhāga yad dhitaṃ te tad ucyate 
 tathā tvayā samādhāya caritavyaṃ sadādarāt  Rm 
 yad ayaṃ muṇḍito bhikṣuḥ kuladharmavināśakṛt 
 jātidharmaparibhraṣṭaḥ saṃsāravṛttiniṃdakaḥ  Rm 
 māyāvī kutsitācāro duḥśīlo lokavaṃcakaḥ 
 svayaṃ naṣṭaḥ parāṃś cāpi nāśayitum ihāgataḥ  Rm 
 tad asya darśanaṃ rājaṃ karttavyaṃ na kadā cana 
 grahītavyaṃ na nāmāpi śrotavyaṃ nāpi tad vacaḥ  Rm 
 satkāraṃ na ca karttavyaṃ dātavyaṃ nāpi kiṃ cana 
 āśrame 'pi na gantavyaṃ sthātavyaṃ na tadantike  Rm 
 darśanaṃ ye prakurvanti tasya bhikṣor durātmanaḥ 
 te sarve narake yāyuḥ sadgatiṃ na kadā cana  Rm 
 ye ca śṛṇvanti tad vākyaṃ sarve te nilayaṃ gatāḥ 
 tīvraduḥkhābhisaṃtaptā vaseyur anutāpitāḥ  Rm 
 satkāraṃ ye ca kurvaṃti sarve te vilayaṃ gatāḥ 
 daridrā durgatiṃ gatvā bhrameyur nihatāśayāḥ  Rm 
 ye ca dānaṃ prakurvanti tatrāśirluhitāśayāḥ 
 te 'pi ca narake yātā duḥkhāny evam avāpnuyuḥ  Rm 
 tadāśrame ca gachaṃti sarve te duritāṅkitāḥ 
 kuṣṭhādi rogasaṃtaptā yāyuś ca niraye 'cirāt  Rm 
 ye ca taiḥ saha tiṣṭhanti te sarve pāpasaṃgitāḥ 
 tīvraduḥkhāgnisaṃdagdhā careyu niraye sadā  Rm 
 gṛhnanti ye ca mannāma teṣāṃ geheṣu sarvadā 
 lakṣmīr maiva śrayet tatra nairṛtir eva saṃśrayet  Rm 
 ye buddhaṃ bhajanty atra te te sarve 'py adharmiṇaḥ 
 kadāpi sadgatiṃ naiva yāṃti dūragatim eva hi  Rm 
 iti matvā mahārāja sadā bhadraṃ yadīchasi 
 satkāraṃ darśanaṃ tasya karttavyaṃ naiva ke cana  Rm 
 kiṃ dharmaṃ saugataṃ dharmaṃ yan mithyā parikalpitaṃ 
 tat tasya duryater dharmaṃ śrotavyaṃ naiva kena cit  Rm 
 yasya dharmo hi sarvatra vedaśāstre na gaṇyate 
 sa kiṃ dharmātmako buddhas tat tatra maṃgalaṃ na hi  Rm 
 iti tenoditaṃ śrutvā sa paribodhitaḥ 
 triratnabhajanotsāhaśaithilyakṣubhito 'bhavat  Rm 
 tatas tasya vacaḥ śrutvā tīrthikopāsakasya saḥ 
 nṛpatis tairthike dharme 'bhilalāṣa prasāditaḥ  Rm 
 Rm 
 tatraiko gṛhabhṛc chreṣṭhī saṃbuddhopāsakaḥ sudhīḥ 
 taṃ tīrthyopāsakaṃ dṛṣṭvā bodhayitum abhāṣata  Rm 
 kim evaṃ durmate buddho dharmarājo 'pi niṃdyate 
 mā maivaṃ vadatām atra tvam eva narakaṃ vrajeḥ  Rm 
 yo loke samutpannaḥ sarvakleśān vinirjayan 
 jitvā māragaṇān sarvān saṃbodhijñānam āptavān  Rm 
 sarvai brahmādibhir lokaiḥ saṃstuto vaṃdito 'rcitaḥ 
 mānitaḥ satkṛto buddhas tvayaiva niṃdyate kathaṃ  Rm 
 yenaiva trijagallokāṃ putravat pratipālitaṃ 
 pūjanīyaḥ kathaṃ nāthaṃ dharmarājo munīśvaraḥ  Rm 
 buddha eva jagannātho dayāluḥ sadguṇākaraḥ 
 sarvasatvahitādhāno 'dvayavādī vināyakaḥ  Rm 
 sarvajñaḥ sugato bhadrarūpaḥ sarvahitārthabhṛt 
 sarvavidyādhipaḥ śāstā saṃbodhimārgadeśakaḥ  Rm 
 nirjitakleśa ātmajñaḥ ṣaḍabhijño jagadguruḥ 
 saṃbuddho 'rhañ jinas trāyī dharmarājo munīśvaraḥ  Rm 
 tataḥ sa bhagavānn eva sarvatraidhātukeṣv api 
 agraḥ śreṣṭho mahāñ jeṣṭho nānyaḥ kaścid ato 'dhikaḥ  Rm 
 tasmād asya munīndrasya satkāraṃ śraddhayā sadā 
 śaraṇagamanaṃ kṛtvā śrotavyaṃ dharmam ādarāt  Rm 
 ye buddhe śaraṇaṃ yānti na te gachaṃti durgatiṃ 
 sarvadā sadgatau saukhyaṃ bhuktvā yānti jinālaye  Rm 
 śṛṇvanti ye ca tad dharmaṃ te 'pi no yānti durgatiṃ 
 sadā svarge sukhaṃ bhuktvā yāyuś cānte sunirvṛtiṃ  Rm 
 bhajanti ye ca saṃgheṣu te 'pi na yānti durgatiṃ 
 sadā dharmaratāḥ saukhyaṃ bhuktvā yānti sukhāvatiṃ  Rm 
 evaṃ ye ye triratnānāṃ sarvadā śaraṇaṃ gatāḥ 
 satkṛtya śraddhayā nityaṃ bhajanti bodhimānasāḥ  Rm 
 sarve te sadguṇādhārāḥ sarvasatvahitārthinaḥ 
 kramād bodhicarīḥ pūrya saṃbuddhapadam āpnuyuḥ  Rm 
 tenāyaṃ bhagavānn eva jagannātho jagadguruḥ 
 dharmarājo jagadbharttā jagattrāyī vināyakaḥ  Rm 
 tenāsya sadguroḥ śāstuḥ śraddhayā śaraṇaṃ gatāḥ 
 saddharmaṃ sarvadā śrutvā kartum arhati satkṛtiṃ  Rm 
 ye cāpy asya munīndrasya pratikṣipanti śāsanaṃ 
 sadgatiṃ naiva te yānti durgatim eva sarvadā  Rm 
 iti matvā na karttavyā buddhe niṃdā kathaṃ cana 
 triratnabhajanāny eva karttavyāni śubhārthibhiḥ  Rm 
 ye triratnaṃ bhajanty atra sarve te bodhibhāginaḥ 
 bodhisatvā mahāsatvā bhaveyuḥ sugatātmajāḥ  Rm 
 tena te 'pi mahāsatvās triratnopāsakā api 
 śraddhayā praṇatiṃ tesāṃ karttum arhanti sarvadā  Rm 
 iti tenoditaṃ śrutvā tīrthikopāsakaś ca saḥ 
 Rm 
 taṃ buddhopāsakaṃ dṛṣṭvā punar evam abhāṣata  Rm 
 ā kim evaṃ tvayā proktaṃ kiṃ buddho 'tāpasā 'yatiḥ 
 pūraṇo brahmavijñas tapasvī saṃyamī sudhīḥ  Rm 
 tat tasya pūraṇasyāgre buddhaḥ kiṃ vaktum utsahet 
 bālakān eva vañcitvā hy asaddharmme yunakti saḥ  Rm 
 pūraṇa eva sarveṣāṃ yatīnāṃ brahmacāriṇāṃ 
 ṛddhimatāṃ mahān agro mātraikaś cit tato 'dhikaḥ  Rm 
 iti tenoditaṃ śrutvā sa buddhopāsakas tataḥ 
 tīrthikopāsikaṃ dṛṣṭvā punar eva tam abravīt  Rm 
 are kiṃ jñāyate tasya saṃbuddhasya guṇas tvayā 
 yenaiva kṛpayā dṛṣṭvā pālitaṃ putravaj jagat  Rm 
 yasya loke dayā nāsti tena kiṃ pālyate jagat 
 kevalalobhasatkāraṃ hetunādombhiko hi saḥ  Rm 
 tapasvī yogavit prājña ṛddhimān siddhimān api 
 yasya nāsti dayā satve sa kim śāstā jagadguruḥ  Rm 
 yo dṛṣṭvā sakalān satvān kṛpayā saṃprabodhayan 
 saddharme yojayaty atra sa eva jagatāṃ guruḥ  Rm 
 tasmād atra jagacchāstā sarvasatvahitārthabhṛt 
 buddha eva jagannātho jagattrāyī jagadguruḥ  Rm 
 nāsti buddhasamaḥ kaś cit sarvasatvahitaṃkaraḥ 
 tena brahmādidevaiḥ sa vaṃdanīyo munīśvaraḥ  Rm 
 yato 'yaṃ śrīghanaḥ trāyī ṣaḍabhijño vināyakaḥ 
 munīndro 'rhaṃ subhadrāṃśas tena tasyādhiko hi kaḥ  Rm 
 tenāyaṃ sugato buddho dharmarājas tathāgataḥ 
 satkṛtya śraddhayā sarve bhajanīyaḥ śubhechubhiḥ  Rm 
 iti tenoditaṃ śrutvā tīrthikopāsako 'tha saḥ 
 roṣāgniparidagdhāsyas taṃ bauddham evam abravīt  Rm 
 ā evam ucyate ko 'tra pūraṇāt para uttamaḥ 
 yatīr vijño mahābhijñaḥ sa eva trijagadguruḥ  Rm 
 iti tenoditaṃ śrutvā saṃbuddhopāsako 'pi saḥ 
 sāṃjaliḥ praṇatiṃ kṛtvā bhūmāv evaṃ tam abravīt  Rm 
 buddhād anyo viśiṣṭaḥ kas traidhātubhuvaneṣv api 
 bahudhā kiṃ pravādena buddha eva jagatprabhuḥ  Rm 
 tenety ukte sa ruṣṭātmā tīrthikopāsakas tadā 
 kopāgniparidagdhāṃgas taṃ buddham evam abravīt  Rm 
 yadi buddho viśiṣṭaḥ syāt pūraṇād arhato yateḥ 
 sarvasvaṃ me tavādhīnaṃ dāsaś cāpi bhavāmy ahaṃ  Rm 
 yadi buddhād viśiṣṭo hi pūraṇo 'rhaṃ mahāmatiḥ 
 sarvasvaṃ te mamādhīnaṃ dāsaś cāpi bhaveḥ khalu  Rm 
 iti tenodite tatra saṃbuddhopāsako 'pi saḥ 
 tatheti vaṃdhanikṣepaṃ kṛtvā svīkaraṇaṃ vyadhāt  Rm 
 tayor etat pravādatvaṃ prasenajin narādhipaḥ 
 Rm 
 matvāmātyān samāhūya purar evam abhāṣata  Rm 
 gachadhvaṃ maṃtriṇaḥ sarve buddhatairthikayor api 
 nirṇayitvā vivādatve mimāṃsā kriyatām iha  Rm 
 iti rājñā samādiṣṭaṃ śrutvā te maṃtriṇo janāḥ 
 sahasā taj janān sarvān samāhūyaivam ādiśat  Rm 
 bhavanto nṛpater evam ājñāṃ śrutvā samāhitāḥ 
 sarvatra vijite ghaṇṭānādaiś codaya tad drutaṃ  Rm 
 iti tair maṃtribhiḥ proktaiḥ śrutvā te sajanās tathā 
 ghaṇṭāvaghoṣanaṃ kṛtvā sarvatraivaṃ ghoṣayan  Rm 
 śṛṇvantu paurikāḥ sarve ito 'hni saptame 'hani 
 bauddhatairthikasaṃvāde mimāṃsātra bhaviṣyati  Rm 
 ye ye 'tra draṣṭum ichanti sarve te samupāgatāḥ 
 buddhasya tīrthikasyāpi prabhāvaṃ draṣṭum arhata  Rm 
 evaṃ te vijite tatra sarvatra viṣayeṣv api 
 ghaṇṭāvaghoṣaṇaṃ kṛtvā maṃtriṇāṃ pura āyayuḥ  Rm 
 tatas te sajanāḥ sarve rājño 'ntikam upāgatāḥ 
 praṇatvaitat pravṛttāṃtaṃ purataḥ saṃnyavedayan  Rm 
 tato 'hni saptame prāpte sarve lokāḥ samāgatāḥ 
 vistīrṇe bhūtale ramye tad draṣṭum upatasthire  Rm 
 tathā devā aneke ca taddarśanakutūhalāḥ 
 antarīkṣe samāśritya saṃtasthuḥ pratimoditāḥ  Rm 
 evaṃ sarveṣu lokeṣu nṛpamaṃtrijanādiṣu 
 naikaśatasahasreṣu sannipāteṣu sarvataḥ  Rm 
 tīrthikopāsakas tatra sa gomaye praleṣite 
 maṃḍale gaṃdhapuṣpādipūjāṃgaiḥ samapūjayat  Rm 
 tataḥ sa sāṃjalir natvā jānubhyāṃ bhuvi saṃsthitaḥ 
 udvahann uttarāsaṃgaṃ prārthayad evam ādarāt  Rm 
 yena satyena ṣaḍvijñāḥ śāstāraḥ pūraṇādayaḥ 
 bhagavaṃto mahābhijñā arhanto brahmacāriṇaḥ  Rm 
 anena satyabhāvena sarvān etān yatīśvarān 
 etatpūjopahārāṇi prānugaṃchaṃtu saṃmukhaṃ  Rm 
 evaṃ saṃprārthanāṃ kṛtvā tīrthikopāsako mudā 
 tāni paṃcopahārāṇi prādāya gagaṇe 'kṣipat  Rm 
 tena kṣiprakṣiptamātrāṇi tāni sarvāṇi bhūtale 
 patitāny astaṃgatāny eva sahasādarśane yayuḥ  Rm 
 tad dṛṣṭvā sasurā lokāḥ sarve te bhūmipādayaḥ 
 uccair nādair hasantas taṃ tairthikam eva menire  Rm 
 tad dṛṣṭvā dhikpravādaṃ ca śrutvā sa tairthiko 'patat 
 tataś cirāt samutthāya lajjābhinnamukhāśayaḥ  Rm 
 trasito 'dhomukhodraṣṭo niṣprabhaḥ parikaṃpitaḥ 
 bhrastaskaṃdhaḥ kare kaṇḍaṃ sthāpya tasthau vimurchitaḥ  Rm 
 tad dṛṣṭvā sa prasannātmā buddhopāsako mudā 
 prakṛtvā maṇḍalaṃ tatra gomayapratilepite  Rm 
 Rm 
 paṃcopahārapūjaṃgaiḥ samabhyarcya yathāvidhiḥ 
 udvahann uttarāsaṅgaṃ jānubhyāṃ bhuvi saṃsthitaḥ  Rm 
 sāṃjaliḥ purataḥ sthitvā saṃbuddhaṃ taṃ munīśvaraṃ 
 smṛtvā natvā tathā satyaṃ prārthayad evam ādarāt  Rm 
 yato 'yaṃ bhagavān buddhaḥ sarvalokavināyakaḥ 
 tena satyena sarvāṇi puṣpāṇīmāni sūdakaṃ  Rm 
 idaṃ saurabhyadhūpaṃ ca bhagavantaṃ munīśvaraṃ 
 saṃbuddhaṃ śrīghanaṃ nāthaṃ prābhiyāntu vihāyasā  Rm 
 iti saṃprārthanāṃ kṛtvā sa buddhopāsako mudā 
 tāni sarvopahārāṇi prādāya gagaṇe 'kṣipat  Rm 
 tāni tena prakṣiptāni sarvāṇi gagaṇe 'saran 
 tāni sarvāṇi puṣpāṇi chatrībhūtvācaran kramāt  Rm 
 dhūpo meghavad ambho 'pi vaiḍūryyavat tadācarat 
 tad dṛṣṭvā janatā sarvā mahāścaryyaṃ pralehire  Rm 
 krameṇa tāni sarvāṇi pracaranti vihāyasā 
 jhaṭiti jetakāraṇye vihāre saṃmukhaṃ yayuḥ  Rm 
 dṛṣṭvā sajanakāyo 'pi pratihāryaṃ tad adbhutaṃ 
 jayaśabdaṃ prakurvantaḥ paśyanto 'nuyayur mudā  Rm 
 tatra sarvāṇi puṣpāṇi chatrībhūtvā jagadguroḥ 
 saṃbuddhasya jagacchāstur upari samupāśrayan  Rm 
 tad dhūpam agratas tasya tasthau kṛtvā pradakṣiṇāṃ 
 padāmbujaṃ tad ambho 'pi papāta viyataḥ sarat  Rm 
 tat samālokya sarve te dvijādi paurikā janāḥ 
 prasāditā munīndrasya sabhāyāṃ samupācaran  Rm 
 sarve pradakṣiṇīkṛtya kṛtāṃjalipuṭā mudā 
 bhagāvantaṃ muniṃ natvā sarve te samupāśrayan  Rm 
 sa buddhopāsakaś cāpi natvā taṃ śrīghanaṃ mudā 
 tat saddharmāmṛtaṃ pātum upatasthau kṛtāṃjaliḥ  Rm 
 tīrthikopāsakaḥ so 'pi tad dṛṣṭvā vismayānvitāḥ 
 mahad buddhānubhāvatvaṃ matvā draṣṭum upāśrayat  Rm 
 tataḥ sa bhagavān dṛṣṭvā sarvāns tān samupasthitān 
 āryasatyam upādiśya punar evam upādiśat  Rm 
 śṛṇudhvaṃ sādhavaḥ sarve āryadharmaṃ samucyate 
 yat triratnaṃ samākhyātaṃ tat trilokye mahattaraṃ  Rm 
 tadyathā sarvalokānāṃ traidhātukanivāsināṃ 
 sarveṣām api bhadrārthaṃ saddharmaṃ saṃprakāśaye  Rm 
 sa saṃbuddho jagacchāstā sarvasatvahitaṃkaraḥ 
 jagannātho jagattrātā buddharatnam idaṃ varaṃ  Rm 
 atra yaiḥ śraddhayā karmaṃ dānādi sukṛtaṃ kṛtaṃ 
 teṣām agraprasannānāṃ vipākaiḥ phalam uttamaṃ  Rm 
 aprameyam asaṃkhyeyaṃ saṃbodhipadadāyakaṃ 
 Rm 
 evaṃ matvātra saṃbuddhaṃ bhajata sarvadā mudā  Rm 
 yāvataś cātra saṃsāre saṃskṛtā vāpy asaṃskṛtāḥ 
 dharmās teṣāṃ mahān agro virāgo dharmaṃ uttamaḥ  Rm 
 dharmaratnam idaṃ ye 'tra prabhajanti prasāditāḥ 
 teṣām agraprasannānāṃ vipāke phalam uttamaṃ  Rm 
 aprameyam asaṃkhyeyaṃ saṃbodhijñānadāyakaṃ 
 tad etat saugataṃ dharmaṃ śrutvā bhajaṃti saṃvaraṃ  Rm 
 yāvantaś cātra trailokye saṃghāḥ pūgā gaṇāḥ smṛtāḥ 
 teṣām agro mahān khyāto buddhasaṃgho jagadvaraḥ  Rm 
 saṃgharatnam idaṃ ye 'tra bhajanti śraddhayā mudā 
 teṣām agraprasannānāṃ vipāke phalam uttamaṃ  Rm 
 aprameyam asaṃkhyeyaṃ saṃbodhimārgacālakaṃ 
 tad atra saugate saṃghe bhajata śraddhayādarāt  Rm 
 idaṃ ratnatrayaṃ khyātaṃ sarvasatvaśubhaṃkaraṃ 
 vāñchitārthapradaṃ siddhaṃ saṃbodhijñānadāyakaṃ  Rm 
 tad etat tritayaṃ ratnaṃ saṃbodhipadavāṃchibhiḥ 
 satkṛtya śraddhayā nityaṃ pūjanīyaṃ samādarāt  Rm 
 ye triratnaṃ sadā nityaṃ pūjayanti prasāditāḥ 
 na te māravaśaṃ yātā bhavaṃti bodhilābhinaḥ  Rm 
 iti matvā triratnaṃ tad dṛṣṭvā kṛtvānumodanāṃ 
 sāñjalipraṇatiṃ kṛtvā dūrād vanditum arhatha  Rm 
 ity ādiṣṭaṃ munīndreṇa śrutvā te brāhmaṇādayaḥ 
 sarve lokāḥ prasīdantas triratnaśaraṇaṃ yayuḥ  Rm 
 tatra ke cij janā bhadrāḥ saṃbuddhaśaraṇaṃ gatāḥ 
 śikṣāpadaṃ samādāya prācarat saugataṃ vrataṃ  Rm 
 ke cid bhadrāśayā vijñā saṃbuddhaśaraṇaṃ gatāḥ 
 pravrajyāvratam ādāya prācarad brahmacārikāṃ  Rm 
 tataḥ kleśān vinirjitya saṃsārabhogyanispṛhāḥ 
 sākṣād arhatpadaṃ prāpya babhūva brahmacāriṇaḥ  Rm 
 etat sarvaṃ samālokya tīrthikopāsako 'pi saḥ 
 vismitaḥ suprasannātmā triratnaṃ śaraṇaṃ yayau  Rm 
 tataḥ sa tairthikas tasya munīndrasya padāmbuje 
 sāñjalipraṇataś caivaṃ praṇidhānaṃ vyadhān mudā  Rm 
 adyārabhya sadāpy asya munīndrasya jagadguroḥ 
 saddharmaṃ samupāśritya triratnopāsako bhave  Rm 
 etatpuṇyavipākena loke 'ndhe 'parināyake 
 saṃbodhijñānam āsādya bhaveyaṃ sugato jinaḥ  Rm 
 atīrṇāṃ tārayiṣyāmi mocayiṣyāmy amocitān 
 sarvān āśvāsayiṣyāmi hy anāśvastān suduḥkhinaḥ  Rm 
 satvān nirvāpayiṣyāmi bhavālayād anirvṛtān 
 kariṣyāmi sadā bhadraṃ traidhātubhuvaneṣv api  Rm 
 Rm 
 iti tena kṛtaṃ bodhipraṇidhānaṃ svacetasā 
 matvā sa bhagavān smitaṃ visasarja saraśmikaṃ  Rm 
 tadā tā raśmayaḥ paṃcavarṇāḥ sarvāḥ samaṃtataḥ 
 lokeṣu prasṛtā bhadraṃ saukhyaṃ kṛtvā praserire  Rm 
 yā adhastād gatābhāso sarvatra narakeṣu tāḥ 
 prasṛtā avabhāsyaivaṃ bhadrasaukhyaṃ pracakrire  Rm 
 tatprabhābhiḥ parispṛṣṭā sarve te narakāśritāḥ 
 nirduḥkhā saukhyam āsādya vismayaṃ samupāyayuḥ  Rm 
 tatas te nārakāḥ satvāḥ sarve te narake sthitāḥ 
 ekaikanarakeṣv evaṃ saṃmīlya saṃvabhāṣire  Rm 
 aho citraṃ kim adyaivaṃ mahat saukhyaṃ prajāyate 
 itaś cyutāḥ kim anyatra samutpannā vayaṃ khalu  Rm 
 iti saṃvādināṃ tesāṃ sarveṣāṃ saṃprabodhane 
 bhagavān nirmitaṃ buddhaṃ prerayan narake prati  Rm 
 taṃ dṛṣṭvā nārakāḥ sarve vismitāḥ saṃprasāditāḥ 
 bhūya ekatra saṃmīlya mitha evaṃ vabhāṣire  Rm 
 aho vayam itaś cyutvā naivānyatra gatāḥ khalu 
 kiṃ tv asyāpūrvarūpasya prabhāvān naḥ śubhāyate  Rm 
 nūnam ayaṃ jagannātho buddho 'smān duḥkhapīḍitān 
 samīkṣya kṛpayā dṛṣṭyā samuddharttum ihāgataḥ  Rm 
 tad asyātra vayaṃ sarve satkṛtya śraddhayādarāt 
 sarvadā śaraṇaṃ gatvā bhaktum arhāmahe 'dhunā  Rm 
 iti saṃbhāṣaṇāṃ kṛtvā sarve te saṃprasāditāḥ 
 asyaiva śaraṇaṃ gatvā praṇatvā saṃprabhejire  Rm 
 tatas te nārakāḥ sarve tatpāpaparimocitāḥ 
 pariśuddhāḥ śubhātmānaḥ sadgatiṃ sahasā yayuḥ  Rm 
 evaṃ tān nārakān sarvāḥ samuddhṛtya prabhāś ca tāḥ 
 sarvāḥ pratyāgatās tatra saṃbuddhasya puro 'saran  Rm 
 evam ūrddhaṃ gatāyāś ca raśmayas tāḥ samaṃtataḥ 
 sarvān devālayāṃ lokān avabhāsya praserire  Rm 
 yāvad bhavāgraparyantam avabhāsya samaṃtataḥ 
 prasāritāḥ tato gāthā nisṛtāḥ samacodayan  Rm 
 anityaṃ khalu saṃsāraṃ duḥkhaṃ śūnyam anātmakaṃ 
 puṇyam eva jagatsāraṃ tat puṇyaṃ cinutādarāt  Rm 
 niṣkrāmatārabhadhvaṃ tad yujyadhvaṃ buddhaśāsane 
 dhunīta mṛtyusainyāni carata saugataṃ vrataṃ  Rm 
 yo hy asmin saugate dharme cariṣyati samāhitaḥ 
 sa hitvā janma saṃsāre duḥkhasyāntaṃ kariṣyati  Rm 
 tat triratnaṃ sadā yūyaṃ saṃsmṛtvā śaraṇaṃ gatāḥ 
 satkṛtya śraddhayā nityaṃ bhajata bodhiprāptaye  Rm 
 evaṃ tad ghoṣam ākarṇya sarvadevāḥ prabodhitāḥ 
 triratnaṃ śaraṇaṃ kṛtvā prabhejire sadādarāt  Rm 
 Rm 
 evaṃ tā raśmayo devāñ codayitvā samaṃtataḥ 
 punaḥ pratyāgatās tatra buddhāntikam upāyayuḥ  Rm 
 tatra tā raśmayaḥ sarvā ekībhūtvābhipiṇḍitāḥ 
 tridhā pradakṣiṇīkṛtya sūṣṇīṣe 'ntardadhur muneḥ  Rm 
 taddṛṣṭvā sasabhālokāḥ sarve te vismayānvitāḥ 
 śāstā kim ādiśed dharmam iti dhyātvā niṣedire  Rm 
 athāyuṣmān mahānando matvā tal lokaciṃtitaṃ 
 utthāya sāṃjālir natvā papracha taṃ munīśvaraṃ  Rm 
 vigatoddhavā dainyamadaprahīṇā buddhā jagaty uttamahetubhūtāḥ 
 nākāraṇe śaṃkhamṛṇālagauraṃ smitam upadeśayanti jinā jitārayaḥ  Rm 
 tat kālaṃ svayam evam adhigamya dhīra buddhyā śrotṝṇāṃ śramaṇa jineṃdra kāṅkṣitānāṃ dhīrabhir 
 munivṛṣa vāgbhir uttamābhir utpannaṃ vyapanaya saṃśayaṃ śubhābhiḥ  Rm 
 nākasmāl lavaṇajalādrirājadhairyāḥ saṃbuddhāḥ smitam upadarśayanti nāthāḥ 
 yasyārthe smitam upadarśayaṃti dhīrās taṃ śrotuṃ samabhilaṣanti janoghāḥ  Rm 
 tad bhavān sarvasatvānāṃ cittābhiparibodhane 
 yad abhilaṣitaṃ kāryaṃ tad upadeṣṭum arhati  Rm 
 iti saṃprārthite tena bhagavān sa munīśvaraḥ 
 āyuṣmantaṃ tam ānaṃdaṃ samālokyaivam ādiśat  Rm 
 evam etan mahānaṃda nāhetupratyayaṃ jināḥ 
 saṃbuddhāḥ sugatāḥ sarve darśayanti smitaṃ kvacit  Rm 
 śṛṇv ānaṃda yadarthe 'haṃ smitaṃ muñcāmi sāṃprataṃ 
 tadarthaṃ saṃpravakṣyāmi sarvasatvaprabodhane  Rm 
 paśyasi yad ayaṃ śreṣṭhī tīrthikopāsako mudā 
 mamātra śaraṇaṃ gatvā praṇidhānaṃ karoti hi  Rm 
 etatpuṇyavipākena trikalpāntam anātmavit 
 kramād bodhicārīḥ sarvāḥ paripūrya bhavet sudhīḥ  Rm 
 tataḥ kleśagaṇāñ jitvā sarvān māragaṇān api 
 bodhiṃ prāpyācalo nāma tathāgato bhaviṣyati  Rm 
 ity ādiṣṭaṃ munīndreṇa śrutvānaṃdādi bhikṣavaḥ 
 sarve te suprasannāsyāḥ prābhyanandan savismayāḥ  Rm 
 tathā tena munīndreṇa vyākhyātaṃ sa tairthikaḥ 
 śrutvānumodanāṃ kṛtvā prābhyanandan savismayaḥ  Rm 
 tataḥ sa sarvadā nityaṃ satkṛtya śraddhayā mudā 
 triratnabhajānaṃ kṛtvā prācarat saugataṃ vrataṃ  Rm 
 iti me guruṇākhyātaṃ śrutaṃ mayā tathocyate 
 tvam apy evaṃ mahārāja triratnasevako bhava  Rm 
 prajāś cāpi tathā rājaṃ bodhayitvā prayatnataḥ 
 triratnabhajanotsāhe saṃcārayitum arhasi  Rm 
 tathā te sarvadā nityaṃ sarvatrāpi śubhaṃ bhavet 
 Rm 
 kramād bodhiṃ samāsādya saṃbuddhapadam āpnuyāt  Rm 
 iti tenārhatādiṣṭaṃ śrutvāśokaḥ sa bhūpatiḥ 
 satyam iti pratijñāya prābhyanāndat sa pārthikaḥ  Rm 
 śṛṇvantīdaṃ narā ye munivarakathitaṃ tairthikasyāvadānaṃ ye cāpi śrāvayanti pramuditamānasaḥ śraddhayā bhaktiyuktāḥ 
 te sarve bodhisatvāḥ sakalaguṇabharā bhadracaryā caranto bhuktvā satsaukhyabhadraṃ jinavaranilaye saṃprayānti pramodāḥ  Rm 
  iti śrīratnāvadānatatve tairthikāvadānaṃ samāptam 
 Rm 
 XXVII Mālikāvadāna
 athāśoko mahīnāthaḥ kṛtāṃjalipuṭo mudā 
 upaguptaṃ tam arhantaṃ praṇatvā prārthayat punaḥ  Rm 
 bhadanta śrotum ichāmi punar anyat subhāṣitaṃ 
 tadyathā guruṇādiṣṭaṃ tathādeṣṭuṃ tvaṃ arhati  Rm 
 iti tena narendreṇa prārthitaṃ sa yatīśvaraḥ 
 upagupto narendran taṃ samālokyaivaṃ ādiśat  Rm 
 śṛṇu sādhu mahārāja yathā me guruṇoditaṃ 
 tathāhaṃ tat pravakṣyāmi tava puṇyavivṛddhaye  Rm 
 tadyathā bhagavān buddhaḥ śākyasiṃho jagadguruḥ 
 sarvajñaḥ sugataḥ śāstā dharmarājo munīśvaraḥ  Rm 
 ekasmin samaye tatra śrāvastyā upakaṇṭhike 
 jetāraṇye mahodyāne vihāre śrāvakaiḥ saha  Rm 
 bhikṣubhiś cailakaiś cāpi bhikṣuṇībhir upāsakaiḥ 
 upāsikābhir anyaiś ca bodhisatvagaṇair api  Rm 
 sarvasatvahitārthena bodhicaryaṃ prakāśayan 
 saddharmaṃ samupādiśya vijahāra prabhāsayan  Rm 
 tat saddharmāmṛtaṃ pātuṃ sarve lokāḥ samāgatāḥ 
 śakrādayo 'pi devendrā brahmādilokapālakāḥ  Rm 
 daityeṃdrā garuḍā nāgā yakṣagaṃdharvakiṃnarāḥ 
 siddhā vidyādharāś cāpi rākṣasāś ca maharddhikāḥ  Rm 
 ṛṣayo brāhmaṇā cāpi kṣatriyāś ca narādhipāḥ 
 vaiśyā rājakumārāś ca maṃtriṇo 'mātyakā janāḥ  Rm 
 gṛhasthāḥ sārthavāhāś ca vaṇijaḥ śilpino 'pi ca 
 paurā jānapadā grāmyā anye kārpaṭikā api  Rm 
 sarve te samupāgatya tatra taṃ śrīghanaṃ muniṃ 
 dṛṣṭvā pradakṣiṇīkṛtya praṇatvā samupācaran  Rm 
 yathākramaṃ samabhyarcya natvā sāṃjalayo mudā 
 parivṛtya puraskṛtya sarve te samupāśrayan  Rm 
 tān sarvān samupāsīnāṃ dṛṣṭvā sa bhagavān muniḥ 
 āryasatyaṃ samārabhya dideśa dharmam uttamaṃ  Rm 
 tad dharmaṃ samupākarṇya sarve te saṃprabodhitāḥ 
 dharmavaiśeṣam ājñāya babhuvur bodhivāṃchitāḥ  Rm 
 tadā tatra pure rājā prasenajit kauśalaḥ 
 yadā na sugatas tatra tadā tīrthikabhāg abhūt  Rm 
 yadā tu sugatas tatra sasāṃghikaḥ samāgataḥ 
 tadā sa nṛpatir nityaṃ śrīghanaṃ taṃ sadābhajat  Rm 
 tasmiṃś ca samaye tatra kaścid ārāmiko vanāt 
 Rm 
 navaṃ padmaiḥ samādāya rājñe dātuṃ pure 'viśat  Rm 
 tatraikapathi taṃ dṛṣṭvā tīrthikopāsiko mudā 
 sahasā tasya puro gatvā prārthayat taṃ saroruhaṃ  Rm 
 bho mālinn idaṃ padmaṃ yadi vikretum ichasi 
 ucitaṃ mūlyam ādāya mahyaṃ dātuṃ tvam arhasi  Rm 
 iti tenārthitaṃ śrutvā mālikaḥ lubhitāśayaḥ 
 yadīchati bhavān dadyām iti taṃ dātum aichata  Rm 
 tasminn eva kṣaṇe tatra gṛhastho 'nāthapiṇḍadaḥ 
 puṣpārthī samupāyāto mālikaṃ tam apṛchata  Rm 
 bho mālinn idaṃ padmaṃ yadi vikretum ichati 
 dviguṇaṃ mūlyam ādāya bhavān me dātum arhati  Rm 
 iti tenoditaṃ śrutvā tīrthikopāsako 'pi saḥ 
 taddviguṇena mūlyena tad padmaṃ samayācata  Rm 
 iti tenārthitaṃ śrutvā sa cāpy anāthapiṇḍadaḥ 
 taddvaiguṇyena mūlyena kamalaṃ tam ayācata  Rm 
 tac chrutvā tairthikaḥ so 'pi madadarpābhimāninaḥ 
 tattriguṇamūlyena gṛhītuṃ taṃ samaichata  Rm 
 tad dṛṣṭvā sa gṛhastheṇānāthapiṇḍadotsahī 
 caturguṇena mūlyena padmaṃ tam abhyayācata  Rm 
 evaṃ tau gṛhapatī so tha yāvac chatasaharsrakaiḥ 
 mūlya taṃ padmam ādāya mālinaṃ taṃ yayācatuḥ  Rm 
 tad dṛṣṭvārāmikaḥ sa 'pi pravarddhayan parasparaṃ 
 tayor dvayor adatvaiva manasaivaṃ vyaciṃtayat  Rm 
 ayaṃ gṛhapatiḥ śreṣṭho hy anāthapiṇḍadaḥ sudhīḥ 
 acapalo mahādhīraḥ sthirasatvo vicakṣaṇaḥ  Rm 
 kasyārthe nv idaṃ padmam iyan mūlyena yācate 
 nūnam atra mahaddhetur bhaviṣyati na saṃśayaḥ  Rm 
 tad etat paripṛchāva dāsyāmi sadguṇārthine  Rm 
 iti dhyātvā svacittena sa ārāmika utsukaḥ 
 tairthikaṃ taṃ samālokya paprachaivaṃ samādarāt  Rm 
 bho puruṣa bhavān kasya kāryasyārthe idaṃ kajaṃ 
 iyanmūlyena vikretum ichati tad vadasva me  Rm 
 iti tenoditaṃ śrutvā sa tairthikaḥ pramoditaḥ 
 ārāmikaṃ tam ālokya prabodhayitum abravīt  Rm 
 yaḥ śrīpatir jagadbharttā nārāyano janārdanaḥ 
 tasya pūjāṃ kariṣyāmi tad idaṃ dehi me 'mbujaṃ  Rm 
 iti tenoditaṃ śrutvārāmiko sānubodhitaḥ 
 anāthapiṇḍadaṃ taṃ ca dṛṣṭvā kāryam apṛchata  Rm 
 bho sādho bhavaṃś cāpi kim artham idam ambujaṃ 
 bahumūlyaiva samāharttum ichati tad vadasva me  Rm 
 iti tad vacanaṃ śrutvā so 'nāthapiṇḍadaḥ sudhīḥ 
 ārāmikaṃ tam ālokya prabodhayitum abravīt  Rm 
 sādhu sādhu mahābhāga yad idaṃ te saroruhaṃ 
 bahumūlyena vāṃchāmi tad arthaṃ kathyate śṛṇu  Rm 
 Rm 
 yo 'tra śauddhodanī rājā cakravarttī nṛpādhipaḥ 
 sarvasatvahitārthena saṃbodhisādhanodyataḥ  Rm 
 sarvatra bhuvane loke kleśākulāsamāhite 
 bodhicaryāvihīne 'tra mlechadharmapravarttate  Rm 
 bodhicaryāṃ svayaṃ dhṛtvā prakāśayitum udyataḥ 
 sarvarājyaṃ parityajya sarvāṃś cāpi parigrahān  Rm 
 vairāgyadharmam āśritya saṃsārabhoganispṛhaḥ 
 gayāśīrṣe nage gatvā kṛtvā tapaḥ suduṣkaraṃ  Rm 
 tato loke hitaṃ kartuṃ samutthāya samāhitaḥ 
 bodhivṛkṣatalāsīnas tasthau dhyānasamāhitaḥ  Rm 
 tatra māragaṇān sarvāñ jitvā kleśagaṇān api 
 saṃbodhijñānaṃ āsādya buddho bhavati sāṃprataṃ  Rm

 sarvajñaḥ sa jagacchāstā tam ahaṃ śaraṇaṃ vraje  Rm 
 yo 'smin sudṛṣṭyāt saṃrakṣyati jagacchubhe 
 tasyāhaṃ śaraṇaṃ gatvā bhajāmi satataṃ mudā  Rm 
 yaṃ dṛṣṭvā suprasannās te bhavanti nirmalāśayāḥ 
 tam eva sugataṃ nāthaṃ bhajāmi śaraṇaṃ gataḥ  Rm 
 yenaiva trijagallokaṃ putravat pratipālitaṃ 
 tam eva trijagannāthaṃ bhajāmi śaraṇaṃ tataḥ  Rm 
 yasmai suśraddhayā dattaṃ tat phalaṃ bodhisādhanaṃ 
 tam eva śrīghanaṃ bhaktyā bhajāmi śaraṇaṃ gataḥ  Rm 
 yasmād dharmāmṛtaṃ pītvā sarve satvāḥ pramodinaḥ 
 tam eva saṃti sarve 'pi duḥkhachedanasadguṇāḥ 
 tam eva śrīpradātāraṃ bhajāmi śraddhayādarāt  Rm 
 buddha eva jagacchāstā buddha eva jagadguruḥ 
 buddha eva jagannātho buddha eva munīśvaraḥ  Rm 
 tad ahaṃ sarvabhāvena buddhasya śaraṇaṃ gataḥ 
 śraddhayā dharmam āsādya bhajāmi bodhiprāptaye  Rm 
 ye buddhaṃ śaraṇaṃ yānti na te gachanti durgatiṃ 
 nirmuktapāpakāḥ saukhyaṃ bhuktvā yāṃti jinālayaṃ  Rm 
 Rm 
 śṛṇvanti saugataṃ vākyaṃ ye te na yānti durgatiṃ 
 samantabhadrasaukhyāni bhuktvā yāṃti sukhāvatiṃ  Rm 
 bhajanti lokanāthaṃ ye te 'pi na yānti durgatiṃ 
 pāpamuktāḥ sukhāny eva bhuktvā yāṃti surālayaṃ  Rm 
 etad ratnatrayaṃ loke utpannaṃ sadguṇākaraṃ 
 tad ahaṃ śaraṇaṃ gatvā bhajāmi samupāsikaḥ  Rm 
 etatpuṇyavipākena sarvasatvahitārthakaḥ 
 kramād bodhicarāḥ pūrya saṃbuddhapadam āpnuyāt  Rm 
 tadāhaṃ sugato bhūtvā sarvasatvaśubhārthabhṛt 
 satvān bodhau pratiṣṭhāpya nirvṛtiṃ samavāpnuyāt  Rm 
 evaṃ vijñāya saddharmaṃ yadīchati bhavān api 
 triratnaśaraṇaṃ gatvā bhaja nityaṃ samādarāt  Rm 
 etatpuṇyavipākena sadā tvaṃ sadgatiṃ tataḥ 
 bodhiṃ cāpi samāsādya saṃbuddhapadam āpnuyāḥ  Rm 
 iti tena samākhyātaṃ śrutvā sa paribodhitaḥ 
 tairthyadharmaṃ pratikṣipya saṃbuddhaśrāvako 'bhavat  Rm 
 tadārabhya sadā nityaṃ saddharmaśravaṇotsukaḥ 
 vihāre samupāśritya prābhajat taṃ munīśvaraṃ  Rm 
 iti me guruṇādiṣṭaṃ śrutaṃ mayā tathocyate 
 tvaṃ cāpy evaṃ mahārāja triratnaṃ sarvadā bhaja  Rm 
 prajāś cāpi mahārāja bodhayitvā prayatnataḥ 
 bodhimārge pratiṣṭhāpya pālayasva samāhitaḥ  Rm 
 etatpuṇyavipākena sadā te maṃgalaṃ bhavet 
 kramād bodhicarīḥ pūrya saṃbuddhapadam āpnuyāḥ  Rm 
 iti tenārhatādiṣṭaṃ śrutvāśokaḥ sa bhūmipaḥ 
 tatheti prativijñapya prābhyanandat sapārṣadaḥ  Rm 
 śṛṇvantīdaṃ mudā ye jinavarakathitaṃ mālikasyāvadānaṃ ye cāpi śrāvayanti pramuditamanasaḥ śraddhayā bhadrakāmāḥ 
 te sarve lokanāthās trimalakalijitā bodhisatvā maheśā bhuktvā saukhyaṃ sadānte jinavaranilaye saṃprayānti prasannāḥ 
  iti ratnāvadānatatve mālikāvadānaṃ samāptam 
 Rm 
 XXVIII Pāñcālarājāvadāna
 athāśoko mahīpālaḥ kṛtāṃjalipuṭo mudā 
 upaguptaṃ guruṃ bhikṣuṃ natvaivaṃ punar abravīt  Rm 
 bhadanta śrotum ichāmi punar anyat subhāṣitaṃ 
 tadyathā guruṇākhyātaṃ tathādeṣṭuṃ ca me 'rhati  Rm 
 iti saṃprārthite rājñā sa upagupta ātmavit 
 tam aśokaṃ mahīpālaṃ samāmaṃtryaivam abravīt  Rm 
 sādhu śṛṇu mahārāja yathā me guruṇoditaṃ 
 tathāhaṃ te pravakṣyāmi śrutvānumodanāṃ kuru  Rm 
 tadyathāsau jagacchāstā śākyasiṃhas tathāgataḥ 
 sarvajñaḥ sugato nātho dharmarājā munīśvaraḥ  Rm 
 ekasmin samaye tatra śrāvastyā bahir āśrame 
 vihāre jetakodyāne vijahāra sasāṃghikaḥ  Rm 
 tadā sa bhagavāṃs tatra bhikṣusaṃghaiḥ puraskṛtaḥ 
 sabhāmadhyāsanāsīno dharmam ādeṣṭum ārabhat  Rm 
 tad dharmadeśanāṃ śrotuṃ sarve lokāḥ samāgatāḥ 
 devā daityāś ca nāgāś ca yakṣagaṃdharvakinnarāḥ  Rm 
 siddhā vidyādharāś cāpi garuḍā rākṣasā api 
 ṛṣayo brāhmaṇā vijñā rājānaḥ kṣatriyā api  Rm 
 vaiśyā rājakumārāś ca maṃtriṇaś ca mahājanāḥ 
 vaṇijaḥ sārthavāhāś ca gṛhasthāḥ śilpino 'pi ca  Rm 
 grāmyā jānapadāś cāpi kārpaṭikādayo 'pi ca 
 tīrthikā api te sarve jetārāme upāgatāḥ  Rm 
 vihāre taṃ jagannāthaṃ dṛṣṭvā sāṃjalayo mudā 
 natvā pradakṣiṇīkṛtya samabhyarcya yathākramaṃ  Rm 
 tatas te muditāḥ sarve parivṛtya samaṃtataḥ 
 tat saddharmāmṛtaṃ patum upatasthuḥ samāhitāḥ  Rm 
 tadā sa bhagavān dṛṣṭvā sarvāns tān samupasthitān 
 ādimadhyāntakalyāṇaṃ dideśa dharmam uttamaṃ  Rm 
 tat saddharmāmṛtaṃ pītvā sarve lokāḥ prabodhitāḥ 
 saṃbuddhaṃ śaraṇaṃ kṛtvā pracerur bodhisaṃvaraṃ  Rm 
 tasminn avasare tatra paṃcāla uttarādhipaḥ 
 dakṣiṇādhipapaṃcālaṃ parājetum upākramat  Rm 
 tayoḥ paṃcālayo rājño viruddhāsy abhimāninoḥ 
 mahāyuddham abhūn nityaṃ parasparavighātanaṃ  Rm 
 pravarttite sadā yuddhe tayo rājño hi māninoḥ 
 durbhikṣam api tatrābhūd bahulokavighātanaṃ  Rm 
 Rm 
 tadā tau kṣatriyau krūrau parasparavighātinau 
 viruddhamānasau vīrau vairaśāmyaṃ na jagmataḥ  Rm 
 tad dṛṣṭvā nṛpatī rājā prasenajin sa kauśalaḥ 
 tad vairaśamanopāyaṃ ciraṃ dhyātvā vyaciṃtayat  Rm 
 yad etau nṛpatī vīrau nityaṃ yuddhābhikāṃkṣiṇau 
 saṃbodhisādhanaṃ dharmaṃ śrotuṃ naivābhivāṃchata  Rm 
 sarve 'pi maṃtriṇo 'mātyāḥ sarve lokāś ca yodhinaḥ 
 saṃbuddhadarśane cāpi nātrāgachanti ke cana  Rm 
 evaṃ teṣāṃ sadā nityaṃ hiṃsākarmābhirāgiṇāṃ 
 saddharme śravaṇe vāpi gocaraṃ naiva vidyate  Rm 
 dharmaṃ vinātra saṃsāre kiṃ sāraṃ janma mānuṣe 
 parasparaṃ nihatyaiva yāsyaṃti narake dhruvaṃ  Rm 
 dhig janma mānuṣe teṣāṃ kevalaṃ pāpasādhanaṃ 
 ye kleśamānadarpyāndhā na paśyaṃti munīśvaraṃ  Rm 
 ye cātra saugataṃ dharmaṃ na śṛṇvanti kadā cana 
 kathaṃ te bhadracaryāyāṃ gocaraṃ samavāpnuyuḥ  Rm 
 sadā te māracaryāyāṃ sthitvā kleśābhimāninaḥ 
 bodhicaryāṃ pratikṣipya careyuḥ kāmacāriṇaḥ  Rm 
 tataḥ svayaṃ paribhraṣṭā bhraṃśayantaḥ parān api 
 yathechayā carantas te cinuyur bahupātakaṃ  Rm 
 tatas te kleśasaṃtaptāḥ svaparārthābhighātinaḥ 
 tīvraduḥkhāgnisaṃtaptāḥ pateyur narake dhruvaṃ  Rm 
 narakeṣu bhramantas te sadā duḥkhābhibhojinaḥ 
 paścāttāpāgnisaṃtaptāś careyur ābhavaṃ tathā  Rm 
 tad eṣāṃ sarvalokānāṃ bhadrārthaṃ hitakāraṇaṃ 
 sarvathopāyam ādhātum arhāmi sāṃprataṃ drutaṃ  Rm 
 yāvad etau nṛpau vīrau viruddhau nopaśāmyataḥ 
 tāvad atra bhuvi kvāpi maṃgalaṃ na bhavet sadā  Rm 
 tad etau nṛpatī tāvad bodhayitvā prayatnataḥ 
 maitrasnehasaṃbaddhau kuryāṃ nirvairabhāvinau  Rm 
 etau hi kṣatriyau vīrau pāṃcālau mānagarvitau 
 anayor mitravaṃdhaṃ ko bodhayitvā kariṣyati  Rm 
 buddha eva jagacchāstā dharmarājaḥ prabodhayan 
 anayoś ciravairyāgniṃ śamayituṃ praśaknuyāt  Rm 
 tad atra sahasā gatvā prārthayeyaṃ munīśvaraṃ 
 nūnaṃ buddhānubhāvāt tau nṛpau mitratvam āpsyataḥ  Rm 
 iti niścitya rājā sa prasenajit samutthitaḥ 
 vihāre sahasā gatvā nanāma taṃ munīśvaraṃ  Rm 
 tatra sa purato gatvā sāṃjaliḥ samupāśrayan 
 etat sarvapravṛttāṃtaṃ nivedyaivam abhāṣata  Rm 
 bhagavan nātha sarvajña vijānīyād bhavān api 
 yat tau pāṃcālabhūpālau viruddhau bhavato 'dhunā  Rm 
 yad etayor viruddhe ta sarve lokā virodhitāḥ 
 tad atra sarvadā yuddhaṃ pravarttate divāniśaṃ  Rm 
 Rm 
 tat tesāṃ sarvalokānāṃ saddharme gocaraṃ kadā 
 sadā yuddhābhisaktās te sādhayeyuḥ śubhaṃ kathaṃ  Rm 
 tad atra bhagavāñc chāstā bodhayaṃs tau narādhipau 
 saṃbodhimārgam ādiśya śubhe cārayitum arhati  Rm 
 iti saṃprārthite tena rājñā sa bhagavān muniḥ 
 tasya rājñe nareṃdrasya tūṣṇībhūtvādhyuvāsa tat  Rm 
 tataḥ sa nṛpatī rājā matvā śāstrādhivāsitaṃ 
 sāṃjalis taṃ muniṃ natvā muditaḥ svālayaṃ yayau  Rm 
 tataḥ sa bhagavān pātram ādāya cīvarāvṛtaḥ 
 bhāsayan bhadratāṃ kurvan pratasthe saha sāṃghikaiḥ  Rm 
 evaṃ sarvatra mārgeṣu bhāsayaṃ sa munīśvaraḥ 
 kṛtvā bhadraṃ krameṇaivaṃ vārāṇasīm upācarat  Rm 
 tatra sa bhagavāṃ prāpto bhābhiḥ saṃbhāsayan kramāt 
 caraṃ kṛtvā subhadratvaṃ mṛgadāve upācarat  Rm 
 tatra sa bhagavān prātaḥ sasaṃghaḥ saugatāśrame 
 sabhāmadhyāsanāsīnaḥ saddharmaṃ samupādiśat  Rm 
 tat saddharmāmṛtaṃ pītvā sarve lokāḥ pramoditāḥ 
 triratnaṃ śaraṇaṃ kṛtvā prabhejire samādarāt  Rm 
 tadā dakṣiṇapāṃcālanṛpatiḥ sa pramoditaḥ 
 saṃbuddhadarśanaṃ kartuṃ mṛgadāve upācarat  Rm 
 tatra taṃ śrīghanaṃ dṛṣṭvā nṛpatiḥ sa pramoditaḥ 
 sāṃjaliḥ purato gatvā natvaikānte upāśrayat  Rm 
 tasminn avasare tatra mṛgadāve samāśritaḥ 
 bhagavānn iti śuśrāva pāṃcālauttarādhipaḥ  Rm 
 sa uttarapāṃcālo nṛpatiḥ pratiroṣitaḥ 
 taṃ nṛpaṃ yāmyapāṃcālaṃ parājetum upācarat  Rm 
 tatra sa nṛpatir vīraś caturaṃgavalaiḥ saha 
 jayavādyamahotsāhaiḥ sahasā samupācarat  Rm 
 tatra sa yāmyapāṃcālarājā taṃ ripum āgataṃ 
 niśamya sahasotthāya natvā ha taṃ munīśvaraṃ  Rm 
 bhagavan nātha sarvajña sa me vairā ihāgataḥ 
 tad atra kiṃ kariṣyāmi tad anujñāṃ dadātu me  Rm 
 iti tena narendreṇa prārthite sa jineśvaraḥ 
 dṛṣṭvā taṃ yāmyapāṃcālaṃ samāśvāsyaivam ādiśat  Rm 
 nṛpate mā vibheṣī tvaṃ dhairyyam ālambya tiṣṭhata 
 tad upāyaṃ kariṣyāmi yenāsau te vaśe caret  Rm 
 ity ādiśya sa sarvajñaś caturaṅgabalānvitaṃ 
 mahatsainyādhipaṃ vīraṃ nirmāya 'preṣayat tataḥ  Rm 
 sa sainyādhipatir vīraś caturaṅgabalaiḥ saha 
 carann uttarapāṃcālam abhiyoddhum upācarat  Rm 
 tan mahatsainyaṃ āyātaṃ samālokyābhyupadrutaṃ 
 sarva uttarapāṃcālasainyā bhītāḥ parāyayuḥ  Rm 
 tad dṛṣṭvottarapāṃcālanṛpatiś cāpi kheṭitaḥ 
 ekākī ratham āruhya bhagavatsaṃmukhe 'carat  Rm 
 Rm 
 tatra sa dūrato dṛṣṭvā śrīghanaṃ taṃ sabhāśritaṃ 
 avatīrya rathāt tatra mṛgadāve upācarat  Rm 
 tatra sa nṛpati rājā samupetya kṛtāṃjaliḥ 
 tridhā pradakṣiṇīkṛtya nanāma śaraṇaṃ gataḥ  Rm 
 tataś cirāt samutthāpya sa pāṃcalo narādhipaḥ 
 tat saddharmāmṛtaṃ pātuṃ tatraikānte samāśrayat  Rm 
 tadā sa bhagavān dṛṣṭvā nṛpatiṃ taṃ samāśritaṃ 
 āryyasatyaṃ samārabhya dideśa dharmam uttamaṃ  Rm 
 tad āryasatyam ākarṇya nṛpatiḥ so 'bhibodhitaḥ 
 saṃsārasādhanaṃ dharmaṃ punaḥ śrotuṃ samaichata  Rm 
 tataḥ sa nṛpatī rājā samutthāya kṛtāṃjaliḥ 
 praṇatvā bhagavaṃtaṃ taṃ prārthayad evam ādarāt  Rm 
 bhagavan nātha sarvajña bhavatāṃ śaraṇaṃ vraje 
 tan me 'trānugrahaṃ kṛtvā samyag ādeṣṭum arhati  Rm 
 yad atra bhagavan satvāḥ pravarttanto bhavodadhau 
 sukhaduḥkhābhibhuṃjāno bhramaṃte ṣaḍgatau kathaṃ  Rm 
 karmaṇā kena devāḥ syur mānuṣāḥ kena karmaṇā 
 daityāś ca karmaṇā kena tat samyak samupādiśa  Rm 
 tiryañcaḥ karmaṇā kena pretāś ca kena karmaṇā 
 nārakāḥ karmaṇā kena tat sarvaṃ samupādiśa  Rm 
 tatrāpy anekarūpāś ca sarve bhinnāśayā api 
 nihīnamadhyamotkṛṣṭāḥ sukhaduḥkhānvitā api  Rm 
 etat sarvaṃ samākhyāya bhavāñ chāstā jagad guruḥ 
 saṃsāragatisaṃcāraṃ prabodhayitum arhati  Rm 
 iti saṃprārthite tena rājñā sa bhagavān sudhīḥ 
 taṃ viśuddhāśayaṃ bhūpaṃ dṛṣṭvaivaṃ samupādiśat  Rm 
 sādhu śṛṇu mahārāja saṃsāragaticāraṇaṃ 
 samyag dharmaṃ pravakṣyāmi yuṣmākaṃ paribodhane  Rm 
 kāyavāgmānasaṃ karmakṛtaṃ yac ca śubhāśubhaṃ 
 lokas tasya phalaṃ bhukte karttā nānyo 'sti kasya cit  Rm 
 iti sarve kṛpāviṣṭās trailokye guravo jināḥ 
 uktavantas tathā tad dhi karmaṇo yasya yat phalaṃ  Rm 
 karmaṃ kartuṃ vihātuṃ ca sadasadgatihetukaṃ 
 lobhamohabhayakrodhā ye narā naraghātinaḥ  Rm 
 saṃvaddhyānyāñ ca hi santi saṃjīvaṃ yānti te dhruvaṃ 
 saṃvatsarasahasrāṇi bahūny api hatāhatāḥ  Rm 
 saṃjīvanti yatas tatra tena saṃjīva ucyate  Rm 
 mātāpitṛsuhṛdvaṃdhumitradrohakarāś ca ye 
 paiśunyānṛtavattāraḥ kālasūtrābhigāminaḥ  Rm 
 kālasūtreṇa saṃsūḍya pāṭyante dāruvad yataḥ 
 jvaladbhiḥ krakacais tatra kālasūtras tataḥ smṛtaḥ  Rm 
 dāvādau dahanair dāhaṃ dehināṃ vidadhāti ye 
 sa tīvrajvalanair jantus tapyate tapane raṭan  Rm 
 Rm 
 tīvraṃ tapanasaṃtāpaṃ tanoty eva niraṃtaraṃ 
 yat tato 'nvartham āloke khyātas tapanasaṃjñayā  Rm 
 dharmādharmaviparyāsaṃ nāstiko yaḥ prakāśayan 
 saṃtāpayati cānyāṃś ca tapyate sa pratāpane  Rm 
 pratāpayati tatrasthān satvāns tīvreṇa vahninā 
 tapanātiśayano 'sau proktas tasmāt pratāpanaḥ  Rm 
 ajaiḍakaśṛgālāṃś ca śaśākhumṛgāsukarān 
 anyāṃś ca prāṇino ghnaṃti saṃghātaṃ yānti te narāḥ  Rm 
 saṃhatās tatra ghātyaṃte samyagvāhaiva vaṃyayaḥ 
 tasmāt saṃghāta ity evaṃ vikhyāto 'nvarthasaṃjñayā  Rm 
 kāyavāgmānasaṃ tāpaṃ ye kurvantīha dehināṃ 
 kaṭukyapaṭikā ye ca rauravaṃ yānti te nārāḥ  Rm 
 tīvreṇa vahninā tatra dahyamānā niraṃtaraṃ 
 raudraṃ ravaṃ vimuṃcanti yatas tasmāt sa rauravaṃ  Rm 
 devadvijaguror dravyaṃ hṛtaṃ yair duḥkhinām iha 
 te mahārauravaṃ yānti ye cānyasvāpahāriṇaḥ  Rm 
 raudratvād vahnidāhasya ravasya ca mahattayā 
 rauravo hi mahāṃs tasya mantva rauravād api  Rm 
 kṛtvā guṇādhike tīvram apakāraṃ nihatya ca 
 mātāpitṛgurun kalpam avīcau pacyate dhruvaṃ  Rm 
 asthīny api viśīryyante raudrāgnau tatra dehināṃ 
 yato na vīciḥ saukhyasya nāvīcir udāhṛtaḥ  Rm 
 mithodroharatā ye traṇe ghnantīva dehinaḥ 
 pāpād asinakhās te tu jāyante duḥkhabhāginaḥ  Rm 
 nakhā evāsayas teṣām āyasā jvalitāḥ kharāḥ 
 tair anyonyaṃ nikṛntanti yat tenāsinakhāḥ smṛtāḥ  Rm 
 lohajvalitatīkṣṇāgrāḥ ṣoḍaśāṅgulakaṇṭakāḥ 
 balād ārohyata hraṃdan śālmalīḥ pāladārikaḥ  Rm 
 lohadamṣṭrā mahākāyā jvalitās tīvrabhairavāḥ 
 aśliṣya bhakṣayanty enaṃ paradāropahāriṇaṃ  Rm 
 āraṭanto 'pi khādyante śvagṛdhrolūkavāyasaiḥ 
 aśivaṃ kurvate chinnā viśvāsaghāṭino narāḥ  Rm 
 ayoguḍāni bhujyante prataptāni punaḥ punaḥ 
 yāpyante kvathitaṃ tāmraṃ ye parasvāpahāriṇaḥ  Rm 
 krūraiḥ śvabhir ayodraṃṣṭraiḥ kṛtyante vivaśā bhṛśaṃ 
 varṣakoṭi raṭanto 'pi ye narāḥ kheṭake ratāḥ  Rm 
 matsyādīñ jalajān hatvā jvalanty amradravodakāṃ 
 yāti vaitaraṇīṃ śaśvad vahninā dahyate naraḥ  Rm 
 ye svārthalavasaṃmūḍho vyavahāram adhārmikaṃ 
 karoti narake kradan sa cakreṇābhipīḍyate  Rm 
 pīḍā vahubhir ākāraiḥ kṛtā yair duḥkhinām iha 
 pīḍyante te ciraṃ taptair yatra mudgaraparvataiḥ  Rm 
 bhedakā dharmasetūnāṃ ye cāsan mārgavāhinaḥ 
 Rm 
 kṣuradhārācitaṃ mārgaṃ gatvā krāmanti te narāḥ  Rm 
 nakhaiḥ saṃcūrṇya yūkādīñ cūrṇyante meṣaparvatai 
 bhūyo bhūyo mahākāyāḥ krandantas te śaracchataṃ  Rm 
 vrataṃ yas tu samāśritya saṃpanno parirakṣati 
 śīryamānamānsāsthiḥ kukuṃle pacyate dhruvaṃ  Rm 
 aṇunāpi hi yaḥ kaścin mithyājīvena jīvati 
 bhakṣyate krimibhiś caṇḍaiḥ saṃmagno gūthamṛttike  Rm 
 dṛṣṭvāpi vrīhimadhyasthān prāṇinaś cūrṇayanti ye 
 āyasai mukhalais taptaiḥ kṣobhyante te punaḥ punaḥ  Rm 
 atyantakrodhanāḥ krūrāḥ śaṭhāḥ pāpābhikāṃkṣiṇaḥ 
 paravyasanakṛṣṭvā ca jāyante yamarākṣasāḥ  Rm 
 sarveṣām eva duḥkhānāṃ vījaṃ mṛd vābhibhedataḥ 
 kāyavāgmānasaṃ karma pāpaṃ yat tad aṇv api varttayet 
  narakakāṇḍaṃ samāptam 
 haṃsapārāvatādīnaṃ kharāṇām api rāgiṇāṃ 
 yena rāgeṇa jāyante mūḍhāḥ kīṭādiyoniṣu  Rm 
 sarppāḥ krodhopanāhābhyāṃ mārastabdhā mṛgādhipāḥ 
 abhimānena jāyante gadāmāśvādiyoniṣu  Rm 
 mātsaryerṣyādi doṣeṇa vānarāḥ pretadehinaḥ 
 jāyante mukharā dhṛṣṭāś capalātmānaś ca vāyasāḥ  Rm 
 vadhavaṃdhanamātsaryair gavāśvādiṣu dehinaḥ 
 jāyante krūrakarmāṇo lūtāḥ kharjjūravṛścikaḥ  Rm 
 vyāghramārjāragomāyuṛkṣagṛdhravṛgādāyaḥ 
 jāyante pretamansādoḥ krodhanā matsarā narāḥ  Rm 
 dātāraḥ krodhanāḥ krūrā narā nāgamaharddhikāḥ 
 bhavāntatyāgino darppāt krodhāc ca garuḍeśvarāḥ  Rm 
 kṛtaṃ yat pāpakaṃ karma svayaṃ vākkāyamānasaṃ 
 tiryañcas tena jāyante tan manogatim ākṛthāḥ  Rm 
  iti tiryakkāṇḍaṃ samāptam 
 bhakṣyabhojyāpahartāro ye kṣudrā dānavarji 
 bhavanti kuṇapāhārāḥ pretās te kaṭapūtanāḥ  Rm 
 viheṭhayanti ye bālā vaṃcayanty api tṛṣṇayā 
 te 'pi garbhamalāhārā jāyante kaṭapūtanāḥ  Rm 
 hīnācārātidīnāś ca matsarā nityakāṃkṣiṇaḥ 
 jāyaṃte ye narāḥ pretā 'ṣṭās te galagaṇḍakāḥ  Rm 
 dānaṃ nivārayaty eva na hi kiṃ tid dadāti yaḥ 
 kṣutkṣāmāsau mahākukṣiḥ pretaḥ śūcimukho bhavet  Rm 
 dhanaṃ rakṣati vaṃśārthe na bhuṃkte na dadāti yaḥ 
 dattādāyī tataḥ pretaḥ śrāddhabhoktā sa jāyate  Rm 
 yaḥ parasvāpahārepsur datvā caivānutapyate 
 bhoktā viṭśleṣmavāntānāṃ pretya pretaḥ sa jāyate  Rm 
 apriyaṃ vakti yaḥ krodhād vākyaṃ marmavibhedataṃ 
 bbavanty ulkāmukhaḥ pretaḥ suciraṃ tena karmaṇā  Rm 
 Rm 
 kurute kalahaṃ yas tu niṣkṛpaḥ krūramānasaḥ 
 krimikīṭapataṅgādeḥ prete 'sau jyotiko bhavet  Rm 
 grāmakūṭau dadāty eva yo janaṃ pīḍayanty api 
 kumbhāṇḍo vikṛtākāraḥ pūyāhāraś ca jāyate  Rm 
 nirdayāḥ prāṇino ghnanti bhakṣyārthaṃ ye dadanty api 
 māṃsāhārāś ca te 'vaśyaṃ bhavanti pretarākṣasāḥ  Rm 
 gaṃdhamālāratā nityaṃ maṃdakrodhāḥ pradāyakāḥ 
 gaṃdharvāḥ pretya jāyante devānāṃ ratihetavaḥ  Rm 
 krodhanāḥ piśunaḥ kiñcidarthārthaṃ yaḥ prayachati 
 sa piśācaṃ praduṣṭātmā jāyate vikṛtānanaḥ  Rm 
 nityapraduṣṭāś capalāḥ parapīḍākarā narāḥ 
 saṃpradānaratā nityaṃ bhūtāḥ pretya bhavanti te  Rm 
 krūrāḥ krūddhāḥ pradātāraḥ priyā sarvasurā ca ye 
 jāyante pretya yakṣās tu krūrātmānaḥ surāpriyāḥ  Rm 
 mātāpitṛgurūn yānair ye nayanti yathepsitaṃ 
 vimānacāriṇo yakṣā jāyaṃte susukhānvitāḥ  Rm 
 tṛṣṇāmātsaryadoṣeṇa pretā bhavanty amī sadā 
 yakṣādayaḥ śubhaiḥ kliṣṭair atas tān parivarjayet  Rm 
  iti pretakāṇḍaṃ samāptam 
 devāsuramanuṣyeṣu dīrgham āyur ahiṃsayā 
 jāyate hinsayā svalpām ato hiṃsāṃ vivarjayet  Rm 
 kuṣṭharogajvaronmādā ye cānye vyādhayo nṛṇāṃ 
 bhavanti bhūtaprayuktes te vadhavaṃdhanatāḍanaiḥ  Rm 
 yo na harttā parasvānāṃ na vañcavit prayachati 
 mahatāpi prayatnena sa dravyaṃ nādhigachati  Rm 
 adattaṃ vittam ādāya dānāni ca dadāti yaḥ 
 sa pretya dravyavān bhūtvā bhūyo bhavati nirdhanaḥ  Rm 
 yo na harttā na dātā ca na cātikṛpaṇo naraḥ 
 kṛtsnena mahatā dravyaṃ sthiraṃ sa labhate dhruvaṃ  Rm 
 na harttā yaḥ parasvānāṃ tyāgavān vītamatsaraḥ 
 ahāryaṃ vipulaṃ vittam iṣṭam ca labhate naraḥ  Rm 
 āyurvarṇavalopetaḥ śrīmān rogavivarjitaḥ 
 sukhī ca sa labhen nityaṃ yo dadātīha bhojanaṃ  Rm 
 salajjo rūpavān bhogī suchāyaḥ prāṇināṃ priyaḥ 
 sa bhaved vastralābhī ca yo vāsānsi prayachati  Rm 
 āvāsaṃ yo dadātīha suprasannena cetasā 
 prāsādāḥ sarvakāmāś ca jāyante tasya dehinaḥ  Rm 
 upānatsaṃkramādīni ye prayachanti mānavāḥ 
 bhavanti sukhino nityaṃ yānāni ca labhanti te  Rm 
 vāpīkūpataḍāgādīn kārayitvā jalāśrayān 
 sukhinas tyaktasaṃtāpā niḥpipāsā bhavanti te  Rm 
 puṣpair abhyarcitaḥ śrīmān śaraṇyaḥ sarvadehināṃ 
 samṛddhitaḥ sa syād ārāmaṃ yaḥ prayachati  Rm 
 vidyādānena paṇḍityaṃ prajñābhyāsena cāpyate 
 bhaiṣajyābhayadānena rogamuktas tu jāyate  Rm 
 Rm 
 dīpadānena cakṣuṣmān vādyadānena susvaraḥ 
 śayanāsanadānena sukhī bhavati mānavaḥ  Rm 
 gavādīnn yo dadātīha bhojyaṃ rasasamanvitaṃ 
 balavān varṇavān bhogī dīrghāyuḥ sa bhaven naraḥ  Rm 
 kanyādānena samānyāṃ lābhī syāt parivāravān 
 dhanadhānyasamṛddhas tu bhūmidānena jāyate  Rm 
 patraṃ puṣpaṃ phalaṃ toyam abhayaṃ vacanaṃ priyaṃ 
 yad yad evepsitaṃ śaktyā dātavyaṃ tat tad arthinaḥ  Rm 
 kleśayitvā dadātīha svakārthaṃ vā ha yena vā 
 yaśaḥsaukhyābhilākhād vā sa kliṣṭaṃ labhate phalaṃ  Rm 
 svakāryaṃ nirapekṣeṇa kṛpāviṣṭena cetasā 
 parārthaṃ yo dadātīha so 'kliṣṭaṃ phalam aśnute  Rm 
 yat kiñcid dīyate 'nyasmai yathākālaṃ yathāvidhiṃ 
 tena tena prakāreṇa tat sarvam upatiṣṭhate  Rm 
 parān anvapahaty evaṃ sarvakālaṃ yathepsitaṃ 
 akleśayitvā dātavyaṃ hitaṃ dharmāvirodhiyat  Rm 
 evaṃ hi dīyamānasya dānasyaiva phalādayaḥ 
 dānaṃ hi sarvasaukhyānām ananyat kāraṇaṃ mataṃ  Rm 
 virajaḥ paradārebhyo dārān iṣṭān avāpnuyāt 
 svebhyo 'py adeśakālau ca varjayet puṃstvam archati  Rm 
 paradāreṣu saṃsaktaṃ cittaṃ yo na niyachati 
 anaṃgeṣu cakṣyeta sa pumāṃ strītvam archati  Rm 
 strītvaṃ jugupsate yā tu suśīlamandarāgiṇī 
 puṃstvam ākāṃkṣate nityaṃ sā nārī naratāṃ vrajet  Rm 
 yas tu samyagnirātaṅkaṃ brahmacaryaṃ niṣevate 
 tejasvī sadguṇaḥ śrīmān devair api sa lakṣyate  Rm 
 dṛḍhasmṛtir asaṃmūḍho maghavāno niṣevanāt 
 jāyate satyavādī ca yaśaḥsaukhyānvitaḥ pumān  Rm 
 bhinnānām api satvānāṃ bhedaṃ naiva karoti yaḥ 
 abhedyaparivāro 'sau jāyate sthiramānasaḥ  Rm 
 yas tv ājñāṃ kurute nityaṃ gurūṇāṃ hṛṣṭamānasaḥ 
 hitāhitābhidhāyī ca sa syād ādeyavākkṛtī  Rm 
 nīcāparāyamānena viparyāsena codgataḥ 
 bhavanti sukhinaḥ saukhyaṃ duḥkhaṃ datvā ca duḥkhinaḥ  Rm 
 paraprapañcābhiratāḥ śaṭhāś cānṛtavādinaḥ 
 kubjavāmanatāṃ yānti ye ca rūpābhimāninaḥ  Rm 
 jaḍo vijñānamātsaryād bhaven mūkaḥ priyāpriyaḥ 
 vādhiryaṃ yāti mūḍhātmā hitavākyābhigūḍhakaḥ  Rm 
 duḥkham pāpasya puṇyasya sukhaṃ miśrasya miśritaṃ 
 sarvaṃ sādṛśyaniḥsyandam abhyuhyaṃ karmaṇaḥ phalaṃ  Rm 
 iti manuṣya kāṃdaṃ samāptam 
 śaṭhyena māyayā nityaṃ caraty akṛtakilbiṣaḥ 
 kalipriyaḥ pradātā ca sa bhaved asureśvaraḥ  Rm 
 Rm 
  ity asurakāṇḍam 
 nātmanā yaḥ sukhākāṃkṣī na ca kṛvyeta parigrahaṃ 
 grahāṇām agraṇī cāsau mahārājikatāṃ vrajet  Rm 
 mātāpitṛkulajyeṣṭhapūjakasyāgavān kṛtī 
 hṛṣyame yo na kalahais tridaśeṣu sa jāyate  Rm 
 na vigrahe ratā naiva kalahe hṛṣṭamānasāḥ 
 ekāntakuśalodyuktā ye ca moyāpagās tu te  Rm 
 bahuśrutā dharmadharāḥ suprajñā mokṣakāṃkṣiṇaḥ guṇair 
 ye parihṛṣṇāś ca narās te tuṣitopagāḥ  Rm 
 śīlapradānavinaye pravṛttā ye svayaṃ narāḥ 
 mahotsāhāś ca te 'vaśyaṃ nirmāṇaratigāminaḥ  Rm 
 adīnasatvā me śreṣṭhāḥ pradāne damasaṃyamaiḥ 
 guṇādhikāś ca ye yānti paranirmitatāṃ dhruvaṃ  Rm 
 śīlena svargam āpnoti dhyānena ca viśeṣataḥ 
 yathābhūtaparijñānāt paryante vo punarbhavaḥ  Rm 
 śubhāśubhaphalaṃ karma yad etat kathitaṃ sphuṭaṃ 
 śubhena labhyate saukhyaṃ duḥkhaṃ tv aśubhasaṃbhavaṃ  Rm 
 mṛtyur vyādhir jarā caiva cintanīyam idaṃ trayaṃ 
 viprayogā priyaiḥ sārddhaṃ karmaṇāṃ ca svakaṃ phalaṃ  Rm 
 evaṃ virāgam āpnoti viviktaḥ puṇyam archati 
 pāpaṃ ca nārjayed evaṃ tac ca saṃkṣepataḥ śṛṇu  Rm 
 samyakparārthakaraṇaṃ parānarthavivarjanaṃ 
 puṇyaṃ viparyayāt pāpabhuktam eva munīśvaraiḥ  Rm 
  iti devakāṇḍaṃ samāptam 
 evaṃ matvā mahārāja ṣaḍgatikārikāṃ bhave 
 saṃbodhidharmam ādhāya caritavyaṃ sadā śubhe  Rm 
 ye saṃbodhivrataṃ dhṛtvā pracaranti samāhitāḥ 
 sarvasatvahitārthena bodhisatvā bhavanti te  Rm 
 evaṃ vijñāya rājendra sadā bhadraṃ yadīchasi 
 triratnaṃ śaraṇaṃ kṛtvā bhaja nityaṃ samādarāt  Rm 
 etatpuṇyavipākena sarvakleśan vinirjayan 
 kramād bodhiṃ samāsādya saṃbuddhapadam āpnuyāḥ  Rm 
 iti tena munīndreṇa samākhyātaṃ niśamya saḥ 
 rājāpy uttarapāṃcālaḥ pravrajituṃ samaichata  Rm 
 tataḥ sa nṛpatī rājā samutthāya kṛtāṃjaliḥ 
 bhagavantam ānatvā prārthayad evam ādarāt  Rm 
 bhagavan nātha sarvajña bhavatāṃ śaraṇaṃ gataḥ 
 saṃbodhivratam ādhāya prechāmi carituṃ sadā  Rm 
 yad bhavāñ jagatāṃ śāstā saṃbodhidharmadeśikaḥ 
 tan me 'nugrahatāṃ kṛtvā pravrajyāṃ dātum arhati  Rm 
 iti saṃprārthite tena rājñā sa bhagavān sudhīḥ 
 tasya rājño manaḥśuddhaṃ vijñāyaivam upādiśat  Rm 
 sādhu rājan mahābhāga yadīchasi śubhāṃ gatiṃ 
 ehi cara samādhāya cara me śāsane vrataṃ  Rm 
 ity ādiśya munīndro 'sau pāṇinā tac chiraḥ spṛśan 
 Rm 
 saṃbuddhe śāsane dharme taṃ nareṃdraṃ samagrahīt  Rm 
 ehīti tena śāstrokte nṛpatiḥ sa prabodhitaḥ 
 khikkhirīpātradharo bhikṣu 'bhūc cīvarāvṛtaḥ  Rm 
 tataḥ sa bhūpatiś cāpi virakto bhogyanispṛhaḥ 
 niḥkleśaḥ pariśuddhātmā babhūva vijiteṃdriyaḥ  Rm 
 sākṣād arhatvam āsādya brahmacārī niraṃjanaḥ 
 saṃbodhipadam āsādya saṃbuddhaḥ śrāvako 'bhavat  Rm 
 tataḥ sa brahmavid yogī traidhātuvāsinām api 
 sadevāsuralokānāṃ vandyo mānyo 'bhavad guruḥ  Rm 
 tato dakṣiṇapāṃcālarājā sa pratimoditaḥ 
 utthāya sāṃjalir natvā prārthyat taṃ munīśvaraṃ  Rm 
 bhagavan nātha sarvajña kṛpayā me prasīdatu 
 traimāsyaṃ bhaktum ichāmi tat kurutām anugrahaṃ  Rm 
 iti saṃprārthite rājñā bhagavān sa munīśvaraḥ 
 nṛpatiṃ taṃ samālokya tūṣṇībhūtvādhyuvāsa tat  Rm 
 tataḥ sa nṛpatī rājā bhagavatādhyuvāsitaṃ 
 viditvā sarvasāmagrīṃ sahasā samasādhayat  Rm 
 tataḥ sa rājā bhagavaṃtaṃ sasāṃghikaṃ 
 yathārhabhojanair nityaṃ samabhyarcya 'bhyatoṣayat  Rm 
 vicitracīvaraiś cāpi śrīghanaṃ taṃ sasāṃghikaṃ 
 āchādya sāṃjalir natvā praṇidhānaṃ mudā vyadhāt  Rm 
 etatpuṇyavipākena loke 'ṃdhe 'parināyake 
 saddharmabhāskaraḥ śāstā saṃbuddho 'rhaṃ bhaveya hi  Rm 
 evaṃ tena narendreṇa praṇidhānaṃ kṛtaṃ mudā 
 matvā sa bhagavān smitaṃ prāmuñcac chubharociṣaṃ  Rm 
 tat smitasamutpannāḥ paṃcavarṇāḥ suraśmayaḥ 
 prasāritās trilokeṣu bhāsayantyaḥ pracerire  Rm 
 tadrasmisaṃparispṛṣṭāḥ sarve 'pi nārakāśritāḥ 
 nirmuktavedanākhedā mahatsaukhyaṃ pralebhire  Rm 
 tadā te vismitāḥ sarve nārakīyāḥ pramoditāḥ 
 kim evaṃ jāyate saukhyam iti dhyātvā niṣedire  Rm 
 tataḥ sa bhagavāṃs teṣāṃ vismayākrāṃtacetasāṃ 
 manāṃsi paribodhārthaṃ praiṣayat tatra nairmitaṃ  Rm 
 tadā te nārakāḥ sarve dṛṣṭvā taṃ sugataṃ mudā 
 upetya praṇatiṃ kṛtvā prābhajañ charaṇaṃ gatāḥ  Rm 
 tatas tat puṇyaliptās te sarve vimuktapāpakāḥ 
 pariśuddhāḥ śubhātmānaḥ sadgatiṃ samupāyayuḥ  Rm 
 tatas tā raśmayaḥ sarvā avabhāsya samaṃtataḥ 
 akaniṣṭhālayaṃ yāvat prasṛtāḥ samabhāsayan  Rm 
 gāthāghoṣaiś ca sarvatra sarvān devān pramodinaḥ 
 bodhayitvā śubhe dharme pratiṣṭhāpya pacerire  Rm 
 tatas tā raśmayaḥ sarvā piṇḍībhūtā muneḥ puraḥ 
 tridhā pradakṣiṇīkṛtvā mahoṣṇīṣe samāviśat  Rm 
 tad dṛṣṭvā te sabhālokāḥ sarve 'tivismayoddhatāḥ 
 Rm 
 śāstā kim ādiśed dharmam iti dhyātvā niṣedire  Rm 
 iti teṣāṃ manastarkaṃ matvānaṃdaḥ samutthitaḥ 
 upetya sāṃjalir natvā prārthayet taṃ munīśvaraṃ  Rm 
 bhagavan hetunā kena smitaṃ muṃcati sāṃprataṃ 
 nāhetvapratyayaṃ smitaṃ na muṃcaṃti munīśvarāḥ  Rm 
 tad yadarthe bhavān smitaṃ muṃcatīme sabhājanāḥ 
 śrotum ichaṃti sarve tad artham ādeṣṭum arhati  Rm 
 ity ānaṃdoditaṃ śrutvā bhagavān sa jagadguruḥ 
 sarvāṃl lokān samālokya tam ānaṃdaṃ samabravīt  Rm 
 evam eva sadānaṃda sarve buddhā munīśvarāḥ 
 nāhetupratyayaṃ smitaṃ vimuṃcanti kadā cana  Rm 
 paśyatām ayam ānaṃda rājātisaṃprasāditaḥ 
 satkṛtya śraddhayāsmākaṃ traimāsyaṃ bhajate mudā  Rm 
 etatpuṇyavipākena rājāyaṃ sadguṇākaraḥ 
 kramāt pāramitāḥ sarvāḥ paripūrya balānvitaḥ  Rm 
 sarvakleśagaṇāñ jitvā mārāñ cāpi vinirjayan 
 bodhim āsādya sarvajñas tathāgato munīśvaraḥ  Rm 
 sarvavidyādhipaḥ śāstā dharmarājo vināyakaḥ 
 vijayo nāma saṃbuddho bhaviṣyati bhavāntare  Rm 
 evam ānaṃda vijñāya buddhakṣetraśubhaṃkṛtaṃ 
 tadvipāke mahatsaukhyaṃ bhadraṃ saṃbodhisādhanaṃ  Rm 
 triratnaśaraṇaṃ kṛtvā satkāraiḥ śraddhayā sadā 
 saṃbodhivāñchibhir lokaiś caritavyaṃ śubhe mudā  Rm 
 ity ādiṣṭaṃ munīndreṇa śrutvānaṃdādayo 'pi te 
 sarve lokās tathety uktvā prābhyanandan prasāditāḥ  Rm 
 so 'pi dakṣiṇapāṃcālo rājā śrutvā pramoditaḥ 
 triratnabhajanaṃ kṛtvā pracacāra śubhe sadā  Rm 
 tadārabhya sadā tatra maṃgalaṃ nirupadravaṃ 
 samaṃtato mahotsāhaṃ kṛtayuga ivābhavat  Rm 
 iti me guruṇākhyātaṃ śrutaṃ mayā tathā 'dhunā 
 kathyate 'tra tvayāpy evaṃ caritavyaṃ śubhe sadā  Rm 
 prajāś cāpi mahārāja bodhayitvā prayatnataḥ 
 bodhimārge pratiṣṭhāpya pālanīyāḥ sadā tvayā  Rm 
 tathā te sarvadā bhadraṃ sarvatrāpi bhaved dhruvaṃ 
 kramād bodhiṃ samāsādya saṃbuddhapadam āpnuyāḥ  Rm 
 iti tenārhatādiṣṭaṃ śrutvāśokaḥ sa bhūmipaḥ 
 tathety abhyanumoditvā prābhyanandat sapārṣadaḥ  Rm 
 rājño pāñcālayor yan munikathitam idaṃ tat prasiddhāvadānaṃ 
 śṛṇvanti śrāvayanti pramuditamanasaḥ śraddhayā ye prasannāḥ 
 sarve te bodhisatvāḥ sakalaguṇadharāḥ sarvasaṃpatsukhāḍhyāḥ 
 kṛtvā lokeṣu bhaddraṃ munivaranilaye saṃprayānti pramodāḥ  Rm 
 Rm 
  iti ratnāvadānatatve pāṃcālarājāvadanaṃ samāptam 
 Rm 
 XXIX Upapādukāvadāna
 athāśoko mahīpālaḥ samupetya kṛtāṃjaliḥ 
 upaguptaṃ yatiṃ natvā prārthayad evam ādarāt  Rm 
 bhadanta śrotum ichāmi punar anyat subhāṣitaṃ 
 tadyathā guruṇādiṣṭaṃ tathākhyātuṃ ca me 'rhati  Rm 
 iti saṃprarthitaṃ rājñā śrutvā so 'rhan mahāmatiḥ 
 upagupto nareṃdraṃ taṃ samālokyaivam ādiśat  Rm 
 sādhu śṛṇu maharāja yathā me guruṇoditaṃ 
 tathāhaṃ te pravakṣyāmi śrutvā cāpy anumodaya  Rm 
 tadyathā bhagavān buddhā śākyasiṃho munīśvaraḥ 
 sarvajñaḥ sugataḥ śāstā dharmarājo vināyakaḥ  Rm 
 ekasmin samaye mātur māyādevyā hitechayā 
 saddharmaṃ samupādeṣṭuṃ prācarat tridaśālaye  Rm 
 tatra sa bhagavān gatvā suramye naṃdane vane 
 pārijātatale pāṇḍusacchilāyām upāśrayat  Rm 
 tatra śakrādayo devāḥ sarve taṃ sadguṇākaraṃ 
 śākyamuniṃ samālokya muditāḥ samupācaran  Rm 
 tatra taṃ śrīghanaṃ dṛṣṭvā sarve devāḥ pramoditāḥ 
 tridhā pradakṣiṇīkṛtya sāñjalayaḥ praṇemire  Rm

 utthāya samupāsṛtya praṇatvaivam abhāṣata  Rm

 pūjāṃgais taṃ jagannāthaṃ māyādevīṃ ca prārcayan  Rm
