 śrutvā sa bhagavāṃc chāstā mamaivaṃ samupādiśat  Rm 
 ito 'hni saptame svargād avatareya bhūtale 
 sāṃkāśanagaropāpajjure vane udumvare  Rm 
 ity ādiśya munīndreṇa preṣito 'ham ihācare 
 etad yūyaṃ parijñāya prābhyanandata sāṃprataṃ  Rm 
 iti tenārhatākhyātaṃ śrutvā te saṃghikā mudā 
 sevaṃ nṛpādi lokāś ca prābhyanandan pramoditāḥ  Rm 
 Rm 
 tatas te sāṃghikāḥ sarve lokā bhūpādayo 'pi ca 
 sāṃkāśanagaropāpajjure vane upācaran  Rm 
 tadā sa bhagavāṃs tatra svarge sendrān surān api 
 mātaraṃ samupāmaṃtrya pura evam upādiśat  Rm 
 mātaḥ sendrādi devāś ca yūyaṃ sarve samādarāt 
 triratnabhajanaṃ kṛtvā pracaradhvaṃ sadā śubhe  Rm 
 gacheyaṃ sāṃprataṃ dharmam upadeṣṭuṃ mahītale 
 nṛṇām api hitārthena gantum ichāmi nānyathā  Rm 
 ity ādiṣṭaṃ munīndreṇa sarve sendrāḥ surā api 
 mātāpi sāṃjalir natvā prārthayat taṃ munīśvaraṃ  Rm 
 bhagavan nātha sarvajña ko 'smākaṃ dharmam ādiśet 
 tad atra kṛpayā dharmam ādeṣṭuṃ sthātum arhati  Rm 
 iti taiḥ prārthite bhūyo bhagavān sa munīśvaraḥ 
 mātaraṃ tān surān sarvān dṛṣṭvaivaṃ ca samādiśat  Rm 
 mātar nāhaṃ sadaikatra tiṣṭheyaṃ dharmam ādiśan 
 sarvasatvahitārthena saṃbuddho 'smi jagadguruḥ  Rm 
 tan mātar aham ālokya martyānāṃ hitakāmpayā 
 saddharmāmṛtasaṃdānaṃ dātuṃ gachāmi sāṃprataṃ  Rm 
 ity ādiṣṭaṃ munīndreṇa śrutvā mātā surā api 
 sendrāḥ sarve 'pi te śāstuḥ pādāmbuje praṇemire  Rm 
 tatas te tridaśāḥ sarve mātāpi tasya tāyinaḥ 
 tridhā pradakṣiṇīkṛtya natvā svasvālayaṃ yayuḥ  Rm 
 tataḥ sa bhagavāṃs tatra devālaye samāhitaḥ 
 tat samādhiṃ samādhāya kṣaṇād antarhito 'carat  Rm 
 tataḥ sa bhagavāṃs tatra jambudvīpe prabhāsayan 
 sāṃkāśanagaropāpajjure dāve udumvare  Rm 
 avatīrya kṣaṇāt tatra śuddhāsane surāstṛte 
 samādhāya samāsīnas tasthau dhyānasamāhitaḥ  Rm 
 taṃ dṛṣṭvā svāsanāsīnaṃ śrīghanaṃ samupāgataṃ 
 sarve te sāṃghikā lokā bhūpādayo 'py upācaran  Rm 
 tatra taṃ śrīghanaṃ natvā sarve te saṃpramoditāḥ 
 tridhā pradakṣiṇīkṛtya samabhyarcyopatasthire  Rm 
 brahmaśakrādi devāś ca yakṣagaṃdharvakinnarāḥ 
 daityā vidyādharā nāgā garuḍāḥ siddhādayo 'pi ca  Rm 
 śrīghanaṃ samāyātaṃ draṣṭuṃ sarve samāgatāḥ 
 natvā pradakṣiṇīkṛtya samabhyarcyopatasthire  Rm 
 tatropapāduko bhikṣur bhagavantaṃ sasāṃghikaṃ 
 devādi sarvalokāṃś ca bhojayituṃ nyamaṃtrayat  Rm 
 bhagavān api devādi lokāḥ sarve prasāditāḥ 
 tasyānugraham ādhātuṃ tatheti pratyamodayan  Rm 
 atha sa bhagavāṃs tatra bhojanasamayāgate 
 saṃghamelāpane gaṇḍīm ākoṭayan pranādinīṃ  Rm 
 tadgaṇḍīdeśanākāle tasya bhikṣor yathehitaṃ 
 tathāsanāṃ vastrāṇi divyāni rucirāni ca  Rm 
 Rm 
 pūjāṅgāny api divyāni bhojyapānāmṛtāny api 
 sarvāṇy upacāravastūni punaḥ prādurbabhūvire  Rm 
 tadā sa bhikṣur ālokya sarvasāmagrasaṃyutaṃ 
 bhagavaṃtaṃ sasaṃghaṃ taṃ natvaivaṃ prārthayan mudā  Rm 
 bhagavan bhojanasyātra samayo varttate 'dhunā 
 tat sasaṃgho bhavān atra svasvāsane niṣīdatu  Rm 
 tataḥ sa bhagavāṃs tatra pādyaṃ gṛhya sasāṃghikaḥ 
 svasvāsane samāruhya samāśrayad yathākramaṃ  Rm 
 tathā devādi lokāś ca sarvasvasvāsaneṣu tat 
 yathākramaṃ samāśritya saṃniṣeduḥ prasāditāḥ  Rm 
 tān buddhapramukhān sarvān svasvāsanasamāśritān 
 dṛṣṭvā sa mudito bhikṣur yathāvidhiṃ samarcayat  Rm 
 tato divyopacārais tair bhojyapānāmṛtādibhiḥ 
 tān buddhapramukhān sarvan yathechaiḥ samatoṣayat  Rm 
 saṃbuddhapramukhāḥ sarve saṃghā lokāḥ surādayaḥ 
 tad divyabhojanaṃ bhuktvā vismitās tṛptim āyayuḥ  Rm 
 tataḥ sa bhikṣur ālokya sarvāns tān saṃpratoṣitān 
 tatpātrāṇy apanītvā taddhastādīn samaśodhayat  Rm 
 tataḥ sa bhikṣur oṣadhyatāmbūlādi rasāyanaiḥ 
 tān buddhapramukhān sarvān saṃmoditān akārayat  Rm 
 tatropapāduko bhikṣuḥ sāṃjaliḥ saṃpramoditaḥ 
 sasāṃghikaṃ munīndraṃ taṃ natvā tatpura āśrayat  Rm 
 tataḥ sa bhagavāṃs tasya bhikṣor matvā śubhāśayaṃ 
 āryasatyaṃ samārabhya dideśa dharmam uttamaṃ  Rm 
 taddharmadeśanāṃ śrutvā sa upapāduko yatiḥ 
 bhitvā 'vidyāgaṇaṃ prāptavidyābhijñāpado bhavan  Rm 
 paṃcagaṇḍamayaṃ dehaṃ saṃsāram aticañcalaṃ 
 viditvā sarvasaṃskāragatīś cāpi vighātinīḥ  Rm 
 kleśān māragaṇāñ cāpi jitvārhatvam avāptavān 
 tataḥ so 'rhaṃ mahābhijñaḥ pariśuddhatrimaṃḍalaḥ  Rm 
 jiteṃdriyo viśuddhātmā nirvikalpo niraṃjanaḥ 
 saṃsāralābhasatkāranispṛhas trijagatsv api  Rm 
 vaṃdyaḥ pūjyo 'bhimānyo 'bhūd brahmacārī jinātmajaḥ  Rm 
 tad dṛṣṭvā bhikṣavaḥ sarve vismayākulitāśayaḥ 
 bhagavaṃtaṃ tam ānamya paprachus tat purākṛtaṃ  Rm 
 bhagavan kiṃ purānena bhikṣuṇā sukṛtaṃ kṛtaṃ 
 yenopapāduko 'rhaṃ ca bhavaty ayaṃ mahāsudhīḥ  Rm 
 yac cāpy asya yater bhikṣoḥ prārthitaṃ tat samṛdhyati 
 etat sarvaṃ samākhyāya sarvān asmān prabodhaya  Rm 
 evaṃ tair bhikṣubhiḥ prārthite sa munīśvaraḥ 
 tān sarvān sāṃghikāl lokān samālokyaivam ādiśat  Rm 
 śṛṇudhvaṃ bhikṣavānena bhikṣuṇā yat purākṛtaṃ 
 tat sarvaṃ saṃpravakṣyāmi yuṣmaccittaprabodhane  Rm 
 Rm 
 purāsīn bhagavān buddho vipaścī nāma sarvavit 
 dharmarājo jagacchāstā tathāgato munīśvaraḥ  Rm 
 sa saṃbuddho jagannātho vandhumato mahīpateḥ 
 vandhumatyā mahāpūryyā rājadhānyā upāśraye  Rm 
 jināśrame mahodyāne sarvasatvahitechayā 
 saddharmaṃ samupādiśya vijahāra sasāṃghikaḥ  Rm 
 tasya vipaścinaḥ śāstuḥ sāṃghikāḥ paṃcabhikṣavaḥ 
 anyasmin mahodyāne varṣāsu vyaharans tadā  Rm 
 tatraikabhikṣuṇā teṣāṃ caturṇāṃ brahmacāriṇāṃ 
 vaiyāvṛtyakṛtaṃ karma suprasannānucāriṇā  Rm 
 tatas te bhikṣavas sarve catvāras tatprasādhanāt 
 sarvavidyāsamudyuktāḥ samādhisādhanodyatāḥ  Rm 
 klesān māragaṇāñ jitvā pariśuddhatrimaṇḍalāḥ 
 sākṣād arhattvasaṃprāptā babhūvu brahmavittamāḥ  Rm 
 tān arhato mahābhijñān dṛṣṭvā sa paṃcamo yatiḥ 
 muditas taccaraṇān natvā praṇidhānaṃ tathā vyadhāt  Rm 
 yad etebhir mamāgamya sākṣād arhattvam āgataṃ 
 etaddharmavipākena pravrajyārhattvam āpnuyāṃ  Rm 
 sarvopakaraṇair dravyair avaikalyaṃ yathehitaṃ 
 tat tathā sarvam apy eva sarvatrāpi samṛddhyatu  Rm 
 etatpuṇyavipākena sa bhikṣuḥ paṃcamaḥ sudhīḥ 
 ayam eva mahābhijño bhavati hīti manyatāṃ  Rm 
 punar api bhavaty atra yenāyam upapādukaḥ 
 tat karmaṃ pravakṣyāmi śṛṇuta yūyam ādarāt  Rm 
 purāsīd bhagavān buddhaḥ kāśyapo nāma sarvavit 
 arhan nātho jagacchāstā dharmarājas tathāgataḥ  Rm 
 sa saṃbuddho mahāpūryā vārāṇasyā upāśrame 
 mṛgadāve 'diśad dharmaṃ vijahāra sasāṃghikaḥ  Rm 
 tasmiṃś ca samaye tatra vārāṇasyaṃ gṛhādhipaḥ 
 āsīt tasya priyā bhāryyā garbhiṇī garbhapīḍitā  Rm 
 prasūtisamaye 'krandad ārttasvarā vilāpitā 
 tasyā ārttaravaṃ śrutvā sa bharttā karuṇārditaḥ 
 śokālaye samudvignaḥ niśrityaivaṃ vyaciṃtayat  Rm 
 hā duḥkhaṃ garbbhapīḍāsyā jāyate kiṃ kariṣyate 
 evaṃ duḥkhaṃ hi saṃsāre rogiṇāṃ bhavacāriṇāṃ  Rm 
 mātur evaṃ mahad duḥkhaṃ garbbhasthasya śiśor na kiṃ 
 etad duḥkham ahaṃ soḍhuṃ na śaknuyāṃ kathaṃ cana  Rm 
 tad atra kāśyapasyāhaṃ śāsane śaraṇaṃ gataḥ 
 pravrajya saṃvaraṃ dhṛtvā careyaṃ saṃvṛtiṃ sadā  Rm 
 iti niścitya sa śreṣṭhī gatvā kāśyapaśāsane 
 pravrajya saṃvaraṃ dhṛtvā cacāra saṃvṛtiṃ sadā  Rm 
 tataḥ kāle samāghrāte śreṣṭhī sa parikheditaḥ 
 triratnasmaraṇaṃ kṛtvā praṇidhānaṃ vyadhāt tadā  Rm 
 etatpuṇyavipākena sarvadātra punarbhave 
 Rm 
 mātur garbhe hy ajāyeyaṃ bhaveyam upapādukaḥ  Rm 
 etena praṇidhānena kāśyapaśaraṇaṃ gataḥ 
 triratnabhajanaiḥ kṛtvā pracacāra samāhitaḥ  Rm 
 etatpuṇyavipākena sārthavāhaḥ sa sanmatiḥ 
 bhavaty ayaṃ mahābhijñaḥ sāṃpratam upapādukaḥ  Rm 
 yathānena tadā tatra praṇidhānaṃ kṛtaṃ mudā 
 tathātra śāsane bauddhe pravrajyārhattvam āpyate  Rm 
 evaṃ hi manyatāṃ sarve saṃsāre karma yat kṛtaṃ 
 tat phalaṃ bhujyate nūnaṃ yathehitaṃ tathā dhruvaṃ  Rm 
 yenaiva yat kṛtaṃ karmaṃ tenaiva bhujyate phalaṃ 
 abhuktaṃ kṣīyate naiva kṛtakarmaphalaṃ kvacit  Rm 
 nāgnibhir dahyate karmaṃ kriyate nāpi codakaiḥ 
 vāyubhiḥ śuṣyate nāpi kṣīyate naiva bhūmiṣu  Rm 
 anyāthāpi bhaven naiva yat kṛtaṃ tat phalaṃ khalu 
 sarvatra bhujyate sarvair jantubhir bhavacāribhiḥ  Rm 
 kṛṣṇasya karmaṇaḥ pāke duḥkhataiva sadā bhave 
 śubhasya sukhatā nityaṃ miśritasyāpi miśritaṃ  Rm 
 evaṃ matvātra saṃsāre sarvadā sukhavāṃchibhiḥ 
 triratnabhajanaṃ kṛtvā caritavyaṃ śubhe sadā  Rm 
 ity ādiṣṭaṃ munīndreṇa śrutvā te bhikṣavas tathā 
 satyam iti parijñāya prābhyanandan prabodhitāḥ  Rm 
 so 'pi bhikṣuḥ parijñāya śrutvaivaṃ sugatoditaṃ 
 prabodhitaḥ prasannātmā prācaran sarvadā śubhe  Rm 
 iti me guruṇādiṣṭaṃ śrutaṃ mayā tathocyate 
 śrutvā rājans tvayāpy evaṃ caritavyaṃ śubhe sadā  Rm 
 prajāś cāpi mahārāja bodhayitvā prayatnataḥ 
 prerayitvā śubhe dharme pālanīyās tvayādarāt  Rm 
 evaṃ te sarvadā rājan sarvatrāpi śubhaṃ bhavet 
 krameṇa bodhim āsadya saṃbuddhapadam āpnuyāḥ  Rm 
 iti tenārhatākhyātaṃ śrutvāśokaḥ sa bhūpatiḥ 
 tatheti prativijñapya prābhyanaṃdat sapārṣadaḥ  Rm 
 yadāvadānaṃ hy upapādukasya śṛṇvaṃti ye cāpi niśāmayaṃti 
 sarve 'pi te kleśavimuktadehā bhuktvā sukhaṃ yānti jinālayaṃ te  Rm 
  iti śrīratnāvadānatatve upapādukāvadānaṃ samāptam 
 Rm 
 XXX Anityatāsūtra
 athāśoko mahīpālaḥ kṛtāṃjaliḥ purogataḥ 
 upaguptaṃ yatiṃ natvā punar evam abhāṣata  Rm 
 bhadanta śrotum ichāmi punar anyat subhāṣitaṃ 
 tadyathā guruṇādiṣṭaṃ tathādeṣṭuṃ ca me 'rhati  Rm 
 iti saṃprārthitaṃ rājñā śrutvā so 'rhaṃ sudhīr yatiḥ 
 upagupto nareṃdraṃ taṃ samāmaṃtryaivam abravīt  Rm 
 sādhu śṛṇu mahārāja tava puṇyapravṛddhaye 
 yāthā me guruṇākhyātaṃ tathā mayā pravakṣyate  Rm 
 tadyathā bhagavān buddhaḥ śākyasiṃho mahāmuniḥ 
 ekasmin samaye tatra śrāvastyā bahir āśrame  Rm 
 jetodyāne manoramye vihāre maṇimaṇḍite 
 sarvalokahitārthena vijahāra sasāṃghikaḥ  Rm 
 tatra sa bhagavāṃc chāstā sabhāsthitaḥ prabhāsayan 
 tāṃ sarvān sāṃghikān dṛṣṭvā samāmaṃtryaivam ādiśat  Rm 
 anityā bhikṣavaḥ sarve saṃskārā adhruvāḥ kṣaṇāḥ 
 vipariṇāmadharmāṇo 'sthirā nāsvāsikā api  Rm 
 yāvanto bhikṣavaḥ satvāś caturyonisamudbhavāḥ 
 bhautikāḥ prāṇinaḥ sarve jaṃgamā acalā api  Rm 
 ete 'pi prāṇinaḥ sarve saṃskārabhavacāriṇaḥ 
 svakṛtakarmabhuṃjāno bhramanti ṣaḍgatiṣv api  Rm 
 yāvantaḥ prāṇinaḥ satvāḥ sarveṣu narakeṣv api 
 svakṛtakarmabhuṃjāno bhramaṃti duḥkhapīḍitāḥ  Rm 
 te sarve 'pi svadaivāṃtte kāle mṛtyuṃ vrajanty api 
 kṛtakarmānusāreṇa punarbhave bhramaṃti te  Rm 
 kasya na janma mṛtyuś ca maraṇāṃtaṃ hi jīvitaṃ 
 yāvaṃtaḥ pretikāḥ satvāḥ sarve pretālayeṣv api  Rm 
 svakṛtakarmabhuṃjāno bhramaṃti duḥkhapīḍitāḥ 
 te ca sarve 'pi karmāṃte kāle mṛtyuṃ prayāṃty api  Rm 
 kṛtakarmānusāreṇa punarjanma labhaṃti te 
 sarveṣām api jantūnāṃ saṃskāragaticāriṇāṃ  Rm 
 kasya na janma mṛtyuś ca maraṇāṃtaṃ hi jīvitaṃ 
 tiryaggatiṣu yāvaṃtas tiryañcuḥ prāṇinaś ca te  Rm 
 sarve 'pi karmabhuṃjāno bhramaṃti svakṛtānugāḥ 
 te ca sarve 'pi karmānte kāle mṛtyuṃ vrajaṃty api  Rm 
 te ca karmānusāreṇa punarjanma labhanty api 
 Rm 
 sarveṣām api jaṃtūnāṃ saṃskāragaticāriṇāṃ  Rm 
 kasya na janma mṛtyuś ca maranāṃtaṃ hi jīvitaṃ 
 yāvanto manujāḥ satvā martyalokeṣu bhūmiṣu 
 svakṛtakarmabhuṃjānā bhramaṃti sukhaduḥkhitāḥ  Rm 
 te ca sarve 'pi karmānte kāle mṛtyuṃ prayāṃty api 
 te ca karmānusāreṇa punarjanma labhaṃty api  Rm 
 ye cāpi brāhmaṇā dhīrāḥ sarve śāstravicakṣaṇāḥ 
 ṣaṭkarmaniratā vijñāś caturbrahmavihāriṇaḥ  Rm 
 te 'pi sarve svakarmānubhuṃjāno bhavacāriṇaḥ 
 prayāṃti samaye mṛtyuṃ kasya mṛtyur bhave na hi  Rm 
 yāvanto ṛṣayo dhīrāḥ paṃcābhijñāguṇābdhayaḥ 
 te sarve samaye mṛtyuṃ prayāṃti bhavacāriṇaḥ  Rm 
 ye cāpi tīrthikā dhīrā mahatkaṣṭatapodharāḥ 
 te 'pi ca samaye mṛtyuṃ gachaṃti bhavagāminaḥ  Rm 
 ye dhīrā yoginaś cāpi yogadhyānasamāhitāḥ 
 te 'pi sarve prayāṃty eva samaye maraṇaṃ dhruvaṃ  Rm 
 ye cāpy upāsakā dhīrāḥ śuddhaśīlā vrataṃdharāḥ 
 te cāpi samaye sarve prayāṃti maraṇaṃ dhruvaṃ  Rm 
 ye cāpi kṣatriyā vīrā rājāno lokapālakāḥ 
 te 'pi sarve prayāṃty eva samaye maraṇaṃ dhruvaṃ  Rm 
 ye cāpi maṃtriṇo vijñā hitārthaṃ maṃtradeśakāḥ 
 te 'pi sarve prayāṃty eva samaye maraṇaṃ dhruvaṃ  Rm 
 ye cāpy evaṃ mahāmātyā rājyapālanatatparāḥ 
 te sarve prayānty eva samaye maraṇaṃ dhruvaṃ  Rm 
 ye ca bhaṭṭā mahāvīrā duṣṭamardanatatparāḥ 
 te 'pi sarve prayānty eva samaye maraṇaṃ dhruvaṃ  Rm 
 ye cāpi dhaninaḥ śreṣṭhāḥ sādhavo bhadrakārakāḥ 
 te 'pi sarve prayānty eva samaye maraṇaṃ dhruvaṃ  Rm 
 ye cāpi vaṇijo dhīrāḥ sārthavāhā dhanādhipāḥ 
 te 'pi sarve prayānty eva samaye maraṇaṃ dhruvaṃ  Rm 
 ye cāpi śilpino vijñā hitārthaṃ guṇasādhakāḥ 
 te 'pi sarve pragachaṃti samaye maraṇaṃ dhruvaṃ  Rm 
 ye cāpi kṛṣikarttāraḥ prāṇahitārthasādhakāḥ 
 te 'pi sarve vrajanty eva maraṇaṃ samaye dhruvaṃ  Rm 
 ye ca vaiśyāḥ prajānāthāḥ sarvadravyahitaṃkarāḥ 
 te 'pi sarve vrajanty eva samaye maraṇaṃ dhruvaṃ  Rm 
 ye cāpi sadguṇādhānā daivajñā vidhivittamāḥ 
 te cāpi samaye sarve prayāṃti maraṇaṃ dhruvaṃ  Rm 
 ye ca vaidyā mahāvijñāḥ sarvarogaśamaṃkarāḥ 
 te 'pi sarve vrajanty eva maraṇaṃ samaye dhruvaṃ  Rm 
 ye capi bhautikā vijñāḥ sarvabhūtapraśāṃtakāḥ 
 Rm 
 te 'pi sarve visaṃyogād vrajaṃti maraṇaṃ dhruvaṃ  Rm 
 ye cāpi maṃtriṇo vīrāḥ sarve karmārthasādhakāḥ 
 te 'pi sarve visaṃyogāt prayāṃti maraṇaṃ dhruvaṃ  Rm 
 evam anye 'pi lokāś ca nihīnamadhyamottamāḥ 
 sarve mṛtyuṃ prayānty eva kasya mṛtyur vaśe khalu  Rm 
 gaṃdharvāś ca mahāvīrā devādhikā maharddhikāḥ 
 te 'pi sarve vrajanty eva nissārā maraṇaṃ dhruvaṃ  Rm 
 kumbhāṇḍāś ca mahāvīrā mahābhīmā mahāvalāḥ 
 te 'pi kāle prayānty eva sarvatra maraṇaṃ dhruvaṃ  Rm 
 nāgāś cāpi mahābhimā garuḍāś cā maharddhikāḥ 
 te 'pi sarve prayānty eva kāle mṛtyuṃ bhaved dhruvaṃ  Rm 
 yakṣāś cāpi mahāvīrā devāsuramaharddhikāḥ 
 te 'pi sarve prayānty eva kāle mṛtyuṃ nirudyamāḥ  Rm 
 kinnarāś ca mahāvīrāḥ khagāmino maharddhikāḥ 
 te 'pi sarve nirutsāhāḥ kāle yānti yamālayaṃ  Rm 
 siddhāś cāpi mahāvīrāḥ sarvakāryārthasādhakāḥ 
 te 'pi sarve vrajanty eva kāle mṛtyuṃ nirudyamāḥ  Rm 
 sādhyāś cāpi mahādhīraḥ sarvahitārthasādhakāḥ 
 te 'pi sarve prayānty eva maraṇaṃ sarvadā dhruvaṃ  Rm 
 rākṣasāś ca mahābhīmā mahāvīryaparākramāḥ 
 te 'pi sarve prayānty eva nivīryā maraṇaṃ dhruvaṃ  Rm 
 evam anye 'pi satvāś ca siṃhavyāghrādi jaṃtavaḥ 
 paśavaḥ pakṣiṇaś cāpi krimikīṭādayo 'pi ca  Rm 
 aṇḍajāḥ svedajāś caiva sarve 'pi prāṇino 'pi te 
 kāle daivānubhoktāro vrajanti maraṇaṃ dhruvaṃ  Rm 
 daityāś cāpi mahāvīrā māhāvīryā maharddhikāḥ 
 te 'pi sarve prayāṃty evaṃ samaye maraṇaṃ dhruvaṃ  Rm 
 śakrādayo 'pi devendrāḥ sārve devāḥ sudhāṃśinaḥ 
 te 'pi kāle divaś cyutvā bhramaṃti ṣaḍgatiṣv api  Rm 
 apsaraso 'pi divyāṃgā yathākāma sukhaṃcarāḥ 
 tāś cāpi samaye sarvāś cyutvā yāṃti yamālayaṃ  Rm 
 vidyādharā mahābhijñā yathechā sukhacāriṇaḥ 
 te 'pi sarve nirutsāhāḥ kāle yāṃti yamāntike  Rm 
 evam anye 'pi lokāś ca janmino bhavacāriṇaḥ 
 sarve 'pi karmabhuṃjānaḥ kāle mṛtyuṃ vrajanty api  Rm 
 rasātalacarā ye svakṛtakarmabhojinaḥ 
 teṣāṃ api ca sarveṣāṃ maranāṃtaṃ hi jīvitaṃ  Rm 
 kāmadhātucarā ye ca svakṛte karmacāriṇaḥ 
 teṣām api ca sarveṣāṃ maraṇāṃtaṃ hi jīvitaṃ  Rm 
 rūpadhātugatā ye cā dhyānabhogasamāhitāḥ 
 teṣām api ca sarveṣāṃ maraṇāṃtaṃ hi jīvitaṃ  Rm 
 ye cāpy ārūpiṇo devā nirālokyā niraṃjanāḥ 
 teṣām api ca sarveṣāṃ maranāṃtaṃ hi jīvitaṃ  Rm 
 ye cāpi bhikṣavo 'rhanto vītakleśā jiteṃdriyāḥ 
 Rm 
 māracaryāvinirmuktā nirvikalpā niraṃjanāḥ  Rm 
 teṣām api ca sarveṣāṃ maraṇāṃtaṃ hi jīvitaṃ 
 kasya mṛtyur bhave nāsti janmino maraṇaṃ dhruvaṃ  Rm 
 pratyekasugatā ye ca niḥkleśā vijiteṃdriyāḥ 
 nirvikalpā nirāsaṃgā ekāṃtadhyānacāriṇaḥ  Rm 
 teṣām api ca sarveṣāṃ maraṇāṃtaṃ hi jīvitaṃ 
 kasya nāsti bhave mṛtyur jātasya maraṇaṃ dhruvaṃ  Rm 
 bodhisatvā mahāsatvāḥ sarvasatvahitaṃkarāḥ 
 mahābhijñā mahādhīrāś caturbrahmavihāriṇaḥ  Rm 
 daśabhūmīśvarā nāthā daśapāramitāratāḥ 
 satvārthavaśitāprāptā dhāraṇībalasaṃyutāḥ  Rm 
 teṣām api ca sarveṣāṃ maranāṃtaṃ hi jīvitaṃ 
 kasya nāsti bhave mṛtyur janmino maraṇaṃ dhruvaṃ  Rm 
 tathāgatāś ca saṃbuddhāḥ sarvajñāḥ sugatā jināḥ 
 mārajito jagannāthāḥ ṣaḍabhijñā munīśvarāḥ  Rm 
 dharmarājāḥ suśāstāro daśavalā vināyakāḥ 
 samaṃtabhadrakarttāraś caturbrahmavihāriṇaḥ  Rm 
 te sarve bhagavanto 'pi traidhātubhuvaneṣv api 
 bodhicaryāṃ kṛtvā samādiśya saddharmaṃ ca samaṃtataḥ  Rm 
 sarvatra maṃgalaṃ kṛtvā kṛtvā dharmamayaṃ jagat 
 bodhimārge pratiṣṭhāpya sarvasatvāñ chubhānvitān  Rm 
 sarvasaṃbuddhakāryāṇi samāpya parinivṛtāḥ 
 supariśuddhanirvāṇaṃ samaye saṃvrajanty api  Rm 
 evaṃ matvātra saṃsāre sarveṣāṃ maraṇaṃ dhruvaṃ 
 sarvān saṃskārajān duḥkhāns tyaktuṃ prārabhatodyamaṃ  Rm 
 anityā vata saṃskārā avidyākalpanodbhavāḥ 
 kleśāśrayā mahāduḥkhamūlā vidhvaṃsino 'śubhāḥ  Rm 
 tasmāt saṃsāraduḥkhāni tyaktum ichaṃti ye narāḥ 
 te māyāsaṃratiṃ tyaktvā caraṃtu buddhaśāsane  Rm 
 ye buddhaśāsane bhaktyā triratnaṃ śaraṇaṃ gatāḥ 
 saṃbodhisaṃvaraṃ dhṛtvā saṃcaraṃte samāhitāḥ  Rm 
 te sarve śubhātmāno niḥkleśā vimalāśayāḥ 
 bodhicaryāṃ samāsādya kuryus satvahitaṃ sadā  Rm 
 tataḥ pāramitāḥ sarvāḥ paripūrya yathākramaṃ 
 samyakṣaṃbodhim āsādya bhaveyuḥ sugatā jināḥ  Rm 
 tataḥ sarvatra lokeṣu kṛtvā loke subhadratāṃ 
 bodhimārge jagallokaṃ pratiṣṭhāpya prayatnataḥ  Rm 
 tato nirvāṇam āsādya nirviśeraṃ jinālaye 
 tadā te vimalātmāno nilīnāḥ syu nijālaye  Rm 
 evaṃ matvā nijānaṃdaṃ prāptuṃ saṃbodhisādhane 
 trikāye vīryam utthāpya carantu buddhaśāsane  Rm 
 Rm 
 kiṃ kāyena vinā dharmaṃ vācāpi kiṃ vinā guṇaṃ 
 manaso kiṃ vinā vīryyaṃ kiṃ vīryaṃ saṃvaraṃ vinā  Rm 
 yathā puṣpaṃ tathā dehaṃ yathā pakvaphalaṃ tanuḥ 
 kṣaṇāc cyutvāyate bhumau tathā kiṃ śobhate tanuḥ  Rm 
 kumbhakārakṛtaṃ yadvan mṛnmayaṃ māmabhājanaṃ 
 tadvad dehaṃ kṣaṇadhvaṃsi matvā carantu saṃvaraṃ  Rm 
 kadalīstambhasaṃkāśaṃ nissāraṃ bhedano sahaṃ 
 matvā dehaṃ samutthāya carantu saugataṃ vṛsaṃ  Rm 
 phenapiṇḍopamaṃ kāyaṃ nirguṇaṃ kṣaṇabhaṃguraṃ 
 matvā vīryamahotsāhaṃ dhṛtvā caraṃtu saṃvaraṃ  Rm 
 āyurdehe sthiraṃ naiva tṛṇaṃ patragatāmbuvat 
 matvā saṃbodhisaṃprāptyai carantu saugataṃ vrataṃ  Rm 
 ye saugatavrataṃ dhṛtvā caraṃti bodhilabdhaye 
 durgatiṃ na gachaṃti gachaṃti sadgatiṃ sadā  Rm 
 tasmād ichaṃti ye bhadraṃ saṃsāre bodhisādhanaṃ 
 te triratnaṃ sadā bhaktyā bhajaṃtu śaraṇaṃ gatāḥ  Rm 
 triratnabhajanotpannaṃ puṇyaṃ na kṣiṇute kvacit 
 etatpuṇyabalenaiva jīyate sarvapātakaṃ  Rm 
 puṇyam eva jaganmitraṃ pāpa eva jagadripuḥ 
 tat puṇyamitram ārādhya jayaṃtu pāpakaṃ ripuṃ  Rm 
 puṇyavān puruṣaḥ śreṣṭhaḥ sarvatra jagate sadā 
 yathābhilaṣitaṃ saukhyaṃ bhuktvā yāṃti sukhāvatiṃ  Rm 
 ity evaṃ bhagavān āha śrutvā te sarvasāṃghikāḥ 
 satyam iti paribuddhvā praceruḥ saugataṃ vrataṃ  Rm 
 etan me guruṇākhyātaṃ tathā tatra mayocyate 
 tvayāpy evaṃ mahārāja caritavyaṃ śubhe vṛṣe  Rm 
 prajāś cāpi mahārāja bodhayitvā prayatnataḥ 
 śubhe dharme pratiṣṭhāpya pālanīyāḥ sadādarāt  Rm 
 tathā te maṃgalaṃ nityaṃ sarvatrāpi bhavet sadā 
 kramād bodhiṃ samāsādya saṃbuddhapadam āpnuyāḥ  Rm 
 iti tenārhatādiṣṭaṃ śrutvāśokaḥ sa bhūmipaḥ 
 tathety uktvā praṇatvā ca prābhyanadat sapārṣadaḥ  Rm 
 anityatāsūtram idaṃ subhāṣyaṃ śṛṇvanti ye cāpi narāḥ prasannāḥ 
 sukhāni bhuktvā śubhadharmaraktāḥ samyāṃti cānte sugatālaye te  Rm 
  iti śrīratnāvadānatatve 'nityatāsūtraṃ parisamāptam 
 Rm 
 XXXI Pretībhūtāvadāna
 athāśoko mahīpālaḥ kṛtāṃjaliḥ puraḥsthitaḥ 
 upaguptaṃ tam ānamya mudaivaṃ punar abravīt  Rm 
 bhadanta śrotum ichāmi punar anyat subhāṣitaṃ 
 tadyathā guruṇākhyātaṃ tathādeṣṭuṃ ca me 'rhati  Rm 
 iti saṃprārthite rājñā sa yatīśaḥ prasannadhīḥ 
 tam aśokaṃ mahārājaṃ samālokyaivam ādiśat  Rm 
 śṛṇu sādhu mahārāja yathā me guruṇoditaṃ 
 tathāhaṃ te pravakṣyāmi śrutvānumodanāṃ kuru  Rm 
 tadyathā bhagavān buddhaḥ śākyasiṃho munīśvaraḥ 
 sarvajño 'rhañ jagacchāstā dharmarājas tathāgataḥ  Rm 
 puraikasamaye tatra śrāvastyā bahir āśrame 
 jetavane mahodyāne vihāre maṇimaṃḍite  Rm 
 sarvasatvahitārthena bodhicaryāṃ prakāśayan 
 saddharmaṃ samupādiśya vijahāra sasāṃghikaḥ  Rm 
 tatra te bhikṣavo 'rhantaḥ sāṃghikāś cailakā api 
 bodhisatvā mahāsatvāḥ sarvasatvahitārthinaḥ  Rm 
 bhikṣuṇyaḥ śuddhaśīlāś ca vratinaś ca śubhāśayāḥ 
 triratnasevakāḥ śrāddhā upāsakā upāsikāḥ  Rm 
 sarve 'pi sāṃghikās tatra saddharmaṃ śrotum āgatāḥ 
 kramāt taṃ śrīghanaṃ natvā kṛtvā tridhā pradakṣiṇāṃ  Rm 
 tat sabhāyāṃ krameṇaiva puraskṛtya samaṃtataḥ 
 kṛtāṃjalipuṭo dṛṣṭvā samupatasthur ādarāt  Rm 
 tadā tatra sureṃdrāś ca saśakrojamaheśvaraḥ 
 sarve 'pi lokapālāś ca sasainyabalavāhanaḥ  Rm 
 asurendrāḥ sasainyāś ca yakṣagaṃdharvakiṃnarāḥ 
 rākṣasā garuḍā nāgāḥ siddhā vidyādharādayaḥ  Rm 
 evam anye 'pi lokāś ca brāhmaṇāś ca maharṣayaḥ 
 yatayo yoginaś cāpi tīrthikāś ca tapaśvinaḥ  Rm 
 rājānaḥ kṣatriyāś cāpi nṛpo rājakumārakāḥ 
 vaiśyāś ca maṃtriṇaḥ śreṣṭhā amātyāś ca mahājanāḥ  Rm 
 senānyaḥ sabalāś cāpi gṛhasthāḥ paurikā janāḥ 
 vaṇijaḥ sārthavāhāś ca dhaninaḥ śilpino 'pi ca  Rm 
 anye jānapadāś cāpi grāmyāḥ kārpaṭikā api 
 evam anye 'pi lokāś ca saddharmaguṇavāṃchinaḥ  Rm 
 sarve tatra samāyātā dṛṣṭvā taṃ śrīghanaṃ muniṃ 
 natvā pradakṣiṇīkṛtya samabhyarcya kramān mudā  Rm 
 tataḥ sarve 'pi te natvā puraskṛtya samaṃtataḥ 
 tat saddharmāmṛtaṃ pātum upatasthuḥ samāhitāḥ  Rm 
 tadā sa bhagavān dṛṣṭvā tān sarvān samupasthitān 
 Rm 
 bodhicaryāṃ samārabhya dideśa dharmam uttamaṃ  Rm 
 tat saddharmāmṛtaṃ pītvā sarve lokāḥ prabodhitāḥ 
 saṃbodhisādhanotsāhaṃ labdhvā saṃmumudur bhṛśaṃ  Rm 
 tasmiṃś ca samaye tatra śrāvastye yo gṛhādhipaḥ 
 āḍhyo mahādhanaḥ śrāddhaḥ śrīmāñc chrīdopamaḥ kṛtī  Rm 
 sa tadā tatra saṃbuddhaṃ śrīghanaṃ taṃ munīśvaraṃ 
 draṣṭuṃ jetāśrame ramye vihāre samupācarat  Rm 
 tatra sabhāsamāsīnaṃ śrīghanaṃ taṃ munīśvaraṃ 
 dṛṣṭvā sa muditaḥ śreṣṭhī praṇatvā samupācarat  Rm 
 tatra pradakṣiṇīkṛtvā praṇatvā sāṃjalir mudā 
 tat saddharmāmṛtaṃ pātuṃ purataḥ samupāśrayat  Rm 
 taṃ dṛṣṭvā samupāsīnaṃ bhagavān sa munīśvaraḥ 
 matvā tasyāśayaṃ śuddham āryasatyam upādiśat  Rm 
 tadāryasatyam ākarṇya sa śreṣṭhī pratibodhitaḥ 
 saṃsāraviratas tatra pravrajituṃ samaichata  Rm 
 tatra sa suprasannātmā śreṣṭhī mudā samutthitaḥ 
 sāṃjalis taṃ muniṃ natvā pravrajyāṃ samayācata  Rm 
 bhagavan nātha sarvajña bhavatāṃ śaraṇaṃ vraje 
 tat pravrajyāṃ vrataṃ mahyaṃ kṛpayā dātum arhati  Rm 
 iti saṃprārthite tena dṛṣṭvā sa bhagavān muniḥ 
 tasyāśayaṃ viśuddhatvaṃ samālokyaivam ādiśat  Rm 
 yadi śrāddhāsti te vatsa saugataśāsane vrate 
 ehi cara samādhāya brahmacaryaṃ vratottamaṃ  Rm 
 ity uktvā sa jagacchāstā savyahastena tac chiraḥ 
 saṃspṛṣṭvā śāsane bauddhe śreṣṭhinaṃ taṃ samagrahīt  Rm 
 tatra pravrajitas tena munīndreṇa sa muṇḍitaḥ 
 khikkhirīpātradhṛg bhikṣu rarāja cīvarāvṛtaḥ  Rm 
 tataḥ sa bhikṣur ātmajño lābhī lokābhipūjitaḥ 
 āgṛhītapariṣkārā labdhadravyaṃ samācinot  Rm 
 tallabdhaṃ saṃcitaṃ dravyaṃ sa saha brahmacāribhiḥ 
 saṃvibhāgaṃ guroḥ kiṃcid apy akarot kadā cana  Rm 
 tathā sa matsarākrāntahṛdayo duritāśayaḥ 
 svayam eva prabhuṃjānaḥ kiṃcin naiva dadau kvacit  Rm 
 tataḥ sa samaye kāladharmayukto rujāturaḥ 
 tad dravyasaṃcayaṃ smṛtvā nitaḥ pretālayaṃ yayau  Rm 
 pretībhūto 'pi sa smṛtvā tad dravyasaṃcayaṃ punaḥ 
 svakoṣṭhālaya āgatya tasthau svāsana āśrayan  Rm 
 tatas te bhikṣavaḥ sarve tatkoṣṭhe taṃ mṛtakaṃ yatiṃ 
 dṛṣṭvā gaṇḍīṃ parāhatya saṃskārtuṃ vidhi cārcayan  Rm 
 tato nītvā bahirdeśe saṃskṛtya vahnināpitaṃ 
 tataḥ pratyāgatāḥ sarve tat koṣṭhadvāram āyayuḥ  Rm 
 tatas tal layanadvāraṃ vimucya pātracīvaraṃ 
 pratyaveksitum ālabdhās taṃ pretaṃ samapaśyata  Rm 
 Rm 
 taṃ pretaṃ vikṛtaṃ pātraṃ dhṛtaṃ cīvaraprāvṛtaṃ 
 dṛṣṭvā te bhikṣavaḥ sarve samudvignā vicerire  Rm 
 tatas te bhikṣavaḥ sarve bhagavataḥ purogatāḥ 
 etat sarvapravṛttāṃtaṃ praṇatvā saṃnyavedayat  Rm 
 tac chrutvā bhagavāṃs tasya pretasyānugrahārthataḥ 
 sa lokodvejanārthaṃ ca tad deśaṃ samupācarat  Rm 
 tatrāsau preta ārāt taṃ bhagavaṃtam upāgataṃ 
 dvātriṃsallakṣaṇāśītivyaṃjanapratimaṇḍitaṃ  Rm 
 śatasūryyādhikodbhāsaṃ vyāmābhāsam alaṃkṛtaṃ 
 ratnāṃgam iva bhadrāṃśaṃ dadarśa śrīghanaṃ muniṃ  Rm 
 tatra sa preta ālokya lajjāvibheditāśayaḥ 
 prarudan sāṃjalir natvā tasthau prasāditāśayaḥ  Rm 
 tataḥ sa bhagavān dṛṣṭvā taṃ pretaṃ saṃprasāditaṃ 
 brahmagambhīranirghoṣavacasā paryabhāṣata  Rm 
 bhadramukha tvayaivaitad ātmavadhāya durdhiyā 
 pātracīvaram ādhāya caritaṃ saṃvaraṃ vṛthā  Rm 
 yenāpāyasamutpannaḥ pretībhūto durākṛtiḥ 
 kim idānīṃ ruditvātra svakṛtaṃ paribhuktavān  Rm 
 sādhv atra sāṃprataṃ cittaṃ prasādaya mamāntike 
 asmāc cāpi pariṣkāradravyāc cittaṃ virāgaya  Rm 
 mā haivetaḥ punaḥ kālaṃ kṛtvā yāsyasi nairaye 
 tat saṃghe śaraṇaṃ gaccha tena tvaṃ sadgatiṃ vraje  Rm 
 ity ādiṣṭaṃ munīndreṇa śrutvā sa preta utthitaḥ 
 sa pātracīvaraṃ dravyaṃ saṃghebhyo nirayātayat  Rm 
 tataḥ saṃghān praṇatvaiva bhagavatpādayo pure 
 nipatya svakṛtaṃ pāpaṃ dideśa sāṃjalir mudā  Rm 
 bhagavan nātha sarvajña yat pāpaṃ prakṛtaṃ mayā 
 mātsaryākrāntacittena mahāmūḍhena durdhiyā  Rm 
 tat sarvaṃ sāṃprataṃ śāstar darśayāmi bhavatpuraḥ 
 tat kṣamasvāparādhaṃ me prasīdatu bhavān guruḥ  Rm 
 iti saṃprārthite tena bhagavān sa kṛpānvitaḥ 
 tat pretaṃ sudṛśālokya samapaśyac ciraṃ mudā  Rm 
 tataś ca bhagavāṃs tasya tadupāyavimuktaye 
 sadgatipreraṇārthena dakṣiṇām evam ādiśat  Rm 
 etaddānād dhi yat puṇyaṃ tat puṇyaṃ tvam avāpnuyāḥ 
 uttiṣṭha kṣipram etasmāt pretalokāt sudāruṇāt  Rm 
 ity ādiṣṭaṃ munīndreṇa śrutvā pretaḥ sa moditaḥ 
 tatheti pratinaṃditvā natvānumodito 'bhavat  Rm 
 tataḥ sa bhagavāṃs tasya pretasya śubhasādhanaṃ 
 saddharmaṃ samupādiśya sasaṃghaḥ svāśraye yathā  Rm 
 tathā sa preta ākarṇya saddharmaṃ taj jinoditaṃ 
 triratnaśaraṇaṃ kṛtvā bheje nityaṃ prabodhitaḥ  Rm 
 tataḥ kāle samāghrātaḥ ca preto jvaradāhitaḥ 
 Rm 
 triratnasmaraṇaṃ kṛtvā mṛto yayau yamālayaṃ  Rm 
 tataḥ pretaḥ sa satpuṇyais triratnasmaraṇodbhavaṃ 
 yamena preritas tasmāt pretamaharddhike yāyau  Rm 
 tatrāpi sa samutpanne vismitas taṃ munīśvaraṃ 
 smṛtvā nityaṃ sadā bheje śraddhayā śaraṇaṃ gataḥ  Rm 
 tataḥ so cintayed evaṃ kutaḥ kutrāham āgataḥ 
 kena puṇyānubhāvena mahatsaukhyaṃ labhe nv iti  Rm 
 iti ciṃtāhate tasya cittapuṇyānubhāvataḥ 
 triratnasmaraṇāt puṇyād iti mene sa puṇyabhāk  Rm 
 tataś cāsau parijñāya triratnabhajanotsukaḥ 
 saṃbuddhadarśanaṃ karttuṃ manasaivaṃ vyaciṃtayat  Rm 
 aho mayā sukhaṃ labdhaṃ tat saṃbuddhaprasādataḥ 
 tad idāniṃ munīṃdraṃ taṃ draṣṭum arhāmi sarvathā  Rm 
 ity evaṃ manasā dhyātvā so 'pi pretamaharddhikaḥ 
 snātva śuddhāmvaro divyaratnālaṃkārabhūṣitaḥ  Rm 
 paṃcagaṃdhaviliptāṃgaṃ pariśuddhāśayaḥ śuciḥ 
 pūjāpaṃcopahārāṇi dhṛtvā jetāśrame 'sarat  Rm 
 tatra jetāśrame bhābhir avabhāsya samaṃtataḥ 
 vihāre śrīghanaṃ draṣṭuṃ muditaḥ samudācarat  Rm 
 tatra taṃ śrīghanaṃ dṛṣṭvānaṃditaḥ sa kṛtāṃjaliḥ 
 natvā pradakṣiṇīkṛtya purataḥ samupācarat  Rm 
 tatas taṃ sugataṃ nāthaṃ samabhyarcya pramoditaḥ 
 natvā sa sāṃjalir dharmaṃ śrotum ekāṃta āśrayat  Rm 
 tataḥ sa bhagavāṃs tasya dṛṣṭvā cittaṃ viśodhitaṃ 
 bodhicaryāṃ samārabhya saddharmam evam ādiśat  Rm 
 śṛṇu sādho 'tra saṃsāre sukhaduḥkhārthakāraṇaṃ 
 vakṣyāmy etat parijñāya samādhāya śubhe cara  Rm 
 yaḥ pumān atra saṃsāre satsaukhyaṃ sarvadechati 
 sa ādau śraddhayā bhaktyā triratnaśaraṇaṃ gataḥ  Rm 
 sarvasatvahitārthena dānaṃ dadyād yathepsitaṃ 
 etatpuṇyavipākaṃ saṃbodhau me pariṇāmayet  Rm 
 itthaṃ kṛtaṃ pradānaṃ yat tad vipāke mahat phalaṃ 
 kramād vṛddhitaraṃ yāyān na kṣiṇuyāt kadā cana  Rm 
 etat puṇyaparītātmā cakravarttī narādhipaḥ 
 śāstā dharmādhipo rājā bodhisatvaḥ sudhīr bhavet  Rm 
 tadāpi sa mahādātā sarvasatvahitechayā 
 triratnabhajaṇaṃ kṛtvā dadyād dānaṃ yathepsitaṃ  Rm 
 etatpuṇyavipākena sa viśuddhāśayaḥ sudhīḥ 
 suśīlasaṃvaraṃ dhṛtvā triratnaṃ sarvadā bhajan  Rm 
 etatpuṇyavipākena sa bhavet tridaśādhipaḥ 
 tatrāpi śraddhayā nityaṃ triratnaṃ sarvadā bhajan  Rm 
 sarvasatvahitārthena śīlapāramitā caran 
 tatpuṇyaṃ bodhisaṃprāptyai manasā pariṇāmayet  Rm 
 etatpuṇyavipākena sa suyāmādhipo bhavet 
 Rm 
 tatrāpi śraddhayā nityaṃ triratnabhajanodyataḥ  Rm 
 sarvasatvahitārthena kṣāṃtipāramitā caran 
 saṃbodhipadalābhāya tatpuṇyaṃ pariṇāmayet  Rm 
 etatpuṇyavipākena sa bhavet tuṣitādhipaḥ 
 tatrāpi śraddhayā nityaṃ triratnaśaraṇaṃ gataḥ  Rm 
 sarvasatvahitārthena vīryyapāramitodyataḥ 
 saṃbodhipadasaṃprāptyai tatpuṇyaṃ pariṇāmayet  Rm 
 etatpuṇyavipākaiḥ sa nirmāṇaratiyo bhavet 
 tatrāpi śraddhayā nityaṃ triratnabhajanodyatat  Rm 
 sarvasatvahitārthena dhyānapāramitārataḥ 
 saṃbodhijñānasaṃprāptyai tatpuṇyaṃ pariṇāmayet  Rm 
 etatpuṇyavipākaiḥ sa vaśavartīśvaro bhavet 
 tatrāpi śraddhayā nityaṃ triratnabhajano rataḥ  Rm 
 sarvasatvahitārthena prajñāpāramitārataḥ 
 tatpuṇyaṃ bodhisaṃprāptyai manasā pariṇāmayet  Rm 
 etatpuṇyavipākena sa brahmādhipatir bhavet 
 tatrāpi śraddhayā nityaṃ triratnārāgaṇodyataḥ  Rm 
 sarvasatvahitārthāya samupāyavidhānadhṛk 
 tatpuṇyaṃ bodhisaṃprāptyai cetasā pariṇāmayet  Rm 
 etatpuṇyavipākena mahābrahmādhipo bhavet 
 tatrāpi śraddhayā nityaṃ triratnārādhanodyataḥ  Rm 
 sarvasatvahitārthāya praṇidhānasamāhitaḥ 
 tatpuṇyaṃ bodhisaṃprāptyai sarvathā pariṇāmayet  Rm 
 etatpuṇyavipākena sa maheśādhipo bhavet 
 tatrāpi śraddhayā nityaṃ triratnabhajanodyataḥ  Rm 
 sarvasatvahitārthena balapāramitodyataḥ 
 tatpuṇyaṃ bodhisaṃprāptyai pradhyānaṃ pariṇāmayet  Rm 
 etatpuṇyavipākena bodhisatvādhipo bhavet 
 tatrāpi śraddhayā nityaṃ triratnasaṃprasāditaḥ  Rm 
 sarvasatvahitārthasya jñānapāramitārataḥ 
 tatpuṇyair bodhisaṃprāpto dharmarājo jino bhavet  Rm 
 tataḥ sa sugataḥ śāstā jagannātho vināyakaḥ 
 sarvajño 'rhan mahābhijñas tathāgato munīśvaraḥ  Rm 
 tato māragaṇāñ jitvā bodhicaryāṃ prakāśayan 
 sarvasatvāñ chubhe sthāpya nirvṛtaḥ saugatiṃ vrajet  Rm 
 evaṃ matvātra saṃsāre ya ichati śivāṃ gatiṃ 
 sa evaṃ śraddhayā nityaṃ triratnabhajanodyataḥ  Rm 
 sarvasatvahitārthena karotu dānam ādarāt 
 tataḥ kramāt sa tatpuṇyaiḥ sarvāḥ pāramitā api  Rm 
 paripūrya mahābhijñā prāpto bodhim avāpnuyāt 
 iti matvā śubhe nityaṃ caritavyaṃ śubhārthibhiḥ  Rm 
 śubhena sadgatiṃ yāyā pāpena durgatīṃ vrajet 
 pāpas tu jāyate lobhāt mātsaryamalināśrayāt  Rm 
 vopakārāṃ sukhecho 'pi na kiṃ cit sukham āpnuyāt 
 sarvadā durmatir duṣṭo durgatinirayāśrayaḥ  Rm 
 Rm 
 saddharmmanindako mūḍho pāpakarmarato bhavet 
 tasmāt mātsaryyam utsṛjya sarvasatvahitārthabhṛt 
 saṃbodhipraṇidhiṃ kṛtvā caren nityaṃ susaṃvare  Rm 
 etatpuṇyavipākena saṃsārasukhabhāk sadā 
 triratnabhajanotsāhī bodhicaryārato bhavet  Rm 
 tataḥ pāramitāḥ sarvāḥ paripūrya yathākramaṃ 
 śivāṃ bodhiṃ samāsādya saṃbuddhapadam āpnuyāt  Rm 
 evaṃ tvaṃ vā parijñāya triratnaśaraṇaṃ gataḥ 
 bodhicittaṃ samādhāya cara nityaṃ susaṃvare  Rm 
 tathā te sarvadā bhadraṃ bhaven nityaṃ samantataḥ 
 kramād bodhiṃ samāsādya saṃbuddhapadam āpnuyāḥ  Rm 
 ity ādiṣṭaṃ munīndreṇa śrutvā sa paribodhitaḥ 
 tatheti hi pratiśrutvā prābhyanaṃdat prasāditaḥ  Rm 
 tataḥ sa taṃ jagannāthaṃ praṇatvā sāṃjalir mudā 
 tridhā pradakṣiṇīkṛtvā praṇatvā svālaye 'carat  Rm 
 tatra prāptaḥ prasannātmā so 'pi pretamaharddhikaḥ 
 triratnaṃ śaraṇaṃ kṛtvā pracaran sarvadā mudā  Rm 
 tad rātrau tatprabhāṃ dṛṣṭvā bhikṣavo vismayānvitāḥ 
 sarve te prātar utthāya natvāpṛchan munīśvaraṃ  Rm 
 bhagavan nātha sarvajña ko 'dya rātrāv ihāgataḥ 
 etad vṛttaṃ samākhyāya sarvān naḥ paribodhaya  Rm 
 iti tair bhikṣubhiḥ pṛṣṭe bhagavān sa munīśvaraḥ 
 tān sarvān sāṃghikān dṛṣṭvā bodhayitum upādiśat  Rm 
 śṛṇuta bhikṣavaḥ sarve yo 'dya rātrāv ihāgataḥ 
 etat sarvaṃ pravṛttāṃtaṃ pravakṣyāmi suvistaraṃ  Rm 
 yo 'sau śreṣṭhī mahāśrāddhaḥ saugate śāsane mudā 
 śraddhayā pravrajitvātra brahmacaryaṃ mudā caran  Rm 
 pravrajitaḥ sa mātsaryaparibhūto durāśayaḥ 
 labdhadravyaṃ na kasmai cid dadau kiñcit kadā cana  Rm 
 kevalaṃ saṃcayaṃ kṛtvā koṣṭhāgāre nidhāya tat 
 guptīkṛtvā prayatnena vyabhajan naiva kiṃ cana  Rm 
 tataḥ kāle samāghrāte dhyātvā tad dravyasaṃcayaṃ 
 mṛtaḥ pretālayotpannaḥ pretodbhavad bhayānakaḥ  Rm 
 tad dravyasaṃcayaṃ smṛtvā mātsaryākulitāśayaḥ 
 punaḥ pratyāgatas tatra svālaye saṃnyaṣīdata  Rm 
 tatra taṃ saṃsthitaṃ pretaṃ dṛṣṭvāhaṃ samupācaran 
 āryadharmam upādiśya prābodhayaṃ prasādayan  Rm 
 tataḥ sa suprasannātmā sasaṃghasya mamāṃtike 
 sa pātracīvaraṃ sarvaṃ taddravyaṃ nirayātayat  Rm 
 etatpuṇyānubhāvena triratnaśaraṇaṃ gataḥ 
 kāle tataḥ paricyutvā pretamaharddhiko 'bhavat  Rm 
 tatra sa suprasannātmā smṛtvā ratnatrayaṃ mudā 
 matsaddharmāmṛtaṃ pātum iha rātrau samāgataḥ  Rm 
 Rm 
 sa saddharmāmṛtaṃ pītvā mamāntike prasāditaḥ 
 saṃbodhisādhanotsāhī muditaḥ svālaye 'carat  Rm 
 yo 'yaṃ śreṣṭhī na cānyo hi rātrāv iha samāgataḥ 
 yat sa mṛto 'bhavat pretas mātsaryaduritāśrayāt  Rm 
 tasmāt mātsaryam uddhṛtya tyajantu śubhavāṃchinaḥ 
 mātsaryaṃ hi trilokeṣu pāpamūlaṃ nigadyate  Rm 
 evaṃ matvātra saṃsāre duḥkhākaraṃ sukhāṃtakaṃ 
 mātsaryaṃ sumaduṣṭaṃ ripuṃ jayata sarvathā  Rm 
 mātsaryaṃ jīyate yair hi samuddhṛtya svamānasāt 
 te eva mānino vīrāḥ śūrāḥ prājñā vicakṣaṇāḥ  Rm 
 ye ca jetuṃ na mātsaryaṃ śaknuvaṃti kathaṃ cana 
 kiṃ te śūrā vijetāro virā na kleśabhojinaḥ  Rm 
 yeṣāṃ na jāyate citte mātsaryan duḥkṛtākaraṃ 
 te eva sukhino virā jayinaḥ kleśaghātakāḥ  Rm 
 yāvan na jīyate citte mātsaryaṃ duritāśayaṃ 
 tāvat kiṃ te suvīrā vā kṣaṇāt kleśānucāriṇaḥ  Rm 
 ye ca kleśavaśā vīrā na te dhīrā vicakṣaṇāḥ 
 kṣaṇāt kiṃ cin nimitteti careyur vikṛtāśayāḥ  Rm 
 tatas te kleśasaṃtaptā mūḍhā rāgāgnidāhitāḥ 
 duṣṭāḥ krodhāgnisaṃdagdhāḥ saṃpaśyeyur na kiṃ cana  Rm 
 tatas te 'ndhā ivāloke careyur na ca satpathe 
 kumārga eva saṃraktāḥ pracareyuḥ pramāditāḥ  Rm 
 tato durjanasaṃraktā māracaryānucāriṇaḥ 
 asanmitropadeśena pracareyur mṛṣādṛśaḥ  Rm 
 tataḥ saddharmanindāṃ kṛtvā dānādi saṃcare 
 vighnaṃ kartuṃ samudyogaṃ kuryur nityaṃ samāhitāḥ  Rm 
 tatas te pāpino duṣṭā unmattā iva tāyinaḥ 
 svayaṃ naṣṭāḥ parāṃś cāpi nāśayeyuḥ pravaṃcakāḥ  Rm 
 tatas te kleśasaṃtaptā mahopāyānurāgiṇaḥ 
 sughorāṇi pāpāni kuryāttiḥ śaṃkitāśayāḥ  Rm 
 tato bhakṣam apīchaṃtaṃ bhuktvāgamye 'pi saṃratāḥ 
 viparītasamācārāḥ pracāreyur virodhitāḥ  Rm 
 tatas te pātakālīḍhā mahāduḥkhābhighātitāḥ 
 tīvrātivedanāghrātā mṛtā yāyur yamālayaṃ  Rm 
 tatra yamo mahārājā dṛṣṭvā taṃ duritāśayaṃ 
 sahasā karmaśāsibhyaḥ samarpya saṃpracodayan  Rm 
 tatra tair yamadūtās tāṃ gṛhītvā sahasā balāt 
 yathā karmānusāreṇa śāsayeyur yathāvidhiṃ  Rm 
 tatra te daivabhogyāṃ bhuktvā bhoktuṃ samaṃtataḥ 
 coditā yamadūtaiś ca bhrameyur narakeṣv api  Rm 
 tatra te daivabhogyāni bhuktvātitīvraduḥkhitāḥ 
 asahyavedanākrāṃtā niṣīdeyuḥ prakheṭitāḥ  Rm 
 evaṃ te daivabhogyāṃ bhuktvā tathā ciraṃ sadā 
 Rm 
 narakān narake gatvā duḥkhāny evāśnuyu vabha  Rm 
 yadā te daivayogānte tīvrātivedanāhatāḥ 
 triratnasaṃsmṛtiṃ kṛtvā praṇameyuḥ samānatāḥ  Rm 
 tadā tān sugatān dṛṣṭvā kṛpayā saṃpracoditāḥ 
 dṛkprabhābhiḥ samuddhṛtya preṣayeyuḥ surālaye  Rm 
 tatra te sukhasaṃpannāḥ smṛtvā ratnatrayaṃ mudā 
 sarvadā śaraṇaṃ kṛtvā pracareyuḥ samāhitāḥ  Rm 
 tathaitatpuṇyapākena saṃbuddhaśāsane gatāḥ 
 śraddhayā satkṛtiṃ kṛtvā śṛṇuyur dharmam ādarāt  Rm 
 tat saddharmāmṛtāsvādaṃ labdhvā te parimoditāḥ 
 bodhicittaṃ samāsādya prakuryu dānam ādarāt  Rm 
 tatas tatpuṇyapākena suśīlāḥ saṃvarodyatāḥ 
 sarvasatvahitaṃ kṛtvā sādhayeyuḥ śubhāṃ cariṃ  Rm 
 tato vīryabalenaiva jitvā kleśagaṇān ripūn 
 tatas te vimalātmāno dhyātvā yogasamāhitāḥ  Rm 
 prajñābdhipāram āsādya jñānaratnam avāpnuyuḥ 
 tato māragaṇāṃ jitvā pariśuddhās trimaṇḍalāḥ  Rm 
 samyakṣaṃbodhim āsādya saṃbuddhapadam āpnuyuḥ  Rm 
 evaṃ matvātra saṃsāre mātsaryaṃ mūlam enasāṃ 
 bodhicittāsinochitvā caritavyaṃ śubhe sadā  Rm 
 tato vo maṃgalaṃ nityaṃ bhaved bhave samaṃtataḥ 
 kramād bodhiṃ samāsādya saṃbuddhapadam āpsyatha  Rm 
 ity ādiṣṭaṃ munīndreṇa śrutvā te sāṃghikā mudā 
 sarve 'pi pratibuddhitvā prābhyanaṃdan prasāditāḥ  Rm 
 iti me guruṇādiṣṭaṃ śrutaṃ mayā tathocyate 
 evaṃ tvaṃ nṛpa mātsaryyaṃ tyaktvā cara śubhe sadā  Rm 
 prajāś cāpi tvayā rājan bodhayitvā prayatnataḥ 
 bodhicaryāśayāḥ kṛtvā pratiṣṭhāpyāḥ śubhe sadā  Rm 
 evaṃ te sarvadā bhadraṃ bhaved bhave samaṃtataḥ 
 kramād bodhiṃ samāsādya saṃbuddhapadam āpnuyāḥ  Rm 
 iti tenārhatādiṣṭaṃ śrutvāśokaḥ sa bhūpatiḥ 
 tatheti prativijñapya prābhyanandat sapārṣadaḥ  Rm 
 pretībhūtāvadānaṃ duritahṛtamataiḥ śreṣṭhino lobhino ye śṛṇvaṃti śravayaṃti pramuditamanasaḥ śraddhayedaṃ manuṣyāḥ 
 mātsaryaṃ te vihāya trimaṇiśaraṇagāḥ sarvasatvānurāgā dānaṃ datvā prasannāḥ satataśubhacarā yānti buddhālayaṃ te  Rm 
  iti śrīratnāvadānatatve pretībhūtāvadānaṃ samāptam 
 Rm 
 XXXII Virūpāvadāna
 athāśoko maharājaḥ kṛtāṃjalipuṭo mudā 
 upaguptaṃ yatiṃ natvā prārthayec caivam ādarāt  Rm 
 bhadanta śrotum ichāmi punar anyat subhāṣitaṃ 
 tad yathā guruṇādiṣṭaṃ tathādeṣṭuṃ ca me 'rhati  Rm 
 iti saṃprārthite rājñā śrutvā so 'rhan sudhīr yatiḥ 
 tam aśokaṃ mahārājaṃ samālokyaivam ādiśat  Rm 
 sādhu śṛṇu mahārāja yathā me guruṇoditaṃ 
 tathāhaṃ te pravakṣyāmi tava dharmapravṛddhaye  Rm 
 tad yathaivaṃ puraikasmin samaye sa munīśvaraḥ 
 bhagavāṃ trijagacchāstā dharmarājas tathāgataḥ  Rm 
 sarvajñaḥ sākyasiṃho 'rhaṃ chrāvstyā bahir āśrame 
 jetodyāne vihāre 'smin vijahāra sasāṃghikaḥ  Rm 
 tadā tatra sabhāmadhye siṃhāsane sumaṃḍite 
 sarvasatvahitārthena dharmam ādeṣṭum āśrayat  Rm 
 tatra te bhikṣavaḥ sarve bhikṣuṇyo 'pi samāgatāḥ 
 yatinaś cailakāś caivam upāsakā upāsikāḥ  Rm 
 vratino bodhisatvāś ca saṃbodhiguṇalālasāḥ 
 nirgranthās tīrthikāś cāpi tāpasāś ca maharṣayaḥ  Rm 
 brahmaśakrādayo devā lokapālā maharddhikāḥ 
 daityā yakṣāś ca gaṃdharvāḥ kinnarāś cāpi rākṣasāḥ  Rm 
 siddhā vidyādharāś cāpi nāgāś ca garuḍā api 
 sādhyā grahāḥ satārāś ca vasavaś cāpsarogaṇāḥ  Rm 
 brāhmaṇāḥ kṣatriyāś cāpi nṛpā rājakumārakāḥ 
 vaiśyāś ca maṃtriṇo 'mātyāḥ śreṣṭhinaś ca mahājanāḥ  Rm 
 gṛhasthā vaṇijaḥ sārthavāhāś ca dhanino 'pi ca 
 śilpinaḥ paurikāś cāpi jānapadāś ca nairgamāḥ  Rm 
 grāmyāḥ kārpaṭikāś cāpi saddharmaśravaṇārthinaḥ 
 sarve te samupāgatya vihāre samupāviśan  Rm 
 tatra taṃ śrīghanaṃ dṛṣṭvā sarve te saṃprasāditāḥ 
 natvā pradakṣiṇīkṛtya purataḥ samupācaran  Rm 
 tatra sarve 'pi te lokāḥ samabhyarcya yathākramaṃ 
 taṃ munīndraṃ praṇatvaiva dharmaṃ śrotum upāśrayan  Rm 
 tataḥ sa bhagavān dṛṣṭvā tān sarvān samupāśritān 
 bodhicaryāṃ samārabhya saddharmaṃ samupādiśat  Rm 
 tat saddharmāmṛtaṃ pītvā sarve te tridaśādayaḥ 
 lokāḥ satyam iti jñātvā prābhyanandan prabodhitāḥ  Rm 
 Rm 
 tasminn avasare tatra śrāvastyāḥ pauriko gṛhī 
 āsīn mahādhanaḥ śrīmāñ chṛdopamo mahājanaḥ  Rm 
 sa svakulasamārāmāṃ svakuladharmacāriṇīṃ 
 kāṃtāṃ bhāryyāṃ samānīya samyakvyūhe yathāvidhiḥ  Rm 
 tataḥ sa kāmasaṃraktaḥ sukāminyā tayā saha 
 yathechayā sukhaṃ bhuktvā reme nityaṃ pracoditaḥ  Rm 
 tatas tasya gṛhasthasya yathākāmaṃ prabhuṃjataḥ 
 samaye sā satī bhārya garbhitābhūt kṛśāṃgikā  Rm 
 tataḥ sā samaye 'sūta dārakaṃ durbhagākṛtiṃ 
 durvarṇaṃ duritākāraṃ virūpaṃ vikṛtāśrayaṃ  Rm 
 dṛṣṭvā taṃ dārakaṃ mātā bhinnāśayā viṣeditāḥ 
 kiṃ īdṛg ātmajenāpi dhig mām iti vyaciṃtayat  Rm 
 tataḥ sa janakaḥ śrutvā taṃ jātaṃ vikṛtāśrayaṃ 
 virūpaṃ durbhagākāram ity evaṃ samaciṃtayat  Rm 
 aho kiṃ prakṛtaṃ pāpaṃ janmāṃtare purā mayā 
 yenāyaṃ durbhagākāro virūpo jāyate sutaḥ  Rm 
 tad atra kiṃ mayopāyaṃ karttavyaṃ nāpi manyate 
 dhig māṃ yena sute jāte lajjayā me sukhaṃ hṛtaṃ  Rm 
 tathāpi kiṃ kariṣyāmi daivāt me jāyate hy ayaṃ 
 tad virūpo 'pi putro 'yaṃ pālanīyo mayātmajaḥ  Rm 
 iti bhartroditaṃ śrutvā sā bhāryyāpy evam abravīt 
 yad ābhyāṃ prakṛtaṃ pāpaṃ tatphalaṃ bhujyate khalu  Rm 
 yad abhāvi na tad bhogyaṃ bhāvi cen na tad anyathā 
 sarvatra bhāvino bhogyaṃ bhuṃjate sarvajaṃtavaḥ  Rm 
 tad atrāham imaṃ bālaṃ pālayeyaṃ prayatnataḥ 
 ity uktvā sā vibhinnāsyā nārī tasthau pralajjitā  Rm 
 taṃ virūpaṃ sutaṃ jātaṃ vīkṣya sa janako 'pi ca 
 lajjāvidīrṇacitto 'bhūn nirutsāhaviṣāditaḥ  Rm 
 hā mayā kiṃ kṛtaṃ pāpaṃ manyate na bhavāṃtare 
 yato 'yaṃ dārako jāto virūpo durbhagākṛtiḥ  Rm 
 tathāpi kiṃ kariṣyāmi daivān no jāyate hy ayaṃ 
 daivabhogyaṃ prabhoktavyaṃ sarvair api hi jaṃtubhiḥ  Rm 
 avaśyaṃ bhāvino bhavanti sarvadehināṃ 
 tad ayaṃ svātmajo bālaḥ pālanīyotmayā mayā  Rm 
 iti dhyātvā pitā so 'thadṛṣṭvā tasya śiśor mukhaṃ 
 lajjayā pratibhinnāsyas tasthau daivānucintayan  Rm 
 tato jñātīn samāhūya kṛtvā jātimahaṃ sa ca 
 pitāsya nāma vikhyāte kuruteti samabravīt  Rm 
 tatas te jñātayaḥ sarve saṃkṛtvā samataṃ tathā 
 tad gṛhasthaṃ samāmaṃtrya pura evam upādiśan  Rm 
 gṛhapate virūpo 'yaṃ putro yat tava jāyate 
 tasmād bhavatun āmnāyaṃ prasiddho bālako bhuvi  Rm 
 Rm 
 tataḥ snehād virūpo 'sau mātrā yatnena pālitaḥ 
 krāmāt puṣṭo vivṛddhābhūd hradastham iva paṃkajaṃ  Rm 
 tadā yadā kumāratvaṃ prāptaḥ sa vikṛtāśrayaṃ 
 svarūpaṃ darppaṇe dṛṣṭvā virūpo lajjito 'bhavat  Rm 
 tato jehrīyamāno 'sau virūpaḥ parimohitaḥ 
 pāpaciṃtāparitātmā manasaivaṃ vyaciṃtayat  Rm 
 hā mayā kiṃ kṛtaṃ pāpaṃ yenāhaṃ duritākṛtiḥ 
 kiṃ mamānena kāyena mṛtyuṃ me 'tra varaṃ dhruvaṃ  Rm 
 kiṃ kariṣye virūpo 'haṃ kva yāsyāmi durākṛtiḥ 
 kiṃ mamānena jīvena kevalaṃ duḥkhabhoginā  Rm 
 tad atrāhaṃ gṛhaṃ tyaktvā vanodyāne samāśrayan 
 saṃbuddhaṃ sugataṃ dhyātvā mṛtyuṃ gaccheya muktaye  Rm 
 avaśyam eva sarveṣāṃ jaṃtūnaṃ maraṇaṃ bhave 
 tan mamedṛg virūpo 'smin śarīre jīvite spṛhā  Rm 
 yady atrāhaṃ ciraṃ jīvī nindito duḥkham āpnuyāṃ 
 tad buddhaṃ sugataṃ dhyātvā tiṣṭheyaṃ prāṇamuktaye  Rm 
 tat saṃbuddhaṃ jinaṃ dhyātvā mṛto 'haṃ yadi sāṃprataṃ 
 tat puṇyaḥ paritātmā sugatiṃ gacheya sarvathā  Rm 
 ye buddhaṃ sugataṃ smṛtvā gachanti mṛtyum ātmanā 
 durgatiṃ te na gachanti samyānty eva sukhāvatīṃ  Rm 
 tasmāt te sudhiyaḥ santaḥ tyaktvā yāyāt kulaṃ gṛhaṃ 
 saṃbuddhasmaraṇaṃ dhyātvā tiṣṭhanti nirjane vane  Rm 
 tathāhaṃ tat samālokya saṃbuddhaṃ śaraṇaṃ gataḥ 
 samādhāya sadā smṛtvā vaseyaṃ vijane vane  Rm 
 ity evaṃ manasā dhyātvā virūpaḥ sa prasannadhīḥ 
 sa saṃpadaṃ gṛhaṃ tyaktvā jīrṇodyānaṃ samāśrayat  Rm 
 tatrodyāne vivikte sa parṇakuṭṭiṃ samāśrayan 
 bhagavantam anusmṛtvā tasthau dhyānasamāhitaḥ  Rm 
 tadā sa bhagavāñ chāstā taṃ tathā sthitaṃ 
 viśuddhāśayam ālokya samuddhartuṃ samudyataḥ  Rm 
 tataḥ sa bhagavān nātho bhikṣusaṃghasamanvitaḥ 
 tatrodyāne virūpaṃ taṃ paśyan bhāsvān upācarat  Rm 
 tatprabhāparispṛṣṭo 'sau virūpaḥ satsukhānvitaḥ 
 vismitas taṃ samāyātaṃ sasāṃghikam apaśyata  Rm 
 taṃ munīṃdraṃ samālokya virūpaḥ sa vimohitaḥ 
 jehrīyamāna utthāya parāyituṃ tato 'carat  Rm 
 tatra sa bhagavān dṛṣṭvā virūpaṃ taṃ parāyitaṃ 
 sahasarddhyā diśo mārge nirudhyābhyatiṣṭhata  Rm 
 tathā nirudhyamānaḥ sa virūpas tena śāsinā 
 parāyituṃ prayatnena na śaśāka kathaṃ cana  Rm 
 sa parikhinnātmā virūpo lajjitāśayaḥ 
 parṇakuṭṭisamāsīnaṃs tasthau bhīto divāndhavat  Rm 
 tatra sa bhagavān dṛṣṭvā nilīnaṃ lajjayāsane 
 Rm 
 saṃnirodhasamāpattiṃ samādhiṃ vidadhe tadā  Rm 
 tataḥ sa bhagavañ chāstā tat samādheḥ samutthitaḥ 
 svayaṃ virūpam ātmānaṃ nirmāya vikṛtāśrayaṃ  Rm 
 bhojanapūrṇam ādāya śarāvaṃ mṛnmayaṃ tataḥ 
 śanais tasya virūpasya parṇakuṭṭyantike 'carat  Rm 
 tatra taṃ samupāyātaṃ virūpaṃ vikṛtāśrayaṃ 
 sa virūpaḥ samālokya harṣita evam abravīt  Rm 
 svāgataṃ bho sahāye hi kutra gantum ihāgataḥ 
 tiṣṭhātrāvāṃ sadāvāse vatsyāvahe sukhānvitā  Rm 
 iti tenoditaṃ śrutvā bhagavān sa virūpadhṛk 
 tvāṃ draṣṭum ihāyāmi proktveti samupāśrayet  Rm 
 tatra sthitaḥ kathāṃ kṛtvā bhagavān sa virūpadhṛk 
 dadau tasmai virūpāya surasāmṛtabhojanaṃ  Rm 
 tat pradattaṃ prabhuktvānnaṃ sa virūpaḥ sa moditaḥ 
 tatkṣaṇāt paripuṣṭāṅgo babhūva prīṇitendriyaḥ  Rm 
 tataḥ sa bhagavāñ chāstā dṛṣṭvā taṃ saṃpramoditaṃ 
 svarūpeṇa sthitas tatra vyarājat saṃprabhāsayan  Rm 
 taṃ saumyabhadrarūpāṅgaṃ śrīghanaṃ śubhiteṃdriyaṃ 
 sa virūpaḥ samālokya vismitaś caivam abravīt  Rm 
 aho kathaṃ bhavaty evam abhirūpataro bhavān 
 kasya puṇyavipākān tad vaktum arhati me puraḥ  Rm 
 iti saṃprārthite tena bhagavān sa munīśvaraḥ 
 bodhayituṃ virūpaṃ taṃ samālokyaivam ādiśat  Rm 
 mahāvidyāsti me sādho saṃbodhisādhanottamā 
 cittaprasādasaṃjātajananyākhyā mahebalaḥ  Rm 
 tasyā eva prabhāvena bhavāmy ahaṃ śubheṃdriyaḥ 
 samaṃtabhadrarūpāṅgaḥ sarvasatvamanoharaḥ  Rm 
 ity ādiśya munīndraḥ sa bhagavāṃs tatra śubhāsane 
 saddharmaṃ samupādestuṃ samāśrayat prabhāsayan  Rm 
 tatas te sāṃghikāḥ sarve saumyarūpāḥ śubheṃdriyāḥ 
 parivṛtya munīndraṃ taṃ puraskṛtyopatasthire  Rm 
 tān sarvān samupāsīnān saumyarūpāñ chubhendriyān 
 dṛṣṭvā taṃ sugataṃ matvā babhūva vismayānvitaḥ  Rm 
 aho bhāgya mayā labdhaṃ mahatpuṇyam ihādhunā 
 yan mamārthe munīndro 'yaṃ sasāṃghika upāgataḥ  Rm 
 nūnam atra munīndro 'yaṃ matkarmaparicoditaḥ 
 saddharmaṃ samupādeṣṭuṃ sasaṃghaḥ kṛpayāgataḥ  Rm 
 tad aham asya munīndrasya śraddhayā śaraṇaṃ gataḥ 
 satkṛtya saugataṃ dharmaṃ śrotum arhe samāhitaḥ  Rm 
 ity evaṃ manasā dhyātvā virūpaḥ sa pramoditaḥ 
 upetya sāṃjalir natvā taṃ munīndram upāśrayat  Rm 
 tadā tasya virūpasya buddhapuṇyānubhāvataḥ 
 lakṣmī prādurabhūt tatra divyabhogapradāyinī  Rm 
 Rm 
 tadā so 'bhūd virūpo 'pi divyābhirūpasundaraḥ 
 pariśuddhatrikāyo 'pi sadguṇārtho śubhāṃśikaḥ  Rm 
 tataḥ so 'tiprasannātmā dṛṣṭvaitat mahad adbhutaṃ 
 mudā tasya muneḥ pādau vavande sa kṛtāṃjaliḥ  Rm 
 tataḥ utthāya taṃ nāthaṃ bhagavaṃtaṃ sasāṃghikaṃ 
 samālokya prasannātmā prārthayat sa samādarāt  Rm 
 bhagavan bhavatā śāstaḥ kṛpādṛṣṭiprasādataḥ 
 prādurbhūtātra me lakṣmī bhavāmi yātisuṃdaraḥ  Rm 
 tad etan mahad āścaryaṃ dṛṣṭvā me rocate manaḥ 
 bhavatāṃ śaraṇe sthitvā carituṃ saṃvaraṃ sadā  Rm 
 tad atra bhagavan nātha kṛpayā buddhaśāsane 
 anvāhṛtya śubhe dharme niyoktuṃ māṃ samarhati  Rm 
 śraddhayāhaṃ jagannātha bhavatāṃ śaraṇaṃ gataḥ 
 pravrajya saṃvaraṃ dhṛtvā cariṣye 'tra samāhitaḥ  Rm 
 iti tat saṃprārthitaṃ śrutvā bhagavān sa munīśvaraḥ 
 tasya śuddhāśayam ālokya samāmaṃtryaivam ādiśat  Rm 
 yadi vāṃchāsti te vatsa carituṃ saugataṃ vrataṃ 
 pitur ājñāṃ samāsādya prāgacha dāsyate tadā  Rm 
 ity ādiṣṭaṃ munīndreṇa śrutvā sa pratiharṣitaḥ 
 mudā tasya muneḥ pādau praṇatvaiva tato 'carat  Rm 
 tatra sa svagṛhe gatvā pādau pituḥ kṛtāṃjaliḥ 
 praṇatvā purataḥ sthitvā prāvadad evam ādarāt  Rm 
 tatodyāne virūpo 'ham iti lajjāviṣāditaḥ 
 parṇakuṭyāṃ samāsīno dhyatvā vasāmi yogavit  Rm 
 tatra sa bhagavān buddhaḥ sasaṃghaḥ svayam āgataḥ 
 bodhayitvāmṛtaṃ bhogyaṃ dadāti samupāyavit  Rm 
 tad dattam amṛtaṃ bhuktvā bhavāmi suṃdarākṛtiḥ 
 lakṣmīś cāpi samudbhūtā mamaivaṃ jāyate śubhaṃ  Rm 
 etat sarvaṃ munīndrasya kṛpādṛṣṭiprasādataḥ 
 nānyathā hīti vijñāya prasīda sugate sadā  Rm 
 evam etat mahaccitraṃ dṛṣṭvā me saṃprasāditaṃ 
 mano 'dya śāsane bauddhe carituṃ rocate vrataṃ  Rm 
 etatsaṃprārthanāṃ kartum ihāhaṃ prāgato mudā 
 tad atra kṛpayā tāta tad anujñāṃ pradehi me  Rm 
 etatpuṇyavibhāgena tvaṃ cāpi sugatīṃ vrajeḥ 
 tatra ca sarvadā saukhyaṃ bhuktvā yāyāj jinālayaṃ  Rm 
 iti matvā prasīdātra mā kuruṣva mano 'nyathā 
 śraddhayānugrahaṃ kṛtvā tad anujñāṃ pradehi me  Rm 
 iti saṃprārthitaṃ śrutvā sa gṛhasthaḥ savismayaḥ 
 pitā taṃ svātmajaṃ dṛṣṭvā sucirād evam abravīt  Rm 
 aho hi bhāgyavān putra puṇyavāñchābhi sāṃprataṃ 
 yato 'sau kṛpayopetya buddhat tvām abhirakṣati  Rm 
 tat te 'sti yadi vāñchati carituṃ saugataṃ vrataṃ 
 taṃ buddhaśaraṇaṃ gatvā vrataṃ cara samāhitaḥ  Rm 
 Rm 
 iti pitroditaṃ śrutvā sa virūpaḥ prasāditaḥ 
 pādau pitroḥ praṇatvaiva sahasā prācarad gṛhāt  Rm 
 tato jetāśrame gatvā sa virūpaḥ pramoditaḥ 
 pādau tasya muner natvā prārthayed evam ādarāt  Rm 
 bhagavan nātha sarvajña labdhānujñaḥ sāmāgatāḥ 
 tad bhavān kṛpayā mahyaṃ saṃvaraṃ dātum arhati  Rm 
 iti saṃprārthite tena bhagavāṃs tasya mastake 
 savyahastena saṃspṛṣṭvā śāsane taṃ samagrahīt  Rm 
 tatra sa vrājitaḥ sāstrā virūpo muṇḍito 'pi saḥ 
 khikkhiripātrabhṛc cīvaraprāvṛto vabhau  Rm 
 tataḥ sa bhikṣur ātmajñaḥ saṃyamī vijiteṃdriyaḥ 
 matvā saṃsārasaṃskāragatīḥ kṣaṇavighātinīḥ  Rm 
 bhitvāvidyāgaṇān bodhipakṣe dharmeṣu prodyataḥ  Rm 
 tataḥ sa dhāraṇīvidyāsamādhinirato yatiḥ 
 sarvakleśagaṇāñ jitvā sākṣād arhatvam āptavān  Rm 
 saṃsāralābhasatkāraniḥspṛho nirmalāśayaḥ 
 pariśuddhatrikāyaś ca nirvikalpo niraṃjanaḥ  Rm 
 sa devāsuralokānām api traidhātucāriṇāṃ 
 mānyaḥ pūjyo 'bhivandyo 'bhūd brahmacarī sa yogavit  Rm 
 tadā te bhikṣavaḥ sarve dṛṣṭvā taṃ yatim uttamaṃ 
 vismitās taṃ muniṃ natvā paprachus tat purākṛtaṃ  Rm 
 bhagavann arhatānena kiṃ karma prakṛtaṃ purā 
 yenāyaṃ duritākāro virūpo jāyate 'dhunā  Rm 
 yac cāyaṃ bhagavāc chāsta bhavatā saṃprasāditaḥ 
 lakṣmīvān abhirūpaś ca bhavati sadguṇārataḥ  Rm 
 yac cāyaṃ śāsane bauddhe śraddhayā śaraṇaṃ gataḥ 
 sahasā kleśasaṃghārīñ jitvārhattvaṃ samāptavān  Rm 
 tad asya sarvavṛttāṃtaṃ yad anena purākṛtaṃ 
 suvistaraṃ samākhyāya sarvān naḥ paribodhaya  Rm 
 iti tair bhikṣubhiḥ sarvaiḥ prārthite sa munīśvaraḥ 
 sarvāṃs tān sāṃghikān bhikṣūn samālokyaivam ādiśat  Rm 
 śṛṇuta bhikṣavaḥ sarve yad anena purākṛtaṃ 
 tat sarvaiḥ karma vakṣyāmi sarvalokaprabodhane  Rm 
 yathābhūt purā buddhaḥ puṣyābhidhas tathāgataḥ 
 sarvajño 'rhañ jagacchāstā dharmarājo munīśvaraḥ  Rm 
 sa bhagavāñ jagannāthaḥ kṛtvā bhadraṃ samaṃtataḥ 
 sarvatra saugataṃ dharmam upadeṣṭum upācarat  Rm 
 evaṃ sarvatra lokeṣu sasāṃghikaḥ sa mārajit 
 pūrvottaradiśo bhāge rājadhānīm upāśrayat  Rm 
 tatra sa bhagavāñ chāstā sarvasatvahitārthabhṛt 
 ādimadhyāntakalyāṇam āryadharmam upādiśat  Rm 
 tat saddharmāmṛtaṃ pītvā sarve lokaḥ prabodhitaḥ 
 triratnabhajanaṃ kṛtvā pracerire śubhe sadā  Rm 
 Rm 
 tatra sa bhagavān puṣyo buddhadṛṣṭya samaṃtataḥ 
 loke paśyan hitaṃ kartuṃ dadarśa dvau jinātmajau  Rm 
 ekaḥ śākyamunir nāma maitreyaś cāparaḥ sudhīḥ 
 tasmin kāle ubhav etau bodhisatvau jinātmajau  Rm 
 maitreyasya subuddheḥ svasaṃtatiḥ paripākitā 
 tasya śāstuś ca vaineyāḥ satvā na paripācitāḥ  Rm 
 śākyamunes tu vaineyāḥ paripakvā na saṃtatiḥ 
 evaṃ sa sugataḥ puṣyo dṛṣṭvaivaṃ samaciṃtayat  Rm 
 aho śākyamuner na svasantatiḥ paripācitā 
 tatsvasantatipākārthaṃ careyāhaṃ tadantike  Rm 
 iti vicintya puṣyaḥ sa tathāgataḥ sasāṃghikaḥ 
 himavaṃtaṃ giriṃ gatvā pracakrāma prabhāsayan  Rm 
 tatra ratnaguhāyāṃ sa praviśya sa munīśvaraḥ 
 tejodhātusamāpanno dhyātvā tasthau śubhāsane  Rm 
 tasmiṃś ca samaye tatra śākyamuniḥ sa sanmatiḥ 
 phalamūlasamāhartuṃ tadantikam upācarat  Rm 
 tatra ratnaguhāyāṃ taṃ puṣyaṃ tathāgataṃ muniṃ 
 suparyaṅkasamāsīnaṃ dhyānalīnaṃ prabhāsitaṃ  Rm 
 dvātriṃśallakṣaṇāśītivyaṃjanaiḥ paribhūṣitaṃ 
 ratnāvalim ivojvālaṃ śatasūryyādhikaprabhaṃ  Rm 
 saumyaṃ divyātiriktābhaṃ samaṃtabhadrarūpiṇaṃ 
 suprasannamukhāmbhojaṃ dharmarājaṃ samaikṣata  Rm 
 tatra taṃ sugataṃ dṛṣṭvā śākyamuniḥ sa moditaḥ 
 sahasā sāṃjalir natvā pūjāṃgainārcayan mudā  Rm 
 tataḥ sa ekapādena sthitvā saptaniśāṃ mudā 
 sāṃjaliḥ praṇatiṃ kṛtvā tuṣṭāva gāthayānayā  Rm 
 na divi bhuvi vā nāsmil loke na vaiśravaṇālaye 
 na marubhavane divye sthāne na dikṣu vidikṣu vā  Rm 
 caratu vasudhāṃ sphītāṃ kṛtsnāṃ saparvatakānanāṃ 
 puruṣavṛṣabhasya tulyānyo mahāśramaṇaḥ kutaḥ  Rm 
 etayo gāthayā stutvā taṃ puṣyaṃ sugataṃ muniṃ 
 sa śākyamunir utsāhāt saptarātriṃ mudā bhajan  Rm 
 tataḥ saptadinānte sa puṣyathāgato mudā 
 paristutas tam ālokya śākyamunim abhāṣata  Rm 
 sādhu sādhu mahāsatva tvam evaṃ yat samudyataḥ 
 anena balavīryeṇa saṃpannena dvijottama  Rm 
 navakalpāḥ parāvṛttāḥ saṃstutyādya tathāgataṃ 
 kramāt pāramitāḥ pūrya saṃbodhiṃ samavāpnuyāḥ  Rm 
 ity ādiśya munīndro 'sau puṣyo dharmādhipo jinaḥ 
 parivṛtto maheśākhyais tatra dhyānārato 'bhasat  Rm 
 so 'pi śākyamunir bodhisatvo dvijottamaḥ sudhīḥ 
 tasya puṣyasya sadbhaktya śaraṇasthaḥ sadābhajat  Rm 
 tatra tasmin sthite buddhe devī guhānivāsinī 
 Rm 
 tadguhāyāṃ praveṣṭum 'sau na śaśāka kathaṃ cana  Rm 
 tataḥ sātivirūpākṣā vikṛtāṃśā durākṛtiḥ 
 bhūtvā taṃ sugataṃ puṣyaṃ dhyānālīnam abhīṣapat  Rm 
 tathā sā sucireṇāpi bhīṣapītvāpi durmatiḥ 
 kiñcit tasya muneś cittaṃ cārayituṃ śaśāka na  Rm 
 tadā sā śaṃkitākhinnā vismayāhatamānasā 
 svarūpeṇaiva taṃ draṣṭuṃ praṇatā samupācarat  Rm 
 tatra taṃ sugataṃ puṣyaṃ tathāgatam munīśvaraṃ 
 dvātriṃśallakṣaṇāśītivyaṃjanaiḥ parimaṇḍitaṃ  Rm 
 sarvātikrāṃtasaumyābhaṃ śatasūryādhikaprabhaṃ 
 śāntarūpaṃ subhadrāṃgaṃ dhyānālīnam apaśyata  Rm

 iti dhyātvā surūpeṇa tadantikam upācarat  Rm 
 tatra sā sāṃjalir natvā pādau tasya muneḥ puraḥ 
 sthitvā kṣamārthanāṃ karttuṃ prārthayad evam ānatā  Rm 
 bhagavan nātha sarvajña yan mayā prakṛtaṃ tvayi 
 tat kṣamasva jagannātha kṣāntidharmādhipo 'si hi  Rm 
 tad atrāhaṃ jagacchāstar bhavatāṃ śaraṇaṃ gatā 
 sarvadā samupāśritya bhajeyaṃ śraddhayā mudā  Rm 
 yad atra te sasaṃghasya yathāvidhi samarcituṃ 
 ichāmy ahaṃ jagannātha tad adhyuṣitum arhati  Rm 
 iti tenārthite puṣyo bhagavān sa munīśvaraḥ 
 tāṃ viśuddhāśayāṃ dṛṣṭvā tūṣṇībhūtvādhyuvāsa tat  Rm 
 tathādhivāsitaṃ śāstrā matvā sābhyanumoditā 
 āśu tadbhojyasāmagrīṃ sahasā samasādhayat  Rm 
 tataḥ sā muditopetya pūjāṃgais taṃ munīśvaraṃ 
 abhyarcya bhojanair divyaiḥ sasaṃghaṃ samatoṣayat  Rm 
 tataḥ sā bhojanānte 'pi praṇatvā sāñjalir mudā 
 bhūtvā kṣamāpayitvā ca prārthayad evam ānatā  Rm 
 bhagavan nātha sarvajña bhavatāṃ śaraṇe sthitā 
 sadopasthānam ādhāya bhajiṣyāmi samāhitā  Rm 
 tat kṣamasva jagannātha yan mayāpakṛtaṃ vṛthā 
 prasīdatu bhavāñ chāstā saṃbuddho hi kṣamākaraḥ  Rm 
 iti tayārthitaṃ śrutvā puṣyaḥ sa bhagavān muniḥ 
 devatāṃ tāṃ samālokya saddharmaṃ samupādiśat  Rm 
 śṛṇuṣva devate dharmam ihāmutra śubhāptaye 
 dharmeṇa rakṣitā loke sarvatrāpi sukhī bhavet  Rm 
 tad ādau śraddhayā dharmaṃ śrotavyaṃ saugataṃ varaṃ 
 tatas triratnam abhyarcya dātavyaṃ dānam arthine  Rm 
 tataḥ śuddhatrikāyaḥ syāc chuddhaśīlaḥ śubhāśayaḥ 
 tataḥ satyasamādhānaḥ sarvasatvakṣamākaraḥ  Rm 
 saṃbodhisādhanodyogāt sarvakleśān vinirjayet 
 tato dhyānasamādhisthaḥ prajñāratnam avāpnuyāt  Rm 
 Rm 
 tat suratnānubhāvena sarvamārān vinirjayan 
 sarvasatvahitārthena saṃbuddhapadam āpnuyāt  Rm 
 evaṃ matvātra saṃsāre sarvadā śubhavāñchibhiḥ 
 dharmaṃ śrutvā sadā dānaṃ prakarttavyaṃ yathepsitaṃ  Rm 
 tvaṃ cāpy evaṃ sadā saukhyaṃ yadīchasi śubhānvitaṃ 
 triratnaṃ bhajanaṃ kṛtvā kuru dānaṃ yathepsitaṃ  Rm 
 etat puṇyaṃ tu saṃbodhiprāptaye pariṇāmaya 
 etatpuṇyavipākena nūnaṃ bodhiṃ samāpnuyāḥ  Rm 
 ity ādiṣṭaṃ munīndreṇa śrutvā sā devatā mudā 
 tathā hītipratijñāya prābhyanandat prabodhitā  Rm 
 tataḥ sa sugataḥ puṣyas tathāgataḥ sasāṃghikaḥ 
 prabhāsayan samutthāya svāśrame samupāśrayat  Rm 
 eṣa hy ayaṃ virūpo 'sau devatā yā guhāśritā 
 yuṣmābhiḥ satyam eveti manyatāṃ nānyathā khalu  Rm 
 evaṃ matvātra saṃsāre sarvadā sukhavāñchibhiḥ 
 triratnabhajanaṃ kṛtvā caritavyaṃ śubhe sadā  Rm 
 śubhasya karmaṇaḥ pāke śubhataivaṃ sadā bhave 
 kṛṣṇasya duḥkhataivaṃ hi miśritasyāpi miśritaṃ  Rm 
 abhuktaṃ kṣīyate naiva karma kvāpi kadā cana 
 yenaiva yat kṛtaṃ karma tenaiva bhujyate phalaṃ  Rm 
 nāgnibhir dahyate karma klidyate nāpi codakaiḥ 
 śuṣyate vāyubhir naiva kṣīyate ca na bhūmiṣu  Rm 
 nānyathāpi bhave naiva karma kvāpi kathaṃ cana 
 yad yathā prakṛtaṃ karmaṃ tat tathaiva kuled dhruvaṃ  Rm 
 yad asau devatā tatra guhāśritā durāśayā 
 vikṛtāṅgā virūpākṣā bhūtvā puṣyaṃ vyabhīṣapat  Rm 
 etatpāpavipākena paṃcajanmaśatāny api 
 vikṛtāṅgo virūpākṣo babhūvāyaṃ bhave sadā  Rm 
 etatpāpāvimukto 'yaṃ virūpo vikṛtākṛtiḥ 
 vibhransyo durbhagākāro bhavaty atrāpi sāṃprataṃ  Rm 
 yac cāsau devatā paścāttāpasaṃtapitāśayā 
 tasya puṣyasya buddhasya prasannā śaraṇaṃ gatā  Rm 
 śraddhayā bhojanair divyaiḥ satkṛtya prābhajan mudā 
 etatpuṇyavipākena lebhe 'nantaṃ sukhaṃ bhave  Rm 
 atrāpi śāsane bauddhe śraddhayā samupāgataḥ 
 pravrajyāsaṃvaraprāptaḥ sākṣād arhatvam āptavān  Rm 
 iti yūyaṃ parijñāya caradhvaṃ sarvadā śubhe 
 tato bodhiṃ samāsādya saṃbuddhapadam āpnuyuḥ  Rm 
 ity ādiṣṭaṃ munīndreṇa sarve te sāṃghikā api 
 śrutvānumoditāḥ satyam ity uktvā parimenire  Rm 
 iti me guruṇādiṣṭaṃ mayātra kathyate 
 tvayāpy evaṃ mahārāja caritavyaṃ śubhe sadā  Rm 
 prajāś cāpi tathā rājan bodhayitvā prayatnataḥ 
 bodhimārge pratiṣṭhāpya pālanīyaḥ sadādarāt  Rm 
 tena te sarvadā nityaṃ sarvatrāpi śubhaṃ bhavet 
 Rm 
 kramād bodhiṃ samāsādya saṃbuddhapadam āpnuyāḥ  Rm 
 iti tenārhatādiṣṭaṃ śrutvāśokaḥ sa bhūpatiḥ 
 tathā hīti pratijñāya prābhyanandat prabodhitaḥ  Rm 
 śāstrādiṣṭaṃ prasannā idam api manuja ye virūpāvadānaṃ śṛṇvanti śrāvayanti pramuditamanaso ye ca puṇyābhirāgāḥ 
 sarve te śrīsametāḥ sakalaguṇadharāḥ satsukhāni prabhuktvā saṃbuddhabhaktiraktāḥ sugatavaragṛhe saṃprayānti pramodaṃ  Rm 
  iti ratnāvadānatatve virūpāvadānaṃ samāptam 
 Rm 
 XXXIṃ Kṣemāvadāna
 athāśoko mahārājaḥ kṛtāṃjaliḥ puraḥ sthitaḥ 
 upaguptaṃ yatiṃ natvā punar evam abhāṣata  Rm 
 bhadanta śrotum ichāmi punar anyat subhāṣitaṃ 
 tadyathā guruṇākhyātaṃ tathādeṣṭuṃ samarhasi  Rm 
 iti saṃprārthite rājñā śrutvā so 'rhan sudhīr yatiḥ 
 aśokaṃ taṃ mahīpālaṃ samālokyaivam abravīt  Rm 
 śṛṇu rājan mahābhāga yathā me guruṇoditaṃ 
 tathāhaṃ tat pravakṣyāmi tava dharmavivṛddhaye  Rm 
 tadyathābhūt purā pūryyāṃ śrāvastyāṃ kauśalādhipaḥ 
 prasenajid iti khyāto mahārājā mahīpatiḥ  Rm 
 vārāṇasyāṃ tadācāro brahmadattābhidho nṛpaḥ 
 mahārājo mahīpālanṛpādhipas tadābhavat  Rm 
 tadā tayor mahībhoktroḥ parasparaviruddhayoḥ 
 mahāhavasamāraṃbhād babhūva kṣubhitāśayaṃ  Rm 
 tatra sa kṣatriyo rājā prasenajin narādhipaḥ 
 svastyayanavidhiṃ kṛtvā sarvāntaḥpurikānvitaḥ  Rm 
 caturaṃgavalaiḥ sārddhaṃ mahotsāhaṃ praṇādayan 
 vaijayantīṃ samucchrāya kośalāviṣayāntataḥ  Rm 
 paryante sahasā gatvā vīryotsāhasamanvitaḥ 
 vadhvā kāṣṭapaṭaṃ tatra prāvatasthe pure yathā  Rm 
 tac chrutvā brahmadatto 'pi kṣatriyo bhūpatir nṛpaḥ 
 svastyayanavidhiṃ dhṛtvā svāntaḥpurasamanvitaḥ  Rm 
 caturaṃgavalaiḥ sārddhaṃ jayotsāhaṃ ninādayan 
 vaijayantīṃ samucchrāya nadyā tīram upācarat  Rm 
 tatraiva samupāśritya vīryotsāhasamanvitaḥ 
 vadhvā kāṣṭapaṭaṃ tatra saṃtasthe nagare yathā  Rm 
 tatra sa bhūpatī rājā brahmadatto narādhipaḥ 
 agrarājñyā sahāraktaḥ saṃreme paricārayan  Rm 
 tadā sa mahiṣī rājñā saha krīḍāratā satī 
 svalpāhāraratā gaurā dohadalakṣaṇaṃ dadhau  Rm 
 tathā tasmin kṣaṇe so 'pi prasenajin narādhipaḥ 
 mahiṣyā saha saṃraktaḥ prareme paricārayan  Rm 
 tadā sāpi mahārājñī svāmikrīḍānucāriṇī 
 svalpāhārotsahā gaurā dadhau dohadalakṣaṇaṃ  Rm 
 kramāt to 'pi mahārājñyāṃ pravṛddhagarbhahārite 
 pīnastane haridrābhavarṇe 'bhūtāṃ kṛśāṅgike  Rm 
 Rm 
 tato 'gramahiṣī rājño brahmadattasya bhūpateḥ 
 sā sūta samaye putraṃ divyāṃśam atisuṃdaraṃ  Rm 
 tac chrutvā sa bhūpālo brahmadattaḥ pramoditaḥ 
 sahasopetya taṃ putraṃ dṛṣṭvā na tṛptim āyayau  Rm 
 tasminn eva dine tasya prasenajin mahīpateḥ 
 bhāryāpi samaye sūta sutāṃ divyātisuṃdarīṃ  Rm 
 strīratnalakṣaṇopetaṃ subhadrāṃgīmanoharāṃ 
 ramopamaṃ śubhākārāṃ manāpāṃ ratisaṃnibhāṃ  Rm 
 tac chrutvā sa mahīpālaḥ prasenajit prasāditaḥ 
 sahasopetya tāṃ putrīṃ dadarsātipramoditaḥ  Rm 
 tāṃ dṛṣṭvā sa nareṃdro 'pi me vabhūva samāgataḥ 
 tām eva suciraṃ paśyann avatasthe suniścalaḥ  Rm 
 tayor apy ubhayo rājñoḥ skaṃdhācārāḥ pravarttitāḥ 
 ye nityaṃ tatpravṛttāṃtaṃ svaprabhor upahārakāḥ  Rm 
 ye prasenajitaś cārā brahmadattasya bhūpateḥ 
 putro jāta iti śrutvā parijñāya prasedire  Rm 
 te prasenajito rājñaḥ sahasā samupāgatāḥ 
 kṛtāṃjalipuṭo natvā pura evaṃ nyavedayan  Rm 
 jaya deva mahārāja śṛṇu tatra pravarttitaṃ 
 brahmadattasya bhūpasya putro jāto 'dhunā khalu  Rm 
 sāṃprataṃ tatra rājendraśubhotsāhaṃ pravarttate 
 tat tvayā saha saṃvaṃdhaṃ kṛtvā sa svapuraṃ vrajet  Rm 
 tat prasīda mahārāja mā vibhaiṣīḥ śubhaṃ bhavet 
 tena saṃdhiṃ bhavān kṛtvā viharatāṃ yathāsukhaṃ  Rm 
 iti taiḥ kathitaṃ śrutvā sa prasenajin narādhipaḥ 
 satyam etad iti jñātvā prasasāda 'viśaṃkitaḥ  Rm 
 tathā ye brahmadattasya gūḍhacārāḥ pravarttitāḥ 
 te prasenajitaḥ putrī jāteti śuśruvus tadā  Rm 
 tatas te sahasā tatra brahmadattasya bhūpateḥ 
 purataḥ samupāśritya praṇatvaivaṃ nyavedayan  Rm 
 jaya deva mahārāja śṛṇu tatra pravarttitaṃ 
 prasenajinmahīpasya putrī jātā 'dhunā khalu  Rm 
 dārikā sā subhadrāṃgī divyakāmā ramopamā 
 sarvalakṣaṇasaṃpannā suṃdarī ratisaṃnibhā  Rm 
 tena tatra śubhotsāhaṃ pravarttate 'dhunā prabho 
 tena sahātra saṃvaṃdhaṃ karttum arhati sarvathā  Rm 
 iti taiḥ kathitaṃ śrutvā brahmadatto narādhipaḥ 
 bhadram iti parijñāya tatraivaṃ samaciṃtayat  Rm 
 aho citra mahotsāho bhadram ekasmin divase yataḥ 
 jāto me 'tra suto bhadras tasyāpi jāyate sutā  Rm 
 tat tāṃ bhadrāṃ ramākārāṃ taṃ prasenajitam ādarat 
 prārthayitvātra putrāya sandhiṃ kṛtvā carevahi  Rm 
 iti niścitya sa brahmadatto rājā prasāditaḥ 
 Rm 
 sujanaṃ dūtam āmaṃtrya pura evaṃ samabravīt  Rm 
 gacha dūta mahīpālaṃ taṃ prasenajitam ādarāt 
 mamaivaṃ vacasopetya prārthayasva prabodhayan  Rm 
 brahmadatto mahīpālo vadaty evaṃ samādarāt 
 bhavatā saha saṃvaṃdhaṃ karttum ichāmi sāṃprataṃ  Rm 
 yad ekasmin dine jātau dārakāv āvayor api 
 sutā te bhadrikā khyātā mama putro 'pi bhadrikaḥ  Rm 
 tad etayor hi saṃvaṃdhaṃ karttum arhāvahe dhruvaṃ 
 tad bhavān mama putrāya svātmajāṃ dātum arhati  Rm 
 evaṃ kṛte 'pi saṃvaṃdhe yāvajjīvaṃ sadāvayoḥ 
 vairotsargo bhaven nūnaṃ prītisaṃdhir na bhetsyati  Rm 
 tadāvayoḥ sadā bhadraṃ viṣayeṣu samaṃtataḥ 
 nirītikaṃ śubhotsāhaṃ bhaviṣyati na saṃśayaḥ  Rm 
 iti me vacasā rājā prasenajit sa kauśalaḥ 
 prārthanīyas tvayā sādho gachāstu te sumaṃgalaṃ  Rm 
 ity ādiṣṭaṃ narendreṇa śrutvā dūtaḥ sa bodhitaḥ 
 tathety uktvā nṛpaṃ natvā samutthāya tato 'carat  Rm 
 tatra sa sahasā gatvā taṃ prasenajitaṃ nṛpaṃ 
 upetya sāṃjalir natvā purastha evam abravīt  Rm 
 jaya deva mahārāja yadarthe 'ham ihāgataḥ 
 tadarthaṃ saṃpravakṣyāmi bhavāṃ śrotuṃ samarhati  Rm 
 brahmadatto mahārājo bhavatāṃ kuśalaṃ mudā 
 pṛchati sarvadā nityaṃ sarvatra viṣayeṣv api  Rm 
 punar evaṃ sa bhūpālo brahmadatto bravīty api 
 bhavatā saha saṃvaṃdhaṃ kartum ichāmi sāṃprataṃ  Rm 
 yad ekasmin dine jātau dārakāv āvayor iha 
 sutā te bhadrikā khyāto mama putro 'pi bhadrikaḥ  Rm 
 tad etayor hi saṃvaṃdhaṃ kartum arhāmahe dhruvaṃ 
 tad bhavān mama putrāya svātmajāṃ dātum arhati  Rm 
 evaṃ kṛte 'pi saṃvaṃdhe yāvajjīvaṃ sadāvayoḥ 
 vairotsargo bhaven nūnaṃ prītisaṃdhir na bhetsyate  Rm 
 tadāvayoḥ sadā bhadraṃ viṣayeṣu samaṃtataḥ 
 nirītikaṃ śubhotsāhaṃ bhaved eva na saṃśayaḥ  Rm 
 iti me vacasā rājā prasenajit sa kauśalaḥ 
 prārthanīyas tvayā sādho gachāstu tvaṃ samāhitaḥ  Rm 
 ity ādiśya narendreṇa brahmadattena bhūrbhujā 
 preṣito 'haṃ mahārāja bhavatām aṃtike khalu  Rm 
 tat tena bhūpatīśena yathādiṣṭaṃ narādhipa 
 bhavān api tathā kartum arhaty edan na nānyathā  Rm 
 evaṃ hi bhavatāṃ bhadraṃ yāvājjīvaṃ sukhaiḥ sadā 
 sarvatra maṅgalotsāhaṃ bhaven nūnaṃ na saṃśayaḥ  Rm 
 tad bhavān api rājendra brahmadattasya bhūpateḥ 
 putrāya svātmajāṃ bhadrāṃ saṃpradātum ihārhati  Rm 
 Rm 
 iti tena samākhyātaṃ śrutvā sa kośalādhipaḥ 
 tuṣṇībhūtvā kṣaṇaṃ tatra manasaivaṃ vyaciṃtayet  Rm 
 aho me jāyate kṣemaṃ yad asau kṣatriyādhipaḥ 
 vairaṃ vihāya saṃvandhaṃ karttum ichati sāṃprataṃ  Rm 
 tad ahaṃ tena bhūpena yathādiṣṭaṃ tathā 'dhunā 
 datvaināṃ svātmajāṃ bhadrāṃ saṃdhiṃ kuryāṃ śubhāptaye  Rm 
 evaṃ kṛte sadā kṣemaṃ sarvatra viṣayeṣv api 
 mama tasyāpi bhūpasya bhaven nūnaṃ na cānyathā  Rm 
 iti dhyātvā viniścitya prasenajit sa kauśalaḥ 
 taṃ dūtaṃ samupāmaṃtrya samālokyaivam abravīt  Rm 
 sādho tena narendreṇa yathādiṣṭaṃ tathādarāt 
 ājñāṃ śirasā dhṛtivā kariṣyāmi sadāpy ahaṃ  Rm 
 evaṃ me vacasā sādho sarvam etat suvistaraṃ 
 samākhyāya narendraṃ taṃ prasādayitum arhasi  Rm 
 iti tena narendreṇa samākhyātaṃ niśamya saḥ 
 dūtas tatheti vijñapya prābhyanandat prasāditaḥ  Rm 
 tataḥ sa dūtas taṃ bhūpaṃ kośalādhipatiṃ mudā 
 natvā dṛṣṭvā samāmaṃtrya tato 'carat pramoditaḥ  Rm 
 tataḥ sa sahasā gatvā brahmadattasya bhūpateḥ 
 upetya sāṃjaliḥ pādau praṇatvevam abhāṣata  Rm 
 jaya deva mahārāja diṣṭyā varddhasva sāṃprataṃ 
 yathābhilaṣitaṃ sarvaṃ tat siddham iti manyatāṃ  Rm 
 tad yathā bhavatādiṣṭaṃ tathā vijñāpitaṃ mayā 
 tac chrutvānena bhūpena pramoditvādhyuvāsitaṃ  Rm 
 iti satyaṃ samādhāya pālayasva yathoditaṃ 
 sarvadā te bhaved bhadraṃ sarvatra viṣayeṣv api  Rm 
 iti tenoditaṃ śrutvā brahmadattaḥ sa bhūpatiḥ 
 prabodhito 'numoditvā prābhyanaṃdat prasāditaḥ  Rm 
 tataḥ sa bhūpatī rājā brahmadatto mahotsavaiḥ 
 caturaṃgavalaiḥ sārddhaṃ jayavādyaṃ pravādayan  Rm 
 tataḥ saṃprasthito lokaiḥ stūyamānaḥ surair api 
 pracaran sahasā tatra svapuraṃ samupāyayau  Rm 
 tataḥ so 'pi mahīpālaḥ prasenajit pramoditaḥ 
 caturaṃgavalaiḥ sārddhaṃ jayotsāhaṃ praṇādayan  Rm 
 tataḥ pratyāgato lokai stūyamāno 'marair api 
 pracaran sa nṛpo tatra śrāvastyāṃ samupācarat  Rm 
 tatra svanagare prāptaḥ prasenajit sa kauśalaḥ 
 svaprāsādatalāsīnaḥ sarvāntapurikānvitaḥ  Rm 
 tāṃ bhadarikāṃ sutāṃ dṛṣṭvā suprasannāśayo mudā 
 aho kṣemaṃ prajātaṃ me ity evaṃ muhur abravīt  Rm 
 tatas tasyāḥ sutāyāḥ sa kṛtvā jātimahaṃ mudā 
 sarvañ jñātīn samāhūya pura evam upādiśat  Rm 
 Rm 
 bhadantaḥ śrūyatām asyā bhadrāyā duhitur mama 
 yathāyuktaṃ nāmadheyaṃ sthāpayata prasiddhitaṃ  Rm 
 iti tena narendreṇa samādiṣṭaṃ niśamyate 
 saṃpaśyañ jñātayas tatra saṃmīlyaivaṃ samabruvan  Rm 
 yasmin dine prajāteyaṃ tasminn eva dine yataḥ 
 kṣemaṃ no jāyate tasmāt kṣemābhidhā bhavantv iyaṃ  Rm 
 iti te jñātayaḥ sarve kṛtvaivaṃ saṃmataṃ tataḥ 
 kauśalendraṃ tam āmaṃtrya praṇatvaivaṃ samabruvan  Rm 
 śṛṇu rājan yad asmākam abhiprāyaṃ pracakṣyate 
 tad asyā nāmadheyaṃ karotu bhuvi viśrutaṃ  Rm 
 yasmin dine prajāteyaṃ kṣemaṃ bhavati sarvataḥ 
 tenāsyā kriyatāṃ nāma kṣemeti viśrutaṃ bhuvi  Rm 
 tathā tair gaditaṃ śrutvā rājā sa janako mudā 
 tasyāḥ putryās tathā nāma kṣemeti prārthitaṃ vyadhāt  Rm 
 tataḥ sā dārikāṣṭābhir dhātribhiḥ pratipālitā 
 paripuṣṭā pravṛddhābhūd dhradastham iva paṃkajaṃ  Rm 
 tathā sa brahmadatto 'pi rājā svāntargṛhe gataḥ 
 taṃ putrāṃ muhur ālokya prābhyanaṃdat pramoditaḥ  Rm 
 tatra tasya śiśo rājā kṛtvā jātimahaṃ pitā 
 sarvāñ jñātīn samāhūya pura evam abhāṣata  Rm 
 bhavaṃto dārakasyāsya putrasya me śubhākṛteḥ 
 kriyatāṃ nāmadheyan sanmaṃgalākṣarasaṃyutaṃ  Rm 
 ity ādiṣṭaṃ narendreṇa śrutvā te jñātayo mudā 
 sarve 'py ekatra saṃgamya mithar evaṃ samabruvan  Rm 
 yad ayaṃ jātamātro 'pi kṣemaṃ karoti sarvataḥ 
 tathāsya bhavatu kṣemaṃkara ity āhvayaṃ dhruvaṃ  Rm 
 iti te jñātayaḥ sarve brahmadattasya bhūpateḥ 
 purataḥ samupāsṛtya praṇatvaivaṃ nyavedayan  Rm 
 śṛṇu rājan yad asmābhir nāmāsya kriyate śiśoḥ 
 tan nāma kṣemasaṃpannaṃ prathayatu bhāvān bhuvi  Rm 
 yad ayaṃ jātamātro 'pi kṣemaṃ karoti sarvataḥ 
 tena kṣemaṃkarākhyo 'yaṃ bhavaṃtu lokanaṃdanaḥ  Rm 
 etat taiḥ kathitam śrutvā brahmadattaḥ sa bhūpatiḥ 
 tad eva nāme putrasya tasyākarot pravisṛtaṃ  Rm 
 tataḥ sa dārako 'ṣṭābhi dhātribhiḥ pratipālitaḥ 
 paripuṣṭaḥ pravṛddho 'bhūd dhradasthaṃ kamalaṃ yathā  Rm 
 tataḥ kramāt kumāratvam āptavān sa nṛpātmajaḥ 
 gurūṇāṃ samupāśritya lipī kramād aśikṣat  Rm 
 yathākramam adhītyevaṃ kṣemaṃkaraḥ sa buddhimān 
 sarvaśāstrakalāsv ādi vidyāparaṃ yayau laghu  Rm 
 tataḥ sa daharaḥ kāntaḥ kumāro ratilālitaḥ 
 Rm 
 savayeḥsacivaiḥ sārddhaṃ reme pure paribhraman  Rm 
 tadā sa dārikā kṣemā prasenajitsutāpi ca 
 kramād abhūt kumārītvaprāptā kāntābhisuṃdarī  Rm 
 tataḥ sā bhadrikā kanyā sumatir guṇalālasāḥ 
 gurūṇāṃ samupāśritya kramāl lipir aśikṣata  Rm 
 yathākramam adhītyaivaṃ sā subuddhimatī satī 
 sarvaśāstrakalāvidyāpāraṃ yayau vicakṣaṇā  Rm 
 tadā sā bhāvinī kṣemā svasakhībhiḥ samanvitā 
 saṃbuddhabhāṣitaṃ dharmam anuśrutvā mudānamat  Rm 
 tadā sa brahmadattasya kumāro 'tivicakṣaṇaḥ 
 tāṃ kṣemāṃ suṃdarīṃ draṣṭuṃ samaichad ratilālasaḥ  Rm 
 tataḥ sa dūtam āhūya bodhayitvā prasādayan 
 datvā suratnamālāṃ taṃ kṣemāyāḥ preṣayet svayaṃ  Rm 
 tataḥ sa dūta ādāya tāṃ mālāṃ sahasā caran 
 śrāvastyāḥ puri saṃprāptaḥ kṣemāyāḥ sadane 'carat  Rm 
 tatra sa dūta ālokya sakhīm ekām upāgatāṃ 
 tām upetya samāmaṃtrya suguptam evam abravīt  Rm 
 kṣemaṃkarakumāreṇa kṣemāye prahitām imāṃ 
 ratnamālāṃ tvam ādāya bhadre tasyai samarpaya  Rm 
 ity uktvā ratnamālāṃ tāṃ kṣemāsakhīkare rahaḥ 
 datvā sa dūta āmaṃtrya sahasā svapuraṃ yayau  Rm 
 tatra sāpi sakhī tasyāḥ kṣemāyāḥ purato gatā 
 prābhṛtaṃ tam upasthāpya rahasy evaṃ nyavedayat  Rm 
 ayi bhadram imaṃ paśya prahitaṃ svāminā tava 
 tad idaṃ tvaṃ samāśliṣya patim iva vibhāvaya  Rm 
 iti tayoditaṃ śrutvā sā kṣemā lajjitāśayā 
 kāmaviṣāgnisaṃtrastā tasthau dinam adhomukhā  Rm 
 tataḥ sā kanyakā kṣemā tāṃ sakhīṃ purataḥ sthitāṃ 
 sucirāt samupārabhya hartsayanty evam abravīt  Rm 
 are re kiṃ vadasy evaṃ svāmī me kātra vidyate 
 nilajje vada tat kena prahitaṃ prābhṛtaṃ tava  Rm 
 ity uktaṃ sā sakhī śrutvā kṣemāyā durituḥ prabhoḥ 
 ājanme sarvavṛttāṃtaṃ vistareṇa nyavedayat  Rm 
 evaṃ sakhyā samākhyātaṃ śrutvā sā nṛpanaṃdinī 
 kṣemā saṃsārasaṃcārasamudvignāśayābhavat  Rm 
 tata utthāya sā kṣemā kanyāpi sahasā pituḥ 
 upetya caraṇau natvā sāṃjalir evam abravīt  Rm 
 tāta kāmārthinī nāham api tu sadguṇārthinī 
 sadguṇāṃ sādhayiṣyāmi tad anujñāṃ dadātu me  Rm 
 yad ahaṃ śāsane bauddhe pravrajitvā samāhita 
 brahmacaryaṃ samādhāya prechāmi carituṃ prabho  Rm 
 tad bhavāṃ kṛpayā tāta saṃbodhivratasādhane 
 anujñāṃ saṃpradatv me sarvathānugrahaṃ kuru  Rm 
 Rm 
 ity arthitaṃ tayā putryā śrutvā sa kośalādhipaḥ 
 tāṃ kumārīṃ samālokya tasthau saṃdigdhamānasaḥ  Rm 
 tataḥ sa janako rājā tāṃ kṣemāṃ svātmajāṃ priyāṃ 
 bodhayituṃ samāmaṃtrya samālokyaivam abravīt  Rm 
 naivaṃ putri mayā kartuṃ śakyate tat kṣamasva me 
 yat te janmani me rāṣṭre kṣemam evaṃ prajāyate  Rm 
 tadāpi tvaṃ pratijñaya brahmadattasya bhūpateḥ 
 kṣemaṃkarāya putrāya saṃkalpitā mayātmaje  Rm 
 tad yathā me pratijñātaṃ vacanaṃ pūrayātmaje 
 mā kṛthāḥ sarvathā kṣeme pravrajyāsādhane mama  Rm 
 yathā mayā pratijñātaṃ kariṣye na tad anyathā 
 matveti me vacaḥ śrutvā kuladharme carātmaje  Rm 
 evaṃ pitroditaṃ śrutvā sā kṣemā prahatāśayā 
 utthāya svālaye gatvā tūṣṇībhūtā nyaṣīdata  Rm 
 tadā sa janako rājā dūtam āhūya sādaraṃ 
 sarvam etat pravṛttāṃtaṃ samākhyāyaivam abravīt  Rm 
 gacha sādho narendrasya brahmadattasya bhūpateḥ 
 pura etat pravṛttāṃtaṃ nivedyaivaṃ prabodhaya  Rm 
 yad iyaṃ me sutā kṣemā pravrajituṃ samichati 
 tad imāṃ sahasāgatvā bhavān ādātum arhati  Rm 
 iti rājñā samādiṣṭaṃ śrutvā puraḥ sa sādaraṃ 
 tatheti saṃpratijñāya praṇatvā taṃ tato 'carat  Rm 
 tatra sa sahasā gatvā brahmadattasya bhūpateḥ 
 upetya sāṃjalir natvā pura evaṃ nyavedayat  Rm 
 jaya eva yadarthe 'haṃ preṣito 'tra mahībhṛtā 
 kośalendreṇa tad bhavāṃ śṛṇotv evaṃ bravīti saḥ  Rm 
 yad iyaṃ me sutā kṣemā pravrajituṃ samichati 
 tad imāṃ sahasāgatvā bhavān āhartum arhati  Rm 
 yathā mayā pratijñātaṃ karttuṃ na śakyate 'nyathā 
 tad ahaṃ te kumārāya dāsyāmi svātmajām imāṃ  Rm 
 evaṃ tena nareṃdreṇa samākhyāya bhavatpuraḥ 
 preṣito 'ham iti jñātvā tat tatrāgaṃtum arhati  Rm 
 iti tenoditaṃ śrutvā brahmadattaḥ sa bhūpatiḥ 
 taṃ dūtaṃ sahasāmaṃtrya pura evam abhāṣata  Rm 
 evaṃ ced āgamiṣyāmi saputraḥ saptame 'haṃ 
 yat tat kṛtyaṃ hi tat sarvaṃ karttavyam iti kathyatāṃ  Rm 
 ity ādiṣṭaṃ nareṃdreṇa brahmadattena sāṃjaliḥ 
 natvā tatheti vijñapya samutthāya tato 'carat  Rm 
 tatra sa sahasā gatvā svapuraṃ samupācaran 
 nṛpatiṃ sāṃjalir natvā pura evaṃ nyavedayat  Rm 
 jaya deva yathādiṣṭaṃ brahmadattasya bhūpateḥ 
 tathā vijñāpitaṃ sarvaṃ tad uktaṃ yācyate śṛṇu  Rm

 evaṃ ced āgamiṣyāmi saputraḥ saptame 'hani

 tadarhasarvasāmagrīṃ sahasā samasādhayat  Rm

 kāmabhogaṃ parityajya vāṃchāmi saugatavrataṃ  Rm

 saṃsmṛtvā śaraṇaṃ gatvā prārthaye sādhunādarāt  Rm 
 nūnaṃ buddho jagannātho jagacchāstā munīśvaraḥ 
 kṛpayā māṃ samālokya buddhavrate niyojayet  Rm

 saṃbuddhaśaraṇodbhūtaṃ puṇyaṃ tu labhyate dhruvaṃ  Rm 
 saṃbuddhasmṛtijaṃ puṇyaṃ na kṣiṇoti kadā cana 
 saṃbuddhasaṃvaraṃ dadyād iti prajñair nigadyate  Rm

 iti niścitya sā kṣemā snātvā śuddhāmvarāvṛtā 
 śaraṇapṛṣṭham āruhya abhavad dinmukhā sthitā  Rm

 brahmacārin mahābhijña maharṣe duritāntakaḥ  Rm 
 praśamopāyavid vijña śānta citta mahāmune 
 tvam eva hi jagannātha tat te 'haṃ śaraṇaṃ vraje  Rm 
 tan māṃ bhavodadhau magnāṃ kṛpayoddhartum arhati 
 iti saṃprārthite satyo kanyayā kṣemayā tayā 
 bhagavān kṛpayā dṛṣṭyā dadarśa tāṃ śubhāśayāṃ  Rm 
 tataḥ sa bhagavān dṛṣṭvā tāṃ kṣemāṃ bodhibhāvinīṃ 
 ṛddhyākaśāt samāgatya tatra kṣemāntike yayau  Rm

 Rm

 pitrā saha samāgatya tatrāsane upāviśat  Rm

 sa devāsuralokānāṃ vaṃdyā pūjyābhavat satī  Rm

 tatheyaṃ bhavati hy atra prajñāvatīgaṇādhipā  Rm 
 evaṃ hi yat kṛtaṃ yena tenaiva bhujyate phalaṃ 
 abhuktaṃ kṣīyate naiva karma kvāpi kadā cana  Rm 
 nāgnibhir dahyate karma klidyate nodakair api 
 vāyubhiḥ śuṣyate naiva kṣīyate nāpi bhūmiṣu  Rm 
 na praṇaśyaṃti karmāṇi janmakalpaśatair api 
 sāmāgrīṃ prāpya kāle hi phalanti prāṇināṃ khalu  Rm 
 anyathāpi bhaven naiva kṛtakarmaphalaṃ kvacit 
 kṛṣṇakarmavipāke hi duḥkhataiva sadā bhave  Rm 
 śubhakarmavipāke tu sukhataiva sadā bhavet 
 miśritakarmapākena miśritatā sadaiva hi  Rm 
 yathaiva yat kṛtaṃ karma tathaiva tat phalaṃ dhruvaṃ 
 evaṃ matvātra saṃsāre sarvadā śubhavāṃchibhiḥ  Rm 
 triratnabhajanaṃ kṛtvā caritavyaṃ sadā śubhe  Rm 
 ity ādiṣṭaṃ munīndreṇa śrutvā te sarvasāṃghikāḥ 
 tatheti prativijñapya prābhyanandan prabodhitāḥ  Rm 
 etan me guruṇādiṣṭaṃ śrutaṃ mayā tathocyate 
 tvaṃ cāpy evaṃ mahārāja cara nityaṃ śubhe sadā  Rm 
 prajāś cāpi tathā rājan bodhayitvā prayatnataḥ 
 bodhimārge pratiṣṭhāpya pālayasva samāhitaḥ  Rm 
 tena te sarvadā nityaṃ sarvatrāpi śubhaṃ bhavet 
 kramād bodhiṃ ca saṃprāpya saṃbuddhapadam āpnuyāḥ  Rm 
 iti tenārhatādiṣṭaṃ śrutvā 'śokaḥ sa bhūpatiḥ 
 tatheti prativijñapya prābhyanandat sapārṣadaḥ  Rm 
 kṣemāvadānaṃ manujā idaṃ ye śṛṇvaṃti cāpi niśāmayanti 
 te sarva evaṃ satataṃ sukhāni bhuktvā prayānty eva jinālayan te  Rm 
  iti ratnāvadānatatve kṣemāvadānaṃ samāptam 
 Rm 
 XXXIV Ārāmikāvadāna
 athāśoko mahīpālaḥ kṛtāñjaliḥ pramoditaḥ 
 upaguptaṃ yatiṃ natvā punar evam abhāṣata  Rm 
 bhadanta śrotum ichāmi punar anyat subhāṣitaṃ 
 tadyathā guruṇādiṣṭaṃ tathādeṣṭuñ ca me 'rhati  Rm 
 iti saṃprārthitaṃ rājñā śrutvā so 'rhan mahāmatiḥ 
 tam aśokaṃ mahārājaṃ samālokyaivam ādiśat  Rm 
 śṛṇu sādhu mahārāja yathā me guruṇoditaṃ 
 tathātrāhaṃ pravakṣyāmi tava dharmapravṛddhaye  Rm 
 tadyathā bhagavān buddhaḥ śākyasiṃho munīśvaraḥ 
 sarvajñaḥ sugato śāstā dharmarājas tathāgataḥ  Rm 
 śrāvakair bhikṣubhiḥ sārddhaṃ bhikṣuṇībhir upāsakaiḥ 
 upāsikāgaṇaiś cāpi cailakaiś cāpi tīrthikaṃ  Rm 
 bodhisatvair mahāsatvaiḥ sarvasatvahitaṃkaraṃ 
 ṛṣibhir yogibhiś cāpi yatibhir brahmacāribhiḥ  Rm 
 śrāvastyā bahir udyāne jetāraṇye jināśrame 
 vihāre vyaharal lokahitārthaṃ dharmam ādiśan  Rm 
 tat saddharmāmṛtaṃ pātuṃ sarve satvāḥ pramoditāḥ 
 śakrabrahmādayo devāḥ sarvalokādhipā api  Rm 
 nagendrā asurendrāś ca yakṣagaṃdharvakinnarāḥ 
 siddhā vidyādharāḥ sādhyā garuḍā rākṣasā api  Rm 
 brāhmaṇāḥ kṣatriyā bhūpā rājaputrāś ca maṃtriṇaḥ 
 amātyāḥ śreṣṭhinaḥ paura gṛhādhipā mahājanāḥ  Rm 
 vaṇijaḥ sārthavāhāś ca śilpino 'pi śubhārthinaḥ 
 grāmyā jānapadāś cānyalokāḥ kārpaṭikādayaḥ  Rm 
 sarve te samupāśritya vihāre taṃ munīśvaraṃ 
 dṛṣṭvā sāñjalayo natvā muditāḥ samunpāviśan  Rm 
 tatra sarve 'pi te nāthaṃ tam abhyarcya yathākramaṃ 
 tridhā pradakṣiṇīkṛtya praṇatvā samupāśrayan  Rm 
 tadā tān samupāsīnāṃ dṛṣṭvā sa bhagavāñ jinaḥ 
 āryasatyaṃ samārabhya saddharmaṃ samupādiśat  Rm 
 tat saddharmāmṛtaṃ pītva sarve brahmādayo 'pi te 
 lokāḥ satyam iti matvā prābhyanandan prabodhitāḥ  Rm 
 tasminn avasare kaścit'sau 'tha āramikaḥ sudhīḥ 
 dantakāṣṭhaṃ samādāya śrāvastyāṃ samupāviśat  Rm 
 tatra naimittiko dvāre 'vasthitas tam āgataṃ 
 dṛṣṭvā tad dantakāṣṭhaṃ ca samālokyaivam upāgamat  Rm 
 Rm 
 vataitad dantakāṣṭhaṃ yo bhakṣayiṣyati mānavaḥ 
 nūnam ṇataraṇaṃ bhogyaṃ prabhokṣyati sa bhāgyavān  Rm 
 etat tenoditaṃ śrutvā sa āramika unmukhaḥ 
 tatraiva kṣaṇam āśritya manasaivaṃ vyacintayat  Rm 
 kasmāy etad ahaṃ dadyāṃ saṃmāno yena me bhavet 
 evaṃ dhyātvā punas tatra manasaivaṃ vyacintayat  Rm 
 yad ayaṃ bhagavān buddhaḥ sarvatraidhātukādhipaḥ 
 jagacchāstā jagannātho dharmarājo munīśvaraḥ  Rm 
 yad asmai dīyate kiñcid api tat phalam uttamaṃ 
 aprameyam asaṃkhyeyaṃ mahatkhyātaṃ śrutaṃ mayā  Rm 
 tad asmai dharmarājāya buddhāya sarvatāyine 
 jagacchāstre munīndrāya dadyāṃ kāṣṭham idaṃ nv ahaṃ  Rm 
 iti dhyātvā viniścitya sa āramika ādarāt 
 dantakāṣṭhaṃ tad ādāya jetodyāne upācarat  Rm 
 tatra taṃ śrīghanaṃ dṛṣṭvā bhikṣusaṃghapuraskṛtaṃ 
 vihāre sa prasannāsyāḥ praviṣṭaḥ samupācarat  Rm 
 tatra tasya munīndrasya dantakāṣṭhaṃ tad ādarāt 
 upasthāpya praṇatvā sa sāṃjalir evam abravīt  Rm 
 bhagavan nātha sarvajña mamānugrahakāraṇāt 
 dantakāṣṭham imaṃ śāstā bhavān ādātum arhati  Rm 
 evaṃ saṃprārthite tena bhagavān sa munīśvaraḥ 
 dṛṣṭvā tat kāṣṭham ādāya tasyāgrato vyasṛjata  Rm 
 tadā tat kāṣṭham ādāya sa udyānapālako mudā 
 tatraiva saugatārāme nikhanya nidadhe bhuvi  Rm 
 tatra nihitamātraṃ tat kāṣṭhaṃ mūlapratiṣṭhitaṃ 
 mahacchākhāharitpatrapuṣpaphalasamṛddhitaḥ  Rm 
 tatkṣaṇena mahān vṛkṣo nyagrodhaḥ parimaṇḍalaḥ 
 sarvasatvamanohārī mahāmegha ivābhavat  Rm 
 tatra sa bhagavān gatvā tacchāyāṃ samupāśrayan 
 sabhāmadhyāsanāsīnaḥ saddhārmaṃ samupādiśat  Rm 
 etad adbhutam ālokya sarve lokāḥ savismayāḥ 
 tat saddharmāmṛtaṃ pītvā prābhyanandan pramoditāḥ  Rm 
 tadā tatra mahātmā sa gṛhīśo 'nāthapiṇḍadaḥ 
 samāgatya munīndraṃ taṃ natvaivaṃ prārthayan mudā  Rm 
 bhagavann aham adyeha bhagavantaṃ sasāṃghikaṃ 
 pūjayituṃ samichāmi tan mamānugrahaṃ kuru  Rm 
 iti tat prārthitaṃ śrutvā bhagavān sa munīśvaraḥ 
 tatheti taṃ samālokya tūṣṇīṃ bhūtvādhyuvāsa tat  Rm 
 tad adhivāsitaṃ śāstra matvā so 'nāthapiṇḍadaḥ 
 tatrāsanāni prajñapya tat sāmagrīṃ samānayat  Rm 
 tadā sa bhagavāns tatra sasāṃghikaḥ samutthitaḥ 
 tad dattaṃ pādyam ādāya svasvāsane samāśrayat  Rm 
 tatrāsanasamāsīnaṃ taṃ munīndraṃ sasāṃghikaṃ 
 Rm 
 dṛṣṭvā sa muditaḥ śreṣṭhī yathākramaṃ samarcayet  Rm 
 tataḥ śatarasai bhojyaiḥ supraṇītaiḥ sa dīnabhṛt 
 saṃbuddhapramukhaṃ sarvasaṃghaṃ taṃ samatarpayat  Rm 
 tataḥ sa śrīghanaṃ sarvasaṃghaṃ ca parituṣṭitaṃ 
 matvā panīyapātrāṇi tad dhastādīṃ vyaśodhayat  Rm 
 tataḥ kramukatāmbūlagaṇauṣadhīrasāyanaṃ 
 datvā sa sāṃjalir natvā sasaṃghaṃ tam upāśrayat  Rm 
 tataḥ sa bhagavān dṛṣṭvā taṃ gṛhastham upasthitaṃ 
 ādimadhyāmṭakalyāṇaṃ sāśiṣaṃ dharmam ādiśat  Rm 
 tad dṛṣṭva samahotsāham āramikaḥ sa mohitaḥ 
 naimittikasamākhyātaṃ satyaṃ matvābhyanaṃdata  Rm 
 tataḥ sa suprasannātmā ārāmikaḥ pramoditaḥ 
 samutthāya munīndrasya purataḥ samupācarat  Rm 
 tatra tasya munīndrasya pādayoḥ sa kṛtāñjaliḥ 
 praṇatvā manasā bodhipraṇidhānaṃ vyadhān mudā  Rm 
 yad asmai dharmarājāya jagacchāstrai jagadbhute 
 mayātra śraddhayā dattakāṣṭhamātraṃ samarppitaṃ  Rm 
 etatpuṇyavipākena caritvāhaṃ śubhe sadā 
 pratyekāṃ bodhim āsādya nirvṛtipadam āpnuyāṃ  Rm 
 iti tena sucittena praṇidhānam kṛtaṃ sadā 
 matvā sa bhagavān smitaṃ visasarja saraśmikaṃ  Rm 
 tatas te raśmayaḥ sarvā munimukhābjaniḥsṛtāḥ 
 nānā varṇāḥ samanteṣu bhuvaneṣu sa bhāsayan  Rm 
 ye cādho bhuvane yātāḥ sarvatra narakeṣu te 
 avabhāsya sukhīkṛtya nārakīyān pracerire  Rm 
 tadraśmisaṃparispṛṣṭāḥ sarve te narakasthitāḥ 
 nirduḥkhāḥ sukhasaṃpannā vismitā evam ūcire  Rm 
 aho citraṃ kathaṃ duḥkhaṃ prasrabdhaṃ jāyate sukhaṃ 
 itaś cyutāḥ kuhānyatra saṃprāptāḥ sāṃprataṃ vayaṃ  Rm 
 iti saṃdigdhacittānāṃ teṣāṃ narakavāsināṃ 
 bodhārthaṃ nirmitaṃ buddhaṃ bhagavān vyasṛjat tadā  Rm 
 tan nirmitaṃ muniṃ dṛṣṭvā sarve te narakasthititāḥ 
 mahaccitrasamākrāntahṛdayāś caivam ūśire  Rm 
 naivānyatra gatā sarve ihaiva saṃsthitā vayaṃ 
 kintv ayaṃ puruṣo 'pūrvadarśanaḥ samupāgataḥ  Rm 
 nūnam ayaṃ mahāsattvaḥ samīkṣyāsmān suduḥkhinaḥ 
 kṛpayā coditaḥ sarvān samuddharttum ihāgataḥ  Rm 
 tad asya puruṣasyātra sarvair asmābhir ādarāt 
 śraddhayā śaraṇaṃ gatvā karttavyaṃ bhajanaṃ mudā  Rm 
 iti saṃbhāṣya te sarve nārakīyā prasāditāḥ 
 tasya nirmitabuddhasya prābhajañ charaṇaṃ gatāḥ  Rm 
 Rm 
 tadaitadbhajanotpannaiḥ puṇyais te narakotthitāḥ 
 nirmuktapātakāḥ sarve śuddhakāyā divaṃ yayuḥ  Rm 
 evaṃ te raśmayaḥ sarve sarvāns tān nirayāśṛtān 
 avabhāsya samuddhṛtya pratyāyayur muneḥ puraḥ  Rm 
 evam urddhagatā ye ca raśmayas te prasāritāḥ 
 avabhāsya diśaḥ sarvāḥ saṃprasusruḥ surālayān  Rm 
 sarvān devālayāṃś caivam avabhāsya samantataḥ 
 gatvākaniṣṭhaparyantaṃ sarvān devān acodayan  Rm 
 anityaṃ khalu saṃsāraṃ duḥkhaśūnyam anātmakaṃ 
 puṇyam eva jagatsāraṃ matvā tac cinutādarāt  Rm 
 niṣkrāmatārabhadhvaṃ tad yujyadhvaṃ buddhaśāsane 
 mārasainyān vinirjitya caradhvaṃ saṃvare sadā  Rm 
 yo 'pramatto munīndrasya śāsane saṃcariṣyate 
 sa hitvā janma saṃsāre duḥkhasyāntaṃ kariṣyati  Rm 
 ity udghoṣaiḥ surān sarvāñ codayitvā samantataḥ 
 sarve te raśmayas tatra puraḥ pratyāyayur muneḥ  Rm 
 tatra te raśmayaḥ sarve 'py ekībhūtāś ca piṇḍitāḥ 
 muniṃ pradakṣiṇīkṛtya tad ūrṇāyāṃ samāviśan  Rm 
 tad dṛṣṭvā sabhāsīnāḥ sarve lokāḥ savismayāḥ 
 kiṃ śāstehādiśed dharmam ity evaṃ samacintayat  Rm 
 athānaṃdaḥ samutthāya kṛtāṃjaliḥ savismayaḥ 
 bhagavantaṃ tam ānamya prārthayad evam ādarāt  Rm 
 nāhetupratyayaṃ śāstar hasanti sugatāḥ kvacit 
 tat kim arthañ jagannātha bhavān hasati sāṃprataṃ  Rm 
 yad bhavataḥ smitaṃ dṛṣṭvā sarve ime sabhājanāḥ 
 vismayasamupākrāntacittās tiṣṭhanti sarvavit  Rm 
 tad yad arthe bhavān smitaṃ muṃcati taj jagadguro 
 samupādiśya sarveṣāṃ saṃśayaṃ chetum arhati  Rm 
 ity ānandoditaṃ śrutvā bhagavān munīśvaraḥ 
 tam ānandaṃ sabhāṃ cāpi samālokyaivam ādiśat  Rm 
 evam etat tathānaṃda yathākhyātaṃ tvayā kila 
 nāhetupratyayaṃ buddhā muñcaṃti hi smitaṃ kva cit  Rm 
 yadarthe 'ham ihānanda smitaṃ muñcāmi sāṃprataṃ 
 tat satyaṃ saṃpravakṣyāmi śṛṇuta yūyam ādarāt  Rm 
 yad ayaṃ śraddhayānanda sudhīr udyānapālakaḥ 
 dantakāṣṭham upasthāpya satkāraṃ kurute mama  Rm 
 etatpuṇyavipākena kalpāny api trayodaśa 
 vinipātam ayaṃ kvāpi gamiṣyati kadā cana  Rm 
 sarvadāyaṃ mahāsatvaḥ saddharmasādhanodyataḥ 
 sadguṇī sukhasaṃbhoktā bodhisatvo bhaviṣyati  Rm 
 tato 'nte 'yaṃ mahābhijñaḥ pariśuddhatrimaṇḍalaḥ 
 pratyekaṃ bodhim āsādya pratyekasugato jinaḥ  Rm 
 vimalo nāma satvānāṃ hitakarī śubhaṃkaraḥ 
 Rm 
 brahmacārī viśuddhātmā lokanātho bhaviṣyati  Rm
