 śrutvānaṃdaḥ sa saṃpaśyans taṃ dvijam evam abravīt  Rm 
 śṛṇu vipra munīndreṇa yāthādiṣṭaṃ mayā śrutaṃ 
 tathāhaṃ te pravakṣyāmi śrīvratasya vidhiṃ kramāt  Rm 
 bhādrapade 'śite pakṣe tṛtīyāyāṃ tithau tathā 
 māghe vāpi śite pakṣe śuklapakṣe 'pi vā sadā  Rm 
 tīrthe devālaye śuddhabhūpradeśe gṛheṣu vā 
 samyag bhūśodhanaṃ kuryād gomayena mṛdāmbunā  Rm 
 prātar utthāya tīrtheṣu snātvā śucisamācaraḥ 
 tridhācamyāmṛtaṃ kāyaṃ paṃcagavyena śodhayet  Rm 
 śuddhaśīlasamādhānaḥ pariśuddhāmvarāvṛtaḥ 
 Rm 
 saṃbodhicittam ādhāya sadguror upadeśa dhṛk  Rm 
 subhūmau maṇḍalaṃ samyag varttayitvā yathāvidhi 
 dhvajachatrapatākābhi vitānaiś cābhimaṃḍayet  Rm 
 maṃḍalasya vahis tasya jvālāvalyā vahiḥ punaḥ 
 paṃcavalyāvalībhiś ca sa lājākṣatasaṃyutaiḥ  Rm 
 veṣṭayitvā tato vāhye kramān saṃsthāpayed ghaṭān 
 tīrthāmbupūritān pītavastrāvṛtān saciṃhnitān  Rm 
 tātra śrīvasudhāṃ devīṃ sagaṇāṃ vidhinā kramāt 
 samāvāhya samabhyarcya pratiṣṭhāpyādhivāsayet  Rm 
 tṛtīyāyāṃ tathā prātaḥ snātvā śuddhāmvarāvṛtaḥ 
 madhyāhne svāsanāsīna uttarādigmukhasthitaḥ  Rm 
 ādau guruṃ samabhyarcya ratnatrayaṃ samarcayet 
 tato dhyātvā mahādevīṃ vasudhārāṃ śubhakarīṃ  Rm 
 sagaṇāṃ tāṃ samāvāhya datvā pādārgham ādarāt 
 pītamayopahāreṇa samabhyarcya yathāvidhi  Rm 
 sarvopakaraṇāny agre nivesya samaḍhokayat 
 tatas taddhāraṇīṃ samyak paṭhen maṃtrāṇi ca kramāt  Rm 
 tataḥ kṛtāṃjaliḥ stutvā kuryāś ca pāpadeśanāṃ 
 puṇyānumodanāṃ cāpi kuryāc ca praṇatiṃ smaran  Rm 
 kuryāt pradakṣiṇāny evam aṣṭāṅgaiḥ praṇamet punaḥ 
 bodhicittaṃ samādhāya saṃprārthayed abhīpsitaṃ  Rm 
 tato valiṃ pradatvā ca sa bhūtān paritoṣayet 
 tataḥ kṣamārthanāṃ kṛtvā vratasūtraṃ ca prārthayet  Rm 
 ṣoḍaśabheditaṃ sūtram ṣoḍaśagraṃthisaṃyutaṃ 
 vratasūtraṃ samādāya rakṣārthaṃ vaṃdhayet kare  Rm 
 tato guruṃ samārādhya deyād dānaṃ samichitaṃ 
 sadakṣiṇaṃ susatkāraiḥ satkṛtya samatoṣayet  Rm 
 tatas tṛtīyā yāme 'hneḥ prāśnuyād yavapūrakān 
 paṃcāmṛtaphalaskaṃdamūlapatrādikān api  Rm 
 pālanānte punaḥ snātvā tāṃ śrīdevīm anusmaran 
 taddhāraṇīṃ paṭhan rātrau pūjayec ca samāhitaḥ  Rm 
 evaṃ nityaṃ catuḥ saṃdhyaṃ pūjayec chrīvasuṃdharāṃ 
 tat paredyus tathābhyarcya tan maṃḍalaṃ visarjayet  Rm 
 tad rajāṃsi samādāya saṃnidhāya śubhe ghaṭe 
 bhaṃḍāgāre pratisthāpya sadārān bhajen namet  Rm 
 śeṣarajaḥ sa nirmālyaṃ nadyāṃ nāgān yathāvidhi 
 samabhyarcya samarppitvā sarvaṃ jale pravāhayet  Rm 
 tatas taj jalam ādāya gṛhe gatvā samantataḥ 
 prokṣya tan maṃḍalasthāne kumārīṃ vidhinārcayet  Rm 
 tatas tan sagaṇaṃ cakraṃ samabhyarcya yathāvidhi 
 bhojanaiḥ saṃparitoṣya prārthayed yat samīchitaṃ  Rm 
 Rm 
 tathā tat sagaṇaṃ cakraṃ kṛtvā kṣamārthanāṃ tataḥ 
 sāṃjaliś ca kramān natvā visarjayet prasādayan  Rm 
 tadā śrīvasudhā devī svayam āgatya tadgṛhe 
 samāśritya sadā sarvadravyaiḥ saṃpūrayed dhruvaṃ  Rm 
 tatas tatra gṛhe nityaṃ maṃgalaṃ nirupadravaṃ 
 dānapuṇyamahotsāhapravarttitaṃ bhavet sadā  Rm 
 evaṃ tasyā mahādevyā vasulakṣmyā vratodbhavaṃ 
 puṇyaṃ mahad asaṃkhyeyam aprameyaṃ vidur jināḥ  Rm 
 evaṃ mahattaraṃ puṇyaṃ vijñāya dvija tat tathā 
 śraddhaye tadvrataṃ kuryā yadi saṃpattim ichasi  Rm 
 yaś ca tāṃ śrīmahādevīṃ vasudhārām anusmaran 
 yat kāryyam ārabhet tasya tat sarvaṃ hi samṛddhyati  Rm 
 ratnārthī labhate ratnaṃ dhanārthī labhate dhanaṃ 
 bhogyārthī labhate bhogyaṃ yaso 'rthī labhate yaśaḥ  Rm 
 dravyārthī labhate dravyān guṇārthī labhate guṇān 
 vidyārthī labhate vidyāṃ śubhārthī labhate śubhaṃ  Rm 
 mānyārthī labhate mānyaṃ jayārthī labhate jayaṃ 
 dharmārthī labhate dharmān sukhārthī labhate sukhaṃ  Rm 
 rājyārthī labhate rājyaṃ gṛhārthī labhate gṛhaṃ 
 kṣetrārthī labhate kṣetrān rasārthī labhate rasān  Rm 
 bhāryārthī labhate bhāryāṃ sutārthī labhate sutāṃ 
 putrārthī labhate putrān pautrārthī pautram āpnuyāt  Rm 
 jñānārthī labhate jñānaṃ mokṣārthī mokṣam āpnuyāt 
 evam anyāni vastūni sarvopakaraṇāny api  Rm 
 sarvāṇi dravyajātāni vastrādi bhūṣaṇāny api 
 samāpnuyāt samṛddhāni vasulakṣmyāḥ prasādataḥ  Rm 
 tato dānāni dadyāt sa śuddhaśīlaḥ samācaret 
 kṣāntiṃ ca bhāvayen nityaṃ dharmavīryyaṃ samārabhet  Rm 
 tathā dhyānaṃ samādhāya prajñābdhiṃ saṃtared drutaṃ 
 sarvopāyavidhānajño bodhipraṇidhimānasaḥ  Rm 
 sadbuddhibalavān dhīraḥ sa bodhijñānam āpnuyāt 
 sarvamāragaṇāñ jitvā niḥkleśo 'rhañ jitendriyaḥ 
 saṃbuddhapadam āsādya nirvṛtapadam āpnuyāt  Rm 
 evaṃ brāhmaṇa vijñāya saddharmmaṃ yadi vāṃchasi 
 tāṃ śrīdevīṃ mahālakṣmīṃ vasudhārāṃ sadā bhaja  Rm 
 tathā te sarvadā gehe maṃgalaṃ nirupadravaṃ 
 sarvatreha paratrāpi bhaven nūnaṃ na saṃśayaḥ  Rm 
 tathā dānāni datvā tvaṃ svayaṃ tadvrataṃ saṃcaran 
 sarvasatvahitaṃ kṛtvā yāvajjīvaṃ sukhaṃ cara  Rm 
 tataḥ kleśavimuktātmā saṃbodhipraṇidhānadhṛk 
 bodhicaryāvratāraktā bodhisatvo bhaved dhruvaṃ  Rm 
 sarve 'pi sugatā bodhisatvāś cāpi jinātmajāḥ 
 Rm 
 vasudhārāvrataṃ dhṛtvā saṃvibhrati jagattrayaṃ  Rm 
 iti tenārhatādiṣṭaṃ śrutvā sa brāhmaṇo mudā 
 tathā śrīvasudhārāyā vrataṃ caritum aichata  Rm 
 tataḥ sa viṣṇudāso 'pi bhāryāṃ tāṃ dhīmatīṃ mudā 
 suprasannamukhāmbhojaḥ samālokyaivam abravīt  Rm 
 priye dhanyāsi kalyāṇī yad ahaṃ tvatprayatnataḥ 
 śrīdevyā vrataṃ ratnaṃ prāpnomi sāṃprataṃ khalu  Rm 
 tad yathānena śāstrātra samādiṣṭaṃ tathā khalu 
 śrīdevyāḥ śaraṇaṃ gatvā vāṃchāmi carituṃ vrataṃ  Rm 
 tat tvam api samādhāya mayā sārddhaṃ tathādarāt 
 śrīdevyāḥ śaraṇaṃ kṛtvā vrataṃ caritum arhati  Rm 
 iti bhartroditaṃ śrutvā dhīmatī sānumoditā 
 bharttāraṃ taṃ samālokya punar evam abhāṣata  Rm 
 tathā satyaṃ samādhāya śraddhayā śaraṇaṃ gatau 
 śrīdevyā vratam atrāvāṃ samādarāc carāvahe  Rm 
 ity uktvā sā satī bhadrā dhīmatī sahasādarāt 
 vratopacārasāmagrīṃ muditā samasādhayat  Rm 
 tatas taṃ gurum ānaṃdaṃ natvā sā sāṃjalir mudā 
 tad vratārambham ādhātuṃ prārthayed evam ādarāt  Rm 
 bhadanta śrīmahādevyā vratadina upāsthitaḥ 
 tad yathāvidhim ādiśya saṃcārayatāṃ vrataṃ  Rm 
 tayeti prārthitaṃ śrutvā sa ānaṃdo jinātmajaḥ 
 sarvavidhiṃ samādiśya vratāraṃbhaṃ samākramat  Rm 
 tatra bhūśodhanaṃ kṛtvā sa ānaṃdo yathāvidhi 
 maṃḍalaṃ varttayitvā tat pratisthāpyādhyavāsayat  Rm 
 tathā tau daṃpatī tīrthe snātvā śuddhāmvarāvṛtau 
 yathā śāstrā samādiṣṭaṃ sarvaṃ kṛtvopatasthatuḥ  Rm 
 tatas tau daṃpatī tasya śāstur ādeśataḥ kramāt 
 śuddhāsanasamāsīnāv uttarābhimukhasthitau  Rm 
 gavyaiḥ kāmādi vastūni sarvāṇi śuddhitāny api 
 kṛtvā śāstrā yathādiṣṭaṃ tathāraṃbhaṃ pracakratuḥ  Rm 
 ādau guruṃ samabhyarcya tato ratnatrayaṃ mudā 
 abhyarcya śaraṇaṃ kṛtvā praṇatvā vidhinādarāt  Rm 
 tatas tanmaṇḍale devīṃ sagaṇāṃ śrīvasuṃdharāṃ 
 dhyātvā tathā samāvāhya datvā pādārgham ādarāt  Rm 
 tatas tāṃ sagaṇāṃ devīṃ samabhyarcya yathākramaṃ 
 sarvapūjopacāraiś ca paṭhitvā dhāraṇīṃ tataḥ  Rm 
 sahṛdvījādimaṃtrāṇi yathākramaṃ jajalpatuḥ 
 tato 'ṣṭāṅgapraṇāmaiś ca natvā kṛtvā pradakṣiṇāṃ  Rm 
 guṇābhivādanai stotrai stutvā natau vavaṃdatuḥ  Rm 
 tatas tau sāṃjalī sthitvā prakṣitvā pāpadeśanāṃ 
 Rm 
 puṇyānumodanāṃ cāpi saṃprārthya śrīsamṛddhyatāṃ  Rm

 tato rātrau samādhāya sagaṇāṃ vasuṃdharāṃ 
 devīṃ dhyātvā samabhyarcya dharmmaṃ śrutvā niṣedatuḥ  Rm 
 tataḥ prātaḥ samutthāya snātvā śuddhāmvarāvṛtau 
 tathā tāṃ sagaṇāṃ devīm āvāhyānarcatuḥ kramāt  Rm 
 tatas tad vratasaṃpūrṇaṃ kṛtvā dānaṃ sadakṣiṇaṃ 
 pradatvā gurave natvā tan maṇḍalaṃ vyasarjatāṃ  Rm 
 tatas tad rajam ādāya bhaṃḍāgāre yathoditaṃ 
 nidhāya tat sa nirmālyaṃ śeṣaṃ nadyāṃ yathāvidhiṃ  Rm 
 gurur nāgān samabhyarcya samarpya prākṣipaj jale 
 tatas taj jalam ādāya mahotsāhair gṛhaṃ yayau  Rm 
 tata gṛhe tad ambhobhir abhiṣiṃcya samantataḥ 
 kumārīṃ vidhinārādhya gaṇacakraṃ samarcayat  Rm 
 tatas tau daṃpatī natvā sāṃjali sādaraṃ mudā 
 saṃpattiprārthanāṃ kṛtvā kṣamāpya tad vyasarjatāṃ  Rm 
 tatas tasyā gṛhe devī vasundhārā svayaṃ sthitā 
 sarvadravyasamāpūrṇaṃ kṛtvā tasthau prasāditā  Rm

 vismayānaṃdasaṃpannau mitha evaṃ samūcatuḥ  Rm 
 aho satyaṃ jagacchāstur yathādiṣṭaṃ tathā khalu 
 tathāvāṃ śaraṇaṃ gatvā devyā vrataṃ carevahi  Rm 
 ity uktvā tau prasīdaṃtau śaraṇaṃ gatvā samāhitau 
 tasyāḥ śrīmahādevyāḥ sadā vrataṃ praceratuḥ  Rm 
 tadārabhyaḥ sadārthibhyo datvā dānaṃ yathārthitaṃ 
 triratnabhajanaṃ kṛtvā praceratuḥ śubhe sadā  Rm 
 tato 'sau yatir ānaṃdas tau samāmaṃtrya daṃpatī 
 pakṣivat sahasākāśāt kauśāṃvyāṃ samupācarat  Rm 
 tatra sa taṃ jagannāthaṃ praṇatvā sāṃjaliḥ punaḥ 
 etat sarvaṃ pravṛttāṃtaṃ nivedyaikāntam āśrayat  Rm 
 tataḥ sa bhagavān dṛṣṭvā tam ānaṃdaṃ sabhāṃ ca tāṃ 
 dhīmatyāḥ śāṃtamatyāś ca prasāditvaivam ādiśat  Rm 
 dhanyā sā dhīmatī śāntamatī cāpi subhāvinī 
 yat te śrīvasudhārāyā bhavetāṃ vratadhāriṇī  Rm 
 tan me ubhe mahatpuṇyalābhinyau śrīsamanvite 
 Rm 
 sarvasatvahitādhānabodhicaryāsamudyate  Rm 
 kramād bodhiṃ samāsādya buddhapadam avāpsyata  Rm 
 ity ādiṣṭaṃ munīndreṇa śrutvā te sarvasāṃghikāḥ 
 tāṃ śrīvasuṃdharāṃ devīṃ smṛtvā nityaṃ prabhejire  Rm

 samudbhūtā mahāsaṃpad ity aśroṣīj janoditaṃ  Rm

 katham etad bhavet satyam iti taṃ patim abravīt  Rm

 savismayenākhyātaṃ śrutvā caivam abhāṣata  Rm 
 priye śrutaṃ mayā satyaṃ dhīmatyā yad gṛhe 'dhunā 
 mahāsaṃpatsamudbhūtā vasundhārāprasādataḥ  Rm 
 yadi naitat pratīto 'pi janaiḥ sā dhīmatī sutā 
 svagṛhe 'tra samāhūya tvam evaṃ paripṛchyatāṃ  Rm 
 kathaṃ saṃjāyate saṃpan mahatī te gṛhe 'dhunā 
 etat satyaṃ tvayā putrī puro me kathyatām iti  Rm 
 evaṃ bhartrā samākhyātaṃ śrutva sā dhīmatīprasūḥ 
 tatheti prativijñāya svasakhīm evam abravīt  Rm 
 śṛṇu sakhi sutāyā me dhīmatyā yad gṛhe 'dhunā 
 saṃbhūtā mahatī saṃpad vasuṃdhārā prasādataḥ  Rm 
 iti śrutaṃ mayā satyaṃ draṣṭum ichāmi tat khalu 
 tat tāṃ sutāṃ samāhūya samādarād ihānaya  Rm 
 iti tayā samākhyātaṃ śrutvā sā supriyā sakhī 
 tatheti prativijñapya dhīmatyā bhavane yayau  Rm 
 tatra sā samupāsṛtya dhīmatīṃ tāṃ subhadrikāṃ 
 dṛṣṭvā savismayānaṃdayuktā natvaivam abravīt  Rm

 sahasā tvaṃ samāgaṃtum arhasi svātmajānvitā  Rm 
 iti tayā samākhyātaṃ śrutvā sā dhīmatī mudā 
 hasantī tāṃ sakhīṃ mātuḥ samālokyaivam abravīt  Rm 
 ayi māṃ smarate mātā kim arthaṃ sāṃprataṃ kathaṃ 
 tadāhaṃ na smṛtā mātrā dāridriyaduḥkhinī yadā  Rm 
 tathāpy ahaṃ mukhaṃ mātur draṣṭum ichāmi sāṃprataṃ 
 tathāham āgamiṣyāmi yathā mātuḥ samīhitaṃ  Rm 
 ity uktvā dhīmatī sātha putraṃ ca bhūṣaṇaṃ 
 bhūṣayitvā suvastraiś ca prāvārya samamaṇḍayat  Rm 
 svayaṃ ca sā prasādhitvā duṣyapaṭṭāmvarāvṛtā 
 śrīmad ratnāmvalaṃkārair maṇḍitāṃgābhiśobhitā  Rm 
 Rm 
 tataḥ sakhyā tayā sārddhaṃ putraputrīsamanvitā 
 saṃprasthitā janaiś cāpi saha mātur gṛhe yayau  Rm

 taṃ suputraṃ suputrīṃ ca paśyantī samupācaran  Rm 
 tatra tāṃ jananīṃ dṛṣṭvā dhīmatī sātmajānvitā

 janakaṃ taṃ samālokya dhīmatī sātmajānvitā

 putraputryau ca saṃbhāṣya papracha kauśalaṃ mudā  Rm 
 pitā sa jananī sāpi dhīmatīṃ tāṃ subhāvinīṃ

 pādān prakṣālayitvāśu svakam ānayat  Rm

 tatrāsane samāśritya pārśvayor vāmadakṣayoḥ 
 putrīṃ putram upasthāpya tasthau sā dhīmatī smitā  Rm

 sahasā draṣṭum āgatya sā daraṃ samupāyayuḥ  Rm 
 tathā te vāṃdhavāḥ sarve suhṛtminrajanā api 
 tāṃ tathā svagṛhāyātāṃ kuśalaṃ praṣṭum āyayuḥ  Rm 
 tathā tāś ca bhaginyo 'pi tāsāṃ sarve 'pi cātmajāḥ 
 tāṃ dhīmatīṃ tathāyātāṃ śrutvā draṣṭu samā yayuḥ  Rm 
 evam anye 'pi lokāś ca dhīmatīṃ tāṃ subhūṣaṇāṃ 
 svamātur gṛhamāyātāṃ śrutvā draṣṭum upāyayuḥ  Rm 
 tatretaṃ dhīmatīṃ kāṃtāṃ suvastrabhūṣaṇāvṛtāṃ

 tathā sā dhīmatī cāpi jñātivaṃdhusuhṛjjanān

 Rm 
 gṛhṇāṇa surasaṃ bhogyaṃ bhukṣva hṛd dhīmati priye 
 yo sauta saute ca saudārdda procyutaṃ yadabhīpsitaṃ  Rm 
 janako vitathya sarvo bhaginyo bhrātaro 'pi ca

 bhūṣaṇāni prasāryaivaṃ sādaraṃ pratyabhāṣata  Rm 
 bho bho bhavanti sarvāṇi bhūṣaṇāni priyāṇi me 
 idaṃ saurasikaṃ bhojyaṃ prāśnuta svechayā sukhaṃ  Rm 
 saṃsāre mānanīyaṃ hi dhanam eva sadādarāt 
 dhanānurūpeṇa yal loke mānyate niṃdyate naraḥ  Rm

 nirdhanā guṇavāṃś cāpi sujāto 'pi na mānyate  Rm

 yadā saṃpad vihīne tu tadā sa bhūtavac caret  Rm 
 iti sābhilapanty eva sarvāṇi bhūṣaṇāny api 
 tāni punaḥ samādāya yathā sthānaṃ nyayojayat  Rm

 natvaiva pitarau bharttur gṛhe yayau prasāditā  Rm

 śrīdevīvratam ādhāya samāpnomi susaṃpadaṃ  Rm 
 Rm 
 priye tvām atra tadratnasaṃbhavakulasaṃbhavāṃ

 priye sakhi mahābhāge bhavatkṛpāprasādataḥ 
 pāpaṃ me kṣīyate sarvaṃ taj janma saphalaṃ bhave  Rm 
 saṃpattiḥ saṃprajātā me naiva kṣīṇā bhaved api 
 tad yāvajjīvitaṃ devyāḥ śaraṇastho bhajāni hi  Rm 
 tvam eva śāstā na cānyā hi saddharmopadeśinī 
 tan me puṇyānubhāvena saṃbuddhapadam āpnuhi  Rm 
 ity udite tam āśrutvā śāṃtamatiś ca sā mudā 
 dhīmatīṃ tāṃ samālokya punar evam abhāṣāta  Rm 
 bhadre dhīmati saṃbuddhaśaraṇasthā sadādarāt 
 śrīdevyāvratam ādhāya śubhe cara samāhitā  Rm 
 etatpuṇyavipākena sarvadā sadgatīṃ gatā 
 kramāt saṃbodhim āsādya saṃbuddhapadam āpnuyāḥ  Rm 
 iti matvātra saṃsāre śubhaṃ dharmārthasādhanaṃ 
 dharmo lokahitārthāya tal lokārthe dharmam ācareḥ  Rm 
 iti tayoditaṃ śrutvā dhīmatī sā prabodhitā 
 tatheti pratinaṃditvā muditā svagṛhe yayau  Rm 
 tataḥ prabhṛti sā sādhvī dhīmatī sarvadā gṛhe 
 śrīdevyā bhajanaṃ kṛtvā datvā dānaṃ śubhe 'carat  Rm 
 tathā tasyā gṛhe saṃpad dine dine pravarddhitā 
 sarvasatvopabhogyārthaṃ babhūva dharmasādhinī  Rm 
 tathā sā dhīmatī dṛṣṭvā sarvasaṃpatpravarddhitāṃ 
 mudā lokahitaṃ kṛtvā pracacāra śubhe sadā  Rm 
 iti me guruṇādiṣṭaṃ śrutaṃ mayā tathocyate 
 tathā tvam api rājendra vasudhārāvrataṃ cara  Rm 
 prajāś cāpi mahārāja bodhayitvā prayatnataḥ 
 Rm 
 śrīdevyāḥ śaraṇe sthāpya vrataṃ cāraya sarvadā  Rm 
 tathā te sarvadā kṣemaṃ sarvatrāpi bhaved dhruvaṃ 
 kramād bodhiṃ samāsādya saṃbuddhapadam āpnuyāḥ  Rm 
 iti tenārhatādiṣṭaṃ śrutvāśokaḥ sa bhūpatiḥ 
 tathety abhyanumoditvā prābhyanandat sapārṣadaḥ  Rm 
 dhīmatyā ye 'vadānaṃ śubhaphaladam idaṃ suprasannāḥ śṛṇvanti 
 śrāvayanti pramuditamanasā bodhicaryānurāgāḥ 
 sarve te bodhisatvāḥ sakalaguṇadharāḥ sarvasaṃpatsamṛddhāḥ 
 śrīmanto lokaśreṣṭhā jinanilayagatāḥ saṃvasaṃti sukhāḍhyāḥ  Rm 
  iti śrīratnāvadānatatve dhīmatyāvadānaṃ samāptam 
 Rm 
 XXXVIII Vasundharāvadāna
 athāśoko maharājaḥ kṛtāñjalipuṭo mudā 
 upaguptaṃ yatiṃ natvā punar evam abhāṣata  Rm 
 bhadanta śrotum ichāmi vasudhārāvrataṃ kadā 
 kena kuha kathaṃ martyaloke pracāritaṃ purā  Rm 
 tad atra no bhavāñ cchāstar yathā pravarttitaṃ purā 
 tathā sarvaṃ samākhyātuṃ vistareṇa samarhati  Rm 
 iti saṃprārthitaṃ rājñā śrutvā so 'rhan mahāmatiḥ 
 aśokaṃ taṃ mahīpālaṃ samālokyaivam abravīt  Rm 
 śṛṇu rājan yathākhyātaṃ guruṇā me srutaṃ mayā 
 tathāhaṃ te pravakṣyāmi vasudhārāvratodbhavaṃ  Rm 
 tadyathā bhagavān buddhaḥ śākyamunis tathāgataḥ 
 sarvajño 'rhaṃ jagacchāstā dharmarājo vināyakaḥ  Rm 
 sa ekasamaye tatra kauśānvyā upakaṇṭhike 
 Ms ekaḥ samaye
 vihāre ghoṣirārāme vijahāra sasāṃghikaḥ  Rm 
 tadā śakrādayo devā brahmādi brāhmaṇā api 
 daityendrā lokapālāś ca saddharmaśravaṇotsukāḥ  Rm 
 rākṣasā garuḍā nāgā yakṣagaṃdharvakinnarāḥ 
 siddhā vidyādharāś cāpi tathā cāpy apsarogaṇāḥ  Rm 
 yogino yatayas tīrthā ṛṣayo brahmacāriṇaḥ 
 rājāno rājaputrāś ca vaiśyāś ca maṃtriṇo janāḥ  Rm 
 amātyāḥ sainikāś cāpi gṛhasthāś ca mahājanāḥ 
 vaṇijaḥ sārthavāhāś ca śilpinaḥ paurikā api  Rm 
 grāmyā jānapadāś cāpi tathānyadeśavāsinaḥ 
 evam anye 'pi lokāś ca saddharmāmṛtavāṃchinaḥ  Rm 
 sarve te tatra kauśāṃvyā ghoṣilārāma āgatāḥ 
 sabhāsanasamāsīnaṃ prādrākṣus taṃ munīśvaraṃ  Rm 
 dṛṣṭvā te muditāḥ sarve praṇatvā samupāsṛtāḥ 
 yathākramaṃ samabhyarcya kṛtvā tritvaḥ pradakṣiṇaṃ  Rm 
 tat saddharmāmṛtaṃ pātum upatasthuḥ samāhitāḥ  Rm 
 tatra te tatsabhāsīnā bhikṣavaḥ śrāvakā api 
 bhikṣuṇyaś cailakāś caivam upāsakā upāsikāḥ  Rm 
 bodhisatvā mahāsatvāḥ saṃbodhivratacāriṇaḥ 
 vasuṃdharāvratotpattiṃ śrotuṃ sarve samīchire  Rm 
 tatrānaṃdaḥ parijñāya teṣāṃ manaḥsamīhitaṃ 
 sāṃjaliḥ purataḥ sthitvā natvaivaṃ prārthayan muniṃ  Rm 
 bhagavan sarvavic chāstān ime sarve sabhājanāḥ 
 vasulakṣmīvratotpattiṃ śrotum ichanti āsṛtāḥ  Rm 
 Rm 
 tad bhavāṃs trijagacchāstā sarvasatvābhibodhane 
 vasulakṣmīvratotpattiṃ samupādeṣṭum arhati  Rm 
 ity ānaṃdena bhadreṇa prārthite sa munīśvaraḥ 
 tān sabhāsaṃsthitān sarvān samālokyaivam ādiśat  Rm 
 śṛṇv ānanda pravakṣyāmi munīndreṇa yathoditaṃ 
 vajradharābdhigambhīranirghoṣeṇa śrutaṃ mayā  Rm 
 tadyathābhūt purā rājā sūryodayābhidho nṛpaḥ 
 śrīpure nagare ramye cakravarttī nṛpādhipaḥ  Rm 
 daśākuśalasaṃraktaḥ pramadājanavaśyagaḥ 
 tadā tatra narāḥ sarve 'py asanmitropadeśataḥ 
 daśākusalamūleṣu karmasu saṃpracerire  Rm 
 tadā tatpāpadoṣeṇa mahetayaḥ pravarttitāḥ 
 tad ītisamupākrāntā saṃkṣobhitābhavan mahī  Rm 
 tataḥ sarvatra deśeṣu durbhikṣam abhavad bhuvi 
 tadā te manujāḥ sarve daridrā abhavan kramāt  Rm 
 tatas te nirdhanāḥ sarve kṣutpipāsāhatāturāḥ 
 lobhitā nirdayāḥ krūrāḥ praduṣṭā duritāratāḥ 
 svakuladharmamaryādaṃ vilaṃghyāpy aśubhe 'caran  Rm 
 tataḥ sarve 'pi te lokā andhā iva kumārgagāḥ 
 asatsaṃgānusaṃraktāḥ pracerur narakāmukhāḥ  Rm 
 tadā tatpāpasaṃghṛṣṭaduḥkhāgniparitāpitā 
 śoṣitevābhavad bhūmī nirguṇā nīrasā kharā  Rm 
 tadā sarve 'pi satvāś ca kṣuttṛṣṇāgnyahidāhitāḥ 
 nirāśā mṛtyum ichanto niṣeduḥ parimohitāḥ  Rm 
 tadaikasmin dine tatra tuṣitabhuvane sthitāḥ 
 śrīdevīpramukhā devyo vasundharyyāḥ sahāyikāḥ  Rm 
 sarvās tā militā martyaloke gaṃtuṃ samipsavaḥ 
 kim idānīṃ manuṣyāṇām avastheti samīkṣire  Rm 
 tatas tān manujān sarvān daridrān pāpacāriṇaḥ 
 dṛṣṭvā tāḥ sakalā devyā dayārttā evam abruvan  Rm 
 aho duḥkhaṃ manuṣyāṇāṃ yat pāpe niratā narāḥ 
 daridrā nirdayāḥ krūrā bhavanti narakāmukhāḥ  Rm 
 tat tatra martyaloke 'pi daridryaduḥkhaśāntaye 
 yatnāc chrīvasudhārāyā vrataṃ cārayemahi  Rm 
 tatas te manujāḥ sarve śrutvā dṛṣṭvānumoditāḥ 
 śrīdevyāḥ śaraṇaṃ gatvā careyur vratam ādarāt  Rm 
 tadā tatpuṇyasaṃpūtāḥ sarve te mānavā api 
 śrīmantaḥ sukhino bhadre careyuḥ sarvadādarāt  Rm 
 tatas te manujāḥ sarve daśakuśalasaṃratāḥ 
 parasparahitaṃ kṛtvā careyur bodhisaṃvaraṃ  Rm 
 tatas te bhadritātmānaḥ sarvasatvahitodyatāḥ 
 bodhisatvā mahāsatvā bhaveyur bodhicāriṇaḥ  Rm 
 tatas te sadguṇādhānās triratnabhajanāratāḥ 
 kramāt saṃbodhim āsādya saṃbuddhapadam āpnuyuḥ  Rm 
 Rm 
 iti hetor vayaṃ sarvāḥ śrīdevyāḥ purato gatāḥ 
 etat sarvapravṛttāṃtaṃ vijñāpayema sāṃprataṃ  Rm 
 ity evaṃ saṃmataṃ kṛtvā sarvā devvyo 'pi tās tataḥ 
 śrīvasudhāmahādevyā ālaye samupācaran  Rm 
 tatra tāḥ sakalā devyaḥ sāṃjalaya upāsṛtāḥ 
 tāṃ śrīvasuṃdharāṃ devīṃ praṇatvaivaṃ nyavedayan  Rm 
 bhagavati mahādevi vijānīyād bhavaṃty api 
 yan manuṣyā daridrās te bhavanti pāpacāriṇaḥ  Rm 
 tad bhavatī prayatnena manujāns tān suduḥkhitān 
 kṛpayā sahasālokya sarvānn uddharttum arhati  Rm 
 iti saṃprārthite tābhir devībhiḥ sā vasundharā 
 tā devī sakalā dṛṣṭvā prasannāsyaivam abravīt  Rm 
 aho duḥkhaṃ manuṣyāṇāṃ yatra śāstā na sadguruḥ 
 tena te 'kuśalācārāḥ sarve narā daridratāḥ  Rm 
 pāpābhis saṃratā duṣṭā kṣuttṛṣṇāgnyabhidāhitāḥ 
 durbhagā nirdayāḥ krūrāḥ pateyur narake dhruvaṃ  Rm 
 iti hetor ahaṃ tesāṃ martyānāṃ duḥkhaśāṃtaye 
 saṃvare tānn upasthāpya bodhau niyojayemahi  Rm 
 iti niścitya sā devī vasulakṣmī kṛpārditā 
 tatra samādhim ādhāya trimurttiṃ sā samādadhau  Rm 
 tadyathaikā vasuṃdharyyā mahālakṣmī dvitīyakā 
 tṛtīyikā kumāryyāś ca trimūrttir iti sā dadhe  Rm 
 tataḥ sā śrīmahādevī gaṃtuṃ martyālaye svayaṃ 
 naṃdīmukhāśvaghoṣau dvau samāmaṃtryaivam ādiśat  Rm 
 naṃdīmukhāśvaghoṣau yan mayā saṃprārthitaṃ yathā 
 tathā tan me mahatkāryaṃ harttum arhatha sarvathā  Rm 
 ity ādiṣṭaṃ tayā devyā niśamya tau kṛtāṃjaliḥ 
 nandimukhāśvaghoṣau tāṃ devīṃ natvaivam ūcatuḥ  Rm 
 devi kiṃ te mahat kāryaṃ tadā jñāpayatu dhruvaṃ 
 yathādiṣṭaṃ bhavaty āśu kariṣyāvas tathā khalu  Rm 
 iti tābhyāṃ samākhyātaṃ śrutvā sā śrīvasuṃdharā 
 mahādevī prasannāsyā tau dṛṣṭvaivam abhāṣata  Rm 
 śṛṇuta bhadramukhau yan me kāryaṃ vāṃ tan mayocyate 
 tathā yuvāṃ samādhāya karttum arhatha sāṃprataṃ  Rm 
 yan narā bhūtale sarve daridrā atiduḥkhitā 
 pāpābhiniratā duṣṭā bhavanti narakāmukhāḥ  Rm 
 tat tān sarvān samuddharttum ichāmi sarvathā 'dhunā 
 tridhā mūrttim ahaṃ dhṛtvā gacheyaṃ tan mahītale  Rm 
 tayo rājā mahīpālaḥ sarvalokādhipaḥ prabhuḥ 
 taṃ evaṃ prathamaṃ dharme vinīya yojayemahi  Rm 
 yatra rājā svayaṃ dharme sthitvā caret samāhitaḥ 
 tatra sarve 'nugā rājño dharme careyur ādarāt  Rm 
 yatrābhinirato rājā carate 'py aśubhe śubhe 
 Rm 
 tatra sarve 'pi lokās te pracareyur hi sādaraṃ  Rm 
 ity ādau nṛpati dharme yojanīyaḥ prayatnataḥ 
 tataḥ sa nṛpatiḥ sārvāl lokān dharme niyojayet  Rm 
 tataḥ sarve 'pi lokās te daśākuśalavaimukhāḥ 
 saddharme hi ratā bhadre pracareyuḥ samāhitāḥ  Rm 
 tataḥ sarve 'pi te lokāḥ parasparahitonmukhāḥ 
 triratnabhajanaṃ kṛtvā careyuḥ saṃvare sadā  Rm 
 tatas te sarvadā śreyaḥ kṛtvā yāyuḥ sukhāvatīṃ 
 tatrāpi saṃvaraṃ dhṛtvā pracareyuḥ sukhānvitāḥ  Rm 
 tataḥ kramāt samādhāya sarvapāramitāsv api 
 carantaḥ sarvasatvānāṃ hitaṃ kuryuḥ sadādarāt  Rm 
 tatas te bodhisatvāḥ syuḥ saddharmaguṇaratninaḥ 
 śuddhātmāno mahāsatvā bhaviṣyanti jinātmajāḥ  Rm 
 tataḥ sarve 'pi te dhīrāḥ pariśuddha trimaṇḍalāḥ 
 triyānabodhim āsādya saṃbuddhapadam āpnuyuḥ  Rm 
 iti hetor ahaṃ teṣāṃ satvānāṃ vinayārthataḥ 
 trimūrttirūpam ādhāya gachāmi bhūtale 'dhunā  Rm 
 tad yuvāṃ me vaco dhṛtvā gantum arhatha bhūtale 
 tatra gatvā prayatnena sarvathāhara taṃ nṛpaṃ  Rm 
 tato 'haṃ taṃ vaśīkṛtya bodhayitvā prayatnataḥ 
 saddharmacāriṇaṃ kṛtvā cārayiṣyāmi me vrataṃ  Rm 
 iti tayā mahādevyā samādiṣṭaṃ niśamya tau 
 nandimukhāśvaghoṣau tāṃ devīṃ natvaivam ūcatuḥ  Rm 
 bhadre devi tavādeśaṃ dhṛtvāvāṃ śirasā tathā 
 gatvā nṛpaṃ samāhṛtya prāṇayiṣyāvahe puraḥ  Rm 
 ity uktvā tau prasannāsyau kṛtāṃjalipuṭo mudā 
 pādau devyāḥ praṇatvaivaṃ prajagmatus tato bhuvi  Rm 
 trimūrttirūpam ādhāya vasulakṣmīr api svayaṃ 
 śrīdevyādisakhīyuktā gaṃgātīram upāgatāḥ  Rm 
 tatra tau bhūtale gatvā prāpaśyataṃ samaṃtataḥ 
 ramaṇīyaṃ mahodyāne puṣkariṇīpraśobhitaṃ  Rm 
 dṛṣṭvā tāv ubhau tatra kṣaṇaṃ viśramya saṃsthitau 
 tato mithasamāsīnau dṛṣṭvaivaṃ samabhāṣatāṃ  Rm 
 aho ramyaṃ mahīlokaṃ taḍāgodyānamaṇḍitaṃ 
 tat katham iha rājānam apaharttuṃ carevahi  Rm 
 tatra nandīmukhaḥ prāha divyastrīsuṃdaraṃ vapuḥ 
 dhṛtvāvāṃ surasaṃgītaṃ gāyantau prācarevahi  Rm 
 nūnaṃ sa nṛpatī rājā dṛṣṭvā nau divyasuṃdaraṃ 
 vapuḥ kāmāgnisaṃtaptaḥ samāharttum upācaret  Rm 
 tadāvāṃ sahasāhṛtya nṛpatiṃ taṃ prayatnataḥ 
 mohayitvā vaśīkṛtya devyā upānayevahi  Rm 
 iti saṃbhāṣaṇaṃ kṛtvā vidhāya ca susaṃmataṃ 
 nandimukhāśvaghoṣau tau strīrūpaṃ dadhatus tathā  Rm 
 tatas te divyarāmāṃśe manābhirāmaniḥsvanaiḥ 
 Rm 
 gāyaṃtyau surasaṃgītaṃ durgāsthane niṣedatuḥ  Rm 
 tayos tat surasaṃgītaṃ śrutvā tatpuravāsinaḥ 
 janāḥ kautūhalākrāntacittā draṣṭum upāsaran  Rm 
 dṛṣṭvā te divyarūpāṃśe sarve te vismayānvitāḥ 
 devakanye ime nūnam iti proktvā samīkṣire  Rm 
 divyāṃśe te samālokya sarve te vismayoddhatāḥ 
 aho citram iti proktvā pratyāyayuś cirāt puraṃ  Rm 
 tatra te surakanyāṃśe naikasthāne niṣedatuḥ 
 pratidinaṃ caturddikṣu pragāyaṃtyau praceratuḥ  Rm 
 tathā te caritaṃ dṛṣṭvā sarve te paurikā api 
 atyadbhutasamākrāṃtacittā ceruḥ praśaṃkitāḥ  Rm 
 tatas te paurikā lokāḥ sādbhutaśaṃkitāśayāḥ 
 nṛpateḥ purato gatvā praṇatvaivaṃ nyavedayet  Rm 
 jaya deva mahārāja vijānīyā bhavānn api 
 tathāpy atra mahac citraṃ vijñaptuṃ vayam āgatāḥ  Rm 
 tad atra surarāmāṃśe ubhe striyau sulakṣaṇau 
 gāyantyau surasaṃgītaṃ durgāsthāne samāśrite  Rm 
 pratidinaṃ caturdikṣu tathā te devakanyake 
 gāyaṃtyo surasaṃgītaṃ bhramitvā carato mudā  Rm 
 tan nimittaṃ kathaṃ rājaṃ cchubhaṃ vā syād athāśubhaṃ 
 iti praṣṭuṃ samāyāmo vayaṃ sarve 'pi nānyathā  Rm 
 iti taiḥ paurikaiḥ sarvair niveditaṃ niśamya saḥ 
 mahīpatiḥ kṣaṇaṃ dhyātvā tato dṛṣṭvaivam abravīt  Rm 
 strībhir ālāpitaṃ gītaṃ śubhāya na bhavet kvacit 
 ity uktvā sa viṣaṇṇātmā manasaivaṃ vyacintayat  Rm 
 kṣemaṃ neme bhaven nūnaṃ yat te striyau na mānave 
 strīrūpā vahinirmāya preṣite kena māyayā  Rm 
 tad atra kiṃ bhaven nūnaṃ tan nimittaṃ śubhaṃ na hi 
 kim upāyaṃ kariṣyāmi na manye ko hitaṃ diśet  Rm 
 iti ciṃttā viṣaṇṇātmā nṛpatiḥ sa viniśvasan 
 śokālaye samāsīno vahi naivācaret kvacit  Rm 
 tathā sthitaṃ narendraṃ taṃ matvā vahir anirgataṃ 
 nandīmukho 'svaghoṣaṃ taṃ samālokyaivam abravīt  Rm 
 aśvaghoṣa narendro 'sau tathāpi na vahiś caret 
 tad atra kiṃ kariṣyāvo yan nṛpo na vahiś caret  Rm 
 iti tenoditaṃ śrutva so 'śvaghoṣo vicintayan 
 taṃ nandimukham ālokya bodhayann evam abravīt  Rm 
 śṛṇu naṃdimukhopāyaṃ yena nṛpaḥ sa nicaret 
 tad ahaṃ saṃpravakṣyāmi tan nṛpāharaṇaṃ prati  Rm 
 yat tatra nṛpater gehe māyāgninābhidhakṣyate 
 tadā sa nṛpatis trastaḥ kopito niḥsared vahi  Rm 
 tadā taṃ nṛpatiṃ dūrāt samāhṛtya prayatnataḥ 
 sahasā purato devyā upaneṣyāvahe drutaṃ  Rm 
 Rm 
 iti tenoditaṃ śrutvā nandīmukhaḥ sa bodhitaḥ 
 tathā hīti pratiśrutya tathā kartuṃ samaichata  Rm 
 tatas tau saṃmataṃ kṛtvā tato 'py antarhitau drutaṃ 
 gatvā māyāgninā tābhyāṃ pradāhitaṃ nṛpālayaṃ  Rm 
 tad dṛṣṭvā nṛpatis trastaḥ sahasā niścarans tataḥ 
 upāyais taj jvaladvahniṃ śamayām āsa satvaraṃ  Rm 
 tataḥ sa bhūpatī rājā taccintāparikheṭitaḥ 
 śokāgare viṣaṇṇātmā sthitaś caiva vyacintayat  Rm 
 aho sadyaphalaṃ hy etad yat strīgītanimittajaṃ 
 tad atra kiṃ kariṣyāmi yenaitac chāmyate 'śubhaṃ  Rm 
 bhūyo 'py atra bhaved anyan mahotpātam amaṃgalaṃ 
 katham atra pratīkāraṃ kariṣyāmi na manyate  Rm 
 iti ciṃtāviṣaṇṇātmā nṛpatiḥ sa vimohitaḥ 
 śokāgāre samāsīno naiva vahir viniryayau  Rm 
 tathāpi svālayāsīnaṃ dṛṣṭvā vahir ayāyinaṃ 
 nandīmukhāśvaghoṣau tau punar evaṃ samūcatuḥ  Rm 
 tathāpi sa nṛpo rājā naiva vahir viniḥsaret 
 tad atra kiṃ kariṣyāvo yenāśu niścaren nṛpaḥ  Rm 
 tataś cāpi samālokya so 'śvaghoṣo vicintayan 
 naṃdīmukhaṃ sahāyaṃ taṃ samāmaṃtryaivam abravīt  Rm 
 bho sakhe sa mahārājas tathāpi nātra niścaret 
 tad atra kiṃ vilambena yatnena taṃ harevahi  Rm 
 varāharūpam ādhāya tasyodyāne manorame 
 sarvatrotpātanaṃ kastuṃ pracārevo 'dhunā drutaṃ  Rm 
 iti tenoditaṃ śrutvā naṃdīmukhas tatheti sā 
 pratiśrutya sakhāyaṃ taṃ samālokyaivam abravīt  Rm 
 evam api kariṣyāvo devīkāryābhisiddhaye 
 iti tau saṃmataṃ kṛtvā tatrodyāne prajagmatuḥ  Rm 
 tatra tau samupālokya puṣkariṇīṃ manoramāṃ 
 nānāpuṣpasamākīrṇāṃ paśyaṃtau tasthatuś ciraṃ  Rm 
 tato nandīmukho dṛṣṭvā tam udyānaṃ manoramaṃ 
 puskariṇīṃ ca prāmodya gaṃdhāḍhyām evam abravīt  Rm 
 ahodyānaṃ manoramyaṃ suramyaṃ ca saro varaṃ 
 nedaṃ vidhvaṃsanīyaṃ hi kathaṃ vidhvaṃsayevahi  Rm 
 iti tenoditaṃ śrutvā so 'śvaghoṣo viciṃtayan 
 udyānaṃ tat saro dṛṣṭvācirād evam abhāṣata  Rm 
 yathābhilaṣitaṃ devyāḥ sādhayeva tathā drutaṃ 
 tan nṛpatim apāharttuṃ tad idaṃ dhvaṃsayāvahe  Rm 
 ity uktvā saumataṃ kṛtvā tāv ubhau mahadāśrayaṃ 
 varāharūpam āsthāya prajagmatus sarastaṭe  Rm 
 raktākṣau hṛṣṭaromāṇau nādāpuritadiṅmukhau 
 siṃhaśārdūlasadṛśau damṣṭravibhīṣaṇānanau  Rm 
 tatra tau prasarantau tad udyānaṃ tat saro 'pi ca 
 vindhvaṃsitum upākramya praceratuḥ samaṃtataḥ  Rm 
 Rm 
 tau varāhau samālokya traste udyānapālakaḥ 
 sahasā sa vinirgatya tato rājakule yayau  Rm 
 tatra sa samupāsṛtya rājñaḥ pādau kṛtāṃjaliḥ 
 natvā trāsavibhinnāsyaḥ pura evaṃ nyavedayat  Rm 
 jaya deva vijānīyā yad udyāne sarovaraṃ 
 dvau varāhāv upākramya dhvaṃsituṃ caratā 'dhunā  Rm 
 tad atra sahasā deva sarvasainyajanānn api 
 samupāhūya tau haṃtuṃ preṣayasva drutaṃ vane  Rm 
 iti tenoditaṃ śrutvā sa rājā parikopitaḥ 
 sahasā sainyam āhūya svayaṃ tau hantum udyayau  Rm 
 tataḥ sa nṛpatī rājā samaṃtrīsainyapaurikāḥ 
 sahasā nādayan vādyāns tatrodyāne upācarat  Rm 
 tatra sa nṛpatir dṛṣṭvā samaṃtrisainyapaurikān 
 tān sarvān samupāmaṃtrya punar evam upādiśat  Rm 
 bho bhavanto janāḥ sarve sajjīkṛtya samāhitāḥ 
 atra dṛṣṭvopatiṣṭhantu parivṛtya samaṃtataḥ  Rm 
 ahaṃ prāgdiśi tiṣṭhāmi yāmye 'mātyāḥ samaṃtriṇaḥ 
 paścimādiśi sainānyaḥ paurās tiṣṭhantu cottare  Rm 
 evaṃ sarve 'py amātyādyāḥ sarvadikṣu samāhitāḥ 
 sajjīkṛtyābhitiṣṭhantu parivṛtya samaṃtataḥ  Rm 
 yatra sthāne varāhau tau boddhuṃ naivābhiśaknutha 
 yataś cāsau parāyetāṃ taddiksthān daṇḍayeya hi  Rm 
 iti me vacanaṃ śrutvā sarve yūyaṃ samāhitāḥ 
 sajjīkṛtya samālokya parivṛtyānutiṣṭhata  Rm 
 iti rājñā samādiṣṭaṃ śrutvā sarve 'pi te janāḥ 
 tatheti prativijñapya tathā sthātuṃ pracerire  Rm 
 tathā rājā sthitaḥ prācyāṃ yāmye 'mātyagaṇās tathā 
 senānyo paścimāyāṃ ca paurās tasthus tathottare  Rm 
 evaṃ te sanṛpā lokāḥ sāmātyasainyapaurikāḥ 
 sajjīkṛtya samālokya sarve tasthuḥ samāhitāḥ  Rm 
 evaṃ te sarvato dikṣu nirudhya samavasthitāḥ 
 sarvavādyābhinirghoṣaṃ mahārāvair akheṭayan  Rm 
 tat savādyamahārāvaṃ śrutvā tau tān upasthitān 
 samaṃtataḥ samālokya mahāśabdaṃ vyamuṃcatāṃ  Rm 
 tatas tau sahasotpātamahāvāte pravarttataiḥ 
 kṛtvāndhakāraṇair lokya rājānam adhyadhāvatāṃ  Rm 
 tatra sa nṛpatis tābhyāṃ spṛśyamāno vimūrchitaḥ 
 saṃtrāsaparibhūyātmā kaṃpito nyapatad bhuvi  Rm 
 tataś cirāt samutthāya kutremāv iti lokya saḥ 
 sahasāśvaṃ samāruhya tad anuprāsaran yayau  Rm 
 tathā te maṃtriṇo 'mātyāḥ sainyalokāś ca paurikāḥ 
 sarve te 'py anudhāvantaḥ pradudruvur nṛpānugāḥ  Rm 
 sa nṛpāśvasamārūḍhas tadvarāhānugaḥ śaraṃ 
 maurvīyuktaiḥ samādhāya vegād vanam upāviśat  Rm 
 Rm 
 tatra tau māyikau tyaktvā vārāhadeham āśu tau 
 niviśyāśvaṃ samāhṛtya prerayatāṃ vanāṃtare  Rm 
 tatra so 'śvo mahāvegād vāyunā riva mahājavi 
 vilaṃghya nimnagāṃ chailāṃ pradudrāva mahāvane  Rm 
 tatas te maṃtriṇo 'mātyāḥ sainānyaḥ sainikāḥ prajāḥ 
 nṛpaṃ dūravanāviṣṭaṃ dṛṣṭvā pratyāyayuḥ śramāt  Rm 
 sena eko mahāvīraḥ svāmyamārgānusaṃcaran 
 asakteḥ asahas tūrṇaṃ kamaṇḍalukaras tadā  Rm 
 chāyeva sahago vegād vanāṃtare tathānvagāt  Rm 
 tatrātivegato rājā vāyuhato samāhitaḥ 
 aśvavṛkṣatale so 'śvād dhāvatā nyapatad bhuvi  Rm 
 tatra sa mūrchito rājā kṣaṇaṃ tasthāv acetanaḥ 
 tataḥ senaḥ prayatnena niḥśvasanrudatiṣṭhata  Rm 
 tataḥ sena samāśvāsya dhṛtvā taṃ nṛpam ātmanā 
 saha tatrāsane sthāpya vyaśrāmayec chramānvitaṃ  Rm 
 tataḥ sa nṛpa ālokya tam aśvaṃ samupasthitaṃ 
 tṛṣārtto niḥśvasan senaṃ muhur dṛṣṭvaivam abravīt  Rm 
 aho sena mahat kaṣṭaṃ jāyate nāv ihā 'dhunā 
 yat sudūre mahāraṇye majjāvahe sudustare  Rm 
 tad atra kiṃ kariṣyāvo yat sarve nirvṛto janāḥ 
 sudūre nirjane 'raṇye ko 'tra mārgaṃ hi nirdiśet  Rm 
 yad atrātitṛṣārtto 'haṃ tāpavātāhatāturaḥ 
 śramakleśāgnisaṃdagdho dhairyeṇāpi vimocitaḥ  Rm 
 tad atra sahasā sena mama jīvitarakṣaṇaṃ 
 yatas tato 'pi vānviṣya śītalāmṛtam ānaya  Rm 
 iti rājñoditaṃ śrutvā sa seneḥ sahasotthitaḥ 
 svāminaṃ taṃ samāśvāsya paśyann evam abhāṣata  Rm 
 mā viṣīdāta rājendra yat kṣatriyo 'si dhīravān 
 tad bhavān dhairyam ālambya muhurttaṃ sthātum arhati  Rm 
 yatas tato 'pi vānviṣya pāṇīyam amṛtopamaṃ 
 sahasā samupānīya dāsyāmi te narādhipa  Rm 
 tad yāvannātra pāṇīyaṃ dhṛtvāgachāmi sarvathā 
 tāvad dhairyaṃ samālambya tiṣṭhāśvena saha prabho  Rm 
 iti vijñapya seno 'sau svāminaṃ taṃ narādhipaṃ 
 samāśvāsya supāṇīyam anveṣituṃ drutaṃ yayau  Rm 
 tatra sa samupālokya sarvatrāpy abhilokayan 
 supāṇīyam anasādya paśyan dūratare yayān  Rm 
 tatra suranadīśabdaṃ śrutvā senaḥ sa satvaraḥ 
 tac chabdaṃ samanuśrutvā tatrābhyanusaran yayau  Rm 
 tatra tīraṃ samāsādya suranadyāḥ samāditaḥ 
 sahasā samupāśritya pānīyaṃ surasaṃ papau  Rm 
 tatra sa parituṣṭātmā samaṃtato vilokayan 
 tatpāre śuddhite dvīpe prādrākṣīd apsarogaṇān  Rm 
 Rm 
 tān apsarogaṇān dṛṣṭvā sa seno vismayānvitaḥ 
 mudā vilokayann eva tasthau citrārppitā yathā  Rm 
 tatrasthaṃtaṃ samālokya sarvā apsaraso 'pi tāḥ 
 katham atrāgataḥ kas tvaṃ prehīti samakandayan  Rm 
 iti tābhiḥ samāhūtaṃ śrutvā sa sena ātmanā 
 suranadīṃ vilaṃghyāśu tatprabhāvād upāsarat  Rm 
 tatra sa samupāśritya sarvāns tān apsarogaṇān 
 sāṃjaliḥ suprasannāsyaḥ praṇatvaivaṃ nyavedayat  Rm 
 mahādevyā vijānīdhvaṃ yat trailokyeṣu viśrutaḥ 
 sūryodayo mahārājas tasyāhaṃ sevako 'nugaḥ  Rm 
 yan nṛpasya varāhābhyāṃ udyānaṃ dhvaṃsitaṃ tataḥ 
 tau varāhau nihaṃtuṃ sa nṛpo 'nudhāvati drutaṃ  Rm 
 aśvenāpahṛto rājā sa mayaikena naujjhitaḥ 
 atyabhidhāvato 'raṇye patito 'śvād ihā 'dhunā  Rm 
 aśokavṛkṣa āśritya gharmavātā hato 'turaḥ 
 śramatṛsārditas tatra sthito 'mbu pātum ichati  Rm 
 tad ambu sarvato 'nviṣya kutrāpi labhyate na hi 
 nadīśabdam ihākarṇya sahasāham upāsare  Rm 
 atra me bhāgyayogena preṣito 'ham ihāgataḥ 
 labhāmi darśanaṃ devyo bhavāṃtīnam aho 'dhunā  Rm 
 ity uktvā sena ālokya sāṃjaliḥ purato gataḥ 
 tāḥ sarvā apsarā devīnatvaitaṃ samapṛchata  Rm 
 bho devyo bhavantyo 'pi kim artham iha tiṣṭhatha 
 vaktavyaṃ cet tad arthaṃ me samupādeṣṭum arhatha  Rm 
 iti saṃprārthitaṃ tena niśamyāyāpsaro 'dhipāḥ 
 sā taṃ senaṃ samāmaṃtrya purar evam upādiśat  Rm 
 mānava tvaṃ na jānāsi yad idaṃ vratam uttamaṃ 
 śrīvasudhāmahādevyā vayaṃ sarvāś carāmahe  Rm 
 iti devyā tayākhyātaṃ śrutvā senaḥ sa moditaḥ 
 tad vrataṃ dharttum ichaṃs tāṃ devīṃ natvaivam abravīt  Rm 
 prasīda me mahādevi yac chrīdevyā idaṃ vrataṃ 
 aham api samichāmi dhartuṃ tan me upādiśa  Rm 
 iti tenārthitaṃ śrutvā sā devī paritoṣitā 
 taṃ senaṃ sudhiyaṃ dhīraṃ matvaivam abravīt punaḥ  Rm 
 mānava vadi te vāṃchāpy asti śrīvasudhāvrate 
 tat tāvad iha saṃpaśya samāpyetā 'dhunā vrataṃ  Rm 
 paścāt te 'haṃ samākhyāya śrīdevyā vratasādhanaṃ 
 vidhiṃ samupadekṣyāmi saṃbuddhena yathoditaṃ  Rm 
 ity uktvā sāpsaro devī sarvās tā apsarogaṇāḥ 
 prāhūya tan nadītīre vratārambhaṃ tathākarot  Rm 
 tatra tāḥ samupāśritya sarvā devyā yathākramaṃ 
 yathāvidhi samārabhya vrataṃ pūrṇaṃ pracakrire  Rm 
 Rm 
 tad vrataṃ samupālokya sa seno 'bhyanumoditaḥ 
 aṣṭāṃgapraṇatiṃ kṛtvā sāṃjalir evam abravīt  Rm 
 aho bhāgyena saṃprāptaṃ śridevīvratadarśanaṃ 
 tan metiḥ kṣīyate pāpam ātmāri śuddhyate 'dhunā  Rm 
 prasīdata mahādevyaḥ sarvā me kṛpayā dṛśā 
 paśyantyo 'nugrahaṃ kṛtvā vrate pradātum arhataṃ  Rm 
 sarvadāhaṃ cariṣyāmi śrīdevyāḥ śaraṇaṃ gatāḥ 
 tad vratavidhi saṃpūrṇaṃ samupādeṣṭum arhatha  Rm 
 iti saṃprārthitaṃ tena śrutvā devī pradhānikā 
 sā taṃ senaṃ viśuddhāṃśaṃ dṛṣṭvaivaṃ samupādiśat  Rm 
 śṛṇu sādho samādhāya vratavidhiṃ samucyate 
 vajradharābdhigaṃbhīranirghoṣeṇa yathoditaṃ  Rm 
 bhādrapade 'site pakṣe śuklapakṣe 'pi vā tathā 
 māghe māse ca tadvac ca sarveṣv api ca māsu vā  Rm 
 dvitīyāyām upātīrthe snātvā śuddhāmvarāvṛtaḥ 
 śuddhabhūmī pradeśeṣu saṃśodhayet samaṃtataḥ  Rm 
 mṛdgomayaśubhāmbhobhiḥ pralipya pariśodhayan 
 tatra ratnamayaraṅgai dhātucūrṇaiś ca paṃcabhiḥ  Rm 
 pauṣpikair vrīhicūrṇair vā tathā pāṣāṇacūrṇakaiḥ 
 yathāvidhi samārabhya sūtrayitvā yathākramaṃ  Rm 
 guruḥ śiṣyaiḥ sahālakṣya varttayen maṇḍalaṃ kramāt 
 tatra devyādi cihnāni likhed yathāvidhi kramāt  Rm 
 saptavrīhyāvalībhiś ca saṃveṣṭayet samaṃtataḥ 
 tatas tīrthāmbusaṃpūrṇān pītavastrāvṛtān ghaṭān 
 ṣoḍaśadevatācihna lakṣitān pariśuddhitān  Rm 
 paṃcaratnāmṛtauṣadhyapallavapratisaṃyutān 
 suvarṇatilakachatradhvajapatākikānvitān  Rm

 dhvajacāmarasaṃyuktavitānaiḥ parimaṃḍayet  Rm 
 vicitrapuṣpamālābhiḥ sugaṃdhibhiḥ samaṃtataḥ 
 saurabhyadhūpanai dīpai paṃktibhiś cābhiśobhayet  Rm 
 tatas tanmaṇḍale devīṃ sagaṇāṃ śrīvasuṃdharāṃ 
 dhyātvāvāhya samabhyarcya pratiṣṭhāpyādhivāsayet  Rm 
 tato rātrau trisaṃdhyaṃ ca samabhyarcya yathāvidhiḥ 
 baliṃ paṃcāmṛtair yuktaṃ datvā devīṃ smaraṃś caret  Rm 
 tataḥ prātas tṛtīyāyāṃ tīrthe dravyaiḥ sugaṃdhibhiḥ 
 saha śuddhāmbubhiḥ snātvā śuddhapītāmvarāvṛtaḥ  Rm 
 paṃcagavyaiḥ svam ātmānaṃ pariṣiṃcya viśodhayet

 vratīnāpi tathā snātvā śuddhapītāmvarāvṛtāḥ 
 paṃcagavyais tathā sarvār abhisiṃcya viśodhayet  Rm 
 tatas te vratinaḥ sarve ācāryyapramukhāḥ kramāt 
 madhyāhne yakṣarājasya digmukhāḥ svāsanāḥ śritāḥ  Rm 
 Rm 
 yathācāryasamādiṣṭaṃ tathādhārya samāhitāḥ 
 ādau vajradharaṃ natvā triratnaṃ śaraṇaṃ gatāḥ  Rm 
 maṃtrale sagaṇāṃ devīṃ dhyātvārcaye yathākramaṃ  Rm 
 tadyathā gurur ācāryaḥ śūnye drīkārasaṃbhavaṃ 
 pītavarṇaṃ mahāpad maṃ tatrasthaṃ candramaṇḍalaṃ 
 tadutthaṃ śrībhavaṃ ratnaparvataṃ tasya copari 
 tvaṃja bhadraghaṭāsīnāṃ bhāvayec chrīvasuṃdharāṃ  Rm 
 pītām ekamukhāṃ kāṃtām ṣaḍbhujāṃ lalitāsanāṃ 
 savye varadasaṃbuddhaṃ praṇāmaratnamaṃjalīṃ  Rm 
 vāme bhadraghaṭaprajñā pustakadhānyamaṃjaliṃ 
 dadhānaṃ ratnasaṃbuddhamakuṭinīṃ susuṃdarīṃ  Rm 
 pītapaṭṭāvṛtāṃ divyaratnālaṃkārabhūṣitaṃ 
 tad dvitīyapuṭe pṛṣṭhe pīto vajrāsano jināḥ  Rm 
 vajradharābdhinirghoṣo varābhayapradānabhṛt  Rm 
 dakṣiṇe dvibhujārakto varadavajrahastakaḥ 
 lokeśvaro rājallīlāvajraparyaṃkasaṃsthitaḥ  Rm 
 vajrapāṇis tathā vāme varadavajrabhṛtkaraḥ 
 haritā rājasaṃlīlā vajraparyaṃkasaṃsthitaḥ  Rm 
 līlā devī puraḥ pītā satvaparyaṃkasaṃsthitā 
 bhujadvayena sarvopakaraṇādhikṛtiṃ tadā  Rm 
 tad vāme varuṇaḥ śvetaḥ satvaparyaṃkasaṃsthitaḥ 
 vījapūrakam utsaṅgasthitiṃ karadvayena bhṛt  Rm 
 nīlobhe dakṣiṇe bhadraḥ satvaparyaṃkasaṃsthitaḥ 
 bījapūrakam ekena vibhrat kroḍaṃ tathāparaṃ  Rm 
 civikuṇḍalir āgneye iṣadraktas tathāsthitaḥ 
 bījapūrakam utsaṅge sthitiṃ dorbhyāṃ samā tathā  Rm 
 nairṛtye kelimālī ca śyāmavarṇas tathā sthitaḥ 
 bījapūrakam utsaṃgasthitaṃ dadhat karadvayaḥ  Rm 
 vāyavye ca mukhendrākhyaḥ pītavarṇas tathā sthitaḥ 
 bījapūrakam utsaṃgasthitiṃ dadhat karadvayaṃ  Rm 
 carendro gaurar iśāne satvaparyaṃkasaṃsthitaḥ 
 bījapūrakam utsaṃgasthitiṃ dadhad bhujadvayaḥ  Rm 
 tat tṛtīyapuṭe pūrve guptā devī tathā sthitā 
 haridvarṇā bhujābhyāṃ sa cāmaraṃ vibhratī dharā  Rm 
 nairṛte vasuguptākhyā devī raktās tathā sthitā 
 bhujābhyāṃ vibhratī chatraṃ sarvaratnasamujvalaṃ  Rm 
 sarasvatī ca vāyavye devī pītā tathā sthitā 
 dhvajahastā subhadrāṃgī sarvavidyārthadāyinī  Rm 
 iśāne caṃdrakāṃtākhyā devī śvetā tathā sthitā 
 patākā vibhratī sarvaratnālaṃkārabhūṣitā  Rm
